40001001	Igitabo kidondora ukuvuka kwa Yesu Kristo, umwana wa Dawidi. Dawidi ni umwana wa Aburahamu.
40001002	Aburahamu yavyaye Isaka. Isaka yavyaye Yakobo. Yakobo yavyaye Yuda n'abandi bavukana.
40001003	Yuda yavyaye Peresi na Zera kuri Tamari. Peresi yavyaye Hesironi. Hesironi yavyaye Ramu.
40001004	Ramu yavyaye Aminadabu. Aminadabu yavyaye Nahasoni. Nahasoni yavyaye Salumoni.
40001005	Salumoni yavyaye Bowazi kuri Rahabu. Bowazi yavyaye Obedi kuri Rusi. Obedi yavyaye Isayi.
40001006	Isayi yavyaye umwami Dawidi. Dawidi yavyaye Salomo kuri muka Uriya.
40001007	Salomo yavyaye Rehobowamu. Rehobowamu yavyaye Abiya. Abiya yavyaye Asa.
40001008	Asa yavyaye Yehoshafati. Yehoshafati yavyaye Yoramu. Yoramu yavyaye Uziya.
40001009	Uziya yavyaye Yotamu. Yotamu yavyaye Ahazi. Ahazi yavyaye Hezekiya.
40001010	Hezekiya yavyaye Manase. Manase yavyaye Amoni. Amoni yavyaye Yosiya.
40001011	Yosiya yavyaye Yekoniya n'abandi bavukana, mu gihe co kujanwa mu buja i Babuloni.
40001012	Kuva mu gihe co kujanwa mu buja i Babuloni Yekoniya yavyaye Shalutiyeli, Shalutiyeli yavyaye Zerubabeli.
40001013	Zerubabeli yavyaye Abihudi. Abihudi yavyaye Eliyakimu. Eliyakimu yavyaye Azori.
40001014	Azori yavyaye Sadoki. Sadoki yavyaye Akimu. Akimu yavyaye Elihudi.
40001015	Elihudi yavyaye Eleyazari. Eleyazari yavyaye Matani. Matani yavyaye Yakobo.
40001016	Yakobo yavyaye Yosefu, umugabo wa Mariya nyina wa Yesu yitwa Kristo.
40001017	Nuko ba sekuruza bose guhera kuri Aburahamu gushitsa kuri Dawidi n'icumi na bane, kandi guhera kuri Dawidi gushitsa ku gihe co kujanwa mu buja i Babuloni ni icumi na bane, kandi guhera ku gihe co kujanwa mu buja i Babuloni gushitsa kuri Kristo ni icumi na bane nyene.
40001018	Ukuvuka kwa Yesu Kristo kwabaye gutya: Mariya, nyina wiwe yari, akowe na Yosefu ataramurongora bamubona afise inda yavuye kuri Mpwemu Yera.
40001019	Ariko umugabo wiwe Yosefu, kuko ari umugororotsi, kandi kuko atagomvye kumutetereza, yiyumvira kumubengera mu mpisho.
40001020	Akivyiyumvira, umumarayika w' Umwami Imana amwiyerekera mu nzozi, aramubarira ati: "Yosefu, mwana wa Dawidi, ntutinye kurongora Mariya umugeni wawe, kuko atwaye inda ya Mpwemu Yera.
40001021	Azovyara umwana w'umuhungu, nawe uzomwite YESU, kuko ari we azokiza abantu biwe ivyaha vyabo."
40001022	Ivyo vyose vyabaye bityo ngo ivyo Umwami Imana yavugiye mu kanwa k'uwavugishwa na we biboneke,
40001023	ngo raba, inkumi izotwara inda, ivyare umwana w'umuhungu, Bazomwita Imanuweli; risobanurwa ngo Imana iri kumwe natwe.
40001024	Yosefu yikanguye aravyuka, agira nk'uko umumarayika w'Umwami Imana yamubariye, arongora umugeni wiwe.
40001025	Kandi ntiyigera amwegera gushitsa aho yavyariye umwana w'umuhungu; araheza amwita YESU.
40002001	Yesu amaze kuvukira i Betelehemu mu gihugu c'Ubuyuda ku butware bw'umwami Herode, haza abanyabwenge bavuye mu buseruko, baja i Yerusalemu,
40002002	barabaza bati: "Umwami w'Abayuda yavutse ari hehe? Kuko twabonye inyenyeri yiwe?" "ri mu buseruko, none tukaba tuzanywe no kumushengerera."
40002003	Umwami Herode avyumvise, ahagarikana umutima n'abo i Yerusalemu bose.
40002004	Akoranya abakuru b'abaherezi n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe bose bo muri ubwo bwoko, arababaza ati: "Kristo azovukira hehe?"
40002005	Bati: "Ni i Betelehemu mu gihugu c'i Yudaya, ni ko vyanditswe n'umuntu yavugishwa n'Imana,
40002006	Kandi wewe Betelehemu mu ntara y'Ubuyuda, Nturi mutoya mu baganwa b'Ubuyuda, Kuko kuri wewe hazova uwuganza, Ni we azoragira abantu banje b'Abisirayeli."
40002007	Buno Herode ahamagaza ba bahinga mu mpisho, abasiguza igihe iyo nyenyeri yabonekeye.
40002008	Abatuma i Betelehemu ati: "Nimugende, mubaze mushirutse umwete ivyo uwo mwana. Ni mwamubona muce muza kumbarira, ngo nanje ngende kumushengerera." "
40002009	Na bo bumvise iryo umwami, baragenda. Maze iyo nyenyeri babonye mu buseruko irabarongora, ibashikana hejuru y'aho uwo mwana ari, ihagararaho.
40002010	Babonye iyo nyenyeri banezerwa akaneza kenshi cane.
40002011	Bashitse mu nzu babona uwo mwana na Mariya nyina wiwe; bikubita hasi, baramupfukamira, barumura ibiseke vyabo, bamushikanira amashikanwa, izahabu, imibavu n'isenga.
40002012	Babwiriwe n'Imana mu nzozi ngo ntibasubire guca kwa Herode, baca mu yindi nzira, bisubirira mu gihugu c'i wabo.
40002013	Bamaze kugenda, umumarayika w'Umwami Imana yiyerekera Yosefu mu nzozi, aramubwira ati:" "Vyuka, ujane umwana na nyina, uhungire mu Misiri, ugumeyo gushitsa aho nzokubaririra, kuko Herode agira arondere umwana ngo amwice."
40002014	Ahenga mw'ijoro aravyuka, ajana umwana na nyina, aja mu Misiri,
40002015	aguma yo gushitsa Herode amaze gupfa, ngo ivyo Umwami Imana yavugiye mu wavugishwa na we bishike, ngo Nahamagaye umwana wanje ngo ave mu Misiri.
40002016	Maze Herode abonye ko yahenzwe n'abo banyabwenge, ararakara cane. Atuma kugeseza abana b'abahungu bose b'i Betelehemu no mu misozi yose ihakikije, abamaze imyaka ibiri n'abatarayimara, yagerereje igihe yasigurije abanyabwenge.
40002017	Ni ho ivyavuzwe na Yeremiya yavugishwa n'Imana vyashikiye,
40002018	ngo induru yumvikana i Rama, Amarira n'amaborogo menshi; Rakeli aririra abana biwe, Yanka kwirurwa, kuko batakiriho.
40002019	Herode amaze gupfa, umumarayika w'Umwami Imana yiyerekera Yosefu mu nzozi ari mu Misiri,
40002020	aramubwira ati: "Vyuka, ujane umwana na nyina, uje mu gihugu c'i Bwisirayeli, kuko abarondera kwica umwana bapfuye."
40002021	Avyutse, ajana umwana na nyina, aragenda, ashika mu gihugu c'i Bwisirayeli.
40002022	Ariko yumvise yuko Arukelayo yimitswe i Yudaya, asubiye ku butware bwa se Herode, atinya kujayo. Abwiriwe mu nzozi, aja mu bihugu vy'i Galilaya.
40002023	Ashitseyo, agerera mu gisagara citwa Nazareti, ngo ivyavuzwe n'abavugishwa n'Imana bishike, ngo azokwitwa Umunyanazareti.
40003001	Muri iyo misi haza Yohana Umubatizi, yigishiriza mu bugaragwa bw'i Yudaya
40003002	ati: "Mwihane, kuko ubwami bwo mw'ijuru buri hafi."
40003003	Uwo ni we yavuzwe na Yesaya yavugishwa n' Imana ati: "Ijwi ry'uwusemererera mu bugaragwa Ngo ni mutegure inzira y' Uhoraho, Mugorore izagutse ziwe."
40003004	Uwo Yohana, imyambaro yiwe yari iyo ubwoya bw'ingamiya, yayikenyeza umukanda w'urusato mu rukenyerero; indya ziwe zari inzige n'ubuki bwo mw'ishamba.
40003005	Maze abo i Yerusalemu n'abo i Yudaya bose n'igihugu giherereye kuri Yorodani cose, bava i wabo baza kuri we,
40003006	babatizwa na we mu ruzi Yorodani, batura ivyaha vyabo.
40003007	Abonye benshi bo mu Bafarisayo no mu Basadukayo bazanywe no kugira ngo ababatize, arababaza ati: "Mwa bana b'inzoka mwe, ni nde yababuriye ngo muhunge ishavu rizoza?"
40003008	Nuko ni mukore ibiberekana ko mwihanye koko.
40003009	Ntimwiyumvire mu mitima ngo mufise Aburahamu, ko sogokuruza. Ndababwira yuko aya mabuye Imana ishobora kuyakuramwo abana ba Aburahamu.
40003010	Ariko incabiti itumberejwe ku bitsina vy'ibiti; nuko rero igiti cose kitama ivyiza kiracibwa, kigatererwa mu muriro.
40003011	Ni ukuri jeho ndababatiza mu mazi ngo mwihane; ariko uwuzoza hanyuma yanje andusha ubushobozi, ntibimbereye no kumutwaza ibirato. Uwo azobabatiza muri Mpwemu Yera no mu muriro.
40003012	Urutaro rwiwe ruri mu kuboko kwiwe, kandi azokubura imbuga yiwe neza, yimburire ingano ziwe mu kigega, maze umuguruka awuturire mu muriro utazima.
40003013	Ico gihe Yesu ava i Galilaya, aja kuri Yorodani aje kuri Yohana, azanywe no kubatizwa na we.
40003014	Ariko Yohana agomba kumwankira ati: "Ko ari jewe nkwiye kubatizwa nawe; none unjeko?"
40003015	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Bikunde kuko ari vyo bidukwiye, ngo dushitse ukugororoka kwose." Buno aramukundira.
40003016	Yesu amaze kubatizwa, aca ava mu mazi; maze ijuru riruguruka, abona Mpwemu w'Imana, amanuka asa n'inuma, amugwako.
40003017	Buno rero ijwi riva mw'ijuru riti: "Uwu ni we Mwana wanje nkunda akampimbara."
40004001	Buno Yesu aduganwa na Mpwemu mu bugaragwa ngo ageragezwe n'Umwansi Satani.
40004002	Amaze imisi mirongo ine n'amajoro mirongo ine yisonzesheje, abona gusonza.
40004003	Umugeragezi aza kuri we ati: "Ni waba uri Umwana w' Imana, bwira aya mabuye acike imitsima."
40004004	Aramwishura ati: "Vyanditswe ngo umuntu ntatungwa n'umutsima gusa, ariko atungwa n'ijambo ryose riva mu kanwa k'Imana."
40004005	Buno Umwansi Satani amujana mu gisagara cera, amuhagarika ku gatwe k'urusengero,
40004006	aramubwira ati: "Ni waba uri Umwana w'Imana, ikororere hasi, kuko vyanditswe, ngo azokuragiza abamarayika biwe, Na bo bazokuramira mu maboko yabo, Ngo kumbure ntutsitare kw'ibuye."
40004007	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Vyongeye haranditswe, ngo Ntukagerageze Uhoraho, Imana yawe."
40004008	Umwansi Satani yongera kumujana ku musozi uhagaze cane, amwereka ubwami bwose bwo mw'isi n'ubwiza bwabwo
40004009	ati: "Ivyo vyose ndabiguha, ni wampfukamira, ukansenga."
40004010	Buno Yesu aramubwira ati: "Mvako, Satani, kuko vyanditswe, ngo Uhoraho, Imana yawe, ube ari yo usenga, kandi ube ari yo usaba yonyene." "
40004011	Maze Umwansi Satani aramureka, kandi abamarayika baraza, baramukorera.
40004012	Yumvise ko Yohana yashizwe mw'ibohero, aja i Galilaya.
40004013	Yimuka i Nazareti, aja kuba i Kaperinawumu hafi y'ikiyaga mu rubibe rwa Zebuloni na Nafutali,
40004014	ngo ivyanditswe na Yesaya yavugishwa n'Imana bishike,
40004015	ngo igihugu ca Zebuloni n'igihugu ca Nafutali, Aherekeye ku kiyaga, hakurya ya Yorodani, I Galilaya mu gihugu c'abanyamahanga,
40004016	Abantu bari bicaye mu mwiza, Babonye umuco mwinshi, Kandi abari bicaye mu gihugu c'urupfu no mu gitutu carwo, Umuco urasiye kuri bo.
40004017	Guhera ubwo, Yesu atangura kwigisha ati:" "Mwihane, kuko ubwami bwo mw'ijuru buri hafi."
40004018	Aciye i ruhande y'ikiyaga c'i Galilaya, abona abavukana babiri b'abarovyi, Simoni yitwa Petero na Andereya mwene nyina, bariko baraterera urusenga mu kiyaga.
40004019	Arababwira ati: "Ni munkurikire, nzobagira abaroba abantu." "
40004020	Baca bareka insenga, baramukurikira.
40004021	Yigiye imbere yaho, abona abandi bavukana babiri, Yakobo umwana wa Zebedayo na mwene nyina Yohana, bari kumwe na se Zebedayo mu bwato, bariko barasanura insenga zabo, arabahamagara.
40004022	Baca bareka ubwato na se, baramukurikira.
40004023	Yesu agendagenda i Galilaya hose, yigisha mu nsengero z'Abayuda, ababwira ubutumwa bwiza bw'ubwami, akiza abantu indwara n'ubumuga vy'uburyo bwose.
40004024	Inkuru yiwe ikwira i Siriya hose, bamuzanira abarwaye bose bafashwe n'indwara zitandukanye n'ibibasesereje, n'abinjiwemwo n'abadayimoni, n'abarwaye intandara, n'ibimuga; arabakiza.
40004025	Kandi ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira bavuye i Galilaya, i Dekapoli, i Yerusalemu n'i Yudaya no hakurya ya Yorodani."
40005001	Abonye iryo shengero, aduga umusozi. Amaze kwicara, abigishwa biwe baramwegera.
40005002	Aherako aravuga, arabigisha
40005003	ati: "Harahiriwe aboro mu mitima yabo, kuko ubwami bwo mw'ijuru ari ubwabo."
40005004	Harahiriwe abatuntuye, kuko ari bo bazokwirurwa.
40005005	Harahiriwe abatekereza, kuko ari bo bazoragwa isi.
40005006	Harahiriwe abafise inzara n'inyota vyo kugororoka, kuko ari bo bazohazwa.
40005007	Harahiriwe abagira imbabazi, kuko ari bo bazozigirirwa.
40005008	Harahiriwe abafise imitima itanduye, kuko ari bo bazobona Imana.
40005009	Harahiriwe ababanguranya, kuko ari bo bazokwitwa abana b'Imana.
40005010	Harahiriwe abahamwa bahorwa ukugororoka, kuko ubwami bwo mw'ijuru ari bwabo.
40005011	Namwe muzoba muhiriwe aho bazobatuka bakabahama bakabarementaniriza ibibi vyose babampoye.
40005012	Munezerwe, muhimbarwe, kuko impera zanyu ari nyinshi mw'ijuru; kuko ari ko bahama abavugishwa n'Imana ba mbere.
40005013	Muri umunyu w'isi. Ariko umunyu, iyo ushize uburyohe, uba ukiryoshwa ni igiki? Nta co uba ukimaze atari ugutabwa hanze ugahonyangwa n'abantu.
40005014	Muri umuco w'isi. Igisagara cubatswe mw'itaba ry'umusozi ntigishobora guhishwa.
40005015	Nta bodomeka itara ngo baryubikeko igiseke, ariko barishira ku gitereko caryo, ngo riboneshereze abari mu nzu bose.
40005016	Abe ari ko umuco wanyu ubonesha imbere y'abantu, ngo babone ibikorwa vyanyu vyiza, bashemagize So wo mw'ijuru.
40005017	Ntimugire ngo naje gusenyura ivyagezwe canke amajambo y' abavugishwa n'Imana. Sinaje kubisenyura, naje kubishitsa.
40005018	Ndababwire ukuri, ijuru n'isi bikiriho nta n'akadome na kamwe canke n'akazatsa bizova ku vyagezwe, gushitsa aho vyose bizoheraherezwa.
40005019	Nuko uwuzorenga ibwirizwa na rimwe ryo mu yoroshe hanyuma y'ayandi, akigisha abantu ngo bagire batyo, mu bwami bwo mw'ijuru azokwitwa muto hanyuma y'abandi. Ariko uwuyitondera, akayigisha, uwo we azokwitwa mukuru mu bwami bwo mw'ijuru.
40005020	Ariko ndababwira yuko ukugororoka kwanyu ni kutaruta uko abahinga b'ivyanditswe n'uko Abafarisayo, mutazoruha mwinjira mu bwami bwo mw'ijuru. "
40005021	Mwarumvise ko aba kera babwiwe, ngo Ntukice; uwica aba ashikiwe no gutsindwa n'urubanza.
40005022	Ariko jeho ndababwira yuko umuntu wese azoshavurira umuvukanyi wiwe azoba ashikiwe no gushirwa imbere y'intahe; uwuzotuka umuvukanyi wiwe, ngo wa kijuju we! azoba ashikiwe no gutsindwa n'urubanza; uwuzomutuka ati: "Wa gipfu we !" azoba ashikiwe no gutabwa mu muriro wa Gehinomu.
40005023	Ni wajana ishikanwa ryawe ku gicaniro, ukahibukira ko hari ico upfa na mugenzawe,
40005024	usige ishikanwa ryawe imbere y'igicaniro, ubanze ugende utunganye na mugenzawe, uce ugaruka, ushikane ishikanwa ryawe.
40005025	Wuzure vuba n'uwukurega mukiri mu nzira; uwukurega ntagushikirize umucamanza, umucamanza akaguha umusoda, ugashirwa mw'ibohero.
40005026	Ndakubwira ukuri yuko utazohava na gatoya utishuye n'imeya ry'imperera." "
40005027	Mwarumvise ko vyavuzwe, ngo Ntugasambane.
40005028	Ariko jeho ndababwira yuko umuntu wese araba umugore w'uwundi akamwifuza, aba amaze gusambana na we mu mutima wiwe.
40005029	Ijisho ryawe ry'i buryo ni ryagutsitaza, urinogore, urite kure; vyokubera vyiza gupfa ijisho ryawe rimwe, hako umubiri wawe wose wotabwa muri Gehinomu.
40005030	N'ukuboko kwawe kw'i buryo ni kwagutsitaza, uguce igikonjo, ugite kure; vyokubera vyiza gupfa urugingo rwawe rumwe, hako umubiri wawe wose woja muri Gehinomu.
40005031	Kandi vyaravuzwe, ngo umuntu wese yirukana umugore wiwe ni amuhe ikete ryo kuvavanura.
40005032	Ariko jeho ndababwira yuko umuntu wese yirukana umugore wiwe atamuhoye ubusambanyi, aba amusambanishije, kandi uwuzorongora uwahukanye azoba asambanye."
40005033	Mwarumvise kandi ko aba kera babwiwe, ngo Ntukarahire ngo wirahuruze, ariko uzokorere Uhoraho ivyo wamusezeraniye;
40005034	ariko jeho ndababwire; Ntukarahire na mba; nturahire ijuru, kuko ari intebe y'Imana;
40005035	canke isi, kuko ari yo ndava y'ibirenge vyayo; canke i Yerusalemu, kuko ari umurwa w'Umwami ahambaye.
40005036	Nturahire umutwe wawe, kuko udashobora guhindura agashatsi na kamwe ngo kere canke ngo kirabure.
40005037	Ariko ijambo ryanyu ribe Ego, ego; Oya, oya; ikirenze ivyo kiva kuri wa Mubi.
40005038	Mwarumvise ko vyavuzwe, ngo ijisho rihorwe irindi, n'iryinyo rihorwe irindi;
40005039	ariko jeho ndababwire: Ntimurwanye umunyakibi. Uwugukubise urushi mu musaya w'i buryo umuhindukirize n'uwundi;
40005040	umuntu ni yagomba kukuburanya ngo akunyage ikanzu, umuhebere n'umutamana;
40005041	uwugufata ngo umurenze umusozi umwe, umurenze n'uwa kabiri.
40005042	Uwugusaba, umuhe, uwugomba ko umugurana, ntumutere ibitugu.
40005043	Mwarumvise ko vyavuzwe, ngo mukunde umubanyi wanyu, mwanke umwansi wanyu.
40005044	Ariko jeho ndababwire; Mukunde abansi banyu, musabire ababahama,
40005045	kugira ngo mube abana ba So wo mw'ijuru, kuko atuma izuba ryiwe rirasira ababi n'abeza, kandi aha imvura abagororotsi n'abagabitanya.
40005046	Ni mwakunda ababakunda, muri n'impera ki? Mbega abatozakori bo si ko bagira?
40005047	Ni mwaramukanya n'incuti zanyu gusa, abandi muzoba mubarusha iki? Abanyamahanga bo si ko bagira?
40005048	Mwebwe ni mube intungane, nk'uko So wo mw'ijuru ari intungane.
40006001	Mwirinde ntimugakorere ivyiza vyanyu mu maso y'abantu kugira ngo babarabe. Ni mwagira mutyo, ntimuzogira impera kuri So wo mw'ijuru.
40006002	Ni wagira ubuntu, ntuzovugishe inzumbeti imbere yawe, nk'uko indyarya zikora mu nsengero z'Abayuda no mu nzira, ngo bashimwe n'abantu; ndababwire ukuri. Baramaze guhabwa impera zabo.
40006003	Ariko weho ni wagira ubuntu, ntumenyeshe ukubamfu kwawe ico ukuryo kwawe gukora,
40006004	kugira ngo ubuntu bwawe bugirirwe mu mpisho; kandi So, abona ibihishijwe, azoguhera.
40006005	Iyo musenga ntimukabe nka za ndyarya, kuko bakunda gusenga bahagaze mu nsengero z'Abayuda no mu mayirabiri, ngo biyerekane imbere y'abantu; ndababwire ukuri, baramaze guhabwa impera zabo.
40006006	Ariko weho, iyo usenga, uje haruguru mu nzu yawe, wugare umwango, usenge So aba mu mpisho, kandi So, akuboneye mu mpisho azoguhera.
40006007	Kandi ni mwasenga, ntimukabomboranye amanwa nk'uko abanyamahanga bagira; biyumvira yuko bazokwumvirwa kubwo amajambo yabo menshi.
40006008	Ntimuzose na bo, kuko So azi ivyo mukenye mutaramusaba.
40006009	Nuko musenge mutya muti: ""Data wa twese wo mw'ijuru, izina ryawe ni ryubahwe,
40006010	ubwami bwawe ni buze, ivyo ugomba ni bibe mw'isi nk'uko biba mw'ijuru.
40006011	Uduhe ivyo kurya dukwiranye uyu musi;
40006012	utubabarire ibicumuro vyacu, nk'uko natwe tubibabarira abaducumuyeko;
40006013	kandi ntutujane mu bitwosha nabi, ariko udukize wa Mubi. [Kuko ubwami, ubushobozi n'icubahiro ari ivyawe ibihe bidashira. Amina. ]"
40006014	Kuko ni mwaharira abantu ivyaha vyabo, na So wo mw'ijuru azobaharira namwe.
40006015	Ariko ni mutaharira abantu ivyaha vyabo, na So na we ntazobaharira ivyaha vyanyu.
40006016	Kandi iyo mwisonzesha, ntimwijirwe nk'uko za ndyarya zigira. Kuko biyoberanya mu maso ngo babonwe n'abantu ko bisonzesheje. Ndababwire ukuri, baramaze guhabwa impera zabo.
40006017	Ariko weho, ni wisonzesha, wisige amavuta mu mutwe, wiyuhagire mu maso,
40006018	ngo ntubonwe n'abantu ko wisonzesheje, ariko ubonwe na So aba mu mpisho, kandi So, abona ivyo mu mpisho, azoguhera."
40006019	Ntimukirundanirize ubutunzi mw'isi, aho inyenzi n'ingese bibumara, n'ibisuma bikimba bikabwiba.
40006020	Ariko mwirundanirize ubutunzi mw'ijuru, aho inyenzi n'ingese bitabumara, hatariyo n'ibisuma vyimba ngo vyibe.
40006021	Kuko aho ubutunzi bwawe buri, ari ho umutima wawe uzoba.
40006022	Itara ry'umubiri ni ijisho. Ijisho ryawe iyo ari ryiza, umubiri wawe wose uba uri n'umuco.
40006023	Ariko ijisho ryawe iyo ari ribi, umubiri wawe wose uba uri n'umwiza. Nuko wa muco uba muri wewe, woramuka ubaye umwiza, uwo mwiza wongana ute!
40006024	Nta wusaba abami babiri, kuko yokwanka umwe, agakunda uwundi, canke yoguma kuri umwe, akagaya wa wundi. Ntimushobora gusaba Imana n'Itunga.
40006025	Ni co gitumye ndababarira nti: "Ntimukaganyire amagara yanyu ku vyo muzorya canke ku vyo muzonywa, canke umubiri wanyu ku vyo muzokwambara. Mbega amagara ntaruta ivyo kurya, canke umubiri nturuta imyambaro?"
40006026	Ni murabe ibiguruka vyo mu kirere, ntibibiba, ntibishwabura, kandi ntivyimburira mu bigega, ariko So wo mw'ijuru arabitunga; mbega mwebwe ntimubiruta cane?
40006027	Ni nde muri mwebwe yoshobozwa n'amaganya kwisumvya uko yareha nk'ukuboko kumwe?
40006028	Ni kuki mwiganyira kuvyerekeye impuzu? Ni murabe amashurwe yo ku misozi ingene akura, ntiyirirwa aratama, ntajisha impuzu;
40006029	ariko ndababwira yuko na Salomo mu bwiza bwiwe bwose atari ashajije nka rimwe muri ayo.
40006030	None Imana ko yambika ivyatsi vyo ku misozi ityo, biriho uyu musi, ariko nk' ejo bigatererwa mu ziko, mbega ntizorushiriza kubambika, mwebwe abo ukwizera guke mwe?
40006031	Nuko ntimukiganyire, ngo tuzorya iki? canke tuzonywa iki? canke tuzokwambara iki?
40006032	Kuko ivyo vyose abanyamahanga ari vyo bitwaririka; ariko So wo mw'ijuru arazi ko ivyo vyose mubikena.
40006033	Ariko mubanze mwitwaririke ubwami bw'Imana n'ukugororoka kwayo, ni ho ivyo vyose muzovyongerwa.
40006034	Ntimukiganyire ivyo ejo, kuko umusi w'ejo uzoba wiganyira ku vyawo; umusi ukwiranye n'amagorwa yawo.
40007001	Ntimugahinyurire mu mitima yanyu, namwe mukazohinyurwa.

40007010	Canke yomusaba ifi, akamuha inzoka?

40007013	Muce mw'irembo ripfunganye; kuko irembo ryagutse, n'inzira yagutse, ari vyo bijana abantu mu mahonero, kandi abahaca ni benshi.
40007014	Ariko irembo ripfunganye, n'inzira ntoya, ni vyo bija mu bugingo, kandi abahabona ni bake.
40007015	Mwirinde abigira abavugishwa n'Imana; baza kuri mwebwe bambaye nk'intama; ariko imbere ari amabingira y'inkazi.
40007016	Muzobamenyera ku vyo bama. Mbega hari uwokwamura inzabibu ku munyinya, canke insukoni ku bitovu?
40007017	Nuko igiti ciza cose cama ivyiza, ariko igiti kibi cama ibibi.
40007018	Igiti ciza ntigishobora kwama ibibi, kandi igiti kibi ntigishobora kwama ivyiza.
40007019	Igiti cose kitama ivyiza kiracibwa, kigatererwa mu muriro.

40008001	Amanutse uwo musozi, ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira.

40010001	Ahamagara abigishwa biwe icumi na babiri, abaha ububasha ku mpwemu zihumanye n'ubwo kuzisenda, no gukiza indwara zose n'ubumuga bwose.

40010026	Nuko ntimuzobatinye, kuko ata catwikiriwe kitazotwikururwa, canke kinyegejwe kitazomenyekana.

40011005	Impumyi zirahumuka, abacumbagira bagenda neza, abanyamibembe barakizwa, ibipfamatwi birumva, abapfuye barazurwa, aboro barabwirwa ubutumwa bwiza.
40011006	Kandi Harahiriwe uwo ivyanje bitazotsitaza.
40011007	Abo bagiye, Yesu atangura kubwira ishengero ivya Yohana ati: "Mwagiye mu bugaragwa kuraba iki?"Mbega ni irenga rihungabanywa n'umuyaga?

40011009	Ariko mwajanywe ni igiki? Mbega kwari ukuraba umuntu avugishwa n'Imana? Ego me ni co; kandi ndababwire, aruta uwuvugishwa n' Imana cane.

40011017	bati: "Twavugije imyironge ntimwatamba; twakomye induru, ntimwaboroga."

40011020	Buno atangura guhambarira ibisagara yakoreyemwo ibikomeye vyinshi, kuko batihanye.
40011021	Ati: "Uzobona ibara Korazini; uzobona ibara Betsayida; kuko ibikomeye vyakorewe muri mwebwe iyo biba vyarakorewe muri Tiro n'i Sidoni, baba barihanye kera, bakambara amagunira, bakisiga iminyota."
40011022	Ariko ndababwire; muri Tiro n'i Sidoni hazogira agahengekezo ku musi w'imanza kurusha mwebwe.
40011023	Nawe, Kaperinawumu, mbega uzoshirwa hejuru ushike kw'ijuru? Oya, uzocokezwa i kuzimu; kuko ibikomeye vyakorewe muri wewe, iyo biba vyarakorewe i Sodomu, haba hakiriho gushika n'ubu.
40011024	Ariko ndababwira yuko igihugu c'i Sodomu kizogira agahengekezo ku musi w'imanza kurusha wewe.
40011025	Muri ico gihe Yesu aravuga ati: "Ndaguhimbaza, Data, Mwami w'ijuru n'isi, kuko ivyo wabihishije abanyabwenge n'abahanga, ukabihishurira inzoya."
40011026	Ego me, Data, kuko washimye ko biba bityo imbere yawe.

40012001	Muri ico gihe Yesu aca mu mirima y'ingano kw'isabato. Abigishwa biwe bashonje, batangura kumyoza ingano, barazihekenya.
40012002	Abafarisayo babibonye, baramubwira bati: "Mbega abigishwa bawe ko bakora ikizira gukorwa kw'isabato!"
40012003	Na we arababaza ati: "Nta ho murasoma ico Dawidi yakoze, aho yari asonzanye n'abari kumwe na we;
40012004	ingene yinjiye mu nzu y'Imana, akarya imitsima yagenewe gushikanirwa Imana, yari umuziro kuri we no ku bari kumwe na we, uretse abaherezi bonyene?
40012005	Canke nta ho murasoma mu vyagezwe ingene kw'isabato abaherezi, iyo bari mu rusengero, bazirura isabato, ntibabeko igicumuro?"
40012006	Ariko ndababwira yuko hano hari uwuruta urusengero.
40012007	Iyo muba mwari muzi iri jambo ico rivuga, ngo imbabazi ni zo ngomba, si ibimazi; ntimuba mutsindishije abatariko igicumuro.
40012008	Kuko Umwana w'umuntu ari Umwami w'isabato.
40012009	Avayo, yinjira mu rusengero rw'Abayuda.
40012010	Kandi harimwo umuntu anyunyutse ukuboko. Baramubaza bati: "Mbega biremerwa gukiza kw'isabato? Ngo baronke uko bomurega."

40012012	Mbega none umuntu ntaruta intama cane? None rero biremerwa gukora ivyiza kw'isabato.
40012013	Maze abwira uwo muntu ati: "Gorora ukuboko kwawe." Arakugorora, kurakira, gukomera nk'ukundi.

40012024	Ariko Abafarisayo bavyumvise baravuga bati: "Uwu nta kindi kimushoboza kwirukana abadayimoni, atari Beyezebuli, umukuru w'abadayimoni."

40012026	Na Satani, yosenda Satani, yoba yitandukanije ubwiwe; none ubwami bwiwe bworama bute?
40012027	Ariko jewe namba Beyezebuli ari we anshoboza kwirukana abadayimoni, abana banyu bashobozwa na nde kubasenda? Ni co gituma ari bo bazobatsindisha.
40012028	Ariko Mpwemu w'Imana ni yaba ari we anshoboza kwirukana abadayimoni, noneho ubwami bw' Imana burabashikiriye.
40012029	None umuntu yoshobora ate kwinjira mu nzu y'umuntu w'inkomezi kumusahura ibintu atabanje kuboha wa munyenkomezi? Maze akabona kumusahura ivyo mu nzu yiwe.
40012030	Uwutamperereyeko ni umwansi wanje, kandi uwudasukiranya nanje arasanzaza.
40012031	Kubwo ivyo ndababwira yuko icaha cose n'ugutyoza, abantu bazobiharirwa; ariko ugutyoza kuri Mpwemu ni icaha kitazoharirwa.
40012032	Umuntu wese azotyoza umwana w'umuntu azobiharirwa, ariko uwutyoza Mpwemu Yera ntazobiharirwa, naho hoba muri iki gihe canke mu gihe kizoza.
40012033	Ni mube muvuga igiti ko ari ciza n'ivyo camye ko ari vyiza, canke mube muvuga igiti ko ari kibi n'ivyo camye ko ari bibi; kuko igiti kimenyekanira ku vyo camye.
40012034	Mwa bana b'inzoka mwe, mwoshobora mute kuvuga ivyiza muri babi? Ibibogaboga mu mutima ni vyo akanwa kavuga.
40012035	Umunyangeso nziza akura ivyiza mw'itunga ryiwe ryiza; umunyangeso mbi akura ibibi mw'itunga ryiwe ribi.

40012040	Nk'uko Yona yamaze imisi itatu n'amajoro atatu mu nda y'urufi, ni ko n'Umwana w'umuntu azomara imisi itatu n'amajoro atatu i kuzimu.

40012046	Akivugana n'ishengero, nyina n'abavukanyi biwe bari bahagaze hanze, bagomba kubonana na we.

40013001	Kuri uwo musi Yesu asohoka ava mu nzu, yicara ku nkombe y'ikiyaga.

41006026	Umwami arababara cane, ariko kubwa za ndahiro ziwe, no ku bwo abasangira na we, bimunanira kuwumwima.

41006029	Abigishwa biwe bavyumvise baraza, bajana ikiziga ciwe, bagihamba mu cobo.
41006030	Nuko za ntumwa zikoranira aho Yesu ari, zimudondera ivyo zakoze vyose n'ivyo zigishije.
41006031	Arababwira ati:" "Ni muze mwebwe mwenyene ahiherereye mu gahinga, muruhuke gatoya." Kuko hari uruja n'uruza, babura n'ingene botamira utwo kurya.
41006032	Bagenda mu bwato, baja ahantu h'agahinga kwihererayo.
41006033	Bababona bagenda, benshi barabamenya, bava mu bisagara vyose, barirukanga, bajana inkokoro y'ikiyaga, babatangayo.
41006034	Yesu avuye mu bwato, abona ishengero ryinshi, rimutera akagongwe kuko bameze nk'intama zitagira umwungere; atangura kubigisha vyinshi.
41006035	Buriko burira, abigishwa biwe baramwegera bati: "Mbega hano hantu ko ari mu gahinga, bukaba buhaye burira;
41006036	basezere, baje mu misozi no mu mihana impande zose, kwirondererayo ivyo kurya."
41006037	Arabishura ati: "Mube ari mwebwe mubagaburira." Baramubaza bati: "Tugende tugure imitsima y'idenariyo amajana abiri, tuyibahe ga barye?"
41006038	Na we arababaza ati: "Mufise imitsima ingahe?" Ni mugende muyirabe. Babimenye baramwishura bati: "Ni dutanu, n'udufi tubiri."
41006039	Ababarira ko bose bicara ku vyatsi bibisi bari mu mirwi.
41006040	Bicara imirongo imirongo, hamwe ijanijana ahandi mirongo itanitanu, batyo batyo.
41006041	Yakira ya mitsima itanu na za fi zibiri, ararangamiza, araba mw'ijuru, arabihezagira, amanyagura iyo mitsima, ayiha abigishwa ngo bayishire imbere y'abantu, n'ifi zompi na zo arazibagaburira bose.
41006042	Bararya bose barahaga.
41006043	Begeranya utumanyagu tw'imitsima n'utw'ifi, twuzura ibiseke icumi na bibiri.
41006044	Abariye iyo mitsima bari abagabo ibihumbi bitanu.
41006045	Uwo mwanya Yesu agobera abigishwa biwe ngo batambukire mu bwato, batangure kujabuka hakurya i Betsayida, aheze gusezera rya shengero.
41006046	Ahejeje gusezerana na bo avayo, aduga umusozi gusenga.
41006047	Bwagorovye, bwa bwato bushitse mw'ibenga, ariko we yari i musozi wenyene.
41006048	Abonye ko batamijwe no gusoza, kuko umuyaga wari ubaturutse imbere, ku muteramyi agira kane aza aho bari, agendesha amaguru hejuru ku kiyaga, yagira abarengane.
41006049	Ariko babonye agendesha amaguru hejuru ku kiyaga, bagira ngo ni igihume, bakoma induru y'ubwoba.
41006050	Bose baramubona, basimbwa n'umutima. Ariko uwo mwanya arabavugisha ati: "Humura ni jewe, ni mureke gutinya."
41006051	Aratambuka, aja mu bwato barimwo; umuyaga uraca. Barumirwa cane mu mitima yabo;
41006052	kuko batatahuye ivya ya mitsima, ariko imitima yabo yari ikomantaye.
41006053	Bamaze kujabuka hakurya, bagenda mu misozi mu ntara y'i Genesareti, bazirika ubwato ku nkombe.
41006054	Bavuye mu bwato, abaho baca baramumenya.
41006055	Birukanga impande zose muri ico gihugu cose, batangura guterura abarwaye mu nderuzo, babakwiragirana aho bamwumvise hose.
41006056	Kandi aho yaja, mu mihana, mu bisagara canke mu misozi, bashira abarwaye mu tuguriro, bakamwinginga ngo bamukore naho hoba ku buyonga bw'impuzu yiwe gusa; abamukozeko bose bagakira.
41007001	Abafarisayo bakoranira kuri we n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe bamwe bavuye i Yerusalemu.
41007002	Babona abigishwa biwe bamwe barisha ivyo kurya intoke zihumanye, bisobanurwa ngo zidakaravye.
41007003	Ariko Abafarisayo n'Abayuda bose, iyo batifyikinyuye mu gukaraba ntibarya, kuko bakurikiye imigenzo babwirijwe n'aba kera.
41007004	Kandi bavuye mu kaguriro, iyo batimijagiye amazi ntibarya, kandi hariho ibindi vyinshi babwirijwe n'aba kera ngo bavyumireko, nko kwoza mu buryo bwinshi ibikombe, inzavya n'inkono zikozwe mu miringa.
41007005	Abafarisayo n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe baramubaza bati: "Ni igiki gitumye abigishwa bawe badakurikira ingeso twabwirijwe n'aba kera, bagapfa kurisha ivyo kurya intoke zihumanye?"
41007006	Arabishura ati: "Yesaya yavuze neza ivyo yavugishijwe n'Imana kuri mwebwe indyarya, nk'uko handitswe, ngo aba bantu banyubahisha iminwa yabo, Ariko imitima yabo iri kure yanje."
41007007	Bansengera ubusa, Kuko inyigisho bigisha ari ivyagezwe n'abantu.

41007013	ijambo ry'Imana mukaritituza imigenzo yanyu mwigishije: kandi mukora n'ibindi vyinshi bene ivyo."
41007014	Kandi yongera guhamagara ishengero, araribarira ati: "Munyumve mwese, mubitahure:
41007015	nta kintu kiri inyuma, iyo kigiye imbere mu muntu gishobora kumuhumanya, ariko ibivuye mu muntu ni vyo bimuhumanya." [
41007016	Namba hari uwufise amatwi yumva, ni yumve. ]
41007017	Yinjiye mu nzu asize ishengero hanze, abigishwa biwe bamusiguza uwo mugani.
41007018	Na we arababaza ati: "Mbega namwe muri imburabwenge mutyo? Ntimutahura yuko ata kintu kiri inyuma iyo kigiye imbere mu muntu gishobora kumuhumanya,
41007019	kuko kitagiye mu mutima wiwe, ariko kija mu nda, kigaca mu nzira yaco?" Ivyo yabivugiye guhumanura ivyo kurya vyose.
41007020	Kandi aravuga ati: "Ibiva imbere mu muntu, ni vyo bimuhumanya,
41007021	kuko imbere mu mitima y'abantu havamwo ivyiyumviro bibi, ubushakanyi,
41007022	ubwivyi, ubwicanyi, ubusambanyi, ukwifuza, kugira nabi, ubugunge, ivyo isoni nke, ijisho ribi, ibitutsi, ubwibone, ubupfu.
41007023	Ivyo bibi vyose biva imbere ni vyo bihumanya umuntu."
41007024	Ava aho hantu, aja mu ntara yo muri Tiro n'i Sidoni. Yinjira mu nzu atagomba ko hogira umuntu abimenya, ariko ntiyashobora kuyoberana.
41007025	Ariko uwo mwanya, umugore afise akigeme kinjiwemwo n'impwemu ihumanye, amwumvise, araza, yikubita imbere y'ibirenge vyiwe.
41007026	Uwo mugore yari Umugirikikazi, amamo yiwe n'i Sirofoyinike, aramwinginga ngo yirukane dayimoni mu mukobwa wiwe.

41009001	Arababwira ati: "Ndababwira ukuri; muri aba bahagaze hano harimwo bamwe batazobona urupfu gushitsa aho bazobonera ubwami bw'Imana buzananye n'ubushobozi."

41010001	Arikora avayo, aja mu gihugu c'i Yudaya no hakurya ya Yorodani, ishengero ryongera gukoranira kuri we, yongera kubigisha nk'uko yamenyereye.
41010002	Abafarisayo baza kuri we, baramugeza bati: "Mbega biremerwa ko umuntu yirukana umugore wiwe?"
41010003	Na we arababaza ati: "Mose yabagereye iki ?"
41010004	Baramwishura bati: "Mose yemeye ko handikwa ikete ryo kuvavanura, akamwirukana."
41010005	Yesu arababwira ati: "Gukomantara kw'imitima yanyu ni kwo kwamwandikishije ico cagezwe."
41010006	Ariko uhereye kw'itanguriro ry'ukuremwa, Imana yabaremye bari uburyo bubiri.
41010007	Ni co gituma umuntu azosiga se na nyina, akabana n'umugore wiwe ubutakivana,
41010008	bompi bakaba umubiri umwe. Bituma batakiri babiri, ariko baba babaye umubiri umwe.
41010009	Nuko ico Imana yamatanije umuntu ntazokimature.
41010010	Yinjiye mu nzu abigishwa bongera kumubaza iryo jambo.
41010011	Arababwira ati: "Umuntu wese yirukana umugore wiwe, akarongora uwundi, aba asambanye kandi amuhemukiye."
41010012	Kandi na we ubwiwe, ni yahukana n'umugabo wiwe, akarongorwa n'uwundi, azoba asambanye."
41010013	Maze bamuzanira abana bato, ngo abakoreko; abigishwa barabakankamira.
41010014	Maze Yesu abibonye, araraka, arababarira ati: "Ni mureke abana bato baze aho ndi, ntimubabuze, kuko ubwami bw'Imana ari ubwo abameze batyo."
41010015	Ndababwire ukuri, uwutazokwakira ubwami bw'Imana nk'umwana muto, ntazobwinjiramwo na gatoya. "
41010016	Arabarera, arabahezagira, abarambitseko ibiganza.
41010017	Agisohoka ngo akomeze urugendo, haza umuntu kuri we yirukanga, aramupfukamira, aramubaza ati:" "Mwigisha mwiza, nkore iki, ngo nze ndagwe ubugingo budashira?"
41010018	Yesu aramubaza ati: "Unyitira iki mwiza? Nta mwiza, atari umwe, ni we Mana."
41010019	Ko uzi ivyagezwe, ngo Ntukice, ntugasambane, ntukibe, ntukagirize abandi ibinyoma, ntukagunge, wubahe so na nyoko.
41010020	Aramubwira ati: "Mwigisha, ivyo vyose naravyitondeye, mpereye mu buto bwanje."
41010021	Yesu amwitegereje aramukunda, aramubwira ati: "Uhajije kimwe: genda, ushore ivyo utunze vyose, ugabire aboro, ni ho uzogira itunga mw'ijuru, uteko uze, unkurikire."
41010022	Yumvise iryo jambo arijirwa, agenda ababaye, kuko yarafise itunga ryinshi.
41010023	Yesu yeraguza amaso, abwira abigishwa biwe ati: "Erega biragoye ko aba vyinshi binjira mu bwami bw'Imana !"
41010024	Abigishwa batangazwa n'amajambo yiwe. Yesu yongera kubabwira ati: "Bana banje, erega biragoye ko abizigiye ubutunzi binjira mu bwami bw' Imana!
41010025	Icoroshe ni uko ingamiya yoca mu zuru ry'urushinge biruta umutunzi ko yinjira mu bwami bw' Imana."
41010026	Baratangara rwose bati: "None rero, ni nde ashobora gukizwa?"

41010028	Maze Petero atangura kumubwira ati: "Raba, twebwe twaretse vyose turagukurikira."
41010029	Yesu arababwira ati: "Ndababwire ukuri, Nta waretse inzu, canke abavukanyi biwe, canke bashiki biwe, canke nyina, canke se, canke abana, canke itongo, kubwanje no ku bwo ubutumwa bwiza,
41010030	atazobishumbushwa ijana muri iki gihe ca none, inzu, n'abavukanyi biwe, na bashiki biwe, na ba nyina, n'abana, n'itongo, bisukiranijwe no guhamwa, kandi mu gihe kizoza azohabwa ubugingo budashira."
41010031	Ariko benshi b'imbere bazoba abo inyuma, kandi abo inyuma bazoba abo imbere.
41010032	Bari mu nzira baduga i Yerusalemu. Yesu yari abagiye imbere, baratangara, abamukurikira baratinya. Yongera kujana bamwe icumi na babiri bari ukwabo, atangura kubabarira ibigira bimubeko
41010033	ati: "Ehe, turaduze i Yerusalemu, kandi Umwana w'umuntu azoshirwa mu maboko y'abaherezi bakuru n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe, bazomucira urubanza rwo gupfa, bamuhe abanyamahanga,
41010034	bamushinyagurire, bamuvume amate, bamukubite cane, bamwice, maze imisi itatu ishize azozuka."
41010035	Yakobo na Yohana abana ba Zebedayo baramwegera baramubwira bati: "Mwigisha, turagomba ko uduha ico tugusaba cose."
41010036	Arababaza ati: "Mugomba ko ndabaha iki?"

41010038	Maze Yesu arabishura ati: "Ntimuzi ico musaba. Mwoshobora kunywera ku gikombe nywerako, canke kubatizwa umubatizo mbatizwa jewe?"
41010039	Baramwishura bati: "Turashobora." Yesu arababwira ati: "Igikombe nywerako, muzokinywerako, kandi muzobatizwa umubatizo mbatizwa jewe."
41010040	Ariko gutanga ivyicaro i buryo bwanje canke mu bubamfu, si ivyanje, kiretse abo vyateguriwe.
41010041	Bamwe icumi bavyumvise batangura kwitonganiriza ivya Yakobo na Yohana.
41010042	Yesu arabahamagara, arababwira ati: "Murazi yuko abavugwa ko baganza amahanga bayatwaza amanyama, kandi n'abakuru bayo bayagirako ububasha.
41010043	Ariko muri mwebwe si ko biri. Yamara uwugomba kuba mukuru muri mwebwe, azobe umukozi wanyu.
41010044	Kandi uwugomba kuba uwo imbere, azobe umushumba wa mwese.
41010045	Kuko na none Umwana w'umuntu atazanywe no gukorerwa, atari ugukorera abandi, no gutanga ubugingo bwiwe ko incungu ya benshi."
41010046	Nuko bashika i Yeriko. Akivana i Yeriko n'abigishwa biwe n'ishengero ryinshi, umwana wa Timayo yitwa Barutimayo, impumyi yasegerereza, yari yicaye i ruhande y'inzira.

41011003	Kandi ni hagira uwubabaza ati: "Ivyo mubikoreye iki?" Mumwishure muti: "Databuja ni we ayigomba." Uwo mwanya arayirungika ino.

41011009	Abari imbere yiwe n'abamukurikiye barasemerera bati: "Hoziyana, hashemezwe uwuje mw'izina ry' Uhoraho,

41011011	Ashika i Yerusalemu, yinjira mu rusengero, maze ahejeje kweraguza vyose, kuko bwari bugorovye, arasohoka, aja i Betaniya, ajanye na bamwe icumi na babiri.
41011012	Bukeye bamaze kuva i Betaniya, yumva arashonje.
41011013	Akiri kure, abona umusukoni uriko amababi, arawegera ngo kumbure yogira ico awusangako; awushitseko ntiyagira ico awubonako, atari amababi; kuko kitari igihe co kwama c'umusukoni.

41011015	Bashika i Yerusalemu. Yinjira mu rusengero, atangura guhindira hanze abarudandarizamwo n'abaruguriramwo, ahenura imeza y'abavunja amahera n'intebe z'abariko baragurwako inuma,
41011016	ntiyakundira umuntu n'umwe guhita mu rusengero atwaye ikintu co mu bikoresho.
41011017	Arigisha arababwira ati:" "Mbega ntivyanditswe, ngo ingoro yanje izokwitwa inzu yo gusengerwamwo n'amahanga yose ?" Ariko mwebwe mwayihinduye nk'isenga ry'abambuzi. "
41011018	Abaherezi bakuru n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe bavyumvise barondera ingene bomwica, kuko bamutinya, kuko abantu bose batangazwa n'inyigisho ziwe.
41011019	Iyo bugorovye, yama ava mu gisagara.
41011020	Bukeye mu gitondo ca kare bariko barahita babona wa musukoni, wahereye ku mizi wakabiranye.

41011023	Ndababwira ukuri yuko umuntu wese yobwira uwu musozi ati: "Shinguka utabwe mu kiyaga, ntabikekeranye mu mutima, ariko akizera yuko ico avuze gikorwa, azokibona.

41011025	Kandi ni mwahagarara musenga, ni haba hari ico mupfa n'uwundi, mukimuharire, ngo So wo mw'ijuru na we abaharire ivyaha vyanyu, [

41011027	Bongera kuja i Yerusalemu. Akigendagenda mu rusengero, abaherezi bakuru, abahinga b'ivyanditswe n'abashingantahe baza kuri we,

41011029	Yesu arabishura ati: "Nanje hinge ndababaze ijambo rimwe, munyishure; mpeze ndababarire ububasha bunkoresha ivyo.
41011030	None ukubatiza kwa Yohana kwaturutse mw'ijuru, canke se mu bantu? Ni munyishure."
41011031	Baravugana bati: "Ni twavuga ko ari mw'ijuru; ahava atubaza ati: 'Ni igiki cababujije kumwemera?'"

41012001	Hanyuma Yesu atangura kubabwira mu migani ati: "Habaye umuntu yateye umurima w'inzabibu, awuzitirira uruzitiro, yimbamwo ubwato bw'ikinogo, yubakamwo umutara, arusigarana abarimyi, aja mu mahanga."
41012002	Hageze mw'iyera atuma umukozi ku barimyi, ngo aze yake abo barimyi ivyamuwe mu ruzabibu.
41012003	Baramufata, baramushishagura, bamurungika iminwe iri gusa.
41012004	Yongera kubatumako uwundi mukozi, uwo bamuca uruguma mu mutwe, baramutetereza.

41012008	Baramufata, baramwica, bamukwegera inyuma y'umurima w'inzabibu.
41012009	None nyene uwo murima azogenza ate? Abo barimyi azoza abice rubi, umurima w'inzabibu awusigarane abandi.

41012012	Barondera ingene bomufata, batinya abantu, kuko bamenye yuko ari bo yaciyeko uwo mugani; bamusiga hano, baragenda.

41012015	Turitange, canke dusigeho?" Maze amenye uburyarya bwabo arababaza ati: "Mungereza iki? Ni munzanire idenariyo, ndayirabe."

41012020	Habaye abavukana indwi: uwa mbere ararongora, arapfa, ntiyasiga abana;
41012021	uwa kabiri acura umupfakazi wiwe, na we apfa adasize abana n'uwa gatatu aba atyo;
41012022	bose uko ari indwi ntibasiga abana. Hanyuma ya bose, na wa mugore arapfa.
41012023	Mbega mw'izuka azoba muka nde muri bo? Ko bari bamufise bose uko ari indwi!"
41012024	Yesu arabishura ati: "Igituma muzimira mbega si uko mutamenye ivyanditswe canke ubushobozi bw'Imana?
41012025	Aho bazozukira mu bapfuye ntibazorongora kandi ntibazoshingirwa; bazoba nk'abamarayika bo mw'ijuru."
41012026	Ariko ivyo abapfuye yuko bazurwa, nta ho murasoma mu gitabo ca Mose hamwe havuga ivyo Igisaka c'amahwa, ingene Imana yamubwiye iti: "Ni jewe Mana ya Aburahamu, Imana ya Isaka, Imana ya Yakobo?"
41012027	Imana si iyo abapfuye, ni iyo abariho; mwarazimiye cane.
41012028	Haza umwe mu bahinga b'ivyanditswe yumva babazanya, amenye ko abishuye neza, aramubaza ati: "Ibwirizwa ry'imbere muri yose ni irihe?"
41012029	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Iryo imbere ni iri, ngo ni mwumve, yemwe Bisirayeli, Uhoraho Imana yacu ni we Uhoraho wenyene."
41012030	Kandi mukundishe Uhoraho Imana yanyu imitima yanyu yose, n'ubugingo bwanyu bwose, n'ubwenge bwanyu bwose, n'inkomezi zanyu zose.
41012031	Irya kabiri ngiri, Mukunde abavukanyi banyu nk'uko mwikunda; nta rindi bwirizwa risumba ayo.

41012033	kandi kuyikundisha umutima wose, n'ugutahura kwose, n'inkomezi zose, bo n'ugukunda mugenzawe nk'uko wikunda, biruta cane ibimazi vyose bituriwe n'ibidaturiye."
41012034	Yesu abonye amwishuranye ubwenge, aramubwira ati: "Nturi kure y'ubwami bw'Imana." Ntihagira uwusubira kwubahuka kugira ico amubaza.

41013001	Ariko arasohoka mu rusengero, umwe mu bigishwa biwe aramubwira ati: "Mwigisha, raba aya mabuye uko ari, n'iyi nyubako uko iri !"
41013002	Yesu aramubaza ati: "Uraraba iyi nyubako ihambaye?" Ntihazosigazwa ibuye rigeretse ku rindi, ridasamburiwe hasi.
41013003	Yicaye ku musozi wa Elayono yerekeye ku rusengero, Petero, Yakobo, Yohana na Andereya baramubaza bihereranye
41013004	bati: "Tubwire, ivyo bizobaho ryari, ikimenyetso kizoba iki, c'igihe ivyo vyose bizoba bigira bishike?"
41013005	Yesu atangura kubabwira ati: "Mwirinde ntihagire uwubazimiza."
41013006	Benshi bazoza mw'izina ryanje bati: "Ndi we; kandi bazozimiza benshi."
41013007	Kandi ni mwumva intambara n'impuha z'intambara, ntimuzohagarike imitima; ntibizobura kubaho, ariko umuhero uzoba utaraza.
41013008	Kuko ihanga rizotera irindi hanga, n'ubwami buzotera ubundi bwami, isi izonyiganyiga henshi, amapfa azotera. Ivyo n'itanguriro ryo kuramukwa.
41013009	Ariko mwirinde, kuko bazobashengerana mu manza, muzokubitirwa mu masengero y'Abayuda, kandi muzohagarara imbere y'abaganza n'abami babampora, mube ikimenyetso kibabere icabona.
41013010	Ubutumwa bwiza bukwiye kubanza kuvugwa mu mahanga yose.
41013011	Kandi ni babajana babashengeranye, ntimuzohagarikire imitima ico muzovuga; ico muzohabwa cose muri ako kanya, muzobe ari co muvuga, kuko atazoba ari mwebwe muvuga, azoba ari Mpwemu Yera.
41013012	Umuntu azoshengerana uwo bavukana ngo bamwice, na se w'umwana azomushengerana, n'abana bazogabagabira abavyeyi babicishe.
41013013	Muzoba mwanswe na bose, babahora izina ryanje, ariko uwihangana, agashitsa iherezo, ni we azokira.
41013014	Ariko, aho muzobonera ca kizira c'ishano ry'ubugesera gihagaze aho kidakwiye, (uwusoma ni yiyubare), ico gihe abazoba bari i Yudaya bazohungire ku misozi miremire,
41013015	uwuzoba ari hejuru ku nzu ntazokwururutswe no kwinjira gusahura ikintu cose mu nzu yiwe;
41013016	uwuzoba ari mu mirima ntazosubizwe inyuma no gusahura umutamana wiwe.
41013017	Ariko muri iyo misi abazoba batwaye inda n'abonsa bazobona ibara;
41013018	kandi muzosenge kugira ngo ntibizobe mu gatasi.
41013019	Kuko iyo misi izoba iyo amarushwa atigeze kubaho, kuva kw'itanguriro ry'ibiremwa Imana yaremye ugashitsa n'ubu, kandi atazokwongera kubaho.
41013020	Iyaba Umwami Imana itogeruye iyo misi, ntihorokotse umuntu n'umwe, ariko ku bwo abatoranijwe yatoranije, yarayigeruye.
41013021	Ico gihe ni hagira umuntu ababwira ati: "Ehe Kristo ari hano;" canke ati: "Ari hariya: ntimuzovyemere."
41013022	Kuko hazokwaduka abigira Kristo n'abigira abavugishwa n'Imana, bagakora ibimenyetso n'ibitangaza, kugira ngo bazimize n'abatoranijwe, ni vyashoboka.
41013023	Ariko mweho mwirinde; raba ndabibabwiye vyose bitaraba.
41013024	Ariko muri iyo misi, hanyuma y'ayo marushwa, izuba rizocura umwiza, n'ukwezi ntikuzoba kucaka umuco wakwo,
41013025	n'inyenyeri zizoba ziriko zirakoragurika ziva kw'ijuru, n'ivyo inkomezi vyo mu majuru bizonyiganyizwa.
41013026	Ni ho bazobona Umwana w'umuntu aje mu bicu, ari n'ububasha bwinshi n'ubwiza.
41013027	Ni ho azotuma abamarayika, akoranye abatoranijwe biwe, bave mu birere bine, guhera ku mpera y'isi kugeza impera y'ijuru.
41013028	Ni mwigire ku musukoni umugani wawo, ishami ryawo iyo ritoshe, amababi agatutuza, mumenya yuko agatasi kari hafi.
41013029	Nuko namwe ni mwabona ivyo bibaye, muzomenye ko ari hafi, ku rugi.
41013030	Ndababwire ukuri; abo iki gihe ntibazorangira, ivyo vyose bitarashika.
41013031	Ijuru n'isi bizorangira, ariko amajambo yanje nta co azoba.
41013032	Ariko uwo musi canke iyo saha, nta wubizi, n'iyo boba abamarayika bo mw'ijuru, canke Umwana w'Imana, atari Data gusa.
41013033	Mwiyubare, mube maso, musenge; kuko mutazi igihe bizoshikira.
41013034	Ni nk'umuntu yasize urugo rwiwe, aja mu kindi gihugu, asigarana abashumba biwe urugo, kandi ahejeje kugerera umuntu wese igikorwa ciwe, abarira umuteramyi ngo yame agavye.
41013035	Nuko mwame mugavye, kuko mutazi igihe nyene urugo azozamwo, namba ari ku mugoroba, canke mu gicugu, canke mu nkoko, canke umutwenzi ukitse;
41013036	kugira ngo ni yaza giturumbuka, ntasange musinziriye.
41013037	Ariko ico ndababariye, ndakibarira bose nti: "Mwame mugavye."
41014001	Hari hasigaye imisi ibiri, imisi mikuru ya Pasika ikagera, ni yo yo kurya imitsima itambiwe. Abaherezi bakuru n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe barondera uburyo bwo guhenda Yesu ngo bamufate bamwice;
41014002	kuko bavuga ko batamufata mu misi mikuru, abantu bogumuka.
41014003	Ari i Betaniya mu nzu kwa Simoni umunyamibembe, yicaye ariko ararya, haza umugore afise agacupa k'amavuta amota cane, y'igiciro kinini cane, y'agati kitwa narada; amena ako gacupa k'amavuta ayamusuka ku mutwe.
41014004	Bamwe muri bo baritonganya bati: "Mbega ubu buhombe bw'aya mavuta ni ubwo iki?"
41014005	Kuko yoshoboye kugurwa idenariyo amajana atatu arenga, zigahabwa aboro; baramwidodombera.
41014006	Yesu arababarira ati: "Ni mumureke! Mumubabariza iki? Ankoreye igikorwa ciza.
41014007	Aboro muramana imisi yose; aho mwogombera mwobagirira neza; ariko jeho ntituja kwamana imisi yose.
41014008	Akoze uko ashoboye, ansutse amavuta ku mubiri awutegurira guhambwa bitaraba.
41014009	Ndababwire ukuri, aho ubutumwa bwiza buzovugwa hose mw'isi yose, n'ico uwu akoze kizovugwa, kibe icibutso ciwe." "
41014010	Kandi Yuda Isikaryota, yari umwe muri bamwe icumi na babiri, aja ku baherezi bakuru, ngo azomubaronkere.
41014011	Bavyumvise baranezerwa, basezerana kumuha amahera y'ifeza. Arondera uburyo bwo kumubaronkera.
41014012	Ku musi wo gutangurirako ivyo kurya imitsima itambiwe, uwo babagako umwagazi w'intama wa Pasika, abigishwa biwe baramubaza bati:" "Ugomba ko twoja hehe gutegura ivya Pasika ngo ubirye?"
41014013	Atuma babiri mu bigishwa biwe, arababarira ati: "Ni muje mu gisagara, umugabo muribuhure yikoreye umubindi w'amazi mumukurikire.
41014014	Aho aja kwinjira mubwire nyene urwo rugo muti:'Umwigisha agize ngo indaro yiwe y' aho asangirira ivya Pasika n'abigishwa biwe iri hehe?"
41014015	Ubwiwe aribubereke inzu nini yo hejuru, isezeye, iteguritse; mube ari yo muduteguriramwo." "
41014016	Ba bigishwa baragenda, baja mu gisagara, babisanga uko yabibabariye; bategura ivya Pasika.
41014017	Bugorovye Yesu azanana na bamwe icumi na babiri.
41014018	Bicaye bariko bararya, Yesu arababwira ati:" "Ndababwire ukuri; umwe muri mwebwe, dusangira, agira angure."
41014019	Batangura kubabara, bamubaza umwumwe bati: "Mbega ni jewe?"
41014020	Arabishura ati: "Umwe muri mwebwe icumi na babiri, turiko turakoreza amaboko rimwe mu mubehe, ni we."
41014021	Umwana w'umuntu agira agende nk'uko vyanditswe kuri we; ariko uwo muntu agura Umwana w'umuntu azobona ibara; uwo muntu ivyomubereye vyiza iyaba atavutse.
41014022	Maze bariko bararya, yakira umutsima; awuhezagiye arawumanyagura, arawubaha ati: "Ni mwakire, uwu ni umubiri wanje."
41014023	Yakira igikombe; agishimiye Imana arakibaha, bakinywerako bose.
41014024	Arababarira ati: "Ico ni amaraso yanje y'isezerano, aviriye benshi."
41014025	Ndababwire ukuri, sinzokwongera kunywa ku nzabibu, gushitsa kuri wa musi nzonywera umutobe wazo musha mu bwami bw'Imana.
41014026	Bahejeje kuririmba, barasohoka, baja ku musozi wa Elayono.
41014027	Maze Yesu arababwira ati: "Mwese muhava mutsitazwa; kuko handitswe, ngo nzokubita umwungere, intama zisanzare."
41014028	Ariko ni namara kuzurwa, nzobitangira imbere kuja i Galilaya.
41014029	Maze Petero aramubwira ati: "N'iyo vyotsitaza bose, urakura jeho."
41014030	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Ndakubwira ukuri yuko wewe ubwawe uwu musi muri iri joro nyene, inkoko itarabika uhava unyihakana gatatu."
41014031	Ariko arihanukira cane ati: "Ni iyo noba nkwiye gupfana nawe, sinokwihakana." N'abandi na bo bavuga batyo bose."
41014032	Maze bashika ahantu hitwa i Getsemane, abarira abigishwa biwe ati: "Ba muricaye hano, mbanze nje gusenga."
41014033	Ajana Petero, Yakobo na Yohana, atangura kugira ubwoba no guhagarika umutima cane.
41014034	Arababwira ati: "Umutima wanje uri n'akabonge kagomba kunyica; ba muragumye hano, mube maso."
41014035	Yunguruza imbere gatoya, yubama hasi arasenga ngo ico gihe kimurengane, asangwa bishoboka
41014036	Ati: "Abba, Data, vyose biragushobokera; kura iki gikombe kindengane, ariko ntibibe uko jewe ngomba, yamara bibe uko wewe ugomba."
41014037	Aragaruka, asanga basinziriye, abaza Petero ati: "Simoni, urasinziriye? Nturushe uba maso n'isaha n'imwe?
41014038	Ni mube maso, musenge, ntimuje mu mosha mabi. Umutima ni wo ukunze, ariko umubiri ufise intege nke."
41014039	Yongera kugenda, arasenga, avuga amajambo amwe n'aya mbere.
41014040	Yongera kugaruka, asanga basinziriye, kuko amaso yabo yari aremerewe cane, ntibamenya ico bamwishura.
41014041	Agaruka ubugira gatatu, arababarira ati: "Ni mwisinzirire noneho, muruhuke; biraheze. Igihe kirashitse; raba Umwana w'umuntu ashizwe mu maboko y'abanyavyaha.
41014042	Ni muvyuke, tugende, ehe uwunguze ari hafi."
41014043	Buno nyene akivuga, Yuda, umwe muri bamwe icumi na babiri, araza, azananye n'igitero kizanye inkota n'amahiri, kivuye ku baherezi bakuru n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe n'abashingantahe.
41014044	Ariko uwumugura yari yabahaye ikimenyetso ati: "Uwo nja gusoma azoba ari we, mumufate, mumujane mumugumije."
41014045	Ashitse, aca aramwegera ati: "Mwigisha;" maze aramusomagura.
41014046	Bamushorerako amaboko, baramufata.
41014047	Maze umwe mu bahagazeho asokora inkota, ayikubita umushumba w'umuherezi mukuru, amuca ugutwi.
41014048	Yesu arababaza ati: "Mbega munziye kumfata nk'umwambuzi, muzanye inkota n'amahiri?
41014049	Ko namana namwe mu rusengero nigisha imisi yose, ntimumfate; ariko ibi bibaye kugira ngo ivyanditswe bishike." "
41014050	Maze bose baramuta barahunga.
41014051	Kandi umuhungu umwe w'umusore amuja inyuma, yizingiyeko impuzu imwe gusa, baramufata;
41014052	abatana impuzu yiwe, ahunga ataco yambaye.
41014053	Bajana Yesu ku muherezi mukuru, abaherezi bakuru bose n'abashingantahe n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe bakoraniraho."
41014054	Petero amuja inyuma barenga arenguka, ashika imbere mu rugo rw'umuherezi mukuru; yicarana n'abagendanyi yota umuriro.
41014055	Maze abaherezi bakuru n'abashingantahe ba sentare bose baronderera Yesu ibirego vyomwicisha, barabibura.
41014056	Naho abamurega ibinyoma bari benshi, ibirego vyabo ntivyari bihuye.
41014057	Bamwe bava hasi, baramubeshera
41014058	bati: "Twebwe twaramwumvise avuga ngo yosambura uru rusengero rwubatswe n'intoke akubaka urundi rutubatswe n'intoke mu misi itatu."
41014059	Ariko na ho nyene amajambo yabo ntiyari ahuye.
41014060	Umuherezi mukuru arahaguruka, ahagarara hagati, abaza Yesu ati: "Nta co wiregura? Aba bakwagirije iki?"
41014061	Arihorera, ntiyamwishura na rimwe. Umuherezi mukuru yongera kumubaza ati: "Ni wewe Kristo, Umwana w'Iyishimwa?"
41014062	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Ndi we; kandi muzobona Umwana w'umuntu yicaye i buryo bw'ububasha bw'Imana, azananye n'ibicu vyo kw'ijuru."
41014063	Maze umuherezi mukuru yitabagurirako imyambaro yiwe, aravuga ati: "Turacaronderera iki ivyabona?
41014064	Muriyumviye ingene atutse Imana; mugira ngo iki?" Bose bamucira urubanza ngo akwiye gupfa.
41014065	Bamwe batangura kumuvuma amate, bamupfuka mu maso, bamukubita ibipfunsi bati: "Ni udupfindure." " Abagendanyi bamushikizako amashi.

41014067	abonye Petero yota umuriro, aramwitegereza, aramubwira ati:" "Nawe nyene mwari kumwe na wa Munyanazareti Yesu."
41014068	Na we arabihakana ati: "Sinzi ico uvuze, sindagitahuye." Maze arunguruza, ashika mu bikingi vy'irembo; inkoko irabika.
41014069	Ya ncoreke imubonye, itangura kwongera kubwira abahagazeho iti: "Uwu ni uwo muri bo."
41014070	Na we yongera kubihakana. Maze hahise akanya, abahagazeho bongera kubwira Petero bati: "Ni ivyo ukuri uri uwo muri bo, bitayeko uri Umunyagalilaya."
41014071	Na we atangura kurahira arisiba ati: "Uwo muntu muvuga sindanamuzi."
41014072	Uwo mwanya inkoko ibika ubugira kabiri. Petero yibuka rya jambo Yesu yamubwiye ati: "Inkoko itarabika, uja kunyihakana gatatu;" avyiyumviriye, ararira.
41015001	Umutwenzi utambitse, uwo mwanya abaherezi bakuru, abashingantahe, abahinga b'ivyanditswe n'abashingantahe ba sentare bose baja inama, baboha Yesu, baramujana, bamushikiriza Pilato.
41015002	Pilato aramubaza ati: "Ni wewe Mwami w'Abayuda?" Na we aramwishura ati: "Urarivuze."
41015003	Abaherezi bakuru bamurega vyinshi.
41015004	Pilato yongera kumubaza ati: "Nta co wiregura?" Umve ivyo bakwagiriza ingene ari vyinshi. "
41015005	Maze Yesu ntiyasubira kwishura ijambo na rimwe, bituma Pilato atangara.
41015006	Muri iyo misi mikuru yahora abarekurira imbohe imwe, uwo bamusavye.
41015007	Hariho umwe yitwa Baraba, yabohanywe n'abagararije, bishe abantu muri ukwo kugarariza.

41015009	Pilato arababaza ko bagomba ko abarekurira Umwami w'Abayuda?
41015010	Kuko yamenye yuko ishari ari ryo ryatumye abaherezi bakuru bamutanga.

41015015	Pilato agomvye kumara ishavu ishengero, abarekurira Baraba, maze atanga Yesu ngo abambwe, amaze kumutonagura.
41015016	Maze abasoda bamujana imbere mu rugo, ari rwo boma, bahamagara ingabo zose, ziraterana.

41015019	Bamukubita irenga mu mutwe, bamuvuma amate, barapfukama, bamukomera amashi.
41015020	Bamaze kumucurira, bamwambura ya mpuzu y'agahama, bamwambika impuzu ziwe, bamurengana irembo bamushoreye kumubamba.

41015035	Maze bamwe mu bahahagaze bavyumvise baravuga bati: "Umve, ahamagaye Eliya."

41015039	Intwazangabo y'abasoda ijana yari ihahagaze bahanganye, ibonye acikanye atyo, iravuga ati: "Ni ivyo ukuri, uwu muntu yari Umwana w'Imana."
41015040	Hariho n'abagore bari kure babiraba, muri bo harimwo Mariya Magadalene, na Mariya nyina wa Yakobo mutoya na Yose, harimwo na Salome.
41015041	Abo bagore, aho yaba i Galilaya, baramukurikira bakamukorera; kandi hariho n'abandi bagore benshi bari baduganye na we i Yerusalemu.

41015043	haza Yosefu w'i Arimataya, umushingantahe w'icubahiro, kandi na we yari areretse ubwami bw'Imana, ararinduka aja kuri Pilato, asaba ikiziga ca Yesu.
41015044	Ariko Pilato biramutangaza ko yoba amaze gupfa; ahamagaza ya ntwazangabo y'abasoda, ayibaza yuko amaze umwanya apfuye.

41016001	Maze isabato ishize, Mariya Magadalene, Mariya nyina wa Yakobo na Salome bagura ibimota neza, ngo baje kubimusiga.
41016002	Kandi mu mutwenzi ku wa mbere w'imisi indwi barazinduka, bashika ku mva izuba rirashe.

41016004	Maze bunamuye amaso babona ca kibuye catembagajwe cavuyeho, kandi cari kinini cane.
41016005	Maze binjiye mu mva, babona umusore yicaye mu ruhande rw'i buryo, yambaye imvune yera, barumirwa cane.
41016006	Arababwira ati: "Nta co mwumirwa, ndazi yuko murondera Yesu Umunyanazareti umwe yabambwa; none yazutse, ntari hano; ehe, raba aho bari bamushize !"

41016008	Bava mu mva, barahunga, kuko bari bafashwe n'ubwoba bwinshi n'akumiza, maze ntibagira ico babwira umuntu n'umwe, kuko batinye. ]

41016011	Na bo bumvise ko ari muzima, kandi ko yamwiboneye, ntibavyemera.

41016013	Na bo nyene baragenda, babibwira abasigaye, maze ntibabemerera na bo.
41016014	Hanyuma yiyereka bamwe icumi n'umwe, bicaye bariko bararya, abagaya ukutizera kwabo no gukomantara kw'imitima yabo, kuko batemereye abamubonye, amaze kuzuka.
41016015	Arababarira ati:" "Mugende muje mu bihugu vyose, mubwire abaremwe bose ubutumwa bwiza.
41016016	Uwizera akabatizwa azokizwa, ariko uwutizera azotsindwa n'urubanza.
41016017	Kandi ibimenyetso bizokwama biboneka ku bizera ni ibi: bazosenda abadayimoni mw'izina ryanje; bazovuga indimi nshasha;
41016018	bazofata inzoka; ni banywa ikintu cica, nta co kizobagira na gatoya; bazorambika ibiganza ku barwaye, bakire."
41016019	Kandi Umwami Yesu ahejeje kubibabarira, aduzwa mw'ijuru, avyagira i buryo bw'Imana.
41016020	Abo bavayo, bigisha hose, Umwami Yesu akorana na bo, ijambo ryiwe arishingishiriza intahe ibimenyetso birikurikira. Amina. ]
42001001	Abantu benshi bagerageje kwandika amajambo adonda ivyabaye muri twebwe,
42001002	nk'uko twabirazwe n'abahereye ubwa mbere ari ivyabona vyavyo n'abakozi b'ijambo ry'Imana.
42001003	Nuko nanje, mpejeje gukurikiranya vyose neza mpereye ku vya mbere, nabonye ko ari vyiza kubikwandikira uko bikurikirana, wewe Teyofilo umwubahwa,
42001004	kugira ngo umenye neza yuko amajambo wigishijwe ari ayo ukuri adakekeranywa.
42001005	Ku butware bwa Herode, umwami w'i Yudaya, hariho umuherezi yitwa Zakariya, wo mu mutigiri wa Abiya, kandi yarafise umugore wo mu nzu ya Aroni, yitwa Elisabeti.
42001006	Bompi bagororoka imbere y'Imana, bagendera mu vyagezwe n'amabwirizwa vy' Umwami Imana vyose, batagawa.
42001007	Ariko ntibagira umwana, kuko Elisabeti yari ingumba, kandi bompi bari bageze mu zabukuru.
42001008	Maze yariko arakora igikorwa c'ubuherezi imbere y'Imana, uko bagenda bakurikirana;
42001009	kandi nk'uko umugenzo w'abaherezi wari uri, ni we yari yatoranijwe n'ubupfindo kwinjira ahera h'urusengero rw'Umwami Imana, guturira imibavu.
42001010	Kandi ishengero ryose ry'ubwo bwoko ryariko rirasengera hanze mu gihe co guturira.
42001011	Maze umumarayika w'Umwami Imana aramwiyereka, ahagaze i buryo bw'igicaniro baturirirako imibavu.
42001012	Zakariya amubonye ahagarika umutima, aterwa n'ubwoba.
42001013	Umumarayika aramubwira ati: "Nta co utinya, Zakariya, kuko ivyo wasavye vyumviswe, umugore wawe Elisabeti azokuvyarira umuhungu, uzomwite Yohana.
42001014	Uzonezerwa, uzohimbarwa, kandi benshi bazonezererwa ukuvuka kwiwe;
42001015	kuko azoba mukuru mu maso y'Umwami Imana; ntazonywa umuvinyu canke ikiboreza na kimwe; azokwuzuzwa Mpwemu Yera, ahereye ku kuva mu nda ya nyina,
42001016	kandi azogarura benshi bo mu Bisirayeli bumvire k'umwami Imana yabo."
42001017	Azoyiza imbere ari n'umutima wa Eliya n'ubushobozi bwiwe, ngo ahuze imitima y'abavyeyi n'abana, n'intabarirwa azisubize ku bwenge bw'abagororotsi, ategurire Umwami Imana ubwoko burorane.
42001018	Zakariya abaza umumarayika ati: "Ivyo nzovyerekwa n'iki, ko ndi umutama, n'umugore wanje akaba ageze mu zabukuru?"
42001019	Umumarayika aramwishura ati: "Ndi Gaburiyeli, nama mpagaze mu maso y'Imana, kandi natumwe kubonana nawe no kukubwira ubwo butumwa bwiza.
42001020	Umve, uragobwa ururimi, kandi ntuzoshobora kuvuga, kugeza ku musi ivyo bizoberako, kuko utemeye ijambo ryanje, rizoshika mu gihe caryo."
42001021	Abantu bari barorereye Zakariya batangazwa n'uko atevye ahera h'urusengero;
42001022	Maze asohotse ntiyagira ico ashobora kuvugana na bo, bamenya yuko hari ico yerekewe ahera h'urusengero: arabagereraniriza, akomeza kuba ikiragi.

42004021	Atangura kubabwira ati: "Ivyo vyanditswe birashitse uwu musi, nk'uko amatwi yanyu yiyumviye."
42004022	Bose baramushima, batangazwa n'amajambo y'igikundiro avuye mu kanwa kiwe bati: "Mbega uwu si we umwana wa Yosefu?"
42004023	Arababwira ati: "Ntimuzobura kuncirako uwu mugani muti: 'Muvuzi ni wivure.'" Ivyo twumvise vyose ko wakoreye i Kaperinawumu, ubikorere n'ino mu ntara y'i wanyu.
42004024	Kandi avuga ati: "Ndababwire ukuri, Nta muntu avugishwa n'Imana yemerwa mu ntara y'i wabo."
42004025	Kandi ati: "Ni ivyo ukuri, hariho abapfakazi benshi mu Bisirayeli mu gihe ca Eliya, hamwe ijuru ryakingwa, imvura igatara imyaka itatu n'amezi atandatu, ikigoyi cinshi kigatera mu gihugu cose;
42004026	yamara Eliya ntiyatumwa kuri n'umwe muri bo, ariko atumwa i Zarefati mu gihugu c'i Sidoni ku mugore w'umupfakazi."
42004027	Kandi hariho abanyamibembe benshi mu Bisirayeli mu gihe c'uwavugishwa n'Imana Elisa, ntihakizwa n'umwe muri bo, atari Namani Umusiriya. "
42004028	Abo mu rusengero rw'Abayuda bose bumvise ivyo banigwa n'ishavu,
42004029	bava hasi, baramukwega bamukura mu gisagara cabo, bamujana ku manga y'umusozi wubatsweko igisagara cabo, ngo bamutembagarizeyo;
42004030	ariko aca hagati muri bo, arigira.
42004031	Aramanuka aja Kaperinawumu, igisagara c'i Galilaya: kandi ariko arabigisha kw'isabato,
42004032	batangazwa n'inyigisho ziwe, kuko ijambo ryiwe ryari n'ububasha.
42004033	Kandi mu rusengero rw'Abayuda hari umuntu yinjiwemwo n'impwemu ya dayimoni ahumanye, asemerera n'ijwi rirenga
42004034	ati: " "Yo! Duhuriye hehe ga Yesu Munyanazareti? Uje kuduhonya? Ndakuzi uwo uri we, uri Uwera w'Imana."
42004035	Yesu aramuzibiza ati: "Hora, muvemwo." Dayimoni amutuye hasi hagati yabo, amuvamwo, atagize ico amugira.
42004036	Bose baratangara, barabazanya bati: "Iryo ni ijambo ki? Kubwo ububasha n'ubushobozi afise, ategeka impwemu zihumanye zigasohoka." "
42004037	Inkuru yiwe ikwira hose mu ntara ihakikije.
42004038	Ava hasi, arasohoka ava mu rusengero rw'Abayuda, yinjira mu nzu kwa Simoni. Kandi inabukwe wa Simoni yari afashwe n'umururumbo ukomeye, baramumwingingira.
42004039	Amuhagarara i ruhande, akankamira umururumbo, urazima; avyuka uwo mwanya, arabazimana.
42004040	Kandi ku kirengazuba, abari bafise abarwaye bose barwaye indwara zitandukanye barabamuzanira. Abarambikako ibiganza umwumwe, arabakiza.
42004041	Kandi n'abadayimoni bava muri benshi, basemerera bati: " "Uri Umwana w'Imana." Arabazibiza, ntiyabakundira ko bavuga, kuko bari bazi yuko ari Kristo.
42004042	Kandi ijoro rikeye, arasohoka, aja mu gahinga; ishengero riramurondera, bashika aho ari, bageza kumubuza ngo ntave muri bo.
42004043	Maze arababwira ati: "Nkwiye kuvuga ubutumwa bwiza bw'ubwami bw'Imana no mu bindi bisagara, kuko ari co natumwe."
42004044	Nuko avugira ijambo ry'Imana mu nsengero z'Abayuda y'i Galilaya.
42005001	Nuko ishengero ririko rirahita ryumva ijambo ry'Imana, yari ahagaze ku musenyi w'ikiyaga c'i Genesareti.
42005002	Abona amato abiri aziritswe ku nkombe y'ikiyaga, ariko abarovyi bari bayavuyemwo, boza insenga.
42005003	Atambukira mu bwato bumwe, bwari ubwa Simoni, aramusaba ngo abwigizeyo buve ku nkombe gatoya; aricara, yigisha ishengero, ari mu bwato.
42005004	Ahejeje kuvuga, abarira Simoni ati: "Igira hagati, muterere insenga zanyu murobe."
42005005	Simoni aramwishura ati: "Erega Mwigisha, twakesheje ijoro ryose twarushe, nta co twafashe; ariko ku bwo ijambo ryawe ndaterera insenga."
42005006	Babigize, baroba ifi nyinshi cane, insenga zabo zigomba gucika.
42005007	Bakura abagenzi babo bari mu bundi bwato, ngo bazobafashe. Baraza, buzuza ubwato bwompi, bwagomba kwibira.
42005008	Ariko Simoni Petero abibonye yikubita imbere y'amavi ya Yesu ati: "Va aho ndi, Mugenzi, kuko ndi umunyavyaha."
42005009	Kuko atangaye, n'abari kumwe na we bose, babonye ifi barovye.
42005010	Na Yakobo na Yohana abana ba Zebedayo na bo baratangara, bari bafatanije na Simoni. Yesu abwira Simoni ati: "Nta co utinya, kuva ubu uzoroba abantu. "
42005011	Bahejeje gushikana ubwato bwabo ku nkombe, basiga vyose, baramukurikira.
42005012	Ikindi gihe ari mu gisagara kimwe muri vyo, haza umuntu ajejeta imibembe. Abonye Yesu yikubita hasi yubamye, aramwinginga ati: " "Mugenzi, ukunze, woshobora kumpumanura."
42005013	Agorora ukuboko, amukorako ati: "Ndakunze, humanuka." Imibembe ica imuvako.
42005014	Aramwihanikiriza ati: "Ntagire umuntu ubibarira mugabo genda, wiyereke umuherezi, utange ivyo uguhumanurwa kwawe, nk'uko Mose yabitegetse, bibe ikimenyetso kibabere icabona." "
42005015	Ariko inkuru yiwe irushiriza gukwira, ishengero ryinshi rikoranira kumwumva no gukizwa indwara zabo.
42005016	Ariko we yiherera mu bugaragwa, asenga.
42005017	Umusi umwe Yesu ariko arigisha, Abafarisayo n'abigisha ivyagezwe bari bicayeho, bavuye mu mihana yose y'i Galilaya, i Yudaya n'i Yerusalemu; kandi ubushobozi bw'Imana bwo gukiza indwara bwari muri we."
42005018	Maze haza abagabo bazanye ikimuga, bagiteruye mu nderuzo, barondera ingene bacinjiza ngo bagishire imbere yiwe.
42005019	Babuze aho bocinjiriza ku bwo ishengero, burira hejuru ku nzu, bagicisha mu mategura ayisakaye, bacururutsa mu nderuzo hagati y'abantu imbere ya Yesu.
42005020	Abonye ukwizera kwabo, aravuga ati: "Ewe muntu, ivyaha vyawe urabihariwe."
42005021	Abahinga b'ivyanditswe n'Abafarisayo batangura kwiburanya bati: "Uwo ni nde arogose? Ni nde ashobora guharira ivyaha atari Imana yonyene?"
42005022	Maze Yesu, amenye ivyo biburanya, arababaza ati: "Mwiburanya ibiki mu mitima yanyu?"
42005023	Icoroshe ni ikihe ni ukuvuga nti: 'Uhariwe ivyaha vyawe;' canke ni ukuvuga nti: ' Vyuka ugende?'
42005024	Ariko kugira ngo mumenye ko Umwana w'umuntu afise ububasha mw'isi bwo guharira ivyaha-" abwira ico kimuga ati: "Ndakubariye nti Vyuka, wikorere inderuzo yawe, utahe."
42005025	Aca avyuka imbere yabo, yikorera inderuzo yari aryamyemwo, arataha, ahimbaza Imana.
42005026	Bose barumirwa cane, bahimbaza Imana, baterwa n'ubwoba bwinshi bati: "Uwu musi tubonye ibitangaza."
42005027	Ivyo bishize, arasohoka, abona umutozakori yitwa Lewi, yicaye aho yatoreza ikibuguro, aramubarira ati: "Nkurikira."
42005028	Asiga vyose, ava hasi, aramukurikira.
42005029	Lewi amuteguriza izimano ryinshi mu nzu yiwe; kandi hari abantu benshi b'abatozakori n'abandi bicaranye na bo basangira.
42005030	Abafarisayo n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe bafatanye na bo bidodombera abigishwa ba Yesu bati: "Ni igiki gitumye musangira n'abatozakori n'abanyavyaha?"
42005031	Yesu arabishura ati: "Abakomeye nta co bagombera umuvuzi, atari abarwaye.
42005032	Sinaje guhamagara abagororotsi, ariko naje guhamagara abanyavyaha ngo bihane."
42005033	Na bo baramubwira bati: "Abigishwa ba Yohana barisonzesha kenshi bagasenga, n'abo Abafarisayo ni uko, ariko abawe baririra, barinywera."
42005034	Yesu arababaza ati: "Mbega mwoshobora mute kugera abatowe ngo bisonzeshe, bakiri kumwe n'umukwe?"
42005035	Ariko hari imisi izoza; kandi umukwe ni yabakurwamwo, bazoca bisonzesha muri iyo misi.
42005036	Kandi abacira umugani ati: "Ntawotabura ikiraka ku mpuzu nshasha, ngo acomeke ku mpuzu y'umushire. Uwogira atyo yoba atabuye nshasha, kandi ikiraka atabuye kuri nshasha nticomatana n'iyo umushire."
42005037	Kandi nta wotara umutobe w'umuvinyu mu mikuza y'insato ibombotse; kuko umuvinyu woturitsa iyo mikuza, igashirira hasi, imikuza igapfa.
42005038	Ariko igikwiye ni ugutara umutobe w'umuvinyu mu mikuza y'insato.
42005039	Kandi nta muntu yanyoye umuvinyu uhiye yogomba umutobe; kuko avuga ati: "Iyihiye ni yo nziza."
42006001	Kw'isabato agenda aca mu mirima y'ingano; abigishwa biwe bamyoza ingano, barazihekenya, bazivungavunze mu minwe.
42006002	Bamwe mu Bafarisayo barababaza bati: "Ni igiki gitumye mukora ikizira gukorwa kw'isabato?"
42006003	Yesu na we arababaza ati: "Nta ho murigera musoma ivyo Dawidi yakoze, aho yari ashonje, asonzanye n'abari kumwe na we;
42006004	ingene yinjiye mu nzu y'Imana, akakira imitsima yagenewe gushikanirwa Imana, akayirya, akayihako n'abari kumwe na we, ari umuziro kuribwa, uretse abaherezi bonyene?
42006005	Kandi arababwira ati: "Umwana w'umuntu ni Umwami w'isabato."
42006006	Ku yindi sabato yinjira mu rusengero rw'Abayuda, arigisha; kandi hari umuntu anyunyutse ukuboko kw'i buryo.
42006007	Abahinga b'ivyanditswe bo n'Abafarisayo baramugenza ngo barabe ko akiza kw'isabato, ngo baronke ingene bomurega.
42006008	Na we amenya ivyo biyumvira; abarira uwo muntu anyunyutse ukuboko ati: "Va hasi, uhagarare hagati." Ava hasi, arahagarara.
42006009	Yesu arababwira ati: "Ndababaze, mbega ivyemerwa ni ugukora ivyiza kw'isabato, canke ni ugukora ibibi; gukiza umuntu, canke kumwica?"
42006010	Aberaguzamwo amaso bose, aramubarira ati: "Ramvura ukuboko kwawe." " Arabigira, ukuboko kwiwe kurakira.
42006011	Ariko bo birabasaza rwose, baja inama y'ico bogira Yesu.
42006012	Muri iyo misi avayo, aja ku musozi gusenga. Akesha ijoro asenga Imana.
42006013	Ijoro rikeye, ahamagara abigishwa biwe, atoranyamwo icumi na babiri, abita intumwa.
42006014	Simoni, uwo yise Petero, Andereya mwene nyina, Yakobo, Yohana, Filipo, Barutolomayo,
42006015	Matayo, Toma, Yakobo umwana wa Alufayo, Simoni yitwa Zelote,
42006016	Bari Yuda umwana wa Yakobo na Yuda Isikaryota yabaye umuguranyi. "
42006017	Amanukana na bo, ahagarara ahateze, kandi hariho ishengero ryinshi ry'abigishwa biwe, n'ishengero ryinshi ry'abantu bavuye i Yudaya hose n'i Yerusalemu no mu gihugu co muri Tiro n'i Sidoni gihereranye n'ikiyaga kinini, baje kumwumva no gukizwa indwara zabo.
42006018	Kandi n'abababazwa n'impwemu zihumanye barakizwa.
42006019	Kandi ishengero ryose rigerageza kumukorako, kuko ubushobozi bwamuvamwo bukabakiza bose.
42006020	Yunamurira amaso abigishwa biwe arababwira ati: "Murahiriwe mwebwe aboro; kuko ubwami bw' Imana ari ubwanyu.
42006021	Murahiriwe mwebwe mushonje ubu, kuko muzohazwa. Murahiriwe mwebwe murira ubu, kuko muzotwenga.
42006022	Muzoba muhiriwe abantu ni babanka bakabaca, bakabatuka, bakanegura izina ryanyu nk'aho ari ribi, babahoye Umwana w'umuntu.
42006023	Uwo musi muzonezererwe mwitere hejuru, kuko impera yanyu ari nini mw'ijuru; kuko ari ko ba sekuruza babo bagize abavugishwa n'Imana.
42006024	Ariko muzobona ibara, mwebwe abatunzi; kuko muhejeje gutunganirwa.
42006025	Muzobona ibara, mwebwe muhaze ubu; kuko muzosonza. Muzobona ibara, mwebwe mutwenga ubu; kuko muzoboroga murira.
42006026	Muzobona ibara, aho abantu bose bazobashemagiza; kuko ari ko ba sekuruza babo bashemagije abigira abavugishwa n'Imana.
42006027	Ariko mwebwe mwumviriza ndababwire: " Ni mukunde abansi banyu, mugirire neza ababanka."
42006028	Muhezagire ababavuma, musabire ababagirira nabi.
42006029	Uwugukubise mu musaya, umuhindukirize n'uwundi; uwukwaka umutamana, ntumwime n'ikanzu.
42006030	Uwugusaba wese umuhe, uwunyaga ivyawe ntuzosubire kubimwaka.
42006031	Kandi uko mugomba ko abantu babagirira, mube ari ko mubagirira namwe.
42006032	Kandi ni mwakunda ababakunda, muzoshimwa iki? Kuko abanyavyaha na bo bagira batyo.
42006033	Kandi ni mwagirira neza ababagirira neza, muzoshimwa iki? Kuko abanyavyaha na bo bagira batyo.
42006034	Kandi ni mwagurana abo muziga ko bazobishura, muzoshimwa iki? Abanyavyaha na bo bagurana abandi banyavyaha, ngo bishurwe nk'ivyabo.
42006035	Ariko mukunde abansi banyu, mubagirire neza, mugurane abantu, mutaziga ko muzokwishurwa; kandi impera zanyu zizoba nyinshi, namwe muzoba abana b'Iyisumbavyose; kuko igirira neza intashima n'ababi.
42006036	Mugire imbabazi, nk'uko So agira imbabazi.
42006037	Kandi ntimugahinyurire mu mitima yanyu, namwe mukazohinyurwa; kandi ntimugatsindishe, namwe mukazotsindishwa. Mubohore, namwe muzobohorwa. Mutange, namwe muzohabwa.
42006038	Ingero nziza, itsindagiye, inyingishe, isesekaye, ni yo bazobaha mu co muteze. Kuko ingero mugeramwo ari yo muzosubirizwamwo namwe.
42006039	Kandi abacira umugani ati: "Mbega impumyi yoshobora kujana iyindi mpumyi?" Zompi ntizogwa mu cobo?
42006040	Umwigishwa ntaruta umwigisha wiwe, ariko umwigishwa wese arangije azoba nk'umwigisha wiwe.
42006041	Urabira iki akabango kari mu jisho rya mugenzawe, ikigiga kiri mu jisho ryawe ntucitegereze?
42006042	Woshobora ute kubwira umuvukanyi wawe uti: "Zana muvukanyi ndagutosore ikigiga kiri mu jisho ryawe; nawe ubwawe nturabe ikigiga kiri mu jisho ryawe? Wa ndyarya we, banza witosore ikigiga kiri mu jisho ryawe, uheze ubone neza gutosora akabango kari mu jisho ry'umuvukanyi.
42006043	Kuko ata giti ciza cama ibibi, kandi nta giti kibi cama ivyiza.
42006044	Igiti cose kimenyekanira ku vyo camye. Nta bokwamura insukoni ku munyinya, canke inzabibu ku mukere.
42006045	Umunyangeso nziza akura ivyiza mw'itunga ryiza ryo mu mutima wiwe, n'umunyangeso mbi akura ibibi mw'itunga ribi. Ibibogaboga mu mutima ni vyo akanwa kiwe kavuga.
42006046	Kandi mumpamagarira iki ngo Mwami, Mwami; ntimukore ivyo mvuga?
42006047	Umuntu wese aza aho ndi, akumva amajambo yanje, akayakora, ndabereka uko asa.
42006048	Asa n'umuntu yubaka inzu, yimvye hasi cane, akubaka umushinge ku rutare. Maze umugezi wuzuye usurira kuri iyo nzu, ntiwashobora kuyinyiganyiza, kuko yubatswe neza.
42006049	Ariko uwumva, ntabikore, asa n'umuntu yubatse inzu ko ivu, atimvye umushinge; maze umugezi uyisurirako, ica irasenyuka, uguhomvoka kw'iyo nzu kwabaye ugukomeye.
42007001	Yesu ahereje kubwira ishengero ayo majambo yose mu matwi y'abantu, aja i Kaperinawumu.
42007002	Hariyo intwazangabo y'abasoda ijana, umushumba wiwe akunda cane yari arwaye, ari ku mpfiro.
42007003	Yumvise inkuru ya Yesu, imutumako abashingantahe b'Abayuda kumwinginga, ngo aze gukiza umushumba wiwe.
42007004	Na bo bashitse aho Yesu ari, baramwinginga cane bati: "Birabereye ko umugirira utyo,
42007005	kuko akunda ubwoko bwacu, n'urusengero rwacu ni we yarutwubakiye."
42007006	Yesu ajana na bo. Ashitse hafi y'inzu, ya ntwazangabo imutumako incuti ziwe ati: "Mugenzi, nturinde kwigora, kuko bitambereye ko winjira mu nzu yanje;
42007007	ni co catumye niyumvira ko bitambereye ko noza aho uri. Ariko vuga ijambo gusa, uwo muhungu arakira."
42007008	Kuko nanje ndi umuntu agendera musi y'abanganza, mfise abasoda ntwara. Iyo mbariye umwe nti: "Genda," aragenda; n'uwundi nti: "Ngwino," akaza; nabarira umushumba wanje nti: "Kora iki," akagikora.
42007009	Yesu yumvise ivyo, aramutangarira, ahindukirira ishengero rimukurikiye ati: "Ndababwire, Sinaribwabone ukwizera kungana gutyo no mu Bisirayeli." "
42007010	Abatumwe basubiye mu nzu, basanga wa mushumba akomeye.
42007011	Hashize igihe gitoya, aja mu gisagara citwa Nayini; abigishwa biwe n'ishengero ryinshi bajana na we.
42007012	Ashitse hafi y'irembo ry'igisagara, hasokoroka abagiye guhamba umuntu, yari ikinege, kandi nyina yari umupfakazi. Abantu benshi bo muri ico gisagara bari kumwe na we bamuherekeje ku maziko.
42007013	Umwami Yesu amubonye amutera akagongwe, aramubarira ati: " "Nta co urira."
