42007015	Uwari yapfuye aravyuka, aricara, atangura kuvuga; Yesu amuha nyina.
42007016	Bose baterwa n'ubwoba, bahimbaza Imana bati: "Uwuvugishwa n'Imana ahambaye aserutse muri twebwe; kandi Imana igendeye abantu bayo." "
42007017	Iyo nkuru yiwe ikwira i Yudaya hose no mu gihugu cose gihereranye na ho.
42007018	Abigishwa ba Yohana bamudondera ivyo vyose.
42007019	Yohana ahamagara babiri mu bigishwa biwe, abatuma ku Mwami Yesu ngo bamubaze ko ari wa wundi akwiye kuza, canke ko bitega uwundi.
42007020	Abo bagabo bamushikiriye, baramubwira bati: " "Yohana Umubatizi yakudutumyeko, ngo tukubaze ko uri wa wundi canke ko twitege uwundi?"
42007021	Muri ako kanya akiza benshi indwara n'ivyago n'ibisigo bibi; n'impumyi nyinshi arazihumura.
42007022	Maze arabishura ati: "Ni mugende, mubarire Yohana ivyo mubonye n'ivyo mwumvise." Impumyi zirahumuka, abacumbagira bagenda neza, abanyamibembe barakizwa, ibipfamatwi birumva, abapfuye barazurwa, aboro barabwirwa ubutumwa bwiza.
42007023	Kandi Hahiriwe uwo ivyanje bitazotsitaza."
42007024	Abatumwe na Yohana bagiye, atangura kubwira ishengero ivya Yohana ati: "Mwagiye mu bugaragwa kuraba iki?"Mbega ni irenga rihungabanywa n'umuyaga?
42007025	Ariko mwagiye kuraba iki? Mbega ni umuntu yambaye impuzu nziza? Erega abambara impuzu zishajije n'abidibamiye baba mu ngo z'abami.
42007026	Ariko mwajanywe no kuraba iki? Umuntu avugishwa n'Imana? Ego me ni vyo; kandi ndababwire, Aruta uwuvugishwa n'Imana cane.
42007027	Uwo ni we yanditswe, ngo Umve, ngira ntume integuza yanje imbere y'amaso yawe, Ikuroranirize inzira imbere yawe.
42007028	Ndababwire, Mu bavyawe n'abagore nta wuruta Yohana; ariko umutoya mu bwami bw' Imana aramuruta.
42007029	Kandi abantu bose n'abatozakori bumvise Yohana bemeye ukugororoka kw' Imana, kuko babatijwe na Yohana.
42007030	Ariko Abafarisayo n'abigisha ivyagezwe bibujije inama z'Imana, kuko batabatijwe na we.
42007031	Nuko abantu b'iki gihe ndabagereranya ni iki, kandi basa ni igiki?
42007032	Basa n'abana bicaye mw'isoko bahamagarana bati: 'Twavugije imyironge, ntimwatamba; twakomye induru, ntimwarira.'
42007033	Yohana Umubatizi yaje atarya umutsima, atanywa umuvinyu, mugira muti: 'Ahagazweko na dayimoni.'
42007034	Umwana w'umuntu yaje arya, anywa, mugira muti: 'Nguwu umukunzi w'inda kandi ari n'umunoho w'umuvinyu, incuti y'abatozakori n'abanyavyaha.'
42007035	Kandi ubwenge bw'Imana bwerekanwa ko ari ubwo ukuri n'abana babwo bose.
42007036	Maze umwe mu Bafarisayo aramuhamagara ngo amuzimane. Yinjira mu nzu y'uwo Mufarisayo, aricara ngo arye.
42007037	Umugore wo muri ico gisagara, yari umunyavyaha, amenye yuko arira mu nzu y'uwo Mufarisayo, azana agacupa k'amavuta amota cane.
42007038	Ahagarara inyuma yiwe, hafi y'ibirenge vyiwe, arira. Atangura kumutonyangiriza amosozi ku birenge, abihanaguza umushatsi wiwe. Arabisomagura, abisiga ya mavuta.
42007039	Wa Mufarisayo yamuhamagaye abibonye, aribwira ati: "Uwu muntu iyo aba uwuvugishwa n'Imana, yari kumenya uwu mugore amukozeko, uko ari n'uko asa, ko ari umunyavyaha."
42007040	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Simoni, mfise ico ngomba kukubwira." Aramwishura ati: "Mbarira, Mwigisha."
42007041	Aramubwira ati: "Habaye umuntu yagurana, hariho abantu babiri bamufitiye umwenda. Umwe yari amufitiye idenariyo amajana atanu, uwundi mirongo itanu.
42007042	Maze badafise ico kumwishura, azibahebera bompi. Mbega uwuzorushiriza kumukunda ni uwuhe?
42007043	Simoni aramwishura ati: "Ngira ngo ni uwo yahebeye nyinshi." Na we aramubwira ati: "Uvuze ukuri."
42007044	Ahindukiriye wa mugore, abwira Simoni ati: "Urabona uwu mugore?" Ninjiye mu nzu yawe, ntiwampa amazi yo kwoga ibirenge; ariko uwu antonyangirije amosozi ku birenge, abihanaguza umushatsi wiwe.
42007045	Ntiwansomye; ariko uwu uhereye aho ninjiriye ntiyasizeho kunsomagura ibirenge.
42007046	Ntiwansutse amavuta ku mutwe; ariko uwu ansize amavuta amota cane ku birenge.
42007047	Iki ni co gitumye ndakubwira yuko ahariwe vya vyaha vyiwe vyinshi; kuko yagize urukundo rwinshi; ariko uhariwe bike agira urukundo ruke.
42007048	Abwira wa mugore ati: "Urahariwe ivyaha vyawe."
42007049	Maze abasangira na we batangura kwibaza bati: "Uwo ni nde, ko aharira n'ivyaha?"
42007050	Abwira wa mugore ati: "Ukwizera kwawe kuragukijije, genda amahoro."
42008001	Hashize igihe gitoya, agendagenda mu bisagara no mu mihana, ababwira ijambo ry'Imana, avuga ubutumwa bwiza bw'ubwami bwayo; bamwe icumi na babiri bajana na we,
42008002	n'abagore bamwe bakijijwe ibisigo n'indwara, Mariya ari we Magadalene, abadayimoni indwi bari baramuvuyemwo,
42008003	na Yowana muka Kuza, umukuru w'abakozi bo mu rugo wa Herode, na Susana, n'abandi bagore benshi, bafashisha Yesu n'abigishwa biwe ivyabo.
42008004	Ishengero ryinshi rirakorana, kandi abavuye mu bisagara vyose baza kuri we, abacira umugani
42008005	ati: " "Umubivyi yasohoye imbuto ziwe; akibiba, zimwe zigwa i ruhande y'inzira, barazikandagira, inyoni zo mu kirere zirazinobagura."
42008006	Izindi zigwa ku rutare, zihejeje kumera ziruma, kuko zibuze ahabomvye.
42008007	Izindi zigwa mu mahwa hagati, amahwa amerana na zo, arazinyoha.
42008008	Izindi zigwa mw'ivu ryiza, ziramera, zama impeke, imwe ijana, iyindi ijana, bityobityo." Avuze ivyo, avuga n'ijwi rirenga ati: "Uwuri n'amatwi yumva ni yumve."
42008009	Maze abigishwa biwe bamubaza uwo mugani, ico usobanura.
42008010	Arababwira ati: ""Mwebwe mwahawe kumenya amabanga y'ubwami bw' Imana; ariko abasigaye babibarirwa mu migani; ngo barabe, yamara ntibavyitegereze; bumve, yamara ntibabitahure."
42008011	Umugani ni uwu. Imbuto ni ijambo ry'Imana.
42008012	Abo i ruhande y'inzira n'abaryumvise, maze Umwansi yaza, agakura iryo jambo mu mitima yabo, kugira ngo ntibizere ngo bakizwe.
42008013	Abo ku rutare ni aba: iyo bumvise iryo jambo, baryakirana umunezero, ariko ntibagira imizi, bizera akanya gato, maze mu gihe c'igeragezwa bakarireka. "
42008014	Izaguye mu mahwa ni abaryumvise, maze bariko barigira umwitwaririko wo muri ubu bugingo, bo n'ubutunzi n'ibihimbaro vyo muri bwo, bikabanyoha, ntibame imbuto nziza.
42008015	Izo mw'ivu ryiza ni abumvise iryo jambo bakarigumya mu mitima myiza itunganye, bakamishwa imbuto n'ukwihangana.
42008016	Kandi nta wodomeka itara, ngo aryubikeko ikintu, canke ngo arishire mu rutara, ariko arishira ku gitereko caryo, ngo abinjira basange habona.
42008017	Kuko ata canyegejwe kitazozanwa ahabona, canke icagizwe ibanga kitazomenyekana kikaja ahabona.
42008018	Mwiyubare uburyo mwumva; kuko uwufise azohabwa kandi uwudafise azokwakwa n'ico yiyumvira ko afise.
42008019	Maze nyina n'abavukanyi biwe baza aho ari, ntibashobora kumushikira ku bwo ishengero.
42008020	Baramubwira bati: "Umuvyeyi wawe na barumuna bawe bahagaze hanze bagomba kubonana nawe."
42008021	Na we arabishura ati: "Mama na bene mama ni aba bumva ijambo ry'Imana bakarikora."
42008022	Igihe kimwe Yesu n'abigishwa biwe batambukira mu bwato, arababwira ati: "Tujabuke, tuje hakurya y'ikiyaga." Baherako baragenda, bava ku nkombe.
42008023	Bariko baragenda, arasinzira; haduka igihuhusi c'umuyaga mu kiyaga, ubwato bwariko buruzura amazi, bari mw'irinde.
42008024	Baraza, baramukangura bati: "Mwigisha, Mwigisha, turapfuye!" Arikangura, azibiza ingunza n'ugusuriranya kw'amazi; birahora, haba agahwekere.
42008025	Arababaza ati: "Mbega ukwizera kwanyu kuri hehe?" Baratinya baratangara, barabazanya bati: "Mbega uwu n'umuntu ki, ko abarira n'umuyaga n'amazi bikamwumvira?"
42008026	Bafata hakurya mu gihugu c'Abageraseni, kirabana n'i Galilaya.
42008027	Ashitse i musozi, umuntu yavuye mu gisagara, yinjiwemwo n'abadayimoni, aramusanganira. Yari amaze imisi myinshi ata mpuzu acambara; nta nzu yabamwo, yaba mu masenga y'imva.
42008028	Abonye Yesu arasemerera, amwikubita imbere, avuga n'ijwi rirenga ati: "Unshakako iki ga Yesu, Mwana w'Imana Isumbavyose?" Ndakwinginze, ntunyice rubi.
42008029	Kuko yari abariye iyo mpwemu ihumanye kuva muri uwo muntu Yahora imutera kenshi, kandi bamubohesha iminyororo ku maboko no ku maguru, bakamurinda, agacagagura ibimuboshe, dayimoni akamutwara nk'agashururu mu bugaragwa.
42008030	Yesu aramubaza ati: "Witwa nde?" Aramwishura ati: "Ndi Gitero." Kuko abadayimoni benshi bari baramwinjiyemwo.
42008031	Ziramwinginga ngo ntazibarire kuja i kuzimu.
42008032	Kandi hari ubusho bw'ingurube nyinshi zirisha kuri uwo musozi; ziramwinginga ngo azemerere kuzinjiramwo; arazemerera.
42008033	Abadayimoni basokoroka muri uno muntu, binjira muri nya ngurube, umukuku wirukira ku gatembwe, zisuka mu kiyaga, amazi araziniga. "
42008034	Abaziragira babibonye barahunga, babivuga mu gisagara no mu misozi.
42008035	Na bo bavayo, baza kuraba ivyabaye, bashika aho Yesu ari, basanga wa muntu dayimoni zamuvuyemwo, yicaye i ruhande y'ibirenge vya Yesu, yambaye, ubwenge bwagarutse; baratinya.
42008036	Ababibonye babiganira ingene uwari yinjiwemwo n'abadayimoni yakize.
42008037	Abantu bose bo mu gihugu c'Abageraseni gikikije aho baramwinginga ngo ave i wabo, kuko bari batewe n'ubwoba bwinshi. Atambukira mu bwato, asubira inyuma.
42008038	Ariko wa muntu dayimoni zavuyemwo aramwinginga ngo agumane na we. ariko aramusezera
42008039	ati: " "Subira i muhira i wawe, ubadondere ivyo Imana igukoreye vyose." " Aragenda, akwiza mu gisagara cose ivyo Yesu yamukoreye vyose.
42008040	Yesu agarutse, ishengero riramusanganira, kuko bose bari bamurorereye.
42008041	Maze haza umuntu yitwa Yayiro, umukuru w'isengero ry'Abayuda: yitembagaza imbere y'ibirenge vya Yesu, aramwinginga ngo aze i muhira i we,
42008042	kuko yarafise umukobwa w'ikinege, yari amaze imyaka nka icumi n'ibiri avutse, kandi yariko arahwera. Ariko aragenda, ishengero riramubanda.
42008043	Umugore arwaye ubutinyanka, yari abimaranye imyaka icumi n'ibiri, yamariye utwiwe twose ku bavuzi adutangamwo ingemu, ntihagira uwushobora kumukiza,
42008044	amuturuka inyuma, akora ku buyonga bw'impuzu yiwe, ako kanya umugende w'amaraso urakama.
42008045	Yesu arabaza ati: " "Ni nde ankozeko?" Bose bahakanye, Petero n'abari kumwe na we baramwishura bati: "Erega Mwigisha, n'ishengero rigutaye hagati rikugundanirako."
42008046	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Hari uwunkozeko, kuko numvise ubushobozi bumvuyemwo."
42008047	Wa mugore abonye yuko atayoberanye, aza ahinda agashitsi, amwikubita imbere, amubwirira mu maso y'abantu bose icatumye amukorako, n'uko akize uwo mwanya.
42008048	Aramubwira ati: "Mwana wanje, ukwizera kwawe kuragukijije, genda amahoro."
42008049	Akivuga, haza umuntu avuye kwa wa mukuru w'isengero ry'Abayuda ati: "Wa mwana wawe aracikanye, ureke kugora umwigisha."
42008050	Maze Yesu avyumvise aramubwira ati: "Ntutinye, wizere gusa, arakira."
42008051	Ashitse ku nzu, ntiyagira uwundi muntu akundira kwinjirana na we, atari Petero, Yohana na Yakobo, na se wa nya mukobwa na nyina.
42008052	Asanga bamuririra bose, bishishitira. Arababarira ati: "Nta co murira, ntahwereye, ariko arasinziriye."
42008053	Baramutwenga bamushimanga, kuko bari bazi ko yapfuye.
42008054	Amufata ukuboko, avuga n'ijwi rirenga ati: "Mukobwa, vyuka. "
42008055	Ubuzima bwiwe buragaruka, aca ava hasi uwo mwanya; Yesu ababarira ngo bamugaburire.
42008056	Abavyeyi biwe baratangara, ariko arabihanikiriza ngo ntihagire umuntu n'umwe babwira ibibaye.
42009001	Akoranya bamwe icumi na babiri, abaha ubushobozi n'ububasha bwo kwirukana dayimoni bwose no gukiza indwara.
42009002	Abatuma kubarira abantu ivyo ubwami bw' Imana, no gukiza abarwaye.
42009003	Arababarira ati: "Ntimugire ico mujana ku nzira, ari inkoni canke isaho, canke induhuro, canke amahera; kandi ntimutware imyambaro ibiri."
42009004	Kandi inzu yose muzokwinjiramwo, mube ari yo mugumamwo, kugeza aho muzovira aho hantu.
42009005	Aho bazokwanka kubakira bose, mukiva muri ico gisagara, muzokunkumure umukungugu wo mu birenge vyanyu, kibe ikimenyetso kibabere icabona. "
42009006	Baragenda, bagendagenda mu mihana, bavuga ubutumwa bwiza, bakiriza abarwaye hose.

42009008	abandi bati: "Ni Eliya yiseruye;" abandi bati: "Ni umwe mu bavugishwa n'Imana ba kera yazutse."
42009009	Herode aravuga ati: "Yohana ni jewe namwiciriye izosi; mbega uwo ni nde, numvako ibimeze bityo?" " Arondera uko yomubona.

42009011	Maze ishengero ribimenye riramukurikira. Arabakira, ababwira ivyo ubwami bw'Imana, kandi abagomba kuvurwa arabakiza.

42009014	Kuko bari abagabo nk'ibihumbi bitanu. Abarira abigishwa biwe ati: "Ni mubicarike bari mu mirwi y'abantu nka mirongo itanitanu." "
42009015	Babigira batyo, barabicarika bose.

42009017	Bararya, barahaga bose, batororokanya utumanyagu tw'imisigazwa, twuzura ibiseke icumi na bibiri.
42009018	Maze yariko arasenga yiherereye, abigishwa biwe bari kumwe na we; arababaza ati: " "Abantu bagira ngo ndi nde?"

42009020	Arababaza ati: "Ariko mweho mugira ngo ndi nde?" Petero aramwishura ati: "Uri Kristo w'Imana."
42009021	Arabihanikiriza, ababarira kutagira umuntu babwira ivyo
42009022	ati: "Umwana w'umuntu akwiye kuzobabazwa uburyo bwinshi, no kuzokwankwa n'abashingantahe n'abakuru b' baherezi n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe, no kuzokwicwa, no kuzozurwa ku musi ugira gatatu."
42009023	Abwira bose ati: "Umuntu ni yagomba kunkurikira, ni yiyanke, yikorere umusaraba wiwe uko bukeye, ankurikire."
42009024	Kuko ugomba gukiza ubugingo bwiwe azobubura; ariko uwuzoheba ubugingo bwiwe ku bwanje azobukiza.
42009025	Kandi umuntu vyomumarira iki gutunga ivyo mw'isi vyose ni yiyica canke akiyaka ubugingo ubwiwe?
42009026	Kuko umuntu wese bizotera isoni kunyemera no kwemera amajambo yanje, n'Umwana w'umuntu bizomutera isoni kumwemera, aho azozira afise ubwiza bwiwe n'ubwa Se n'ubwo abamarayika bera.
42009027	Ariko ndababwire ukuri: muri aba bahagaze hano, harimwo bamwe batazobona urupfu gushitsa aho bazobonera ubwami bw'Imana.
42009028	Hanyuma y'ayo majambo, hashize imisi nk' umunani, ajana Petero, Yohana na Yakobo aduga igisozi, aja gusenga.
42009029	Ariko arasenga, ishusho yo mu maso hiwe ihinduka ukundi, imyambaro yiwe yera derere, irakayangana.
42009030	Abagabo babiri bavugana na we, bari Mose na Eliya.
42009031	Baboneka bafise ubwiza, bavuga ivyo kurangiza kwiwe, yagira aheraheze i Yerusalemu.
42009032	Petero n'abari kumwe na we bari baremerewe n'itiro, bikanguye rwose babona ubwiza bwiwe na ba bagabo babiri bahagararanye na we.
42009033	Bagira batandukane na we, Petero abwira Yesu ati: "Mwigisha, bitubereye vyiza ko turi hano; nuko twubake amahema atatu, rimwe ribe iryoiwawe, irindi rya Mose, irindi rya Eliya." Ntiyari azi ico avuga.
42009034	Akibivuga, igicu c'igipfungu kiraza, kirabatwikira; ico gipfungu kikibashikako, baratinya.
42009035	Ijwi riva muri nya gicu riti: "Nguwu Umwana wanje natoranije, ni mumwumve." "

42009039	kandi hari impwemu imufata, agatura akaborogo, ikamujegeza, akabimba ifuro, kandi ihejeje kumukungagura ikagora cane kumuvamwo."
42009040	Nanje ninginze abigishwa bawe kuyisenda, irabananira.

42009049	Yohana aramwishura ati: "Mwigisha, twabonye umuntu yirukana abadayimoni mw'izina ryawe, turamubuza, kuko atadukurikira."

42009052	atuma integuza imbere yiwe. Ziragenda, zija mu mihana y'Abasamariya kumuteguriza.

42010001	Mu nyuma y'ivyo, Umwami Yesu atoranya abandi mirongo irindwi, atuma babiribabiri, ngo babe baragenda mu gisagara vyose n'ahantu hose aho yagira ace.
42010002	Arababwira ati: "Ivyimburwa ni vyinshi, ariko abimbuzi ni bo bake. Nuko ni mwinginge nyene ivyimburwa, arungike abimbuzi mu vyimburwa vyiwe."
42010003	Ni mugende; raba ndabatumye muri nk'abana b'intama mu mabingira hagati.
42010004	Ntimujane umupfuko w'amahera, canke isaho, canke ibirato; kandi ntihagire n'uwo muramukanya mu nzira.
42010005	Inzu yose muzokwinjiramwo, muzobanze muvuge muti: "Amahoro abe muri iyi nzu."
42010006	Ni yaba irimwo umunyamahoro, amahoro yanyu azoba kuri we. Ni bitamera bityo, azobagarukako.
42010007	Kandi iyo nzu nyene muzoyigumemwo, murya munywa ivyo babahaye; kuko umukozi akwiye ingero yiwe. Ntimugende murararaguza.
42010008	Kandi igisagara cose mujamwo bakabakira, muzorye ivyo babahaye,
42010009	mukize abarwaye baho, mubabwire muti: 'Ubwami bw'Imana burabegereye.'
42010010	Ariko igisagara cose mujamwo ntibabakire, muzosohoke muje mu nzira zaco
42010011	muti: 'Ni umukungugu wo mu gisagara canyu, ufashe mu birenge vyacu, turawubakunkumuriye. Ariko mumenye iki, yuko ubwami bw'Imana buri hafi.'
42010012	Ndababwire, Kuri wa musi w'imanza, Sodomu hazogira agahengekezo kurusha nya gisagara.
42010013	Uzobona ibara, Korazini; uzobona ibara, Betsayida; kuko ibikomeye vyakorewe muri mwebwe iyo biba vyarakorewe muri Tiro n'i Sidoni, baba barihanye kera, bicaye bambaye amagunira, bisize umunyota.
42010014	Ariko muri Tiro n'i Sidoni hazogira agahengekezo ku musi w'imanza kurusha mwebwe.
42010015	Nawe, Kaperinawumu, mbega uzoshirwa hejuru, ushike kw'ijuru? Oya, uzocokezwa i kuzimu.
42010016	Uwubumviye ni jewe aba yumviye; uwubanse, ni jewe aba yanse; uwunyanse, aba yanse uwantumye.
42010017	Nuko bamwe mirongo irindwi bagarukana umunezero bati: "Mugenzi, abadayimoni na bo baratwumvira mw'izina ryawe."
42010018	Arababwira ati: "Nabonye Satani, avuye mw'ijuru, akoroka nk'umuravyo."
42010019	Ehe ndabahaye ububasha bwo gukandagira inzoka na sikorupiyo, n'ubwo kunesha ubushobozi bwa wa Mwansi bwose, kandi nta kintu kizogira ico kibagira na gatoya.
42010020	Ariko ntimunezerezwe n'uko izo mpwemu zibumvira, yamara munezerezwe n'uko amazina yanyu yanditswe mw'ijuru.
42010021	Uwo mwanya anezererwa cane muri Mpwemu Yera, aravuga ati: "Ndaguhimbaza Data, Mwami w'ijuru n'isi, kuko ivyo wabihishije abanyabwenge n'abahanga, ukabihishurira inzoya. Ego me Data, kuko washimye ko biba bityo imbere yawe.
42010022	Vyose nabihawe na Data; kandi nta wuzi Umwana uwo ari we, atari Data; na Data nta wumuzi uwo ari we atari Umwana, n'uwo Umwana agomba kumuhishurira."
42010023	Ahindukirira abigishwa, ababwira biherereye ati: "Harahiriwe amaso abona ivyo mubona.
42010024	Ndababwira yuko abavugishwa n'Imana benshi n'abami benshi bagomvye kubona ivyo mubona ntibabibona, no kwumva ivyo mwumva, ntibavyumva."
42010025	Maze umwe mu bigisha ivyagezwe ava hasi, aramugeza ati: "Mwigisha, nkore iki, ngo nzoragwe ubugingo budashira?"
42010026	Na we aramubaza ati: "Vyanditswe bite mu vyagezwe, kandi usoma iki?"
42010027	Aramwishura ati: "Mukundishe Uhoraho, Imana yanyu, imitima yanyu yose, n'ubugingo bwanyu bwose, n'inkomezi zanyu zose, n'ubwenge bwanyu bwose; kandi mukunde ababanyi banyu nk'uko mwikunda."
42010028	Aramubwira ati: "Wishuye neza, gira utyo, uzogira ubugingo."
42010029	Maze uwo agomvye kwiyerekana nk'uwugororotse, abaza Yesu ati: "Mbega umubanyi wanje ni nde?"
42010030	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Habaye umuntu yari avuye i Yerusalemu, ariko aramanuka aja i Yeriko, agwa mu bambuzi, baramukoba, baramukubita, barigira. Basiga asigaje gatoya agahwera."
42010031	Hariho n'umuherezi amanuka muri iyo nzira, amurengukako, amubonye aca i ruhande.
42010032	Kandi n'Umulewi ahashitse agira kuno, amubonye aca i ruhande.
42010033	Maze Umusamariya yari mu nzira ashika kuri we, amubonye amutera akagongwe.
42010034	Aramwegera, amupfuka inguma, amutimburisha amavuta ya elayo n'umuvinyu, amushira ku ndogoba yiwe, amujana mu ndaro y'abahita, aramurwaza.
42010035	Bukeye asokorora idenariyo zibiri, aziha nyene indaro ati: "Umurwaze, kandi ivyo uzotanga vyose birenze ivyo ni nagaruka nzobikwishura."
42010036	Muri abo batatu ugira ngo ni nde yabonetse ko ari umubanyi w'uwaguye mu bambuzi?
42010037	Aramwishura ati: "Ni uwamugiriye imbabazi." Yesu aramubarira ati: "Nawe genda ugire utyo."
42010038	Maze bariko baragenda bashika mu mihana. Umugore yitwa Marita aramwakira amushikiza mu nzu yiwe.
42010039	Uwo mugore yari afise mwene nyina yitwa Mariya, yicara imbere y'ibirenge vy'Umwami Yesu, yumva ijambo ryiwe.
42010040	Ariko Marita ahagarikira umutima kuzimana vyinshi; aramwegera, aramubwira ati: "Mugenzi, ntibikubabaje yuko mwene mama yantereranye ibikorwa?" Nuko mubarire amfashe.
42010041	Umwami Yesu aramwishura ati: "Marita, Marita, uriganyira wigora muri vyinshi.
42010042	Ariko igikwiye rwose ni kimwe; erega Mariya ahisemwo umugabane mwiza atazokwakwa."
42011001	Umusi umwe Yesu yari ahantu ariko arasenga. Ahejeje, umwe mu bigishwa biwe aramubwira ati: "Mugenzi, twigishe gusenga, nk'uko Yohana yigishije abigishwa biwe."
42011002	Arababarira ati: "Ni mwasenga, muvuge muti: 'Data, izina ryawe ni ryubahwe, ubwami bwawe ni buze;
42011003	imisi yose uduhe ivyo kurya bidukwiye.
42011004	Uduharire ivyaha vyacu, kuko natwe duhebera abari n'imyenda yacu bose; kandi ntutujane mu bitwosha nabi."
42011005	Arababwira ati: "Ni nde muri mwebwe afise umugenzi yoja i we mu gicugu, akamubwira ati: "Mugenzi wanje, ngurana udutsima dutatu,
42011006	kuko haje umugenzi wanje avuye ku rugendo, nanje ntagira ico ndamuzimana."
42011007	Uwo mu nzu yomwishura ati: "Sigaho kungora, namaze kwugara, kandi turi kumwe n'abana banje ku buriri, sinshoboye kuvyuka ngo ndayiguhe."
42011008	Ndababwire, Naho atovyurwa n'uko ari umugenzi wiwe ngo ayimuhe, ariko kuko atagize isoni zo kumugobera, aravyuka, akamuha ivyo agomba vyose.
42011009	Nanje ndababwire; Musabe muzohabwa; murondere muzoronka; muramutse muzokwugururirwa.
42011010	Kuko uwusaba wese ahabwa; uwurondera aronka; uwuramutsa yugururirwa.
42011011	Canke muri mwebwe hari umuvyeyi umwana wiwe yomusaba umutsima, akamuha ibuye; canke yomusaba ifi, akamuha inzoka;
42011012	canke yomusaba irigi, akamuha sikorupiyo?
42011013	None mwebwe, ko muzi guha abana banyu ingabire nziza muri babi, mbega So wo mw'ijuru ntazorushiriza rwose guha Mpwemu Yera abamumusavye?
42011014	Kandi yirukana mu muntu dayimoni itera uburagi. Iyo dayimoni imuvuyemwo, uno muntu w'ikiragi aravuga; ishengero riratangara.
42011015	Ariko bamwe muri bo baravuga bati: "Beyezebuli, umukuru w'abadayimoni, ni we amushoboza kwirukana abadayimoni."
42011016	Abandi bamuronderako ikimenyetso kiva mw'ijuru, bamugeza.
42011017	Na we amenye ivyo biyumvira, arababwira ati: "Ubwami bwose iyo bwitandukanije ubwabwo burahona, n'inzu, iyo yitandukanije, iragwa."
42011018	Na Satani, namba yitandukanije ubwiwe, ubwami bwiwe buzorama bute? Kuko muvuga yuko Beyezebuli ari we anshoboza kwirukana abadayimoni.
42011019	Ariko jewe namba Beyezebuli ari we anshoboza kwirukana abadayimoni, abana banyu bashobozwa na nde kubasenda? Ni co gituma ari bo bazobatsindisha.
42011020	Ariko urutoke rw'Imana ni rwaba ari rwo runshoboza kwirukana abadayimoni, noneho ubwami bw'Imana burabashikiriye. "
42011021	Umuntu w'inkomezi afise ibirwanisho iyo ateramiye urugo rwiwe, ibintu vyiwe biba amahoro;
42011022	ariko uwumurusha inkomezi iyo aramutse amuteye, akamunesha, amwaka ivyo arwanisha vyose yari yizigiye, akanyaga ibintu vyiwe, akabigaba.
42011023	Uwutamperereyeko aba ari umwansi wanje, kandi uwudafatanije nanje kwegeranya aba asanzaje.
42011024	Iyo impwemu ihumanye ivuye mu muntu, ica ahatagira amazi, irondera uburuhukiro, ikabubura, ikavuga iti: "Reka nsubire mu nzu yanje navuyemwo."
42011025	Ihashitse, igasanga ikubuye, iteguritse.
42011026	Igaca igenda, ikazana izindi mpwemu indwi ziyirusha ububi, zikinjira, zikahaba. Ivya nyuma vy'uwo muntu bikarusha ivya mbere ububi. "
42011027	Yesu akivugana n'Ishengero umugore umwe ashira ijwi hejuru aramubwira ati: "Irahiriwe inda yakuvyaye, n'amabere yakwonkeje."
42011028	Na we aramwishura ati: "Canecane hahiriwe abumva ijambo ry'Imana bakaribungabunga."
42011029	Ishengero rimaze kugwirirana atangura kubabwira ati: "Abo iki gihe ni abantu babi; barondera ikimenyetso, ariko nta kimenyetso bazohabwa, atari ikimenyetso ca Yona."
42011030	Nk'uko Yona yabaye ikimenyetso ku Banyaninewe, ni ko Umwana w'umuntu azoba ku b'iki gihe.
42011031	Umwamikazi w'igihugu c'i Sheba. Azovana hasi n'abagabo b'iki gihe ku musi w'imanza, azobatsindisha; kuko yavanywe ku mpera y'isi no kwumva ubwenge bwa Salomo; kandi raba, uwuruta Salomo ari hano.
42011032	Abagabo b'i Ninewe bazovana hasi n'abo iki gihe ku musi w'imanza, babatsindishe; kuko bihanye aho bumviye ubutumwa buvuzwe na Yona; kandi raba, uwuruta Yona ari hano.
42011033	Nta wodomeka itara ngo arishire mu mwobo, canke ngo aryubikeko igiseke, ariko arishira ku gitereko caryo, ngo abinjira basange habona.
42011034	Itara ry'umubiri wawe n'ijisho ryawe. Ijisho ryawe iyo ari ryiza, umubiri wawe wose uba uri n'umuco; ariko iyo rirwaye, umubiri wawe uba uri n'umwiza.
42011035	Nuko rero ugabe umuco uri muri wewe ntube umwiza.
42011036	Kandi umubiri wawe wose ni waba uri n'umuco, ata gice na kimwe gifise umwiza, wose uzoba uri n'umuco, nk'uko ukwaka kw'itara kukuboneshereza.
42011037	Akibivuga, Umufarisayo aramuhamagara ngo amuzimane. Arinjira, aricara ngo arye.
42011038	Wa Mufarisayo abonye atabanje gukaraba atararya biramutangaza.
42011039	Umwami Yesu aramubwira ati: "Erega mwebwe Abafarisayo mwoza inyuma y'igikombe n'inkoko, ariko imbere muri mwebwe mwuzuye ubwambuzi n'ububi."
42011040	Mwa bijuju mwe, iyaremye urukoba si yo yaremye n'imbere?
42011041	Ariko Muzotange ibiri imbere mu gikombe no mu nkoko mubitangishijwe n'ubuntu, kandi umve, vyose bizobabera ibiziruwe.
42011042	Ariko muzobona ibara, Bafarisayo, kuko mutanga icacumi c'imbwija, ico isogi n'ico imboga zose, ariko ubutungane n'ugukunda Imana mukavyirengagiza. Ivyo mwari mukwiye kubikora, vya bindi na vyo ntimubireke.
42011043	Muzobona ibara, Bafarisayo, kuko mukunda intebe z'icubahiro mu nsengero, no kugirwako bwakeye mu kibanza c'amakoraniro.
42011044	Muzobona ibara, kuko musa n'imva zitamenyekana, abantu bakazicako batabizi.
42011045	Umwe mu bigisha ivyagezwe aramwishura ati: "Mwigisha, ko uvuze utyo, natwe uradututse."
42011046	Na we ati: "Namwe abigisha ivyagezwe muzobona ibara, kuko mwikoreza abantu imitwaro itokwikorerwa, namwe ubwanyu iyo mitwaro ntimuyikozeko urutoke na rumwe."
42011047	Muzobona ibara, kuko mwubakira imva z'abavugishwa n'Imana, ba sogokuruza banyu ari bo babishe.
42011048	Uko ni ko mwiyagirije, kandi mwemeye ivyo ba sogokuruza banyu bakoze, kuko ari bo babishe, namwe mububakira imva.
42011049	Ni co catumye Imana ivugisha ubwenge bwayo iti: "Nzobatumako abo mvugisha n'intumwa, bamwe muri bo bazobica, abandi bazobahama,
42011050	ngo amaraso y'abavugishwa n' Imana bose yavishijwe, uhereye ku kuremwa kw'isi, aronderwe ku b'iki gihe,
42011051	uhereye ku maraso ya Abeli, ukageza ku maraso ya Zakariya yiciwe hagati y'igicaniro n'ahera h'urusengero: ni koko, ndababwire, azoronderwa ku b'iki gihe."
42011052	Muzobona ibara, abigisha ivyagezwe, kuko mwatwaye urupfunguruzo rw'ubwenge; ntimwinjiye ubwanyu, n'abagomba kwinjira mwarababujije.
42011053	Maze asohotse, abahinga b'ivyanditswe n'Abafarisayo batangura kumusugereza no kumwiyandagazako ngo bamuvugishe vyinshi,
42011054	bamutega ngo bafate ijambo bokwumva avuga ngo bamurege.
42012001	Muri ico gihe, ishengero ry'abantu ibihumbi vyinshi rikoranira kuri we, bakandagirana, ahera ku bigishwa biwe, arababarira ati: ""Mwirinde umwambiro w'Abafarisayo, ni wo buryarya."
42012002	Nta catwikiriwe kitazotwikururwa, canke icanyegejwe kitazomenyekana.
42012003	Nuko ivyo mwavugiye mu mwiza vyose bizokwumvikanira mu muco, n'ico mwongoreraniye mu mazu haruguru kizovugirwa ku mazu hejuru.
42012004	Kandi ndabwira mwebwe abakunzi banje; Ntimugatinye abica umubiri, hanyuma batagira ikindi bazobagira.
42012005	Ariko ndabereka iyo mukwiye gutinya; mutinye Iyiheza kwica umuntu, ikagira ububasha bwo kumukororera muri Gehinomu. Ni koko, ndababwire, ni mube ari yo mutinya.
42012006	Mbega utunyoni dutanu ntitugurwa amakuta abiri? Ariko kamwe muri two ntikibagirwa imbere y'Imana.
42012007	Ariko n'umushatsi wo ku mitwe yanyu wose waraharuwe. Ntimutinye; muruta utunyoni twinshi. "
42012008	Kandi ndababwire; Umuntu wese azonyaturira imbere y'abantu, Umwana w'umuntu azomwaturira imbere y'abamarayika b'Imana.
42012009	Ariko uwunyihakanira imbere y'abantu, azokwihakanirwa imbere y'abamarayika b'Imana.
42012010	Kandi umuntu wese azodedemba ku Mwana w'umuntu, azobiharirwa; ariko uwuzodedemba kuri Mpwemu Yera ntazobiharirwa.
42012011	Kandi ni babajana mu nsengero z'Abayuda bakabashira abakuru n'abaganza, ntimuzohagarikishwe imitima n'ico muzokwireguza n'ingene muzokwiregura canke n'ico muvuga.
42012012	Kuko muri ako kanya nyene, Mpwemu Yera ababwiriza ivyo mukwiye kuvuga.
42012013	Maze umuntu wo mw'ishengero ryari rikoraniye aho aramubwira ati: "Mwigisha, mbaririra mwene mama tugabure umwandu."
42012014	Aramubaza ati: "Mbega wa mugabo, ni nde yanshizeho kuba umucamanza wanyu, canke kubagaburira ivyanyu?"
42012015	Kandi arababarira ati: "Murumva, mwirinde ukwifuza kwose, kuko ubugingo bw'umuntu butava mu bihinda vy'ibintu atunze."
42012016	Kandi abacira umugani ati: "Habaye umuntu w'umutunzi yarafise itongo rimera cane."
42012017	Yiyumvira mu mutima wiwe ati: "Ndagira nte, ko ntagira aho nimburira imirima yanje?"
42012018	Ati: "Ndabigenza gutya: ndasambura ibigega vyanje, nubake ibindi bininibinini, abe ari ho nimburira imirima yanje yose n'ibintu vyanje vyose."
42012019	Mpeze mbwire umutima wanje nti: "Mutima, ufise ibintu vyinshi bizohitira imyaka myinshi, ruhuka, urye, unywe, unezerwe."
42012020	Maze Imana iramubwira iti: "Wa gipfu we muri iri joro barakwaka ubugingo bwawe; none ivyo woziganije bizoba ivya nde?"
42012021	Umuntu yishingurira ni ko amera, atari umutunzi mu vy'Imana.
42012022	Abwira abigishwa biwe ati: "Ni co gitumye ndababarira nti: 'Ntimukaganyire amagara yanyu ku vyo muzorya, canke umubiri wanyu ku vyo muzokwambara.'
42012023	Kuko amagara aruta ivyo kurya, n'umubiri uruta imyambaro.
42012024	Ni mwitegereze ibikona, ingene bitabiba, ntibishwabure, ntibigire ububiko canke ikigega, kandi Imana irabitunga. Erega mwebwe muruta ibisiga cane.
42012025	Ni nde muri mwebwe ku bwo amaganya yiwe yoshobora kwiyongerako n'akangana n'ukuboko kumwe?
42012026	Nuko ko mudashobora gukora gito rwose ni iki gituma mwiganyira ibindi?
42012027	Ni mwitegereze amashurwe, ingene akura; ntiyirirwa araruha, ntajisha impuzu; ariko ndababwire na Salomo mu bwiza bwiwe bwose ntiyari ashajije nka rimwe muri ayo.
42012028	None Imana ko yambika ivyatsi vyo ku misozi ityo, biriho uwu musi, ariko nk'ejo bigatererwa mu ziko, mbega ntizorushiriza kubambika, mwebwe abo ukwizera guke mwe?
42012029	Kandi ntimukitwaririke ivyo murya n'ivyo munywa, ntimukiganyire.
42012030	Kuko ivyo vyose abanyamahanga bo mw'isi ari vyo bitwaririka, ariko So arazi ko mubikena ivyo.
42012031	Ariko mwitwaririke ubwami bwiwe, ni ho ivyo muzovyongerwa.
42012032	Yemwe mwa busho buto, ntimutinye; kuko So bimuhimbara kubaha ubwami.
42012033	Mugurishe ivyo mufise, Muzotange ibiguzi vyavyo ku bwo ubuntu; mwibaririre imipfuko idashira, ubutunzi budashira buri mw'ijuru, ahategerwa n'igisuma, ata n'inyenzi zonona;
42012034	kuko aho ubutunzi bwanyu buri ari ho imitima yanyu izoba.
42012035	Mwame mukenyeye, kandi amatara yanyu yame yaka.
42012036	Ni mube nk'abantu barorereye shebuja, igihe agarukira ava mu bukwe, ngo ni yaza, akaramutsa, bace bamwugururira.
42012037	Harahiriwe abo bashumba, abo shebuja azoza agasanga bari maso. Ndababwire ukuri; azokenyera, abicarike, aze, abagaburire.
42012038	Ni yaza mu gicugu canke mu nkoko, akabasanga atyo, bazoba abahirwe.
42012039	Kandi mumenye iki, yuko iyaba nyene urugo yari asanzwe azi igihe igisuma kiziramwo, yogavye, ntiyokunze ko inzu yiwe yimbwa.
42012040	Namwe mwame mwiteguye, kuko Umwana w'umuntu azoza mu gihe mutiyumviriye.
42012041	Petero aramubaza ati: "Mbega Mugenzi, uwo mugani ni twebwe twenyene uwuciriye, canke uwuciriye n'abandi bose?"
42012042	Umwami Yesu na we aramubaza ati: "Ni nde munyabigega wo kwizigirwa w'ubwenge, shebuja yosigarana abo mu rugo rwiwe, ngo abagaburire ku ngero yabo igihe kigeze?"
42012043	Harahiriwe uwo mushumba shebuja agarutse azosanga akora atyo.
42012044	Ndababwira ukuri yuko azomuha kugaba ivyo afise vyose.
42012045	Ariko uwo mushumba ni yibwira mu mutima wiwe ati: "Databuja aracatevye kuza; maze agatangura gukubita abashumba n'incoreke, akaja mu vyo kwirira no kwinywera akaborerwa,
42012046	shebuja w'uwo mushumba azoza ku musi atamwiteze, no mu gihe atazi, azomuhana vy'akarorero, amusangize umugabane wiwe n'abatizera.
42012047	Kandi uwo mushumba yari azi ivyo shebuja agomba, ntiyitegure, ntakore ivyo agomba, azokubitwa nyinshi.
42012048	Ariko uwutari abizi, agakora ibikwiye kumukubitisha, azokubitwa nkeya. Uwahawe vyinshi wese azobazwa vyinshi; uwabikijwe vyinshi ni we bazorushiriza kwaka vyinshi.
42012049	Naje guta umuriro mw'isi, none iyaba wari umaze gufatwa, nta kindi mba nkigomba?
42012050	Hariho umubatizo nkwiye kubatizwa. Umubabaro mfise mu mutima ntuzohera ntarawubatizwa.
42012051	Mbega mwiyumvira ko naje kuzana amahoro mw'isi?
42012052	Ndababwire, si ko biri, ariko naje kubaryanisha. Kuko uhereye ubu, ahazoba batanu mu nzu imwe bazokwicamwo ibice, batatu barwanye babiri na babiri barwanye batatu.
42012053	Umwana azotandukana na se, na se n'umwana ni uko; umukobwa azotandukana na nyina, na nyina n'umukobwa ni uko; inabukwe azotandukana n'umukazana wiwe, n'umukazana na inabukwe ni uko.
42012054	Kandi abwira ishengero ati: "Iyo mubonye igicu kivuye mu burengero, muca mugira ngo imvura iraguye; kandi ni ko biba."
42012055	Iyo mubonye umuyaga uturutse mu bumanuko mugira ngo Haraba indugumba, kandi ni ko biba.
42012056	Mwa ndyarya mwe, murazi kugenzura isi n'ijuru, ni iki kibabuza kugendeza iki gihe?
42012057	Kandi namwe ubwanyu ni iki kibabuza kugenzura ivyo kugororoka?
42012058	Ni wajana n'uwukurega muja ku mushingantahe, mukiri mu nzira ushishikare kuringaniza na we, ngo ntagukwegere ku mucamanza, umucamanza akaguha umusoda, akagushira mw'ibohero.
42012059	Ndakubwire, Ntuzohava na gatoya, utishuye n'ihera rya nyuma.
42013001	Ico gihe abantu bari aho bamwiganira ivyo Abanyagalilaya Pilato yishe akavanga amaraso yabo n'ayo ibitungwa bariko barashikana.
42013002	Arababaza ati: "Mbega mwiyumvira yuko abo Banyagalilaya barusha abandi Banyagalilaya kuba abanyavyaha, kuko bagizwe batyo?"
42013003	Ndababwire, si ko biri; ariko ni mutihana, namwe muzohona mutyo mwese.
42013004	Canke ba bandi icumi n'umunani, bamwe umunara muremure w'amatafari w'i Silowamu wahomvokeyeko, ukabica, mwiyumvira yuko barusha abandi b'i Yerusalemu bose kuba abanyabicumuro?
42013005	Oya na mba! Si ko biri. Na mwebwe ni mutihana muzohona mutyo mwese.

42024032	Baravugana bati: "Mbega imitima yacu ntiyari iriko irasimbagurika, aho yariko aravugana natwe mu nzira, aduhishurira ivyanditswe!"

42024034	kandi bavuga bati: "Ni ukuri Umwami Yesu yazutse, kandi yabonywe na Simoni."
42024035	Na bo babadondera vya bindi vyo mu nzira, kandi yuko bamumenyeshejwe n'uko yamanyaguye umutsima.

42024037	Ariko bafatwa n'ubwoba bacika ivutu, bagira ngo n'umuzimu babonye.

42024039	Ni murabe ibiganza vyanje n'ibirenge vyanje, mumenye ko ari jewe ubwanje. Ni munkorakore, murabe, kuko umuzimu utagira inyama n'amagufa, nk'ivyo mumbonana.
42024040	Avuze ivyo, abereka ibiganza vyiwe n'ibirenge.

42024042	Bamuha igice c'ifi yokeje,
42024043	aracakira, akirira imbere yabo.

42024045	Maze abungura ubwenge ngo batahure ivyanditswe.

43001001	Mu ntango Jambo yariho, kandi Jambo yahoranye n'Imana, kandi uwo Jambo yari Imana.

43001003	vyose vyaremwe na we, mu vyaremwe vyose nta kintu na kimwe kitaremwe na we.

43001015	Yohana amushingira intahe, arasemerera ati: "Uwo ni we navuze ko uwuza inyuma yanje ni we yari uwa mbere kuri jewe, kuko yariho ntarabaho." "

43001028	Ivyo vyabereye i Betaniya, hakurya ya Yorodani aho Yohana yabatiriza.

43004038	Nabatumye kwimbura ibitabatamije; abandi baratamye, namwe mwashikiye mu vy'ubutame bwabo.
43004039	Benshi mu Basamariya bo muri ico gisagara bamwizera ku bwo amajambo ya wa mugore, yavuze ashinga intahe ati: "Ambariye ivyo nakoze vyose."
43004040	Maze Abasamariya baje aho ari, baramwinginga ngo agume i wabo; asibirayo kabiri.
43004041	Hizera abandi benshi baruta aba mbere, kuko biyumviye ijambo ryiwe;
43004042	maze babwira uwo mugore bati: "Ubu ho ntitwizeye ku bwo amajambo yawe gusa, kuko natwe twiyumviye kandi tumenye ko uwu ari Umukiza w'isi vy'ukuri."
43004043	Iyo misi ibiri ishize, avayo aja i Galilaya.
43004044	Kandi Yesu ubwiwe yashinze intahe yuko umuntu avugishwa n'Imana atagira icubahiro mu ntara y'i wabo.
43004045	Ashitse i Galilaya, Abanyagalilaya baramwakira, kuko babonye ivyo yakoreye i Yerusalemu vyose muri ya misi mikuru, kuko na bo bari bagiyeyo mu misi mikuru.
43004046	Maze asubira kuja i Kana i Galilaya, hamwe yahindurira amazi agacika umuvinyu. Hari umutware atwarira umwami, umwana wiwe w'umuhungu yari arwariye i Kaperinawumu;
43004047	uwo yumvise ko Yesu avuye i Yudaya ashitse i Galilaya, aza kuri we, aramwinginga ngo amanuke gukiza umwana wiwe, kuko yari ku mpfiro.
43004048	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Iyo mutabonye ibimenyetso n'ibitangaza nta ho mwizera na mba."
43004049	Uwo mutware ati: "Mugenzi, ngwino se umanuke umwana wanje atarapfa."
43004050	Yesu aramubarira ati: "Ni wigire, umwana wawe ni muzima." Uwo muntu yizera ijambo Yesu amubwiye, aragenda.
43004051	Ariko aramanuka abantu biwe baramusanganira bati: "Umwana wawe ni muzima."
43004052	Abasiguza cane igihe yatanguye kworoherwa. Baramubwira bati: "Ejo, kw'isaha indwi, ni ho umururumbo wamuvuyeko."
43004053	Maze se aca amenya ko hari muri nya saha nyene Yesu yamubwiriyemwo ati: "Umwana wawe ni muzima." Arizera ubwiwe n'abo mu rugo rwiwe bose.
43004054	Ico ni co kimenyetso ca kabiri Yesu yakoze, avuye i Yudaya ashitse i Galilaya.
43005001	Hanyuma y'ivyo haba imisi mikuru y'Abayuda; Yesu aduga i Yerusalemu.
43005002	Kandi i Yerusalemu hafi y'irembo ry'intama, hari ikidengeri, mu Giheburayo citwa Betesida, cariko amabaraza atanu.
43005003	Muri yo hari haryamye abantu benshi barwaye, n'impumyi, n'abacumbagira, n'abanyunyutse. [Bari barorereye ko amazi azikuruka.
43005004	Kuko rimwerimwe umumarayika yamanuka aja muri kino kidengeri, akazikurura amazi. Maze uwitangiye gutambukiramwo, amazi azikurutse, ni we yakira indwara yamufashe iyo ari yo yose. ]
43005005	Hariho umuntu yarafise indwara ayimaranye imyaka mirongo itatu n'umunani.
43005006	Yesu amubonye aryamyeho, kandi amenye ko amaze igihe kirekire, aramubaza ati: "Wumva ugomba gukira?"
43005007	Uno arwaye aramwishura ati: "Mugenzi, nta muntu mfise wo kunyinikira mu kidengeri iyo amazi azikurutse; kuko ngira ngo ndaza uwundi akantanga gushungurukiramwo."
43005008	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Va hasi, ikorere ikirago cawe, ugende."
43005009	Buno nyene uwo muntu arakira, yikorera ikirago ciwe, aragenda. Ariko uwo musi hari kw'isabato.
43005010	Nuko Abayuda babwira uwakijijwe bati: "Erega ni kw'isabato, ntivyemerwa ko wikorera ikirago cawe."
43005011	Na we arabishura ati: "Uwankijije ni we yambariye ati: 'Ikorere ikirago cawe, ugende.'"
43005012	Baramubaza bati: "Uwo muntu ni nde yakubariye ngo ikorere ugende?" "
43005013	Ariko uwakijijwe ntiyari azi uwo ari we, kuko Yesu yaciye yigira, kuko aho hantu hari abantu benshi.
43005014	Hanyuma y'ivyo Yesu amubona mu rusengero, aramubwira ati: " "Raba wakize; ntugasubire gukora icaha, kugira ngo ntuzobone ibiruta ivya mbere."
43005015	Uno muntu aragenda, abwira Abayuda ko ari Yesu yamukijije.
43005016	Ni co catumye Abayuda bahama Yesu, kuko yakoze ivyo kw'isabato.
43005017	Yesu arababwira ati: "Data arakora kugeza n'ubu, nanje ndakora."
43005018	Ni co catumye Abayuda barushiriza kurondera ingene bomwica, kuko atakengereye isabato gusa, ariko agatako akita Imana ko ari Se bwite, akiringaniza n'Imana.
43005019	Nuko Yesu asubira kubabwira ati: "Ni ukuri, ni ukuri ndababwire. Nta co Umwana ashobora kwigenera, atabonye Se agikora, kuko ivyo Se akora vyose n'Umwana aca abikora kuno.
43005020	Kuko Se akunda Umwana, akamwereka ivyo akora vyose ubwiwe, kandi azomwereka ibikorwa biruta ivyo, kugira ngo mwebwe mutangare.
43005021	Nk'uko Se azura abapfuye akabaha ubugingo, ni ko n'Umwana aha ubugingo abo agomba.
43005022	Kuko Se ata n'umwe acira urubanza, ariko imanza zose yazishikirije Umwana,
43005023	ngo bose bubahe Umwana nk'uko bubaha Se; uwutubaha Umwana ntaba yubaha Se yamutumye."
43005024	Ni ukuri ndakubwire koko, Uwumva ijambo ryanje, akizera uwantumye, ni we afise ubugingo budashira, kandi ntazoshirwa mu rubanza, ariko aba avuye mu rupfu, ashitse mu bugingo.
43005025	Ni ukuri ndakubwire koko. Igihe kiza, kandi kirashitse, aho abapfuye bazokwumvira ijwi ry'Umwana w'Imana, kandi abazoryumva bazoba bazima.
43005026	Nk'uko Se ari n'ubugingo muri we, ni ko yahaye Umwana kugira ubugingo muri we na we.
43005027	Yamuhaye ububasha bwo guca imanza, kuko ari Umwana w'umuntu.
43005028	Ntimutangazwe n'ico; kuko igihe kija kuza, aho abari mu mva bose bazokwumvira ijwi ryiwe,
43005029	bakazivamwo; abakoze ivyiza bakazukira ubugingo, abakoze ibibi bakazukira gutsindwa n'urubanza.
43005030	Nta co nshobora gukora nigeneye; uko numvise ni ko nca urubanza, kandi urubanza nca rurabereye, kuko ntarondera ivyo nigombera, ariko ndondera ivyo uwantumye agomba.
43005031	Asangwa nishingira intahe, intahe yanje ntizoba ari iyo ukuri;
43005032	ariko hari Uwundi anshingira intahe, nanje nzi yuko intahe yiwe anshingira ari iyo ukuri.
43005033	Mwebwe mwatumye kuri Yohana, ashingira ukuri intahe,
43005034	mugabo jewe sindinda gushingirwa intahe n'umuntu; ariko ico mvugiye ivyo ni ukugira ngo mukizwe.
43005035	Uwo yari itara ryaka rikabonesha, kandi namwe mwamaze igihe muhimbawe n'ukwaka kwiwe.
43005036	Ariko jewe mfise ikinshingira intahe kuruta Yohana, kuko ibikorwa Data yampaye ngo ndabiheraheze, ivyo bikorwa nyene nkora ni vyo binshingira intahe yuko Data ari we yantumye.
43005037	Kandi Data yantumye ni we anshingira intahe. Nta ho murumva ijwi ryiwe, kandi ntimurabona ishusho yiwe,
43005038	bitayeko ntimufise ijambo ryiwe riguma muri mwebwe, kuko uwo yatumye mutamwizeye.
43005039	Mwebwe murasoma mwitonze mu vyanditswe, kuko mugira ngo muri vyo ni ho mufise ubugingo budashira, kandi ari vyo binshingira intahe,
43005040	ariko mukanka kuza kuri jewe ngo muronke ubugingo.
43005041	Singomba gushimwa n'abantu,
43005042	ariko mwebwe ndabazi yuko mutagira urukundo rw'Imana mu mitima yanyu.
43005043	Jewe naje mw'izina rya Data, ntimwanyakira, ni hagira uwundi aza mw'izina ryiwe ubwiwe, we muzomwakira.
43005044	Mwoshobora kwizera mute, ari mwebwe mwubahana, ariko icubahiro kiva ku Mana imwe nsa mutakirondera?
43005045	Ntimugire ngo nzobarega kuri Data; hariho uwubarega, ni Mose uwo mwishimiye.
43005046	Iyo mwizera Mose, nanje muba munyizeye, kuko ari ivyanje yanditse.
43005047	Ariko ni mutizera ivyo uwo yanditse, amajambo yanje muzoyizera mute?
43006001	Hanyuma y'ivyo Yesu avayo, yigira hakurya y'ikiyaga c'i Galilaya citwa Tiberiya.
43006002	Ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira kuko ribonye ibimenyetso akora ku barwaye.
43006003	Yesu aduga umusozi, yicaranayo n'abigishwa biwe.
43006004	Kandi imisi mikuru ya Pasika y'Abayuda yari hafi.
43006005	Yesu yunamutse, abona ishengero ryinshi riza kuri we, abaza Filipo ati: "Tugurira hehe imitsima, ngo barye bose?"
43006006	Icatumye avuga atyo kwari ukumugeza, kuko ubwiwe yari azi ico agira akore.

43006011	Maze Yesu yakira ya mitsima, arayihezagira, ayigaburira abicaye, n'ifi na zo nk'uko bagomba.
43006012	Bamaze guhaga, abwira abigishwa biwe ati: "Ni mwegeranye utumanyagu tw'imisigazwa, ntihagire igipfa ubusa."
43006013	Baratwegeranya, buzuza ibiseke icumi na bibiri vy'utumanyagu twa ya mitsima itanu ya sayiri, utwo abariye bashigaje.

43006020	Maze arababwira ati: "Ni jewe, nta co mutinya." "

43006023	(mugabo hari amato ajabuka ava i Tiberiya, afata hafi ya ha hantu baririye imitsima ihezagiwe n'Umwami Yesu).

43006025	Bamubonye hakurya y'ikiyaga baramubaza bati: "Mwigisha, waje ino ryari?"
43006026	Yesu arabishura ati: "Ni ukuri ni ukuri ndababwire. Ntimundondera kuko mwabonye ibimenyetso, ariko ni uko mwariye kuri ya mitsima, mugahaga.
43006027	Ntimukorere ivyo kurya biyoka, ariko mukorere ivyo kurya bihoraho bizana ubugingo budashira, ni vyo Umwana w'umuntu azobaha, kuko ari we Imana Data yashizeko ikimenyetso.
43006028	Baramubaza bati: "Tugire dute ngo dukore ibikorwa vy'Imana?"

43006030	Nuko baramubaza bati: "None ukora ikimenyetso ki, ngo tukirabe tukwizere? Ukora ikimeze gite?

43006032	Yesu arababwira ati: "Ni ukuri ni ukuri ndababwire; Si Mose yabahaye umutsima uvuye mw'ijuru; Data ni we abaha umutsima w'ukuri uvuye mw'ijuru.

43006036	Ariko narababwiye yuko mwambonye, muraheza ntimwizera.

43006044	Nta n'umwe ashobora kuza kuri jewe Data yantumye atamukwegakweze; nanje nzomuzura ku musi w'iherezo."
43006045	Mu majambo y'abavugishwa n'Imana handitswe ko bose bazoba abigishijwe n'Imana. Uwumvise ivya Data wese akavyiga, aza kuri jewe.

43006047	Ni ukuri ndakubwire koko; Uwizera afise ubugingo budashira.

43006051	Ni jewe mutsima w'ubugingo wamanutse uvuye mw'ijuru; ni hagira uwurya kuri uwo mutsima azohoraho ibihe bidashira, kandi umutsima nzobaha n'umubiri wanje, utangirwa abari mw'isi ngo bagire ubugingo.
43006052	Abayuda batanako ibirake bati: "Uwu ashobora ate kuduha umubiri wiwe ngo tuwurye?"
43006053	Yesu arababwira ati: "Ni ukuri ni ukuri ndababwire; Ni mutarya umubiri w'Umwana w'umuntu, ngo munywe amaraso yiwe, nta bugingo mwogira muri mwebwe."
43006054	Uwurya umubiri wanje akanywa amaraso yanje, ni we afise ubugingo budashira, nanje nzomuzura ku musi w'iherezo.
43006055	Kuko umubiri wanje ari ico kurya c'ukuri, n'amaraso yanje ari ico kunywa c'ukuri.
43006056	Uwurya umubiri wanje akanywa amaraso yanje, aguma muri jewe, nanje nkaguma muri we.

43007019	Mbega Mose si we yabahaye ivyagezwe? Ariko muri mwebwe nta n'umwe yitondera ivyo vyagezwe. Muronderera iki kunyica?"

43007023	None se, ko umuntu ahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo kw'isabato, kugira ngo icagezwe ca Mose ntimukirenge, none jewe mumpora iki ko kw'isabato nakijije umuntu akwiye?

43007029	jeho ndamuzi, kuko navuye kuri we, kandi ari we yantumye."
43007030	Buno barondera ingene bomufata, ariko ntihagira uwumukozako n'intoke, kuko igihe ciwe kitaribwagere.

43007032	Abafarisayo bumvise ko ishengero rimuvugavuganako ivyo mu twongoshwe, abaherezi bakuru n'Abafarisayo batuma abagendanyi kumufata.

43007034	Muzondondera, ariko ntimuzombona, kandi iyo nzoba ndi ntimuzoshobora gushikayo."
43007035	Maze Abayuda baravugana bati: "Mbega uwo agira aje hehe, aho twebwe tutazoshobora kumubona? Agira aje mu basabagiriye mu Bagiriki, ngo azokwigishe Abagiriki?
43007036	Mbega iryo jambo atubwiye ni iriki, ngo Muzondondera, ariko ntimuzombona, kandi ngo iyo nzoba ndi mwebwe ntimuzoshobora gushikayo?"

43008044	Mwebwe muri aba so wa mugarariji, kandi ivyo so yifuza ni vyo mushaka gukora. Uwo yahereye mu ntango ari umwicanyi, kandi ntiyahagaze mu kuri, kuko ata kuri kuri muri we. Iyo avuga ibinyoma, avuga ivyiwe, kuko ari umunyabinyoma, kandi ari we se wavyo.

43009001	Ariko arahita, abona umuntu yavutse ari impumyi.

43010001	Ni ukuri ni ukuri ndababwire, uwudaca mw'irembo ry'urugo rw'intama, ariko akuririra ahandi, uwo aba ari igisuma n'umwambuzi.
43010002	Ariko uwuca mw'irembo ni we mwungere w'intama.
43010003	Umurarizi w'irembo aramwugururira, kandi intama zumva ijwi ryiwe; ahamagara intama ziwe mu mazina yazo, akaziturutsa.
43010004	Kandi iyo amaze guturutsa iziwe zose, azija imbere, zikamukurikira kuko zizi ijwi ryiwe.
43010005	Ariko uwo zitazi ntizomukurikira na mba, zomuhunga, kuko zitazi amajwi y'abandi.
43010006	Yesu abacira uwo mugani, ariko bo ntibatahura ivyo ababwira ivyo ari vyo.
43010007	Nuko Yesu yongera kubabwira ati: "Ni ukuri ni ukuri ndababwire, ni jewe rembo ry'intama."
43010008	Abanyitangiye imbere bose bari ibisuma n'abambuzi, ariko intama ntizabumviye.
43010009	Ni jewe rembo, kandi uwushika mu rugo wese aciye muri jewe arakizwa; agataha, agaturuka, akaronka ubwatsi butotahaye.
43010010	Igisuma ntikizanwa n'ikindi, atari ukwiba, ukwica n'ugutikiza; nayo jeho nazanywe no kugira ngo zironke ubugingo, kandi ngo ziburonke busagutse.
43010011	Ni jewe mwungere mwiza; umwungere mwiza yigura intama ziwe.
43010012	Ariko umucangero, atari umwungere bwite, n'intama ntizibe iziwe, iyo abonye ibingira rije, ata intama, agahunga, ibingira rikazisahura, rikazishwiragiza.
43010013	Arahunga, kuko ari umucangero, atababaye intama.
43010014	Ni jewe mwungere mwiza, ndazi izanje, n'izanje ziranzi,
43010015	nk'uko Data anzi, nanje nkamumenya; kandi ndigura intama zanje.
43010016	Kandi mfise n'izindi ntama zitari izo muri uru rugo, na zo nyene birankwiye kuzija imbere, zizokwumva ijwi ryanje, hazoba umukuku umwe n'umwungere umwe.
43010017	Igituma Data ankunda, ni uko ndekura ubugingo bwanje, ngo mpeze nsubire kubwakira.
43010018	Nta n'umwe abunyaka, kuko ndaburekura kubwanje; mfise ububasha bwo kuburekura, mfise n'ububasha bwo gusubira kubwakira. Ico ni co cagezwe nahawe na Data."
43010019	Abayuda bongera kumupfa kubwo ayo majambo,

43010029	Data yabampaye ni we aruta bose; nta wushobora kubashikura mu kuboko kwa Data.
43010030	Jewe na Data turi umwe."
43010031	Buno Abayuda bongera gutora amabuye, ngo bayamutere.

43010034	Yesu arabishura ati: "Mbega ntihanditswe mu vyagezwe vyanyu, ko navuze nko muri imana?"
43010035	None ko yabise imana, bamwe ijambo ry'Imana ryashitseko (kandi ivyanditswe ntibishobora guhinduka),

43010039	Nuko bongera kurondera ingene bomufata, abava mu maboko.
43010040	Avayo, yongera kuja hakurya ya Yorodani, ha hantu Yohana yabatiriza ubwa mbere, agumayo.
43010041	Benshi baza kuri we; baravuga bati: "Yohana nta kimenyetso yakoze, ariko ivyo Yohana yavuze vyose kuri uwo vyari ivyo ukuri."
43010042	Kandi benshi bamwizererayo.
43011001	Hariho uwari arwaye, ni Lazaro w'i Betaniya, ni wa musozi Mariya na mwene nyina Marita babako.
43011002	Uwo Mariya ni we yasize Umwami Yesu amavuta amota cane ku birenge, amuhanaguza umushatsi wiwe; uwo Lazaro yari arwaye ni we musaza we.
43011003	Bashiki biwe batuma kuri Yesu bati: "Mugenzi, wa wundi ukunda ararwaye."
43011004	Yesu avyumvise aravuga ati: "Iyo ndwara si iyo kumwica, ariko ni iyo gutuma bashimagiza Imana, kugira ngo n'Umwana w'Imana itume ashemagizwa."
43011005	Kandi Yesu yarakunda Marita na mwene nyina na Lazaro.

43011007	Hanyuma y'ivyo abwira abigishwa biwe ati: "Dusubire i Yudaya."
43011008	Abigishwa baramubwira bati: "Mwigisha, Abayuda baheruka gushaka kugutera amabuye, none usubireyo?"
43011009	Yesu arabishura ati: "None isaha z'umurango si icumi na zibiri? Uwugenda ku murango ntatsitara, kuko abona umuco w'iyi si.
43011010	Ariko uwugenda mw'ijoro aratsitara, kuko umuco utari muri we."
43011011	Amaze kuvuga ivyo, arababwira ati: "Lazaro, umukunzi wacu, arasinziriye, nanje ndagiye kumukangura."

43011019	Nuko Abayuda benshi bari baje kwa Marita na Mariya ku bagarukirako kuko musaza wabo yapfuye.

43011028	Avuze ivyo, asubira inyuma, yongorera Mariya, mwene nyina ati: "Umwigisha ari hano, araguhamagaje."

43011032	Mariya ashitse aho Yesu ari, amubonye, yikubita imbere y'ibirenge vyiwe ati: "Mugenzi, iyo uba wari hano, musazanje ntaba yahwereye."

43012001	Nuko hasigaye imisi itandatu Pasika igashika, Yesu aja i Betaniya, ni ho haba Lazaro yari yazuye mu bapfuye.

43012024	Ni ukuri ni ukuri ndababwire; iyo agatete k'ingano kataguye mw'ivu ngo gapfe, kaguma uko kari konyene; ariko iyo gapfuye, gahunda impeke nyinshi.

43012026	Ni hagira uwunkorera, ni ankurikire, kandi aho nzoba ndi, umukozi wanje ni ho azoba, ni hagira uwunkorera, Data azomuha icubahiro.

43012028	Data, shimagiza izina ryawe." Maze ijwi riva mw'ijuru riti: "Ndarishimagije, kandi nzokwongera kurishimagiza."

43013001	Umusi wa Pasika utarashika, Yesu amenye ko igihe ciwe gishitse co kuva mw'isi ngo aje kwa Se, uko yakunda abiwe bari mw'isi, ni ko yabakunze gushitsa ku muhero.
43013002	Bakiriko bararya ku mugoroba, wa mugarariji amaze kwinjiza ubuguranyi mu mutima wa Yuda Isikaryota, umwana wa Simoni,
43013003	Yesu yari azi ko Se yamuhaye vyose yabishize mu maboko yiwe, kandi ko yavuye ku Mana, kandi ko agira asubire ku Mana,
43013004	ava hasi mw'iriro, akura umutamana, yakira icambazo, arakenyera;
43013005	araheza asuka amazi mu mubehe, atangura kwoza ibirenge vy'abigishwa, no kubihanaguza icambazo akenyeje.
43013006	Nuko ashika kuri Simoni Petero, na we aramubaza ati: "Mugenzi, ni wewe unyoza ibirenge?"
43013007	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Ico jewe ndiko ndakora, wewe nturibukimenye ubu; ariko uzokimenya hanyuma."
43013008	Petero aramubwira ati: "Nta ho uzokwigera unyoza ibirenge gushitsa ibihe vyose." Yesu aramwishura ati: "Ni ntakwoza, nta ho tuzoba duhuriye."

43013010	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Uwari yiyuhagiye nta kindi agomba, atari ukwoga ibirenge, kuko aba akeye umubiri wose, namwe murakeye, ariko si mwese." "
43013011	Kuko yari azi uwuzomugura uwo ari we; ni co catumye avuga ati: "Ntimukeye mwese."
43013012	Nuko ahejeje kuboza ibirenge, yakira umutamana wiwe, yongera kwicara; arababaza ati: " "Mbega muramenye ico ndabagiriye?
43013013	Munyita Mwigisha na Shobuja, kandi mubivuga ko, kuko ari ko ndi.
43013014	Nuko rero, ko jewe ndabogeje ibirenge, ndi Shobuja n'Umwigisha, namwe mukwiye kwozanya ibirenge.
43013015	Kuko ndabahaye akarorero, kugira ngo nk'uko jewe ndabagiriye, mube ari ko namwe mugira.
43013016	Ni ukuri ni ukuri ndababwire, umushumba ntaruta shebuja, kandi n'intumwa ntiruta uwayitumye.

43013018	Simvuze mwese, kuko nzi abo natoranije, ariko ni ukugira ngo ivyanditswe bishike, ngo Uwurya ivyo kurya vyanje ni we ambanguriye umugere.
43013019	Uhereye ubu ndabibabariye bitaraba, kugira ngo aho bizobera, mwizere ko ndi we.
43013020	Ni ukuri ndababwire, uwakira uwo nzotuma azoba anyakiriye, uwunyakira aba yakiriye uwantumye."
43013021	Yesu avuze ivyo, ahagarika umutima, abivuga avyataguye ati: "Ni ukuri ni ukuri ndababwire, umwe muri mwebwe agira angure."
43013022	Abigishwa bararabana, bazazaniwe uwo avuze uwo ari we.
43013023	Hariho umwe mu bigishwa biwe yari yegamiye mu gikiriza ca Yesu bariko bararya, umwe Yesu yakunda.
43013024	Simoni Petero amuvunira akagohe ati: "Tubwire uwo avuze uwo ari we."
43013025	Uwo rero ahengamira inyuma, uko yari hano nyene mu gikiriza ca Yesu, aramubaza ati: "Ni nde ga Mugenzi?"
43013026	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Uwo nkorezamwo intore, nkayimuha, azoba ari we." Akojejemwo intore, arayikuramwo, ayihereza Yuda, umwana wa Simoni Isikaryota.
43013027	Hanyuma y'iyo ntore, Satani aca yinjira muri we. Nuko Yesu aramubarira ati: "Ico ukora, gikore ningoga."
43013028	Ariko muri abo bicaranye nta n'umwe yamenye ico abimubwiriye.
43013029	Ariko kuko Yuda ari we yarafise umupfuko, bamwe bagize ngo Yesu yamubwiye, ngo Gura ibizodukwira ku musi mukuru, canke ngo agire ico aha aboro.
43013030	Na we amaze kwakira intore, aca asohoka ako kanya, kandi hari mw'ijoro.

43013033	Bana bato, ndacari kumwe namwe akanya gato. Muzondondera, ariko, nk'uko nabwiye Abayuda nti: 'Aho nja ntimushobora gushikayo, ni ko none ndababwira namwe.'
43013034	Ndabaha icagezwe gishasha, ni mukundane; nk'uko nabakunze, mube ari ko namwe mukundana.
43013035	Ni mwagiriranira urukundo, ni ho bose bazomenya ko muri abigishwa banje."
43013036	Simoni Petero aramubaza ati: "Mugenzi, uja hehe?" Yesu aramwishura ati: "Aho nja ntushobora kunkurikira ubu, ariko uzonkurikira hanyuma."

43013038	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Ugize ngo uzonyigura?" Ni ukuri ndakubwire koko, inkoko itarabika, uhava unyihakana gatatu.
43014001	Ntimuhagarike imitima yanyu, mwizere Imana, nanje munyizere.
43014002	I muhira kwa Data hari inzu nyinshi, iyo ziba zitariho, mba ndabibabwiye, kuko ngiye kubategurira ahanyu.
43014003	Kandi ko ngiye kubategurira ahanyu, nzogaruka kubajana i wanje, ngo aho ndi namwe mube ari ho muba.
43014004	Kandi iyo nja murazi inzira ijayo.
43014005	Toma aramubwira ati: "Mugenzi, ntituzi iyo uja, dushobora dute kumenya inzira?"
43014006	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Ni jewe nzira, ukuri n'ubugingo; nta wushika kuri Data ntamujanye.
43014007	Iyo muba mwaramenye, na Data muba mumuzi. Uhereye ubu muramuzi, kandi mwamubonye.
43014008	Filipo aramubwira ati: "Mugenzi, twereke So, bizoba bihaye."
43014009	Yesu aramubaza ati: "Mbega ko nabanye namwe igihe kingana gityo, nturakaruha umenya ga Filipo? Uwubonye jewe aba abonye Data; none uvuga ute ngo Twereke So?"
43014010	Ntiwizeye ko jewe ndi muri Data, na Data ari muri jewe? Amajambo ndababwira si ayo nigeneye, ariko Data aba muri jewe ni we akora ibikorwa vyiwe.
43014011	Ni munyizere ko ndi muri Data, na Data ari muri jewe, bibuze, mupfe kwizera ku bwo ibikorwa ubwavyo.
43014012	Ni ukuri, ni ukuri ndababwire; uwunyizera, ibikorwa jewe nkora na we azobikora, kandi azokora ibibiruta, kuko jewe ngiye kwa Data.
43014013	Kandi ico muzosaba cose mw'izina ryanje nzogikora, kugira ngo Data ashimagizwe mu Mwana.
43014014	Ni mwagira ico musaba mw'izina ryanje, nzogikora."
43014015	Ni mwankunda, muzokwitondera ivyagezwe vyanje,
43014016	nanje nzosaba Data, na we azobaha uwundi Mwitsa, ngo azobane namwe ibihe bidashira,
43014017	ni we Mpwemu w'ukuri, uwo abo isi badashobora kwakira, kuko batamubona, kandi batamuzi; mweho muramuzi, kuko abana namwe kandi azoba muri mwebwe.
43014018	Sinzobasiga nk'impfuvyi, nzoza kuri mwebwe.
43014019	Hasigaye igihe gito, abo isi ntibabe bakimbona, ariko mweho muzombona; kuko ndiho, namwe muzobaho.
43014020	Uwo musi muzomenya ko ndi muri Data, namwe muri muri jewe, nanje ndi muri mwebwe.
43014021	Uwuri n'ivyagezwe vyanje akavyitondera, uwo ni we ankunda, kandi uwunkunda azokundwa na Data, nanje nzomukunda, kandi nzomwihishurira.
43014022	Yuda (atari Isikaryota), aramubaza ati: "Mugenzi, bibaye bite, ko ugira wihishurire twebwe, ntiwihishurire abo isi?"
43014023	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Ni hagira uwunkunda, azokwitondera ijambo ryanje, kandi Data azomukunda, maze tuzoza kuri we, tubane na we.
43014024	Uwutankunda ntiyitondera amajambo yanje, kandi ijambo mwumva si iryanje, ariko ni irya Data yantumye."
43014025	Ivyo ndabibabariye nkiri kumwe namwe,
43014026	ariko Umwitsa, ari we Mpwemu Yera, uwo Data azorungika mw'izina ryanje, ni we azobigisha vyose, kandi azobibutsa ivyo nababariye vyose.
43014027	Amahoro ndayabasigaranye, amahoro yanje ndayabagabiye. Jeho sindayabagabira nk'uko abo isi bagaba. Imitima yanyu ntihagarare, kandi ntitinye.
43014028	Mwumvise ko nababwiye nti: "Ndagiye, ariko nzobagarukako. Iyo muba munkunda, muba munezerejwe ni uko ngiye kwa Data, kuko Data ari we anduta.
43014029	Nuko none ndabibabwiye bitaraba, ngo aho bizobera muzokwizere.
43014030	Sinkivugana namwe vyinshi, kuko umwami w'isi ari mu kuza, yamara muri jewe nta kintu ahafise;
43014031	ariko ni ukugira ngo abo isi bamenye ko nkunda Data, kandi uko Data yangeze ko ari ko nkora. Ve hasi, tuve hano tugende."
43015001	Jewe ndi umuzabibu w'ukuri, kandi Data ni nyene wo.
43015002	Ishami ryose ryo muri jewe ritama, arikuraho; kandi iryama ryose ararituturira, ngo rirushirize kwama.
43015003	N'ubu mwebwe mumaze kwezwa kubwo ijambo nababwiye.
43015004	Ni mugume muri jewe, nanje ngume muri mwebwe. Nk'uko ishami ritabasha kwama ubwaryo, ritagumye mu muzabibu, ni ko namwe mutabibasha, mutagumye muri jewe.
43015005	Ni jewe muzabibu, namwe muri amashami; uwuguma muri jewe, nanje nkaguma muri we, uwo ni we yama cane, kuko ata co mubasha gukora mutamfise.
43015006	Umuntu ni ataguma muri jewe atabwa nk'uko ishami ritererwa inyuma y'umurima w'inzabibu, akuma; maze bakayegeranya, bakayaterera mu muriro, agasha.
43015007	Ni mwaguma muri jewe, amajambo yanje akabagumamwo, musabe ico mugomba cose, kizobabera kuno.
43015008	Muri ivyo Data arashimagizwa, ni mwama cane, kandi mukaba abigishwa banje."
43015009	Nk'uko Data yankunze, ni ko nanje nabakunze; ni mugume mu rukundo rwanje.
43015010	Ni mwitondera ivyagezwe vyanje, muzoguma mu rukundo rwanje, nk'uko nanje nitondeye ivyagezwe vya Data, nkaguma mu rukundo rwiwe.
43015011	Ivyo ndabibabwiye, kugira ngo umunezero wanje ubabemwo, kandi n'umunezero wanyu wuzuzwe.
43015012	Ngiki icagezwe canje: ni mukundane, nk'uko nabakunze.
43015013	Nta wogira urukundo ruruta urwo uko umuntu yigura abakunzi biwe.
43015014	Muri abakunzi banje, ni mwakora ivyo ndabategetse.
43015015	Sinkibita abashumba, kuko umushumba atamenya ico shebuja akora; ariko mweho nabise abakunzi, kuko ivyo numvanye Data vyose nabibamenyesheje.
43015016	Si mwebwe mwantoranije, ariko ni jewe nabatoranije, nabashizeho kugira ngo mugende murama imbuto, kandi ngo imbuto zanyu zigumeho, kugira ngo ico muzosaba Data cose mw'izina ryanje, akibahe.
43015017	Ivyo ndabibategetse kugira ngo mukundane.
43015018	Isi ni yabanka, mumenye ko jewe yabanje kunyanka, itarabanka.
43015019	Iyo muba abo isi, isi iba ikunze icayo, maze kuko mutari abo isi, ariko nabatoranije mu bo isi, ni co gituma isi ibanka.
43015020	Mwibuke rya jambo nababwiye nti: "Umushumba ntaruta shebuja; namba barampamye, namwe bazobahama; namba baritondeye ijambo ryanje, n'iryanyu bazoryitondera."
43015021	Ariko ivyo vyose bazobibagirira babahora izina ryanje, kuko batazi uwantumye.
43015022	Iyo ntaba naraje ngo ngire ico ndababarira, nta caha baba bafise, ariko none ntibari n'ico bireguza icaha cabo.
43015023	Uwunyanka aba yanka na Data.
43015024	Iyo ntaba narakoreye ibikorwa muri bo bitigeze gukorwa n'uwundi, nta caha baba bafise, ariko noneho twe na Data baratubonye, baraheza baratwanka.
43015025	Ariko vyabaye bityo kugira ngo ijambo ryanditswe mu vyagezwe vyabo rishike, ngo Banyankiye ubusa.
43015026	Ariko Umwitsa aho azozira, uwo nzobarungikira ava kuri Data, ni we Mpwemu w'ukuri akomoka kuri Data, uwo ni we azonshingira intahe,
43015027	kandi namwe nyene muranshingira intahe, kuko mwari kumwe nanje uhereye mu bihe vya kera.
43016001	Ico ndababaririye ivyo, ni ukugira ngo ntimuzotsitazwe.
43016002	Bazobaca mu nsengero z'Abayuda, kandi igihe kigiye kuza, uwuzobica wese azogira ngo agiriye Imana ikimazi.
43016003	Kandi ivyo bazobikora kuko batamenye Data, nanje ntibamenye.
43016004	Ico ndababaririye ivyo, ni ukugira ngo igihe cavyo ni cashika, muzovyibuke ko nanje nabibabwiye. Uhereye ubwa mbere sinaribwabibabwire, kuko nari nkiri kumwe namwe.
43016005	None ngira ngende ku wantumye, kandi nta n'umwe muri mwebwe arushe ambaza ati: "Uja hehe?"
43016006	Ariko kuko ndababariye ivyo, umubabaro waciye wuzura mu mitima yanyu.
43016007	Ariko jewe ndababwira ukuri; Ikizogira ico kibamarira, ni uko jewe ngenda; kuko ni ntagenda, Umwitsa ntazoza kuri mwebwe; ariko ni nagenda nzomubarungikira.
43016008	Uwo ni yaza, azohinyuza abo isi, abemeze ivyo icaha, ivyo ukugororoka n'ivyo urubanza;
43016009	ivyo icaha, kuko batanyizeye,
43016010	ivyo ukugororoka, kuko nja kwa Data, kandi namwe muzoba mutakimbona,
43016011	ivyo imanza, kuko umwami w'iyi si yaciriwe urubanza.
43016012	Nari ngifise vyinshi vyo kubabwira, ariko ntimushobora kuvyihanganira ubu.
43016013	Ariko uwo Mpwemu w'ukuri ni yaza, azobarongora abashitse ku kuri kwose, kuko atazovuga ivyo yigeneye, ariko ivyo azokwumva vyose ni vyo azovuga, kandi azobamenyesha ibigira bize.
43016014	Uwo azoshimagiza jewe, kuko azokwakira ku vyanje, akabibamenyesha.
43016015	Ivyo Data afise vyose ni ivyanje, ni co gitumye mvuga nti: "Yakira ku vyanje, akabibamenyesha."
43016016	Hasigaye igihe gito ntimube mukimbona, maze hazoca ikindi gihe gito musubire kumbona.
43016017	Bamwe mu bigishwa biwe barabazanya bati: "Mbega ivyo atubwiye ni ibiki ngo Hasigaye igihe gito ntimube mukimbona, ngo maze hazoca ikindi gihe gito musubire kumbona, kandi ngo kuko nja kwa Data?"
43016018	Kandi bati: "Ivyo atubwiye ni ibiki, ngo igihe gito?" Ntitumenye ico avuze ico ari co.
43016019	Yesu amenya ko bagomba kumubaza, arababaza ati: "Mbega mubazanya ico ari co, ko mbababariye nti: "Hasigaye igihe gito ntimube mukimbona kandi hazoca ikindi gihe gito musubire kumbona?"
43016020	Ni ukuri, ni ukuri ndababwire, mweho muzorira muboroge, ariko abo isi bo bazonezerwa; mweho muzobabara, ariko umubabaro wanyu uzocika umunezero.
43016021	Umugore iyo aramutswe, aja mu mubabaro, kuko igihe ciwe kigeze, ariko iyo umwana amaze kuvuka ntaba acibuka kugorwa kwiwe, kuko anezerejwe n'uko umuntu avutse mw'isi.
43016022	Ni ko namwe muri mu mubabaro, ariko nzosubira kubabona, kandi imitima yanyu izonezerwa, umunezero wanyu nta n'umwe azowubanyaga.
43016023	Kuri uwo musi nta na kimwe muzombaza. Ni ukuri ndakubwire koko, ni hagira ico musaba Data cose azokibaha mw'izina ryanje.
43016024	Kugeza ubu nta co mwasavye mw'izina ryanje; musabe muzohabwa, ngo umunezero wanyu wuzuzwe.
43016025	Ivyo ndabibabwiriye mu migani, ariko igihe kizoza sinzoba ngisubira kuvuganira namwe mu migani, mugabo nzobabwira ivya Data ndabifoboye.
43016026	Kuri uwo musi muzosaba mw'izina ryanje, kandi sindababwira ngo nzobasabira Data.
43016027	Kuko Data na we ubwiwe abakunda, kuko mwankunze kandi mwizeye ko naturutse ku Mana.
43016028	Navuye kwa Data, nza mw'isi; ikindi, isi ndiko ndayivamwo, nje kwa Data.
43016029	Abigishwa biwe baravuga bati: "Ubuho urabifoboye, nta mugani uduciriye.
43016030	Ubuho tumenye ko uzi vyose, kandi ko ku bwawe utarinda ko hogira uwukubaza; ni co gituma twizera ko waturutse ku Mana."
43016031	Yesu arabishura ati: "Mbega noneho murizeye?
43016032	Igihe kigira kize, mbere kirashitse, aho muhava musabagira, umuntu wese aje mu vyiwe, munte jenyene, ariko sindi jenyene, kuko Data ari kumwe nanje.
43016033	Ivyo ndabibabwiye, kugira ngo mugire amahoro muri jewe. Mw'isi muri n'amarushwa, ariko ni muhumure, jewe naranesheje isi."
43017001	Yesu avuze ivyo, arangamiza mw'ijuru ati: "Data, igihe kirashitse; shimagiza Umwana wawe, ngo Umwana agushimagize;
43017002	nk'uko wamuhaye ububasha ku bafise umubiri bose, ngo abo wamuhaye bose abahe ubugingo budashira.
43017003	Ubu ni bwo bugingo budashira, ko bamenya wewe, Imana yonyene y'ukuri, n'uwo watumye, Yesu Kristo.
43017004	Nagushimagije mw'isi, nonosoye igikorwa wampaye gukora.
43017005	Na none Data, unshimagizanye nawe, unshimagirishije bwa bwiza nahoranye ndi kumwe nawe, isi itararemwa.
43017006	Nahishuriye izina ryawe abantu wampaye mu b'isi; bari abawe, urabampa, kandi bitondeye ijambo ryawe.
43017007	None bamenye yuko ivyo wampaye vyose biva kuri wewe;
43017008	kuko amajambo wampaye nayabahaye, na bo bakayakira, bakamenya vy'ukuri ko naturutse kuri wewe; bakizera ko ari wewe wantumye.
43017009	Ndabasabira; sinsabira abo isi, ariko nsabira abo wampaye, kuko ari abawe;
43017010	kandi ivyanje vyose ni ivyawe, n'ivyawe na vyo ni ivyanje, kandi nashimagijwe muri bo.
43017011	Sinkiri mw'isi, ariko bo bari mw'isi, nanje ndaje kuri wewe. Data wera, ubazigamire mw'izina ryawe wampaye, ngo babe umwe nk'uko natwe turi.
43017012	Nkiri kumwe na bo, nabazigamiye mw'izina ryawe wampaye. Narabashibamyeko, kandi nta n'umwe muri bo yapfuye rubi, atari wa mwana wo gupfa rubi, kugira ngo ivyanditswe bishike.
43017013	Ariko none ndaje kuri wewe, kandi ibi ndabivuga ndi mw'isi, kugira ngo bagire umunezero wanje wuzure muri bo.
43017014	Nabahaye ijambo ryawe; kandi ab'isi barabanka, kuko atari abo isi, nk'uko nanje ntari uwo isi.
43017015	Sindagusaba ngo ubakure mw'isi, ariko ngo ubarinde wa Mubi.
43017016	Si ab'isi, nk'uko nanje ntari uwo isi.
43017017	Ubeze mu kuri, ijambo ryawe ni ryo kuri.
43017018	Nk'uko wantumye mw'isi, ni ko nanje nabatumye mw'isi,
43017019	kandi nanje niyeza kubwabo, kugira ngo na bo babe bejejwe mu kuri.
43017020	Sinsabira aba gusa, ariko ndasabira n'abo bazonyizera ku bwo ijambo ry'aba,
43017021	kugira ngo bose babe umwe, nk'uko wewe, Data, uri muri jewe, nanje nkaba muri wewe, ngo na bo babe ari ko baba muri twebwe, ngo isi yizere ko ari wewe wantumye.
43017022	Nanje nabahaye ubwiza wampaye, ngo babe umwe, nk'uko natwe turi umwe.
43017023	Jewe mbe muri bo, nawe ube muri jewe, ngo bahingurwe babe umwe, kugira ngo isi imenye ko ari wewe wantumye, ukabakunda, nk'uko wankunze.
43017024	Data, abo wampaye ndagomba ko aho ndi na bo bahabana nanje, ngo barabe ubwiza bwanje wampaye, kuko wankunze itanguriro ry'isi ritarashirwaho.
43017025	Data ugororotse, isi ntiyakumenye, ariko jewe narakumenye, n'aba na bo bamenye ko ari wewe wantumye.
43017026	Nabamenyesheje izina ryawe, kandi nzoribamenyesha, ngo urukundo wankunze rube muri bo, nanje mbe muri bo."
43018001	Yesu avuze ivyo, avanayo n'abigishwa biwe afata hakurya y'umugezi witwa Kidironi; aho hari itongo; ashikaho, bo n'abigishwa biwe.
43018002	Kandi na Yuda amugura yari azi aho hantu, kuko Yesu yahora ajanayo n'abigishwa biwe kenshi.
43018003	Nuko Yuda amaze guhabwa n'abaherezi bakuru n'Abafarisayo ingabo z' abasoda, bo n'abagendanyi, ajayo, bari n'amatara, ibimuri n'ibirwanisho.

43018009	Ukwo kwari ukugira ngo rya jambo yavuze rishike, ngo mu bo wampaye nta n'umwe najimije.
43018010	Simoni Petero yari n'inkota, arayisokora, aca ugutwi kw'i buryo kw'umuntu w'umuherezi mukuru, uwo muntu yitwa Malikusi.

43018015	Simoni Petero akurikira Yesu, bo n'uwundi mwigishwa. Uwo mwigishwa yari azinanyi n'umuherezi mukuru, ashikana na Yesu mu rugo rw'uwo muherezi mukuru,
43018016	ariko Petero asigara ahagaze kw'irembo. Wa wundi mwigishwa yari azinanyi n'umuherezi mukuru, ashika kw'irembo, avugana n'umukumirizi, araheza ashikana Petero imbere.

43018018	Abashumba n'abagendanyi bari bahagaze bacanye umuriro w'amakara, kuko hari imbeho, bariko barota; kandi Petero na we yari kumwe na bo, ahagaze yota.

43018020	Yesu aramwishura ati: " "Nabarira abo isi ndavyeruye, nahora nigishiriza mu nsengero z'Abayuda no mu rundi rusengero aho Abayuda bose bakoranira, nta co navugiye mu mpisho.
43018021	Umbarije iki? Baza abahora bavyumva ico nababariye: erega ni bo bazi ivyo navuze."

43018026	Umwe mu bashumba b'umuherezi mukuru, yari incuti y'umwe Petero yaciye ugutwi, aramubaza ati: "Sinakubonye uri kumwe na we muri rya tongo?" "

43018036	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Ubwami bwanje si ubwo muri iyi si; iyaba ubwami bwanje bwari ubwo muri iyi si, abagendanyi banje baba barwanye, ngo simpabwe Abayuda. Ariko noneho ubwami bwanje si ubwo ino."
43018037	Nuko Pilato aramubaza ati: "Ubwo wewe uri umwami?" Yesu ati: "Ni wewe uvyivugiye ko ndi umwami." Iki ni co navukiye, kandi iki ni co canzanye mw'isi, ni ukugira ngo nshingire intahe ukuri. Uwo ukuri wese yumva ijwi ryanje.
43018038	Pilato aramubaza ati: "Mbega ukuri ni iki?" Amaze kuvuga ivyo, asubira gusohoka, aja aho Abayuda bari, arababwira ati: "Jewe nta kibi nabonye kuri we.
43018039	Ariko musanganywe umugenzo ko ndabarekurira umwe mu misi ya Pasika; none muragomba ko ndabarekurira umwami w'Abayuda?"
43018040	Nuko basubira gusemerera bati: "Si uyo, ariko turekurire Baraba." Yamara Baraba yari umwambuzi.
43019001	Maze Pilato afata Yesu, aramukubitisha.

43019019	Pilato yandika icandiko, agishira ku musaraba; canditswe ngo YESU UMUNYANAZARETI UMWAMI W'ABAYUDA.
43019020	Benshi mu Bayuda basoma ico candiko, kuko aho hantu Yesu yabambwe hari hafi y'igisagara; kandi cari canditswe mu Giheburayo no mu Kiroma no mu Kigiriki.
43019021	Nuko Abaherezi bakuru b'Abayuda babwira Pilato bati: " "Nta co wandika ngo Umwami w'Abayuda, ariko ko yivuze ngo Ni jewe Mwami w'Abayuda."
43019022	Pilato arabishura ati: "Ico nanditse, nacanditse."
43019023	Nuko abasoda, bamaze kubamba Yesu, bakira impuzu ziwe, bazigaburamwo imigabane ine, umusoda wese umugabane wiwe; hasigara umutamana. Kandi uwo mutamana ntiwari ufise umubariro, wari ujishwe kumwe, uhereye hejuru kugeza hasi.
43019024	Nuko baravugana bati: "Ntituwutabure, tuwupfindire, ugire uwuwegukiye." Kwari ukugira ngo ivyanditswe bishike,ngo Bagabuye impuzu zanje,Bapfindira umwambaro wanje. Ivyo ni ko abasoda babikoze.
43019025	Ariko i ruhande y'umusaraba wa Yesu hari hahagaze nyina, nyinabo, Mariya muka Kilopa na Mariya Magadalene.
43019026	Yesu abonye nyina na wa mwigishwa yakunda ahagazeho, abarira nyina ati: "Nyina wanje, nguwo umwana wawe."
43019027	Maze abarira wa mwigishwa ati: "Nguwo nyoko." " Uhereye ako kanya uwo mwigishwa ajana Mariya i we.
43019028	Hanyuma y'ivyo Yesu amenye yuko noneho vyose birangiye, kugira ngo icanditswe gishike, aravuga ati: " "Ndafise inyota."
43019029	Aho hantu hari hateretse inkono yuzuye inkarisha, nuko bashira sipongo yuzuyemwo inkarisha kw' irenga, bayirungika ku munwa wiwe.
43019030	Yesu amaze kuyihabwa, aravuga ati: "Birarangiye." " Araheza ajondamika umutwe, umutima uraca.
43019031	Uwo musi wari uwo kwitegurira Pasika; nuko kugira ngo ababambwe ntibagume ku misaraba kw'isabato, kuko uwo musi w'isabato wari mukuru, Abayuda basaba Pilato ngo amaguru yabo avunwe, kandi ngo babamburwe.
43019032	Maze abasoda baraza, bavuna amaguru y'uwa mbere n'ayo uwundi yabambanywe na we.
43019033	Ariko bashitse kuri Yesu, babonye amaze gupfa, ntibaba bakimuvuna amaguru,
43019034	ariko umwe mu basoda amucumita icumu mu rubavu; ako kanya hava amaraso n'amazi.
43019035	Uwabibonye ni we yabishingiye intahe kandi intahe yiwe ni iyo ukuri, kandi arazi ko avuga ukuri, kugira ngo namwe mwizere.
43019036	Kuko ivyo vyabayeho kugira ngo icanditswe gishike, ngo nta n'igufa ryiwe rizovunwa. "
43019037	Kandi hari ikindi canditswe, kivuga ngo Bazobona uwo bacumise.
43019038	Hanyuma y'ivyo Yosefu Umunyarimataya, yari umwigishwa wa Yesu, ariko mu mpisho, ku bwo gutinya Abayuda, yaka Pilato ikiziga ca Yesu ngo akijane, Pilato aremera; nuko araza ajana ikiziga ciwe.
43019039	Kandi haza na Nikodemu, umwe yaza kuri Yesu mw'ijoro ubwa mbere, azana ikivange c'isenga n'imbazi nk'ibilo mirongo itanu.
43019040	Nuko bakira ikiziga ca Yesu, bakizingira mu mpuzu zera derere, hamwe n'ivyo bimota neza, nk'uko umugenzo w'Abayuda wo guhamba wari uri.
43019041	Kandi aho hantu yabambwe hari itongo; kandi muri iryo tongo hari imva nshasha itarahambwamwo umuntu;
43019042	aho ni ho bahamvye Yesu, kuko wari umusi wo kwitegura kw'Abayuda, kandi iyo mva ikaba hafi.
43020001	Ku wa mbere w'imisi indwi mu gaturuturu, hatarabona, Mariya Magadalene aja ku mva, abona ikibuye gikuwe ku mva;
43020002	agenda ariruka ashikira Simoni Petero na wa mwigishwa wundi Yesu yakunda, arababwira ati: "Bakuye Umwami Yesu mu mva, kandi ntituzi aho bamushize."
43020003	Nuko Petero arasohoka, na wa mwigishwa wundi, baja ku mva.
43020004	Bose birukira icarimwe, kandi wa mwigishwa wundi asiga Petero, amutanga ku mva.
43020005	Yunamye, arungurutseyo, abona za mpuzu zera derere zirambitseho, ariko ntiyinjira.
43020006	Maze Simoni Petero arashika amukurikiye, yinjira mu mva, abona za mpuzu zirambitseho,
43020007	n'igitambara cari mu mutwe wiwe, kitarambitse hamwe na za mpuzu, ariko kizinze kiri ahaco ukwa conyene.
43020008	Ni ho hinjiye wa mwigishwa wundi na we, umwe yabanje gushika ku mva, abibonye arizera.
43020009	Kuko bataribwamenye ivyanditswe yuko akwiye kuzozuka mu bapfuye.
43020010	Maze abo bigishwa bavayo basubira i wabo.
43020011	Mariya yari ahagaze ku mva arira. Akiriko ararira, arunama, arunguruka mu mva,
43020012	abona abamarayika babiri bambaye impuzu zera, bicaye umwe ku mutwe, uwundi mu mirambizo y'aho ikiziga ca Yesu cari kiryamye.
43020013	Baramubaza bati: "Mbega nyina wanje, urizwa ni iki?" Na we ati: "Ni uko bakuyeho Umwami wanje, nanje nkaba ntazi aho bamushize."
43020014	Avuze ivyo, arakebuka, abona Yesu ahagaze, ariko ntiyamenya ko ari Yesu.
43020015	Yesu aramubaza ati: "Mbega nyina wanje, urizwa n'iki? Urondera nde?" Na we yiyumvira ko ari umurimyi waho, aramubwira ati: "Mugenzi, namba ari wewe wamukuye hano, ndangira aho wamushize, ndamukureyo."
43020016	Yesu aramuhamagara ati: "Mariya." Na we arahindukira, amwitaba mu Giheburayo ati: "Rabuni (risobanurwa ngo Mwigisha)."
43020017	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Ntunkoreko, kuko ntaraduga kwa Data; ariko genda ku bavukanyi banje, ubabarire uti: 'Agira aduge kwa Se ari we So' kandi ku Mana yiwe ari yo Mana yanyu."
43020018	Mariya Magadalene aragenda, abarira abigishwa inkuru ati: "Nabonye Umwami;" " abadondera ivyo yamubariye.
43020019	Nuko kuri uwo musi bugorovye, ni wo musi wa mbere w'imisi indwi, imiryango yari yugaye aho abigishwa bari, kubwo gutinya Abayuda, Yesu araza abahagarara hagati, arababwira ati: " "Amahoro abe muri mwebwe."
43020020	Amaze kuvuga atyo, abereka ibiganza vyiwe no mu rubavu. Maze abigishwa baranezerwa, babonye Umwami.
43020021	Yesu yongera kubabwira ati: "Amahoro abe muri mwebwe." Nk'uko Data yantumye ni ko nanje nabatumye."
43020022	Avuze ivyo, abahumekerako ati: "Ni mwakire Mpwemu Yera.
43020023	Kandi abo muzoharira ivyaha bose, bazoba babihariwe; ariko abo mutazobiharira bose, ntibazoba babihariwe."
43020024	Ariko Toma ari we Hasa, umwe wo muri bamwe icumi na babiri, ntiyari kumwe na bo aho Yesu yaza.
43020025	Abandi bigishwa baramubwira bati: "Twabonye Umwami." Na we arabishura ati: "Ni ntabona inkovu z'imambo mu biganza vyiwe, ngo nkoze urutoke rwanje mu nkovu z'imambo, ngo nshire urushi mu rubavu rwiwe, sinemera."
43020026	Maze imisi umunani ishize abigishwa bari mu nzu ukundi gusha, na Toma bari kumwe. Yesu araza, imyango yari yugaye, abahagarara hagati ati: "Amahoro abe muri mwebwe."
43020027	Maze abwira Toma ati: "Zana hano urutoke rwawe, urabe ibiganza vyanje; zana n'urushi, urushire mu rubavu rwanje, nta co uba uwutizera, ariko ube uwizeye."
43020028	Toma aramwishura ati: "Mwami wanje, kandi Mana yanje."
43020029	Yesu aramubwira ati: "Wijejwe n'uko umbonye. Harahiriwe abatarinze kubona, yamara bakizera."
43020030	Hariho n'ibindi bimenyetso vyinshi Yesu yakoreye imbere y' abigishwa, bitanditswe muri iki gitabo.
43020031	Ariko ibi vyandikiwe kugira ngo mwizere yuko Yesu ari we Kristo, Umwana w'Imana, no kugira ngo mwizeye mugire ubugingo mw'izina ryiwe.
43021001	Hanyuma y'ivyo Yesu yiyereka abigishwa ukundi gusha, ari ku kiyaga c'i Tiberiya. Kandi uburyo yiyerekanye ni ubu:
43021002	Simoni Petero, Toma ari we Hasa bari kumwe na Natanayeli w'i Kana i Galilaya, n'abana ba Zebedayo, n'abandi bigishwa babiri.
43021003	Simoni Petero arababwira ati: "Ndagiye kuroba." Na bo bati: "Natwe turajana nawe." Barikora, batambukira mu bwato. Muri iryo joro ntibagira ico bafata.
43021004	Umutwenzi ugitambika, Yesu ahagarara ku musenyi, ariko abigishwa ntibamenya ko ari we.
43021005	Nuko Yesu arababaza ati: "Bana, hari ico kurya mufise?" Bati: "Oya."
43021006	Arababwira ati: "Ni muterere urusenga i buryo bw'ubwato, muraronka." Nuko baraterera, ntibaba bakibasha kurukwega, kuko ifi zari isinzi.
43021007	Wa mwigishwa Yesu yakunda abwira Petero ati: "Ni Umwami Yesu." Simoni Petero yumvise ko ari Umwami, akenyera impuzu, kuko yari gusa, araheza yikubita mu kiyaga.
43021008	Ariko abandi bigishwa baza mu bwato, kuko bari hafi y'umusenyi, hari nk'intambuko ijana, bakwega urusenga rurimwo ifi.
43021009	Bafashe i musozi, babonaho umuriro w'amakara n'ifi zigeretseko, n'umutsima.
43021010	Yesu arababwira ati: "Ni muzane ifi ku zo muhejeje kuroba."
43021011	Simoni Petero aja mu bwato, akwegera urusenga i musozi rwuzuye ifi nininini ijana na mirongo itanu na zitatu, kandi naho zari zingana zityo, urusenga ntirwacitse.
43021012	Yesu arababarira ati: "Ni muze murye." " Ariko mu bigishwa ntihagira uwutinyuka kumubaza ati: "Uri nde?" Kuko bari bamenye ko ari Umwami Yesu.
43021013	Yesu araza, yakira umutsima, arawubaha, n'ifi ni uko.
43021014	Ubwo bwari ubugira gatatu Yesu yiyereka abigishwa, amaze kuzuka mu bapfuye.
43021015	Nuko barangije kurya, Yesu abaza Simoni Petero ati: " "Simoni, umwana wa Yohana, mbega urankunda kurusha aba?" Na we ati: "Ego, Mugenzi, wewe urazi ko nkunogera." Aramubwira ati: "Ahura imyagazi y'intama zanje."
43021016	Yongera kumubaza ubugira kabiri ati: "Simoni, umwana wa Yohana, mbega urankunda?" Na we ati: "Ego, Mugenzi, wewe urazi ko ndagukunda." Aramubwira ati: "Ragira intama zanje."
43021017	Amubaza ubugira gatatu ati: "Simoni, umwana wa Yohana, mbega urankunda?" Petero arababara, kuko yamubajije ubugira gatatu ngo mbega urankunda? Aramwishura ati: "Mugenzi, weho urazi vyose, urazi ko ndagukunda." Yesu aramubwira ati: "Ahura intama zanje."
43021018	Ni ukuri ndakubwire koko; ukiri umusore, warikenyeza, ukaja aho ugomba; ariko aho uzosazira, uzogorora amaboko, uwundi agukenyeze, akujane aho utagomba.
43021019	Icatumye avuga atyo, kwari ukwerekana urupfu azopfa, ashimagirisha Imana. Amaze kuvuga atyo, aramubarira ati: "Nkurikira."
43021020	Petero arakebuka, abona wa mwigishwa Yesu yakunda abakurikiye, umwe yari yegamiye mu gikiriza ca Yesu hamwe basangira, akamubaza ati: "Mugenzi, ni nde azokugura?"
