43021022	Yesu aramwishura ati: "Namba ngomba ko azogumaho kugeza aho nzozira, bigutwaye iki?"Wewe nkurikira. "
43021023	Ni co catumye iri jambo rikwira mu bavukanyi, ngo uwo mwigishwa ntazopfa. Ariko Yesu ntiyamubwiye ko atazopfa, ariko yavuze ati: "Namba ngomba ko agumaho kugeza aho nzozira, bigutwaye iki?"
43021024	Uwo ni wa mwigishwa yashingiye intahe ivyo, kandi ni we yavyanditse, kandi natwe tuzi yuko intahe yiwe ari iyo ukuri.
43021025	Ariko hariho n'ibindi vyinshi Yesu yakoze, vyokwandikwa bidondowe kimwekimwe, ngira ngo n'isi na yo ntiyokwirwamwo ibitabo vyokwanditswe."
44001001	Teyofilo we, muri ca gitabo ca mbere nanditse, mvuga ivyo Yesu yatanguye gukora no kwigisha vyose,
44001002	gushitsa ku musi yadugijwe mw'ijuru, ahejeje gusigarana amategeko intumwa muri Mpwemu Yera, zimwe yatoranije.

44001010	Bagihanze amaso mw'ijuru akigenda, abagabo babiri bambaye impuzu zera bahagarara i ruhande yabo;

44001012	Buno basubira i Yerusalemu, bavuye ku musozi witwa Elayono, uri hafi y'i Yerusalemu nk'urugendo rwemewe kugendwa kw'isabato.

44001017	kuko yari yaharuwe muri twebwe, agahabwa umugabane w'iki gikorwa. "

44002024	Ariko Imana yaramuzuye, ibahoye imigozi y'urupfu, kuko bitashobotse ko rumugumya.
44002025	Kuko Dawidi yavuze ivyo uwo ati: "Nabonye Uhoraho imbere yanje imisi yose, kuko ari i buryo bwanje, ngo sinyiganyige. "

44002031	yavuze ivyo ukuzuka kwa Kristo abibonye bitaribwabe, yuko atarekewe mu kuzimu, kandi n'umubiri wiwe ata ho wigeze ubora.

44002037	Bumvise ivyo, bibacumita mu mitima, babaza Petero n'izindi ntumwa bati: "Bagabo bavukanyi mbega tugire dute? "
44002038	Petero arabishura ati: "Ni mwihane, umuntu wese muri mwebwe abatizwe mw'izina rya Yesu Kristo, mubone guharirwa ivyaha vyanyu, kandi muzohabwa ingabire, ari yo Mpwemu Yera.
44002039	Kuko isezerano ari iryanyu kandi ari iryo abana banyu, n'abari kure bose, abazohamagarwa bose n'Umwami Imana yacu. "
44002040	Kandi ashingisha intahe ayandi majambo menshi, arabahanura ati: "Ni mwikize abo iki gihe kigoramye. "
44002041	Nuko abemeye amajambo yiwe barabatizwa; abongewe kuri uwo musi ku bari basanzweho bari nk'ibihumbi bitatu.
44002042	Bashishikara cane ivyo intumwa zigisha, kugira ubumwe, bamanyagura umutsima hamwe no gusenga.
44002043	Umuntu wese aterwa n'ubwoba. Kandi utwumiza n'ibimenyetso vyinshi vyakorwa n'intumwa.
44002044	Abizeye bose baba hamwe, basangira ivyabo vyose.
44002045	Amatongo yabo n'ibintu vyabo barabigurisha, bakabibagabanganya bose, bakurikije ukuntu umuntu wese akenye.
44002046	Kandi imisi yose bashishikara kuja mu rusengero n'umutima uhuye, kandi i wabo bamanyagura umutsima, bakarya banezerewe n'imitima itagira akarohe,
44002047	bahimbaza Imana, kandi na bo bashimwa n'abantu bose. Umwami Imana akabongera imisi yose abama barakizwa.
44003001	Petero na Yohana bariko baraduga baja mu rusengero mu gihe co gusenga, ni co saha icenda.
44003002	Hari umuntu yamugaye ibirenge uhereye kuva mu nda ya nyina, yama aterurwa, bakamushira kw'irembo ry'urusengero ryitwa Ryiza uko bukeye, kugira ngo asege abinjira mu rusengero.
44003003	Uwo abonye Petero na Yohana bagira binjire mu rusengero, arabasega ngo bamuhe.
44003004	Petero amuhanga amaso, bo na Yohana, aramubarira ati: "Ni uturabe. "
44003005	Abashirako umutima agira ngo hari ico bamuha.
44003006	Petero aramubarira ati: "Nta feza n'izahabu mfise, ariko ico mfise ndakiguha; mw'izina rya Yesu Kristo Umunyanazareti, va hasi utambuke. "
44003007	Maze amufata ukuboko kw'i buryo, amukura hasi; ako kanya ibirenge vyiwe n'ingingo zavyo bica birakomera.
44003008	Arasimbasimba arahagarara, atangura gutambuka, yinjirana na bo mu rusengero, atambuka yitera hejuru, ahimbaza Imana.
44003009	Abantu bose babona atambuka ahimbaza Imana,
44003010	bamenya ko ari we yahora yicara kw'irembo ry'urusengero ryitwa Ryiza asegerereza; barumirwa cane, batangazwa n'ibimubayeko.
44003011	Agifashe Petero na Yohana, abantu bose biruka baja aho bari, bakoranira kw'ibaraza ryitwa irya Salomo, batangaye cane.
44003012	Petero abibonye, abaza abo bantu ati: "Yemwe bagabo b'Abisirayeli, ni iki gitumye mutangazwa n'ibi, muduhangiye amaso iki, nk'aho ubushobozi bwacu canke ukwubaha Imana kwacu ari vyo vyaduhaye kumugendesha?
44003013	Imana ya Aburahamu, Isaka na Yakobo, ari yo Mana ya ba sogokuruza, yashimagije Umushumba wayo Yesu, umwe mwebwe mwatanze mukamwihakanira mu maso ya Pilato, amaze kwahukanya urubanza rwo kumurekura.
44003014	Ariko mweho mwihakana Uwera kandi Umugororotsi, musaba ko babarekurira umwicanyi,
44003015	wa Mukuru w'ubugingo muramwica; ariko Imana imuzura mu bapfuye, natwe turi ivyabona vyo gushingira intahe ivyo.
44003016	Kandi uwu, uwo mubona kandi muzi, kuko yizeye izina ry'uwo, iryo zina ryamuhaye inkomezi. Mbere ukwizera ahawe na we ni kwo kumukirije rwose imbere yanyu mwese.
44003017	Kandi none, bavukanyi, ndazi yuko mwabikoze mutabizi, n'ababaganza na bo ni uko.
44003018	Ariko ivyo Imana yavugiye mu kanwa k'abavugishwa na yo bose bitaribwabe, yuko Kristo wayo azobabazwa, ivyo yabishikije ityo.
44003019	Nuko mwihane, muhindukire, ivyaha vyanyu bihanagurwe, ibihe vyo guhembuka bibone ingene biza, bivuye mu maso y'Umwami Imana,
44003020	kugira ngo na yo izotume Kristo yabatoranirijwe kera, ni we Yesu.
44003021	Ariko ijuru rikwiye kumwakira, gushitsa ku bihe vyo gusubira guhindura ibintu vyose bishasha, nk'uko Imana yavuze mu kanwa k'abera bayo yavugisha bose, uhereye mu ntango. "
44003022	Mose koko yaravuze ati: "Uhoraho Imana azobahagurukiriza uwuvugishwa na we mu b'i wanyu ameze nkanje; uwo muzomwumvire mu vyo azobabarira vyose. "
44003023	Kandi umuntu wese atazokwumvira uno avugishwa n'Imana, azorandurwa mu bantu.
44003024	Mbere abavugishwa n'Imana bose, uhereye kuri Samweli n'abamukurikiye, abavuze bose baramenyekanishije ivyo iyi misi.
44003025	Namwe muri abana b'abavugishwa n'Imana, kandi muri ab'isezerano Imana yasezeranye na ba sogokuruza banyu, ibarira Aburahamu ati: "Mu ruvyaro rwawe ni ho imiryango yose yo mw'isi izoherwa umugisha. "
44003026	Ni mwebwe Imana yatanguye gutumako Umushumba wayo imaze kumuzura, kugira ngo abahe umugisha, abahindure, umuntu wese ave mu bibi vyiwe.
44004001	Bakivugana n'abantu, abaherezi bazanana aho bari n'umukuru w'abacungera irembo ry'urusengero, n'Abasadukayo,
44004002	bababajwe cane n'uko bigisha abantu, bababarira yuko ukuzuka kw'abapfuye kwabonetse kuri Yesu.
44004003	Babashorerako amaboko, babashira mw'ibohero gushitsa mu gitondo, kuko bwari bugorovye.
44004004	Ariko benshi mu bumvise iryo jambo barizera, igitigiri c'abagabo gishika nk'ibihumbi bitanu.
44004005	Bukeye bw'aho, abashingantahe babo, abakuru n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe bakoranira i Yerusalemu,
44004006	Anasi umuherezi mukuru, Kayafa, Yohana, Alekisandero n'abo umuryango bose w'abaherezi bakuru.
44004007	Babashize hagati, barababaza bati: "Ni ubushobozi ki, canke ni izina riki, vyabateye gukora ivyo? "
44004008	Nuko Petero, yuzuye Mpwemu Yera, arababarira ati: "Yemwe bashingantahe b'abantu n'abakuru,
44004009	uwu musi ko ducunaguzwa ivyo twagiriye neza umuntu yanyogomba, kandi n'icamukijije,
44004010	ni mumenye mwese, n'ubwoko bwose bw'Abisirayeli, yuko ari mw'izina rya Yesu Kristo, Umunyanazareti, uwo mwebwe mwabamvye, Imana ikamuzura mu bapfuye, ko ari ho hatumye uwu muntu ahagarara imbere yanyu, akomeye.
44004011	Uwo ni we buye mwebwe abubatsi mwatituye, kandi ryahindutse irigumya imfuruka.
44004012	Kandi nta wundi agakiza kabonerwamwo, kuko ata rindi zina musi y'ijuru ryahawe abantu dukwiye gukirizwamwo.
44004013	Babonye ugushira amanga kwa Petero na Yohana, kandi babona ko batigishijwe, atari abanyabwenge, baratangara; maze bamenya ko babana na Yesu;
44004014	kandi babonye uwo muntu yakijijwe ahagararanye na bo, babura ico bavuga.
44004015	Barabataramura, maze baja inama
44004016	bati: "Mbega aba bantu tubagire dute? Ko vyamenyekanye mu baba i Yerusalemu bose yuko bakoze ikimenyetso kibaye rurangiranwa, natwe ntidushobora kubihakana;
44004017	ariko ntibarushirize kwamamara mu bantu, tubahahirize, ntibongere kugira umuntu n'umwe babarira muri iryo zina. "
44004018	Babahamagaje, barabihanikiriza ngo ntibihende ngo bavuge canke bigishe mw'izina rya Yesu.
44004019	Petero na Yohana barabishura bati: "Namba ari vyiza mu maso y'Imana kubumvira kubarutisha Imana, ni mubitandukanye;
44004020	kuko tweho tudashobora kureka kuvuga ivyo twabonye n'ivyo twumvise. " "
44004021	Na bo bongeye kubahahiriza, barabarekura, babuze uko bobahana kubwo abantu, kuko bose bahimbaza Imana ku vyabaye.
44004022	Kuko uwo muntu yari arengeje imyaka mirongo ine avutse, uwakozweko ico kimenyetso co kumukiza.
44004023	Nuko barekuwe basubira muri bagenzi babo, babiganira ivyo abakuru b'abaherezi n'abakuru bababwiye vyose.
44004024	Na bo bavyumvise bavuga n'ijwi rirenga, babwira Imana n'umutima uhuye bati: " "Databuja, ni wewe waremye ijuru n'isi, n'ikiyaga n'ibirimwo vyose,
44004025	kandi wavugiye mu kanwa ka sogokuruza Dawidi, umusavyi wawe, ubivugisha Mpwemu Yera uti: "Abanyamahanga ni iki kibateye umuvurungano, N'amoko yagiriye ingingo iki ivyo ubusa? "
44004026	Abami bo mw'isi batonze urugamba, N'abakuru bakoraniye hamwe, Kurwanya Uhoraho n'Uwo yarobanuje amavuta.
44004027	Kandi vy'ukuri muri iki gisagara, Herode, bo na Pontiyo Pilato hamwe n'abanyamahanga n'imiryango ya Isirayeli, bakoraniye kurwanya Umushumba wawe yera Yesu, uwo warobanuje amavuta,
44004028	ngo bashitse ivyo ukuboko kwawe n'inama yawe vyari vyaragabiye vyose ko bizoba.
44004029	Kandi none, Mwami, raba agahahirizo kabo, uhe abasavyi bawe kuvuga ijambo ryawe bashize amazinda rwose.
44004030	Ukigoroye ukuboko kwawe gukiza indwara, ibimenyetso n'ibitangaza bikorwe mw'izina ry'Umushumba wawe yera Yesu. " "
44004031	Bahejeje gusenga, aho bakoraniye haratigita, bose buzuzwa Mpwemu Yera, bavuga ijambo ry'Imana bashize amazinda.
44004032	Kandi abizeye umurwi bari bahuje umutima n'inama, kandi nta n'umwe yakimbukira ikintu cose atunze ngo ni iciwe, ariko vyose barabisangira.
44004033	Kandi intumwa zashingira intahe ukuzuka kw'Umwami Yesu ziri n'ubushobozi bwinshi, kandi ubuntu bw'Imana bwinshi buba kuri bo bose."
44004034	Nta mukene yari muri bo, kuko abari bafise amatongo bose canke inzu babigurisha, bakazana ibiguzi vy'ivyo bagurishije,
44004035	bakabishira imbere y'ibirenge vy'intumwa; maze bakabigabanganya abantu, umuntu wese uko akenye.
44004036	Na Yosefu, uwo intumwa zise Barunaba, risobanurwa ngo Umwana wo guhanura, Umulewi yavukiye i Kupuro,
44004037	yari afise itongo ararigurisha, azana ibiguzi vyaryo, abishira imbere y'ibirenge vy'intumwa.
44005001	Kandi hari umugabo yitwa Ananiya, agurisha itongo afatanije n'umugore wiwe Safira,
44005002	yisigariza ku biguzi vyayo, umugore wiwe abizi, azana ikigabane, agishira imbere y'ibirenge vy'intumwa.
44005003	Petero aramubaza ati: "Ananiya, ni iki gitumye Satani yuzuza umutima wawe guhenda Mpwemu Yera, ukisigariza ku biguzi vy'itongo?
44005004	Ukiyifise ntiyari iyawe? Kandi umaze kuyigurisha, ibiguzi vyayo ntuba warabikoze uko ugomba? Ni igiki catumye wigira ingingo mu mutima wawe gukora utyo? Si abantu uhenze, Imana ni yo uhenze. "
44005005	Ananiya yumvise ayo majambo agwa bukumbi. Abavyumvise bose baterwa n'ubwoba bwinshi.
44005006	Imisore iva hasi, iramutekera, iramujana, iramuhamba.
44005007	Hahise nk'isaha zitatu, umugore wiwe arinjira, atazi ivyabaye;
44005008	Petero aramubaza ati: "Mbarira, mbega itongo mwarigurishije ayo nyene? " Aramwishura ati: "Ego me, ni ayo. "
44005009	Petero aramubaza ati: "Ni igiki gitumye muhuza inama kugerageza Mpwemu w'Uhoraho Imana? Ehe ibirenge vy'abahejeje guhamba umugabo wawe biri ku rugi, nawe barakujana. "
44005010	Uwo mwanya agwa imbere y'ibirenge vyiwe bukumbi. Ya misore yinjiye isanga amaze guhwera, iramujana, imuhamba i ruhande y'umugabo wiwe.
44005011	Ishengero ryose n'abavyumvise bose baterwa n'ubwoba bwinshi.
44005012	Ibimenyetso n'ibitangaza vyinshi bikorwa mu bantu n'amaboko y'intumwa. Kandi bose bakoranira mw'ibaraza rya Salomo n'umutima uhuye.
44005013	Ariko mu bandi nta muntu yatinyuka kwifatanya na bo, yamara abantu bose barabashimagiza,
44005014	barushiriza kwongerwako ishengero ryinshi ry'abagabo n'abagore, abizeye Umwami Yesu;
44005015	bituma banaterurira abarwaye ku nzira, babashira mu nderuzo no ku birago, kugira ngo Petero ni yahaca, naho coba igitutu ciwe gishike kuri bamwe.
44005016	Hakoranira ishengero rivuye no mu bisagara bihereranye n'i Yerusalemu, bazana abarwaye n'abababazwa n'impwemu zihumanye, bakizwa uko bangana.
44005017	Maze umuherezi mukuru ahagurukana n'abari kumwe na we bose, ni bo muce witwa uwo Abasadukayo, buzura ishari,
44005018	bashorera amaboko ku ntumwa, bazishira mu nzu y'ibohero rya bose.
44005019	Maze umumarayika w' Umwami Imana ahenga mw'ijoro yugurura imyango y'ibohero, abakurayo, arababwira
44005020	ati: "Ni mugende, muhagarare mu rusengero, mubarire abantu amajambo yose ya bwa Bugingo. "
44005021	Bavyumvise, binjira mu rusengero hari nko mu mutwenzi, barigisha. Maze umuherezi mukuru azanana n'abari kumwe na we, bahamagaza abacamanza, n'abakuru bose b'Abisirayeli, maze batuma mu nzu y'abanyororo kuzana za ntumwa.
44005022	Abagendanyi bagiye ntibazisanga mw'ibohero. Baragaruka barababwira
44005023	bati: "Inzu y'abanyororo dusanze yugaye ata nkomanzi iriho na mba, n'abarinzi bahagaze ku myango, maze twuguruye ntitwasangamwo umuntu. "
44005024	Bumvise ayo majambo umukuru w'abacungera irembo y'urusengero n'abaherezi bakuru bazazanirwa n'ivyabo, n'inkurikizi yavyo.
44005025	Haza umuntu arababarira ati: "Erega ba bagabo mwashira mw'ibohero bari mu rusengero bahagaze bigisha abantu. "
44005026	Maze uwo mukuru w'abacungera irembo ajana n'abagendanyi, babazana ku neza, kuko batinya abantu, ngo ntibabatere amabuye.
44005027	Bamaze kubazana babashira mw'ikoraniro ry'abashingantahe; umuherezi mukuru arababaza
44005028	ati: "Mbega ntitwabihanije cane kutigisha muri rya zina? None raba mwujuje Yerusalemu inyigisho zanyu; ico murondera ni ukudushirako amaraso ya wa muntu. "
44005029	Maze Petero n'intumwa barabishura bati: "Igikwiye ni ukwumvira Imana kuyirutisha abantu.
44005030	Imana ya ba sogokuruza yazuye Yesu, uwo mwebwe mwishe mumumanitse ku giti.
44005031	Uwo Imana yaramushize hejuru n'ukuboko kwayo kw'i buryo, ngo abe Umukuru n'Umukiza, ngo ahe Abisirayeli kwihana no guharirwa ivyaha.
44005032	Natwe turi ivyabona vyo gushingira intahe ivyo, na Mpwemu Yera na we ni uko, uwo Imana yahaye abayumvira. "
44005033	Ariko bo bavyumvise baribwa mu mitima, bashaka kubica.
44005034	Maze hahaguruka umwe mw'ikoraniro ry'abashingantahe, w'Umufarisayo yitwa Gamaliyeli, umwigisha w'ivyagezwe, yubahwa n'abantu bose, avuga ko bataramura abo bantu akanya gato.
44005035	Maze arababarira ati: "Yemwe bagabo b'Abisirayeli, ni mwirinde mumenye uko mugirira aba bantu;
44005036	kuko mu misi ishize Teyuda yadutse yiyita agakomeye, igitigiri c'abantu gishika nk'amajana ane baramukurikira. " Maze aricwa, abamwumvira bose barasabagira, bacika ubusa.
44005037	Hanyuma yiwe haduka Yuda Umunyagalilaya, mu misi yo kwandikwa, yikwegera abantu inyuma; na we apfa rubi, n'abamwumvira bose uko bangana barasabagira.
44005038	Kandi none ndababwire; ni muzibukire aba bantu, mubarekure; kuko iyi nama n'iki gikorwa ni vyaba biturutse mu bantu, bizosendwa;
44005039	ariko ni vyaba biturutse ku Mana, ntimuzoshobora kubatsinda, ntimuzosange muhaye murwanya Imana.
44005040	Baramwemerera, maze bahamagaje intumwa, barazitonagura, barazihanikiriza ngo ntizizokwigishe mw'izina rya Yesu, maze barazirekura.
44005041	Nuko bava mu maso y'abacamanza, banezerejwe n'uko bemerewe gukurwako urupfasoni ku bw'iryo zina.
44005042	Kandi imisi yose mu rusengero no mu mihana ntibahengeshanya kwigisha no kuvuga ubutumwa bwiza bwa Yesu, ko ari we Kristo.
44006001	Kandi muri iyo misi, abigishwa bariko baragwira, Abayuda bavuye i Bugiriki bidodombera Abaheburayo kavukire, kuko abapfakazi babo birengagizwa ku ngaburo y'imisi yose.
44006002	Bamwe icumi na babiri bakoranya ishengero ry'abigishwa bati: "Ntibibereye yuko twebwe tureka kwigisha ijambo ry'Imana kubwo kugaburira ivyo ku meza.
44006003	Nuko, bavukanyi, ni murabe muri mwebwe abantu indwi bashimwa, buzuye Mpwemu Yera n'ubwenge, tubashire muri iki gikorwa.
44006004	Ariko tweho tuzoshishikara gusenga no kugabura ijambo ry'Imana. "
44006005	Ayo majambo ishengero ryose rirayashima, batoranya Stefano, umuntu yuzuye ukwizera na Mpwemu Yera, Filipo, Purokoro, Nikanori, Timoni, Parumena na Nikolayo, Umunyantiyokiya yatoye idini y'Abayuda.
44006006	Babashira imbere y'intumwa, kandi bamaze gusenga zibarambikako ibiganza.
44006007	Nuko ijambo ry'Imana riragwira; abigishwa barongerekana cane i Yerusalemu, n'isinzi ry'abaherezi bumvira ukwizera.
44006008	Stefano yari yuzuye ubuntu bw' Imana n'ubushobozi, yakora ibitangaza n'ibimenyetso bikomeye mu bantu.
44006009	Ariko hava hasi abantu bamwe bo mu rusengero rw'Abaliberutino, urwo Abanyakurene, urwo Abanyalekisanderiya, n'urwo Abanyakilikiya n'iyo Abanyasiya, baja impari na Stefano,
44006010	ariko ntibashobora gutsinda ubwenge na Mpwemu bimuvugisha.
44006011	Nuko bahera abagabo bo kuvuga bati: "Twumvise avuga amajambo yo gutyoza Mose n'Imana. "
44006012	Bosha abantu, abakuru n'abahinga b'ivyanditswe baramugira, baramufata, bamujana mw'ikoraniro ry'abashingantahe.
44006013	Bahagarika ivyabona vy'ibinyoma, baravuga bati: "Uwu muntu nta ho ahumeka gutuka aha hantu hera n'ivyagezwe;
44006014	kuko twumvise avuga ko Yesu Umunyanazareti azosambura aha hantu, kandi ngo azohindura imigenzo twahawe na Mose. "
44006015	Abicaye mw'ikoraniro ry'abashingantahe bose bamuhanze amaso babona mu maso hiwe, hasa n'aho umumarayika.
44007001	Umuherezi mukuru aramubaza ati: "Mbega ivyo ni ko biri? "
44007002	Na we aramwishura ati: "Yemwe bavukanyi kandi ba data, ni mwumve; Imana y'icubahiro yiyeretse sogokuruza Aburahamu, ari i Mesopotamiya, ataraja kugerera i Harani,
44007003	iramubarira iti: 'Va mu gihugu canyu no mu muryango wanyu, uje mu gihugu nzokwereka.'
44007004	Maze ava mu gihugu c'i Bukaludaya, agerera i Harani. Se amaze gupfa, iramwimura, imuzana muri iki gihugu mubamwo ubu.
44007005	Ariko ntiyakimuhayemwo umugabane, naho hoba aho gushinga ikirenge; isezerana kuzokimuha ngo kibe itongo ryiwe n'iryo uruvyaro rwiwe, kandi ataragira umwana. "
44007006	Kandi Imana ivuga itya iti: "Uruvyaro rwawe ruzoba abanyamahanga mu kindi gihugu, bazobagira abaja, babagirire nabi imyaka amajana ane.
44007007	Kandi ihanga rizobagira abaja ni jewe nzoricirako iteka, Imana ni ko yagize iti: "Ariko amaherezo bazovayo, bansengere aha hantu. "
44007008	Maze imuha isezerano ryo guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo. Nuko avyara Isaka, amuhimbura igikoba c'ubugabo ku musi ugira umunani; Isaka avyara Yakobo, Yakobo avyara ba sogokuruza bakuru icumi na babiri.
44007009	Ba sogokuruza bagirira Yosefu ishari, baramugurisha ngo ajanwe mu Misiri. Imana ibana na we,
44007010	imukiza mu marushwa yiwe yose, imuha amahirwe n'ubwenge kuri Farawo, umwami wo mu Misiri, amugira icegera ciwe ngo aganze mu Misiri, amuzeza n'urugo rwiwe rwose.
44007011	Ikigoyi gitera mu Misiri hose n'i Kanani, hatera n'amarushwa menshi, kandi ba sogokuruza babura ivyo kurya.
44007012	Maze Yakobo yumvise yuko mu Misiri hari amasumo, atuma ba sogokuruza ubwa mbere.
44007013	Kandi ubugira kabiri Yosefu yibarira abavukanyi biwe, umuryango wa Yosefu umenywa na Farawo.
44007014	Yosefu atuma kuzana se Yakobo n'abo mu nzu yabo bose, uko ari mirongo irindwi na batanu.
44007015	Yakobo aramanuka, aja mu Misiri; agwayo, bo na ba sogokuruza.
44007016	Babajana i Shekemu, babahamba mw'isenga Aburahamu yaguze igiciro c'ifeza n'abana ba Hamori i Shekemu.
44007017	Ariko igihe c'isezerano kigira gishike, iryoImana yasezeraniye Aburahamu, abantu baragwira, baba benshi mu Misiri,
44007018	gushitsa aho uwundi mwami yimikiwe mu Misiri atigeze kumenya ivya Yosefu.
44007019	Uwo mwami agirira ubugunge ubwoko bwacu, agirira ba sogokuruza nabi, abategeka guheb'abana babo b'inzoya kugira ngo ntibabeho.
44007020	Muri ico gihe Mose aravuka, yari mwiza cane, bamurerera mu nzu kwa se amezi atatu;
44007021	amaze gutabwa, umukobwa wa Farawo aramutora, amurerera kuba umwana wiwe.
44007022	Mose yigishwa ubwenge bwose bw'Abanyamisiri, agira ubushobozi mu majambo yiwe no mu bikorwa vyiwe.
44007023	Maze ariko aramara imyaka mirongo ine avutse, haza iciyumviro mu mutima wiwe co kugendera abavukanyi b'Abisirayeli.
44007024	Abonye umuntu agirirwa nabi, aramutabara, ahora iyo mpahazwa, yica wa Munyamisiri.
44007025	Yibwira yuko abo i wabo botahura ko Imana ibakirisha ukuboko kwiwe; ariko ntibabimenya.
44007026	Bukeye bw'aho, asanga abarwana, ageza kubatatura ati: "Yemwe bagabo, muri umuryango umwe, ni iki gitumye mugiriranira nabi? "
44007027	Ariko uwagirira umubanyi wiwe nabi aramusunika, aramubaza ati: "Ni nde yakugize umukuru canke umucamanza wacu?
44007028	Mbega ugomba kunyica, nk'uko ejo wishe wa Munyamisiri? "
44007029	Mose yumvise iryo jambo, arahunga, aba umwimuka mu gihugu c'I Midiyani, avyarirayo abahungu babiri.
44007030	Imyaka mirongo ine ishize, umumarayika amubonekerera mu rubeya rw'umuriro waka mu gisaka c'amahwa mu bugaragwa bwo ku musozi Sinayi.
44007031	Mose abonye ivyo biramutangaza; akivyegera ngo avyihweze, havuga ijwi ry'Uhoraho
44007032	riti: "Ni jewe Mana ya ba sogokuruza bawe, Imana ya Aburahamu, Imana ya Isaka, Imana ya Yakobo. " Mose ahinda agashitsi, ntiyatinyuka kwihweza.
44007033	Uhoraho aramubarira ati: "Kura ibirato mu birenge vyawe, kuko aho hantu uhagaze ari ahera. "
44007034	Ni ukuri nabonye amarushwa abantu banje bari mu Misiri barimwo, numvise ukuniha kwabo, none manukanywe no kubarokora; kandi rero ni uze ndagutume mu Misiri. "
44007035	Uwo Mose, umwe banka bati: "Ni nde yakugize umukuru canke umucamanza? ni we Imana yatumye kuba umukuru n'umucunguzi, abihawe n'ukuboko kw'umumarayika yamubonekereye muri ca gisaka.
44007036	Uwo abakurayo, amaze gukora ibitangaza n'ibimenyetso mu gihugu ca Misiri, no ku Kiyaga Gitukura no mu bugaragwa, imyaka mirongo ine.
44007037	Uwo Mose ni we yabwiye Abisirayeli ati: "Imana izobahagurukiriza uwuvugishwa na yo mu b'i wanyu, ameze nkanje. "
44007038	Kandi uwo Mose ni we yari mw'ishengero ryo mu bugaragwa, ari kumwe n'umumarayika yavuganiye na we ku musozi Sinayi, kandi ari kumwe na ba sogokuruza; kandi yaherejwe amajambo y'ubugingo ngo ayaduhe.
44007039	Ba sogokuruza banse kumwumvira, baramwikunkumura, basubira mu Misiri mu mitima yabo,
44007040	babwira Aroni bati: "Ni uturonkere imana zo kutuja imbere; kuko umwe Mose yaturongoye adukura mu gihugu ca Misiri, tutazi ico yabaye. "
44007041	Bironkera igishushanyo c'inka muri iyo misi, ico kigirwamana bakizanira ibimazi, bahimbarwa n'ibikorwa vy'intoke zabo.
44007042	Ariko Imana iraba hirya, irabaheba ngo basenge ingabo zo kw'ijuru; nk'uko vyanditswe mu gitabo c'abavugishwa n'Imana, ngo Mbega hari ibitungwa bibazwe canke ibimazi mwanshikaniye, Ya myaka uko ari mirongo ine yo mu bugaragwa, yemwe ab'inzu ya Isirayeli?
44007043	Mwareruye ihema rya Moloki, N'inyenyeri y'ikigirwamana Refani, ari ibishushanyo mwironkeye ngo mubisenge; Nanje nzobambukana hirya y'i Babuloni.
44007044	Ba sogokuruza bari bafise ihema ry'ibisate vy'amabuye vy'amabwirizwa icumi, hamwe bari mu bugaragwa, nk'uko iyavuganye na Mose yabigeze, yamubwiye kurigereranya n'ikigereranyo yabonye.
44007045	Iryo, ba sogokuruza barihawe na ba sekuru babo, barishikana ino, Yosuwa ari kumwe na bo, hamwe batsinda amahanga, Imana iyirukana imbere ya ba sogokuruza, gushitsa ku gihe ca Dawidi.
44007046	Kandi Dawidi aronka amahirwe imbere y'Imana, asaba kwubakira Imana ya Yakobo aho kuba.
44007047	Ariko Salomo ni we yayubakiye ingoro.
44007048	Yamara Iyisumbavyose ntiba mu zubakishijwe amaboko; nk'uko uwavugishijwe n'Imana yavuze
44007049	ati: "Ijuru ni ryo ntebe yanje y'ubwami, Isi na yo ni indava y'ibirenge vyanje; Muzonyubakira inzu ki? ni ko Uhoraho abajije, Canke nzoruhukira ahantu ki?
44007050	Mbega intoke zanje si zo zaremye ivyo vyose?
44007051	Yemwe abadaca bugufi, mwa badadaza imitima mukiziba amatwi, na ntaryo murwanya Mpwemu Yera. Uko ba sogokuruza banyu bakora, ni ko namwe mukora.
44007052	Ni nde mu bavugishijwe n'Imana ba sogokuruza banyu batahamye? Bishe ababanje kumenyekanisha ivyo kuza kwa wa Mugororotsi, none namwe mwaramuguze muramwica.
44007053	Ari mwebwe mwahawe ivyagezwe bizanywe n'abamarayika, ntimwavyitondera. "
44007054	Bavyumvise baribwa mu mitima, bamuhekenyera imisaya.
44007055	Ariko Stefano yuzuye Mpwemu Yera, ahanga amaso mw'ijuru, abona ubwiza bw'Imana, na Yesu ahagaze i buryo bw'Imana.
44007056	Aravuga ati: "Ehe ndabonye ijuru rikingurutse, n'Umwana w'umuntu ahagaze i buryo bw'Imana. "
44007057	Barayogora n'amajwi arenga, biziba amatwi, bamugwirako icarimwe,
44007058	bamuhindira inyuma y'igisagara, bamwicisha amabuye; kandi abamwagirije bari bafashije hasi imitamana yabo imbere y'ibirenge vy'umusore yitwa Sawuli.
44007059	Maze bakiriko baratera Stefano amabuye, arambaza, aravuga ati: "Mwami Yesu, akira ubugingo bwanje. "
44007060	Araheza arapfukama, asemerera n'ijwi rirenga ati: "Mwami, ntubaharureko iki caha. " Amaze kuvuga atyo, aca aracikana. Kandi Sawuli na we yarabishimye ko yicwa.
44008001	Bahera kuri uwo musi bahama cane ishengero ry'i Yerusalemu. Bose basabagirira mu ntara z'i Yudaya n'i Samariya, ukuyemwo intumwa gusa.
44008002	Abantu bubaha Imana bahamba Stefano, baramuborogera cane.
44008003	Ariko Sawuli yatikiza ishengero; yinjira mu nzu zose, agakuramwo abagabo n'abagore, akabashira mw'ibohero.
44008004	Ariko abasabagiye bagendagenda bavuga ijambo ry'Imana.
44008005	Na Filipo aramanuka, aja mu gisagara c'i Samariya, abamenyesha ivya Kristo.
44008006	Abantu benshi bashira umutima ku vyo Filipo avuga bashize hamwe, bumvise kandi babonye ibimenyetso akora.
44008007	Kuko benshi muri bo bari binjiwemwo n'impwemu zihumanye zabavamwo, ziboroga n'amajwi arenga; kandi n'abari bamugaye n'abacumbagira benshi barakizwa.
44008008	Haba umunezero mwinshi muri ico gisagara.
44008009	Kandi hariho umuntu yitwa Simoni, yahora akora ivyo ubupfumu muri ico gisagara, akumiza ubwoko bw'Abasamariya, akiyita agakomeye.
44008010	Bama bamushizeko umutima bose, uhereye ku boroshe ugashitsa ku bahambaye bati: "Uwu ni we bwa bushobozi bw'Imana bwitwa Ubuhambaye. "
44008011	Ariko icatuma bamushirako umutima ni uko uhereye kera yabumiza n'ubupfumu bwiwe.
44008012	Ariko bizeye ubutumwa bwiza Filipo ababwiye bw'ubwami bw'Imana, n'ubwo izina rya Yesu Kristo, abagabo n'abagore barabatizwa.
44008013	Na simoni na we arizera, kandi amaze kubatizwa yamana na Filipo. Abonye ibimenyetso n'ibitangaza bihambaye vyakorwa, arumirwa.
44008014	Maze intumwa ziri i Yerusalemu zumvise yuko Abasamariya bemeye ijambo ry'Imana, zirungikayo Petero na Yohana,
44008015	na bo bamanutseyo barabasengera ngo bahabwe Mpwemu Yera;
44008016	kuko Mpwemu ataribwamanuke ngo aje no kuri umwe muri bo, bari babatijwe gusa mw'izina ry'Umwami Yesu.
44008017	Maze babarambikako ibiganza, bahabwa Mpwemu Yera.
44008018	Ariko Simoni, abonye yuko abarambitsweko ibiganza vy'intumwa bahabwa Mpwemu Yera, azizanira amahera
44008019	ati: "Nanje ni mumpe ubwo bushobozi, kugira ngo uwo nzorambikako ibiganza azohabwe Mpwemu Yera. "
44008020	Petero aramubwira ati: "Ifeza zawe ziragapfana nawe, kuko ugira ngo ingabire y'Imana woyironkesha amahera.
44008021	Nta n'agahimba ufise, nta n'akagabane kavyo, kuko umutima wawe udatunganye imbere y'Imana.
44008022	Nuko wihane ubwo bubi bwawe, usenge Umwami Imana, namba kumbure ivyo wiyumviriye mu mutima wawe wobiharirwa.
44008023	Kuko mbona yuko uri mw'ibamba ry'umururazi no mu ngoyi zo kugabitanya. "
44008024	Simoni aramwishura ati: "Munsengere ku Mwami Imana, ivyo muvuze ntihagire ikimbako. "
44008025	Na bo bamaze gushinga intahe, no kuvuga ijambo ry'Umwami Yesu, basubira i Yerusalemu, bagenda baravuga ubutumwa bwiza mu mihana myinshi y'Abasamariya
44008026	Maze umumarayika w'Umwami Imana abarira Filipo ati: " "Va hasi uje mu bumanuko, ushike ku nzira imanuka iva i Yerusalemu ikaja i Gaza; imwe yo mu bugaragwa. "
44008027	Avahasi, aragenda. Haza Umunyetiyopiya, inkone y'ububasha bwinshi yakorera Kanidake, umwamikazi w'Abanyetiyopiya, ni yo yazezwa itunga ryiwe ryose, yari yagiye i Yerusalemu gusenga.
44008028	Yahindukiye yicaye mu mukogote wiwe ukwegwa n'amafarasi, asoma muri Yesaya yavugishwa n'Imana.
44008029	Mpwemu abarira Filipo ati: "Ni wegere uriya mukogote, ugendane na wo. "
44008030	Filipo yirukirayo, yumva asoma muri Yesaya yavugishwa n'Imana; aramubaza ati: "Ivyo usoma urabitahuye? "
44008031	Na we ati: "Nobishobora nte, ntabonye uwubindongoramwo? " Yinginga Filipo ngo yurire bicarane.
44008032	Igice co mu vyanditswe yasoma cari iki, ngo Yajanywe nk'intama bajana mw'ibagiro, Nk'uko umwagazi w'intama utekerereza imbere y'uwuyikata ubwoya Ni ko atakuyeko umunwa.
44008033	Hamwe yacishwa bugufi nta numwe yamuciriye urwo ukuri, Ni nde azoshobora kudonda ivyo uruvyaro rwiwe? Kuko ubugingo bwiwe bukuwe mw'isi.
44008034	Iyo nkone ibaza Filipo iti: "Ndakubaza, uwavugishwa n' Imana yavuze ayo majambo kuri nde? Ni we yayivuzeko, canke yayavuze ku wundi? "
44008035	Filipo ateranura akanwa, atangurira kuri ivyo vyanditswe, amubwira ubutumwa bwiza bwa Yesu.
44008036	Bakigenda mu nzira, bashika ahari amazi; iyo nkone iramubaza iti: "Ehe amazi; ikimbuza kubatizwa ni igiki? " [
44008037	Filipo arayishura ati: "Namba wizeye mu mutima wawe wose birashoboka. " Na yo iti: "Nizeye Yesu Kristo ko ari Umwana w'Imana. " ]
44008038	Ivuga ko bahagarika umukogote, baramanukana baja mu mazi bompi, Filipo n'iyo nkone, arayibatiza.
44008039	Bavuye mu mazi, Mpwemu w'Uhoraho Imana ajana Filipo, iyo nkone ntiyasubira kumubona, kuko yashishikaye kugenda inezerewe.
44008040	Ariko Filipo abonekera muri Azoto, ahahita avuga ubutumwa bwiza mu bisagara vyose, kugeza aho yashikiye i Kayisariya.
44009001	Ariko Sawuli, akigenda afuhagira, afitiye abigishwa b'Umwami imihigo n'ubwicanyi, aja ku muherezi mukuru,
44009002	amusaba amakete yo guha abo nsengero z'Abayuda z'i Damasiko, kugira ngo ni yabona abantu bakurikira Inzira ya Yesu, ari abagabo canke abagore, abajane i Yerusalemu mw'ibohero.
44009003	Maze ariko aragenda, agira ashike i Damasiko, haza umuco giturumbuka, uvuye mw'ijuru, umukayanganira irya n'ino.
44009004	Yikubita hasi, yumva ijwi rimubaza riti: "Sawuli, Sawuli, umpigira iki? "
44009005	Aramubaza ati: "Uri nde ga Mwami? " Na we ati: "Ni jewe Yesu, uwo uriko urahiga;
44009006	ariko va hasi, ushike mu gisagara, uzobarirwa ivyo ukwiye gukora. "
44009007	Abagabo bajanye na we bahagarara badakoma, kuko bumvise ijwi, ata muntu babona.
44009008	Sawuli aravyuka, ava hasi, maze akanuye amaso ntiyagira ico abona. Bamufata ukuboko, bamushikana i Damasiko.
44009009	Amarayo gatatu, atabona, ata co arya, ata co anywa.
44009010	I Damasiko hari umwigishwa yitwa Ananiya. Umwami Yesu aramwiyereka, aramuhamagara ati: "Ananiya. " Na we ati: "Sabwe, Mwami. "
44009011	Umwami aramubarira ati: "Va hasi, uje mu nzira yitwa Iyigororotse, ubarizeyo mu rugo kwa Yuda umuntu yitwa Sawuli w'i Taruso, kuko ariko arasenga.
44009012	Kandi yabonye umuntu yitwa Ananiya yinjira aho ari, amurambikako ibiganza, kugira ngo ahumuke. "
44009013	Ananiya aramwishura ati: "Mwami, uwo mugabo ko numvise benshi bavuga ivyiwe, vy'inabi nyinshi yagirira abera bawe i Yerusalemu;
44009014	kandi n'ino ahafise ububasha abuhawe n'abaherezi bakuru, bwo kuboha abambaza izina ryawe bose. "
44009015	Umwami aramwishura ati: "Pfa kugenda, kuko uwo muntu ari ikintu nitoranirije, ngo ajane izina ryanje imbere y'abanyamahanga, abami n'Abisirayeli.
44009016	Nanje nzomwereka imibabaro uko ingana azoba akwiye kubabazwa ahorwa izina ryanje. "
44009017	Ananiya aragenda, yinjira mu nzu, amurambikako ibiganza, aramubwira ati: "Sawuli, muvukanyi wanje, Umwami arantumye, ni we Yesu yakubonekereye mu nzira wazananye, ngo uhumuke, wuzuzwe Mpwemu Yera. "
44009018	Uwo mwanya ibisa n'ibikaragashi bimuva ku maso, arahumuka, ava hasi, arabatizwa;
44009019	maze ararya, intege ziragaruka. Amarana imisi n'abigishwa b'i Damasiko;
44009020	aca aherako avuga mu nsengero z'Abayuda ivya Yesu, yuko ari Umwana w'Imana.
44009021	Abamwumvise bose barumirwa bati: "Mbega uwu si we yatikije abambaza iryo zina i Yerusalemu? Kandi ni co cari kimuzanye n'ino, kugira ngo abashire abaherezi bakuru bari baboshwe. "
44009022	Ariko Sawuli arushiriza kugira ubushobozi, atsinda Abayuda baba i Damasiko, abereka yuko Yesu ari we Kristo.
44009023	Hashize imisi myinshi, Abayuda baja inama yo kumwica.
44009024	Maze Sawuli amenya inama yabo. Bamutegera ku marembo ku murango no mw'ijoro kugira ngo bamwice.
44009025	Maze abigishwa biwe bamujana mw'ijoro, bamucisha ku ruhome rw'amabuye, bamwururukiriza mu giseke.
44009026	Ashitse i Yerusalemu, agerageza kwifatanya n'abigishwa. Bose baramutinya, ntibemera ko ari umwigishwa.
44009027	Maze Barunaba aramwakira, amushira intumwa, aziganira ingene yaboneye Umwami Yesu mu nzira, n'ingene yavuganye na we, kandi n'ingene yavuze ashize amanga mw'izina rya Yesu i Damasiko.
44009028	Aba kumwe na bo uko bukeye uko bwije i Yerusalemu,
44009029	avuga ashize amanga mw'izina ry'Umwami Yesu; yaravuga aharira n'Abayuda bavuye i Bugiriki; na bo barondera ingene bomwica.
44009030	Ariko abavukanyi babimenye, bamumanukana i Kayisariya, bamurungika i Taruso. "
44009031	Nuko ishengero ryose ryari hose i Yudaya; Galilaya n'i Samariya rigira amahoro, rirahangama. Kandi rigenda ryubaha Umwami Yesu, rihagarikiwe na Mpwemu Yera, riragwira.
44009032	Nuko Petero agendagenda hose, amanuka no ku bera baba i Luda,
44009033	asangayo umuntu yitwa Ayineya, yari amaze imyaka munani avundira mu buriri, kuko yari yaramugaye.
44009034	Petero aramubwira ati: " "Ayineya, Yesu Kristo aragukijije; vyuka, wizingire ikirago. " " Aca avyuka ako kanya.
44009035	Ababa i Luda n'i Saroni bose bamubonye bahindukirira Umwami Yesu.
44009036	Kandi i Yopa hari umwigishwa yitwa Tabita, risobanurwa ngo Doruka. Uwo mugore yari n'ibikorwa vyiza vyinshi, n'ubuntu bwinshi yagira.
44009037	Muri iyo misi ararwara, arapfa. Bamaze kwuhagira ikiziga, bagishira mu nzu yo hejuru.
44009038	Kandi kuko i Luda hari hafi y'i Yopa, abigishwa, bumvise ko Petero ari yo ari, bamutumako abantu babiri, bamwinginga bati: " "Ntutebe kudushikira. "
44009039	Petero arahaguruka, ajana na bo. Ashitseyo bamujana muri ya gorofa, abapfakazi bose bahagarara i ruhande yiwe barira, berekana amakanzu n'imitamana Doruka yajishe akiri muri bo.
44009040	Petero arabataramura bose, arapfukama, arasenga; maze ahindukirira umuvyimba ati: "Tabita, vyuka. " Arakanura; maze abonye Petero, aravyuka, aricara.
44009041	Amufata ukuboko, aramuhagarika. Maze ahamagara abera n'abapfakazi, amubaha ari muzima.
44009042	Bimenyekana i Yopa hose, benshi bizera Umwami Yesu.
44009043	Maze amara imisi myinshi i Yopa, kwa Simoni umuhinguzi w'insato.
44010001	I Kayisariya hari umuntu yitwa Koruneliyo, intwazangabo z'abasoda ijana wo mu ngabo zitwa Abanyetaliya.
44010002	Yari umuntu yubaha Imana akayitinyana n'abo mu nzu yiwe bose, yarafasha cane abagowe, agasenga Imana ubudasiba.
44010003	Abona yeretswe imbonankubone, umumarayika w'Imana yinjiye i we hari nk'isaha icenda z'umurango, aramuhamagara ati: "Koruneliyo. "
44010004	Na we amukanurira amaso, afise ubwoba, aramubaza ati: "Ni iki ga Mwami? " Aramwishura ati: "Ugusenga kwawe n'ubuntu bwawe vyaduze biba icibutso imbere y'Imana.
44010005	None rero tuma abantu i Yopa, utumeko umuntu yitwa Simoni, ari we Petero;
44010006	yatse indaro kwa Simoni umubamvyi w'insato, urugo rwiwe ruri i ruhande y'ikiyaga. " "
44010007	Umumarayika vyavugana amaze kugenda, Koroneliyo ahamagara babiri bo mu bakozi biwe, n'umusoda yubaha Imana wo mu bamugendanira.
44010008	Ahejeje kubiganira vyose, abatuma i Yopa.
44010009	Bukeye bw'aho, bakigenda, bari hafi gushika mu gisagara, Petero yurira hejuru mw'igorofa gusenga, hari nk'isaha zitandatu.
44010010	Yumva arashonje, agomba kurya. Bakibirondera, amera nk'uwurota. "
44010011	Abona ijuru ryugurutse, maze hamanuka ikintu kimeze nk'uruhuzu runiniya, rufashwe ku mitwe ine, kija hasi,
44010012	harimwo ubwoko bwose bw'ibigenza amaguru ane, ibikwega inda hasi vyo kw'isi n'ibiguruka vyo mu kirere.
44010013	Haza ijwi, riramubarira riti: "Va hasi, Petero, ubage, urye. "
44010014	Petero ati: "Oyaye, Mwami, kuko ntigeze ndya ikizira canke igihumanya. "
44010015	Iryo jwi risubira kuza ubugira kabiri, riramubarira riti: "Ivyo Imana ihumanuye, reka kuvyita ibizira. "
44010016	Biba bityo gatatu, ico kintu gica gisubizwa mw'ijuru.
44010017	Petero akizazaniwe mu mutima n'ivyo abonye yeretswe ivyo ari vyo, abantu batumwe na Koruneliyo, bahejeje kubaza urugo rwa Simoni, bahagarara kw'irembo,
44010018	barahamagara, babaza yuko Simoni ari we Petero ari ho yatse indaro.
44010019	Petero aciyumvira ivyo yeretswe, Mpwemu aramubarira ati: "Hari abantu batatu bariko barakurondera.
44010020	None va hasi, wururuke ujane na bo ata co ukekeranya, kuko ari jewe ndabatumye. "
44010021	Petero arururuka, asanga abo bantu aho bari, arababarira ati: "Ni jewe uwo murondera. Mbega mugenzwa ni iki? "
44010022	Baramwishura bati: "Koruneliyo, intwazangabo z'abasoda ijana, umuntu agororoka yubaha Imana, ashimwa n'ubwoko bwose bw'Abayuda, yabariwe n'umumarayika yera kugutumako, ngo uze i we, yumve amajambo yawe. " "
44010023	Maze arabinjiza, abaha indaro. Bukeye bw'aho, Petero arikora, avanayo na bo, n'abavukanyi bamwe b'i Yopa bajana na we.
44010024	Bukeye bw'aho bashika i Kayisariya, Koruneliyo yari abiteze, yakoranije incuti ziwe n'abakunzi bo ku mutima.
44010025	Petero agira yinjire, Koruneliyo aramusanganira, yikubita imbere y'ibirenge vyiwe, aramupfukamira.
44010026	Maze Petero amukura hasi ati: " "Va hasi, nanje ndi umuntu nkawe. "
44010027	Bakivugana, arinjira asanga abakoraniyeho benshi,
44010028	arababwira ati: "Ubwanyu murazi yuko kizira ko umuntu w'Umuyuda yifatanya n'uwo ubundi bwoko, canke ko amugendera; ariko jeho, Imana yanyeretse yuko hatogira umuntu nita ikizira canke igihumanya.
44010029	Ni co catumye nza, ntarinze guhakana, ntumweko. None rero ndabaza ico mwantumiyeko ico ari co. "
44010030	Koruneliyo ati: "Hashize imisi ine, nka bugingo ubu, nariko ndasenga ari isaha icenda, ndi mu nzu yanje; maze umuntu ahagarara imbere yanje, yambaye impuzu ikayangana,
44010031	arambwira ati: 'Koruneliyo, ugusenga kwawe kwarumviswe, n'ubuntu bwawe bwibutswe imbere y'Imana.'
44010032	Nuko tuma i Yopa, utumeko Simoni ari we Petero. Yatse indaro mu rugo kwa Simoni umuhinguzi w'insato, i ruhande y'ikiyaga.
44010033	Uwo mwanya nca ndagutumako rero, nawe urayobotse ko uje. None rero twese turi hano imbere y'Imana, kwumva ivyo Umwami Imana yakugeze kutubwira vyose. "
44010034	Petero yanzika kuvuga ati: "Ni ukuri ni ho nkimenya yuko Imana itarobanura abantu ku butoni,
44010035	ariko mu mahanga yose uwubaha, agakora ivyo ukugororoka, iramwemera.
44010036	Ijambo Imana yatumye ku Bisirayeli, ivugisha Yesu Kristo ubutumwa bwiza bw'amahoro, ni we Mwami wa bose;
44010037	iryo jambo mwebwe murarizi, ryamamaye i Yudaya hose, ritanguriye i Galilaya, hanyuma y'umubatizo uwo Yohana yigishije;
44010038	rivuga ivya Yesu Umunyanazareti, ingene Imana yamusutseko Mpwemu Yera n'ubushobozi, akagenda agirira abantu neza, agakiza abo bose wa mugarariji atwaza amanyama, kuko Imana yari kumwe na we. "
44010039	Natwe turi ivyabona vyo gushingira intahe ivyo umwe bishe, bamumanitse ku giti yakoze vyose mu gihugu c'Abayuda bo n'i Yerusalemu.
44010040	Uwo, Imana iramuzura ku musi ugira gatatu, imuha guserurwa ahibonekeza,
44010041	si imbere y'abantu bose, ariko imbere y'ivyabona vyatoranijwe n'Imana ivyo bitarabaho, ni twebwe, abasangira na we, turya kandi tunywa, amaze kuzuka mu bapfuye.
44010042	Atugera kumenyesha abantu no gushinga intahe ko ari we Imana yashinze kuba Umucamanza w'abariho n'abapfuye.
44010043	Abavugishwa n'Imana bose bamushingiye intahe, bavuga yuko uwumwizera wese azoharirwa ivyaha ku bwo izina ryiwe.
44010044	Petero akivuga ayo majambo, Mpwemu Yera aramanuka, aja ku bariko barumva iryo jambo bose.
44010045	Abizeye bo mu bahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo barumirwa, abazananye na Petero uko bangana, kuko n'abanyamahanga na bo basutsweko ingabire, ari yo Mpwemu Yera.
44010046	Kuko bumvise bavuga izindi ndimi, bahimbaza Imana. Maze Petero arababaza
44010047	ati: "Mbega hari uwoshobora kwima amazi abahawe Mpwemu Yera nkatwe, ngo ntibabatizwe? "
44010048	Avuga ko babatizwa mw'izina rya Yesu Kristo. Baca baramwinginga ngo amareyo imisi.
44011001	Intumwa n'abavukanyi biwe bari i Yudaya bumva yuko abanyamahanga na bo bemeye ijambo ry'Imana.
44011002	Maze Petero aduze i Yerusalemu, abo mu bahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo baramutonganya
44011003	bati: "Ko winjiriye abatahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, ugasangira na bo ! "
44011004	Maze Petero atangura kubasobanurira uko bikurikirana
44011005	ati: "Nari mu gisagara c'i Yopa, ndiko ndasenga, mbona neretswe nko mu nzozi ikintu kimanuka kivuye mw'ijuru, kimeze nk'uruhuzu runiniya rufashwe ku mitwe ine, kiza aho ndi.
44011006	Ndagihanga amaso, ndacitegereza, mbonamwo ibigenza amaguru ane vyo kw'isi, ibikoko vyo mw'ishamba, ibikwega inda hasi n'ibiguruka vyo mu kirere.
44011007	Kandi numva ijwi rimbarira riti: 'Va hasi, Petero, ubage urye.'
44011008	Nanje nti: 'Oyaye, Mwami, kuko ata kizira canke igihumanya cigeze kija mu kanwa kanje.'
44011009	Maze ijwi rimbarira ubugira kabiri rivuye mw'ijuru riti: 'Ivyo Imana ihumanuye, reka kuvyita ibizira.'
44011010	Biba bityo gatatu, biraduzwa vyose, bisubizwa mw'ijuru.
44011011	Uwo mwanya abagabo batatu bavuye i Kayisariya, bantumweko, bahagarara imbere y'inzu turimwo.
44011012	Mpwemu ambarira kujana na bo, ata tandukaniro. Kandi n'abo bavukanyi, uko ari batandatu, turajana, twinjira mu nzu y'uwo mugabo.
44011013	Atwiganira ingene yabonye umumarayika mu nzu yiwe, ahagaze amubarira ati: 'Tuma i Yopa, utumeko Simoni ari we Petero,
44011014	azokubarira amajambo yo kugukizanya n'abo mu nzu yawe bose.'
44011015	Ngitanguye kuvuga, Mpwemu Yera arabamanukira, nk'uko yatumanukiyeko ubwa mbere. "
44011016	Nibuka rya jambo ry'Umwami Yesu, uko yavuze ati: "Yohana yabatirishije amazi, ariko mweho muzobatizwa na Mpwemu Yera. "
44011017	None ko Imana yabahaye ingabire imwe n'iyo natwe twahawe hamwe twizera Umwami Yesu Kristo, jewe ndi igiki gishobora gutangira Imana?
44011018	Bumvise ivyo barihorera, bahimbaza Imana bati: "Noneho rero Imana ihaye n'abanyamahanga kwihana ngo baronke ubugingo. "
44011019	Nuko abasabagijwe n'amarushwa yabaye kubwo ivya Stefano baragenda, bashika i Foyinike, i Kupuro no muri Antiyokiya, ata bandi babarira ijambo ry'Imana atari Abayuda bonyene.
44011020	Ariko hari bamwe muri bo b'abagabo bavuye i Kupuro n'i Kurene bashitse muri Antiyokiya babarira n'Abagiriki na bo, bababwira ubutumwa bwiza bw'Umwami Yesu.
44011021	Ukuboko kw'Umwami kwari kumwe na bo, abantu benshi barizera, bahindukirira Umwami.
44011022	Inkuru yabo ishika mu matwi y'ishengero ry'i Yerusalemu, batuma Barunaba ngo ashirwe ashitse muri Antiyokiya.
44011023	Na we amaze gushikayo, abonye ubuntu bw'Imana, biramunezereza, arabahanura bose ngo bafate ingingo mu mitima yo kwifatanya ubutakivana n'Umwami Yesu.
44011024	Kuko yari imico myiza, yuzuye Mpwemu Yera n'ukwizera. Abantu benshi bagwirirana ku Mwami Yesu.
44011025	Avayo, aja i Taruso kurondera Sawuli,
44011026	amubonye, amujana muri Antiyokiya. Bamarayo umwaka wose, bakorana n'ishengero, bigisha abantu benshi, kandi muri Antiyokiya ni ho abigishwa batanguriye kwitwa Abakristo.
44011027	Muri iyo misi, abavugishwa n'Imana bava i Yerusalemu baja muri Antiyokiya.
44011028	Umwe muri bo yitwa Agabo ava hasi abamenyesha, avugishijwe na Mpwemu yuko ikigoyi cinshi kizotera mw'isi yose. Ico yavuga ni kimwe catera ku butware bwa Kilawudiyo.
44011029	Maze abigishwa, umuntu wese nk'uko atunze, bashinga kurungikira abavukanyi babo baba i Yudaya ivyo kubatabara.
44011030	Babigenza batyo, babirungikira abakuru, bijanye Barunaba na Sawuli.
44012001	Maze nko muri ico gihe umwami Herode ata mu maboko bamwe bo mw'ishengero ngo abagirire nabi.
44012002	Yicisha inkota Yakobo mwene nyina wa Yohana.
44012003	Maze abonye ko bihimbaye Abayuda, ariyongeza, afata na Petero. Hari mu misi y'imitsima itambiwe.
44012004	Amaze kumufata, amushira mw'ibohero, amuha abasoda icumi na batandatu kumurinda ari banebane, agira ngo azomushikirize abantu, Pasika iheze.
44012005	Nuko Petero arindirwa mw'ibohero. Ariko abo ishengero baramusengera, batakambira Imana bakobeje.
44012006	Ku musi Herode bwaca amubashikiriza, muri iryo joro Petero yari asinziriye ari hagati y'abasoda babiri, aboheshejwe iminyororo ibiri, abateramyi bari ku rugi barinda inzu y'ibohero.
44012007	Maze umumarayika w'Umwami Imana amuhagarara i ruhande, umuco ubonesha mu nzu. Akoma Petero mu mbavu, aramukangura ati: "Vyuka ningoga. " Iminyororo imuva ku maboko, irakoroka.
44012008	Umumarayika aramubarira ati: "Kenyera, wambare ibirato vyawe. " Abigenza atyo. Kandi aramubarira ati: "Izingireko umutamana wawe, unkurikire. "
44012009	Arasohoka, aramukurikira, yamara ntiyamenya ivyo umumarayika akoze ko ari ivyo ukuri, ariko agira ngo abonye ivyo yeretswe nko mu nzozi.
44012010	Baciye ku bateramyi ba mbere no ku ba kabiri, bashika kw'irembo ryugajwe umwango w'icuma, rija mu gisagara. Urabiyugururira ubwawo, barenga irembo baca mu nzira imwe, uwo mwanya umumarayika aca amusiga hano.
44012011	Akenge kagarutse, Petero aribwira ati: "Noneho ndamenye vy'ukuri yuko Umwami yatumye umumarayika wiwe, akankiza ukuboko kwa Herode, bo n'ivyo ubwoko bw'Abayuda bwari buroreye vyose. "
44012012	Amaze kuvyiyumvira, aja kwa Mariya, nyina wa Yohana ari we Mariko, aho benshi bari bakoraniye benshi, bariko barasenga.
44012013	Petero akomanga ku rugi rw'irembo, umukobwa w'umushumba yitwa Rode aja kwumvira.
44012014	Amenye ijwi rya Petero akanyamuneza kamubuza kwugurura, arirukanga arinjira, ababarira yuko Petero ahagaze kw'irembo.
44012015	Baramwishura bati: "Urasara. " Na we avuga ashimitse ko ari ivyo ukuri. Bati: "Ni umumarayika wiwe. "
44012016	Ariko Petero ashishikara gukomanga. Buguruye baramubona, barumirwa.
44012017	Arabamama, abiganira uko Umwami Imana yamukuye mw'ibohero, arababwira ati: "Ivyo mubibarire Yakobo n'abavukanyi bandi. " Arahava, aja ahandi.
44012018	Ijoro rikeye, havyuka imivurungano itari mike mu basoda, kuko bazazaniwe ukuntu Petero yabaye.
44012019	Herode amurondeye amubuze, acunaguza abateramyi, avuga ko babajana kubica. Maze ava i Yudaya amanuka i Kayisariya, agumayo.
44012020	Maze ashamirana n'abo muri Tiro n'i Sidoni, na bo bahuza inama, bamujako, bahongera Bulasito, umukuru w'abasasira umwami, basaba impore, kuko igihugu cabo casuma mu gihugu c'uwo mwami.
44012021	Nuko ku musi washinzwe, Herode yambara impuzu z'ubwami, avyagira ku ntebe y'icubahiro, abacurira amajambo.
44012022	Abantu barasemerera bati: "Ni ijwi ry'imana, si iryoumuntu. "
44012023	Uwo mwanya umumarayika w'Umwami Imana aramukubita, kuko adahaye Imana Rurema icubahiro, aturika inyo, aracikana.
44012024	Ariko ijambo ry'Imana riragwira, riramenyekana.
44012025	Kandi Barunaba na Sawuli bava i Yerusalemu, basubira inyuma, bashikirije ivyagabuwe, bajana Yohana, ari we Mariko.
44013001	Kandi muri Antiyokiya, mw'ishengero ryaho, hari abavugishwa n'Imana n'abigisha; umwe ni Barunaba na Simeyoni ari we Nigeru, na Lukiyosi Umunyakurene, na Manayeni yarerewe hamwe n'umwami Herode, hariho na Sawuli.
44013002	Bariko barasenga Umwami Imana bisonzesheje, Mpwemu Yera aravuga ati: "Ni mundobanurire Barunaba na Sawuli bankorere igikorwa nabahamagariye. " "
44013003	Nuko bisonzesheje, basenze, babarambitseko ibiganza, barabarungika.
44013004	Nuko bavuyeyo batumwe na Mpwemu Yera bamanuka i Seleyukiya. Bavayo bari mu bwato bafata i Kupuro.
44013005	Maze bashitse i Salamini, bavuga ijambo ry'Imana mu nsengero z'Abayuda. Kandi bari bafise Yohana agenda arabakorera.
44013006	Bararamiriza baca muri ico kizinga cose, bashika i Pafo, basangayo umugabo w'umukinzi, umuraguzi w'ibinyoma, yari Umuyuda, izina ryiwe ni Bari-Yesu;
44013007	yagendanira Serugiyo Pahulo, icegera ca Kayisari, umuntu w'ubwenge. Uwo ahamagaza Barunaba na Sawuli, ashaka kwumva ijambo ry'Imana.
44013008	Ariko Eluma, uwo mukinzi (izina ryiwe ni ko risobanurwa), arabahaririza, ashaka guhuvya ico cegera ngo nticizere.
44013009	Ariko Sawuli ari we Pahulo, yuzuye Mpwemu Yera, amuhanga amaso
44013010	ati: " "Wewe wuzuye ubugunge bwose n'ububi bwose, wa mwana w'Umurwanizi we, wa mwansi w'ivyo kugororoka vyose, ntuzoreka kugoreka inzira z'Umwami Imana zigororotse? "
44013011	Nuko raba, ukuboko kw'Umwami Imana kuraguhanamiye, ugira uhume, umare imisi utabona izuba. " Ako kanya igipfungu n'umwiza bimwubikizako, agenda azimagirika arondera uwo kumufata ukuboko.
44013012	Ico cegera kibonye ibibaye kirizera, gitangajwe n'ivyo cigishijwe vy'Umwami Yesu.
44013013	Maze Pahulo n'abari kumwe na we bava i Pafo bari mu bwato, bafata i Peruga muri Pamfiliya. Yohana abasigayo, asubira i Yerusalemu.
44013014	Ariko bo bava i Peruga, bararamiriza, bashika muri Antiyokiya h'i Pisidiya; ku musi w'isabato binjira mu rusengero rw'Abayuda, baricara.
44013015	Isomwa ry'ivyagezwe n'ivyo abavugishwa n'Imana riheze, abakuru b'urusengero rw'Abayuda batuma kuri bo bati: " "Bavukanyi, ni mwaba mufise ijambo ryo guhanura abantu, ni murivuge. "
44013016	Pahulo ava hasi, arabamama, arababarira ati: "Yemwe bagabo b'Abisirayeli, namwe abubaha Imana, ni mwumve. "
44013017	Imana y'ubu bwoko bw'Abisirayeli yatoranije ba sogokuruza, kandi ishira abantu hejuru hamwe bari abanyamahanga mu gihugu ca Misiri, ikabakuzayo ukuboko gukomeye.
44013018	Yihanganira ingeso zabo nk'imyaka mirongo ine mu bugaragwa.
44013019	Imaze guhonya amahanga indwi mu gihugu c'i Kanani, ibegurira ico gihugu cabo kuba inyegu yabo. Maze nk'imyaka amajana ane na mirongo itanu ishize,
44013020	ibaha abacamanza, gushitsa ku wavugishwa n'Imana Samweli.
44013021	Hanyuma bayisaba umwami, Imana ibaha Sawuli umwana wa Kishi, umugabo wo mu muryango wa Benyamini, amara ku butware imyaka mirongo ine.
44013022	Imukuye, ibahagurukiriza Dawidi kuba umwami wabo, imushingira intahe iti: "Ndabonye Dawidi umwana wa Isayi umuntu ameze nk'uko umutima wanje ugomba, azokora ivyo ngomba vyose.
44013023	Mu ruvyaro rw'uwo, nk'uko Imana yasezeranye, yazaniye Abisirayeli Umukiza, ni we Yesu.
44013024	Ataraza, Yohana yari yigishije ubwoko bwose bw'Abisirayeli ukubatizwa kwo kwihana. "
44013025	Ariko Yohana ariko arasozera urugendo rwiwe, arababaza ati: "Mbega mwiyumvira ko ndi nde? " Jewe sindi we. Mugabo hari uwuzoza mu nyuma yanje, kandi jewe ntibimbereye no gupfundurura ibirato vyo mu birenge vyiwe.
44013026	Bagabo bavukanyi, bana bo mu muryango wa Aburahamu, namwe abubaha Imana, ijambo ry'ako gakiza ni twebwe ryatumweko.
44013027	Kuko ababa i Yerusalemu n'abakuru babo batamumenye, canke amajambo y'abavugishwa n' Imana asomwa ukw'isabato itashe, ni co catumye bashitsa ivyo bavugishijwe, hamwe bamutsindisha.
44013028	Kandi naho babuze inyanduruko yo kumwicisha, basaba Pilato ko amwica.
44013029	Bamaze gushitsa ivyo yandikiwe vyose, bamumanura ku giti, bamushira mu mva.
44013030	Ariko Imana iramuzura mu bapfuye.
44013031	Imisi myinshi abonekera abari baraduganye na we ava i Galilaya aja i Yerusalemu, abo ni bo bamushingira intahe ubu imbere y'abantu.
44013032	Natwe turababwira ubutumwa bwiza bw'ivyasezeraniwe ba sogokuruza,
44013033	yuko Imana yabishikije kuri twebwe abana babo, hamwe yazura Yesu. Kandi ni ko vyanditswe muri Zaburi ya kabiri, ngo uri Ubura bwanje, uwu musi ndakuvyaye.
44013034	Kandi kuko yamuzuye mu bapfuye atazosubira mw'iborero, yavuze itya iti: "Nzobaha imigisha yera ya Dawidi itazovaho. "
44013035	No muri Zaburi yindi yavuze, ngo ntuzotanga Uwera wawe ngo azobore.
44013036	Yamara Dawidi mu gihe ciwe amaze gukora ivyo Imana igomba, arasinzira, arapfa, arabora.
44013037	Ariko uwo Imana yazuye nta ho yigeze abora.
44013038	Nuko bagabo bavukanyi, ni mumenye ko muri uwo ari ho mubwirirwa ivyo uguharirwa ivyaha;
44013039	kandi ni we ahindura intungane uwumwizera wese kuri vyose, ivyo mutashoboye guhindurwa intungane n'ivyagezwe vya Mose.
44013040	Nuko mwirinde, ivyavuzwe n'abavugishwa n'Imana ntibibashikeko,
44013041	ngo raba mwa banyagakengere, mutangare, muzimangane, Kuko ngira nkore igikorwa mu gihe canyu, Igikorwa mutazoruha mwemera, naho umuntu yokibasobanurira.
44013042	Bariko barasohoka, barabinginga ngo ayo majambo azovugwe no kw'isabato izoza.
44013043	Abari mu rusengero rw'Abayuda bamaze gusabagira, benshi mu Bayuda bo n'abatoye idini yabo bakubaha Imana, bakurikira Pahulo na Barunaba; na bo bayaga na bo, barabahanura ngo bashishikare kuguma mu buntu bw' Imana.
44013044	Kw'isabato ikurikira iyo, hakorana nk'abo mu gisagara bose kwumva ijambo ry'Imana.
44013045	Ariko Abayuda babonye ishengero ryinshi, buzura ishari, bahakana ivyo Pahulo avuze, barabicokora.
44013046	Pahulo na Barunaba bavuga bashize amazinda bati: "Vyari bibereye kw'ijambo ry'Imana ribanza kubwirwa mwebwe; none ko murishibuye, mukicira urubanza uko mutabereye ubugingo budashira, ehe-e duhindukiriye abanyamahanga. "
44013047	Kuko Umwami Imana ari ko yatubariye ati: "Ndagushizeho ngo ube umuco w'amahanga, Kugira ngo n'abo ku mpera y'isi ubashikirize agakiza. "
44013048	Abanyamahanga bavyumvise baranezerwa, bashimagiza ijambo ry'Imana; abari baragerewe ubugingo budashira bose barizera.
44013049	Ijambo ry'Umwami Yesu rikwira muri ico gihugu cose.
44013050	Ariko Abayuda bosha abagore b'icubahiro bubaha Imana, n'abakuru bo muri ico gisagara, bavyurira akadenderezo Pahulo na Barunaba, babirukana mu ntara yabo.
44013051	Na bo babakunkumurira umukungugu wo mu birenge vyabo, baja muri Ikoniyo.
44013052	Abigishwa buzuzwa umunezero na Mpwemu Yera.
44014001	Maze bari muri Ikoniyo bompi binjira mu rusengero rw'Abayuda, bavuga amajambo atuma Abayuda n'Abagiriki benshi cane bizera.
44014002	Ariko Abayuda banse kwumvira ivyo, bavyura urwanko mu mitima y'abanyamahanga ngo bagirire inabi abavukanyi.
44014003	Bamara imisi myinshi bavuga batabobotereza kubwo Umwami Yesu, ashingira intahe ijambo ry'ubuntu bwiwe, abaha gukora ibimenyetso n'ibitangaza n'amaboko yabo.
44014004	Ariko abantu bo muri ico gisagara birema ibice, bamwe baherera ku Bayuda, abandi ku ntumwa.
44014005	Kandi abanyamahanga, bo n'Abayuda n'abashingantahe babo baja kubatera ngo babagirire nabi babicishe amabuye;
44014006	barabimenya, bahungira i Lusitira n'i Derube, ibisagara vy'i Lukawoniya, no mu gihugu gihereranye na ho.
44014007	Bagumayo bavuga ubutumwa bwiza.
44014008	I Lusitira hari umugabo yari amugaye ibirenge uhereye aho yakaviriye mu nda ya nyina, nta ho yari yarigeze gutambuka.
44014009	Uwo yumva Pahulo avuga, na we amuhanze amaso abona ko afise ukwizera kwo gukizwa.
44014010	Avuga n'ijwi rirenga ati: "Haguruka uhagarare neza. " Arasimbasimba, aratambuka.
44014011	Maze ishengero ribonye ico Pahulo akoze, bavuga n'ijwi rirenga mu Kinyalukawoniya bati: "Imana zitumanukiyemwo zishushanije n'abantu. "
44014012	Barunaba bamwita Zeyu, Pahulo na we bamwita Herume, kuko ari we yari imvuzi.
44014013	Maze umuherezi wa Zeyu, ingoro y'umusezero wayo yari imbere y'igisagara, azana impfizi zisharijwe, agira acumite ikimazi, we n'ishengero.
44014014	Ariko intumwa, Barunaba na Pahulo, bavyumvise, bitaburirako impuzu zabo, bitera mu bantu, basemerera
44014015	bati: "Yemwe bagabo, ni iki gitumye mugira mutyo? Natwe turi abantu basanzwe, tumeze nkamwe, kandi tubabwira ubutumwa bwiza, ngo mureke ivyo bitagira ikimazi, muhindukirire Imana nzima, yaremye ijuru, isi, ikiyaga n'ibirimwo vyose,
44014016	ni yo yaretse amahanga yose mu bihe vyahise ngo bagendere mu nzira zabo.
44014017	Ariko ntiyabirekeye ngaho, itagira ico kuyishingira intahe, kuko yama ibagirira neza, ibaha imvura iva mw'ijuru, n'ibihe vy'umwimbu mwiza, ibahaza ivyo kurya, yuzuza imitima yanyu umunezero. "
44014018	Aho bavuga ayo majambo, hari hasigaye gatoya ntibabe bakibuza ishengero kubacumitira ikimazi.
44014019	Maze haza Abayuda bavuye muri Antiyokiya no muri Ikoniyo; bamaze kwosha ishengero, batera Pahulo amabuye, bamukwegera inyuma y'igisagara, bagira ngo yapfuye.
44014020	Ariko abigishwa bahagaze bamukikije, aravyuka, aja mu gisagara; bukeye bw'aho avanayo na Barunaba, aja i Derube.
44014021	Bamaze kuvuga ubutumwa bwiza muri ico gisagara no guhindura benshi abigishwa, basubira i Lusitira, muri Ikoniyo no muri Antiyokiya,
44014022	baremesha imitima y'abigishwa, babahanura ngo bagume mu kwizera; kandi yuko dukwiye guca mu marushwa menshi mu kwinjira mu bwami bw'Imana.
44014023	Kandi bamaze kubatorera abakuru mu mashengero yose, no gusenga bisonzesha, babaragiza Umwami Yesu, uwo bizeye.
44014024	Baca i Pisidiya, bashika i Pamfiliya.
44014025	Bamaze kuvuga ijambo ry'Imana i Peruga baramanuka baja muri Ataliya;
44014026	bavayo bari mu bwato bafata muri Antiyokiya, aho bari barazigamishirijwe ubuntu bw'Imana ubwa mbere ku gikorwa baheraheje.
44014027	Bashitseyo bakoranya ishengero, babiganira ivyo Imana yakoranye na bo vyose, n'ingene yugururiye abanyamahanga umuryango rwo kwizera.
44014028	Bamarana n'abigishwa igihe kitari gito.
44015001	Maze haza abantu bamwe bavuye i Yudaya bigisha abavukanyi bati: "Ni mutahimburwa igihimba c'ubugabo, nk'uko umugenzo wa Mose uri, ntimuzoruha mukizwa. "
44015002	Maze Pahulo na Barunaba bamaze kugira ibihari n'imburano itari mike n'abo bantu, abaho bahuza inama gutuma Pahulo na Barunaba n'abandi bamwe bo muri bo, ngo baje i Yerusalemu ku ntumwa n'abakuru ku bwo iyo miburano.
44015003	Nuko abo, ishengero rimaze kubaherekeza, baca i Foyinike bo n'i Samariya, babamenyesha ingene abanyamahanga bahindukiriye Imana, batera mu bavukanyi bose akanyamuneza kenshi.
44015004	Bashitse i Yerusalemu, ishengero n'intumwa n'abakuru barabakira, na bo babiganira ivyo Imana yakoranye na bo vyose.
44015005	Maze hava hasi bamwe bo mu muce w'Abafarisayo bizeye, baravuga bati: "Abanyamahanga birakwiye ko bahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, no kubabwiriza kwitondera ivyagezwe vya Mose. "
44015006	Nuko intumwa n'abakuru bakoranira hamwe kuja inama y'iryo jambo.
44015007	Habaye imburano myinshi, Petero ava hasi, arababwira ati: "Bagabo bavukanyi, murazi yuko kera Imana yantoranije muri mwebwe kugira ngo mu kanwa kanje habe ari ho abanyamahanga bumva ijambo ry'ubutumwa bwiza, bizere.
44015008	Kandi Imana izi imitima, yarabashingiye intahe, hamwe yabaha Mpwemu Yera, nk'uko yamuduhaye natwe;
44015009	ntiyashiraho itandukaniro hagati yacu na bo, yogesheje imitima yabo ukwizera.
44015010	None rero ni iki gitumye mugerageza Imana, mwikoreza abigishwa imitwaro ba sogokuruza batashoboye kwikorera canke twebwe?
44015011	Ariko twizeye yuko tuzokizwa n'ubuntu bw'Umwami Yesu nka bo. "
44015012	Maze ishengero ryose riracereza, bumviriza Barunaba na Pahulo babiganira ibimenyetso n'ibitangaza vyose Imana yabahaye gukora mu banyamahanga.
44015013	Barangije kuvuga, Yakobo aravuga ati: "Bagabo bavukanyi, ni munyumvirize.
44015014	Simoni yabiganiye ingene Imana yatanguye kugendera abanyamahanga ngo ibarobanuremwo ubwoko bw'izina ryayo.
44015015	Amajambo y'abavugishwa na yo ahuye n'ivyo, nk'uko handitswe,
44015016	ngo Hanyuma y'ivyo nzogaruka, Nongere nubake urusago rwa Dawidi rwatemvye, Nongere nsanasane ahashize harwo, ndaruhagarike,
44015017	Kugira ngo amasigarira y' abantu baronderane Uhoraho N'amahanga yose yitirirwa izina ryanje,
44015018	Ni ko Uhoraho avuze, akora ivyo vyose, yabimenye uhereye ku kuremwa kw'isi.
44015019	Nuko rero inama yanje ni uko tureka kugora abo mu banyamahanga bahindukirira Imana,
44015020	ariko tubandikire ngo bareke ibihumanya vy'ibigirwamana, no gusambana, no kurya ibinizwe, bo n'amaraso.
44015021	Kuko uhereye kera hose Mose afise mu bisagara vyose abigisha ivyiwe, bisomwa mu nsengero z'Abayuda uko isabato ishitse. "
44015022	Maze intumwa n'abakuru, bo n'ishengero ryose, bashima gutoranya abagabo muri bo, ni Yuda ari we Barusaba, na Sila, abantu bakuru mu bavukanyi, no kubatumana muri Antiyokiya na Pahulo na Barunaba.
44015023	Bandika ikete, bararibarungikana, ryanditswe ritya, ngo intumwa n'abavukanyi bakuru turabatasha mwebwe bavukanyi bo mu banyamahanga bari muri Antiyokiya, i Siriya n'i Kilikiya.
44015024	Kuko twumvise yuko bamwe bavuye muri twebwe babahagarikishije imitima amajambo, bakayivyimvya, kandi tutabibageze;
44015025	duhuje inama, dushimye gutoranya abo bantu no kubatumana kuri mwebwe n'abo dukunda Barunaba na Pahulo,
44015026	abantu bahevye amagara yabo kubwo izina ry' Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo.
44015027	Nuko abo dutumye ni Yuda na Sila, na bo ubwabo bazobabarira mu rurimi bimwe n'ibi.
44015028	Kuko Mpwemu Yera bimubereye vyiza, natwe ni uko, kutabikoreza uwundi mutwaro urenze ibi bikwiye;
44015029	mureke kurya ivyashikaniwe ibigirwamana, amaraso, n'ibinizwe, mureke no gusambana; ivyo ni mwavyirinda, muzomera neza. Nuko muganuke.
44015030	Nuko abo basezewe bamanuka muri Antiyokiya; bamaze gukoraniriza hamwe ishengero, babashikiriza kino cete.
44015031	Bamaze kugisoma banezererwa iyo mpanuro.
44015032	Na Yuda na Sila, kuko na bo bari abavugishwa n'Imana, bahanura abavukanyi mu majambo menshi, barabaremesha.
44015033	Bahamaze imisi, abavukanyi babasezera amahoro, ngo basubire ku babatumye. [
44015034	Mugabo Sila bimubera vyiza kugumayo. ]
44015035	Kandi Pahulo na Barunaba baguma muri Antiyokiya bigisha abantu, bababwira ijambo ry' Umwami Yesu, bafatanije n'abandi benshi.
44015036	Hashize imisi, Pahulo abwira Barunaba ati: "Ingo dusubire ha handi tugendere mu bavukanyi mu gisagara cose aho twamamaje ijambo ry'Umwami Yesu, tumenye uko bameze. "
44015037	Barunaba agomba ko bajana na Yohana na we, ari we Mariko.
44015038	Ariko Pahulo ntivyamubera vyiza kujana uwabataye i Pamfiliya, ntajane na bo muri ico gikorwa.
44015039	Havyuka imitongano ibatera gutandukana, Barunaba ajana Mariko, avudukayo ari mu bwato, afata i Kupuro;
44015040	Pahulo na we atoranya Sila, avayo, mu bavukanyi bamaze kumuragiza ubuntu bw'Umwami Yesu.
44015041	Aca i Siriya n'i Kilikiya, aremesha amashengero.
44016001	Nuko ashika i Derube n'i Lusitira; hariyo umwigishwa yitwa Timoteyo, umwana w'umugore w'Umuyudakazi yizeye, ariko se yari Umugiriki;
44016002	yashimwa n'abavukanyi b'i Lusitira no muri Ikoniyo.
44016003	Pahulo agomba ko bajana n'uwo aramwakira amuhimbura igikoba c'ubugabo, kubwo Abayuda bo muri izo ntara, kuko bose bari bazi yuko se yari Umugiriki.
44016004	Bariko baraca mu bisagara, bagenda bababwira ivyo intumwa n'abakuru b'i Yerusalemu bashinze, ngo bavyitondere.
44016005	Nuko amashengero akomerezwa mu kwizera, agenda yunguka ibitigiri imisi yose.
44016006	Baca mu gihugu c'i Furugiya n'i Galatiya, babuzwa na Mpwemu Yera kuvuga ijambo ry'Imana muri Asiya.
44016007	Bashitse ahabangikanye n'i Musiya, bagerageza kuja i Bituniya, Mpwemu wa Yesu ntiyabakundira;
44016008	baca i Musiya baramanuka, bashika i Tirowa.
44016009	Maze Pahulo arota inzozi mw'ijoro, abona umugabo w'i Makedoniya ahagaze amwinginga ati: "Jabuka uze i Makedoniya, udutabare. "
44016010	Amaze kurota izo nzozi, duca turondera ingene tuja i Makedoniya, kuko tumenye yuko Imana iduhamagariye kubabwira ubutumwa bwiza. "
44016011	Nuko tuvuduka i Tirowa mu bwato, turaramiriza tuja i Samotirake, bukeye bw'aho dushika i Neyapoli,
44016012	tuvuyeyo dushika i Filipi igisagara gikuru co mu ntara y'i Makedoniya, cubatswe n'Abaroma. Tumara imisi muri ico gisagara.
44016013	Ku musi w'isabato turenga irembo ry'igisagara, tuja ku ruzi, dukeka ko hobayo ahahora hasengerwa. Turicara, tuyaga n'abagore bahakoraniye.
44016014	Umugore umwe yitwa Ludiya yubaha Imana, umudandaza w'impuzu zitukura z'igiciro kinini, wo mu gisagara citwa Tuwatira, aratwumviriza. Umwami Yesu amwugurura umutima, kugira ngo awushire ku vyo Pahulo yavuga.
44016015	Amaze kubatizanywa n'abo mu nzu yiwe, aratwinginga ati: " "Asangwa mubonye ndi uwizeye Umwami Yesu, ni muze i wanje, musembereho. " " Aratugobera.
44016016	Bukeye tugiye aho basengera, duhura n'umwigeme arimwo dayimoni aragura, yari atungishije ba shebuja cane kubwo iyo ndagu.
44016017	Uwo aradukurikira twebwe na Pahulo, asemerera ati: " "Aba bantu ni abasavyi b'Imana Isumbavyose, kandi bababarira inzira y'agakiza. "
44016018	Amara imisi myinshi agenza atyo. Ariko Pahulo adundumiwe, arahindukira, abarira dayimoni ati: "Ndakubariye mw'izina rya Yesu Kristo, muvemwo. " Amuvamwo muri ako kanya.
44016019	Maze ba shebuja babonye yuko ico bazigako inyungu kivuyeho, bafata Pahulo na Sila, barabakwega babajana mu kaguriro imbere y'abashingantahe,
44016020	babashira abacamanza bati: "Aba bantu bahagarika imitima y'abo mu gisagara cacu, kandi ari Abayuda;
44016021	batuzanira imigenzo tuzira kwemera canke gukora, twebwe turi Abaroma. "
44016022	Ishengero ribahagurukira icarimwe, abacamanza babatabagurirako impuzu, bagera ko babakubita.
44016023	Bamaze kubakubita inkoni nyinshi, babashira mw'ibohero, babarira umurinzi kubarinda cane.
44016024	Na we abariwe atyo abashira mu nzu yo hagati, arobeza amaguru yabo mu mpatane z'ibiti.
44016025	Maze nko mu gicugu Pahulo na Sila bariko barasenga baririmbira Imana, izindi mbohe zibumva,
44016026	isi ica inyiganyiga cane giturumbuka, bituma amatanguriro y'inzu y'ibohero anyiganyiga, ako kanya imyango yose iruguruka, iminyororo ya bose iradohoka.
44016027	Uwo murinzi yikanguye, abonye imyango y'ibohero yuguruye, asokora inkota agira yiyahure, kuko yagira ngo imbohe zatorotse.
44016028	Ariko Pahulo asemerera n'ijwi rirenga ati: "Ntiwigirire nabi, twese turi hano. "
44016029	Ahamagaza imuri, yitera mu nzu, ari mu gatengo k'ubwoba, yikubita imbere ya Pahulo na Sila,
44016030	arabasohokana, arababaza ati: "Bagenzi, nkwiye gukora iki ngo nkire? "
44016031	Baramwishura bati: "Izere Umwami Yesu, urakira, mwe n'abo mu nzu yawe. "
44016032	Bamubarira ijambo ry'Umwami Yesu, n'abo mu nzu yiwe bose.
44016033	Muri ico gihe nyene c'ijoro arabajana, abuhagira inguma z'inkoni, aca arabatizwa, bo n'abiwe bose.
44016034	Arabadugana, abajana i we, arabagaburira, anezeranwa cane n'abo mu nzu yiwe bose, kuko yizeye Imana.
44016035	Ijoro rikeye, abacamanza batuma abagendanyi bati: "Rekura abo bantu. "
44016036	Umurinzi w'imbohe abarira Pahulo ayo majambo ati: "Abacamanza baratumye ngo murekurwe, nuko rero ni musohoke, mwigire amahoro. "
44016037	Ariko Pahulo arabishura ati: "Ko badukubitiye imbere y'ishengero, ata kidutsinze, kandi turi Abaroma, bakadushira mw'ibohero; none bagomba kuduhinda mu mpisho? Ekaye, ni babe ari bo biyizira ubwabo badusohore. "
44016038	Abo bagendanyi babarira abacamanza ayo majambo; na bo baratinya, bumvise ko ari Abaroma,
44016039	baraza, babakomera ibobo, barabasohora, babinginga kuva muri ico gisagara.
44016040	Bavuye mw'ibohero, baja kwa Ludiya, barinjira; bamaze kubona abavukanyi, barabahanura, bavayo.
44017001	Bamaze guca muri Amfipoli no muri Apoloniya, bashika i Tesalonike, hariho isengero ry'Abayuda y'Abayuda.
44017002	Nuko Pahulo, nk'uko yamenyereye, yinjira muri bo, amara amasabato atatu avugana na bo ivyo mu vyanditswe,
44017003	abibasobanurira, amenyekanisha yuko Kristo yari uwo kubabazwa, no kuzuka mu bapfuye; kandi ati: "Yesu, uwo ndababwira, ni we Kristo. "
44017004	Bamwe muri bo birabemeza, bifatanya na Pahulo na Sila, n'ishengero ryinshi ryo mu Bagiriki bubaha Imana n'uko, no mu bagore b'icubahiro batari bake.
44017005	Ariko Abayuda bagize ishari, bajana abagabo b'imburakimazi bo mu bigaramangira, bakoranya abantu benshi, bavyura imigumuko mu gisagara, batera inzu ya Yasona, bashaka gukuramwo Pahulo na Sila, ngo babashikirize abantu.
44017006	Bababuze, bakwegera Yasona n'abavukanyi biwe bamwe imbere y'abaganza igisagara, barasemerera bati: "Abateye isi yose umugumuko bashitse n'ino,
44017007	kandi Yasona yabahaye indaro. Abo bose barenze ivyagezwe vya Kayisari, bavuga yuko hariho uwundi mwami, ngo ni Yesu. " "
44017008	Ishengero rihakoraniye n'abaganza igisagara bahagarika imitima bumvise ivyo,
44017009	nuko baka Yasona n'abandi ingwati, barabarekura.
44017010	Nuko abavukanyi baca banyuruza Pahulo na Sila mw'ijoro baja i Beroya; maze bashitseyo binjira mu rusengero rw'Abayuda.
44017011	Ariko abo bo bari imico myiza kuruta abo i Tesalonike, kuko bakiriye ijambo ry'Imana n'umutima ukunze, basesa mu vyanditswe uko bukeye, ngo bamenye yuko ivyo ari ivyo ukuri. "
44017012	Nuko benshi muri bo barizera, n'abagore b'icubahiro b'Abagirikikazi n'abagabo batari bake.
44017013	Ariko Abayuda b'i Tesalonike bamenye yuko ijambo ry'Imana rivugwa na Pahulo i Beroya kandi, bajayo na ho, bavyura imivurungano mu bantu, babahagarika imitima.
44017014	Uwo mwanya abavukanyi biwe banyuruza Pahulo ngo ahave, aje ku kiyaga; ariko Sila na Timoteyo basigarayo.
44017015	Kandi abaherekeje Pahulo bamugejeje muri Atenayi; maze babariwe kubwira Sila na Timoteyo ngo bamusangeyo ningoga, basubira inyuma.
44017016	Ariko Pahulo akibarindiriye muri Atenayi, umutima wiwe utunturira muri we abonye ingene ico gisagara cuzuye ibigirwamana.
44017017	Nuko aharirira n'Abayuda n'abubaha Imana mu rusengero rw'Abayuda imisi yose, no mu kaguriro yahaharirira n'abamusangaho.
44017018	Maze bamwe mu banyabwenge bitwa Abepikureyo, n'abandi bitwa Abasitoyiko bahura na we. Bamwe muri bo barabazanya bati: "Mbega uwu adedemba agomba kuvuga ibiki? " Abandi bati: "Umenga ni uwuzanye imana z'ivyaduka; kuko yavuga ubutumwa bwiza bwa Yesu n'ubwo ukuzuka.
44017019	Baramufata bamujana ahitwa Areyopago, baramubaza bati: "Mbega ubona twoshobora kumenya ukwo kwigisha gusha uvuga uko ari kwo?
44017020	Kuko utuzanye mu matwi ibintu vy'ivyaduka; none rero turagomba kumenya ivyo ari vyo. "
44017021	Kuko Abanyatenayi bose n'ab' akavantara bariho, batagira ikindi bakora, atari ukwumva canke kudonda amakuru mashasha.
44017022	Pahulo ahagarara hagati muri Areyopago, aravuga ati: "Bagabo bo muri Atenayi, ndabonye muri vyose ko mukobeje kwubaha imana zanyu.
44017023	Kuko aho nagendagenda nitegereza ivyo musenga, nasanze hari n'igicaniro canditsweko, ngo ico IMANA ITAZWI. Nuko iyo musenga mutayizi, ni yo ndababarira.
44017024	Imana Rurema, yaremye isi n'ibirimwo vyose, iyo, kuko ari yo Mwami w'ijuru n'isi, ntiba mu nsengero zubatswe n'amaboko,
44017025	kandi ntikorerwa n'amaboko y'abantu, nk'uwuri n'ico akenye; kuko ari yo yahaye bose ubugingo, no guhumeka, n'ibindi vyose.
44017026	Kandi yaremye amahanga yose y' abantu, ibakuye mu muntu umwe, ngo bacumbike mw'isi yose, yashinze ibihe vy'imyaka ko bikuranwa uko yageze, icira abantu imbibe z'aho baba,
44017027	kugira ngo barondere Imana, ngo namba kumbure bakabakavye boyibona, naho itari kure y'umuntu n'umwe muri twebwe.
44017028	Kuko muri yo ari ho tubeshejweho, tugenda, turi n'ubugingo; nk'uko na bamwe bo mu bigeneye indirimbo banyu bavuze bati: 'Kuko natwe, turi uruvyaro rwayo.'
44017029	Nuko rero, ko turi uruvyaro rw'Imana, ntidukwiye kwiyumvira yuko Imana isa n'izahabu, canke ifeza, canke amabuye, ivyabajwe n'ubuhinga n'ubwenge bw'abantu.
44017030	Nuko iyo misi y'ubutamenya, Imana yarayirengagije, ariko noneho, itegeka ko abantu bose bari hose bihana,
44017031	kuko yashinze umusi wo gucirako isi yose imanza z'ukuri, izozicisha umuntu yatoranije, kandi yahaye bose ikimenyetso c'ivyo, mu kumuzura imukuye mu bapfuye. "
44017032	Maze bumvise ivyo ukuzuka mu bapfuye, bamwe barishinyira, abandi bati: "Tuzoba turumva ukundi ivyo utubarira kuri ivyo. "
44017033	Nuko Pahulo ava muri bo.
44017034	Ariko abagabo bamwe bifatanya na we barizera; muri bo umwe ni Diyonisiyo wo mu Bareyopago, kandi n'umugore yitwa Damari, hamwe n'abandi.
44018001	Hanyuma y'ivyo Pahulo ava muri Atenayi, aja i Korinto.
44018002	Abonye Umuyuda yitwa Akwila, amamuko yiwe ni i Ponto, yari avuye muri Italiya muri iyo misi, bo n'umugore wiwe Purisikila, kuko Kilawudiyo yari yageze ko Abayuda bose bava i Roma; Pahulo aja aho bari.
44018003	Kandi kuko bari bahuje ubuhinga, abana na bo, barunganiranira, kuko ubuhinga bwabo bwari ubwo kujisha amahema.
44018004	Aharirira n'abaho mu rusengero rw'Abayuda amasabato yose, ngo yemeze Abayuda n'Abagiriki.
44018005	Maze Sila na Timoteyo bamanutse, bavuye i Makedoniya, Pahulo agoberwa n'ijambo ry'Imana, ashingira intahe Abayuda yuko Yesu ari we Kristo.
44018006	Na bo babiharirije batyoza, akunkumura impuzu ziwe, arababarira ati: "Amaraso yanyu araba ari mwebwe akora! Jeho ndacuna; guhera ubu ndaja ku banyamahanga. "
44018007	Avaho, yinjira mu nzu y'umuntu yitwa Tito Yusito, yubaha Imana, inzu yiwe yari ihereranye n'urusengero rw'Abayuda.
44018008	Ariko Krisipo, umukuru w'urusengero, yizerana Umwami Yesu n'abo mu nzu yiwe bose; n'Abakorinto benshi bumvise barizera, barabatizwa.
44018009	Maze Umwami Yesu abarira Pahulo mw'ijoro nko mu nzozi ati: "Ntutinye, ariko uvuge, ntucereze,
44018010	kuko ndi kumwe nawe, kandi nta muntu azogutera ngo akugirire nabi, kuko mfise abantu benshi muri iki gisagara. "
44018011	Amarayo umwaka n'amezi atandatu, yigisha ijambo ry'Imana muri bo.
44018012	Maze Galiyo abaye icegera ca Kayisari muri Akaya, Abayuda bahuza inama bakurira hasi Pahulo, bamujana imbere y'intebe y'imanza
44018013	bati: "Uwu muntu yemeza abantu gusenga Imana uburyo bunyuranye n'ivyagezwe. "
44018014	Pahulo ariko arahaga amatama, Galiyo abwira Abayuda ati: "Iyo haba hari habonetse ibirego vy'icaha, canke ikibi kigoye, yemwe Bayuda, hari kuboneka inyanduruko yuko ndabihanganira kubumva;
44018015	ariko ko ari ibihari vy'amajambo n'ivyo amazina n'ivyo ivyagezwe vyanyu ubwanyu, ni mubimare ubwanyu. Jeho singomba guca urubanza rwa bene ivyo. " "
44018016	Abirukana imbere y'intebe y'imanza.
44018017	Abagiriki bose basumira Sositene, umukuru w'isengero ry'Abayuda, bamukubitira imbere y'intebe y'imanza. Ariko Galiyo, ivyo vyose ntiyabibabara.
44018018	Hanyuma y'ivyo Pahulo amarayo iyindi misi myinshi, maze asezera abavukanyi, avudukayo ari mu bwato ngo aje i Siriya, Purisikila na Akwila bajana na we, amaze kwimoshereza i Kenkireya; kuko yari mw'isezerano.
44018019	Bashitse muri Efeso, abasiga ngaho; ariko we aragenda yinjira mu rusengero rw'Abayuda, aharira n'Abayuda.
44018020	Bamwinginze ngo amareyo iyindi misi ntiyabakundira.
44018021	Ariko asezerana na bo ati: " "Nzogaruka ikindi gihe, Imana ni yabigomba. " Avuduka muri Efeso ari mu bwato.
44018022	Afashe i Kayisariya, araduga aja i Yerusalemu, aramutsa ishengero, aramanuka, aja muri Antiyokiya.
44018023	Amazeyo imisi avayo, aca mu gihugu c'i Galatiya n'i Furugiya, aja mu bisagara uko bikurikirana, aremesha abigishwa bose.
44018024	Maze Umuyuda yitwa Apolo, amamuko yiwe ni muri Alekisanderiya, yari umuntu w'ubwenge, ashika muri Efeso; yari Umunyabushobozi mu vyanditswe.
44018025	Uwo yari yigishijwe inzira y'Umwami wacu, acanirwa mu mutima n'umwete, yavuga yigisha ivya Yesu avyitondeye, yari azi umubatizo wa Yohana gusa.
44018026	Atangura kuvugira mu rusengero rw'Abayuda ashize amanga. Maze Purisikila na Akwila bamwumvise, bamujana i wabo, barushiriza kumutahuza inzira y'Imana.
44018027	Agomvye kujabuka ngo aje muri Akaya, abavukanyi baramuremesha, bandikira abigishwa ngo bamwakire. Na we ashitseyo, ubuntu bw'Imana bumutera gufasha cane abizeye;
44018028	kuko yatururuza Abayuda abatsindira imbere y'abantu, yerekana mu vyanditswe yuko Yesu ari we Kristo.
44019001	Maze Apolo akiri i Korinto, Pahulo aca mu bihugu vyo haruguru, ashika muri Efeso, asangayo abigishwa bamwe.
44019002	Arababaza ati: "Mbega mwarahawe Mpwemu Yera igihe mwizera? " Baramwishura bati: "Ntitwaribwanavyumve yuko Mpwemu Yera yatanzwe. "
44019003	Arababaza ati: "None mwabatijwe umubatizo ki? " Bati: "Umubatizo wa Yohana. "
44019004	Pahulo ati: "Yohana yabatije umubatizo wo kwihana, abarira abantu ko bakwiye kwizera uwuzoza hanyuma yiwe, ni Yesu. "
44019005	Bavyumvise babatizwa mw'izina ry'Umwami Yesu.
44019006	Pahulo amaze kubarambikako ibiganza, Mpwemu Yera abazako, bavuga izindi ndimi, bavugishwa n'Imana.
44019007	Abo bose bari abagabo nk'icumi na babiri.
44019008	Hanyuma Pahulo yinjira mu rusengero rw'Abayuda, amara amezi atatu avuga ashize amanga; akiranira ivyo ubwami bw'Imana abibemeza.
44019009	Ariko bamwe bikomantaje imitima, b'intumva, batukira Inzira ya Yesu imbere y'abantu, ava muri bo, arobanura abigishwa, uko bukeye aharirira mu nzu yo kwigishirizamwo ya Turano.
44019010	Bimara imyaka ibiri bimeze bityo. Nuko ababa muri Asiya bose Abayuda n'Abagiriki bumva ijambo ry' Umwami wacu.
44019011	Kandi Imana ikoresha amaboko ya Pahulo ibitangaza vy' agaheta.
44019012	Vyatuma bashira abarwaye ibitambara n'ivyambazo bivuye ku mubiri wiwe, bagakira indwara zabo, ibisigo bikabavamwo.
44019013	Ariko inyererezi zimwe zo mu Bayuda zirukana ibisigo zigerera kuvugira izina ry'Umwami Yesu hejuru y'abafashwe n'ibisigo ziti: "Tubarahiye Yesu, uwo Pahulo avuga. "
44019014	Kandi hariho abahungu indwi b' Umuyuda yitwa Sikewa, umwe mu baherezi bakuru, bagenza batyo.
44019015	Igisigo kirabishura kiti: "Yesu ndamuzi, na Pahulo ndamuzi, ariko mweho muri ba nde? "
44019016	Umuntu arimwo igisigo abagurukirako bompi, arabanesha, arabirukana, bahunga muri iyo nzu bambaye ubusa bakomeretse.
44019017	Ivyo bimenyekana mu Bayuda no mu Bagiriki bose baba muri Efeso, bose baterwa n'ubwoba, izina ry'Umwami Yesu rishirwa hejuru.
44019018	Kandi benshi mu bari barizeye baraza, batura ivyo bakoze, barabiserura.
44019019	Benshi no mu bakora ivyo ubupfumu bakoranya ibitabo vyabo vy'ubupfumu, babituririra mu maso ya bose. Baharura igiciro cavyo, basanga gishitse ku ntete z'ifeza ibihumbi mirongo itanu.
44019020	Uko ni ko ijambo ry'Umwami Yesu ryagwiriye cane, rigira ububasha.
44019021	Ivyo bishize Pahulo yiyumvira mu mutima wiwe guca i Makedoniya no muri Akaya aja i Yerusalemu ati: "Ni namara gushikayo, nkwiye kuja kuraba n'i Roma na ho. "
44019022	Atuma abagenda bamukorera babiri, Timoteyo na Erasito, ngo baje i Makedoniya; ariko we, atebera muri Asiya imisi.
44019023	Nko muri ico gihe havyuka imivurungano itari mike ku bwo Inzira ya Yesu.
44019024	Hari umuntu yitwa Demetiriyo, umucuzi w'ifeza, yacura utuzu tw'ibigirwamana twa Arutemi mw'ifeza, akaronkesha abacuzi biwe inyungu nyinshi.
44019025	Nuko abakoraniriza hamwe n'abandi bakora ibikorwa bene ivyo, arababwira ati: "Yemwe bagabo, murazi yuko ubutunzi bwacu buva muri iki gikorwa.
44019026	Murabona kandi murumva yuko atari muri Efeso honyene, ariko nko muri Asiya hose, umwe Pahulo yoheje abantu benshi akabahindura ati: 'Imana zakozwe n'intoke si zo mana.'
44019027	Si uko igikorwa cacu kiri mw'irinde kigiye gukengerwa gusa, ariko kandi n'ingoro y'umusezero w'imanakazi ihambaye Arutemi yotiturwa, mbere yonakurwako icubahiro cayo gikomeye, ari yo abo muri Asiya bose n'isi yose basenga. "
44019028	Bavyumvise karaziriringa, barasemerera bati: "Arutemi y'Abanyefeso irahambaye. "
44019029	Maze igisagara cose kiravurungana, bashwabadukira icarimwe baja ku kibuga c'ibirori, batwara Abanyamakedoniya, Gayo na Arisitariko bagendana na Pahulo amaguru adakora hasi.
44019030	Maze Pahulo agomvye kuja muri iryo koraniro ry'abantu, abigishwa baramutesha.
44019031	Kandi bamwe mu bakuru bo muri Asiya, kuko bari abagenzi, bamutumako bamwinginga ngo ntiyirohe mu kibuga c'ibirori.
44019032	Nuko barayogora, bamwe ukwabo abandi ukwabo, kuko iryo shengero ryavurunganye, abenshi batari bazi icatumye bakorana.
44019033	Maze basokorora Alekisandero mu bantu, Abayuda bamwigiza imbere. Maze Alekisandero arabamama, agira yiregure ku bantu.
44019034	Ariko bamumenye ko ari Umuyuda, bose basemererera icarimwe, bamara nk'amasaha abiri bati: "Arutemi y'Abanyefeso irahambaye. "
44019035	Umwanditsi (ari we mukuru w'igisagara) amaze guhoza ishengero, arababarira ati: "Bagabo b'Abanyefeso, mbega hariho umuntu atazi yuko igisagara c'Abanyefeso ari co kizigama ingoro y'imisezero y'imanakazi ihambaye Arutemi, ari co gishushanyo cakorotse kiva mw'ijuru? "
44019036	None ko ata woshobora guhakana ivyo, mukwiye guhora, no kutagira ico mukora mutitonze.
44019037	Kuko muzanye aba bagabo, bativye ivyo mu ngoro z'imana kandi batatyoje ku manakazi yacu.
44019038	Nuko Demetiriyo n'abacuzi bari kumwe na we, namba bafise uwo barega, imisi y'imanza iriho, kandi hariho n'ivyegera vya Kayisari, ni baregane.
44019039	Ariko ni mwaba mufise ibindi murondera, bizomarirwa mw'ikoraniro risanzwe.
44019040	Mbere turi mw'irinde, kumbure ibibaye uwu musi vyotuma turegwa ubugarariji, kuko ata nyanduruko; kandi ntituzoshobora gusobanura icakoranije iri shengero rivurunganye.
44019041	Avuze ivyo, acura ikoraniro.
