44020001	Umugumuko umaze gushira, Pahulo atumako abigishwa, arabahanura, arabasezera, avayo ngo aje i Makedoniya.
44020002	Amaze guca muri ivyo bihugu, abahanura mu majambo menshi, aja i Bugiriki.
44020003	Amarayo amezi atatu; maze Abayuda bamugiriye inama yo kumutega agira atambukire mu bwato aja i Siriya, yiyumvira gusubira inyuma aciye i Makedoniya.
44020004	Abajana na we bagashikana no muri Asiya ni: Sopatero umwana wa Puro w'i Beroya, abo i Tesalonike ni: Arisitariko, Sekondo, Gayo w'i Derube na Timoteyo, abo muri Asiya ni: Tukiko na Tirofimo.
44020005	Abo bari babaye baragenda imbere, baturorerera i Tirowa.
44020006	Natwe tuvuduka i Filipi turi mu bwato hanyuma y'imisi y'imitsima itambiwe, tubasanga i Tirowa ku musi ugira gatanu, tumarayo imisi indwi.
44020007	Ku wa mbere w'imisi indwi, dukoranira kumanyagura imitsima, Pahulo ayaga na bo, agira ngo buce agenda, atevya mu majambo ashitsa mu gicugu.
44020008	Maze hari amatara menshi mu cumba co mu nzu yo hejuru aho twari dukoraniye.
44020009	Kandi mw'idirisha hari hicaye umusore yitwa Eyutuko, aremerwa n'itiro ryinshi; maze Pahulo arushirije gutevya mu majambo, itiro riramuremera, arakoroka avuye mw'igorofa ya gatatu, bamuyora ahwereye.
44020010	Pahulo arururuka, amwubama hejuru, aramugumbira ati: "Mureke gukoma induru, kuko ubugingo bwiwe bukiri muri we. " "
44020011	Asubira kwurira, amanyagura umutsima, ararya, ayaga na bo igihe kirekire, ashitsa no mu bucagucagu, maze aragenda.
44020012	Bazana uwo muhungu ari muzima, imitima yabo iraruhuka.
44020013	Ariko tweho twabaye turagenda imbere dutambukira mu bwato, turajabuka dufata muri Aso, aho twari dutumbereye guhitana Pahulo; kuko yari yabishinze atyo, kugira ngo we ace i musozi.
44020014	Adusanze muri Aso turamujana, turajabuka dufata i Mitulene.
44020015	Tuvuyeyo, bukeye bw'aho dushika imbere y'i Kiyo, ku musi ugira gatatu dufata i Samo, bukeye dufata i Mileto.
44020016	Kuko Pahulo yari yiyumviriye guca i ruhande ya Efeso, kugira ngo ntatebe muri Asiya; kuko yihuta, ngo ni vyashoboka umusi wa Pentekote uzoshike ari i Yerusalemu.
44020017	Ari i Mileto atuma muri Efeso, atumako abakuru b'ishengero.
44020018	Na bo bashitse aho ari, arababwira ati: " "Ubwanyu murazi ingene nabana namwe na ntaryo, uhereye umusi natanguriye gushika muri Asiya,
44020019	nkorera Umwami wacu n'umutima wicishije bugufi, kandi ndira, nterwa n'ibingerageza ku bwo inama z'Abayuda.
44020020	Kandi murazi yuko ata jambo ribereye nacishije i ruhande kubabwira canke kubigishiriza imbere y'abantu mu nzu no mu yindi.
44020021	Nashinze intahe mu Bayuda no mu Bagiriki y'ukwihana mu maso y'Imana, n'ukwizera Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo.
44020022	None raba, ngiye i Yerusalemu mboshwe mu mutima, ntazi ibizombako nshitseyo;
44020023	atari uko Mpwemu Yera anshingira intahe mu gisagara cose yuko iminyororo n'ivyago bintegeyeyo.
44020024	Ariko simbabaye ubugingo bwanje nk'aho ari ubwo igiciro, kugira ngo ndangize urugendo rwanje, n'igikorwa nahawe n'Umwami Yesu, co gushingira intahe ubutumwa bwiza bw'ubuntu bw'Imana.
44020025	Kandi none raba, ndazi yuko mutazosubira kubona mu maso hanje, abo naciyemwo mwese ndababwira ivyo ubwami bw'Imana.
44020026	Ni co gituma ndabashingira intahe uwu musi ncuna, yuko amaraso ya bose atazonkora,
44020027	kuko ntacishije i ruhande ndababwira ivyo Imana yashatse vyose.
44020028	Mwirinde ubwanyu, muzigame n'ubusho bwose Mpwemu Yera yabashizemwo, ngo mube abo kubuzezwa, kugira ngo muragire ishengero ry'Imana, iryo yaguze amaraso yayo.
44020029	Ndazi yuko ni namara kuhava, amabingira y'inkazi azobinjiramwo atababaye umukuku.
44020030	Kandi no muri mwebwe ubwanyu hazokwadukamwo abantu bavuga ibigoramye kugira ngo bakwegere abigishwa inyuma yabo.
44020031	Nuko mwame mugavye, mwibuke yuko namaze imyaka itatu ntasiba guhanura umuntu wese ndira, ku murango no mw'ijoro.
44020032	Kandi ubu ndabaragije Imana n'ijambo ry'ubuntu bwayo, rishobora kububaka no kubahera ibiragwa hamwe n'abejejwe bose.
44020033	Nta co nifuje, ari ifeza ari izahabu ari imyambaro y'umuntu n'umwe.
44020034	Ubwanyu murazi ko aya maboko yanje yankenurana ivyo nkenye n'abo turi kumwe.
44020035	Nabahaye akarorero muri vyose, yuko mu butame nk'ubwo, ari ko mukwiye gufasha abadakomeye, no kwibuka amajambo y'Umwami Yesu, ingene ubwiwe yavuze ati: 'Gutanga kuzana umugisha, kuruta guhabwa.'
44020036	Amaze kuvuga atyo, arapfukama, asengera hamwe na bo bose.
44020037	Bose bararira cane, bagwa Pahulo mu nda, baramugumbira;
44020038	canecane bababajwe n'ijambo yababwiye ngo ntibazosubira kumubona mu maso. Maze baramuherekeza, bamugeza ku bwato.
44021001	Tumaze gutandukana na bo, no gutambukira mu bwato, turaramiriza tuja i Kosi; bukeye bw'aho dufata i Rodo, tuvayo dufata i Patara.
44021002	Dusanze ubwato bugira bujabuke buja i Foyinike, tubutambukiramwo turagenda.
44021003	Tubonye i Kupuro tuhasiga mu bubamfu, tuja i Siriya, dufata muri Tiro; kuko ari ho bari bategerezwa gukurira ibintu mu bwato.
44021004	Tuhasanze abigishwa, dusibirayo imisi indwi; na bo bavugishijwe na Mpwemu babarira Pahulo ngo ntaje i Yerusalemu.
44021005	Turangije iyo misi, tuvayo turagenda, bose baduherekezanya n'abagore n'abana, baturenza igisagara, dupfukama ku musenyi, turasenga.
44021006	Tumaze gusezerana dutambukira mu bwato, na bo basubira i wabo.
44021007	Natwe turangije urugendo rwo kuva muri Tiro, dufata i Putolemayi, turamutsa abavukanyi, tumarana na bo umusi umwe.
44021008	Bukeye bw'aho tuvayo, dushika i Kayisariya, twinjira mu nzu ya Filipo umuvuzi w'ubutumwa bwiza, n'umwe muri ba bandi indwi, twaka indaro i we.
44021009	Uwo yarafise abakobwa bane b'inkumi, bavugishwa n'Imana.
44021010	Tugitevyeyo imisi myinshi, haza uwuvugishwa n'Imana yitwa Agabo, yari amanutse avuye i Yudaya.
44021011	Aza aho turi, yakira umukaba wa Pahulo, awibohesha amaguru n'amaboko, aravuga ati: "Uku ni ko Mpwemu Yera agize, nyene uwu mukaba, uku ni ko Abayuda bazomubohera i Yerusalemu, bazomushira mu maboko y'abanyamahanga. "
44021012	Maze twumvise ivyo, twebwe n'abantu baho turamwinginga ngo ntaduge i Yerusalemu.
44021013	Maze Pahulo aratubaza ati: "Mukora ibiki, kurira mundandura umutima? Siniteguye kuboherwa gusa i Yerusalemu, ariko no gupfirayo, kubwo izina ry'Umwami Yesu. "
44021014	Yanse guharurwa, turihorera tuti: "Ivyo Umwami agomba ni bibeho! " "
44021015	Hanyuma y'iyo misi dutekera ibintu vyacu, turaduga tuja i Yerusalemu.
44021016	Bamwe mu bigishwa bavuye i Kayisariya turajana, bazana Umunyakupuro yitwa Munasona, yari umwigishwa wa kera, tuba ari we dusemberako.
44021017	Dushitse i Yerusalemu abavukanyi batwakirana umunezero. "
44021018	Bukeye bw'aho Pahulo yinjirana natwe kwa Yakobo, abakuru bose ni ho bari bari.
44021019	Amaze kubaramutsa, ababarira ivyo Imana yakoze mu banyamahanga imukoresheje, abidonze kimwekimwe.
44021020	Na bo bavyumvise bahimbaza Imana; maze baramubwira bati: "Urabona, muvukanyi, ingene Abayuda bizeye ari ibihumbi vyinshi; kandi bose bagira ishaka ry'ivyagezwe.
44021021	Kandi babariwe ivyawe, yuko wigisha Abayuda bose bari mu banyamahanga guheba ivya Mose, ukavuga ngo ntibakwiye guhimbura igikoba c'ubugabo bana babo canke kugendera mu migenzo yacu.
44021022	None icobimara ni igiki? " Ntibazobura kwumva ko waje.
44021023	Nuko genza utya, uko tukubwira. Dufise abagabo bane bari n'ico basezeranye.
44021024	Ubajane, wihumanurane na bo, ubaterere, ngo babone kwimosha. Maze bose bazomenya yuko ivyo baguteranije kuri bo ata kuri kurimwo, kandi ko nawe ubwawe ugenda witonze, witondera n'ivyagezwe.
44021025	Yamara ivyo abizeye bo mu banyamahanga, twanditse dushinze ko birinda kurya ivyashikaniwe ibigirwamana, bo n'amaraso, bo n'ibinizwe, birinde no gusambana. "
44021026	Nuko Pahulo ajana abo bagabo, bukeye bw'aho yihumanurana na bo, yinjirana na bo mu rusengero, avuga igihe imisi yo guhumanurwa izoshirira, agenza atyo gushitsa aho ikimazi c'umuntu wese muri bo catangiwe.
44021027	Nuko iyo misi indwi igira ishire, Abayuda bavuye muri Asiya bamubonye mu rusengero, bavurunga ishengero ryose, bamushorerako amaboko,
44021028	baratabaza bati: "Bagabo b'Abisirayeli, mudutabare! " Nguwu wa muntu yigisha hose abantu bose, akengereza ubu bwoko n'ivyagezwe n'aha hantu. Ikigeretseko yazanye n'Abagiriki mu rusengero, yahumanije aha hantu hera.
44021029	Kuko bari babonye Tirofimo w'Umunyefeso ari kumwe na we mu gisagara, bagira ngo Pahulo yamujanye mu rusengero.
44021030	Igisagara cose kiravurungana, abantu barashwabaduka, basumira Pahulo, baramukwega bamukura mu rusengero; ako kanya bugara imyango.
44021031	Bakirondera ingene bamwica, inkuru ishika ku mukuru w'intwazangabo z'abasoda yuko abo muri Yerusalemu bose bavurunganye.
44021032	Aca ajana abasoda n'intwazangabo zabo, abamanukira yiruka. Na bo babonye uwo mukuru w'abagabisha n'abasoda, basigaho gukubita Pahulo.
44021033	Maze uwo mukuru w'intwazangabo arabashikira, aramufata, avuga ko bamufatisha iminyororo ibiri, abaza uwo ari we, n'ico akoze ico ari co.
44021034	Abo mw'ishengero barayogora, bamwe ukwabo abandi ukwabo; abujijwe n'ukuyogora kumenya ukuri, avuga ko bamujana mu gisagara gikikijwe n'uruhome rw'amabuye.
44021035	Ashitse ku ngazi y'amabuye abasoda baramuterura kubwo ubukari bw' abantu,
44021036	kuko ishengero ry abantu ryabaja inyuma, basemerera bati: "Kuraho uwo. "
44021037	Bagira bamushikane mu gisagara gikikijwe n'uruhome rw'amabuye, Pahulo abaza uwo mukuru w'abagabisha ati: "Wonkundira ijambo nkubarira? " Na we aramubaza ati: "Urazi Ikigiriki? "
44021038	Si wewe wa Munyegiputa yateye umugararizo mu gihe gishize, akajana mu bugaragwa abantu b'abicanyi ibihumbi bine?
44021039	Pahulo aramwishura ati: "Ndi Umuyuda, umuntu w'i Taruso, igisagara c'i Kilikiya kitayoberanye, none ndakwinginze unkundire ico mbarira abantu. "
44021040	Amukundiye, Pahulo ahagarara ku ngazi y'amabuye, amama abantu; hamaze kuba agacerere rwose, ababarira mu Giheburayo,
44022001	Ati: "Yemwe bagabo bavukanyi kandi ba data, ni mwumvirize ivyo nireguza muri mwebwe. "
44022002	Bumvise ababariye mu Giheburayo, barushiriza gucereza. Aravuga
44022003	ati: "Ndi Umuyuda, navukiye i Taruso h'i Kilikiya, ariko nakuriye muri iki gisagara, nigishirizwa imbere y'ibirenge vya Gamaliyeli nk'uko uruhande rugoye rw'ivyagezwe vya ba sogokuruza ruri, ngira ishaka ry'Imana, nk'uko namwe mwese murifise uwu musi. "
44022004	Kandi nahama abakurikira Inzira ya Yesu gushitsa bapfuye, nkababoha abagabo n'abagore nkabashira mu mabohero.
44022005	Kandi n'umuherezi mukuru na we aranshingira intahe y'ivyo, bo n'abacamanza bose. Ni bo bampaye amakete yandikiwe abavukanyi bacu b'i Damasiko, ikinjanyeyo ari ukuzana i Yerusalemu abaho na bo bari mu ngoyi, ngo bishure.
44022006	Nuko nkigenda, nshitse hafi y'i Damasiko, hari nko mu mashoka, umuco uhambaye uza giturumbuka uvuye mw'ijuru, unkayanganira irya n'ino.
44022007	Nikubita hasi numva ijwi rimbaza riti: "Sawuli, Sawuli, umpigira iki? "
44022008	Nanje ndabaza nti: "Uri nde ga Mwami? "Aranyishura ati: "Ndi Yesu Umunyanazareti, uwo uriko urahiga. "
44022009	Kandi n'abo twari kumwe umuco barawubonye, ariko ntibumva ijwi ry'uwo tuvugana.
44022010	Ndamubaza nti: "Ngire nte ga Mwami? " Umwami aranyishura ati: "Va hasi, ushike i Damasiko, ni ho uzobaririrwa ivyashinzwe ko uzokora. "
44022011	Maze ubwiza bw'uwo muco bumpumishije, abo twari kumwe bamfata ukuboko, nshika i Damasiko.
44022012	Umugabo yitwa Ananiya, yubaha Imana mu kwumvira ivyagezwe, yashimwa n'Abayuda bose babayo,
44022013	aza aho ndi, ampagarara hejuru, arambarira ati: "Sawuli, muvukanyi, humuka. " Ako kanya ndahumuka, ndamuraba.
44022014	Aravuga ati: "Imana ya ba sogokuruza yagutoranirije kumenya ivyo igomba, no kubona wa Mugororotsi, no kwumva ijwi riva mu kanwa kiwe,
44022015	kuko uzomubera icabona ku bantu bose ku vyo wabonye kandi wumvise.
44022016	None ikigutevya ni iki? Va hasi, ubatizwe, wiyuhagire ivyaha vyawe, wambaze izina ryiwe. "
44022017	Maze ngarutse i Yerusalemu, nariko ndasenga mu rusengero, mera nk'uwurota,
44022018	ndamubona ambwira ati: "Tebuka, uve i Yerusalemu vuba, kuko batazokwemera ivyo unshingira intahe. "
44022019	Nanje nti: "Mwami, na bo ubwabo barazi yuko nashira abakwizeye mw'ibohero, nkabatonagurira mu nsengero zose z'Abayuda.
44022020	Kandi hamwe amaraso y'uwagushingira intahe Stefano yava, nanje ni ho nari mpagaze, ndabishimye, nsanze impuzu z'abamwica. "
44022021	Aranyishura ati: "Genda, kuko nzogutuma kure ku banyamahanga. "
44022022	Baramwumviriza gushitsa kuri iryo jambo; maze basemerera n'ijwi rirenga bati: "Kura uwumeze atyo mw'isi, na kare ntiyari abereye kubaho. "
44022023	Bakiyogora, bata impuzu zabo, basurira umukungugu mu kirere,
44022024	umukuru w'intwazangabo z'abasoda avuga ko bamwinjiza mu gisagara gikikijwe n'uruhome rw'amabuye, ababarira kumukubitisha ibimoko, kugira ngo amenye icatumye bamuvugiriza urwamo batyo.
44022025	Bamaze kumubohesha imigozi, Pahulo abaza intwazangabo z'abasoda ijana ahagaze aho ati: "Mbega biremerwa ko mukubita umuntu w' Umuroma, kandi ata rubanza rwamutsinze? "
44022026	Iyo ntwazangabo ivyumvise, ija ku mukuru w'abasoda, irabimumenyesha iti: "Ugira ukore iki? Erega wa muntu ni Umuroma. "
44022027	Uwo mukuru w'intwazangabo araza, aramubaza ati: "Mbarira, mbega uri Umuroma? " Na we ati: "Ego me. "
44022028	Uwo mukuru aramubarira ati: "Jewe naguze ubwo buroma amahera menshi. " Pahulo ati: "Ariko jeho nabuvukiyemwo. " "
44022029	Nuko abari bagiye kumucaca baca baramureka; umukuru w'abagabisha na we aratinya, amenye ko ari Umuroma, kandi yamuboshe.
44022030	Ariko bukeye bw'aho, agomvye kumenya neza ico Abayuda bamurega ico ari co, aramubohora, agera ko abaherezi bakuru bakorana n'abacamanza bose, amanukana Pahulo amuhagarika imbere yabo."
44023001	Pahulo ahanga amaso abacamanza, arababwira ati: "Bagabo bavukanyi, namanye umutima utarimwo ijwi rinyagiriza ikibi na kimwe imbere y'Imana gushitsa kuri uwo musi. "
44023002	Ananiya umuherezi mukuru abarira abamuhagaze i ruhande kumukubita ku munwa.
44023003	Maze Pahulo aramubwira ati: "Imana izogukubita, wa rusika rukuyengejeko ingwa, mbega wewe ko wicaritswe no kuncira urubanza nk'uko ivyagezwe biri, ugatako ukavuga ko bankubita ukanyuranya n'ivyagezwe? "
44023004	Abari bahagazeho bati: "Mbega uratuka umuherezi mukuru w'Imana? "
44023005	Pahulo ati: "Sinari ndamuzi, bavukanyi, ko ari umuherezi mukuru; kuko handitswe ngo Ntukavuge nabi umukuru wo mu bwoko bwanyu. "
44023006	Maze Pahulo amenye yuko umuce umwe ari uwo Abasadukayo, uwundi ari uwo Abafarisayo, ashira ijwi hejuru mu bashingantahe ati: "Bagabo bavukanyi, ndi Umufarisayo, ndi umwana w'Abafarisayo; ivyo ivyizigiro vy'ibizoba n'ukuzuka kw'abapfuye ni vyo bimpagaritse muri izi manza. "
44023007	Avuze atyo, havyuka ibihari mu Bafarisayo n'Abasadukayo, abanyarubanza birema ibice.
44023008	Kuko Abasadukayo bahakana yuko ata kuzuka kuriho, canke umumarayika n'impwemu; ariko Abafarisayo bavyemera vyose.
44023009	Habaho urwamo rwinshi; bamwe mu bahinga b'ivyanditswe bo mu muce w'Abafarisayo bava hasi baraharira bati: "Nta kibi twabonye kuri uwo muntu. Kumbure impwemu canke umumarayika yoba yavuganye na we. "
44023010	Habaho ibihari vyinshi, umukuru w'intwazangabo z'abasoda atinye ko bogabangana Pahulo, abarira ingabo ngo zimanuke zimubashikure, zimujane mu gisagara gikikijwe n'uruhome rw'amabuye.
44023011	Ijoro ry'uwo musi, Umwami Yesu amuhagarara hejuru ati: "Humura; nk'uko wanshingiye intahe i Yerusalemu, ni ko ukwiye kuzonshingira intahe i Roma. "
44023012	Iryo joro rikeye, Abayuda barakorana, barahira bisiba yuko batazorya ntibanywe batarica Pahulo.
44023013	Abahize batyo barenga mirongo ine.
44023014	Baja ku baherezi bakuru n'abakuru bati: "Twarahiye twisivye bikomeye yuko ata co tuzotamira tutarica Pahulo. "
44023015	Nuko rero mwebwe n'abashingantahe, ni mubwire umukuru w'intwazangabo z'abasoda amubamanukanire, nk'abarondera kurushiriza gutahura ivyiwe neza. Natwe, atarabashikira, twiteguye kumwica. "
44023016	Umwishwa wa Pahulo yumva uwo mutego, araza ashika mu gisagara gikikijwe n'uruhome rw'amabuye, abibarira Pahulo.
44023017	Pahulo ahamagara umwe mu ntwazangabo z'abasoda ijana ati: "Jana uwu muhungu ku mukuru w'intwazangabo z'abasoda; afise ijambo amubarira. "
44023018	Na we aramujana amushira uwo mukuru w'abagabisha ati: "Ya mbohe Pahulo yampamagaye aranyinginga, ngo nkuzanire uwu muhungu, afise ico akubarira. "
44023019	Uwo mukuru amufata ukuboko, aramukebukanya aramubaza biherereye ati: "Ico ufise kumbarira ni igiki? "
44023020	Aramwishura ati: "Abayuda bahuje inama yo kukwinginga ngo ejo uzomanukane Pahulo mw'ikoraniro ry'abashingantahe, nk'uwugomba kubaza ivyiwe ngo urushirize kubimenya neza. "
44023021	None rero ntuje kubumvira, kuko abantu babo barenga mirongo ine bamuryamiye, barahiye bisivye ko batazorya ntibanywe bataramwica; kandi none bariteguye, barorereye ico uribubemerere.
44023022	Uwo mukuru arungika uwo muhungu, amaze kumwihanikiriza ati: "Ntugire umuntu ubarira yuko umenyesheje ivyo. "
44023023	Ahamagara babiri bo mu ntwazangabo z'abasoda ijana, arababarira ati: "Ni mwitegure abasoda amajana abiri bo kuja i Kayisariya, n'abagendera ku mafarasi mirongo irindwi, n'abo amacumu amajana abiri, bahenge mw'ijoro isaha zitatu bagende. "
44023024	Kandi bazane n'amafarasi kugira ngo bayashireko Pahulo, bamushikane kwa Feliki icegera ca Kayisari akiri muzima.
44023025	Yandika ikete nka bene iri
44023026	ati: "Jewe Kilawudiyo Lusiya ndakuganutsa wewe Feliki umwubahwa, icegera ca Kayisari.
44023027	None uwo mugabo Abayuda bari bamaze kumuta mu maboko bagira bamwice, nanje menye ko ari Umuroma nzanana n'ingabo ndamubakiza.
44023028	Kandi nshatse kumenya ico bamurega, ndamumanukana mw'ikoraniro ry'abashingantahe ryabo.
44023029	Mbona yuko bamurega amajambo y'ivyagezwe vyabo, ariko ko ata co yarezwe gikwiye kumwicisha canke kumubohesha.
44023030	Maze mbariwe yuko bahigiye uwo mugabo, nca ndamukurungikira, mbarira abarezi ko bamuregera imbere yawe. Ndakwikebanuye. "
44023031	Nuko abasoda bakira Pahulo uko babariwe, bahenga mw'ijoro bamujana muri Antipatiri.
44023032	Bumaze guca basigayo abagendera ku mafarasi, ngo abe ari bo bajana na we, na bo basubira iyo bavuye ku gisagara gikikijwe n'uruhome rw'amabuye.
44023033	Abo bashitse i Kayisariya bashira icegera ca Kayisari ca cete, bamushikiriza na Pahulo.
44023034	Amaze kugisoma abaza intara y'i wabo iyo ari yo; amenye ko ari uwo i Kilikiya,
44023035	aravuga ati: "Nzokwumva ivyawe abarezi bawe ni bamara kuza. " Agera ko bamurindira mu gisagara ca Herode gikikijwe n'uruhome rw'amabuye.
44024001	Imisi itanu ishize, umuherezi mukuru Ananiya amanukana n'abakuru bamwe n'uwo kubavuganira yitwa Teritulo, barega Pahulo ku cegera ca Kayisari.
44024002	Amaze guhamagazwa, Teritulo atangura kumurega ati: "Ni ku bwawe igituma tugazagaza mu mahoro menshi, n'ibindi vyaroranirijwe ubu bwoko kubwo imigabo yawe;
44024003	nuko turavyemera uburyo bwose ahantu hose, Feliki umwubahwa, tugukengurukiye cane. "
44024004	Reka simpave ndakurambira, ndakwinginze zirikana tuvuge amajambo make, kubwo ubugwaneza bwawe.
44024005	Twabonye uwu muntu ari ikiza, atera umugararizo Abayuda bose bari mu bihugu vyose; ni we mukuru w'igice c'Abanazareti.
44024006	Kandi yagejeje no guhumanya urusengero, turamufata, [twari tugomvye kumucira urubanza nk'uko ivyagezwe vyacu bivuga.
44024007	Ariko umukuru w'intwazangabo z'abasoda Lusiya araza, amudushikura mu maboko,
44024008	abarira abarezi biwe kuza imbere yawe. ] Nawe ni wamwibariza ubwawe urashobora kumenya ivyo tumureze vyose. "
44024009	Abayuda na bo bafatanya na we muri ico kirego, bavuga ko ivyo ari ko biri.
44024010	Icegera ca Kayisari kimaze kumukebura ngo avuge, Pahulo aramwishura ati: "Ndazi ko umaze imyaka myinshi uri umucamanza w'ubu bwoko, ni co gitumye niregura ivyanje ndemye;
44024011	kuko ushobora kumenya yuko imisi itararenga icumi n'ibiri, uhereye aho nadugiye i Yerusalemu gusengerayo.
44024012	Kandi ntibasanze mparira n'umuntu n'umwe, canke nkoraniriza abantu kubakikiza, naho hoba mu rusengero canke mu nsengero z'Abayuda canke mu gisagara.
44024013	Kandi ku vyo bandeze ubu, ntibashobora kuronka ikinyagiriza imbere yawe.
44024014	Ariko iki ni co nkwemerera, ni uko uko iyo Nzira iri, iyo abo bita igice, ari ko nkorera Imana ya ba sogokuruza bacu, nemera vyose bifatanije n'ivyagezwe kandi vyanditswe mu vy'abavugishwa n'Imana;
44024015	mfise ivyizigiro ku Mana bimwe n'ivyo aba na bo biteze, yuko hazoba ukuzuka kw'abagororotsi n'abagabitanya.
44024016	Ni co gituma na ntaryo nkobereza kugira umutima utanyagiriza ikibi ku Mana canke ku bantu.
44024017	Maze imyaka myinshi ishize, njanwayo no gushira ubwoko bwacu ivyo ubuntu, no gutanga ibimazi.
44024018	Nkiri muri vyo bansanga mu rusengero nihumanuye, ata bantu nkoranije, ata n'urwamo ruriho. " Ariko hari Abayuda bamwe bavuye muri Asiya,
44024019	ni bo bari bakwiye kuza hano imbere yawe no kundega, iyaba bafise ico bangaya.
44024020	Canke na bano na bo ni bavuge icaha bambonyeko, aho nari mpagaze imbere y'abacamanza,
44024021	kiretse ryoba rya jambo rimwe navuze n'ijwi rirenga mpagaze muri bo nti: "Ukuzuka kw' abapfuye ni kwo kumpagaritse muri izi manza imbere yanyu uwu musi. "
44024022	Ariko Feliki, kuko yari azi neza ivyo Iyo Nzira ivyo ari vyo, arabibika ati: "Lusiya umukuru w'intwazangabo z'abasoda ni yaza, nzoca urubanza rw'amajambo yanyu. "
44024023	Abarira intwazangabo y' abasoda ijana kumurinda ico amaso, no kutabuza n'umwe mu bagenzi kumukorera.
44024024	Imisi mike ishize, Feliki azanana n'umugore wiwe Durusila w'Umuyudakazi, ahamagaza Pahulo, yumviriza ivyo avuga ku vyo ukwizera Kristo Yesu.
44024025	Akiriko aravuga ivyo ukugororoka n'ivyo ukwirinda n'ivyo ubutungane azocibwa, Feliki acika intege, aramubarira ati: " "Ubu ni wigire, ni naronka uburyo bwiza nzogutumako. "
44024026	Kandi yanaziga ko Pahulo yomuhera amahera; ico ni co camutera kwama amuhamagaza ngo bayage.
44024027	Imyaka ibiri ishize, Porukiyo Fesito akura Feliki. Maze Feliki agomvye kwikundisha Abayuda asiga Pahulo akiboshwe.
44025001	Nuko Fesito ashikiriye intara amara gatatu, araheza ava i Kayisariya aduga i Yerusalemu.
44025002	Abaherezi bakuru n'abahambaye bo mu Bayuda bamuregako Pahulo, baramwinginga,
44025003	bamusaba kubagirira neza kuri uwo, ngo amutumeko, aze i Yerusalemu, na bo baze bamwibundire bamutsinde mu nzira.
44025004	Ariko Fesito abishura yuko Pahulo arindirwa i Kayisariya, kandi ubwiwe ko agiye kujayo vuba.
44025005	Arababwira ati: "Nuko abakuru bo muri mwebwe ni bamanuke tujane, maze namba kuri uwo mugabo hari ikidakwiye, bakimurege. "
44025006	Amaze muri bo imisi itarenga umunani canke icumi, aramanuka aja i Kayisariya; bukeye bw'aho yicara ku ntebe y'imanza avuga ko bazana Pahulo.
44025007	Na we ashitse, Abayuda bamanutse bavuye i Yerusalemu baramukikiza, bamurega ibirego vyinshi bikomeye, ivyo badashobora kuronkera icagiriza.
44025008	Pahulo ariregura ati: "Nta caha nakoze, ari ku vyagezwe vy'Abayuda, canke ku rusengero, canke kuri Kayisari. "
44025009	Fesito agomvye kwikundiriza Abayuda, abaza Pahulo ati: "Wokwemera kuduga i Yerusalemu gucirirwayo urubanza rw'ivyo mu maso yanje? "
44025010	Ariko Pahulo aramwishura ati: "Mpagaze aha imbere y'intebe y'imanza ishinzwe na Kayisari, ni ho nkwiye gucirwa urubanza. " Nta kibi nagiriye Abayuda, kandi nawe urabizi neza.
44025011	Nuko namba naragabitanije, canke narakoze ibikwiye kunyicisha, sinanka gupfa; ariko namba ivyo aba bandega atari ko biri, nta muntu ashobora kubampa. Nzokwitwara kuri Kayisari.
44025012	Fesito amaze kuja inama n'abacamanza, aramwishura ati: "Ko ugomvye kwitwara kuri Kayisari, imbere ya Kayisari ni ho uzoja. "
44025013	Hashize imisi, umwami Agiripa na Berenike bashika i Kayisariya, baja kuramutsa Fesito.
44025014	Bamazeyo imisi myinshi, Fesito ashira imbere y'umwami ivya Pahulo ati: "Hariho umuntu Feliki yasize ari imbohe.
44025015	Aho nari i Yerusalemu abaherezi bakuru n'abakuru b'Abayuda bambariye ivyiwe, basaba ko ndamucira urubanza. "
44025016	Ndabishura nti: "Si umugenzo w'Abaroma gutanga umuntu uwo ari we wese, umuregwa atabanje kuba kumwe n'abamureze imbonankubone, no kubona uburyo bwo kwiregura ibirego bamureze. "
44025017	Nuko bakoraniye hano, sinarinze guteba, ariko bukeye bw'aho nicara ku ntebe y'imanza, ndahamagaza uwo muntu.
44025018	Abarezi bavuye hasi, ntibamurega ikirego na kimwe co mu bibi nakeka;
44025019	ariko bamurega ibihari vyo mw'idini yabo, n'ivyo umuntu yitwa Yesu, yapfuye, uwo Pahulo yavuga ashimitse ko ari muzima.
44025020	Nanje nzazaniwe ingene nobaza ivyo ivyo, ndamubaza yuko agomba kuja i Yerusalemu, gucirirwayo urubanza rw'ivyo.
44025021	Ariko Pahulo asavye kurindwa kugira ngo azocirwe urubanza na Augusito, mvuga ko arindwa gushitsa aho nzomurungikira Kayisari.
44025022	Agiripa yishura Fesito ati: "Nanje nagomba kwumva uwo muntu. " Na we ati: "Ejo uzomwumva. "
44025023	Bukeye bw'aho, Agiripa na Berenike bazanana icubahiro cinshi, binjirana mw'ikoraniro ry'abashingantahe n'abakuru b'intwazangabo z'abasoda n'abahambaye bo muri ico gisagara; maze Fesito avuga ko bazana Pahulo.
44025024	Nuko Fesito aravuga ati: "Mwami Agiripa, namwe mwese abo turi kumwe hano, murabona uwu, uwo ishengero ry'Abayuda bose bansabira i Yerusalemu bo n'ino, basemerera ngo ntagikwiye kubaho. "
44025025	Ariko nsanga ntiyakoze igikwiye kumwicisha, kandi ubwiwe agomvye kwitwara kuri Augusito, nigira imigabo yo kumumurungikira.
44025026	None mbuze ijambo rimenyekanisha ivyiwe ryo kwandikira umwami wanje, ni co gitumye ndamuzana imbere yanyu, kandi canecane imbere yawe, mwami Agiripa, kugira ngo ni twamara kumusiguza, mbone ico kwandika.
44025027	Kuko ngira ngo n'ico ubwenge buke kurungika imbohe, sinerekane ibirego vyayo. "
44026001	Agiripa abarira Pahulo ati: "Uremerewe kwiregura. " Maze Pahulo agorora ukuboko, ariregura
44026002	ati: "Ivyo narezwe n'Abayuda vyose, mwami Agiripa, numva nezerewe ko ari wewe ngira ndavyiregureko uwu musi;
44026003	kandi canecane kuko uzi imigenzo n'impari vyo mu Bayuda vyose: ni co gitumye nkwinginga ngo wihangane, unyumvirize.
44026004	Ingeso zanje, uhereye mu buto bwanje, izo narukanye mu bwoko bwacu n'i Yerusalemu, Abayuda bose barazizi.
44026005	Kandi bokwemera kubishingira intahe, baranzi, uhereye mu bihe vya kera, yuko nari Umufarisayo wo mu muce urusha iyindi yo mw'idini yacu gushimikira imigenzo.
44026006	None mpagaze ngo ncirwe urubanza, kuko nizigira kuzobona ivyo Imana yasezeraniye ba sogokuruza,
44026007	ivyo ubwoko bwacu icumi na bubiri bwizigira kuzobona, bukorera Imana bushizeko umwete mwinshi ku murango no mw'ijoro. Kandi ni kubwo ivyo vyizigiro ndezwe n'Abayuda, databuja!
44026008	Ni igiki gituma mugira ngo ni ikintu kitoruha cemerwa ko Imana izura abapfuye?
44026009	Nanje ubwanje nahora niyumvira muri jewe yuko nkwiye gukora vyinshi birwanya izina rya Yesu Umunyanazareti.
44026010	Kandi ivyo narabikora nyene ndi i Yerusalemu, ngashira abera benshi mu mabohero, mpawe ubushobozi n'abaherezi bakuru, kandi aho babica, nanje nishira mu bemera ko bicwa.
44026011	No mu nsengero z'Abayuda yose nabahana kenshi, nkagerageza cane kubatukisha Yesu; kandi kuko nasazwa cane ndabazira, narabatuza no gushitsa mu bisagara vy'abanyamahanga.
44026012	Ngikora ivyo, nja i Damasiko mpawe ubushobozi ndungitswe n'abaherezi bakuru.
44026013	Nuko databuja, nkigenda mu mashoka, mbona umuco uvuye mw'ijuru, urusha uko izuba rica ibibatsi, unkayanganira irya n'ino, twe n'abo tugendanye.
44026014	Twese twikubise hasi, numva ijwi rimbwira mu rurimi rw'Igiheburayo riti: "Sawuli, Sawuli, umpigira iki? Erega birakugoye gutera imigere ku mihunda. "
44026015	Nanje ndabaza nti: "Uri nde ga Mwami? " Umwami aranyishura ati: "Ndi Yesu, uwo uriko urahiga. "
44026016	Ariko va hasi, hagarara n'ibirenge vyawe, kuko igitumye nkwiyereka, ari ukugira ngo ngutoranye nkugire umukozi wanje n'icabona co gushingira intahe ivyo umbonanye, n'ivyo nzokwiyerekeramwo;
44026017	ndagukize abo muri ubu bwoko bo n'abanyamahanga, ni bo ndagutumyeko,
44026018	kubahumura amaso kugira ngo bahindukire bave mu mwiza baje mu muco, bave no mu bubasha bwa Satani baje ku Mana, bateko baharirwe ivyaha vyabo, baraganwe n'abejejwe n'ukunyizera.
44026019	Nuko, mwami Agiripa, sinanka kwumvira ivyo neretswe vyavuye mw'ijuru.
44026020	Ariko nabanje kubwira abo i Damasiko hanyuma abo i Yerusalemu, n'abo mu gihugu cose c'i Yudaya, n'abanyamahanga na bo, yuko bakwiye kwihana, no guhindukirira Imana, bakore ibikorwa bikwiranye n'ukwihana.
44026021	Ni co catumye Abayuda bamfatira mu rusengero, bakageza kunyica.
44026022	None nabonye gutabarwa kwavuye ku Mana, ndacahagaze kugeza n'ubu, nshingira intahe aboroshe n'abahambaye, nta kindi mvuga atari ivyo abavugishwa n'Imana na Mose bavuze ko bizoba,
44026023	yuko Kristo atazobura kubabazwa, kandi ko ari we azobanza kuzuka mu bapfuye, no kubwira ubwoko bwacu n'abanyamahanga ubutumwa bw'umuco.
44026024	Aciregura atyo, Fesito avuga n'ijwi rirenga ati: "Erega Pahulo urasaze; ubwenge bwawe bwinshi buragushajije. "
44026025	Pahulo aramwishura ati: "Sinsaze, Fesito umwubahwa, ariko mvuga amajambo y'ukuri kandi aroranye. "
44026026	Umwami arazi ivyo neza, kandi ndamubarira nshize amanga; kuko nzi yuko ata na kimwe muri ivyo ahishijwe, kuko ivyo bitakorewe mu mfuruka.
44026027	Mwami Agiripa, uremeye ivyo abavugishwa n'Imana? Ndazi yuko uvyemeye.
44026028	Agiripa yishura Pahulo ati: "Unkwegesha ivyo bike ngo umpindure Umukristo? "
44026029	Pahulo ati: "Ndasaba Imana ari bike ari vyinshi, yuko atoba wewe wenyene, ariko n'abanyumva uwu musi mwese, ko vyobahindura nkanje, ukuye iyi minyororo. "
44026030	Umwami ahagurukana n'icegera ca Kayisari na Berenike, n'abari bicaranye na we;
44026031	maze basohotse baravugana bati: "Nta co uwu muntu yakoze gikwiye kumwicisha canke kumubohesha. "
44026032	Agiripa abarira Fesito ati: "Uwu muntu aba arekuwe, iyo ataba yari agomvye kuzokwitwara kuri Kayisari. "
44027001	Bamaze gushinga ngo tujabuke tuje muri Italiya, Pahulo n'izindi mbohe babaha intwazangabo z'abasoda ijana yitwa Yuliyo, wo mu ngabo za Augusito.
44027002	Dutambukira mu bwato bwavuye muri Aduramutiyo, bugira bugende bujabukiranya ahantu ho muri Asiya haherereye ku kiyaga, tuvayo turi kumwe na Arisitariko Umunyamakedoniya w'i Tesalonike.
44027003	Bukeye bw'aho dufata i Sidoni, Yuliyo agirira Pahulo neza, amukundira kugendera abagenzi ngo bamuzimane.
44027004	Tuvayo, duca musi y'i Kupuro ngo tuhikinge umuyaga, kuko wari uduturutse imbere.
44027005	Tujabutse ikiyaga gihereranye n'i Kilikiya n'i Pamfiliya, dufata mu gisagara c'i Lukiya citwa Mura.
44027006	Iyo ntwazangabo y'abasoda ijana ahasanga ubwato buvuye muri Alekisanderiya buja muri Italiya, adushiramwo.
44027007	Tumaze imisi myinshi tugenda buhoro, dushika hafi y'i Kinido bitugoye cane, maze umuyaga utubujije duca musi y'i Kirete, imbere y'i Salumone, ngo tuhikinge umuyaga.
44027008	Tujana inkengera bitugoye cane, dushika ahantu hitwa Vyambuvyiza, hafi y'igisagara citwa Laseya.
44027009	Hashize igihe kirekire, kandi kujabuka kubaye irinde, kuko igihe co kwisonzesha cari gishize, Pahulo arabahanura,
44027010	arababarira ati Yemwe bagabo, ndabonye yuko uru rugendo rugira rubemwo ivyago n'ubuhombe bwinshi, si ivyo ubwato n'ibirimwo gusa, ariko n'ivyo amagara yacu na yo.
44027011	Ariko, intwazangabo z'abasoda yumvira uwutumbereza ubwato na nyene bwo kurusha ivyo Pahulo avuze.
44027012	Kandi kuko icambu atari ciza co kugumamwo kuhamara urushana, abenshi babagira inama yo kuvayo, ngo bishobotse bashike i Foyinike, kuba ari ho bamara agatasi, hari icambu c'i Kirete, cerekeye hagati yo mu buraruko no mu buseruko, kandi hagati yo mu buseruko no mu bumanuko.
44027013	Maze umuyaga uturutse mu bumanuko uhuhuse buhorobuhoro, bibwiye ko baronse ico bagomba, bazitura ubwato, bagenda bajana inkengera hafi cane y'i Kirete.
44027014	Ariko igihe kitari kinini gishize, hatera umuyaga w'igihuhuta witwa Ewurakulo, uturutse kuri ico kizinga.
44027015	Ubwato bumaze guhuhwa n'uwo muyaga, butagishobora gutumbera umuyaga, turabureka burakubebwa.
44027016	Duca musi y'akazinga kitwa Kilawuda, tuhikinga umuyaga, tubona uko tuboha akato k'inyuma bitugoye cane;
44027017	bamaze kugaterura, bakira ibitsibo vy'integakiba, babicisha musi y'ubwato, barabuboha, kandi kuko batinya gusukwa ku musenyi ushaya witwa Suriti, bamanura igihuzu kigendesha ubwato, bagenda batyo bakubebwa.
44027018	Tuzungagizwa cane n'igihuhuta, bukeye bw'aho bata imitwaro mu kiyaga.
44027019	Kw'igenekerezo rya gatatu batesha amaboko yabo ibikoresho vyo mu bwato.
44027020	Kandi izuba n'inyenyeri bimaze imisi myinshi bitaboneka, turi mu gihuhuta cinshi gityo, twihebura rwose ko ata wuzokira.
44027021	Bamaze igihe kirekire batakirya, Pahulo ahagarara hagati muri bo, arababarira ati: "Yemwe bagabo, mwari mukwiye kunyumvira, ntimuve i Kirete, ngo mugire ibi vyago n'ubuhombe. "
44027022	Kandi none ndabaremesha, ni muhumure, kuko muri mwebwe hatazopfa n'umwe, atari ubwato.
44027023	Kuko muri iri joro umumarayika w'Imana, ndi uwayo, kandi ni yo nkorera, yahagaze i ruhande yanje,
44027024	arambwira ati: "Nta co utinya, Pahulo; ukwiye guhagarara imbere ya Kayisari, kandi ehe Imana ikwemereye n'abo mugendanye bose. "
44027025	Nuko ni muhumure, yemwe bagabo, kuko nizeye Imana, yuko bizoba nk'uko nabariwe.
44027026	Ariko hari ikizinga dukwiye gusukwako.
44027027	Ijoro ry'icumi na kane rishitse, dukubebwa irya n'ino mu kiyaga ca Adiriya; maze nko mu gicugu abagendesha ubwato bakeka ko hari igihugu begereye.
44027028	Bagera uburebure bw'amazi yo hasi, babona ingero mirongo ibiri; hashize umwanya muto bongera kugera, babona ingero icumi na zitanu.
44027029	Kandi kuko batinya gusukwa ahantu h'amabuye baterera mu mazi ivyuma bine vyo kuzirika ubwato babicishije mu mutwe w'inyuma; bifuza ko buca.
44027030	Maze abasoza ubwato barondeye ingene bobuvamwo, bururukiriza ka kato mu kiyaga, bibonekesha nk'abagomba kuzirikisha ivyuma umutwe w'imbere.
44027031	Pahulo abarira ya ntwazangabo y'abasoda ijana, hamwe n'abasoda na bo ati: "Aba ni bataguma mu bwato ntimushobora gukira. "
44027032	Maze abasoda baca imigozi ifashe akato, ngo bakareke gakoroke.
44027033	Bugira buce Pahulo arabinginga bose ngo barye ati: "None uwu musi ni uwugira icumi na kane mukirorereye mutarya, ata co mutamira.
44027034	Nuko ndabinginze, ni murabe utwo murya; kuko ari vyo vyobakiza, kandi ntihazohara agashatsi na kamwe ko ku mitwe yanyu. " "
44027035	Amaze kuvuga ivyo, yakira umutsima, ashimira Imana imbere yabo bose, arawumanyagura, atangura kurya.
44027036	Bose basubiza umutima mu nda, na bo bararya.
44027037	Kandi twese abari mu bwato twari abantu amajana abiri na mirongo irindwi na batandatu.
44027038	Bamaze guhaga, baremurura ubwato, bata ingano mu kiyaga.
44027039	Ijoro rikeye, ntibamenya ico gihugu, ariko babonye ikigobe kirimwo umusenyi, baja inama yuko boshobora gushikanaho ubwato.
44027040	Bazitura imigozi ifashe ivyuma biziritse ubwato, babirekera mu kuzimu; bariko barabikora, batenzura imigozi yari igumije ingafe zihindukiza ubwato, baduza igihuzu c'imbere kibugendesha ngo gihuhwe n'umuyaga, batumbereza ku musenyi.
44027041	Ariko bashitse mw'ihuriro ry'amazi, basekura ubwato ku gataka, maze umutwe wabwo w'imbere winjiramwo, urahamangira, uwo inyuma na wo utangura kumenagurwa n'inkomezi z'imipfunda. "
44027042	Inama y' abasoda kwari uko bokwica imbohe, kugira ngo ntihagire uwo muri zo yokwoga agatoroka.
44027043	Ariko ya ntwazangabo y'abasoda, agomvye gukiza Pahulo, ababuza iyo nama yabo, avuga yuko abazi kwoga bokwisuka mu mazi, kugira ngo babanze gushika ku nkombe,
44027044	abandi na bo, bamwe bagende ku mbaho, abandi ku bindi bivuye mu bwato. Nuko bagenza batyo, bashika ku nkombe bose, barakira.
44028001	Tumaze gukira, tumenya ico kizinga yuko citwa Melita.
44028002	Abanyamahanga badebagura baratugirira neza cane bitangaje, baducanira umuriro kubwo imvura n'imbeho vyariho, batwakira twese.
44028003	Ariko Pahulo amaze gusenya umuganda w'inkwi, arazikomanya, inzoka iva mu muriro, imukomora ku kuboko.
44028004	Abo badebaguzi babonye ico gikoko cenena ku kuboko kwiwe, baravugana bati: "Uwu muntu ntabuze kuba umwicanyi; kandi naho yakize ikiyaga, Iyidaca urwa nkunzi ntimukundiye ko abaho. "
44028005	Ariko akunkumurira ico gikoko mu muriro, ntiyagira ico aba.
44028006	Ba bandi barereka ko avyimba, canke ko agwa bukumbi; ariko bamara umwanya munini babireretse, babonye ata co abaye, barahindura bati: "Ni Imana. "
44028007	Hafi y'aho hantu hari amatongo y'umukuru w'ico kizinga, yitwa Pubiliyo aratwakira, atuzimana neza imisi itatu.
44028008	Se wa Pubiliyo yari arwaye inyonko kandi agacibwamwo amaraso. Maze Pahulo yinjira i we, arasenga; amurambikako ibiganza, aramukiza.
44028009	Ivyo bibaye, abandi bari n'indwara bo muri ico kizinga baraza, arazibakiza.
44028010	Baduha icubahiro mu buryo bwinshi; maze mu gihe co kujabuka kwacu bashira mu bwato ivyo dukenye.
44028011	Tuhamaze amezi atatu, tuvayo mu bwato bwari bwavuye muri Alekisanderiya, bwari bumaze iyo misi y'urushana ku kizinga. Ikimenyetso cabwo cari Imana z'Amahasa.
44028012	Dufata i Surakusa, tuhamara imisi itatu.
44028013	Turahava, turazunguruka, dufata i Regiyo. Hashize umusi umwe umuyaga uturutse mu bumanuko urahuhuta, tugenda imisi ibiri, dufata i Puteyoli.
44028014	Tuhasanga abavukanyi bamwe, baratwinginga ngo tumarane na bo imisi indwi; uko ni ko twashitse i Roma.
44028015	Abavukanyi b'i Roma bumvise inkuru yacu, baza kudusanganirira ahitwa Akaguriro ka Apiyo, n'ahitwa Amaduka Atatu. Pahulo ababonye ashima Imana, umutima urarema. "
44028016	Tumaze gushika Roma, intwazangabo z'abasoda ijana ashikiriza imbohe intwazangabo z' abasoda bahora bacungera kwa Kayisari, ariko bakundira Pahulo kuba ukwiwe, ari kumwe n'umusoda amurinda.
44028017	Imisi itatu iheze ahamagara abakuru bo mu Bayuda abakoraniriza hamwe; bamaze gukorana, arababarira ati: " "Bagabo bavukanyi, naho ntagize ikibi nakoze ku bwoko bwacu canke ku migenzo ya ba sogokuruza, bampaye Abaroma ndi imbohe, bamvanye i Yerusalemu. "
44028018	Na bo bamaze kuncunaguza, bashaka kundekura, kuko ata nyanduruko yambonetseko yo kunyicisha.
44028019	Ariko Abayuda batagaye, numva nkwiye kwitwara kuri Kayisari; ariko si uko mfise ico ndega ubwoko bwacu.
44028020	Ivyo ni vyo nabatumiyeko ngo tuvugane tubonana; kuko ivyo Abisirayeli bizigira kuzobona ari vyo vyatumye mboheshwa uwu munyororo.
44028021	Na bo baramwishura bati: "Nta vyete twaronse bivuye i Yudaya bivuga ivyawe, kandi mu bavukanyi baje nta watubariye inkuru mbi yawe, canke ngo akuvuge nabi. "
44028022	Ariko turagomba kwumva ivyo wiyumvira, kuko ico gice tuzi yuko bakivuga nabi hose.
44028023	Basezerana na we umusi, baza iyo ari ari benshi, mu nzu bamuhaye, arabibasobanurira, ashingira intahe ivyo ubwami bw' Imana, abemeza ivya Yesu, abikuye mu vyagezwe vya Mose no mu vyo abavugishwa n'Imana, ahera mu gitondo ashitsa ku mugoroba.
44028024	Maze bamwe bemera ivyo avuze, abandi ntibavyemera.
44028025	Batemeranije ubwabo barataha, Pahulo asubiye kuvuga ijambo rimwe ati: "Ivyo Mpwemu Yera yabaririye ba sogokuruza banyu mu kanwa k'uwavugishwa n'Imana Yesaya, yabivuze neza,
44028026	ati: 'Ja kuri ubwo bwoko ' Uti: "Kwumva muzokwumva, ariko ntimuzoruha mubitahura; Kuraba muzoraba, ariko ntimuzoruha muvyihweza.
44028027	Kuko umutima w'ubu bwoko ucuramye, Amatwi yabo akaba ari bihurugutwi, Amaso yabo bakayahumiriza. Ngo ntibarabishe amaso, Ntibumvishe amatwi, Ntibatahurishe imitima, Ngo bahindukire, Ndabakize.
44028028	Nuko mumenye yuko ako gakiza k'Imana karungitswe ku banyamahanga, kandi abo bazokwumva. " "[
44028029	Amaze kuvuga atyo, Abayuda bagenda baharirizanya bikomeye. ]
44028030	Amara mu nzu yiwe yirihira imyaka ibiri ikwiye, yama yakira abaje kumugendera bose,
44028031	akabahanura mu vyo ubwami bw'Imana, akigisha ivyo Umwami Yesu Kristo, ashize amanga rwose, ata wumubuza."
45001001	Jewe Pahulo umushumba wa Yesu Kristo nahamagariwe ubutumwa bw'Imana.
45001002	Imana yabubasezeraniye kera ibivugiye mu bo yavugisha na bo bakabwandika mu vyanditswe vyera.
45001003	Buvuga ivyo Umwana wayo yavutse mu buryo bw'umuntu mu ruvyaro rwa Dawidi.
45001004	Ariko mu buryo bwa Mpwemu Yera, yerekanywe ko ari Umwana w'Imana ukuzuka kwiwe yakwerekanishije ubushobozi, uwo ni Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu.
45001005	Twaronse ubuntu n'ibanga ryo kuba intumwa ku bwiwe kugira ngo mu mahanga yose habemwo abumvira Imana, babiheshwa no kwizera.
45001006	Kandi namwe muri muri bo, mwahamagariwe kuba aba Yesu Kristo.
45001007	Ndabandikiye mwese muri i Roma mukundwa n'Imana, mwahamagariwe kuba abera. Ubuntu n'amahoro bubabemwo, biva ku Mana, Data wa twese, no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo bibabemwo.
45001008	Irya mbere, ndashimiye Imana yanje muri Yesu Kristo ku bwanyu mwese, kuko inkuru y'ukwizera kwanyu ikwiye mw'isi yose.
45001009	Imana, nkorera mu mutima wanje mvuga ubutumwa bwiza bw'Umwana wayo, ni yo ntanzeko icabona yuko ndabahoza mu kanwa ubudasiba.
45001010	Imisi yose uko nsenze, nsaba ngo ubu hoho ibigomvye Imana yemere kunzana amahoro no kunzana i wanyu. "
45001011	Kuko nifuza kubabona, kugira ngo ndabahe ingabire y'impwemu, ibaremeshe;
45001012	ni kwo guhumurizanya namwe, mpumurizwe n'ukwizera kwanyu, namwe muhumurizwe n'ukwanje.
45001013	Kandi bavukanyi, singomba ko mutamenya yuko kenshi nari mfise imigabo yo kuza i wanyu, kugira ngo namwe ndabamuremwo imbuto, nk'uko nazibonye mu yandi mahanga, ariko ngira ikimbuza kugeza n'ubu.
45001014	Mfitiye umwenda Abagiriki n'abanyamahanga badebagura, abanyabwenge bo n'ibijuju.
45001015	Ni co gituma jeho kubwanje niteguye kubabwira ubutumwa bwiza namwe muri i Roma.
45001016	Ubutumwa bwiza ntibuntera isoni kuko ari ubushobozi bw' Imana, buzanira uwizera wese agakiza, uhereye ku Muyuda ukageza ku Mugiriki.
45001017	Kuko muri bwo ari ho ukugororoka kuva ku Mana guhishurwa, guheshwa n'ukwizera kukagwiza ukwizera, nk'uko vyanditswe," ngo umugororotsi azobeshwaho n'ukwizera.
45001018	Ishavu ry'Imana ryarahishuwe, rivuye mw'ijuru, irisuka ku bayigarariza n'abagabitanya bakayongesha ukuri ukugabitanya kwabo.
45001019	Kuko ivyo umuntu yomenya vy'Imana vyerekanwa muri bo, Imana ari yo yabiberetse.
45001020	Mbere kuva isi ikiremwa ivyo Imana bitunganye bitabonwa n'amaso ari vyo bushobozi bwayo budashira be n'ubumana bwayo, biragaragara; bimenyekanishwa kuko bibonekera mu vyo yaremye, kugira ngo ntibagire ico bireguza.
45001021	Kuko bamenye Imana ntibayubahe nk' Imana, ntibayishime; ariko bacitse abiyumvira ivyo ubusa, imitima yabo y'ubujuju icura umwiza.
45001022	Biyise abanyabwenge bacika ibipfu.
45001023	Icubahiro c'Imana idapfa baragikaba no gusenge ibishushanyo bisa n'umuntu apfa, ivyo ibiguruka, ivyo ibigenza amaguru ane n'ivyo ibikwega inda hasi.
45001024	Ni co catumye Imana ibaheba ngo bakore ibiteye isoni, bumvire ivyo imitima yabo yifuza, bonone imibiri yabo,
45001025	kuko ukuri kw'Imana bagukavye ibinyoma, bagasenga bagakorera icaremwe, bakakirutisha Iyakiremye, ni yo ikwiye gushimwa ibihe bidashira. Amina.
45001026	Ni co catumye Imana ibaheba ngo bipfuze ivyonona; kuko abagore babo bahinduye ukundi ico imibiri yabo yaremewe bayikoresha ico itaremewe.
45001027	Kandi n'abagabo ni uko, baretse kugirira abagore ivyo imibiri yabo yaremewe, bashuha babegukana, abagabo bagirira abandi bagabo ibiteye isoni, kandi mu mibiri yabo bahabwa ingero zikwiranye n'ikosa ryabo.
45001028	Kandi nk'uko banse kumenya Imana mu mitima yabo, ni ko Imana yabahevye ngo bagire imitima y' akahebwe, bakore ibitabereye.
45001029	Buzuye ukugabitanya kwose, ukugira nabi, ukwifuza n'urwanko rw'ubusa. Buzuye igono, ubwicanyi, ugutongana, ubugunge, ukwitamba ku muvyimba; abaneguranira mu vyongorerano,
45001030	abavuga abandi nabi, abanka Imana, abatukana, abibona, abirarira, abigenera ibibi, abatumvira abavyeyi,
45001031	ibipfu, abava mw'isezerano, abadakunda n'ababo n'imburakigongwe.
45001032	Abo, naho bamenye urubanza Imana ica, yuko abakora ibisa bityo bakwiye gupfa, ntibabikora gusa, ariko batako bagashima n'ababikora.
45002001	Ni co gituma utagira ico wireguza, wewe muntu wese uhinyura uwundi. Ko uhinyura uwundi, uba witsindishije; kuko wewe umuhinyura ukora nk'ivyo nawe nyene akora.
45002002	Ariko turazi yuko urubanza Imana icira abakora ibisa bityo ari urwo ukuri.
45002003	Wewe ga muntu, uhinyura abakora ibisa bityo, nawe ubikora, mbega wiyumvira yuko uzokira urubanza Imana ica?
45002004	canke ukengera itunga ryo kugira neza kwayo, iryo imbabazi zayo n'iryo ukwihangana kwayo? Ntuzi yuko kugira neza kw'Imana kugushikana ku kwihana?
45002005	Ariko kuko uwufise umutima ukomantaye utihana, wirindiriza ishavu ry'inkazi rizoza ku musi wo kuraka, aho imanza zibereye z'Imana zizohishurirwa.
45002006	Izokwishura umuntu wese ibikwiranye n'ivyo yakoze.
45002007	Abarondera ubwiza n'icubahiro no kudapfa, bahora bakora ivyiza bihanganye, izobishura ubugingo budashira.
45002008	Ariko ku bakebana ntibumvire ivyo ukuri, ariko bakumvira ukugabitanya, hazoba ishavu no guhambarirwa
45002009	n'amarushwa n'ivyago ku bugingo bw'umuntu wese akora ibibi, uhereye ku Muyuda, ukageza ku Mugiriki.
45002010	Ariko ubwiza n'icubahiro n'amahoro bizoba ku muntu wese akora ivyiza, uhereye ku Muyuda, ukageza ku Mugiriki,
45002011	kuko Imana itarobanura abantu ku cubahiro.
45002012	Abakoze ivyaha bose, batazi ivyagezwe, bazohona ivyagezwe bitarinze kwiyumvirwa; kandi abakoze ivyaha bose bazi ivyagezwe bazotsindishwa n'ivyagezwe.
45002013	Kuko abumvise ivyagezwe atari bo bagororoka imbere y'Imana, abavyumviye ni bo bazotsindanishirizwa.
45002014	Abanyamahanga badafise ivyagezwe n'Imana iyo bakoze ibibwirizwa na vyo ku bwabo, baba bihindukiye ivyagezwe naho batabifise.
45002015	Berekana ko uburyo bakora bakurikije ivyagezwe, vyanditswe mu mitima yabo, ijwi ryo mu mitima yabo rirabishingira intahe ari icabona cavyo, kandi ivyo biyumvira bifatanya kubarega canke kubaregura.
45002016	Ni ko bizoba ku musi Imana izocira urubanza muri Yesu Kristo ivyo abantu bagize amabanga, nk'uko ubutumwa bwiza nahawe buvuga.
45002017	Ko witwa Umuyuda, ukishimira ivyagezwe, ukirata Imana,
45002018	ukamenya ivyo igomba, ukarobanura ibidahwana, kuko wigishijwe ivyo ivyagezwe,
45002019	ukishima yuko ushobora kujana impumyi, kandi ko uri umuco w'abari mu mwiza,
45002020	n'umuhanuzi w'abanyabwenge buke, n'umwigisha w'utwana, kuko mu vyagezwe ufise icerekana ubwenge n'ukuri.
45002021	Nuko wewe wigisha abandi, mbega ntiwiyigisha? Wewe wihaniza abiba, weho ntiwiba?
45002022	Wewe ubabuza gusambana, weho ntusambana? Wewe wanka ibishushanyo vy'ibigirwamana, weho ntiwiba ivyo mu nsengero zavyo?
45002023	Wewe wirata ivyagezwe, mbega ntugayisha Imana kuko ubicumurako?
45002024	Izina ry'Imana muritukisha mu mahanga, nk'uko vyanditswe.
45002025	Kuko guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo kugira ico kukumarira, iyo witondeye ivyagezwe; ariko iyo ucumuye ku vyagezwe, guhimbura igikoba c'ubugabo kwawe kuba gucitse ukudahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo.
45002026	None uwutakebwe igikoba c'ubugabo ni yitondera ibibwirijwe n'ivyagezwe, mbega kudahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo kwiwe ntikuzomuharurwako nko guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo?
45002027	Kandi uwutahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo ku mubiri ni yitondera ivyagezwe, azogutsindisha, wewe ucumura ku vyagezwe, ufise inyuguti zavyo no guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo.
45002028	Kuko Umuyuda wo ku rukoba atari we Muyuda; kandi guhimbura igikoba c'ubugabo kwo ku mubiri atari kwo guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo.
45002029	Ariko Umuyuda wo mu mutima ni we Muyuda, kandi guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo ni uko umutima, n'ukwo mu buryo bw'impwemu, atari ukwo mu buryo bw'inyuguti; uwumeze atyo ntashimwa n'abantu, ariko ashimwa n' Imana.
45003001	None Umuyuda aruta abandi ate? Canke guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo kumara iki?
45003002	Arabibarusha vyose. Ica mbere, ni uko Abayuda babikijwe ivyavuzwe n'Imana.
45003003	Tuvuge iki? Naho bamwe batizeye, mbega kutizera kwabo kuzohindura ubusa ivyo Imana yizigiweko?
45003004	Oya namba. Ariko Imana iboneke ko ari inyakuri, n'iyo umuntu wese yoba ari umubeshi; nk'uko handitswe, ngo Kugira ngo mu majambo yawe uboneke ko ugororotse, Kandi utsinde ni washika mu rubanza. "
45003005	Ariko namba ukugabitanya kwacu kwashimagije ukugororoka kw' Imana, tuvuge iki? Mbega Imana iragabitanya, kuko iduhanisha ishavu ryayo? Ndabivuze nk'imvugo y'abantu.
45003006	Eka na mba! Iyo biba bityo, Imana yociriye abari mw'isi urubanza ite?
45003007	Ariko namba ibinyoma vyanje vyatumye ukuri kw'Imana kurushiriza kwerekanwa, bikayitera icubahiro, ni igiki gituma nanje ncirwa urubanza nk'umunyavyaha?
45003008	Kandi ni igiki kitubuza gukora ibibi kugira ngo ivyiza bibeho? (nk'uko batubeshera bakanavuga ko twigisha ibibi). Abakora batyo bazocirwa urubanza bakwiranye.
45003009	Nuko tuvuge iki? Mbega turuta abandi? Oya, ntitubaruta na gatoya, kuko tumaze kwagiriza Abayuda n'Abagiriki bose ko baganzwa n'icaha;
45003010	nk'uko handitswe," ngo Nta wugororoka, nta n'umwe,
45003011	Nta wutahura, Nta wurondera Imana.
45003012	Barazimiye iyo bava bakagera, bose bacitse imburakimazi, Nta wukora ivyiza, eka nta n'umwe.
45003013	Imihogo yabo n'imva zirangaye, Bahendahendanishije indimi zabo; Ubumara bw'inzoka buri mu binyigishi vyabo.
45003014	Akanwa kabo kuzuye ukuvuma no kujingitwa,
45003015	Ibirenge vyabo vyihutira kuvisha amaraso.
45003016	Guhonya n'ugusinzikaza biri mu nzira zabo,
45003017	Inzira y'amahoro ntibayimenye;
45003018	Nta gutinya Imana kuri mu maso yabo.
45003019	Ariko turazi yuko ivyo ivyagezwe bivuga vyose bibibwira abaganzwa na vyo, kugira ngo akanwa kose kazibwe, kandi abari mw'isi bose babe abo gutsindwa n'urubanza imbere y'Imana;
45003020	kuko imbere yayo ata muntu azoba umwere kubwo ibikorwa vyubahiriza ivyagezwe, kuko ivyagezwe ari vyo bimenyekanisha icaha.
45003021	Ariko noneho ivyagezwe bitariho, ukugororoka kuva ku Mana kurahishuwe, gushingirwa intahe n'ivyagezwe n'ivyo abavugishwa n'Imana,
45003022	ni ukugororoka kuva ku Mana, kuzanwa no kwizera Yesu Kristo, kugira ngo abizeye bose baguhabwe. Kuko ata tandukaniro;
45003023	bose bakoze ivyaha, ntibashikira ubwiza bw'Imana.
45003024	Ubuntu bwayo bubagira abera, ibibahereye ubusa, ku bwo gucungurwa kubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu.
45003025	Uwo Imana yashizeho kuba indishi y'uwizera, ayigirwa n'amaraso yiwe, kugira ngo Imana yerekane ukugororoka kwayo, kuko yirengagije ivyaha vyakozwe kera ku bwo imbabazi zayo;
45003026	no kugira ngo yerekane ukugororoka kwayo muri iki gihe, ngo ibe Iyigororoka n'Iyigira abantu abera uwizeye Yesu.
45003027	None rero ukwihaya kuri hehe? Kwarabujijwe. Kwabujijwe n'ivyagezwe ki? Mbega ni ivyo ibikorwa? Haba na mba; kwabujijwe n'ivyo ukwizera.
45003028	Ni co gituma twiyumvira yuko umuntu agirwa umwere n'ukwizera, ibikorwa vyubahiriza ivyagezwe bitarinze kwiyumvirwa.
45003029	Canke Imana ni iyo Abayuda bonyene? Mbega si iyo abanyamahanga na bo? Ego me, ni iyo abanyamahanga na bo.
45003030	Ko Imana ari imwe, izobagira abere abahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo ku bwo ukwizera, kandi izobagira abere batahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo babiheshwa n'ukwizera.
45003031	Mbega none ivyagezwe tubihinduza ubusa ukwizera? Eka na mba; ushime turabitsindagiye.
45004001	None rero, ico twovuga yuko Aburahamu sogokuruza ku mubiri yaronse ni igiki?
45004002	Iyo Aburahamu agirwa umwere kubwo ibikorwa, aba afise ico yihaya. Ariko imbere y'Imana nta co afise.
45004003	Ivyanditswe bivuga iki? Bivuga ngo Aburahamu yizeye Imana, ibimuharurako nk'ukugororoka.
45004004	Yamara uwukora, ingero yiwe ntiharurwa nk'ubuntu iharurwa nk'inyishu.
45004005	Ariko uwudakora, akizera Iyigira abatayubashe abere, ukwizera kwiwe rurwa nk'ukugororoka.
45004006	Nk'uko Dawidi na we yavuze ubuhirwe bw'umuntu uwo Imana iharura nk'uwugororotse, atari kubwo ibikorwa
45004007	ati: "Harahiriwe abahariwe ibigabitanyo vyabo," kandi ivyaha vyabo bigahishwa,
45004008	Harahiriwe umuntu Uhoraho atazoharurako icaha.
45004009	Mbega ubwo buhirwe buvugwa ku bahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo bonyene, canke ku batahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo na bo? Kuko tuvuga tuti: "Ukwizera kwaharuwe kuri Aburahamu nk'ukugororoka."
45004010	Kwaharuwe ryari? Yari yarahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, canke ntiyaribwagihimburwe? Ico gihe si uko yari amaze guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo ariko ntiyaribwagihimburwe.
45004011	Kandi ahabwa ikimenyetso, ni kwo guhimburwa igikoba co ku mutwe w'igihimba c'irondoka, kuba ikimenyetso c'ukugororoka kwavuye kuri kwa kwizera yarafise atarahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo, kugira ngo abe sekuruza w'abizera bose batahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, ngo bibaharurweko ukugororoka;
45004012	kandi abe na sekuruza w'abahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, batahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo gusa, ariko bagera ikirenge mu c'ukwo kwizera kwa sogokuruza Aburahamu, ukwo yarafise, atarahimburwa igikoba co ku mutwe w'igihimba c'irondoka.
45004013	Kuko atari kubwo ivyagezwe Aburahamu yasezeraniwe canke uruvyaro rwiwe, yuko azoragwa isi yose, ariko ni kubwo ukugororoka kuva ku kwizera.
45004014	Abizigira ivyagezwe iyo baba ari bo baragwa, ukwizera kuba kwarahindutse ubusa, ivyasezeranywe bikaba bititutse.
45004015	Kuko ivyagezwe bizana ishavu, ariko aho ivyagezwe bitari, nta gicumuro kiba kiriho.
45004016	Ni co gituma abaragwa babihawe kubwo kwizera ngo bibe ivyo bahawe ku buntu kugira ngo ivyasezeraniwe uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu bibe ivya bose, bitari ivyo abaganzwa n'ivyagezwe gusa; ariko ngo bibe n'ivyabaganzwa n'ukwizera kwa Aburahamu, sogokuruza wacu twese.
45004017	Nakugize sekuruza w'amahanga menshi. Imbere y'Imana yacu yizeye ari yo izura abapfuye ikita n'ibitariho nk'ibiriho; ni we Sogokuruza wacu twese.
45004018	Aburahamu yizera yizigiye ibitokwizigiwe, ngo abe sekuruza w'amahanga menshi, nk'uko vyavuzwe, ngo uruvyaro rwawe ni ko ruzongana.
45004019	Kandi ntiyagabanukako ukwizera, yitegereje umubiri wiwe umaze kuba akaheze, kuko yari amaze imyaka nk'ijana y'amavuka yiwe, na Sara yari yaraciye.
45004020	Ariko yiyumviriye ico Imana yamusezeraniye, ntiyakekeranishwa no kutizera, ariko aremeshwa cane no kwizera, ahesha Imana icubahiro,
45004021	amenya neza adakekeranya yuko ico yasezeranye ishobora no kugikora.
45004022	Ni co catumye bimuharurwako nk'ukugororoka.
45004023	Ariko ntivyandikiwe we wenyene yuko vyamuharuweko nk'ukugororoka,
45004024	ariko no kubwacu, bizoduharurwako nka kwo, kuko twizeye Iyazuye Yesu Umwami wacu imukuye mu bapfuye,
45004025	yatangiwe ibigabitanyo vyacu, akazurwa kugira ngo tugirwe abera.
45005001	None rero, ko twagizwe abera n'ukwizera, dufise amahoro ku Mana ku bwo Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo,
45005002	yadushikanishije ukwizera muri ubu buntu duhagazemwo, kandi tunezerezwa no kwizigira kuzobona ubwiza bw' Imana.
45005003	Kandi si vyo vyonyene, ariko kandi tunezererwe n'amarushwa yacu, kuko tuzi yuko amarushwa atera ukwihangana;
45005004	kandi ukwihangana kugatera kudatsindwa no kugeragezwa; kudatsindwa no kugeragezwa kugatera kwizigira ibitaraba.
45005005	Ukwo kwizigira ntigutetereza, kuko urukundo rw'Imana rwasutswe hose mu mitima yacu na Mpwemu Yera twahawe.
45005006	Tugifise intege nke, mu gihe gikwiye Kristo yapfiriye abatubaha Imana.
45005007	Ko ari ibigoye k'umuntu apfira umugororotsi, umunyangeso nziza kumbure umuntu yotinyuka kumupfira.
45005008	Ariko Imana yatweretse urukundo rwayo idukunda, kuko Kristo yadupfiriye tukiri abanyavyaha.
45005009	Nuko none tumaze guhindurwa intungane n'amaraso yiwe, tuzorushiriza guheshwa na we gukizwa ishavu ry' Imana.
45005010	Ko twujujwe n'Imana n'urupfu rw'Umwana wayo, tukiri abansi bayo, none tumaze kwuzura na yo, ubugingo bwiwe buzorushiriza kudukiza.
45005011	Kandi si vyo vyonyene, ariko ikindi, tunezererwa Imana ku bwo Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, yaduhesheje kwuzura na yo.
45005012	None rero ko bimeze bityo, nk'uko icaha cazanywe mw'isi n'umuntu umwe, urupfu rukazanwa n'icaha, ni ko urupfu rushika ku bantu bose, kuko bose bakoze ivyaha.
45005013	Ivyagezwe bitarabaho, icaha cari mw'isi, ariko abantu ntibaharurwako icaha, ivyagezwe bitariho.
45005014	Ariko uhereye kuri Adamu, ukageza kuri Mose, urupfu rwaganza n'abatakoze icaha gisa n'igicumuro ca Adamu, yari igishushanyo c'uwagira azoze.
45005015	Ariko ingabire y'Imana ntimera nka ca gicumuro. Ko igicumuro c'umwe catumye abenshi bapfa, ubuntu bw'Imana n'ingabire y'ubuntu bw'umuntu umwe Yesu Kristo vyarushirije gusaguka kuri benshi.
45005016	Kandi iyo ngabire ntiyaje nk'icazanywe n'igicumuro c'umuntu umwe; kuko gucirwa urubanza kwavuye ku muntu umwe, kugatera gutsindwa, ariko ya ngabire yavuye mu bicumuro vyinshi, izana guhindurwa intungane.
45005017	Ko igicumuro c'umwe catumye urupfu rushirwa ku butware n'umwe, abakira ubuntu n'ingabire yo kugororoka bisesekaye bazorushiriza gushirwa ku butware mu bugingo n'umwe, Yesu Kristo.
45005018	None rero nk'uko gucirwa urubanza kwazanywe n'igicumuro kimwe ku bantu bose, ngo batsindwe, ni ko ya ngabire yazanywe n'igikorwa kigororotse kimwe ku bantu bose, ngo bahindurwe abera baronke ubugingo.
45005019	Kandi nk'uko kutumvira Imana kw'umuntu umwe kwatumye benshi bacika abanyavyaha, ni ko kuwumvira kw'umwe kuzotuma benshi bacika abagororotsi.
45005020	Ariko ivyagezwe vyaje na vyo, kugira ngo gucumura kugwire. Yamara, aho icaha cagwiriye ni ho ubuntu bw' Imana bwarushirije kugwira,
45005021	kugira ngo, nk'uko icaha cashizwe ku butware n'urupfu, mube ari ko n'ubuntu bw'Imana bushirwa ku butware n'ukugororoka, buheshe ubugingo budashira, kubwa Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu.
45006001	Nuko tuvuge iki? Mbega twame dukora ivyaha kugira ngo ubuntu bw'Imana bugwire?
45006002	Biragahera. Twebwe twapfuye ku caha, twoba tukikibamwo dute?
45006003	Canke ntimuzi yuko twese ababatirijwe kuba muri Kristo Yesu, twabatirijwe kuba mu rupfu rwiwe?
45006004	None rero kubatizwa kwatumye duhambanwa na we tuba mu rupfu rwiwe, kugira ngo, nk'uko Kristo yazuwe mu bapfuye n'ubwiza bwa Data wa twese, kube ari ko natwe tugendana ubugingo busha.
45006005	Ko twakoranijwe na we n'igishushanyo c'urupfu rwiwe, tuzokoranywa na we n'ico ukuzuka kwiwe na co.
45006006	Kandi tumenye iki, yuko umuntu wacu wa kera yabambanywe na we, kugira ngo umubiri w'icaha uhindurwe ubusa, ntitwame tujakariye icaha:
45006007	kuko uwapfuye aba atsindanishirijwe icaha.
45006008	Ariko bisanzwe twapfanye na Kristo, twizera yuko tuzobanaho na we;
45006009	kuko tuzi yuko Kristo, amaze kuzuka mu bapfuye, atagipfa, urupfu rutakimuganza.
45006010	Ukwo gupfa yapfuye, ni ho yapfuye rimwe ku caha; ariko ko ariho, ariho ari uwo Imana.
45006011	Mube ari ko namwe mwiyumvira ko mwapfuye ku caha, ariko ko muriho muri abo Imana, muri muri Kristo Yesu.
45006012	None rero icaha ntikikabe ku butware mu mibiri yanyu izopfa, ngo mwumvire ivyo yifuza.
45006013	Kandi ntimugahe icaha imibiri yanyu ngo ikoreshwe n'ukugabitanya; ariko mwishikanire Imana nk'abazuke bavuye mu bapfuye, n'imibiri yanyu muyihe Imana kugira ngo ikoreshwe no kugororoka.
45006014	Icaha ntikizobaganza, kuko mutaganzwa n'ivyagezwe, ariko muganzwa n'ubuntu.
45006015	Nuko tugire dute? Mbega dukore ivyaha, kuko tutaganzwa n'ivyagezwe, ariko tuganzwa n'ubuntu? Biragahera.
45006016	Ntimuzi yuko shobuja mwihaye kuba abakozi bo kumwumvira, muri abakozi b'uwo mwumvira uwo? Namba muri abakozi b'icaha kizana urupfu, canke abo kwumvira Imana kuzana ukugororoka.
45006017	Ariko, Imana ishimwe yuko naho mwari abakozi b'icaha, mwumviye mu mitima uburyo bwo kwigishwa mwahawe:
45006018	kandi mwacunguwe ngo ntimuganzwe n'icaha, mujakarira ukugororoka.
45006019	Ndabivuze nk'imvugo y'abantu, ku bwo intege nke z'imibiri yanyu. Nk'uko mwaha imibiri yanyu ibiteye isoni n'umugararizo, kuba abakozi bavyo, bigatuma muba abagarariji, abe ari ko na none muha ukugororoka imibiri yanyu, kuba abakozi bakwo, kugira ngo mwezwe.
45006020	Mukiri abakozi b'icaha, ntimwaganzwa n'ukugororoka.
45006021	None rero ico gihe mwari n'imbuto ki mu bibamaramaza ubu? kuko amaherezo yavyo ari urupfu.
45006022	Ariko noneho, ko mwacunguwe ngo ntimuganzwe n'icaha, mukajakarira Imana, mufise imbuto zanyu zizana ukwezwa, kandi amaherezo ni ubugingo budashira.
45006023	Ingero y'icaha n'urupfu ariko ingabire y'Imana ni ubugingo budashira, bubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu.
45007001	Canke ga bavukanyi, ntimuzi yuko ivyagezwe biganza umuntu akiriho? mbwiye abazi ivyagezwe.
45007002	Kuko ivyagezwe bihambirira umugore ku mugabo wiwe, akiriho; ariko umugabo wiwe iyo apfuye, umugore aba abohowe ngo ntaganzwe na we.
45007003	None rero, umugabo wiwe akiriho, yokurongorwa n'uwundi mugabo, yokwitwa umusambanyikazi: ariko umugabo wiwe iyo apfuye, ntaba akiganzwa n'ivyagezwe, bituma atoba umusambanyikazi, naho yokurongorwa n'uwundi mugabo. "
45007004	None rero namwe, bavukanyi banje, gukoranywa n'umubiri wa Kristo kwatumye mucika abapfuye ku vyagezwe, kugira ngo mube abo uwundi, ni we yazutse mu bapfuye, twamire Imana imbuto.
45007005	Tukiganzwa n'akameremere kacu, ukwifuza kw'ivyaha kw'uburyo bwinshi kwazanywe n'ivyagezwe kwakorera mu mibiri yacu, kugira ngo twamire urupfu imbuto.
45007006	Ariko noneho ntitukiganzwa n'ivyagezwe, kuko twapfuye ku camye kidufashe, ni co gituma tuba abakozi, dukorera Mpwemu adukoresha uburyo busha, tudakoreshwa bwa buryo bwa kera bw'inyuguti.
45007007	Nuko tuvuge iki? Mbega ivyagezwe ni icaha? Eka na mba. Ariko simba naramenye icaha, iyo ntakimenyeshwa n'ivyagezwe; kuko ntaba naramenye ukwifuza, iyo ivyagezwe bitavuga " ngo Ntukifuze.
45007008	Ariko, icaha kibonye urwitwazo mu vyagezwe, kinkoreramwo ukwifuza kw'uburyo bwose; kuko icaha kiba gipfuye, ivyagezwe bitariho.
45007009	Nanje kera nariho, ntafise ivyagezwe. Maze icagezwe kije, icaha kirarabuka, nanje ndapfa;
45007010	kandi ico cagezwe co kuzana ubugingo nakibona kinzanira urupfu.
45007011	Kuko icaha campendahenze, kibonye urwitwazo mu cagezwe, kandi kigitera kunyica.
45007012	None rero ivyagezwe ni ivyera, kandi ibwirizwa ni iryera, rigororotse, ryiza.
45007013	Mbega iciza cambereye urupfu? Eka na mba! ariko icaha ni co carubaye, ngo kimenyekane ko ari icaha, kuko canyicishije iciza, ngo icagezwe gitume icaha kirushiriza kuba kibi.
45007014	Kuko tuzi yuko ivyagezwe ari ivyo impwemu; ariko jewe nganzwa n'akameremere kanje, naguriwe kuba umushumba w'icaha.
45007015	Sinzi ico nkora; kuko ico ngomba atari co nkora, ariko ico nanka akaba ari co nkora.
45007016	Ariko ko nkora ico ntagomba, mba nemeye ivyagezwe ko ari vyiza.
45007017	None rero si jewe nkibikora, ariko ni icaha kimbamwo.
45007018	Ndazi yuko muri jewe, mu kameremere kanje, ata ciza kimbamwo; kuko kugomba gukora iciza kubana nanje, ariko kugikora nta kwo;
45007019	kuko iciza ngomba atari co nkora, ariko ikibi ntagomba akaba ari co nkora.
45007020	Ariko ko nkora ico ntagomba, si jewe nkigikora, ariko ni icaha kimbamwo.
45007021	Ni ko mbona ikingera, yuko naho ngomba gukora iciza, ikibi kibana nanje.
45007022	Nezererwa ivyagezwe n'Imana mu mutima wanje,
45007023	ariko mbona ikindi kingera kiri mu mubiri wanje kirwanya ikingera co mu mutima wanje, kikamfatira mpiri kuganzwa n'ikingera kiri mu mubiri wanje, ikingera c'icaha.
45007024	Ewe jewe ndagowe! Ni nde yonkiza umubiri untera uru rupfu?
45007025	Imana ishimwe, kubwa Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu. Nuko jewe mu mutima wanje njakariye ivyagezwe n'Imana, ariko mu kameremere njakariye ikingera c'icaha.
45008001	Nuko rero noneho abari muri Kristo Yesu nta rubanza ruzobatsinda.
45008002	kuko ikingera ca Mpwemu w'ubugingo bwo muri Kristo Yesu cancunguye ngo singanzwe n'icangera c'icaha n'ico urupfu.
45008003	Ico ivyagezwe bitashoboye gukora kuko bifise intege nke ku bwo akameremere kacu, Imana yatumye Umwana wayo, afise ishusho y'umubiri w'icaha, kuba ikimazi c'icaha, itsindisha icaha kiri mu mubiri,
45008004	kugira ngo ivyo ivyagezwe bibwiriza bishikanwe muri twebwe, tutagenda mu buryo bw' akameremere kacu, ariko tugenda mu bwa Mpwemu w' Imana;
45008005	kuko abaganzwa n'akameremere k'umubiri bitwaririka ivyo umubiri, kandi abaganzwa n'impwemu bitwaririka ivyo impwemu.
45008006	Kwitwaririka ivyo umubiri kuzana urupfu, ariko kwitwaririka ivyo impwemu kuzana ubugingo n'amahoro.
45008007	Kuko kwitwaririka ivyo umubiri gutera kwanka Imana, kuko kutumvira ivyagezwe n'Imana, kandi kudashobora kuvyumvira;
45008008	Kandi abaganzwa n'akameremere k'umubiri ntibashobora guhimbara Imana.
45008009	Ariko mweho ntimuganzwa n'akameremere k'umubiri, ariko muganzwa n'impwemu, bisanzwe Mpwemu w'Imana mubana. ariko iyo umuntu adafise Mpwemu wa Kristo ntaba ari uwiwe.
45008010	Bisanzwe Kristo ari muri mwebwe, umubiri uba upfuye ku bwo icaha, ariko impwemu ni nzima ku bwo kugororoka.
45008011	Ariko bisanzwe Mpwemu w' Iyazuye Yesu imukuye mu bapfuye mubana, Iyazuye Kristo Yesu imukuye mu bapfuye izozura n'imibiri yanyu ipfa, kubwa Mpwemu wayo mubana.
45008012	None rero, bavukanyi, turi n'umwenda, atari uwo akameremere kacu, ngo twitondere ivyako.
45008013	Kuko namba mwitondera ivyo akameremere kanyu, ntimuzobura gupfa; ariko ni mwica ivyo umubiri ukora, muvyicisha impwemu, muzobaho.
45008014	Abarongorwa na Mpwemu w'Imana bose ni bo bana b'Imana.
45008015	Kuko mutahawe impwemu y'ubuja ngo mwongere gutinya; ariko mwahawe impwemu yo kubahindura abana b'Imana, ni yo ituma dutakamba tuti: "Abba"
45008016	Mpwemu ubwiwe abwiririkanya n'impwemu yacu, ari icabona, yuko turi abana b'Imana.
45008017	Ariko ko turi abana bayo, turi abaragwa; turi abaragwa b'Imana, turi abaraganwa na Kristo, namba tubabazanywa na we, ngo tubone guhanwa ubwiza na we.
45008018	Niyumvira yuko imibabaro y'iki gihe idakwiye kugereranywa n'ubwiza tuzohishurirwa.
45008019	Kuko ivyaremwe vyiteze uguhishurwa kw'abana b'Imana biguhahamiye cane.
45008020	Kuko ivyaremwe vyagezwe kuganzwa n'ibitagira ikimazi, kandi si vyo vyavyigombeye, ariko vyagizwe n'Iyageze ko biganzwa bityo,
45008021	kugira ngo vyizigire yuko na vyo bizocungurwa ngo ntibibe ibihumbwa vyo kubora, bizohabwa ukwidegemvya, gufatana n'ubwiza bw'abana b' Imana.
45008022	Kuko tuzi yuko ivyaremwe vyose binihira hamwe bikaramukirwa hamwe kugeza n'ubu.
45008023	Kandi si co gusa, ariko natwe abafise ku vyeze ubwa mbere vya Mpwemu, natwe nyene tunihira mu mitima yacu, twiteze gucika abana b'Imana, ni kwo gucungurwa kw'imibiri yacu.
45008024	Kuko twakijijwe mu buryo bwo kugira ico twiteze; ariko icari citezwe iyo kibonetse ntikiba kicitegwa. Ico umuntu abonye, yoba akicitega ate?
45008025	Yamara ko twiteze ico tutarabona, nuko tukirorera twihangana.
45008026	Ni ko na Mpwemu adufasha mu ntege nke zacu; kuko tutazi uko dukwiye gusenga, ariko Mpwemu ubwiwe aradusengera, aniha iminiho itovugwa;
45008027	ariko Iyisesa imitima irazi ivyo Mpwemu yiyumvira, kuko uko Imana igomba ari ko Mpwemu asengera abera.
45008028	Kandi turazi yuko ku bakunda Imana vyose bifataniriza hamwe kubazanira ivyiza, abahamagawe nk'uko yabigabiye.
45008029	Kuko abo yamenye kera yabatoranirije kera gushushanywa n'ishusho y'Umwana wayo, kugira ngo abe imfura mu bana ba Se benshi.
45008030	Abo yatoranije kera, yarabahamagaye; abo yahamagaye, yabagize abera; abo yagize abera, yabahaye ubwiza.
45008031	Ko bimeze bityo, tuvuge iki? Bisanzwe Imana iri mu ruhande rwacu, uwoturwanya ni nde?
45008032	Iyitimanye Umwana wayo, ikamutanga kubwacu twese, izobura ite kutugabirira vyose kuri we?
45008033	Ni nde azorega abo Imana yatoranije? Mbega ni Imana, kandi ari yo ibahindura intungane?
45008034	Ni nde azobagira abera? Mbega ni Kristo Yesu, kandi ari we yapfuye? Ibibiruta yarazutse, ari i buryo bw'Imana, bitayeko aradusengera.
45008035	Ni nde azodutandukanya n'urukundo rwa Kristo? Mbega ni amarushwa, ni ivyago, ni uguhamwa, ni inzara, ni ukwambara ubusa, ni ukuba mw'irinde, canke ni inkota?
45008036	Nk'uko handitswe, ngo Twirirwa twicwa, bakuduhora, Twagereranijwe n'intama z'imbagwa.
45008037	Ariko muri ivyo vyose turushaho gutsindirwa n'uwadukunze.
45008038	Kuko menye neza ntabikekeranya yuko naho rwoba urupfu, ubugingo, abamarayika, abaganza, ibiriho, ibizoba, abafise ubushobozi,
45008039	uburebure bw' amaja ruguru, uburebure bw' amajepfo canke ikindi caremwe cose, ata kizoshobora kudutandukanya n'urukundo rw'Imana ruri muri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu.
45009001	Ndavuga ukuri muri Kristo, simbesha, ijwi ryo mu mutima wanje rirabinyemeza muri Mpwemu Yera,
45009002	yuko mfise intuntu nyinshi n'umubabaro udahengeshanya mu mutima.
45009003	Iyaba vyashoboka, noshimye kuvumwa no kuba igicibwa kuri Kristo kubwa bene wacu, abo tuvukana ku mubiri,
45009004	ni bo Bisirayeli, ivyabo ni uguhinduka abana b'Imana, ubwiza, amasezerano, guhabwa ivyagezwe, gusenga Imana n'ivyasezeranywe;
45009005	bafise ba sogokuruza ba bandi, kandi ku mubiri Kristo yamutse kuri bo, ni we ari hejuru ya vyose, ni we Mana ikwiye gushimwa ibihe bidashira. Amina.
45009006	Ariko si ukugira ngo ijambo ry'Imana ntiryashitse; kuko abamutse kuri Isirayeli atari bo Bisirayeli bose.
45009007	Kandi kuko ari uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu, si co kibagira abana biwe bose; ariko, kuri Isaka ni ho uruvyaro rwawe ruzokwitirirwa.
45009008	Ni kwo kuvuga ko abana b'umubiri atari bo bana b'Imana, ariko abana b'isezerano ni bo baharurwa nk'uruvyaro.
45009009	Kuko ijambo ry'isezerano ari iri, ngo ikindi gihe nk'iki nzoza, Sara yavyaye umuhungu.
45009010	Kandi si co gusa, ariko na Rebeka, igihe yari amaze gusama inda y'umugabo umwe, Isaka sogokuruza,
45009011	kandi abana bataravuka, batarakora iciza canke ikibi, ngo ivyo Imana yagabiye itoranya bibeho, bitavuye ku vy'abantu bakora, ariko vyavuye ku Iyibahamagara,
45009012	ico gihe yabwiwe, ngo Bukuru azoshumbira Butoyi;
45009013	nk'uko handitswe, ngo Yakobo naramukunze, Esawu na we naramwanse.
45009014	Nuko tuvuge iki? Mbega Imana irarenganya? Eka na mba!
45009015	Kuko yabwiye Mose iti: "Nzogirira ikigongwe uwo nshatse kuzigirira, ngirire n'imbabazi uwo nshatse kuzigirira.
45009016	Ni co gituma bitava ku kugomba kw'umuntu, canke ku gushimika kwiwe, ariko biva ku Mana igira ikigongwe.
45009017	Kuko ivyanditswe vyabwiye Farawo, ngo icatumye ndaguhagarika ni ukugira ngo ndakwerekanireko ubushobozi bwanje, kandi ngo izina ryanje rivugwe hose mw'isi yose.
45009018	Nuko igirira ikigongwe uwo igomba, kandi ikomantaza umutima w'uwo igomba.
45009019	Nuko wombaza uti: "Ni igiki gituma ikigaya umuntu? Ni nde yankiye ivyo igomba?
45009020	Ariko ga wa muntu, uri nde, uharira n' Imana? Mbega icabumbwe cobaza uwakibumvye kiti: 'Ni igiki catumye umbumba utya?'
45009021	canke umubumvyi ntagera ibumba rimwe ngo aribumbemwo urwavya rumwe rwo gukoresha ivyo icubahiro, n'urundi rwo gukoresha ibiteye isoni?
45009022	Mbega hari ico biriko, naho Imana yagomvye kwerekana ishavu ryayo, no kumenyesha ubushobozi bwayo, namba yihangananiye imbabazi nyinshi inzavya z'ukuraka, ziteguriwe guhona;
45009023	kugira ngo yerekanire ubutunzi bw'ubwiza bwayo ku nzavya z'ikigongwe, izo yiteguriye guha ubwiza kera,
45009024	kuri twebwe, abo yahamagaye, si mu Bayuda bonyene ariko no mu banyamahanga?"
45009025	Nk'uko yavugiye mu kanwa ka Hoseya iti: "Abatari abantu banje nzobita abantu banje, Kandi uwutari inkundwakazi nzomwita inkundwakazi.
45009026	Kandi aho hantu babwiriwe, ngo ntimuri abantu banje, Ni ho bazokwitirwa abana b'Imana nzima."
45009027	Kandi Yesaya asemerera ivyo Abisirayeli ati: "Igitigiri c'Abisirayeli n'iyo coba nk'umusenyi wo ku kiyaga, amasigarira ni yo azokira;
45009028	kuko Uhoraho azoshitsa ijambo ryiwe mw'isi, ariringanize kandi arihimbure."
45009029	Kandi nk'uko Yesaya yavuze kera ati: "Iyaba Uhoraho Nyeningabo atadusigarije uruvyaro, Tuba twarabaye nk'i Sodomu, tukagirwa nk'i Gomora."
45009030	None tuvuge iki? Ehe tuvuge yuko abanyamahanga batakurikiye ivyo ukugororoka bashitse ku kugororoka, ni kwo kugororoka kuva ku kwizera.
45009031	Ariko Abisirayeli bakurikiye ivyo ivyagezwe vy'ukugororoka, ntibabishikako.
45009032	Ni ku ki? Ni uko batabironderesheje ukwizera, yamara babironderesheje ibikorwa nk'ivyobibahesha, batsitara kuri rya buye ritsitaza,
45009033	nk'uko handitswe, ngo ehe ndashira i Siyoni ibuye ritsitaza, urutare rugwisha, Kandi uwizera uwo ntazoterwa n'isoni.
45010001	Bavukanyi, ivyohimbara umutima wanje n'ivyo nsengera Abisirayeli ku Mana, ni ukugira ngo bakizwe.
45010002	Ndabashingira intahe yuko bafise ishaka ry'Imana, ariko si mu buryo bw'ubwenge;
45010003	ko batari bazi ukugororoka kuva ku Mana bakarondera kwishingira ukugororoka kwabo ubwabo, ntibaganjwe n'ukuva ku Mana.
45010004	Kuko Kristo ari we ivyagezwe bishikirako, kugira ngo aheshe uwizera wese ukugororoka.
45010005	Mose yanditse ati: "Uwushishikara ukugororoka kuva ku vyagezwe ni kwo kuzomubeshaho."
45010006	Ariko ukugororoka kuva ku kwizera kuvuga gutya, ngo ntiwibaze uti: "Ni nde azoduga, ngo aje mw'ijuru? (risobanurwa ngo kumanukana Kristo),"
45010007	canke uti: "Ni nde azomanuka i kuzimu? (risobanurwa ngo kudugana Kristo, amukuye mu bapfuye)."
45010008	Ariko kwavuze gute? Kwavuze kuti: "Ijambo riri hafi yawe, riri mu kanwa kawe no mu mutima wawe; ni ryo jambo ryo kwizera, iryo tubigisha."
45010009	Kuko ni waturisha akanwa yuko Yesu ari Umwami, ukizera mu mutima yuko Imana yamuzuye imukuye mu bapfuye, uzokizwa;
45010010	kuko umutima ari wo umuntu yizeresha, akaronka ukugororoka; kandi akanwa akaba ari ko yaturisha, akaronka agakiza.
45010011	Kuko ivyanditswe bivuga, ngo uwumwizera wese ntazoterwa n'isoni.
45010012	Nta tandukaniro ry'Umuyuda n'Umugiriki; kuko Umwami umwe ari Umwami wa bose, ni we afise ubutunzi bukwiye abamwambaza bose;
45010013	kuko, Umuntu wese azokwambaza izina ry'Uhoraho azokizwa.
45010014	None bazokwambaza bate uwo batarizera? Kandi bazokwizera bate uwo batarumva? Kandi bazokwumva bate, ata wabasiguriye ivyiwe?
45010015	Kandi bazosigura ivyiwe bate, batatumwe? Nk'uko handitswe, ngo ewe kuntu ibirenge vy'abazanye ubutumwa bw'ivyiza ari vyiza!
45010016	ariko abumviye ubutumwa bwiza si bose. Kuko Yesaya yavuze ati: "Mwami, ni nde yemeye ivyo twumvise?"
45010017	Nuko ukwemera kuva ku kwumva, n'ukwumva kuzanwa n'ijambo rya Kristo.
45010018	Ariko ndabaza. Mbega ntibumvise? Ego, barumvise. Ijwi ryavyo ryumvikanye mw'isi yose, Bo n'amajambo yavyo ku mpera y'isi.
45010019	Ariko ndabaza. Mbega Abisirayeli ntibabimenye? Mose ni we yabanje kuvuga ati: "Nzobateza ishari abatari ihanga ry'ukuri, Nzobarakisha ihanga ry'imburabwenge."
45010020	Kandi Yesaya ashira amanga cane, aravuga ati: "Nabonywe n'abatandondeye, Neretswe abatambaririkije."
45010021	Ariko ku Bisirayeli aravuga ati: "Nirirwa ntegeye amaboko ubwoko butumva butongana."
45011001	Nuko ndabaza: Mbega Imana yaciye abantu bayo? Eka na mba! Kuko nanje ndi Umwisirayeli, wo mu ruvyaro rwa Aburahamu, wo mu muryango wa Benyamini.
45011002	Imana ntiyataye abantu bayo yamenye kera. Canke ntimuzi uko ivyanditswe bivuga kuri Eliya? Ko yareze Abisirayeli ku Mana
45011003	ati: "Mwami, bishe abavugishwa nawe, basambuye ibicaniro vyawe, nanje nsigaye jenyene, kandi barangenza ngo banyice."
45011004	Ariko Imana yamwishuye ngo iki? Iti: " Nisigarije abantu ibihumbi indwi batapfukamiye Bayali."
45011005	Nuko ni ko biri no muri iki gihe, hariho amasigarira nk'uko yatoranijwe n'ubuntu bw'Imana.
45011006	Ariko ni vyaba bivuye ku buntu, ntibikiva ku bikorwa; Namba atari ko biri, ubuntu si bwo buntu.
45011007	None vyabaye bite se? ico Abisirayeli barondeye, ntibakibonye; ariko, abatoranijwe barakironse, abandi bakomantazwa imitima.
45011008	Nk'uko handitswe, ngo Imana yabahaye umutima wo guhunyiza, n'amaso atabona, n'amatwi atumva, gushitsa kuri uwo musi.
45011009	Kandi Dawidi yaravuze ati: "Imeza yabo ibe nk'ururiba, n'umutego, N'ikigwisha, n'inyishu yabo:
45011010	Amaso yabo ni ahumwe, ntibabone, Kandi wame ubahetamitse umugongo imisi yose."
45011011	Nuko ndabaza: Mbega batsitariye kugwa mahera? Eka na mba! Yamara ukugwa kwabo kwazaniye abanyamahanga agakiza, ngo bitere Abisirayeli ishari.
45011012	Ariko, k'ukugwa kwabo ari ubutunzi bw'abari mw'isi, n'ukugabanuka kwabo ari ubutunzi bw' abanyamahanga, ukugwira kwabo ntikuzorushiriza cane?
45011013	Ariko ndababarira mwebwe, abanyamahanga. Ndashimisha igikorwa canje, kuko ndi intumwa ku banyamahanga,
45011014	kugira ngo kumbure ntere ishari abo i wacu, nkize bamwe muri bo.
45011015	Ko gutabwa kwabo kwazaniye abari mw'isi kwuzura n'Imana, ukugarukanwa kwabo kuzoba gute? Mbega ntikuzoba ubugingo buzutse mu bapfuye?
45011016	Kandi ko ifu y'ivyeze ubwa mbere ari iyera, n'irobe ni ko rimeze; kandi ko igishitsi ari icera, n'amashami ni ko ameze.
45011017	Ariko namba amashami amwe yarahanyuwe, nawe uri igihumbwa ca elayo watewe nk'ingurukizi hagati mu mashami, usangira na yo ubukame bw'igishitsi ca elayo bwite,
45011018	ntiwihayagize kuri ayo mashami. Namba uyihayagizako si igishitsi kimeze kuri wewe, ariko ni wewe umeze ku gishitsi.
45011019	Wovuga rero uti: "Amashami yahanyuwe kugira ngo nterweko."
45011020	Ni ko; ukutizera ni kwo kwayahanyuje, nawe ukwizera ni kwo kuguhagaritse. Ntiwibone, ariko wiyubare.
45011021	Kuko Imana, ko itagiriye ikigongwe amashami bwite, nawe ntizokikugirira.
45011022	Raba rero ukugira neza kw'Imana, n'ubuhambazi bwayo; ku baguye ni ubuhambazi, ariko kuri wewe ni ukugira neza kw'Imana, ni waguma muri ukwo kugira neza kwayo; kuko ni yo utagira utyo, nawe uzohanyurwa.
45011023	Kandi ba bandi na bo, ni bataguma mu kutizera, bazosubizwako nk'ingurukizi. Imana ishobora kubasubizako.
45011024	Kuko, ko wahanyuwe ku giti cameze ari igihumbwa ca elayo, ugaterwa nk'ingurukizi muri elayo nziza, mudasangiye ubwoko, ba bandi babusangiye ntibazorushiriza cane guterwa muri elayo yabo?
45011025	Bavukanyi, singomba ko mutamenya iri banga, ntimwiyite abanyabwenge, n'irya uko habaye gukomantaza imitima y'Abisirayeli, ariko si bose, gushitsa aho igitigiri gikwiye c'abanyamahanga kizokwinjirira mw'ishengero.
45011026	Ni vyaba bityo, Abisirayeli bose bazokizwa, nk'uko handitswe, ngo i Siyoni hazova Umurokozi, Azokura muri Yakobo ukutubaha Imana;
45011027	Kandi ni ryo sezerano, nsezeranye na bo, Aho nzobakurako ivyaha.
45011028	Ku vy'ubutumwa bwiza, n'abansi kubwanyu: ariko ku vy'ugutoranya kw'Imana, n'abakundwa kubwa ba sekuruza.
45011029	kuko ingabire z'Imana no guhamagara kwayo itavyicuza.
45011030	Nk'uko mwebwe kera mwagarariza Imana, ariko none umugararizo wabo wazaniye mwebwe kugirirwa imbabazi:
45011031	ni ko na bo none bagararije, kugira ngo imbabazi mwagiriwe zibazanire na bo kuzigirirwa.
45011032	kuko Imana yugaraniye abantu bose mu mugararizo, kugira ngo ibagirire imbabazi bose.
45011033	Yo, uburebure bw'amajepfo bw'ubutunzi bw'ubwenge no kumenya vy'Imana! Imigabo yayo ntishoboka kubariritswa, n'inzira zayo ntizigira akehe!
45011034	Ni nde yamenye umutima w'Uhoraho? Canke ni nde yabaye umuhanuzi wiwe?
45011035	Canke ni nde yabanje kumuha kandi akazokwishurwa?
45011036	Kuko vyose biva muri we, kandi bizanwa na we, kandi vyamuremewe: icubahiro kibe iciwe ibihe bidashira. Amina.
45012001	Nuko bavukanyi, ndabahanura ku bwo imbabazi z' Imana, ngo Muzotange imibiri yanyu ibe ibimazi bizima vyera, bihimbara Imana, ni kwo kuyikorera kwanyu kwogira ikimazi.
45012002	Ntimushushanywe n'ivyo iki gihe, yamara muhinduke rwose, mugize imitima mishasha, kugira ngo mumenye neza ivyo Imana igomba, ni vyo vyiza bishimwa, bitunganye rwose.
45012003	Ndabwira mbwirijwe n'ubuntu nahawe, umuntu wese muri mwebwe, areke kwifata uko atari, yamara yiyumvire yitonze nk'uko Imana yagereye umuntu wese ukwizera.
45012004	Nk'uko mu mubiri umwe dufise ingingo nyinshi, kandi ingingo zose zitagira igikorwa kimwe,
45012005	natwe ni ko turi. Turi benshi, kandi turi umubiri umwe muri Kristo, umuntu wese ni urugingo rw'uwundi.
45012006	Nuko dufise ingabire zitandukana, nk'uko ubuntu twahawe butandukana namba twarahawe kuvugishwa n'Imana, tuvugishwe na yo uko ukwizera kwacu kungana;
45012007	canke namba twarahawe igikorwa co mw'ishengero, tugishishikare; canke uwigisha ashishikarire kwigisha;
45012008	canke uhanura ashishikarire guhanura; ugira ubuntu, abugire ata kinubwe; uganza aganzanye umwete; ugira imbabazi, azigire anezerewe.
45012009	Urukundo rwanyu ntirube uruheyiheyi. Mwanke ibibi, mumatane n'ivyiza.
45012010	Ku vyo gukunda bavukanyi, mukundane rwose. Ku vy'icubahiro, umuntu wese ashire imbere mugenzi we;
45012011	ku vy'ugushishikara, ntimugire urwangara; mukovye mu mitima gukorera Umwami wacu.
45012012	Munezererwe kwizigira ibizoba; mwihanganire amagorwa; mushishikare gusenga.
45012013	Mugabanirize abera, uko bakenye; mushishikare gutanga indaro.
45012014	Ababahama mubahezagire; mubahezagire, ntimubavume.
45012015	Munezeranwe n'abanezerewe, murirane n'abarira.
45012016	Muhuze umutima; ntimushire umutima ku bikomeye, ariko mugendane n'ivyiyoroheje. Ntimwiyite abanyabwenge.
45012017	Ntimusubirize umuntu mu nkoko ikibi yabagiriye; mubabare gukora ivyiza imbere y'abantu bose.
