45012018	Namba bishoboka, mu ruhande rwanyu, mwuzure n'abantu bose.
45012019	Abo nkunda, ntimwihorane, ariko muhe uburyo ishavu ry'Imana; kuko handitswe, ngo Uguhora n'ukwanje, ni jewe nzobasubiriza mu nkoko, ni ko Uhoraho avuze.
45012020	Ariko, Umwansi wawe ni yasonza, umugaburire; ni yagira inyota, umuhe ico anywa; kuko ni wagira utyo, uzoba umurunzeko amakara yaka ku mutwe.
45012021	Ikibi ntikikuneshe, yamara ikibi ukinesheshe iciza.
45013001	Umuntu wese n'agamburukire abamuganza; kuko ata kuganza kutava ku Mana, ukuriho kwagezwe n'Imana.
45013002	Ni co gituma, uwugabagabiye uwuganza aba agabagabiye icagezwe n'Imana. Kandi abakigabagabiye bazoba bihamagariye gutsindwa n'urubanza.
45013003	Kuko abaganza atari abateye ubwoba k'uwukora iciza, kiretse uwukora ikibi. Uragomba kutagirira ubwoba uwuganza? Kora neza, azogushima.
45013004	Kuko ari umukozi w'Imana ku bwawe, ngo akuzanire ivyiza. Ariko ni wakora nabi, ugire ubwoba, kuko atambarira inkota ubusa, kuko ari umukozi w'Imana, umuhozi ashitsa ishavu k'uwukora nabi.
45013005	Ni co gituma ukwiye kugamburuka, atari ku bwo kurakirwa gusa, ariko no kubwo ijwi ryo mu mutima.
45013006	Ni co gituma kandi mutanga ikori; kuko abaganza ari abakozi b' Imana, bashishikarira ico gikorwa nyene.
45013007	Muhe bose ivyo bakwiye; abahabwa ikori mubahe ikori; ababuguza mubabugurire; abo gutinywa mubatinye; abo kwubahwa mububahe.
45013008	Ntihagire uwo mugirira umwenda, atari ugukundana; kuko ukunda uwundi aba ashikije ivyagezwe.
45013009	Kuko ibi, ngo ntugasambane, ntukice, ntukibe, ntukifuze, n'ikindi cagezwe cose, bipoperanirijwe muri iri jambo, ngo Ukunde umubanyi nk'uko wikunda.
45013010	Ufise urukundo ntagirira umubanyi we nabi. Ni co gituma urukundo ari rwo rushitsa ivyagezwe.
45013011	Nuko mwame mugenza mutyo, kuko muzi imisi, yuko igihe gishitse co kwikangura. Noneho agakiza kacu karatwegereye, kurusha igihe twizereye.
45013012	Ijoro rirakuze, bugira buce. Nuko twiyambure ibikorwa vy'umwiza, twambare ibirwanisho vy'umuco.
45013013	Tugendane ingeso nziza, nk' abagenda ku murango, tutadandahirwa, tutaborerwa, tudasambana, tudakora ivyo isoni nke, tudatongana, tutagira ishari.
45013014	Ariko mwambare Umwami Yesu Kristo, kandi ntimubabare ivyo umubiri, ngo mukore ivyo wifuza.
45014001	Uwudakomeye mu vyizerwa, mumwemere, ariko si ukumuhaririza ku vy' akekeranya.
45014002	Umuntu umwe afise ukwizera kwo kumurisha vyose, ariko udakomeye arya ibirimwa gusa.
45014003	Uwurya inyama ntakengere uwutazirya; kandi uwutazirya ntahinyure uwuzirya, kuko Imana yamwemeye.
45014004	Wewe uri nde uhinyura umushumba w'abandi? Kuko imbere ya shebuja ari ho ahagarara canke agatemba; mbere ushime azohagarara, kuko Umwami wacu ashobora kumuhagarika.
45014005	Umuntu umwe ashima umusi umwe kuwurutisha iyindi; uwundi agashima imisi yose. Umuntu wese ni ashirwe mu mutima wiwe.
45014006	Uwiyumvira umusi awiyumvira kubwo Umwami wacu; uwurya inyama azirya kubwo Umwami, kuko ashima Imana; kandi uwutazirya, yanka kuzirya kubwo Umwami, na we ashima Imana.
45014007	Kuko ata muntu muri twebwe ariho kubwiwe, canke apfa kubwiwe.
45014008	Namba turiho, turiho kuba abo Umwami; kandi namba dupfa, dupfira kuba abo Umwami. Nuko namba turiho, canke namba dupfa, turi abo Umwami.
45014009	Kuko icatumye Kristo apfa, akazuka, ari ukugira ngo abe Umwami w'abapfuye kandi n'uwo abariho.
45014010	Ariko weho, ni igiki gituma uhinyura umwana wa So? Kandi nawe, ni igiki gituma ukengera umwana wa So? Kuko twese tuzohagarara imbere y'intebe y'imanza y'Imana.
45014011	Kuko handitswe, ngo nk'uko ndiho, ni ko Uhoraho avuze, amavi yose azompfukamira, N'indimi zose zizovuga ishimwe ry'Imana.
45014012	Nuko rero, umuntu wese muri twebwe azobazwa n'Imana ivyo yakoze.
45014013	Uhereye ubu rero, ntiduhinyurane; yamara tugire iyi migabo; ngo ntihagire uwushira igitsitaza canke ikigwisha imbere y'umuvukanyi.
45014014	Ndabizi, kandi nemejwe neza n'Umwami Yesu, yuko ata gihumanya ubwaco; kiretse uwiyumvira ko ikintu gihumanya, ni we cohumanya.
45014015	Iyo umwana wa So ababajwe n'ivyo urya, ntuba ukigendera mu rukundo. Uwo Kristo yapfiriye ntumuranduze ivyo kurya vyawe.
45014016	Iciza canyu ntigitukwe.
45014017	Kuko ubwami bw'Imana atari ukurya n'ukunywa, ariko ni ukugororoka, amahoro n'umunezero vyo muri Mpwemu Yera.
45014018	Uwukorera Kristo atyo, ahimbara Imana, kandi n'abantu baramwemera.
45014019	Nuko dukurikire ivyo amahoro n'ivyo gukomezanya.
45014020	Ntimusenyure igikorwa c'Imana kubwo ivyo kurya. Vyose ntibihumanya koko, ariko, uwo muntu arya ibimutsitaza, azobona ibara.
45014021	Ni ciza kutarya inyama, canke kutanywa umuvinyu, canke kudakora ikindi cose gitsitaza umwana wa So, canke kimugwisha, canke kimutera intege nke.
45014022	Ukwizera ufise, ukugumane mu mutima wawe imbere y'Imana. Harahiriwe uwutihinyura ku vyo yemeye.
45014023	Ariko, uwukekeranya wese iyo ariye aba atsinzwe, kuko bitaba bivuye ku kwizera; ikitava ku kwizera cose ni icaha.
45015001	Twebwe abakomeye dukwiye kwihanganira intege nke z' abadakomeye, no kutinezereza.
45015002	Umuntu wese muri twebwe anezereze umuvukanyi wiwe, kugira ngo abone ivyiza, akomezwe.
45015003	Kuko na Kristo atinejereje, nk'uko handitswe, ngo ibitutsi vy'abagutuka vyaguye kuri jewe. "
45015004	Kuko ivyanditswe kera vyose vyandikiwe kutwigisha, kugira ngo kwihangana no guhumurizwa guheshwa n'ivyanditswe biduhe kwizigira ibizoba.
45015005	Ariko Imana itanga ukwihangana n'uguhumurizwa ibahe guhuza imitima yanyu, nk'uko Kristo Yesu agomba,
45015006	kugira ngo muhimbaze n'umutima umwe n'akanwa kamwe Imana y'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ni yo Se.
45015007	Nuko mwemerane, nk'uko Kristo na we yabemeye, kugira ngo Imana ishimishwe.
45015008	Ico mvuga ni uko Kristo yacitse umukozi w'abahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo wo kubagaburira ivyo Imana, ku bwo ukuri kwayo, kugira ngo ashike ivyo ba sogokuruza basezeraniwe,
45015009	kandi ngo abanyamahanga bahimbarize Imana imbabazi zayo, nk'uko handitswe hati:" "Ni co gituma nzogutazira mu mahanga, Ndirimbe izina ryawe."
45015010	Kandi yongera kuvuga ati: "Yemwe banyamahanga ni munezeranwe n'abantu bayo."
45015011	kandi arongera ati: "Yemwe banyamahanga mwese, ni mushime Uhoraho, kandi amoko yose amuhimbaze."
45015012	Kandi Yesaya na we yaravuze ati: "Hazobaho igishitsi ca Isayi, Ni we azohaguruka kuganza amahanga, Ni we abanyamahanga bazokwizigira."
45015013	Imana itanga ivyizigiro ibuzuze umunezero wose n'amahoro biva ku kwizera, kugira ngo murushirize kwizigira ibizoba, mubihawe n'ubushobozi bwa Mpwemu Yera.
45015014	Bavukanyi, nanje nyene ndazi ivyanyu ntakekeranya, yuko mwuzuye ineza, mwuzuye ubwenge bwose, mushobora no guhanurana.
45015015	Ariko ndabandikiye hamwe-hamwe ndushirije gushira amanga, nk'ubibutsa, kubwo ubuntu nahawe n'Imana,
45015016	ngo mbe umukozi akora mu gikoni wa Kristo Yesu ku banyamahanga, ntegure ivyo ubutumwa bwiza bw'Imana nk'umuherezi, kugira ngo abanyamahanga babe ishikanwa rishimwa, ryejejwe na Mpwemu Yera.
45015017	Nuko mfise ukwirata mu vy'Imana muri Kristo Yesu.
45015018	Sinzotinyuka kuvuga ikintu na kimwe atari ico nakoreshejwe na Kristo, kugira ngo abanyamahanga bagamburuke, ampaye amajambo n'ibikorwa,
45015019	n'ubushobozi bw'ibimenyetso bikomeye, n'ibitangaza, n'ubushobozi bwa Mpwemu Yera. Ivyo vyatumye nshitsa ubutumwa bwa Kristo, utanguriye i Yerusalemu, ugakikuza, ugashika no muri Iluriko.
45015020	Namanye imigabo yo kuvuga ubutumwa bwiza, aho izina rya Kristo ritaribwamenyekane, ngo sinubake kw'umushinge wubatswe n'uwundi;
45015021	yamara ngo bimere nk'uko handitswe, ngo abatiganiwe ivyiwe bazobibona, Kandi abataravyumva bazovyitegereza.
45015022	Ni co gituma ngira igisivya kenshi co kuza i wanyu.
45015023	Ariko noneho ntihakinyagukiye muri ibi bihugu, kandi uhereye mu myaka myinshi nifuza kuza i wanyu,
45015024	aho nzogira i Sipaniya. Kuko nizigira kuzobaraba nciye iyo, mukamperekeza, mukansezera neza njayo, ni namara kugabanya inkumbu ndabafitiye.
45015025	Ariko ubu ndiko ndaja i Yerusalemu kugaburira abera.
45015026	Kuko abo i Makedoniya no muri Akaya bahimbawe no gusororanya ivyo gutabara aboro bo mu bera b'i Yerusalemu.
45015027	Vyarabahimbaye, kandi babafitiye umwenda: kuko namba abanyamahanga basangiye ivyo impwemu vyabo, bafise umwenda wo kubafasha ku vy'umubiri.
45015028	Ni naheraheza ivyo, maze kubashikiriza neza izo mbuto z'ubuntu, nzovayo, nce i wanyu, nje i Sipaniya.
45015029	Kandi ndazi yuko aho nzozira i wanyu, nzoza nzanye umugisha wa Kristo wuzuye.
45015030	Nuko ndabinginga, bavukanyi, kubwo Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, no kubwo urukundo ruva kuri Mpwemu, murwanane nanje munsabire Imana,
45015031	nkire abo i Yudaya batayumvira, kandi ingaburo yanje ngiye kugabura i Yerusalemu ishimwe n'abera;
45015032	mbone uko nza i wanyu nezerewe, Imana ni yabikunda, nduhukane namwe.
45015033	Imana nyene amahoro ibane namwe mwese. Amina.
45016001	Ndabashimiye Foyibe muvukanyi, ni we mukozi w'ishengero ry'i Kenkireya,
45016002	ngo mumwakire ku bwo Umwami wacu, nk'uko bibereye abera, kandi mumufashe ku c'azogomba cose, kuko na we yafashije benshi, barimwo nanje.
45016003	Muntahirize Purisikila na Akwila abakoranye nanje muri Kristo Yesu,
45016004	kandi bahevye imitwe yabo ngo icibwe kugira ngo bakize amagara yanje. Si jewe jenyene ndabashima, ariko n'amashengero yose yo mu banyamahanga arabashima.
45016005	Kandi muntahirize ishengero ryo mu nzu yabo. Muntahirize Epayineto, uwo nkunda, ni we yatanguriye abo muri Asiya babaye aba Kristo.
45016006	Muntahirize Mariya yabakoreye cane.
45016007	Muntahirize Andironiko na Yuniya, dusangiye umuryango, ababohanywe nanje, ni ba rurangiranwa mu ntumwa, ni bo bantanze kuba muri Kristo.
45016008	Muntahirize Ampuliyato, uwo nkunda mu Mwami wacu.
45016009	Muntahirize Urubano, dukorana muri Kristo, na Sitaku, uwo nkunda.
45016010	Muntahirize Apele yagejejwe akarama muri Kristo. Muntahirize abo mu bo kwa Arisitobulo.
45016011	Muntahirize Herodiyoni dusangiye umuryango. Muntahirize abo mu bo kwa Narukiso, abari mu Mwami wacu.
45016012	Muntahirize Tirufayina na Tirufosa, bakorera mu Mwami wacu. Muntahirize Perusi akundwa, yakoreye mu Mwami cane.
45016013	Muntahirize Rufo, yatoranijwe n'Umwami, na nyina ni nka mama.
45016014	Muntahirize Asunkirito, Fulegoni, Herume, Patiroba, Heruma n'abavukanyi bari kumwe na bo.
45016015	Muntahirize Filologo na Yuliya, na Nereyu na mushiki we, na Olumpa n'abera bose bari kumwe na bo.
45016016	Muramukanishe kugumbirana kwera. Amashengero ya Kristo yose arabaganutsa.
45016017	Ariko bavukanyi, ndabinginga kwitegereza abazana ivyo gutandukanya n'ibitsitaza, bidahura n'ivyo mwize, mubazibukire.
45016018	Kuko abameze batyo, batajakariye Umwami wacu Kristo, ariko bajakariye inda zabo, kandi bohesha imitima y'aberanda amajambo meza n'ivyo kubanezereza.
45016019	Igitumye ndababwira ivyo, ni uko kwumvira Imana kwanyu kwamamaye mu bantu bose. Ni co gitumye ndabanezererwa, ariko ndagomba ko muba abanyabwenge ku vyiza, mukaba abatungu ku bibi.
45016020	Imana nyene amahoro izofyonyorera Satani vuba musi y'ibirenge vyanyu. Ubuntu bw'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane namwe.
45016021	Timoteyo, dukorana, arabaganutsa, bo na Lukiyosi na Yasona na Sosipatiro, dusangiye umuryango.
45016022	Nanje Terutiyo, nanditse iki cete, ndabaganutsa mu Mwami wacu. "
45016023	Gayo arabaganutsa, ni we yampaye indaro, kandi yakiriye n'abo mw'ishengero bose. Erasito, aganza ivyo ikori ry'iki gisagara, na Kwaruto umuvukanyi wacu, barabaganutsa. [
45016024	Ubuntu bw'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane namwe mwese. Amina. ]
45016025	Imana ishobora kubakomeza, nk'uko ubutumwa bwiza nahawe n'ukwigisha ivya Yesu Kristo bivuga, bihura no guhishurwa kw'ibanga ryahozwe uhereye kera hose,
45016026	ariko muri iki gihe riraserutse, kandi ivyanditswe n'abavugishwa n'Imana birimenyesheje amahanga yose, nk'uko Imana ihoraho yageze, kugira ngo bumvire Imana babiheshwa no kwizera,
45016027	Imana ifise ubwenge yonyene, icubahiro kibe icayo kubwa Yesu Kristo, ibihe bitazoshira. Amina. "
46001001	Jewe Pahulo, nahamagariwe kuba intumwa ya Yesu Kristo, nk'uko Imana yagomvye, na Sositene umuvukanyi, "
46001002	turabandikiye mwebwe abo mw'ishengero ry'Imana ry'i Korinto, bejejwe muri Kristo Yesu, bahamagariwe kuba abera, hamwe na bose bambariza ahantu hose izina ry' Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ni we Mwami wabo n'uwacu.
46001003	Ubuntu n'amahoro bibe muri mwebwe, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo.
46001004	Ndashima Imana yanje na ntaryo ku bwanyu, kubwo ubuntu bw'Imana mwaherewe muri Kristo Yesu; "
46001005	kuko muri vyose mwatungiye muri we, mu vyo muvuga vyose, no mu bwenge bwose,
46001006	kuko ugushingira intahe Kristo kwakomejwe muri mwebwe.
46001007	Bituma mutagira ingabire n'imwe muhaza, mwiteze guhishurwa kw' Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo.
46001008	Ni we azobakomeza gushitsa kw'iherezo, kugira ngo ntimuzogawe kuri wa musi w'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo.
46001009	Imana ni iyo kwizerwa, yabahamagariye kugirirana ubumwe n'Umwana wayo Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu.
46001010	Ariko ndabinginga, bavukanyi, mw'izina ry'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, mwese mube imvugarimwe, kandi n'ibice ntibiremwe muri mwebwe, ariko mutunganywe rwose hamwe, muhuje umutima n'inama.
46001011	Kuko nabariwe ivyanyu, bavukanyi banje, n'abo kwa Kilowe, yuko hari imitongano muri mwebwe.
46001012	Ico mvuze, yuko umuntu wese muri mwebwe avuga ati: "Jeho ndi uwa Pahulo;" uwundi ati: "Jeho ndi uwa Apolo;" uwundi ati: "Jeho ndi uwa Kefa;"uwundi ati: "Jeho ndi uwa Kristo."
46001013	Mbega Kristo aragabanijwemwo ibice? Pahulo yarababambiwe? Canke mwabatijwe mw'izina rya Pahulo?
46001014	Nshimira Imana yuko ata n'umwe nabatije muri mwebwe, atari Kirisipo na Gayo;
46001015	kugira ngo ntihagire umuntu avuga yuko mwabatijwe mw'izina ryanje.
46001016	Kandi nabatije n'abo kwa Stefana: atari abo, sinzi ko hari uwundi nabatije.
46001017	Kuko Kristo atantumye kubatiza, ariko yantumye kuvuga ubutumwa bwiza, ntavugishije ubwenge bw'amajambo, kugira ngo umusaraba wa Kristo ntucike ubusa.
46001018	Kuko ijambo ry'umusaraba ku bahona ari ubupfu, ariko kuri twebwe abakizwa ni ubushobozi bw'Imana.
46001019	Kuko handitswe, ngo nzohonya ubwenge bw' abanyabwenge, N'ubuhanga bw'abahanga nzobuhindura ubusa.
46001020	Umunyabwenge ari hehe? Umwanditsi ari hehe? Umunyabihari wo muri iki gihe ari hehe? Mbega Imana ntiyahinduye ubupfu ubwenge bw'iyi si?
46001021	Kuko naho ubwenge bw'Imana bwageze yuko abo isi batazohabwa n'ubwenge bw'isi kumenya Imana, Imana yahimbawe gukirisha abayizera ubupfu bw'ivyigishwa.
46001022	kuko Abayuda basaba ibimenyetso, Abagiriki barondera ubwenge,
46001023	ariko tweho tubabarira ivya Kristo yabambwe. Uwo ku Bayuda ni ikigwisha, ku banyamahanga ni ubupfu.
46001024	Ariko ku bahamagarwa, b'Abayuda n'Abagiriki, ni Kristo, ubushobozi bw'Imana, kandi ni ubwenge bw'Imana.
46001025	Kuko ubupfu bw'Imana burusha abantu ubwenge; kandi n'intege nke z'Imana zirusha abantu inkomezi.
46001026	Nimwibuke ihamagarwa ryanyu, bavukanyi, yuko abo ubwenge bw'abantu bahamagawe atari benshi, abakomeye bahamagawe atari benshi, abapfasoni bahamagawe atari benshi.
46001027	ariko Imana yatoranije ibipfu vyo mw'isi, ngo imaramaze abanyabwenge; kandi yatoranije ibinyantege nke vyo mw'isi ngo imaramaze ibikomeye,
46001028	kandi n'ivyoroshe vyo mw'isi, n'ibikengerwa, mbere n'ibitariho, Imana yarabitoranije ngo ititure ibiriho;
46001029	kugira ngo ntihagire umuntu yirata imbere y'Imana.
46001030	Ni yo ibaha kuba muri Kristo Yesu, yaduhindukiye ubwenge buva ku Mana, n'ukugororoka n'ukwezwa n'ugucungurwa;
46001031	kugira ngo bibe nk'uko handitswe hati: "Uwirata, yirate Uhoraho."
46002001	Nanje, bavukanyi, hamwe nabasanga i wanyu, sinaje ndi agakura mu majambo canke mu bwenge, mu kubamenyesha ibanga ry'Imana.
46002002	Kuko nagabiye kutagira ico menya muri mwebwe, atari Yesu Kristo, we yabambwe.
46002003	Ariko nabana namwe mfise intege nke, ndi n'ubwoba, mpinda agashitsi kenshi,
46002004	imvugo yanje ni ukwigisha kwanje ntivyarimwo amajambo y'ubwenge yo kwemeza abantu, ariko vyaserukamwo Mpwemu n'ubushobozi,
46002005	kugira ngo ukwizera kwanyu ntiguhagarare mu bwenge bw'abantu ariko guhagarare mu bushobozi bw'Imana.
46002006	Yamara, tuvugana ubwenge hagati mu batunganijwe rwose, ariko ubwo bwenge si ubwo iki gihe, canke ubwo abaganza b'iki gihe bagenda bayoka.
46002007	Ariko tuvugishwa n'ubwenge bw'Imana bwari bwaragizwe ibanga, bwari bwaranyegejwe, ubwo Imana yagabiye kera, ibihe vyose bitarabaho ko buzoba icubahiro cacu.
46002008	Kandi mu baganza b'iki gihe nta wabumenye. Iyo baba barabumenye ntibaba barabamvye Umwami w'icubahiro.
46002009	Ariko nk'uko handitswe, ngo ivyo ijisho ritigeze kubona, n'ivyo ugutwi kutigeze kwumva, Ibitigeze kwinjira mu mutima w'umuntu, Vyose Imana yabiteguriye abayikunda.
46002010	Ariko Imana yabiduhishuriye muri Mpwemu wayo; Mpwemu asesa vyose, n'ibihishijwe vy'Imana.
46002011	Ni nde mu bantu azi ibiri mu muntu, atari impwemu yiwe, iri muri we? Ni ko n'ivyo Imana biri, nta wubizi, atari Mpwemu w'Imana.
46002012	Ariko tweho ntitwahawe impwemu y'iyi si, ariko twahawe Mpwemu ava ku Mana, kugira ngo tumenye ivyo Imana yatugabiye.
46002013	Na vyo nyene turabivuga, ariko ntitubivuga mu majambo yigishwa n'ubwenge bw'abantu, ariko tubivuga mu yigishwa na Mpwemu, tugereranya ivyo impwemu n'ivyo impwemu bindi.
46002014	Ariko umuntu afise umubiri n'ubwenge gusa ntiyemera ivya Mpwemu w'Imana; kuko ari ubupfu kuri we, kandi ntashobora kubimenya, kuko vyitegerezwa mu buryo bw'impwemu.
46002015	Ariko umuntu w'impwemu asesa vyose, kandi ubwiwe nta wumusesa.
46002016	Ni nde yigeze kumenya ivyiyumviro vy'Uhoraho ngo yigishe Uhoraho? Ariko twebwe dufise ivyiyumviro vya Kristo.
46003001	Ku bwanje, bavukanyi, sinshoboye kubabwira nk' abo impwemu, ariko nababwiye nk' abaganzwa n'akameremere k'imibiri yabo, nk'abana b'inzoya bo muri Kristo.
46003002	Nabaramije amata, sinabagaburiye ivyo kurya bigumye; kuko mutaribwabishobore. Kandi na none ntimurabishobora,
46003003	kuko mukiganzwa n'ivyo akameremere kanyu. Ko muri mwebwe hari ishari n'ugutongana, ntimuganzwa na vyo? Ntimugenda nk'abantu?
46003004	Umuntu umwe ko avuga ati: "Jeho ndi uwa Pahulo," uwundi ati: "Jeho ndi uwa Apolo, ntimuri abantu se?"
46003005	None Apolo ni igiki? Kandi Pahulo ni igiki? Mbega si abakozi batumye mwizera Imana, nk'uko Imana yahaye umuntu wese?
46003006	Ni jewe nateye imbuto, Apolo arazivomera, ariko Imana ni yo yazikujije.
46003007	Nuko uwuzitera nta co amaze, canke uwuzivomera, atari Imana ikuza.
46003008	Uwuzitera n'uwuzivomera ni bamwe. Ariko umuntu wese azogererwa nk'uko yakoze igikorwa ciwe;
46003009	kuko Imana ari yo dukorana, namwe muri imirima y'Imana, muri inzu yubakwa n'Imana.
46003010	Nk'uko nahawe ubuntu n' Imana, nashizeho umushinge, nk'umwubakisha mukuru w'ubwenge, uwundi yubakako. Ariko umuntu wese ni yiyubare uko yubakako.
46003011	Kuko irindi tanguriro ata muntu ashobora kurishiraho, atari iryashizweho, ni ryo Yesu Kristo.
46003012	Ariko iryo tanguriro, umuntu ni yaryubakishako izahabu, canke ifeza, canke amabuye y'igiciro kinini, canke ibiti, canke ubwatsi, canke ibishakashaka,
46003013	igikorwa c'umuntu wese kizoseruka. Wa musi uzogiserura, kuko uzohishuranwa n'umuriro, kandi igikorwa c'umuntu wese uwo muriro uzokigeza ico kirimwo.
46003014	Igikorwa c'umuntu, ico yubatse kuri iryo tanguriro, ni carama, azohabwa ingero;
46003015	igikorwa c'umuntu ni casha, azobura ingero, yamara ubwiwe azokira, ariko nk'uwokowe mu muriro.
46003016	Mbega ntimuzi yuko muri urusengero rw'Imana, kandi ko Mpwemu w'Imana mubana?
46003017	Umuntu ni yonona urusengero rw'Imana, Imana izomurandura; kuko urusengero rw'Imana ari urwera, kandi urwo rusengero ni mwebwe.
46003018	Ntihakagire umuntu yihenda; umuntu wo muri mwebwe ni yiyumvira ko ari umunyabwenge ku vy'iki gihe, abe igipfu, kugira ngo abone kuba umunyabwenge.
46003019	Kuko ubwenge bw'iyi si ari ubupfu ku Mana. Kuko handitswe, ngo itegesha abanyabwenge ubugunge bwabo.
46003020	Kandi ngo Uhoraho arazi ivyiyumviro vy' abanyabwenge, kandi ko bitagira ikimazi.
46003021	Nuko ntihakagire umuntu yirata abantu. Kuko vyose ari ivyanyu;
46003022	ari Pahulo, canke Apolo, canke Kefa, canke isi, canke ubugingo, canke urupfu, canke ibiriho, canke ibizoba, vyose ni ivyanyu,
46003023	namwe muri aba Kristo, Kristo ni uwo Imana.
46004001	Umuntu ni atwiyumvire yuko turi abakozi ba Kristo, n'abanyabigega b'amabanga y'Imana.
46004002	Kandi ababwiriza abagomba ko babona ari abizigirwa.
46004003	Ariko kubwanje ni nk'ubusa rwose gucirwa urubanza namwe, canke n'urukinja rw'abantu; kandi nanje nyene sinicira urubanza.
46004004	Kuko ata co niyiziko, ariko si co kingira umwere; ariko uwuncira urubanza ni Umwami wacu.
46004005	Ni co gituma mudakwiye guca urubanza rw'ikintu na kimwe igihe carwo kitarashika, ni co kuza kw'Umwami wacu, azomurika ivyari vyanyegejwe mu mwiza, kandi azogaragaza inama zo mu mitima; ni ho umuntu wese azohabwa n'Imana ishimwe rimukwiye.
46004006	Ariko, bavukanyi, ivyo ndavyigereranijeko, jewe na Apolo, ku bwanyu, nk'igishushanyo; kugira ngo ivyo mvuze kuri twebwe bibigishe kutarenga ivyanditswe; ntihagire umuntu yikakisha arwana ishaka ry'umwe akagaya uwundi.
46004007	Ni nde aguteye kwitandukanya n'abandi? Kandi ico ufise utahawe ni igiki? Ariko namba waragihawe, ni igiki gituma wirata, nk'uwutagihawe?
46004008	Mumaze guhaga; mumaze gutunga; mwimitse nk'abami, tutarimwo. Erega icompa mukaba mwarimitswe, kugira ngo natwe twimikanwe namwe.
46004009	Kuko niyumvira yuko twebwe intumwa, Imana yatwerekanye nk'abari hasi inyuma ya bose, nk'abagerewe kwicwa, kuko twacitse akarorero mw'isi, mu bamarayika no mu bantu.
46004010	Twebwe turi ibipfu kubwa Kristo; mweho muri abanyabwenge muri Kristo. Turi abanyantege nke, muri abanyabushobozi; muri abanyacubahiro, turi inkengerwa.
46004011	Gushitsa n'ubu twishwe n'inzara n'inyota, twambaye ubusa, dukubitwa ibipfunsi, tubura uburagamo.
46004012	Dukoresha amaboko yacu tugatama. Iyo badutuka turabahezagira, iyo baduhama turihangana,
46004013	iyo batwambika ibara turabahoyahoya. Twahindutse umwavu w'isi, n'udukokorwa kuri bose gushitsa n'ubu.
46004014	Ivyo sindavyandikiye kubatetereza, ariko ni nko kubahanura, nk'abana banje nkunda.
46004015	Kuko naho mufise muri Kristo ababarera ibihumbi icumi, ntimufise ba so benshi, kuko ari jewe nabavyaje ubutumwa bwiza muri Kristo Yesu.
46004016	Nuko ndabinginga, munyigane.
46004017	Ni co gituma ndabatumyeko Timoteyo, umwana wanje nkunda, agamburukira Umwami wacu; azobibutsa inzira zanje zo muri Kristo, nk'uko nigisha hose mu mashengero yose.
46004018	Ariko bamwe bivyimvya, biyumvira yuko ntazoza i wanyu.
46004019	Ariko nzoza vuba, Umwami wacu ni yabigomba; kandi si amajambo y'abivyimvya nzomenya, ariko n'ubushobozi bwabo.
46004020	kuko ubwami bw'Imana atari ubwo amajambo, ariko n'ubwo ubushobozi.
46004021	Mugomba iki? Ko nza i wanyu nzanye inkoni, canke ko nzana urukundo n'umutima w'ubugwaneza?
46005001	Inkuru yamamaye hose yuko muri mwebwe hariho ubusambanyi; kandi ubwo busambanyi butoba no mu banyamahanga, kubona umuntu gucikiza muka se ngo amurongore.
46005002	Namwe mukikakisha, ntimubabare, nk'uko mwari mukwiye, kugira ngo uwakoze ico caha akurwe muri mwebwe.
46005003	Ku bwanje naho ntariho ku mubiri, ariko ndiho mu mpwemu, nahejeje gutsindisha uwakoze ibimeze bityo nk'aho ndiho,
46005004	mw'izina ry'Umwami Yesu mwebwe n'impwemu yanje dukoranye dufise ubushobozi bw'Umwami wacu Yesu,
46005005	guha Satani umeze atyo, kugira ngo umubiri wiwe uranduke, ubugingo bwiwe buzorokoke ku musi w'Umwami Yesu.
46005006	Kwirata kwanyu si kwiza. Ntimuzi yuko umwambiro muke wambira irobe ryose?
46005007	Nuko ni mukureho umwambiro wa kera, kugira ngo mube irobe rishasha, nk'uko mutarimwo umwambiro. Kuko umwagazi w'intama wa Pasika wacu watanzwe ko ishikanwa, ari we Kristo.
46005008	Nuko tuziririze imisi mikuru, tudafise umwambiro wa kera, canke umwambiro w'urwanko n'ikibi, ariko tugire imitsima itambiwe y'imitima ikeye ni ukuri.
46005009	Nabandikiye muri ca cete ko mutivanga n'abasambanyi.
46005010	Ariko sinavuga abasambanyi bo mu b'iyi si, canke abifuza, canke abasahura, canke abasenga ibigirwamana, kuko iyo biba bityo mwari mukwiye kuva mw'isi.
46005011	Ariko burya nabandikiye ko mutivanga n'uwitwa umuvukanyi, namba ari umusambanyi, canke uwunohoka, canke uwusenga ibigirwamana, canke uwutukana, canke uwuborerwa, canke umunyazi; umeze atyo, no gusangira ntimugasangire na we.
46005012	Mpuriye hehe no gucira urubanza abo hanze? Mbega si mwebwe mucira urubanza abo muri mwebwe?
46005013	ariko abo hanze Imana ni yo izobacira urubanza. Ni mukure umunyakibi muri mwebwe.
46006001	Mbega hari uwo muri mwebwe yogira ico apfa n'umuvukanyi wiwe, akubahuka kuburanira ku bagabitanya, ntaburanire ku bera?
46006002	Ntimuzi yuko abera ari bo bazocira abo isi urubanza? Kandi ko ari mwebwe muzocira abo isi urubanza, none ntimubereye guca imanza ntonto?
46006003	Ntimuzi yuko tuzocira abamarayika urubanza? None ntiturushiriza kuba abo guca imanza z'ivyo ubu bugingo?
46006004	Nuko, iyo mufise imanza zo guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo z'ivyo ubu bugingo, mbega mushiraho abatagira ico bamariye ishengero ngo abe ari bo bazica?
46006005	Ndabivugiye kubatetereza. Mbega vyoshoboka yuko muri mwebwe hatagira umunyabwenge n'umwe yoshobora gucira urubanza abavukanyi?
46006006	Ariko umuvukanyi akaburana n'uwundi muvukanyi, kandi bakaburanira no ku batizera!
46006007	Mbere n'ubu hari ico muhomvye rwose, kuko musubiranamwo mukaburana. Ntimwopfuma mugirirwa nabi? Ntimwopfuma mwemera kugungwa?
46006008	Ariko ni mwebwe mugiriranira nabi, mugungana, kandi abo mugirira mutyo ni abana ba So.
46006009	Ntimuzi yuko abagabitanya batazoragwa ubwami bw'Imana? Ntimuzimire; abashurashuzi, canke abasenga ibigirwamana, abasambanyi, abagabo basambana, abagabo basambana n'abandi bagabo,
46006010	ibisuma, abifuza, imborerwa, abatukana canke abasahura, ntibazoragwa ubwami bw'Imana.
46006011	Kandi bamwe muri mwebwe ni ko mwari muri; ariko mwaruhagiwe, ariko mwarejejwe, ariko mwatsindanishirijwe mw'izina ry'Umwami Yesu Kristo no muri Mpwemu w' Imana yacu.
46006012	Vyose ndavyemererwa, ariko si vyose bingirira ikimazi. Vyose ndavyemererwa, ariko sinzoganzwa n'ikintu na kimwe.
46006013	Ivyo kurya ni ivyo inda, n'inda n'iyo ivyo kurya; yamara Imana izobikuraho vyose. Ariko, imibiri yacu si iyo gushegura, mugabo ni iyo Umwami wacu, kandi Umwami ni uwo imibiri yacu.
46006014	Kandi Imana yazuye Umwami, natwe nyene izotuzurisha ubushobozi bwayo.
46006015	Ntimuzi yuko imibiri yanyu ari ingingo za Kristo? None ntore ingingo za Kristo, ndazihindure ingingo z'umumaraya? Biragahera.
46006016	Ntimuzi yuko uwimatanya n'umumaraya aba ari umubiri umwe na we? Kuko yavuze iti: "Bompi bazoba umubiri umwe."
46006017	Ariko uwimatanije n'Umwami wacu aba abaye impwemu imwe na we.
46006018	Muhunge ubushakanyi. Icaha cose umuntu akora si ico umubiri, ariko usheguye aba acumuye ku mubiri wiwe.
46006019	Ntimuzi yuko imibiri yanyu ari insengero za Mpwemu Yera ari muri mwebwe, uwo mufise, avuye ku Mana? Kandi si mwe mwiganza,
46006020	kuko mwaguzwe igiciro. Nuko rero, mushimishe Imana mu mibiri yanyu.
46007001	Ariko ku vyo mwanyandikiye, iciza ni uko umuhungu uwo ari we atohuye n'icitwa umukobwa.
46007002	Ariko ku bwo kwirinda gushurashura, umugabo wese agire umugore wiwe, n'umugore wese agire umugabo wiwe.
46007003	Umugabo ahe umugore wiwe ivyo akwiye, kandi umugore na we abigenze atyo ku mugabo wiwe.
46007004	Kuko umugore ataganza umubiri wiwe, ariko uganzwa n'umugabo; kandi umugabo na we ntaganza umubiri wiwe, ariko uganzwa n'umugore.
46007005	Ntimukimane, kiretse kumbure musezeranye igihe, kugira ngo mubone uburyo bwo gusenga, kandi mwongere mubane, Satani ntabageragereshe kutirinda kwanyu.
46007006	Ariko mvuze ivyo ari ukwemerana, si ivyagezwe ndabagerera.
46007007	Nagomba ko abantu bose bomera nkanje; ariko umuntu wese afise ingabire yiwe ahabwa n'Imana, umwe ukwiwe, uwundi ukwiwe.
46007008	Abatararongorana, bo n'abapfakazi, ndababwira yuko iciza kuri bo ari uko bogumya kumera nkanje.
46007009	Ariko namba badashobora kwirinda barongorane; kuko kwabirana ari kwiza, kuruta gushuha.
46007010	Abamaze kurongorana, ndabagera, ariko si jewe, n'Umwami wacu, umugore ntavane n'umugabo wiwe.
46007011	Aramutse avanye na we, abe igisubiramuhira, canke yisubize hamwe n'umugabo wiwe. Kandi umugabo ntate umugore wiwe.
46007012	Abandi ni jewe ndababwira, si Umwami wacu. Umuvukanyi asanzwe afise umugore atizera, kandi uwo mugore agakunda kubana na we, ntamute.
46007013	Kandi umugore afise umugabo atizera, na we agakunda kubana na we, ntavane n'umugabo wiwe.
46007014	Kuko umugabo atizera yezwa kubwo umugore wiwe, kandi umugore atizera yezwa kubwo uwo muvukanyi. Iyo bitamera bityo, abana banyu baba ari ibihumane, ariko noneho ni abera.
46007015	Ariko uwutizera, namba agomba kwahukana, ni yahukane. Umuvukanyi w'umugabo canke w'umugore ntahambirwa, iyo bimeze bityo. Imana yaduhamagariye amahoro.
46007016	Yewe mugore, ubwirwa n'iki yuko uzokiza umugabo wawe? Yewe mugabo, ubwirwa n'iki yuko uzokiza umugore wawe?
46007017	Ariko gusa, uko Umwami wacu yagabiye umuntu wese, kandi uko Imana yamuhamagaye, kube ari ko amera. Ni ko ngera mu mashengero yose.
46007018	Mbega hariho umuntu yahamagawe yarahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo? Ntagacike nk'uwutagihimbuwe. Hariho umuntu yahamagawe atarahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo? Ntakagihimburwe.
46007019	Guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo nta co kumaze, no kudahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo nta co kumaze, ariko ikigira ico kimaze n'ukwitondera ivyagezwe n'Imana.
46007020	Umuntu wese, uko yari ari mw'ihamagarwa ryiwe, abigumemwo.
46007021	Wahamagawe uri umushumba? Ntibikubabaze. Ariko, namba bishoboka ko ucika uwidegemvya, ubihitemwo.
46007022	Uwahamagawe n'Umwami wacu ari umushumba, aba acitse uwidegemvya acunguwe n'Umwami. Ni ko, uwahamagawe n'Umwami ari uwidegemvya, aba acitse umushumba wa Kristo.
46007023	Mwaguzwe igiciro, ntimukabe abakozi b'abantu.
46007024	Bavukanyi, umuntu wese uko yari ari aho yahamagarwa, akugumanemwo n'Imana.
46007025	Ku vyo inkumi, simfise icagezwe n'Umwami wacu; ariko ndababwira ivyo niyumvira, nk'umuntu yagiriwe ikigongwe n'Umwami, ngo mbe umwizigirwa.
46007026	Nuko ndiyumvira yuko ari vyiza ku bwo igihe kigoye ca none, yuko ari vyiza k'umuntu aguma uko ari.
46007027	Wahambiriwe ku mugore? Nturondere kubohorwa. Wabohowe ku mugore? Nturondere umugore.
46007028	Ariko iyo urongoye, nta caha uba ukoze. N'inkumi, iyo irongowe nta caha iba ikoze. Mugabo, abameze batyo bazogira amagorwa mu mubiri, ariko jewe nagomba kuyabakingira.
46007029	Ariko, bavukanyi, ibi ni vyo mvuga, ko biri ukwo; uhereye none abari n'abagore bamere nk'abatabagira;
46007030	kandi abarira bamere nk' abatarira, n'abanezerewe bamere nk'abatanezerewe, n'abagura bamere nk'abatagira ico bafise,
46007031	n'abakoresha ivy'isi, bamere nk' abatabishishikaye; kuko ukw'isi imeze uku, kugenda gushira.
46007032	Ariko ndagomba ko mutiganyira. Uwutagira umugore yitwaririka ivyo Umwami wacu, uko yonezereza Umwami.
46007033	Ariko uwumufise yitwaririka ivy'isi, uko yonezereza umugore.
46007034	Kandi hariho itandukaniro ku mugore n'inkumi. Uwutarongowe yitwaririka ivyo Umwami wacu, kugira ngo abe uwera ku mubiri no mu mutima; ariko uwabiriwe yitwaririka ivy'isi, uko yonezereza umugabo.
46007035	Ivyo ndabivugiye kubafasha, si ukubashira mu mpururu, ariko n'ukubiroranya, no kugira ngo mukorere Umwami wacu, mudafise imitima ibiri.
46007036	Ariko umuntu ni yaba yiyumvira ko umukobwa wiwe atetererwa, kuko arengeranye ubukumi, kandi kuko bikwiye kuba gutyo, ni agenze uko agomba; nta caha azoba akoze, ni amureke aje kurongorwa.
46007037	Ariko uwukomeye mu mutima wiwe, adafise ikimuhambira, ariko ashobora gukora ivyo agomba ubwiwe, yagabiye mu mutima kuzigama umukobwa bwiwe ngo ntarongorwe, azoba agize neza.
46007038	Nuko uwutanga umukobwa wiwe ngo arongorwe aba agize neza; kandi uwutamutanga aba arushirije kugira neza.
46007039	Umugore aboherwa ku mugabo wiwe akiriho; ariko iyo umugabo apfuye, nta kimubuza gucurwa n'uwo agomba, mugabo rero, ari uwuri mu Mwami wacu.
46007040	Ariko iyo agumye uko ari, ni ho arushiriza guhirwa, uko niyumvira ku bwanje; kandi ngira ngo nanje mfise Mpwemu w'Imana.
46008001	Ku vyo ivyaterekerejwe ibishushanyo vy'ibigirwamana, turazi yuko twese turi n'ubwenge. Ubwenge butuma umuntu yivyimvya, ariko urukundo rurubaka.
46008002	Ni hagira umuntu yiyumvira yuko hari ico azi, azoba ataramenya nk'uko akwiye kumenya.
46008003	Ariko uwukunda Imana ni we amenywa na yo.
46008004	Nuko, ku vyo kurya ivyaterekerejwe ibigirwamana, turazi yuko igishushanyo atari ikintu mw'isi, kandi yuko ata yindi mana iriho, atari Imwe.
46008005	Naho hari ivyitwa ibigirwamana mw'ijuru canke mw'isi, nk'uko hari ibigirwamana vyinshi n'abami benshi,
46008006	ariko kuri twebwe hari Imana imwe, Data wa twese, yandurukwamwo na vyose, natwe twabesherejweho kuba abayo; kandi hari Umwami umwe, ni Yesu Kristo, abeshaho vyose, natwe akatubeshaho.
46008007	Ariko ubwo bwenge ntibufiswe na bose; kuko bamwe baremariye mu bigirwamana gushitsa n'ubu, barya ikintu bibwira ko caterekerejwe ikigirwamana, kandi umutima ugahumanywa no kudakomera.
46008008	ariko ivyo kurya si vyo bidushikiriza Imana. Iyo tutabiriye, nta co duhomba; canke iyo tubiriye, nta co duhomboka.
46008009	Mwiyubare, kugira ngo ubwo bushobozi bwanyu ntibube igitsitaza c'abadakomeye na gato.
46008010	Kuko umuntu iyo akubonye, wewe wahawe gutahura, wicaye urira mu rusengero rw'ikigirwamana, umutima w'uwo, iyo adakomeye, mbega ntuzorinduka, ukarya ivyaterekerejwe ibigirwamana?
46008011	Nuko uwudakomeye aba aranduwe no gutahura kwawe, kandi ari we muvukanyi Kristo yapfiriye.
46008012	Nuko iyo mukoreye icaha abavukanyi banyu mutyo, mugakomeretsa imitima yabo idakomeye, muba mukoreye icaha Kristo.
46008013	Ni co gituma namba ivyo kurya bigwisha umuvukanyi, sinzopfa nongeye kurya inyama kugira ngo singwishe umuvukanyi wanje.
46009001	Mbega sindi uwidegemvya? Sindi intumwa? Sinabonye Yesu Umwami wacu? Namwe ntimuri igikorwa canje mu Mwami?
46009002	Namba ku bandi ntari intumwa, ariko kuri mwebwe ndi yo; kuko muri ikimenyetso mu Mwami c'uko ndi intumwa.
46009003	Ibi ni vyo nireguza ku bampinyura:
46009004	mbega ntitwemererwa kurya no kunywa?
46009005	Ntitwokwemerewe kujana n'umugore akijijwe nk'uko izindi ntumwa zikora, n'abavukanyi b'Umwami wacu na Kefa?
46009006	Canke jewe na Barunaba ni twebwe twenyene tutemererwa kureka gukora?
46009007	Ni nde yigeze kwitunga, ari umusoda? Ni nde yotera umurima w'inzabibu ntarye inzabibu zarwo? Canke ni nde yoragira ubusho, ntabunywe?
46009008	Mbega ivyo ndabivuze mu buryo bw'abantu, canke ivyagezwe vyo ntibivuga bityo?
46009009	Kuko handitswe mu vyagezwe vya Mose, ngo ntimuze murumye umunwa w'inka iriko irasekura ingano. Mbega inka ni zo Imana ibabaye?
46009010	Canke se yabivuze kubwacu? Ego me, vyanditswe ku bwacu; kuko umurimyi akwiye kurima afise ivyizigiro, kandi umusekuzi akwiye gusekura yizigiye ko azohabwako.
46009011	Mbega ko twababivyemwo ivyo impwemu, none n'ibikomeye ko twokwimbura ivyanyu vy'umubiri?
46009012	Abandi namba baravyemerewe kuri mwebwe, mbega ntitubarusha cane? Ariko ntitwarwaniye ivyo twemerewe, yamara twihanganira vyose, kugira ngo ntituzane ikidehesha ubutumwa bwiza bwa Kristo.
46009013	Ntimuzi yuko abakora ibikorwa vy'ivyera barya ivyo urusengero, kandi abakora ivyo igicaniro basangira n'igicaniro?
46009014	Kandi n'Umwami wacu ni ko yageze ko abavuga ubutumwa bwiza batungwa n'ubutumwa.
46009015	Ariko jewe ubwanje nta co narwaniye muri ivyo; kandi sinandikiye ivyo kugira ngo nkorerwe ntyo. Ivyoba vyiza n'uko nopfuma mpfa, hako umuntu ahindura ubusa ivyo vyirato vyanje.
46009016	Iyo mvuga ubutumwa, singira ico nirata; kuko mfise ikingobera; ntavuze ubutumwa nobona ibara.
46009017	Ngenjeje ntyo ndabikunze, ndagererwa; ariko ngenjeje ntyo ntabikunze na ho nyene ngoberwa n'ububwiriza nizigiweko.
46009018	None ingero yanje ni inki? Ni uko ubutumwa, uko ndabuvuze, ndabuvuga ku buntu, kugira ngo sindwanire ivyo nemerewe mu butumwa.
46009019	Naho kuri bose ndi uwidegemvya, nihinduye umushumba wa bose, kugira ngo ndushirize kuronka benshi.
46009020	Ku Bayuda nabaye nk'Umuyuda, kugira ngo ndonke Abayuda; ku baganzwa n'ivyagezwe nabaye nk'uwuganzwa na vyo, naho ubwanje ntaganzwa na vyo, kugira ngo ndonke abaganzwa n'ivyagezwe.
46009021	Ku bataganzwa n'ivyagezwe, nabaye nk'uwutaganzwa na vyo, kugira ngo ndonke abataganzwa n'ivyagezwe, yamara ku Mana ho sindi uwutaganzwa n'ivyagezwe, kuko kuri Kristo nganzwa na vyo.
46009022	Ku badakomeye nabaye nk'uwudakomeye, kugira ngo ndonke abadakomeye. Kuri bose nabaye vyose kugira ngo nkirishe bamwebamwe uburyo bwose.
46009023	Kandi ivyo vyose ndabikora kubwo ubutumwa bwiza, kugira ngo mfatanye n'abandi muri bwo.
46009024	Ntimuzi yuko mu birori abasiganwa biruka bose, ariko uherwa akaba umwe? Namwe mube ari ko mwiruka, kugira ngo muronke impera.
46009025	Kuko umuntu wese azorushanywa yitegura muri vyose. Abo bagenza batyo, kugira ngo bahabwe igitsibo gishira, ariko twebwe tugenza dutyo kugira ngo duhabwe ikitazoshira.
46009026	Nuko nanje ndiruka, ariko si nk'uwutazi iyo aja; nkubitana ibipfunsi, ariko si nk'uhusha;
46009027	kandi ndwanya umubiri wanje, nkawuhindura umushumba, kugira ngo kumbure maze kwigisha abandi, nanje ubwanje sinze mboneke ko ntemewe.
46010001	Bavukanyi, singomba ko mutamenya yuko ba sogokuruza bose bari musi ya ca gicu, kandi yuko bose baciye hagati ya ca kiyaga cigabanije,
46010002	bose bakabatirizwa kuba aba Mose muri ico gicu no muri ico kiyaga,
46010003	bose bagasangira vya vyo kurya vy'impwemu,
46010004	bose bagasangira vya vyo kunywa vy'impwemu. Kuko banywa ku gitandara c'impwemu cabakurikira, ico gitandara cari Kristo.
46010005	Ariko abenshi muri bo, Imana ntiyabashimye, kuko bahonerejwe mu bugaragwa.
46010006	Ariko ivyo vyatubereye akarorero kugira ngo ntitwifuze ibibi, nk'uko ba bandi bavyifuje.
46010007	Kandi ntimugasenge ibishushanyo vy'ibigirwamana, nk'uko bamwe bo muri ba bandi babisenga; nk'uko handitswe, ngo abantu bicaritswe no kurya no kunywa, bava hasi baravyina.
46010008	Kandi ntitugashurashure, nk'uko bamwe bo muri ba bandi basheguye, maze hagapfamwo abantu ibihumbi mirongo ibiri na bitatu ku musi umwe.
46010009	Kandi ntitukagerageze Umwami wacu, nk'uko bamwe bo muri ba bandi bamugerageje, bakamarwa n'inzoka.
46010010	Kandi ntimukidodombe, nk'uko bamwe bo muri ba bandi bidodomvye, bakamarwa n'umuranduzi.
46010011	Ariko ivyo vyababayeko kugira ngo bitubere akarorero, kandi vyandikiwe kuduhanura twebwe, abashikwako n'amaherezo y'ibihe.
46010012	Nuko rero uwiyumvira ko ahagaze ni yiyubare ntagwe.
46010013	Nta cabagerageje kitari ico umuntu yoshobora kwihanganira. Ariko Imana ni iyo kwizigirwa ntizobakundira ko mugeragezwa n'ibiruta ivyo mushobora, ariko hamwe n'ikibagerageza izobacira icanzo, kugira ngo mubone ingene mushobora kucihanganira.
46010014	Nuko, abo nkunda, ni muhunge gusenga ibigirwamana.
46010015	Ndababwira nk'abanyabwenge; mwiyumvire ivyo mvuga, yuko ari ko biri.
46010016	Igikombe c'umuhezagiro, ico duhezagira, mbega si kwo gusangira amaraso ya Kristo? Umutsima tumanyagura, si kwo gusangira umubiri wa Kristo?
46010017	Nk'uko uwo mutsima ari umwe, twebwe, naho turi benshi, turi umubiri umwe; kuko twese dusangira umutsima umwe.
46010018	Murabe Abisirayeli ku rukoba. Abarya ikimazi, mbega ntibasangira n'igicaniro?
46010019	Nuko ico mvuga n'igiki? Mbega mvuga yuko icaterekerejwe ikigirwamana ari ikintu, canke yuko ikigirwamana ari ikintu?
46010020	Ariko mvuga yuko ibimazi abanyamahanga batanga, babiha abadayimoni, babishikanira abadayimoni, ntibabiha Imana. Nanje Singomba yuko musangira n'abadayimoni.
46010021	Ntimushobora kunywera ku gikombe c'Umwami wacu, no ku gikombe c'abadayimoni. Ntimushobora gusangira ivyo ku meza y'Umwami wacu n'ivyo ku meza y'abadayimoni.
46010022	Canke Umwami tumutere ishari? Mbega tumurusha inkomezi?
46010023	Vyose turavyemererwa, ariko ibitugirira ikimazi si vyose. Vyose turavyemererwa, ariko ivyubaka si vyose.
46010024	Ntihagire umuntu ababara ivyiwe, ariko ababare ivyo uwundi.
46010025	Izo zigurwa mw'ibagiro, mube muzirya ata co mubajije kubwo ijwi ryo mu mutima;
46010026	kuko isi ari iyo Uhoraho, n'ibiyuzuye.
46010027	Umuntu wo mu batizera ni yabahamagara, mukagomba kugenda, ico bazoshira imbere yanyu cose, mube mukirya, ata co mubajije, kubwo ijwi ryo mu mutima.
46010028	Ariko ni hagira umuntu ababwira ati: "Ico ni icaterekerejwe; ntimukakirye, kubwo uwo abiseruye, no kubwo ijwi ryo mu mutima."
46010029	Ariko umutima mvuze si uwawe, ni uwa wa wundi. Ni igiki gituma ukwidegemvya kwanje guhinyurwa n'umutima w'uwundi?
46010030	Ko ndya ndabishimiye, ni igiki gituma ntukirwa ivyo nshimiye?
46010031	Nuko iyo murya, iyo munywa, canke iyo mukora ikindi kintu cose, mube mukorera vyose gushimisha Imana.
46010032	Ntimubere Abayuda igitsitaza, canke Abagiriki, canke ishengero ry'Imana.
46010033	Nk'uko nanje nezereza bose muri vyose, ntarondera ikigira ico kimarira ubwanje, ariko nkarondera ikigira ico kimarira abenshi, kugira ngo bakire.
46011001	Munyigane, nk'uko nanje nigana Kristo.
46011002	Ndabashima, kuko munyibuka muri vyose, mukagumya ivyo nabashikirije, nk'uko nabibahaye.
46011003	Ariko ndagomba ko mumenya k'umutwe w'umugabo wese ari Kristo, kandi k'umutwe w'umugore ari umugabo, kandi k'umutwe wa Kristo ari Imana.
46011004	Umugabo wese iyo asenga canke avugishwa n'Imana umutwe wiwe utwikiriye, aba awuteye isoni.
46011005	Ariko umugore wese iyo asenga canke avugishwa n'Imana, adatwikiriye umutwe, aba awuteye isoni; kuko ari bimwe rwose no kumobwa.
46011006	Ni hagira umugore atitwikira mu mutwe, bamumwe n'umushatsi; namba ari ibiteye isoni k'umugore akererwa umushatsi canke ko amobwa ni yitwikire mu mutwe.
46011007	Umugabo ntakwiye kwitwikira mu mutwe, kuko ari ishusho y'Imana n'ubwiza bwayo; ariko umugore n'ubwiza bw'umugabo.
46011008	Kuko umugabo atamutse ku mugore, ariko umugore ni we yamutse ku mugabo.
46011009	Kandi umugabo ntiyaremwe kubwo umugore, ariko umugore ni we yaremwe kubwo umugabo.
46011010	Ni co gituma umugore akwiye kwambara mu mutwe ikimenyetso co kugabwa, kubwo abamarayika.
46011011	Ariko mu Mwami wacu, umugore agenda ku mugabo, ni ko n'umugabo agenda ku mugore.
46011012	Nk'uko umugore yamutse ku mugabo, ni k'umugabo avyarwa n'umugore; ariko vyose vyamuka ku Mana.
46011013	Ni mwiyumvire ubwanyu uko biri. Mbega birakwiye ko umugore asenga Imana atitwikiriye mu mutwe?
46011014	Akameremere kacu mbega ntikabigisha yuko umugabo yotega umushatsi, womutera isoni,
46011015	kandi ko umugore, iyo ateze umushatsi, uba ari ubwiza bwiwe? Kuko yahawe umushatsi ngo ube umwambaro wo mu mutwe.
46011016	Ariko namba hari umuntu agomba kuvyura ibihari, twebwe ntidufise umugenzo nk'uwo, kandi n'amashengero y'Imana ntawufise.
46011017	Ariko uko ndababarira ibi, sindabashima, kuko mudakoranira iciza, ariko mukoranira ikibi.
46011018	Ica mbere, iyo mukoraniye mw'ikoraniro, numva yuko mwitandukanya, kandi ngira ngo muri bimwebimwe vyoba ari ko biri.
46011019	Kuko n'ibice bitobura kubabamwo, ngo abemewe muri mwebwe baseruke.
46011020	Nuko iyo mukoranye, burya ntikuba ari ukurya ingaburo y'Umwami wacu.
46011021	Kuko mu kurya, umuntu wese yisangiza ivyiwe agacura abandi. Maze umwe agasonza, uwundi akaborerwa.
46011022	Mbega yemwe; ntimufise ingo zo kuriramwo no kunyweramwo? Canke mukengera ishengero ry'Imana, mugatetereza abadafise? Ndababwire iki? Ndabashime? Kuri ivyo sindabashima.
46011023	Kuko ico nahawe n'Umwami wacu ari co nabashikirije namwe, yuko Umwami Yesu mw'ijoro yaguzwemwo yakiriye umutsima,
46011024	akawushimira Imana, akawumanyagura, akavuga ati: "Uwu ni umubiri wanje ubatangiwe, murahora mugira mutya kugira ngo kibe icibutso canje."
46011025	N'igikombe akigenza atyo, bahejeje kurya, arababwira ati: "Iki gikombe n'isezerano rishasha ryo mu maraso yanje; murahora mugira mutya uko muzonywako, kugira ngo kibe icibutso canje.
46011026	Uko murya uwo mutsima kandi uko munywera kuri ico gikombe, muba mumenyekanisha urupfu rw' Umwami wacu, kugeza aho azozira."
46011027	Ni co gituma, umuntu wese azorya umutsima w'Umwami wacu, canke azonywera ku gikombe ciwe, uko bidakwiye, azotsindwa n'urubanza rw'uko yakengereye umubiri n'amaraso vy'Umwami.
46011028	Ariko umuntu yibaze uko ameze, abone kurya kuri uwo mutsima, no kunywera kuri ico gikombe.
46011029	Kuko uwurya canke uwunywa, atamenye umubiri w' Umwami wacu, arya kandi anywa ibimuzanira gutsindwa n'urubanza.
46011030	Ni co gituma muri mwebwe benshi bagira intege nke, abandi bakarwaragurika, kandi abatari bake bakaba barapfuye.
46011031	Ariko iyo twimenye uko turi, ntidutsindwa n'urubanza.
46011032	Ariko iyo dutsinzwe n'urubanza duhanwa n'Umwami, kugira ngo ntituzotsindwe n'urubanza rudashira hamwe n'abo isi.
46011033	Nuko, bavukanyi banje, uko mukoraniye kurya, murorerane.
46011034	Umuntu ni yasonza, ararya i we, kugira ngo ntimukoranire gutsindwa n'urubanza. Ibisigaye nzobiroranya aho nzozira.
46012001	Bavukanyi, ivyo ingabire za Mpwemu, singomba ko mutabimenya.
46012002	Murazi yuko mukiri injabuka mwakwegwa, mukaja ku bigirwamana bitazi kuvuga, nk'uko mwabikwegeweko.
46012003	Ni co gituma ndabamenyesha yuko ata muntu avugishwa na Mpwemu w'Imana, avuga ati: "Yesu n'ikivume, kandi ata muntu ashobora kuvuga ati: 'Yesu n'Uhoraho, atabivugishijwe na Mpwemu Yera.'"
46012004	Yamara hariho ingabire z'uburyo bwinshi, ariko Mpwemu n'umwe.
46012005	Kandi hari amabango menshi, ariko Umwami ni umwe.
46012006	Kandi hariho uburyo bwinshi bwo gukora, ariko Imana n'imwe, ikorera vyose muri bose.
46012007	Yamara, umuntu wese ahabwa ikimwerekanako Mpwemu, kugira ngo bigire ikimazi.
46012008	Kuko umwe aheshwa na Mpwemu ijambo ry'ubwenge, uwundi agaheshwa n'uwo Mpwemu ijambo ryo kumenya.
46012009	Uwundi agaheshwa n'uwo Mpwemu ukwizera, uwundi agaheshwa n'uwo Mpwemu umwe ingabire zo gukiza indwara.
46012010	Uwundi agahabwa gukora ibitangaza, uwundi agahabwa kuvugishwa n'Imana, uwundi agahabwa kurobanura impwemu, uwundi agahabwa kuvuga indimi nyinshi, uwundi agahabwa gusobanura indimi.
46012011	Ariko ivyo vyose uwo Mpwemu umwe ni we abikorera muri bo, agabira umuntu wese uko agomba.
46012012	Nk'uko umubiri ari umwe, ukagira ingingo nyinshi, kandi ingingo z'umubiri zose naho ari nyinshi ari umubiri umwe, ni ko na Kristo ari.
46012013	Kuko muri Mpwemu umwe, twese ari ho twabatijwe ngo tube umubiri umwe, naho boba Abayuda canke Abagiriki, naho boba abakozi canke abidegemvya. Kandi twese twanyweshejwe Mpwemu umwe.
46012014	Umubiri si urugingo rumwe, ariko ni nyinshi.
46012015	Ikirenge covuga kiti: "Ko ntari ikiganza sindi uwo ku mubiri; ivyo ntivyotuma kitaba ico ku mubiri."
46012016	Kandi ugutwi kwovuga kuti: "Ko ntari ijisho, sindi uwo ku mubiri; ivyo ntivyotuma kutaba ukwo ku mubiri."
46012017	Iyo umubiri wose uba ijisho, kwumva kwobaye hehe? Iyo wose uba kwumva, kumoterwa kwobaye hehe?
46012018	Ariko noneho Imana yashizeho ingingo z'umubiri, urugingo rwose aho yagomvye.
46012019	Kandi iyo zose ziba urugingo rumwe, umubiri wobaye hehe?
46012020	Ariko noneho, ingingo ni nyinshi, umubiri ukaba umwe.
46012021	Ijisho ntiryoshobora kubarira ikiganza, ngo nta co umariye; canke umutwe kubarira ibirenge, ngo nta co mumariye.
46012022	Ariko uretse ivyo, ingingo z'umubiri ziyumvirwa ko ari izo intege nke inyuma y'izindi, ni zo zitohara;
46012023	kandi izo ku mubiri twiyumvira ko zidafise icubahiro, ni zo zirushiriza kuronka icubahiro; kandi ingingo zacu ziteye isoni ni zo zirushiriza gusharizwa.
46012024	Yamara izidateye isoni ntizirinda kwambikwa. Ariko Imana yafatanije umubiri hamwe, urugingo rukenye icubahiro iruha icubahiro kirushiriza,
46012025	kugira ngo umubiri ntiwireme ibice, ariko ingingo zibabarane kumwe.
46012026	Kandi urugingo rumwe iyo rubabaye, ingingo zose zirababazanywa na rwo; canke iyo urugingo rumwe ruhawe icubahiro, ingingo zose zihimbaranwa na rwo.
46012027	Namwe muri umubiri wa Kristo, kandi umuntu wese wo muri mwebwe ni urugingo rwawo.
46012028	Kandi Imana yabanje gushira mw'ishengero bamwe baba intumwa, hanyuma aba kabiri ibashiraho kuba abavugishwa na yo, maze aba gatatu, ibashiraho kuba abigisha, yongera ishiraho abakora ibitangaza, maze ishiraho abahawe ingabire zo gukiza indwara, n'abahawe gufasha abandi, n'abahawe kurongora n'abahawe kuvuga indimi nyinshi.
46012029	Mbega bose ni intumwa? Bose ni abavugishwa n'Imana? Bose n'abigisha? Bose bakora ibitangaza?
46012030	Bose bafise ingabire zo gukiza indwara? Bose bavuga izindi ndimi? Bose basobanura indimi?
46012031	Ariko mwifuze cane ingabire ziruta izindi. Kandi ndabereka inzira irushiriza kuba nziza.
46013001	Naho novuga indimi z'abantu n'izo abamarayika, ariko ntagira urukundo, noba ncitse umuringa uvuga, canke icuma kivuzwa kigasama.
46013002	Kandi naho nogira ingabire yo kuvugishwa n'Imana, nkamenya amabanga yose, n'ubwenge bwose, kandi naho nogira ukwizera kwose, ngashobora gukuraho imisozi, ariko ntagira urukundo, noba ndi ubusa.
46013003	Kandi naho notanga ivyanje vyose, ngo ngaburire aboro, kandi naho notanga umubiri wanje ngo nturirwe, ariko ntagira urukundo, nta co vyomarira.
46013004	Urukundo rurihangana, rugira neza, urukundo ntirugira ishari, urukundo ntirwihayagiza, ntirwihimbaza,
46013005	ntirukora ibiteye isoni, ntirurondera ivyarwo, ntirwiciraho, ntirwiyumvira ikibi ku bantu,
46013006	ntirunezererwa ukugabitanya kw'abandi, ariko runezeranwa n'ukuri;
46013007	rurenzako muri vyose, rwizera vyose, rwizigira vyose, rwihanganira vyose.
46013008	Urukundo nta ho rushira. Ukuvugishwa n'Imana kuzokurwaho, ukuvuga izindi ndimi kuzogira iherezo, ubwenge buzokurwaho.
46013009	Kuko tuzi agace, kandi tuvugishwa n'Imana agace,
46013010	ariko, aho igihinguye kizoshikira, ivyo agace bizokurwaho.
46013011	Nkiri umwana mutoya, navuga rwana, niyumvira rwana, nibwira rwana. Maze gukura, mva mu vy'ubwana.
46013012	Kuko ubu turabira mu cirore ivyijiji, ariko ico gihe tuzoraba nk'abarabana imbonankubone. Ubu nzi agace, ariko ico gihe nzomenya rwose nk'uko namenywe rwose.
46013013	None rero hagumyeho ukwizera, n'ivyizigiro, n'urukundo, ivyo uko ari bitatu; ariko ikibiruta n'urukundo.
46014001	Mwirukire urukundo. Yamara mwifuze cane ingabire za Mpwemu, canecane kuvugishwa n'Imana.
46014002	Uvuga ururimi rutamenyekana si abantu abarira, ariko abarira Imana, kuko ata wuvyumva, ariko mu mpwemu avuga amabanga.
46014003	Ariko uwuvugishwa n'Imana, abarira abantu ivyo kubakomeza n'ivyo kubahanura n'ivyo kubirura.
46014004	Uvuga ururimi rutamenyekana ariyubaka, ariko uwuvugishwa n'Imana yubaka ishengero.
46014005	Nagomba ko mwese muvuga indimi zitamenyekana, ariko ikirushiriza, ko muvugishwa n'Imana. Uwuvugishwa na yo aruta uvuga indimi zitamenyekana, kiretse yobisobanura, kugira ngo ishengero ryubakwe.
46014006	Ariko none, bavukanyi, ni naza i wanyu mvuga indimi zitamenyekana, nzobamarira iki, ni ntababarira ivyo mpishuriwe, canke ivyo mpawe kumenya, canke kuvugishwa n'Imana, canke kwigisha?
46014007	Kandi n'ibidafise ubugingo biri n'amajwi: umwironge iyo udatandukanije ijwi, canke inanga, bomenya bate irivuzwa canke iricurarangwa?
46014008	Kandi n'inzumbeti yovuga ijwi ritamenyekana, ni nde yokwitegura gutabara?
46014009	Namwe ni uko, ururimi rwanyu ni rutavuga ibimenyekana, bazomenya bate ivyo muvuga? Kuko muzoba muvuga ibitwarwa n'umuyaga.
46014010	Amajwi yo mw'isi, naho ari menshi ate, nta ridafise uko risobanurwa.
46014011	Nuko iyo ntamenye uko ijwi risobanurwa, uno avuga mba ndamubereye uwudebagura, kandi nanje, uno avuga aba ambereye uwudebagura.
46014012	Namwe ni uko, kuko mwifuza ivya Mpwemu, kuremesha ishengero kube ari kwo gutuma mugomba kurushiriza.
46014013	Nuko uwuvuga ururimi rutamenyekana asenge, kugira ngo ahabwe kubisobanura.
46014014	Iyo nsenga mu rurimi rutamenyekana, impwemu yanje irasenga, ariko ubwenge bwanje buragumbaha.
46014015	Nuko ngire nte? Nzosengesha impwemu yanje, ariko kandi nzosengesha n'ubwenge. Nzoririmbisha impwemu yanje, ariko kandi nzoririmbisha n'ubwenge.
46014016	Iyo ushimye Imana, ushimishije impwemu yawe yonyene, mbega uri ku ruhande rw'abatungu yoshobora ate kuvuga ati: "Amina, ni waheza gushima, kandi atamenye ico uvuze?"
46014017	Ni ukuri ku bwawe ushima neza, ariko wa wundi ntakomezwa.
46014018	Nshimira Imana yuko ndabarusha mwese kuvuga indimi zitamenyekana.
46014019	Ariko mw'ishengero nopfuma mvugisha ubwenge bwanje amajambo atanu, kugira ngo nigishe n'abandi, hako mvuga amajambo ibihumbi icumi mu rurimi rutamenyekana.
46014020	Bavukanyi, ntimube abana mu bwenge, ariko mube ibitazi mu bibi; ariko mu bwenge mube abagabo.
46014021	Mu vyagezwe handitswe, ngo nzovuganira n'ubu bwoko mu kanwa k'abavuga izindi ndimi no mu kanwa k'abanyamahanga, ariko naho nzovuga ntyo, ntibazonyumvira, ni ko Uhoraho avuze.
46014022	Ni co gituma indimi zitamenyekana zitabera abizera ikimenyetso, ariko zikibera abatizera. Ariko kuvugishwa n'Imana kwo, ntikubera abatizera ikimenyetso ariko kukibera abizera.
46014023	Nuko ishengero ryose, iyo rikoraniye hamwe, bose bakavuga indimi zitamenyekana, hakinjiramwo abatungu canke abatizera, ntibovuga yuko mwasaze?
46014024	Ariko bose iyo bavugishwa n'Imana, hakinjiramwo uwutizera canke umutungu, yomenyeshwa ivyaha vyiwe na bose, agahinyuzwa na bose.
46014025	Ibihishijwe mu mutima wiwe bigaseruka; Nuko akubika inda, agasenga Imana, akatura yuko Imana iri muri mwebwe vy'ukuri.
46014026	Ni bite ga bavukanyi? Iyo mukoranye, umuntu wese aba afise indirimbo, canke amajambo yo kwigisha, canke amajambo ahishuriwe, canke ururimi rutamenyekana, canke amajambo yo kurusobanura. Vyose bikorwe kugira ngo abantu bakomezwe.
46014027	Ni haba hariho abavuga ururimi rutamenyekana, havuge babiri canke batatu, badasaga, kandi bavuge bakurikirana, hagire ubisobanura.
46014028	Ariko ni haba hatariho uwubisobanura, uvuga urutamenyekana acereze mw'ishengero, yibwire, kandi abwire Imana.
46014029	Kandi n'abavugishwa n'Imana bavuge ari babiri canke batatu, abandi babigenzure.
46014030	Ariko uwundi yicaye ni yagira ico ahishurirwa, uwabanje ahore.
46014031	Kuko mwese mushobora kuvugishwa n'Imana umwumwe, ngo bose bige, bose bahanurwe.
46014032	Impwemu z'abavugishwa n' Imana ziganzwa na bo;
46014033	kuko Imana atari iyo umuvurungano, ariko ni iyo amahoro. Nk'uko bimeze mu mashengero yose y'abera,
46014034	abagore bacereze mw'ishengero, kuko batemererwa kuvuga. Ariko baganzwe, nk'uko ivyagezwe na vyo bivuga.
46014035	Kandi ni hagira ico bagomba kwiga, babarize abagabo babo i muhira, kuko biteye isoni k'umugore avuga mw'ishengero.
46014036	Mbega kuri mwebwe ni ho ijambo ry'Imana ryandurutse? Canke ryashitse kuri mwebwe mwenyene?
46014037	Ni hagira umuntu yiyumvira ko ari uwuvugishwa n'Imana, canke ko ari uwo impwemu, amenye ivyo ndabandikiye yuko ari icagezwe c'Umwami wacu.
46014038	Ariko, namba hari umuntu atabimenye, ntakabimenye.
46014039	Nuko, bavukanyi banje, mwifuze cane kuvugishwa n'Imana, kandi ntimubuze kuvuga indimi zitamenyekana.
46014040	Ariko vyose bitungane neza, birorane.
46015001	Bavukanyi, ndabamenyesha ubutumwa bwiza, ubwo nababariye, namwe mukabakira, kandi mukabuhagararamwo,
46015002	kandi mugakizwa na bwo, asangwa mukibufashe nk'uko nabubabwiye, kiretse mwoba mwizereye ubusa.
46015003	Kuko nabanje kubashikiriza ico nanje nahawe, yuko Kristo yapfiriye ivyaha vyacu, nk'uko ivyanditswe bivuga,
46015004	agahambwa, akazuka ku musi ugira gatatu, nk'uko ivyanditswe bivuga;
46015005	akiyereka Kefa, maze akiyereka bamwe icumi na babiri,
46015006	akongera akiyerekera hamwe abavukanyi barenga amajana atanu, muri abo abenshi baracariho n'ubu, ariko bamwe barasinziriye.
46015007	Maze yiyereka Yakobo, hanyuma yiyereka intumwa zose.
46015008	Maze hanyuma ya bose nanje aranyiyereka ndi nk'uwavutse atageze.
46015009	Mbere jewe ndi inyuma y'izindi ntumwa zose, sinkwiye no kwitwa intumwa, kuko nahama ishengero ry'Imana.
46015010	Ariko ubuntu bw'Imana ni bwo bwatumye mba uko ndi, kandi ubuntu bwayo nagiriwe ntibwabaye ubwo ubusa, ariko natamye kurusha bose; ariko si jewe yamara ni ubuntu bw'Imana bwari kumwe nanje.
46015011	Nuko ari jewe ari abo, ivyo ni vyo tubabarira, namwe ni vyo mwizeye.
46015012	Ariko, ko Kristo avugwa ko yazutse mu bapfuye, bamwe muri mwebwe bavuga bate yuko ata wuzuka?
46015013	Asangwa ata wuzuka, na Kristo ntarakazuka.
46015014	Kandi asangwa Kristo atazutse, ivyo twigisha n'ivyo ubusa, n'ukwizera kwanyu n'uko ubusa.
46015015	Natwe twoba tubonetse ko turi abashingira Imana intahe y'ikinyoma, kuko twayishingiye intahe yuko yazuye Kristo, uwo itazuye, namba abapfuye batazuka.
46015016	Asangwa abapfuye batazuka na Kristo ntarakazuka.
46015017	Ariko asangwa Kristo atazutse, ukwizera kwanyu ni uko ubusa, muracari mu vyaha vyanyu.
46015018	Kandi asangwa bimeze bityo, n'abasinziririye muri Kristo barayogeye.
46015019	Asangwa muri ubu bugingo bwonyene ari ho twizigirira Kristo, turusha abandi bantu bose kuba abagowe.
46015020	Ariko noneho Kristo yarazutse mu bapfuye, ni we yashurije abasinziriye.
46015021	Kuko nk'uko urupfu rwazanywe n'umuntu, n'ukuzuka kw'abapfuye kwazanywe n'umuntu.
46015022	Nk'uko Adamu yandukije bose gupfa, ni ko muri Kristo bose bazohindurwa bazima.
46015023	Ariko umuntu wese mu mwanya wiwe; arabatangurira, maze aba Kristo bazobonerwa bazuke, aho azozira.
46015024	Iherezo rizoca rishika, aho azoshikiriza Imana ubwami, ni yo Data wa twese, ni yamara gukuraho ubukuru bwose, n'ububasha bwose, n'ubushobozi bwose.
46015025	Kuko ategerezwa guhangama ku butware bwiwe gushitsa aho azoshirira abansi biwe bose musi y'ibirenge vyiwe.
46015026	Urupfu ni we mumenja w'imperera azoherengetezwa.
46015027	Kuko handitswe, ngo Yamuhaye kuganza vyose, ibishira musi y'ibirenge vyiwe. Ariko ko ivuga iti: "Ahawe kuganza vyose;" biraboneka yuko Iyamuhaye kuganza vyose itabiharurwamwo.
46015028	Ariko ni yamara gushikirizwa inganji ya vyose, ni ho n'Umwana ubwiwe azoganzwa n'Iyamuhaye inganji ya vyose, ngo Imana ibe vyose muri vyose.
46015029	Canke ababatizwa mu gishingo c'abapfuye bazobamarira iki? Asangwa abapfuye batazurwa na mba, ni igiki gituma bababatirizwa?
46015030	Natwe Ni igiki gituma twama turi mw'irinde?
46015031	Uko bukeye ndapfa, indahiro ndahiye ni mwebwe vyirato vyanje, ivyo mfise muri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu.
46015032	Asangwa narwaniye n'ibikoko muri Efeso, ndi mu buryo bw' abantu gusa, bimarira iki? Namba abapfuye batazurwa, ni twirire, twinywere, kuko ejo tuzopfa.
46015033	Ntimuzimire; kubana n'ababi kwonona ingeso nziza.
46015034	Mwisubireko, mugororoke, ntimukore ivyaha; kuko bamwe batazi Imana. Ndabivugiye kubatetereza.
46015035	Ariko umuntu yobaza ati: "Abapfuye bazurwa bate, kandi baza bafise umubiri ki?"
46015036	Wa gipfu we, ico ubiba ntikimera kitabanje gupfa.
46015037	Kandi ico ubiba, ntubiba umutumba uzohaba, ariko ubiba akabuto uko kari, ari nk'ako ingano, canke akandi kose.
46015038	Ariko Imana igaha umutumba, nk'uko yagomvye, kandi akabuto kose igaha umutumba wako ukwako.
46015039	Inyama zose si zimwe; izo abantu ziri ukwazo, n'izo ibikoko ziri ukwazo, n'izo inyoni n'ibisiga ziri ukwazo, n'izo ifi ziri ukwazo.
46015040	Kandi hari imitumba yo kw'ijuru n'imitumba yo kw'isi. Ariko ubwiza bw'iyo kw'ijuru buri ukwabwo; n'ubwo iyo kw'isi buri ukwabwo.
46015041	Ubwiza bw'izuba buri ukwabwo, n'ubwiza bw'ukwezi buri ukwabwo, n'ubwiza bw'inyenyeri buri ukwabwo: kandi inyenyeri ntinganya ubwiza n'iyindi nyenyeri.
46015042	N'ukuzuka kw 'abapfuye ni nk'uko. Habibwa ikibora, hazurwa igitabora.
46015043	Habibwa igikengerwa, hazurwa ico icubahiro. Habibwa ikinyantege nke hazurwa ico inkomezi.
46015044	Habibwa umubiri w'inyama, hazurwa umubiri w'impwemu. Asangwa hariho umubiri w'inyama hariho kandi n'uwo impwemu.
46015045	Kandi uko ni ko handitswe, ngo umuntu wa mbere Adamu yabaye uwufise ubugingo; Adamu wo hanyuma yabaye impwemu itanga ubugingo.
46015046	Ariko ico impwemu si co kibanza, yamara ico inyama ni co kibanza, kigaherukirwa n'ico impwemu.
46015047	Umuntu wa mbere yandurutse mw'ivu, ni uwo umukungugu. Umuntu wa kabiri yandurutse mw'ijuru.
46015048	Nk'uko uwo umukungugu ari, ni ko n'abo umukungugu bandi bari. Nk'uko uwo ijuru ari, ni ko n'abo ijuru bandi bari.
46015049	Kandi nk'uko twambaye ishusho y'uwo umukungugu, ni ko tuzokwambara n'ishusho y'uwo ijuru.
46015050	Ariko bavukanyi, ico mvuga, yuko abo inyama n'amaraso badashobora kuragwa ubwami bw' Imana, kandi ibibora bitaragwa ibitabora.
46015051	Ehe, ndababarira akabanga: ntituzosinzira twese, ariko twese tuzohindurwa,
46015052	mu kanya gato, mu kanya nk'ako gukubita ingohe, aho inzumbeti y'iherezo izovugira. Kuko inzumbeti izovuga, abapfuye bakazurwa batagishobora kubora, natwe tuzohindurwa.
46015053	Kuko uwu mubiri ubora ukwiye kuzokwambara ukutabora, kandi uwu mubiri upfa ukwiye kuzokwambara ukudapfa.
46015054	Ariko, uwu ubora ni wamara kwambara ukutabora, n'uwu upfa ni wamara kwambara ukudapfa, ni ho hazoshika rya jambo ryanditswe, ngo urupfu rumizwe n'intsinzi.
46015055	Wa rupfu we, intsinzi yawe iri hehe? Wa rupfu we, uruboyi rwawe ruri hehe?
46015056	Ivyaha ni vyo ruboyi rw'urupfu, kandi ubushobozi bw'ivyaha n'ivyagezwe.
46015057	Ariko Imana ishimwe, iduha gutsinda kubwo Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo.
46015058	Nuko bavukanyi banje nkunda, mukomere ntimunyiganyige, murushirize imisi yose gukora ibikorwa vy'Umwami wacu, kuko muzi yuko ubutame bwanyu atari ubwo ubusa mu Mwami.
46016001	Nuko ku vyo gukoranya ibitabara abera, nk'uko nageze amashengero y'i Galatiya, abe ari ko namwe mukora.
46016002	Ku wa mbere wose w'imisi indwi, umuntu wese muri mwebwe abike i we ibimuhaye uburyo, nk'uko atunze, kugira ngo aho nzozira ntihabe ari ho amashikanwa azokoranirizwa.
46016003	Kandi aho nzoshikira, abo muzoshima, nzobatuma ndabahaye amakete, kugira ngo bajane ivyo ikigongwe canyu i Yerusalemu.
46016004	Kandi namba nzoba nkwiye kugenda nanje, tuzojana Pahulo avuga ko ategekanya kuzoja i Korinto
46016005	Ariko nzoza i wanyu, ni namara guca i Makedoniya; kuko nzorinda gucayo.
46016006	Ariko kumbure nzomarana namwe imisi, canke nzomara n'agatasi, kugira ngo mumperekeze, munsezere neza aho nzoja hose.
46016007	Singomba ko tubonana none ndabakubise rurabwe, ariko nizigira kuzomarana namwe imisi, Umwami wacu ni yankundira.
46016008	Ariko nzotebera muri Efeso gushitsa kuri Pentekote;
46016009	kuko nugururiwe urugi runini ruja mu bikorwa bikomeye, kandi abansi bakaba benshi.
46016010	Timoteyo ni yaramuka aje i wanyu, muze mumubabare kugira ngo abane namwe ata bwoba; kuko akora igikorwa c'Umwami wacu nkanje.
46016011	Nuko ntihazogire uwumukengera, ariko muzomuherekeze mumusezere amahoro, azonsange ino, kuko niteze ko azozanana n'abavukanyi.
46016012	Ariko ivyo Apolo umuvukanyi, naramwinginze cane ngo aze i wanyu, azozanane n'abo bavukanyi; ntiyakunda na gatoya kuza none, ariko azoza, ni yabona uburyo.
46016013	Mwame mugavye, mushikame mu kwizera, mube abagabo, mugire inkomezi.
46016014	Ivyo mukora vyose mubikorane urukundo.
46016015	Nuko ndabinginze, bavukanyi, murazi abo kwa Stefana, ko ari bo batanguye mu Banyakaya, kandi ko ari bo bitangiye gukorera abera.
46016016	Nuko namwe mugamburukire abameze batyo, n'uwundi wese afatanije n'abandi muri ico gikorwa, agatama.
46016017	Biranezereye ko Stefana na Forutunato na Akayiko baje; bamaze inkumbu nari ndabafitiye,
46016018	kuko bahembuye umutima wanje, bo n'uwanyu; mwame mwibuka abameze batyo.
46016019	Abo mu mashengero yo muri Asiya barabaganutsa. Akwila na Purisikila barabaganutsa cane mu Mwami wacu, bo n'ishengero ryo mu nzu yabo.
46016020	Abavukanyi bose barabaganutsa. Muramukanishe kugumbirana kwera.
46016021	Uku ni kwo gutasha kwanje Pahulo, kwanditswe n'ukuboko kwanje.
46016022	Ni hagira umuntu adakunda Umwami wacu, arakavumwa. Maran ata.
46016023	Ubuntu bw'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane namwe.
46016024	Urukundo rwanje rubane namwe mwese muri Kristo Yesu. Amina.
47001001	Jewe Pahulo, intumwa ya Kristo Yesu, nk'uko Imana yagomvye, na Timoteyo umuvukanyi, turabandikiye abo mw'ishengero ry'Imana ry'i Korinto, n'abera bose bari muri Akaya hose.
47001002	Ubuntu n'amahoro biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo bubabemwo.
47001003	Imana y'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ari yo Se, Data wa twese w'imbabazi, kandi Imana yirura imibabaro yose iragahezagirwa,
47001004	itwirura mu marushwa yacu yose, kugira ngo natwe tubone uko twirura imibabaro abari mu marushwa yose, tuyibiruza uko natwe twiruwe n'Imana.
47001005	Nk'uko ivyo Kristo yababajwe vyarushirije kutuzako, ni ko n'ukwirurwa kwacu kwarushirije kugwizwa na Kristo.
47001006	Iyo tubabazwa, kuba ari ukugira ngo bibazanire ukwirurwa, bo n'agakiza; kandi iyo twirurwa, kuba ari ukugira ngo bibazanire ukwirurwa nyene, guserukira mu kwihanganira imibabaro imwe n'iyo natwe tubabazwa.
47001007	Kandi ivyo tubazigako birashikamye, kuko tuzi yuko, ko dusangiye iyo mibabaro, dusangiye n'ukuyirurwa.
47001008	Kuko bavukanyi, tutagomba yuko mutamenya amarushwa yatubayeko muri Asiya, ko twaremerewe cane, biruta uko dushobora, bigatuma twihebura ko tutagikiza amagara yacu.
47001009	Kandi tumenyeshwa mu mitima yuko duciriweko iteka ryo gupfa, kugira ngo ntitwiyizigire ubwacu, ariko twizigire Imana izura abapfuye.
47001010	Yadukijije urupfu rukomeye rutyo, kandi izodukiza; ni yo twizigira yuko izokwama irudukiza,
47001011	namwe muhuje imitima yo kudufasha mudusengera, ngo ingabire twaheshejwe na benshi, benshi bayishimire Imana ku bwacu.
47001012	Kuko ukwirata kwacu ari uku, kandi ijwi ryo mu mitima yacu rirabishingira intahe; ingeso twagirira mw'isi, kandi canecane muri mwebwe, zari ukwera, n'imitima itagira ubugunge iva ku Mana, atari mu bwenge bw' abantu, ariko mu buntu bw'Imana.
47001013	Kuko ata bindi tubandikira, atari ivyo nyene musoma kandi mwemera, kandi nishimiye ko muzovyemera gushitsa ko iherezo,
47001014	nk'uko mwatwemeye agace, yuko turi ivyirato vyanyu, nk'uko namwe muzoba ivyacu ku musi w'Umwami wacu Yesu.
47001015	Kandi nk'uko nizigiye ivyo, nagira ngo nzobanza kuza i wanyu, ngo muhabwe ubuntu ubugira kabiri,
47001016	no kubacako nja i Makedoniya, nkagaruka i wanyu mvuye i Makedoniya, ngo mumperekeze, munsezere neza nja i Yudaya.
47001017	Nuko aho nagomba gukora ntyo, mbega narahindagurika? Canke ivyo ngabira, ndabigabira mbwirijwe n'akameremere kanje, ngo niburanye nti: "Ego, ego," maze nti: "Oya, oya?"
47001018	Ariko nk'uko Imana ari iyo kwizerwa, ijambo tubabarira ntituvuga ngo ego, maze ngo oya.
47001019	Umwana w'Imana Yesu Kristo, umwe twabigisha ivyiwe, twe na Siluwano na Timoteyo, ntiyari ego, kandi ngo abe oya; ariko muri we harimwo ego me.
47001020	Ivyo Imana yasezeranye uko bingana, muri we ni ho Ego me riri; ni co gituma ari we adutera kuvuga ngo Amina, ngo Imana ishimishwe natwe.
47001021	Imana ni yo idukomezanya namwe muri Kristo, kandi ni yo yaturobanuje amavuta.
47001022	Kandi ni yo yadushizeko ikimenyetso, itugwatiriza Mpwemu wayo mu mitima yacu.
47001023	Ariko Imana ni yo ntanzeko icabona ku bugingo bwanje, icatumye ntongera kuza i Korinto, kwari ukwanka kubababaza.
47001024	Si uko tuganza ukwizera kwanyu, ariko dukorana namwe mu bibungura umunezero; kuko ukwizera ari kwo muhagazemwo.
47002001	Ariko nagabiye mu mutima kutazogaruka i wanyu nzanye umubabaro.
47002002	Ni nabatera umubabaro, uwuzonezereza ni nde? Si uwo nteye umubabaro nyene?
47002003	Kandi nandikiye ivyo, kugira ngo aho nzozira sinterwe umubabaro n'abari bakwiye kunezereza; kuko ndabizigira mwese yuko umunezero wanje ari wo wanyu mwese.
47002004	Nabandikiye mfise intuntu nyinshi, umutima wamvuyemwo, ndira amarira menshi; ntikwari ukugira ngo muterwe umubabaro mwebwe, ariko kwari ukugira ngo mumenye urukundo ndushiriza kubagirira.
47002005	Ariko namba hari umuntu ateye umubabaro, si jewe awuteye, ariko ni mwebwe awuteye mwese--singomba kubababaza cane, ariko bamwe ni agace.
47002006	Ico gihano abenshi bamuhanye, kiramaze k'uwumeze atyo.
47002007	None ni co gituma mukwiye canecane kumuharira, no kumwirura, ngo uwumeze atyo ntarengerwe n'umubabaro usagutse.
47002008	Nuko ndabinginga mumukomezeko urukundo.
47002009	Kuko icanteye kubandikira ari iki: kwari ukugira ngo ndabageze, menye uko muri, ko munyumvira muri vyose.
47002010	Ariko uwo muribuharire wese, nanje ndamuharira; kuko nanje ico mpariye, namba hari ico mparira, ndagihariye ku bwanyu, mu maso ya Kristo,
47002011	kugira ngo Satani ntaronke ico adutsindisha, kuko tutayobewe imigabo yiwe.
47002012	Ariko aho naja i Tirowa, njanywe n'ubutumwa bwiza bwa Kristo, ngasanga nugururiwe urugi mu Mwami wacu;
47002013	nabuze uko nduhuka mu mutima wanje, kuko ntasanzeyo Tito umuvukanyi wanje. Nuko narabasezeye, nja i Makedoniya.
47002014	Ariko Imana ishimwe, yama itujana nk'abafashwe mpiri muri Kristo, idutera kwerekana ubumote bwo kumumenyekanisha ahantu hose.
47002015	Kuko turi ubumote bwiza bwa Kristo ku Mana, hagati y'abariko barakira n'abariko barahona.
47002016	Kuri abo turi agacuku k'urupfu kazana urupfu, kuri ba bandi turi ubumote bw'ubugingo buzana ubugingo. kandi ivyo ni nde abishobora?
47002017	Kuko tutari nka bamwe benshi, bacururisha ijambo ry'Imana, ariko tuvuga nk'abatagira ubugunge, bavuga ibiva ku Mana, ni ko tuvuga muri Kristo, imbere y'Imana.
47003001	Mbega dutanguye kwongera kwishimagiza? Canke turinda amakete yo kudushimagiza, mwandikiwe canke mwanditse, nk'uko bamwe bandi bagomba?
47003002	Ni mwebwe cete cacu, canditswe ku mitima yacu, ico abantu bose bamenya bagasoma.
47003003	Kuko muboneka ko muri ikete Kristo yatwandikishije, nk'uko igikorwa cacu kiri; kitandikishijwe irangi, ariko candikishijwe Mpwemu w' Imana nzima; kitanditswe ku bisate vy'amabuye, ariko canditswe ku bisate ni vyo mitima y'inyama.
47003004	Uko ni ko twizigira Imana ku bwa Kristo.
47003005	Si uko dushobora ubwacu kwiyumvira ikintu cose nk'aho ari twebwe candurutseko, ariko dushobozwa n'Imana;
47003006	ni yo yadushoboje kuba abakozi b'isezerano rishasha, yamara si abakozi b'ivyandikishijwe indome, ariko ni abo impwemu; kuko ivyandikishijwe inyuguti vyicisha, ariko impwemu ihesha ubugingo.
47003007	Yamara ubwo bugabuzi bwandikishijwe indome zikorogoshowe mu mabuye bwaganzwa n'urupfu, naho bwari bwazananye n'ubwiza. Ariko ubwo bwiza, naho bwagenda bushira, bwatumye Abisirayeli badashobora gutumbera mu maso ha Mose.
47003008	None ko vyabaye bityo, ubugabuzi buganzwa na Mpwemu ntiburushiriza cane kuzanana n'ubwiza?
47003009	Ubugabuzi bwo gutsindwa ko ari ubwiza, ubugabuzi bwo kugororoka burushiriza kugira ubwiza bw'akaburarugero.
47003010	Mbere icari gisanganywe ubwiza nta bwiza kigifise, kuko haje ubwiza bukirengeye.
47003011	Igishira ko cari n'ubwiza, igihoraho kirushiriza cane kugira ubwiza.
47003012	Nuko ko dufise icizigiro kingana gityo, tuvuga tutabobotereza na gatoya.
47003013	Ntidusa na Mose, yitwikira mu maso, kugira ngo abisirayeli ntibahange amaso iherezo ry'ubwariko buraherengetera.
47003014	Ariko imitima yabo irakomantara. Kuko gushitsa n'ubu, ca citwikiro kikiriho mu gisomwa c'isezerano rya kera, ntikirakurwaho, kuko muri Kristo ari ho giherera.
47003015	Ariko gushitsa n'ubu, ivya Mose iyo bisomwa ico citwikiro kiba ku mitima yabo.
47003016	Yamara, iyo umuntu ahindukiriye Umwami, ico citwikiro gica gikurwaho.
47003017	Ariko uwo Mwami ni we Mpwemu; kandi aho Mpwemu w'Uhoraho ari, ni ho haba umwidegemvyo.
47003018	Tweho twese, ko tutitwikiriye mu maso, tukerekana nk'icirore ubwiza bw'Umwami, turahinduka, tugashushanywa n'iyo shusho, tukava mu bwiza tukaja mu bundi, nk'abahindurwa n'Umwami, ari we Mpwemu.
47004001	Ni co gituma tutihebura, kuko dufise ubwo busuku, nk'uko twagiriwe ikigongwe.
47004002	Twanse ibiteye isoni bikorerwa mu mpisho, ntitugenda mu bugunge, ntidufudika ijambo ry'Imana, ariko kwerekana ukuri ni kwo twishimagirisha mu maso y'Imana ku mutima w'umuntu wese.
47004003	Ariko namba ubutumwa bwiza twahawe butwikirwa, butwikirirwa abahona,
47004004	ni bo batizera, bamwe ikigirwamana c'iki gihe cahumye imitima, ngo umuco w'ubutumwa bw'ubwiza bwa Kristo ntubakire, ni we shusho y'Imana.
47004005	Kuko tutigisha abantu ivyacu, ariko tubigisha ivya Kristo Yesu ko ari we Mwami, natwe yuko turi abashumba banyu ku bwa Yesu.
47004006	Imana, imwe yavuze ngo umuco wake, uvuye mu mwiza, ni yo yakiye mu mitima yacu, kwerekana umuco, ni wo kumenya ubwiza bw'Imana buri mu maso ha Yesu Kristo.
47004007	Ariko dufise ubwo butunzi mu nzavya z'ibumba, ngo ubushobozi buhebuje bube ubwo Imana, butavuye kuri twebwe.
47004008	Dusugerezwa impande zose, ariko ntidushika mu mpatane; turazazanirwa, ariko ntituranduka umutima;
47004009	turahamwa, ariko ntiduhebwa; dukubitwa hasi, ariko ntitugwaho.
47004010	Imisi yose tugendana mu mubiri urupfu rwa Yesu, ngo ubugingo bwa Yesu na bwo buserukire mu mubiri wacu.
47004011	Kuko twebwe abariho, na ntaryo dutangwa ngo dupfe baduhora Yesu, ngo ubugingo bwa Yesu na bwo buserukire mu mubiri wacu uzopfa.
47004012	Nuko rero urupfu rudukoreramwo, ariko ubugingo bubakoreramwo.
47004013	Ariko ko dufise uwo mutima wizera, uboneka mu vyanditswe, ngo nizeye, ni co catumye mvuga; natwe nyene turizera, ni co gituma tuvuga.
47004014	Kuko tuzi yuko iyazuye Umwami Yesu, natwe izotuzurana na Yesu, kandi izomudushira, twe namwe.
47004015	Kuko ivyo vyose biba ku bwanyu, kugira ngo ubuntu bw'Imana bwongeranishwe n'ukugwira kw' abantu, bugwize ishimwe, ngo ritere Imana icubahiro.
47004016	Ni co gituma tutihebura; ariko, naho umuntu wacu wo ku rukoba ariko arabora, umuntu wacu w'imbere yama ahinduka musha uko bukeye.
47004017	Kuko amarushwa yacu ahwahutse y' akanya ka none yiyongeranije cane kudushikiriza ubwiza buremereye bw'ibihe bidashira.
47004018	Natwe ntituraba ku biboneka, ariko turaba ku bitaboneka; kuko ibiboneka ari ivyo igihe gito, ariko ibitaboneka bikaba ivyo ibihe bidashira.
47005001	Turazi yuko inzu y'urusago yacu yo kw'isi ni yaramuka isambuwe, dufise inyubako iva ku Mana, inzu itubatswe n'amaboko, itazoshira yo mw'ijuru.
47005002	Kuko tunihira muri uru rusago, twifuza kurwambikirwako inzu yacu izova mw'ijuru,
47005003	namba tuyambaye tutazosangwa twambaye ubusa.
47005004	Kuko twebwe abari muri uru rusago tuniha turemerewe, si uko tugomba kwamburwa, ariko tugomba kwambikirwa kuri rwo, ngo igipfa kimirwe n'ubugingo.
47005005	Kandi iyaturoranije ku bwo ico nyene n'Imana, iyatugwatirije Mpwemu.
47005006	Ni co gituma na ntaryo turinda mu mutima, kandi tumenya yuko iyo turi i wacu mu mubiri tuba tugerereye kure y'Umwami wacu— "
47005007	kuko tugenda turongorwa n'ukwizera, ntiturongorwa n'ivyo tubona--
47005008	ego me turinda mu mutima, kandi ico turushiriza gukunda ngiki: ni ukugerera kure y'umubiri, tukaba i wacu ku Mwami wacu.
47005009	Kandi ni co gituma tugira umwete wo kumunezereza, iyo turi i wacu mu mubiri, canke iyo tugerereye kure y'umubiri.
47005010	Kuko twese tutazobura kugaragarizwa imbere y'intebe y'imanza ya Kristo, kugira ngo umuntu wese ahabwe ibihwanye n'ico yakoze akiri mu mubiri, ari ciza ari kibi.
47005011	Nuko kuko tuzi ingene ukwubaha Umwami wacu kumeze, twemeza abantu, ariko Imana turayigaragarira kandi rero nizigiye yuko tugaragarira n'imitima yanyu.
47005012	Ntitwongera kubishimagizako, ariko tubaha inyanduruko y'ingene mwokwirata ku bwacu, kugira ngo mubone ivyo mwokwishura abirata ivyo ku rukoba, batirata ivyo mu mutima.
47005013	Namba dusaze, dusaze ivyo Imana; namba dufise ubwenge, ni mwebwe dukorera."
47005014	Kuko urukundo rwa Kristo rutugobera, kandi ico tuzi tudakekeranya ni uko umwe yapfiriye bose, nuko rero bose barapfuye.
47005015	Kandi icatumye apfira bose kwari ukugira ngo abariho babeho batacinezereza, ariko babeho banezereza uwabapfiriye, akabazukira.
47005016	Ni co gituma kuva ubu tutakigira uwo tumenya ku vyo ku rukoba; naho twari tuzi Kristo mu vyo umubiri, ariko noneho ntitukimumenya dutyo.
47005017	Nuko rero umuntu wese iyo ari muri Kristo, aba ari icaremwe gishasha; ivya kera biba bihise, vyose biba bibaye bishasha.
47005018	Ariko ivyo vyose biva ku Mana, yatwiyujujeko kubwa Kristo, ikaduha igikorwa c'ukunywanisha,
47005019	ni kwo kuvuga yuko Imana yari muri Kristo yiyuzuza n'abari mw'isi, ntiyabaharurako ibicumuro vyabo, kandi yatubikije ijambo ry'umwuzuzo.
47005020	Ni co gituma turi intumwa mu gishingo ca Kristo, Imana isa n'iyibaduhanurisha. Turabahanura mu gishingo ca Kristo, mwuzure n'Imana.
47005021	Umwe atigeze kumenya icaha, Imana yamuhinduye icaha ku bwacu, kugira ngo tumuhindukiriremwo ukugororoka kw'Imana.
47006001	Kandi ko dukorana na yo, turabinginga, ntimuherwe ubuntu bw'Imana ngo bubapfeko.
47006002	Kuko yavuze ati: "Mu gihe co kwemererwamwo ndakwumvise, No ku musi wo gukirizwako ndagutabaye. Ehe ubu ni igihe co kwemererwamwo, ehe ubu ni umusi wo gukirizwako."
47006003	Kandi ntitugira ico tuzana gitsitaza mu kintu na kimwe, kugira ngo kugabura ivyo Imana kwacu ntikugawe.
47006004	Ariko twishimagiza muri vyose nk' abakozi b'Imana, twihangana cane mu marushwa, mu mibabaro, mu vyago,
47006005	mu bimoko, mu mabohero, mu migumuko, mu butame, mu kurara maso, mu kwirirwa ubusa,
47006006	mu kugira umutima utanduye, mu kugira ubwenge, mu kutarambirwa, mu kuba inda nziza, muri Mpwemu Yera, mu rukundo rutari uruheyiheyi,
47006007	mw'ijambo ry'ukuri, mu bushobozi bw'Imana, dufise ibirwanisho vy'ukugororoka vyo mu kuryo n'ivyo mu kubamfu;
47006008	mu cubahiro no mu gakengerwe, mu mugayo no mw'ishimwe. Twiyumvirwa nk'abanyabinyoma, ariko turi abanyakuri.
47006009	Twiyumvirwa nk'abatamenyekana, ariko turi ba rurangiranwa. Tuboneka nk'abagira bapfe, ariko Raba, turi bazima. Tuboneka nk'abahanwa, ariko ntitwicwa.
47006010	Tuboneka nk'abababara, ariko tunezerwa imisi yose. Tuboneka nk'aboro, ariko dutungisha benshi. Tuboneka nk'abatagira ico batunze, yamara dutunze vyose.
47006011	Akanwa kacu karabasesekariye, yemwe Bakorinto, umutima wacu uragutse.
47006012	Ntimwagiwe muri twebwe, yamara mwagiwe mu mitima yanyu.
47006013	Nuko ndababwira nk'abana banje, namwe ni mwaguke, mwishure nk'uko mwagiriwe.
47006014	Ntimwifatanye n'abatizera, kandi ata co musangiye. Ukugororoka n'ukugabitanya bifatana bite? Canke umuco n'umwiza bifatanya bite?
47006015	Kandi Kristo ahuriye hehe na Beliyari? Canke uwizera n'uwutizera basangiye iki?
47006016	Kandi urusengero rw'Imana ruhuza rute n'ibigirwamana? Kuko twebwe turi urusengero rw'Imana nzima; nk'uko Imana yavuze iti: "Nzobagereramwo, nzobagenderamwo, Mbe Imana yabo, na bo babe abantu banje."
47006017	Nuko muve hagati ya ba bandi, Mubitandukanyeko, ni ko Uhoraho avuze, Kandi ntimugakore ku kintu gihumanya na kimwe; Nanje nzobakira.
47006018	Kandi nzobabera So, Namwe muzombera abahungu n'abakobwa, Ni ko Uhoraho ashobora vyose avuze.
47007001	Nuko bakundwa, ko dufise ivyo vyasezeranywe, twiyuhagire ubuhumane bwose bw'umubiri n'ubwo umutima, kuba abera tugushikishe kwubaha Imana.
47007002	Muduhe ikibanza mu mitima yanyu; nta we twagiriye nabi, nta we twononye, nta we twagunze.
47007003	Sindabivugiye kubagaya; kuko maze kuvuga yuko muri mu mitima yacu, ngo dupfane kandi ngo tubaneho.
47007004	Ndababwira ndabizigiye cane, ndabiratana. Nuzuye ihumure, ndushiriza kunezerwa mu marushwa yacu yose.
47007005	Hamwe twaja i Makedoniya umubiri wacu ntiwaribwatenzukirwe na gatoya, kuko twababajwe uburyo bwose; inyuma hari intambara, imbere hari ubwoba. "
47007006	Ariko Imana ihumuriza abicisha bugufi yaduhumurishije ukuza kwa Tito.
47007007	Kandi si ukuza kwiwe kwonyene, ariko kandi ni uguhumurizwa mwamuhumurije namwe, n'uko yatwiganiye inkumbu zanyu mwangiriye, n'amarira yanyu, n'ishaka mwandwanira, ni co catumye ndushiriza kunezerwa.
47007008	Naho nabateje umubabaro ca cete canje, sinicuza, naho nari naricujije; kuko ndabonye yuko ico cete cabateye umubabaro, naho mwawugize igihe gito gusa;
47007009	noneho ndanezerewe; sinejerejwe n'uko mwagize umubabaro, ariko n'uko uwo mubabaro wabateye kwihana. Kuko mwagize umubabaro mu buryo bw' Imana, kugira ngo ntihagire ico mubura ku bwacu.
47007010	Umubabaro wo mu buryo bw'Imana utera ukwihana kuticuzwa, kuzana agakiza; ariko umubabaro wo mu buryo bw'isi utera urupfu.
47007011	Ntimubona uwo mubabaro wo mu buryo bw'Imana, ukuntu wabateye umwete mwinshi utyo? Kandi ko wabateye no kwiregura, guhigimanga, gutinya, inkumbu, ishaka no guhana? Muri vyose mwiyerekanye ko mwejejwe muri ivyo.
47007012	Nuko naho nabandikiye, ivyanyandikishije si ivyo uwagize nabi, kandi si ivyo uwagiriwe nabi, ariko ni ukugira ngo umwete mutugirira werekanirwe hagati yanyu mu maso y'Imana.
47007013	Ni co catumye duhumurizwa. Kandi muri ukwo guhumurizwa turushiriza guterwa umunezero n'umunezero wa Tito, kuko umutima wiwe waruhuwe namwe mwese.
