47007014	Namba hari icanteye ko ndabirata ndabaratira Tito, ntivyantetereje; ariko nk'uko twababwiye vyose ukuri, ni ko ni ukwirata kwacu, twaratiye Tito, kwabonetse ko ari ukwo ukuri.
47007015	Kandi umutima wiwe urushiriza kubagirira igishika, uko yibutse ingene mwanyumviye mwese, n'ingene mwamwakiriye mutinya, muhinda agashitsi.
47007016	Nezerewe yuko mfise umutima uremye ku bwo ivyanyu vyose.
47008001	Bavukanyi, turabamenyesha ubuntu bw'Imana amashengero y'i Makedoniya yagiriwe.
47008002	Bakigeragezwa n'amarushwa menshi, umunezero wabo w'akaburarugero, n'ubworo bwabo butagira iyo buherwa, vyarushirije kuzana ubutunzi bw'ivyo ubuntu bwabo.
47008003	Ku bwabo baratanze nk'uko bashoboye, ndabibashingira intahe, kandi bararushije n'ivyo bashoboye,
47008004	badusaba binginga cane kubatera iteka kugira ngo bafatanye n'abagaburira abera.
47008005	Kandi si nk'uko twabiziga gusa, ariko babanje kwitanga biha Umwami wacu, natwe nyene baratwiha, nk'uko Imana yagomvye.
47008006	Ni co catumye twinginga Tito, ngo asozere ico gikorwa c'ugutabara no muri mwebwe, nk'uko yagitanguye kera.
47008007	Ariko nk'uko murushiriza kugira vyose --ukwizera, n'amajambo, ubwenge, umwete mwinshi n'urukundo mudukunda--ni murushirize no kugira ubwo buntu na bwo.
47008008	Sindabivugiye kubategeka, ariko ndabivugiye kugeza urukundo rwanyu ko ari urwo ukuri, ndarugeragereshe umwete w'abandi.
47008009	Kuko muzi ubuntu bw'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, yuko naho yari umutunzi, yahindutse umworo ku bwanyu, kugira ngo ubworo bwiwe bubatungishe.
47008010	Kandi ivyo ndababwiye kuri ivyo ni ukubagisha inama; kuko bibabereye, abatanguriye abandi uhereye ku mwaka ushize, si ukubikora gusa, ariko no kubikunda.
47008011	Nuko rero mushitse no kubikora, kugira ngo nk'uko mwakunze kuvyemera, mube ari ko mubishitsa ku vyo mufise.
47008012	Kuko iyo hari umutima ukunze, wemerwa ku vyo umuntu afise, si ku vyo adafise.
47008013	Simvuze ntyo kugira ngo abandi boroherwe, namwe ngo mugorwe.
47008014	Ariko ni ukugira ngo munganye, ngo ibibasagutseko muri iki gihe bibamare ubukene, kandi ngo ibizobabera umusesekara na bo bizobamare ubukene bwanyu, munganye.
47008015	Nk'uko handitswe, ngo uwegeranije vyinshi asanga ata co asesekaje; uwegeranije bike asanga ata co akehaniwe.
47008016	Ariko Imana ishimwe, ishize mu mutima wa Tito kubagirira umwete nk'uwo ndabagirira.
47008017	Kuko yemeye inama yacu, kandi kuko agize umwete mwinshi, aje i wanyu bivuye ku mutima.
47008018	Kandi hamwe n'uwo turungitse n'umuvukanyi ngo bazanane, ishimwe ryiwe ryo ku vyo ubutumwa bwiza ryamamaye mu mashengero yose.
47008019	Kandi si co gusa, ariko na kare uwo ni we yatoranijwe n'amashengero kwama ajana natwe kubwo ico gikorwa c'ugutabara, ubwo tugabura ngo Umwami wacu ashimishwe, kandi ngo twerekane umutima wacu ko ubikunze
47008020	Kuko ico twirinda ari iki, ari ico umuntu yotugaya kubwo izi ngabire nyinshi tugabura.
47008021	Tubabaye gukora ivyiza, si mu maso y' Umwami wacu gusa, ariko no mu maso y'abantu.
47008022	Kandi abo tubarungikanye n'uwo muvukanyi twagejeje kenshi, akaboneka ko ari umunyamwete muri vyinshi, ariko none arushiriza kugira umwete, kuko abizigira cane.
47008023	Ivya Tito, ni we dufatanije igikorwa, kandi n'umuvukanyi wanje dukorana ivyanyu; kandi ivyo abo bavukanyi, n'intumwa z'amashengero, kandi n'icubahiro ca Kristo.
47008024	Nuko mubereke ivyerekana urukundo rwanyu mu maso y'amashengero, kandi yuko twari dufise inyanduruko yo kubirata.
47009001	Ivyo ukugaburira abera sindinda kubibandikira.
47009002	Kuko nzi umutima ukunze wanyu, ni wo nirata mu Banyamakedoniya yuko muwufise, mvuga yuko Abanyakaya bari basanzwe biteguye, uhereye mu mwaka ushize, kandi gushishikara kwanyu kwateye abenshi umwete.
47009003	Kandi ndungitse abo bavukanyi kugira ngo ukubirata kwacu ntikuzopfe ubusa muri ivyo; kugira ngo muzobe mwiteguye nk'uko nababwiye,
47009004	twebwe (sinovuga mwebwe) ntituzomaramazwe n'ivyo twari twizigiye, namba Abanyamakedoniya bamwe bazozanana nanje bagasanga mutiteguye.
47009005	Ni co gitumye niyumviriye yuko nkwiye kwinginga abo bavukanyi kunyitangira imbere mu kuza i wanyu, ngo babanze gutunganya ivyo ubuntu mwasezeranye kera, bibe biteguwe nk'ivyo ugutabara hatarimwo ubwimanyi.
47009006	Ariko ico mvuga ngiki, ngo Ubiba nke, azokwimbura bike, ubiba nyinshi azokwimbura vyinshi.
47009007	Umuntu wese atange nk'uko abigabiye mu mutima wiwe, atababaye canke atagoberewe, kuko Imana ikunda utanga anezerewe.
47009008	Kandi Imana ishobora kubasazako ubuntu bwose, kugira ngo murushirize gukora ivyiza vyose, mufise ibibahagije muri vyose.
47009009	Nk'uko handitswe, ngo Yatanze isabagire, yahaye abakene, Ukugororoka kwiwe kwamaho ibihe bidashira.
47009010	Kandi Iha umubivyi imbuto n'imitsima yo kurya, ni yo izobaha, ibongeranirize imbuto zanyu zo kubiba, kandi izogwiza imbuto z'ukugororoka kwanyu.
47009011	Namwe muzotungishwa muri vyose, ngo mugire ubuntu bwose, butuma dushimisha Imana.
47009012	Kuko igikorwa c'ukwo kugabura kitamara ubworo bw'abera gusa, ariko kandi kirushiriza gushimisha Imana muri benshi.
47009013	Kuko uburyo mwageragejwe n'ukwo kugabura bwatumye abo bahimbaza Imana yuko muwumvira, mwatura ubutumwa bwiza bwa Kristo, kandi yuko mwatabarishije vyinshi vyo kubafasha no gufasha abandi bose.
47009014	Kandi mu kubasengera babagirira inkumbu, kuko ubuntu bw' Imana burushiriza kuba muri mwebwe.
47009015	Imana ishimirwe ingabire yayo nziza itovugwa.
47010001	Jewe Pahulo ubwanje ndabinginga kubwo ubugwaneza n'ineza vya Kristo, jewe umuntu aciye bugufi muri mwebwe imbere yanyu, ariko iyo tutari kumwe ndabubahuka;
47010002	nuko ndabinginga kugira ngo ni twaba kumwe sinzorinde kububahuka, nk'uko niteguye kuzokwubahuka nshize ubwoba, bamwe batwiyumvira ko tugenda dukurikira ivyo akameremere kacu.
47010003	Naho turi n'umubiri ntiturwana mu buryo bw'umubiri,
47010004	kuko ibirwanisho vy'intambara yacu atari ivyo mu buryo bw'umubiri, ariko imbere y'Imana bifise ubushobozi bwo gushingura akarimbi,
47010005	dushingura impari n'igishizwe hejuru cose, kihashiriwe kurwanya ukumenya Imana, dufata mpiri ivyiyumvirwa mu mitima vyose, ngo tubigomorere Kristo.
47010006	Kandi twiteguye guhana ubutumva bwose, aho mwebwe muzogirira ukwumva gushitse.
47010007	Mbega muraba ibibonwa n'amaso? Namba hari umuntu yizigiye ko ari uwa Kristo, yibwire n'ibi, yuko uko ari uwa Kristo, natwe ari ko turi.
47010008	Kuko ububasha bwacu Umwami wacu yaduhaye kugira ngo tububake, ntitubasambure, naho norushiriza kubwirata, sinzomaramazwa;
47010009	sinzokwiyumvirwe nk'uwubateza ubwoba amakete yanje.
47010010	Kuko bavuga bati: "Amakete yiwe arahambaye, arasogota, ariko iyo ari ino, arakengeretse, kandi amajambo yiwe nta co amaze."
47010011	Uvuga ibisa bityo ni yibwire n'ibi, yuko uko tumeze ku majambo yo mu makete atari ho turi, ari ko tumeze no ku vyo dukora ari ho turi.
47010012	Kuko tutubahuka kwishira mu gitigiri ca bamwe bishimagiza, canke kwigereranya na bo; ariko abo, ko birehesha ubwabo kandi bigereranya ubwabo, nta bwenge bagira.
47010013	Tweho ntituzokwirata ibirenze urugero, ariko tuzokwiyumvira urugero rwacu ko ruhwanye n'urugezo rw'aho Imana yatugereye, ngo dushike no kuri mwebwe.
47010014	Ntiturenga akarimbi kacu, nk'abatabashitseko, kuko twarabashitseko koko, tuzanye ubutumwa bwiza bwa Kristo.
47010015	Ntitwirata ibirenze urugero, ntitwirata ivyo abandi bakoze. Ariko twizigiye yuko ukwizera kwanyu ni kwakura, tuzoshirwa hejuru kubwanyu, ku vyo twagerewe, ngo twagukirwe,
47010016	tuvuge ubutumwa bwiza mu bihugu biri hirya yanyu, kugira ngo ntitwirate ivyo dusanze biteguye, ahagerewe uwundi.
47010017	Ariko uwirata yirate Uhoraho.
47010018	Kuko uwishimagiza atari we yemerwa, ariko hemerwa uwo Umwami wacu ashimagiza.
47011001	Icompa mukanyihanganira ku bupfu buciyemwo, kandi n'ubwo muranyihanganira.
47011002	Ndabafitiye ishari ryo kubwo Imana, kuko nabahaye umugabo umwe, ni we Kristo, ngo ndabamushingire mumeze nk'inkumi itunganye.
47011003	Ariko ndiyubara yuko, nk'uko ya nzoka yahendesheje Eva ukwiyorobeka kwayo, kumbure ivyiyumviro vyanyu vyokwoshwa, mugaca mureka ukugororoka n'ukwera mu vya Kristo.
47011004	Kuko iyo hagize uwuza i wanyu akababarira Yesu wundi, tutababariye, canke iyo mwakiriye iyindi mpwemu mutakiriye, canke ubundi butumwa mutemeye, we muramwihanganira neza!
47011005	Kuko nibwira yuko izo ntumwa zihambaye cane ata co zindusha na gatoya.
47011006	Naho ndi igihwiji mu majambo, sindi igihwiji mu bwenge, kandi ivyo twarabiberetse muri vyose no mu maso ya bose.
47011007	Canke mbega naracumuye kuko nicishije bugufi ngo mushirwe hejuru, ndababwiye ubutumwa bwiza bw'Imana ku busa?
47011008	Nasahuye ayandi mashengero ndayaka ingero, kugira ngo nkorere mwebwe,
47011009	kandi aho nari kumwe namwe ngakena, sinagize uwo ngora; kuko abavukanyi bavuye i Makedoniya Bamaze ubukene. Muri vyose nirinda kubagora, kandi nzoshishikara kuvyirinda.
47011010	Uko ukuri kwa Kristo kuri muri jewe, nta wuzombuza kwirata ntyo mu ntara zo muri Akaya.
47011011	Ni ku ki? Ni uko ntabakunda? Bizi Imana.
47011012	Ariko ivyo nkora nzoshishikara kubikora, kugira ngo mbuze inyanduruko abagomba inyanduruko yo kuboneka nkatwe mu vyo birata.
47011013	Abameze batyo n'intumwa z'ibinyoma, n'abakozi bagunga, bigira intumwa za Kristo.
47011014	Kandi ivyo ntibitangaza, kuko na Satani yigira umumarayika w'umuco.
47011015	Nuko si ikigoye ko abakozi biwe na bo bigira nk'abakozi b'ukugororoka; iherezo ryabo rizohwana n'ibikorwa vyabo.
47011016	Kandi nongere kubivuga. Ntihagire uwunyiyumvira ko ndi igipfu. Ariko ni mwaramuka munyiyumviriye mutyo, munyemere nk'igipfu, kugira ngo nanje nirate gatoya.
47011017	Ivyo mvuga sindabivuga nk'ijambo ry'Umwami wacu, ariko ndabivuga nk'uwuvugishwa n'ubupfu, nizigiye yuko mfise inyanduruko yo kwirata.
47011018	Ko benshi birata ivyo umubiri, reka nanje nyene ndavyirate.
47011019	Mwihanganira ibipfu munezerewe, kuko mwibereye abanyabwenge.
47011020	Murihangana, iyo umuntu abagize abaja, iyo abariye, iyo abafashe, iyo yishize hejuru, iyo abakubise urushi.
47011021	Ndabivuganye isoni; bisa n'aho tweho twabagizemwo intege nke. Ariko ikintu cose gitera umuntu gushiruka umwete (ndabivugishijwe n'ubupfu) nanje kirabintera.
47011022	Mbega abo ni Abaheburayo? Nanje ndi we. Ni Abisirayeli? Nanje ndi we. Ni uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu? Nanje ndi rwo.
47011023	Ni abakozi ba Kristo? (Mvuga nk'umusazi) ndabarusha. Ndabarusha mu butame, ndabarusha gushirwa mu mabohero, ndabarusha mu gukubitwa kurenze urugero; kenshi nari mw'irinde ry'urupfu.
47011024	Abayuda ibihe bitanu bankubise ibimoko mirongo itatu n'icenda.
47011025	Ibihe bitatu nakubiswe ingage; igihe kimwe natewe amabuye; ibihe bitatu ubwato bwaramenekanye, naraye mu kiyaga nirirwaho;
47011026	nari mu ngendo kenshi, mw'irinde ry'inzuzi, mw'irinde ry'abambuzi, mw'irinde ry'ubwoko bwacu, mw'irinde ry'abanyamahanga, mw'irinde ryo mu bisagara, mw'irinde ryo mu bugaragwa, mw'irinde ryo mu kiyaga, mw'irinde ryo mu bigira bavukanyi;
47011027	mu butame no mu bucumukure, ndara maso kenshi, ngira inzara n'inyota, mara ubusa kenshi, nicwa n'imbeho, nambara ubusa.
47011028	Kandi ntarinze kuvuga ibindi, hari ikinzako uko bukeye, n'umwitwaririko w'amashengero yose.
47011029	Ni nde adakomera, nanje simbe uwudakomeye? Ni nde agira ikimugwisha, nanje isoni ntizinyice?
47011030	Namba nkwiye kwirata, nirata ivyo intege nke zanje.
47011031	Imana y'Umwami Yesu, ni yo Se, ishimwa ibihe bidashira, irazi ko ntabesha.
47011032	I Damasiko icegera c'umwami Areta carindishije igisagara c'Abanyadamasiko ngo bamfate.
47011033	Bancisha mu kadirisha k'uruhome rw'amabuye, ndi mu gisangaza, ndahunga ndamuva mu maboko.
47012001	Numva mpambirwa kwirata, naho bitagira ikimazi. Ariko ngira mvuge ivyo kwerekwa no guhishurirwa n'Umwami wacu.
47012002	Ndazi umuntu wo muri Kristo, yaduganywe akajanwa mw'ijuru rya gatatu, ubu hashize imyaka icumi n'ine--namba yari mu mubiri sindabizi; canke namba atari mu mubiri sindabizi, bizi Imana.
47012003	Kandi nzi yuko uwumeze atyo--namba yari mu mubiri, canke Namba atari mu mubiri, sindabizi, bizi Imana--
47012004	yaduganywe, akajanwa muri Paradiso, akumva ibitovugwa, ivyo umuntu atemererwa kuvuga.
47012005	Kubwo umuntu ameze atyo ndirata, ariko ku bwanje sinokwirata, atari intege nke zanje.
47012006	Kandi nogomvye kwirata sinobaye ndi igipfu, kuko noba mvuga ukuri. Ariko nsizeho kugira ngo ntihagire uwunyiyumvira ibiruta ivyo ambonako canke ivyo anyumvako.
47012007	Kandi kugira ngo sinterwe kwishira hejuru birenze urugero, ndabitewe n'uko nahishuriwe ibirushiriza kuba ibihambaye, ni co catumye mpabwa igisata mu mubiri, intumwa ya Satani yo kunkubita ibipfunsi, ngo sinterwe kwishira hejuru birenze urugero.
47012008	Kandi kuri ivyo natakambiye Umwami wacu gatatu ngo kimvemwo.
47012009	Arambarira ati: "Ubuntu bwanje buraguhagije; kuko ubushobozi bwanje buhingurirwa mu ntege nke." Nuko canecane nzonezererwa kwirata intege nke zanje, ngo ubushobozi bwa Kristo bunzeko.
47012010	Ni co gituma kubwa Kristo nzonezererwa intege nke zanje, no gukubagurwa, n'imibabaro, no guhigwa, n'ivyago; kuko iyo mbaye umunyantege nke ari ho ndushiriza kugira ubushobozi.
47012011	Mbaye igipfu, ni mwebwe mwabinteye, kuko ivyari bikwiye ari uko mba narashimagijwe namwe. Za ntumwa zihambaye cane nta co zindushije, naho ndi ubusa.
47012012	Ni ukuri ivyerekana intumwa vyakorewe hagati yanyu mu kwihangana kwose, ni vyo bimenyetso n'ibitangaza n'ibikorwa bikomeye.
47012013	Ayandi mashengero yabarushije iki, atari uko jewe ubwanje ntababereye ikirusha? Mumparire ico caha!
47012014	Ehe niteguye kuza i wanyu ubugira gatatu; sinzoba nje kubaremereza ivyo mu mpa. Kuko atari ivyanyu ndondera ariko ni mwebwe ubwanyu ndondera; kuko abana badakwiye kuziganiriza abavyeyi, ariko abavyeyi ni bo bakwiye kuziganiriza abana.
47012015	Ku bwanje nzonezererwa cane gutanga ivyanje, no kwitanga rwose, nitangira ubugingo bwanyu. Mbega ko ndushiriza kubagirira urukundo, none urwo nkundwa rugabanuke?
47012016	Ivyo vyo birahaye; ubwanje sinabaremereye; ariko, ko naciye mu kandi kenge, ubuhinga ubugunge.
47012017	Mbega mu bo nabatumyeko hari umuntu natumye kubaka inyungu?
47012018	Nagishije inama Tito, ndamurungikana; na wa muvukanyi wundi. Hari inyungu Tito yabatse? Ntitwagendeye muri Mpwemu umwe? Ntiyageze ikirenge mu canje?
47012019	Uhereye kera mwiyumvira yuko tubiregurako. Imbere y'Imana no muri Kristo ni ho tuvugira. Ariko yemwe abo nkunda, vyose tubivugiye kubakomeza.
47012020	Kuko binteye akoba yuko, aho nzozira, kumbure nzosanga mumeze uko ntagomba, nanje muzosanga meze uko mutagomba; kandi yuko kumbure hazoba imitongano, ishari, ishavu, ikeba, ukuvuga abandi nabi, insaku, ukwihimbariza ubusa n'imivurungano;
47012021	kandi yuko, aho nzozira, Imana yanje izosubira kuncisha bugufi muri mwebwe, nanje nkazoririra benshi bacumuye kera, ntibihane ivyonona, n'ubushakanyi, n'ivyo isoni nke bakoze.
47013001	Ubu bugira bube ubwa gatatu nza i wanyu. Ijambo ryose rizoringanizwa bivuye mu kanwa k'ivyabona bibiri canke bitatu.
47013002	Nabivuze nkiri kumwe namwe ubugira kabiri kera, na none ntari iyo ni ko ndabivuga bitaraba, ndabarira abacumuye kera n'abandi bose, yuko ni nagaruka ntazogira akagongwe;
47013003	kuko murondera ikimenyetso co kwerekana yuko Kristo ari we amvugisha, umwe atari umunyantege nke kuri mwebwe, ariko agira ubushobozi hagati yanyu.
47013004	Kuko intege nke zateye ko abambwa, ariko none ariho ku bwo ubushobozi bw'Imana. Natwe turi abanyantege nke muri we, ariko tuzobanaho na we, kubwo ubushobozi bw'Imana tubereyeho mwebwe.
47013005	Ba ari mwebwe mwisuzuma, mumenye yuko muhagaze mu kwizera; ba ari mwebwe mwiraba. Mbega ntimwiyizi, ntimuzi yuko Yesu Kristo ari muri mwebwe? --kiretse ko mwoba muri abahinyuwe!
47013006	Ariko nizigiye yuko muzomenya ko tweho tutari abahinyuwe.
47013007	Kandi turasaba Imana ngo ntimugire ikibi mukora, si ukugira ngo tuboneke ko turi abemewe, ariko ni ukugira ngo mukore iciza, natwe tuboneke nk'abahinyuwe.
47013008	Kuko tudashobora kurwanya ukuri, ariko duherereye mu ruhande rw'ukuri.
47013009	Turanezerwa iyo tugize intege nke, namwe mukagira inkomezi; kandi ico dusaba ngiki, ni uko mutunganywa rwose.
47013010	Ni co gitumye ndabandikira ivyo tutari kumwe, kugira ngo ni twaba kumwe sinzohambare, nk'uko nahawe ububasha n'Umwami wacu bwo kwubaka, ariko si ubwo gusambura.
47013011	Ibisigaye bavukanyi, muganuke; mutungane rwose, mwemere guhanurwa, muhuze imitima, mubane amahoro. Ni ho Imana nyene urukundo n'amahoro izobana namwe.
47013012	Muramukanishe kugumbirana kwera.
47013013	Abera bose barabaganutsa.
47013014	Ubuntu bw'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, n'urukundo rw' Imana, n'ubumwe buva kuri Mpwemu Yera, bibane namwe mwese.
48001001	Pahulo, intumwa itatumwe n'abantu, kandi nta muntu yabariwe kuntuma, ariko natumwe na Yesu Kristo, n'Imana Data wa twese yamuzuye mu bapfuye,
48001002	mfatanije n'abavukanyi turi kumwe bose kubandikira, mwebwe abo mu mashengero y'i Galatiya.
48001003	Ubuntu n'amahoro biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami wacu Yesu Kristo bibe muri mwebwe.
48001004	Uwo mwami Yesu Kristo yitangiye ivyaha vyacu, ngo aturokore muri iki gihe kibi c'ubu, nk'uko Imana yacu yagomvye, ni yo Data we twese.
48001005	Icubahiro kibe icayo ibihe bitazoshira. Amina.
48001006	Natangajwe ni uko muriko murareka vuba mutyo Iyabahamagaye ku bwo ubuntu bwa Kristo, mukemera ubutumwa bunyuranye n'ubwo,
48001007	kandi ata bundi buriho; ariko hariho abantu babahagarika imitima, bakagomba guhindura ukundi ubutumwa bwa Kristo.
48001008	Ariko naho yoba ari twebwe canke umumarayika avuye mw'ijuru, ababarira ubutumwa bunyuranye n'ubwo twababariye, arakavumwa.
48001009	Nk'uko twavuze ubwa mbere, n'ubu nongeye kubivuga ko ni hagira umuntu ababarira ubutumwa bunyuranye n'ubwo mwemeye, arakavumwa.
48001010	Mbega ubu n'ishimwe ry' abantu ngomba, canke ni iryo Imana? Canke se ndondera kunezereza abantu? Iyo mba nkinezereza abantu, simba ndi umushumba wa Kristo.
48001011	Ku vyo ubutumwa navuze, ndabamenyesha bavukanyi, yuko atari ubwo abantu.
48001012	Kuko nanje ntabuhawe n'umuntu, kandi sinabwigishijwe, ariko ni Yesu Kristo yabumpishuriye.
48001013	Mwumvise ingeso zanje nari mfise kera, nkiri mw'idini y'Abayuda, ingene nahiga ishengero ry'Imana birengereje, nkaritikiza.
48001014	Kandi mu bwoko bwacu narushije benshi bo mu bo twarukanye kuja imbere mw'idini y'Abayuda, kuko nabarusha kugira ishaka ry'imigenzo twarazwe na ba sogokuruza.
48001015	Ariko aho bihimbariye Imana yandobanuye nkiri mu nda ya mama, ikampamagara ku bwo ubuntu bwayo,
48001016	guhishurira umutima wanje Umwana wayo, ngo mvuge ubutumwa bwiwe bwiza mu banyamahanga. Ako kanya sinagishije inama abafise inyama n'amaraso,
48001017	kandi sinaduze i Yerusalemu ku bantanguriye kuba intumwa, ariko nagiye muri Arabiya, kandi hanyuma nsubira i Damasiko.
48001018	Maze imyaka itatu ishize nduga i Yerusalemu kwibonanira na Kefa, mara i we imisi icumi n'itanu.
48001019	Ariko mu zindi ntumwa nta wundi nabonye, atari Yakobo, mwene nyina w'Umwami Yesu.
48001020	Ivyo ndabandikiye ni ukuri, ehe ndabivugiye imbere y'Imana, simbesha.
48001021	Maze nja mu ntara z'i Siriya n'i Kilikiya.
48001022	Abo mu mashengero y'i Yudaya yo muri Kristo ntibaribwambone.
48001023	Ariko bumva gusa abamvuga bati: "Umwe yahora aduhiga mbere, ubu asigaye yamamaza ivyizerwa yari yagerageje kuzimanganya."
48001024	Nuko bahimbaza Imana kubwanje.
48002001	Maze hahise imyaka icumi n'ine, nongera kudugana na Barunaba, kandi na Tito ndamujana.
48002002	Kandi naduzeyo ku bwo guhishurirwa, ndabashira imbere ubutumwa bwiza mvuga mu banyamahanga, ariko ndabushira imbere y'abashimwa twiherereye, ngo sinirukire ubusa, canke simbe narirukiye ubusa.
48002003	Ariko na Tito twari kumwe naho yari Umugiriki ntibamugobereye guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo.
48002004	Kandi ari co coshimishije abigira abavukanyi banyegetejwe mw'ishengero, binjiye mu mpisho ngo basume urusaku ukwidegemvya kwacu dufise muri Kristo Yesu, kugira ngo badushire mu buja.
48002005	Abo ntitwabumviye na gatoya ngo tuganzwe na bo; kugira ngo ukuri kw'ubutumwa bwiza kugume muri mwebwe.
48002006	Ariko abashimwa ko ari bakuru --uko bari bameze ubwa mbere sindabibabaye, kubwanje vyose ni bimwe, Imana ntirobanura abantu ku cubahiro--abo bashimwa nta co banyongerereje.
48002007	Ariko babonye yuko najejwe ubutumwa bwo kwigisha abatahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, nk'uko Petero yajejwe ubwo kwigisha abahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo.
48002008	Kuko Iyashoboje Petero gutumwa ku bahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, ari yo yanshoboje nanje gutumwa kubatari Abisirayeli.
48002009	Yakobo, Kefa na Yohana, bashimwa ko ari inkingi, bamaze kumenya ubuntu nahawe, baduha ukuboko twe na Barunaba, ngo dufatanye nabo; ngo twebwe tuje ku batari Abisirayeli, na bo baje ku bahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo.
48002010	Ariko ico bagomvye gusa n'uko twibuka aboro, ari co nyene nanje nari nsanzwe mfitiye umwete.
48002011	Ariko Kefa aje muri Antiyokiya, namuharirije imbonankubone, kuko yari n'ibimutsindishije.
48002012	Kuko imbere yuko abavuye kwa Yakobo bashikayo yasangira n'abanyamahanga; ariko bashitseyo, ariyonjorora, arabanena, kuko atinye abo mu bahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo.
48002013	Kandi n'abandi Bayuda bahumbana na we, bitayeko na Barunaba atwarwa n'ubwo buhumvyi bwabo.
48002014	Ariko ndabonye badaca mu nzira igororotse, nk'uko ukuri kw'ubutumwa bwiza kuri, mbaririra Kefa imbere ya bose nti: "Ko wewe witondera ingeso z'abanyamahanga, zitari izo Abayuda, kandi uri Umuyuda, ugobera ute abanyamahanga kuba nk'Abayuda?"
48002015	Twebwe mu kameremere kacu turi Abayuda, ntituri abanyavyaha bo mu banyamahanga.
48002016	Ariko tuzi yuko umuntu adatsindanishirizwa n'ibikorwa bishinzwe n'ivyagezwe, ariko atsindanishirizwa no kwizera Yesu Kristo. Natwe twizeye Kristo Yesu, ngo kwizera Kristo kube ari kwo kudutsindanishiriza, atari ibikorwa bishinzwe n'ivyagezwe; kuko ata muntu atsindanishirizwa n'ibikorwa bishinzwe n'ivyagezwe.
48002017	Ariko namba twabonetse ko turi abanyavyaha, hamwe twarondera guhindurwa intungane no kuba muri Kristo, mbega Kristo ni umukozi agabura icaha? Eka na mba!
48002018	Nokwongera kwubaka ivyo nasambuye noba niseruye ko ndi umuntu acumura.
48002019	Ivyagezwe vyanteye gupfa ku vyagezwe, ngo mbeho ku Mana.
48002020	Nabambanywe na Kristo, ariko ndiho; yamara si jewe nkiriho, ni Kristo ariho muri jewe. Ivyo nkora vyose nkiriho mu mubiri ndabikoreshwa no kwizera Umwana w'Imana yankunze, akanyigura.
48002021	Simpindura ubusa ubuntu bw'Imana, kuko asangwa ukugororoka kuzanwa n'ivyagezwe, Kristo azoba yapfiriye ubusa.
48003001	Yemwe Bagalatiya b'ibijuju, ni nde yabaroze, kandi ari mwebwe mweretswe Yesu Kristo abambwe, mu maso yanyu?
48003002	Iki conyene ni co ngomba ko mumbwira; mbega Mpwemu mwamuronkeshejwe n'ibikorwa vy'ivyagezwe, canke n'ukwumva gufatanije n'ukwizera?
48003003	Mbega mwakabaye muri ibijuju mutyo? Mwatanguye mu vya Mpwemu, mbega none musozereye mu vyo umubiri?
48003004	Mbega ayo yose mwayaboneye ubusa? Namba yari ayo ubusa koko!
48003005	Iyibaha Mpwemu, igakorera ibitangaza muri mwebwe, mbega ibikoreshwa ni uko mukora ibikorwa vy'ivyagezwe, canke ni uko mwumvise mukizera?
48003006	Ni nk'uko Aburahamu yizeye Imana, akabiharurwako nk'ukugororoka.
48003007	Mumenye rero yuko abishimiye ukwizera ari bo bana ba Aburahamu.
48003008	Kandi ivyanditswe vyabimenye bitaraba yuko Imana izotsindanishiriza abanyamahanga ku bwo ukwizera, bibarira Aburahamu ubutumwa bwiza bw'ibitaraba bati: "Muri wewe ni ho amahanga yose azoherwa umugisha."
48003009	Nuko abishimira ukwizera bahabwa umugisha hamwe na Aburahamu yizera.
48003010	Abishimira ibikorwa vy'ivyagezwe bose bari n'umuvumo; kuko handitswe ngo azoba avumwe umuntu wese adashishikarira ivyanditswe vyose mu gitabo c'ivyagezwe, ngo avyitondere.
48003011	Biraseruka yuko ata muntu atsindanishirizwa n'ivyagezwe imbere y'Imana, kuko handitswe ngo Umugororotsi azobeshwaho n'ukwizera.
48003012	Ariko ivyagezwe ntibiva ku kwizera, yamara ngo Uwuzovyitondera ni vyo bizomubeshaho.
48003013	Kristo yaducunguye umuvumo w'ivyagezwe, yacitse ikivume kubwacu; kuko handitswe ngo azoba avumwe umuntu wese amanitswe ku giti: "
48003014	kugira ngo umugisha wa Aburahamu ushike ku banyamahanga, bawuheshejwe na Yesu Kristo, kugira ngo ukwizera kuturonkeshe Mpwemu twasezeraniwe.
48003015	Bavukanyi, ibi ndabivuga nk'imvugo y'abantu. Isezerano, naho ryoba iryo umuntu gusa, iyo rishinzwe nta muntu arikuraho canke aryongerako.
48003016	Nuko Aburahamu ni we yasezeraniwe amasezerano, bo n'uruvyaro rwiwe. Ntiyavuze iti: ""Imvyaro;"" nk'uwuvuga benshi; yamara yavuze nk'uwuvuga umwe iti: ""Ni uruvyaro rwawe; ni rwo Kristo.""
48003017	Ariko ico mvuze; isezerano ryabanje gushingwa n'Imana, ivyagezwe vyaje hashize imyaka amajana ane na mirongo itatu, ntivyorikuraho ngo bihindure ubusa iryo sezerano.
48003018	Kuko iyo umwandu uzanwa n'ivyagezwe, woba utazanywe n'isezerano, ariko Imana yawuhaye Aburahamu, iwumusezeraniye. "
48003019	Nuko ivyagezwe ni ivyo iki? Vyageretsweko kubwo ibicumuro, ngo bigumeho kugeza aho uruvyaro rwasezeranywe ivyo isezerano ruzozira. Kandi vyahawe abamarayika kubigera, na bo babiha umushikirwa w'amajambo.
48003020	Ariko umuhuza ntahuza umuntu umwe, yamara Imana ni imwe.
48003021	Mbega ivyagezwe birwanya amasezerano y'Imana? Eka na mba! Iyo haba hariho ivyagezwe vyashinzwe bishobora kubeshaho abantu, ni ukuri ukugororoka kuba kwarazanywe n'ivyagezwe.
48003022	Ariko ivyanditswe bivuga yuko vyose vyugaranywe ngo biganzwe n'icaha, kugira ngo abizera bahabwe ivyasezeranywe biheshwa no kwizera Yesu Kristo.
48003023	Ariko ukwizera kutaraza, twarindwa n'ivyagezwe, twugaranywe turindiriye ukwizera kwagira guhishirwe.
48003024	Uko ni ko ivyagezwe vyatubereye umurezi aturera akadushikiriza Kristo, ngo dutsindanishirizwe n'ukwizera.
48003025	Ariko ukwizera ko kwaje, ntitukirerwa n'umurezi.
48003026	Mwese muri abana b'Imana kubwo kwizera Kristo Yesu.
48003027	Kuko mwese ababatirijwe kuba aba Kristo mwambaye Kristo.
48003028	Ntihashobora kuba Umuyuda canke Umugiriki, ntihashobora kuba umuja canke uwidegemvya, ntihashobora kuba umugabo canke umugore; kuko mwese muri umwe muri Kristo Yesu.
48003029	Ko muri aba Kristo, muri uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu, muri basamuragwa nk'uko vyasezeranywe.
48004001	Ariko ndavuga yuko samuragwa, iyo akiri umwana, ata co atandukanako n'umushumba, naho ari we nyene ibintu vyose.
48004002	Ariko aganzwa n'abamuzigama n'ababwiriza kugeza mu gihe cashinzwe na se.
48004003	Natwe ni uko; tukiri abana twari tujakariye ivya mbere vyo mw'isi.
48004004	Maze igihe gikwiye gishitse, Imana ituma Umwana wayo, yavyawe n'umugore, kandi yavutse aganzwa n'ivyagezwe,
48004005	ngo acungure abaganzwa n'ivyagezwe, biduheshe gucika abana bayo.
48004006	Kandi kuko mu bana bayo, Imana yatumye Mpwemu w'Umwana wayo mu mitima yacu, atakamba ati: "Abba, Data."
48004007	Ni co gituma utakiri umushumba, ariko uri umwana wayo; kandi ko uri umwana wayo, uri umuragwa, ubihawe n'Imana.
48004008	Ariko ico gihe, kuko mutari muzi Imana, mwari mujakariye imana zitari zo uhereye mu kameremere kazo.
48004009	Ariko none, ko mwamenye Imana, canecane ko mwamenywe na yo, ni igiki catumye musubira inyuma mugahindukirira ivya mbere vya goyigoyi, bitagira ikimazi, mukagomba kubijakarira ukundi gusha?
48004010	Muziririza imisi, amezi, ibihe n'imyaka.
48004011	Munteye akoba, yuko kumbure ivyo nabakoreye natamijwe n'ubusa.
48004012	Ndabinginze, bavukanyi, mumere nkanje, kuko nanje meze nkamwe. Nta nabi mwangiriye,
48004013	ariko murazi yuko amagara make y'umubiri ari yo yatumye ndababarira ubutumwa bwiza ubwa mbere.
48004014	Kandi ivyabagerageza kubwo umubiri wanje ntimwabitituye, ntimwaciriye inyeri, ariko mwanyakiriye nk'umumarayika w'Imana, canke nka Kristo Yesu.
48004015	None kwa kwishima kwanyu kuri hehe? Ndi icabona canyu yuko iyo biba vyarashobotse, muba mwaremeye kwinogora amaso, mukayampa.
48004016	Mbega mpinduwe umwansi wanyu no kubabwira ukuri?
48004017	Ba bandi babagirira ishaka mu buryo butari bwiza; ariko ico bagomba ni ukubazigira hanze, kugira ngo namwe mubagirire ishaka.
48004018	Mugabo, ni vyiza kugirira ivyiza ishaka ibihe vyose, atari igihe turi kumwe gusa,
48004019	bana banje bato, abo nongera kwibaruka mu marira, gushitsa aho ishusho ya Kristo izoremerwa muri mwebwe.
48004020	Kandi nagomba gushikirana namwe aka kanya, no kworosha ijwi, kuko ivyanyu binzazaniye.
48004021	Mwebwe abagomba kuganzwa n'ivyagezwe, ni mumbarire. Mbega ntimwumva ivyagezwe?
48004022	Kuko vyanditswe yuko Aburahamu yarafise abahungu babiri, umwe ari uwo ku ncoreke, uwundi ari uwo ku mugore bwite.
48004023	Uwo ku ncoreke yavyawe mu buryo bw'umubiri; uwo ku mugore bwite yavyawe kubwo isezerano.
48004024	Ivyo ni nk'umugani. Kuko abo bagore ari nk'amasezerano abiri, rimwe ryavuye ku musozi Sinayi, rivyara abo kuguma mu buja, iryo ni Hagari.
48004025	Nuko Hagari ni umusozi Sinayi wo muri Arabiya, usobanurwa ngo Yerusalemu wa none, kuko usangiye ubuja n'abana bawo.
48004026	Ariko Yerusalemu wo hejuru ni wo mugore bwite, ni wo mama wa twese.
48004027	Kuko handitswe, ngo Nezerwa, yewe mugore w'ingumba utavyara, Turika, usemerere, wewe utaramukwa, Kuko abana b'intabwa ari benshi, baruta abo uwufise umugabo.
48004028	Namwe bavukanyi, muri abana b'isezerano, nk'uko Isaka yari ari.
48004029	Ariko nk'uko ico gihe uwavyawe mu buryo bw'umubiri yahama uwavyawe mu buryo bwa Mpwemu, na none ni ko biri.
48004030	Ivyanditswe bivuga biti: "Irukana incoreke n'umwana wayo, kuko umwana w'incoreke atazoraganwa n'umwana w'umugore bwite."
48004031	Nuko bavukanyi, ntituri abana b'incoreke, turi aba wa mugore bwite.
48005001	Kristo yatugobotoye ngo tube mu mwidegemvyo. Nuko muhagarare mushikamye, ntimukongere kuzingirwa n'ugutwazwa ituntu n'ubuja.
48005002	Umve, jewe Pahulo ndababwira yuko ni mwahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo, Kristo ata co azobamarira.
48005003	Kandi ndabarira umuntu wese ahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo, ndabishingiye intahe, yuko ari n'umwenda wo kwitondera ivyagezwe vyose.
48005004	Yemwe abagomba guhindurwa intungane n'ivyagezwe, erega muhinduye ubusa gufatana kwanyu na Kristo, muratemvye muretse ubuntu bw'Imana.
48005005	Kuko twebwe, mu buryo bwa Mpwemu, twiteze ivyizigiro vy'ukugororoka, kubwo ukwizera.
48005006	Kuko muri Kristo Yesu, ari uguhimbura igikoba c'ubugabo, ari ukudahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo, bitagira ikimazi; ikigira ikimazi ni ukwizera gukoreshwa n'urukundo.
48005007	Ko mwagenda neza; ni nde yabateye gutezura ngo ntimwumvire ukuri?
48005008	Iyo nyosha ntiyavuye kuri uwo abahamagara.
48005009	Umwambiro muke ututumbisha irobe ryose.
48005010	Ndabizigiye ku bwo Umwami wacu yuko mutazogira uwundi mutima; ariko uwubahagarika imitima, uwo ari we wese, urubanza ruzomusubirako.
48005011	Ariko jewe, bavukanyi, namba nkibarira abantu guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo, ni igiki gituma ngihamwa? Igitsitaza c'umusaraba kiba carahindutse ubusa.
48005012	Icompa ababavurunga bakikona rwose.
48005013	Bavukanyi, mwahamagariwe umwidegemvyo; mugabo rero, uwo mwidegemvyo ntimuwugire urwitwazo rw'akameremere kanyu, ariko urukundo rubatere gukorerana.
48005014	Kuko ivyagezwe vyose bihurira muri iri jambo, ngo mukunde ababanyi banyu nk'uko mwikunda.
48005015	Ariko ni mwashikurana, mugatabagurana, mwirinde ntimuhezanye.
48005016	Ndavuga nti: "Mugendeshwe na Mpwemu, ni ho mutazoshitsa ivyo akameremere kanyu kifuza."
48005017	Kuko akameremere kifuza ivyo Mpwemu yanka, kandi Mpwemu yifuza ivyo akameremere kanka. Kuko ivyo bihiganwa, ngo ntimukore ivyo mugomba.
48005018	Ariko namba murongorwa na Mpwemu, ntimuganzwa n'ivyagezwe.
48005019	Kandi ibikorwa vy'akameremere kacu biramenyekana, n'ibi: ubusambanyi, ibihumanya, ivyo isoni nke,
48005020	gusenga ibigirwamana, uburozi, ubwansi, intonganya, ishari, ishavu, ikeba, kwitandukanya, ibice,
48005021	igono, kuborerwa, kudandahirwa, n'ibindi bene ivyo. Ivyo ndabibaburiye, nk'uko nabibaburiye kera, yuko abakora ibisa bityo batazoragwa ubwami bw' Imana.
48005022	Ariko ivyo Mpwemu yama ni: urukundo, umunezero, amahoro, ukwihangana, kugira neza, ingeso nziza, kuba umwizigirwa,
48005023	ubugwaneza, ukwirinda. Ibimeze bityo nta vyagezwe bibibuza.
48005024	Kandi aba Kristo Yesu babambanye akameremere kabo n'ivyo gahahamiye n'ivyo kifuza.
48005025	Namba tubeshwaho na Mpwemu, tuyoborwe na Mpwemu.
48005026	Ntitwifate uko tutari, ngo twandurutsanye, tugiriranire ishari
48006001	Bavukanyi, umuntu n'iyo yobonekako icaha, mwebwe abo impwemu mutunganye uwumeze atyo, mumuhanurishe umutima w'ubugwaneza. Kandi wiyubare ubwawe, nawe nyene ntiwoshwe nabi.
48006002	Mwakirane imitwaro, mushikane mutyo ivyagezwe na Kristo.
48006003	Umuntu ni yiyumvira ko ari agakomeye, kandi ata co amaze, aribesha.
48006004	Ariko umuntu wese asuzume igikorwa ciwe, ni ho azobona ico yirata ku mutumba wiwe bwite, atari kubwo uwundi.
48006005	Kuko umuntu wese azokwiyikorerera uwiwe mutwaro.
48006006	Ariko uwigishwa ijambo ry'Imana ahe umwigisha mu vyiza vyose.
48006007	Ntimuzimire, Imana yo nticokorwa; kuko ico umuntu abiba cose ari co azokwimbura.
48006008	Uwubiba mu buryo bw'umubiri azokwimbura ukubora mu mubiri; ariko uwubiba muri Mpwemu azokwimbura muri Mpwemu ubugingo budashira.
48006009	Twame dukora ivyiza, ntiducobogore, kuko igihe ni cashika tuzokwimbura, ni tutarambirwa.
48006010	Nuko rero, iyo turonse uburyo, tugirire bose neza, canecane abo inzu y'abizera.
48006011	Murabe ingene ndabandikishirije ukuboko kwanje inyuguti nininini.
48006012	Abagomba bose kwiha igikundiro ku vyo umubiri ni bo babagobera guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo; nta yindi nyanduruko, ni ukugira ngo ntibahamwe bahorwa umusaraba wa Kristo.
48006013	Kuko abahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo na bo nyene batitondera ivyagezwe, ariko bashaka ko muhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo, ngo birate imibiri yanyu.
48006014	Ariko jeho sinkirate ikindi, atari umusaraba w'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, watumye isi imbera ikibambwe, nanje isi nkayibera ikibambwe.
48006015	Kuko guhimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo ata kimazi, no kudahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo nta kimazi, ikigira ikimazi ni icaremwe gishasha.
48006016	Abazogendera kuri urwo rugezo, amahoro abe muri bo n'ikigongwe, no mu Bisirayeli b' Imana.
48006017	Uhereye ubu ntihakagire umuntu angora, kuko mfise ku mubiri inkovu za Yesu.
48006018	Bavukanyi, ubuntu bw' Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane n'imitima yanyu. Amina.
49001001	Pahulo, nagizwe intumwa ya Kristo Yesu ni uko Imana yabigomvye, ndabandikiye abera bari muri Efeso, b'abizigirwa bo muri Kristo Yesu.
49001002	Ubuntu bubabemwo n'amahoro, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo.
49001003	Imana y'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ari yo Se, iragahezagirwa, yaduhezagiriye imihezagiro yose y'impwemu ahantu ho mw'ijuru muri Kristo.
49001004	Nk'uko yadutoranirije muri we, itanguriro ry'isi ritarashirwaho, kugira ngo tube abera tutagira agasembwa imbere yayo, turi mu rukundo.
49001005	Kuko yagabiye kera ko duheshwa na Yesu Kristo gucika abana bayo kubwayo, nk'uko yabigomvye bikayihimbara.
49001006	Kugira ngo ubwiza bw'ubuntu bwayo yatugabiriye mu wo ikunda bushimwe.
49001007	Muri we ni ho duherwa gucungurwa n'amaraso yiwe, ni kwo guharirwa ibicumuro vyacu, nk'uko itunga ry'ubuntu bwayo riri.
49001008	Yabudusesekarijemwo mu bwenge bwose no kumenya;
49001009	itwatiye ibanga ry'ivyo igomba, nk'uko vyayihimbaye, ivyigiriye imigabo kuva kera muri we,
49001010	vy'ingene izogenza vyose, igihe gikwiye gishitse, gukoraniriza vyose muri Kristo, ibiri mw'ijuru n'ibiri mw'isi.
49001011	Kuba muri uwo kwaduhesheje gucika ihanga ryayo, twashiriweho kera nk'uko Iyo yabigabiye, ikora vyose nk'uko imigabo yo mu mutima wayo iri;
49001012	kuzoba abo guhesha icubahiro ubwiza bwayo, twebwe abizigiye Kristo kera.
49001013	Muri we namwe mumaze kwumva ijambo ry'ukuri, ni ryo butumwa bwiza bw'agakiza kanyu, mumaze no kumwizera, ni ho mwashiriweko ikimenyetso, ni co Mpwemu Yera yasezeranywe.
49001014	Ni we ngwati y'umwandu tuzohabwa, kugira ngo abo Imana yaronse ibacungure, ngo ubwiza bwayo bushimwe.
49001015	Ni co gituma nanje, numvise ukwizera Umwami Yesu kuri muri mwebwe, n'urukundo mukunda abera bose,
49001016	ntahengeshanya kubashimira Imana, ndabahoza mu kanwa uko nsenze,
49001017	ngo Imana y'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, Data wa twese w'ubwiza, ibahe umutima w'ubwenge no guhishurirwa mu kuyimenya;
49001018	ngo amaso y'imitima yanyu yihweze, kugira ngo mumenye ivyo mwizigizwa n'uguhamagara kwayo ivyo ari vyo, mumenye n'itunga ry'ubwiza bw'umugabane ufise mu bera.
49001019	Mumenye n'ubwinshi buhebuje bw'ubushobozi bwayo ikoreshereza muri twebwe abizera, nk'uko kwa gukora kw'ububasha bw'ubushobozi bwayo kungana,
49001020	ukwo yakoreye muri Kristo, hamwe yamuzura mu bapfuye, ikamuvyagiza i buryo bwayo ahantu ho mw'ijuru,
49001021	imushize hejuru cane y'ubukuru bwose, ububasha bwose, ubushobozi bwose, ubwami bwose n'izina ryose rivugwa, si muri iki gihe gusa, ariko no mu kizoza.
49001022	Kandi yamushikirije vyose, ibishira musi y'ibirenge vyiwe, kandi imuha ishengero ngo abe umutwe waryo wo gusumba vyose,
49001023	ni ryo mubiri wiwe w'ubwuzure, bwuzuza vyose vy'ahantu hose.
49002001	Namwe yarabagize bazima, hamwe mwari mupfuye mwishwe n'ibigabitanyo n'ivyaha vyanyu,
49002002	ivyo mwagenderamwo kera, nk'uko ivyo iyi si bigenda, mwumvira umwami w'abaganza ikirere, ni we mpwemu ikorera mu bantu b'intabarirwa.
49002003	Kandi natwe twese twahora muri bo kera mu kwifuza kw'imibiri yacu, tugakora ivyo imibiri n'imitima vyacu bigomba, kandi mu kameremere kacu twari abo kurakirwa, nk'abandi bose.
49002004	Ariko Imana, kuko ari umutunzi w'ikigongwe, kubwo urukundo rwayo rwinshi yadukunze,
49002005	hamwe twari tugipfuye, twishwe n'ibicumuro vyacu, yatugiranye bazima na Kristo--ubuntu ni bwo bwabakijije—
49002006	yatuzuranye na we, itwicarikana na we ahantu ho mw'ijuru, turi muri Kristo Yesu,
49002007	kugira ngo mu bihe bizoza izokwerekane itunga rihebuje ry'ubuntu bwayo mu kutugirira neza muri Kristo Yesu.
49002008	Ubuntu ni bwo bwabakijije kubwo ukwizera; na vyo nyene ntivyavuye kuri mwebwe, ni ingabire y'Imana;
49002009	ntivyavuye ku bikorwa, kugira ngo ntihagire n'umwe yishimagiza.
49002010	Kuko turi ibiremwa vyayo, twaremewe muri Kristo Yesu ngo dukore ibikorwa vyiza, ivyo Imana yateguye kera ngo tubigenderemwo.
49002011	Nuko mwibuke yuko ubwa mbere, mwebwe abanyamahanga ku rukoba, mwebwe mucitwa abatahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo n'abo bitwa abahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo n'intoke ku mubiri,
49002012	ko ico gihe mwari mutandukanye na Kristo, muri n'itandukaniro n'ihanga rya Isirayeli, atasano mufitaniye n'amasezerano y'ivyasezeranywe, ata co mwizigiye ku bizoba, mwari mw'isi mutagira Imana Rurema.
49002013	Ariko noneho, kuko muri muri Kristo Yesu, mwebwe abari kure kera mwigijwe hafi n'amaraso ya Kristo.
49002014	Ni we mahoro yacu, kuko yahinduye ya macakubiri kuba kimwe, ahomvoye ca gisika co hagati cadutandukanya,
49002015	ubwansi amaze kubuhinduza ubusa umubiri wiwe, ni bwo vya vyagezwe birimwo amabwirizwa ava mu vyashinzwe; kugira ngo muri we ya macakubiri ayarememwo umuntu umwe musha, ngo azane amahoro atyo;
49002016	kandi ngo ayo macakubiri, amaze kuyagira umubiri umwe, ayuzurishe n'Imana umusaraba, awicishije bwa bwansi.
49002017	Yaraje, ababwira ubutumwa bwiza bw'amahoro, mwebwe abari kure. Kandi abari hafi na bo ababwira amahoro.
49002018	Kuko, uko twari amoko abiri, ubu ni we adushikiriza Data wa twese, turi muri Mpwemu umwe.
49002019	Nuko ntimukiri abashitsi n'abanyamahanga, ariko musangiye ubwoko n'abera, muri abo mu ngoro y'Imana;
49002020	kuko mwubatswe ku mabuye y'umushinge, ari yo ntumwa n'abavugishwa n'Imana, Kristo Yesu ari we buye rigumya imfuruka.
49002021	Muri we ingoro yose, yubatswe neza, irakura, ngo ibe urusengero rwera mu Mwami wacu.
49002022	Muri we namwe murubakanwa, kugira ngo muheshwe na Mpwemu kuba ingoro Imana ibamwo.
49003001	Ni co gituma jewe Pahulo, imbohe ya Kristo Yesu, mbohewe mwebwe abanyamahanga,
49003002	namba mwarumvise ububwiriza bwa bwa buntu bw'Imana nahawe kubagaburira;
49003003	yuko mu guhishurirwa natiwe ibanga, nk'uko nabanje kwandika mu majambo make,
49003004	namwe, ni mwayasoma, muzoshobora kubona ingene nzi ibanga rya Kristo.
49003005	Ivyo, abana b'abantu ntibabimenyeshejwe mu bindi bihe, nk'uko muri iki gihe intumwa ziwe zera n'abavugishwa na we babihishuriwe na Mpwemu;
49003006	yuko abanyamahanga basangiye natwe iragi, basangiye natwe umubiri umwe, basangiye natwe ivyasezeranywe muri Kristo Yesu kubwo ubutumwa bwiza.
49003007	Nacitse umukozi wabwo, nk'uko ingabire y'ubuntu bw'Imana iri, nabuhawe, nk'uko ubushobozi bwayo bukora.
49003008	Jewe, uwuri mu nyuma y'uwo mu nyuma y'abera bose. Naherewe ubwo buntu kubwira abanyamahanga ubutumwa bwiza bw'itunga rya Kristo ritagira aho riherera,
49003009	no guserurira bose ububwiriza bw'ibanga ubwo ari bwo. Ryari rihishijwe, uhereye kera hose, mu Mana Umuremyi wa vyose;
49003010	kugira ngo noneho abakuru n'abafise ububasha b'ahantu ho mw'ijuru bamenyere kw'ishengero ubwenge bw'Imana bw'uburyo bwinshi.
49003011	Nk'uko imigabo yayo iri, iyo yagabiye uhereye kera hose muri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu.
49003012	Muri we ni ho duherwa ubushizi bw'ubwoba no gushikira Imana tuyizigiye, kubwo kumwizera.
49003013	Ni co gituma ndabinginga ngo ntimwihebuzwe n'amarushwa yanje yo kubwanyu, kuko ari yo cubahiro canyu.
49003014	Ni co gituma mpfukamira Data wa twese,
49003015	uwo imiryango yose yo mw'ijuru n'iyo mw'isi yitirirwa,
49003016	ngo abahe, nk'uko itunga ry'ubwiza bwiwe riri, kuremeshwa n'ubushobozi imbere mu mitima mubihawe na Mpwemu wiwe.
49003017	Kristo abe mu mitima yanyu kubwo ukwizera; kugira ngo mugize imizi ishinzwe mu rukundo, n'amabuye y'umushinge arwubatswemwo,
49003018	mugire inkomezi zibashoboza gutahurira hamwe n'abera bose uburebure bw'ubwaguke, ubwo amakika, ubwo amaja ruguru n'ubwo amajepfo ubwo ari bwo,
49003019	mumenye urukundo rwa Kristo ruruta uko rwomenywa; ngo mubone kwuzuzwa mushitse ku kwuzura kw'Imana kwose.
49003020	Nuko Iyishobora gukora ibirengeye cane ivyo dusaba n'ivyo twiyumvira vyose, nk'uko ubushobozi bwayo budukoreramwo buri,
49003021	icubahiro kibe icayo mw'ishengero no muri Kristo Yesu, kugeza ku buzukuruza bose b'ibihe bitazoshira. Amina.
49004001	Ni co gitumye ndabinginga, jewe imbohe y'Umwami wacu, ngo mugende uko bibereye ihamagarwa mwahamagawe,
49004002	mwiyoroheje rwose, mufise ubugwaneza, mwihangana, mubabariranira muri mu rukundo.
49004003	Mushishikaye kuzigamisha ubumwe buva kuri Mpwemu umugozi w'amahoro.
49004004	Hariho umubiri umwe, na Mpwemu umwe, nk'uko kandi mwahamagariwe icizigiro kimwe c'ihamagarwa ryanyu.
49004005	Hariho Umwami umwe, ukwizera kumwe no kubatizwa kumwe.
49004006	Hariho n'Imana imwe, ni yo Data wa twese, asumba bose, akoresha bose, ari muri bose.
49004007	Ariko umuntu wese muri twebwe yahawe ubuntu, nk'uko tugererwa ingabire ya Kristo.
49004008	Ni co gituma ivuga iti: "Yaraduze, aja iyo hejuru, ajanye iminyago, Agabira abantu ingabire."
49004009	Ariko iryo jambo ngo Yaraduze, ni ukuvuga iki? Mbega ntiryerekana yuko yabanje kumanuka i kuzimu?
49004010	Uwo yamanutse ni we yaduze, aja hejuru y'amajuru yose, kugira ngo anengesere vyose.
49004011	Kandi yahaye bamwe kuba intumwa, abandi kuba abavugishwa na we, abandi kuvuga ubutumwa bwiza, abandi kuba abungere n'abigisha,
49004012	kugira ngo abera babone gutungana, baheze bakore igikorwa co kugabura ivyo Imana, bubake umubiri wa Kristo;
49004013	kugeza aho twese tuzoshikira ku kugiriranira ubumwe buva ku kwizera n'ukumenya Umwana w'Imana, kandi kugeza aho tuzoshikira kuba abantu bakuze, no ku rugezo rw'ubwinshi bw'ukunengesera kwa Kristo;
49004014	kugira ngo dushire ubwana, ntituzungazungishwe n'imipfunda, ngo tujanwe irya n'ino n'imiyaga yose y'inyigisho n'ububeshi bw'abantu, n'ubugunge bwabo, n'uburyo bwinshi bwo kutuzimiza.
49004015	Ariko tube imvugakuri turi mu rukundo, dukurire muri we muri vyose, ari we mutwe, ni wo Kristo.
49004016	Umubiri wiwe wose, uteranijwe neza, ufatanijwe n'ibifashisho vy'ingingo zawo zose, nk'uko igice cose gikora ibango cagerewe, kuri we ni ho uronka gukura kwawo, ukubakwa mu rukundo.
49004017	Ni co gituma mvuga ibi, nkabishingira intahe mu Mwami wacu, ngo ntimube mukigenda nk'uko abanyavyaha bagenda, bagendera mu bitagira ikimazi vyo mu bwenge bwabo.
49004018	Ivyiyumviro vyabo biri mu mwiza, batandukanijwe n'ubugingo buva ku Mana kubwo ukutamenya kuri muri bo, n'ukudadarara kw'imitima yabo.
49004019	Kandi babaye ibitimbe, bishira mu ngeso z'isoni nke, gukora ibihumanya vy'uburyo bwose bifatanije n'ukwifuza.
49004020	Ariko mweho ntimwize Kristo mutyo,
49004021	namba mwaramwumvise, mukigishirizwa muri we nk'uko ukuri kwo muri Yesu kuri,
49004022	kubabwira ku vyo ingeso zanyu za kera ngo mwiyambure wa muntu wa kera, abozwa n'ukwifuza kw'uruhendo;
49004023	mugahinduka bashasha mu mpwemu y'ubwenge bwanyu,
49004024	mukambara wa muntu mushasha, yaremwe mw'ishusho y'Imana mu kugororoka no mu kwera kw'ukuri.
49004025	Maze mwiyambuye ibinyoma, umuntu wese avugane ivyo ukuri n'umubanyi wiwe, kuko turi ingingo z'abandi.
49004026	Ni mwaraka ntibibakoreshe icaha. Izuba ntirirenge mukiratse,
49004027	kandi ntimuhe wa mugarariji icicaro.
49004028	Uwiba ntakongere kwiba, ariko apfume acumukura, akoreshe ayiwe maboko ivyiza, kugira ngo aronke ivyo gufasha uwukenye.
49004029	Ntihazogire ibiyago bibi biva mu kanwa kanyu, ariko muvuge ijambo ryiza ryose ryo gukuza uwukwiye kuribwirwa, kugira ngo riheshe abaryumvise ubuntu bw'Imana.
49004030	Kandi ntimukababaze Mpwemu w'Imana, yabashiriweko kuba ikimenyetso, gushitsa ku musi wo gucungurwa.
49004031	Umururazi wose ukujingitwa, ishavu, gutongana n'ugutukana bibavemwo, hamwe n'inzigo yose.
49004032	Mugiriranire neza, mugiriranire imbabazi, muharirane, nk'uko Imana na yo yabahariye muri Kristo.
49005001	Nuko mwigane Imana, nk' abana ikunda.
49005002	Kandi mugendere mu rukundo, nk'uko Kristo na we yabakunze, akatwigura, akatubera ishikanwa n'ikimazi bihabwa Imana, umubabwe umota neza.
49005003	Ariko ubusambanyi n'ibihumanya vyose canke ukwifuza ntimukabishire no mu kanwa, mube nk'uko bibereye abera.
49005004	Ibiteye isoni canke amajambo y'ubupfu canke ibitwenza bibi ntibikumvikane muri mwebwe kuko ivyo bitabereye; ikibereye ni ugushima Imana.
49005005	Kuko ibi mubizi neza, yuko ata mushakanyi, canke igihumane, canke uwifuza (ni we asenga ibigirwamana), azogira ico aragwa mu bwami bwa Kristo n'Imana.
49005006	Ntihakagire umuntu abahendesha amajambo y'ubusa; kuko ivyo ari vyo bizanira ishavu ry'Imana abantu b'intabarirwa.
49005007	Nuko ntimugafatanye na bo;
49005008	kuko kera mwari umwiza, none mukaba muri umuco mu Mwami wacu. Mugende nk'abana b'umuco,
49005009	kuko imbuto y'umuco iboneka mu ngeso nziza zose no mu kugororoka no mu kuri.
49005010	Mumenye neza ibihimbara Umwami wacu.
49005011	Kandi ntimugafatanye n'ibikorwa vy'imburakimazi vy'umwiza, ariko canecane mubiserure,
49005012	kuko ibikorwa na bo mu mpisho biteye isoni no kubivuga.
49005013	Ariko vyose, iyo bishizwe ahabona, bigaragazwa n'umuco, kuko ikigaragazwa cose kiri mu muco.
49005014	Ni co gituma bivugwa, ngo ikangure, wewe usinziriye, uzuke uve mu bapfuye, Kristo arakumurikira.
49005015	Nuko mwirinde cane uburyo mugenda, ntimugende nk'imburabwenge, ariko mugende nk' abanyabwenge.
49005016	Akaryo muronse, mugakoresha neza, kuko imisi ari mibi.
49005017	Nuko ntimube ibipfu, ariko mutahure ivyo Umwami wacu agomba ivyo ari vyo.
49005018	Kandi ntimukaborerwe umuvinyu, urimwo ubuhumbu; ariko mwuzure Mpwemu.
49005019	Mubwirane zaburi, indirimbo n'amatazirano y'ivya Mpwemu, muririmba, mucurarangira Umwami wacu mu mitima yanyu.
49005020	Imana, Data wa twese, muyishimire vyose imisi yose, mw'izina ry'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo.
49005021	Mugamburukanire, kuko mwubashe Kristo.
49005022	Bagore, mugamburukire abagabo banyu, nk'uko mugamburukira Umwami wacu.
49005023	Kuko umugabo ari we mutwe w'umugore wiwe, nk'uko Kristo na we ari umutwe w'ishengero, akaba Umukiza waryo, ari wo mubiri wiwe.
49005024	Ariko nk'uko ishengero rigamburukira Kristo, kube ari ko abagore bagamburukira abagabo babo muri vyose.
49005025	Bagabo, mukunde abagore banyu, nk'uko Kristo na we yakunze ishengero, akaryigura,
49005026	ngo aryeze, aryogesheje amazi n'ijambo,
49005027	maze ngo arirengukane imbere yiwe, ari ishengero rifise ubwiza, ridafise amarabaga canke agatotsi canke ikintu cose gisa gityo, ariko ngo ribe iryera ridafise agasembwa.
49005028	Ni ko abagabo na bo bakwiye gukunda abagore babo nk'imibiri yabo bwite. Uwukunda umugore wiwe, aba yikunda,
49005029	kuko ata muntu yigeze kwanka umubiri wiwe, ariko arawugaburira, akawubungabunga, nk'uko Kristo na we agirira ishengero.
49005030	Kuko turi ingingo z'umubiri wiwe.
49005031	Ni co gituma umuntu azosiga se na nyina, akabana n'umugore wiwe ubutakivana, bompi bakaba umubiri umwe.
49005032	Iryo banga rirahambaye, ariko ryerekeye kuri Kristo n'ishengero.
49005033	Ariko namwe nyene, umuntu wese akunde umugore wiwe nk'uko yikunda; umugore na we ni yubahe umugabo wiwe.
49006001	Bana, mwumvire abavyeyi banyu mu Mwami wacu. Kuko ivyo ari vyo bigororotse.
49006002	Wubahe so na nyoko; ico ni co cagezwe ca mbere kirimwo isezerano,
49006003	kugira ngo uronke amahoro, urambire kw'isi.
49006004	Namwe ba se, ntimukaratse abana banyu, ariko mubarere, mubahana mubahanura, uko Umwami wacu agomba.
49006005	Bashumba, mwumvire ba shobuja bo ku mubiri, nk'uko mwumvira Kristo, mububashe muhinda agashitsi, mutagira ubupfunya mu mitima yanyu.
49006006	Ntimubakorere bakibahagarikiye, nk' abanezereza abantu, ariko mubakorere nk'abashumba ba Kristo, mukora ivyo Imana igomba bivuye ku mutima.
49006007	Mubakorere n'umutima ubikunze, nk'abakorera Shobuja mukuru, ntimube nk'abakorera abantu.
49006008	Kuko muzi yuko umuntu wese iyo akoze iciza, azocishurwa na Shebuja mukuru, n'iyo yoba umushumba canke uwidegemvya.
49006009	Namwe ba shebuja, mubagirire mutyo nyene, mwirinde kubakangisha, kuko muzi yuko Shobuja musangiye ari mw'ijuru, kandi ntarobanura abantu ku butoni.
49006010	Ibisigaye, muremesherezwe mu Mwami wacu, no mu bushobozi bwiwe bwinshi.
49006011	Mwambare ibirwanisho vyose vy'Imana, kugira ngo mushobore guhagarara mudatsinzwe n'ubugunge bwa wa mugarariji.
49006012	Kuko abo tunigana atari abo inyama n'amaraso, ariko tunigana n'abakuru n'abafise ububasha n'abaganza iyi si y'umwiza, n'impwemu mbi z'ahantu ho mw'ijuru.
49006013	Kubwo ivyo mwakire ibirwanisho vyose vy'Imana, kugira ngo mushobore kudatsindwa ku musi mubi, kandi ni mwaheza vyose mugahagarara mushikamye.
49006014	Nuko rero mushikame, mukenyeje ukuri, mwambaye ukugororoka nk'inkinzo y'icuma ikingira igikiriza.
49006015	Mwambaye ibirato ari ivyo mwete w'ubutumwa bwiza bw'amahoro.
49006016	Kandi hamwe n'ivyo vyose mwakire inkinzo y'ukwizera, ni yo muzoshoboza kuzimisha imyampi ya wa Mubi yose yaka umuriro.
49006017	Mwakire inkofero y'agakiza, bo n'inkota ya Mpwemu, ni yo jambo ry'Imana.
49006018	Musengere muri Mpwemu ibihe vyose, mu buryo bwose bwo gusenga no kwinginga, kandi ivyo mubibere maso, mukobeje rwose, musengera abera bose.
49006019	Kandi nanje nyene munsengere, kugira ngo mpabwe insiguro uko mvuze kwose, namamaze nshirutse amazinda ibanga ry'ubutumwa bwiza,
49006020	kuko ndi intumwa yabwo iboheshejwe umunyororo, nsigure ivyabwo nshize amazinda, nk'uko bimbereye kuvuga.
49006021	Kandi Tukiko, umuvukanyi nkunda, umukozi w'umwizigirwa mu vy'Umwami wacu, azobiganira vyose, kugira ngo mumenye ivyanje, uko meze.
49006022	Ni we ndabatumyeko kubwo ivyo nyene, ngo mumenye ivyacu, kandi ngo aremeshe imitima yanyu.
49006023	Amahoro abe mu bavukanyi, n'urukundo rufatanije n'ukwizera, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo.
49006024	Ubuntu bw'Imana bubane n'abakunda Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bose ata bupfunya. "
50001001	Pahulo na Timoteyo, abakozi ba Kristo Yesu, turabandikiye abera bose bo muri Kristo Yesu b'i Filipi, hamwe n'abazezwashengero n'abakozi baryo. "
50001002	Ubuntu n'amahoro, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo bibabemwo.
50001003	Nshima Imana yanje, uko ndabibutse kwose.
50001004	Kandi uko nsenze kwose ndabasengera mwese nezerewe,
50001005	kuko mwafatanije nanje gukwiza ubutumwa bwiza, muhereye ku musi wa mbere, mugashitsa n'ubu.
50001006	Kandi ico nizigiye ntakekeranya, ni uko uwatanguye igikorwa ciza muri mwebwe azogiheraheza gushitsa ku musi wa Yesu Kristo.
50001007	Nanje birambereye kubiyumvirako gutyo mwese, kuko ndabafise mu mutima, kuko mu ngoyi zanje, no mu gukiranira ubutumwa bwiza no kubutsimbataza, mwese musangiye nanje ubuntu bw'Imana.
50001008	Imana ni yo ntanzeko icabona c'ingene ndabagirira igishika mwese, mfise imbabazi za Kristo Yesu. "
50001009	Kandi ico nsengera, ni ukugira ngo urukundo rwanyu rugwire rwongerekane mu bwenge no mu kumenya kwose.
50001010	Murobanure ibidahwana, muhore mutagira ubupfunya canke ibigwisha gushitsa ku musi wa Kristo,
50001011	mwuzuye imbuto zo kugororoka ziheshwa na Yesu Kristo, ngo muheshe Imana icubahiro n'ishimwe.
50001012	Bavukanyi, ndagomba ko mumenya yuko ivyambayeko canecane vyashize imbere ubutumwa bwiza.
50001013	Bituma iminyororo yanje yo kubwa Kristo imenyekana mu basoda bose bahora bacungera irembo ryo kwa Kayisari, no mu bandi bose.
50001014	Kandi abenshi bo mu bavukanyi banje bari mu Mwami wacu, baremeshejwe n'iminyororo yanje, barushiriza gutinyuka kuvuga ijambo ry'Imana bashize amazinda.
50001015	Mugabo bamwe ishari n'ibihari ni vyo bibatera kuvuga ivya Kristo; abandi babivugishwa babitumwe n'umutima mwiza.
50001016	Abo babivugishwa n'urukundo, kuko bazi ko nashiriweho gukiranira ubutumwa bwiza.
50001017	Ba bandi ikeba ni ryo ribatera kuvuga ivya Kristo atari uko bivuye ku mutima, biyumvira ko ari ukwongera kumutoneka mu ngoyi zanje.
50001018	Hari ico biriko? Kizima mu buryo bwose, ari mu buryarya ari mu kuri, Kristo avugwa, kandi ivyo ndabinezererewe, kandi nzokwama ndabinezererwa;
50001019	kuko nzi yuko ivyo bizomviramwo agakiza, munsengeye kandi mfashijwe na Mpwemu wa Yesu Kristo,
50001020	nk'uko niteze cane nkizigira yuko hatazogira ikintu kimaramaza, ariko ko mu bushizi bw'amakenga bwanje bwose Kristo aheshwe icubahiro n'umubiri wanje, nk'uko bihora biba, na none ko ari ko bizoba, naho noba ndiho canke naho noba mpfuye.
50001021	Kuko kubwanje kubaho ari Kristo, kandi gupfa ari inyungu.
50001022	Ariko namba ari ukubaho mu mubiri, ico kizonyamira imbuto z'igikorwa, kandi sinzi ico mpitamwo.
50001023	Ndazazaniwe muri ivyo bibiri, kuko nifuza gutaha ngo mbane na Kristo, kuko ari co kirushirije cane.
50001024	Yamara kuguma mu mubiri ni co corushiriza kubagirira ikimazi.
50001025	Kandi ko nizigiye ivyo, ndazi neza yuko nzogumaho, nkabana namwe mwese, kugira ngo muje imbere, munezererwe ukwizera;
50001026	ngo muzorushirize kunyirata muri Kristo Yesu nsubiye kugaruka i wanyu.
50001027	Ariko kimwe gusa, ingeso zanyu zimere nk'uko bibereye ubutumwa bwiza bwa Kristo, kugira ngo nje kubagendera canke ntaje, numve ivyanyu ko muhagaze mushikamye mufise impwemu imwe, muhuje umutima mu kurwanira ukwizera ubutumwa bwiza,
50001028	ko mudakangwa n'abansi ku kintu na kimwe; ico kizobera abo ikimenyetso co guhona, ariko mwebwe ico agakiza, kandi kivuye ku Mana.
50001029	Kuko ico mwagabiwe kubwa Kristo, atari ukumwizera gusa, ariko mwagabiwe no kubabazwa kubwiwe;
50001030	muri muri ya ntambara mwambonanye kandi iyo munyumvana n'ubu.
50002001	Nuko namba hari ukuremeshwa muri Kristo, namba hari ukwirurwa kuva mu rukundo, namba hari ugusangira Mpwemu, namba hari imbabazi n'ikigongwe,
50002002	mwuzuze umunezero wanje mwiyumvira kumwe, musangiye urukundo rumwe, muhuje umutima n'inama.
50002003	Ntimugire ico mukora kubwo gukebana canke ukwifata uko mutari, ariko mwicishije bugufi, umuntu wese yiyumvire yuko uwundi amuruta,
50002004	kandi umuntu wese ntiyiyumvire ivyiwe gusa, ariko yiyumvire n'ivyo abandi.
50002005	Mugire wa mutima muri mwebwe wari muri Kristo Yesu.
50002006	Uwo, naho yari asanganywe ishusho y'Imana, ntiyiyumviriye yuko kuringanira n'Imana ari ikintu co kwumirako.
50002007	Ariko yisiga ubusa, yakira ishusho y'umushumba, acika uwusa n'abantu.
50002008	Kandi abonetse afise ishusho nk'iyo umuntu, yicisha bugufi, aragamburuka no gushitsa ku rupfu, kandi urupfu rwo ku musaraba.
50002009	Ni co catumye Imana imushira hejuru cane, ikamuha rya zina rirengeye ayandi mazina yose.
50002010	Kugira ngo amavi yose azopfukame mw'izina rya Yesu, ayo ivyo mw'ijuru, ayo ivyo kw'isi n'ayo ivyo i kuzimu.
50002011	Kandi indimi zose zizokwature yuko Yesu Kristo ari Uhoraho, ngo biheshe Imana Data wa twese icubahiro.
50002012	Nuko rero abo nkunda, nk'uko mwamye muganduka mube ari ko mushitsa agakiza kanyu, mutinya muhinda agashitsi, yamara si iyo ndiho gusa, ariko n'ubu nyene naho ntari iyo ni murushirize kugenza gutyo.
50002013	Kuko Imana ari yo ikorera mu mitima yanyu, ikabaha gukunda no gukora ibiyihimbara.
50002014	Mukore vyose ata kwidodomba, ata guharira,
50002015	kugira ngo ntimugire umugayo canke akarohe. Mube abana b'Imana batagira agasembwa, hagati y'abo iki gihe bagoramye ibi vy'uburyo bwose, banduye mukababonekamwo mumeze nk'amatara yakira mw'isi,
50002016	mwerekana ijambo ry'ubugingo; kugira ngo mbone ico nzokwirata ku musi wa Kristo, yuko ntirukiye ubusa kandi ntaruhijwe n'ubusa.
50002017	Ariko asangwa nkwiye gutangwa ko ikimazi kubwo ukwizera kwanyu no kubwo igikorwa cakwo, ndanezerwa, nezeranwa namwe mwese.
50002018	Namwe mube ari ko munezerwa, munezeranwe nanje.
50002019	Ariko nizigijwe n'Umwami Yesu yuko nzobatumako Timoteyo vuba, kugira ngo nanje nzoshire umutima hamwe, ni namenya ivyanyu.
50002020	Simfise uwundi ari n'umutima nk'uwo uwo, yobabara ivyanyu vy'ukuri.
50002021	Kuko bose barondera ivyabo, batarondera ivya Yesu Kristo.
50002022	Ariko murazi ingene uwo twagoranywe nka kurya umwana agoranwa na se, ariko twakoranye igikorwa co gukwiza ubutumwa bwiza.
50002023	Nuko uwo ni we nizigiye yuko ari we nzoca ndabatumako, aho nzomenyera ibizombako.
50002024	Ariko nizigijwe cane n'Umwami wacu yuko nanje nyene nzoza vuba.
50002025	Kandi ndabonye yuko bikwiye kubatumako Epafurodito, muvukanyi dufatanije igikorwa n'intambara, ari we ntumwa yanyu inkorera ivyo nkenye;
50002026	kuko abagirira igishika mwese, akarandurwa umutima n'uko mwumvise yuko yari arwaye.
50002027	Kandi koko yari yararwaye ahakwa guhwera. Ariko Imana imugirira imbabazi, kandi si we wenyene, ni jewe yazigiriye, kugira ngo umubabaro wanje ntiwongerekane.
50002028	Ni co gitumye ngira umwete wo kumurungika, kugira ngo ni mwongera kumubona muzonezerwe, nanje nduhuke umubabaro.
50002029	Nuko mumwakirane umunezero mwinshi kubwo Umwami wacu; kandi abameze nk'uwo mwame mububaha;
50002030	kuko yagarukiye hafi yo gupfa kubwo igikorwa ca Kristo, yahevye amagara yiwe, amfasha ivyo mutari mwaheraheje kumfasha.
50003001	Ibisigaye bavukanyi banje, munezererwe mu Mwami wacu. Kubandikira bene ivyo ntikundambira, kandi namwe kurabaremesha.
50003002	Mwirinde za mbwa, mwirinde za nkozi z'ibibi, mwirinde bamwe bikebagura.
50003003	Kuko tweho turi abahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, dusenga Imana mu buryo bwa Mpwemu, tukirata Kristo Yesu, ntitwishimire ivyo umubiri;
50003004	naho jewe nokwishimiye ivyo umubiri. Hogira uwundi wese yokwiyumvira kwishimira ivyo umubiri, nomurusha.
50003005	Nahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo ku musi ugira umunani, ndi uwo mu bwoko bwa Isirayeli, ndi uwo mu muryango wa Benyamini, mu Baheburayo ndi Umuheburayo. Ku vyo gushimikira ivyagezwe, ndi Umufarisayo;
50003006	ku vyo ishaka nahama ishengero; ku vyo ukugororoka kuzanwa n'ivyagezwe nta wobonye ico angaya.
50003007	Ariko ivyahora bimbera inyungu ndavyiyumvira ko ari ubuhombe kubwa Kristo.
50003008	Eka mbere n'ibintu vyose ndavyiyumvira ko ari ubuhombe, kubwo ikibirengeye, ni co kumenya Kristo Yesu Umwami wanje. Kubwo uwo nahomvye ibintu vyose, ndavyiyumvira ko ari ishano, kugira ngo ndonke Kristo,
50003009	kandi mboneke ko ndi muri we, ntafise ukwanje kugororoka, kumwe kuva mu vyagezwe, ariko mfise kumwe kuzanwa no kwizera Kristo, ni kwo kugororoka kuva ku Mana, guhabwa uwizeye,
50003010	ngo ndamumenye, menye n'ubushobozi bw'ukuzuka kwiwe, n'ugufatanya na we imibabaro yiwe, nshushanywe n'urupfu rwiwe,
50003011	ngo kumbure nshike ku kuzuka kw'abapfuye.
50003012	Si ukugira ngo mpejeje kubihabwa, canke ngo mpejeje gutunganywa rwose, ariko ndabandanya kugira ngo mbone gufata kimwe catumye nanje ubwanje mfatwa na Kristo Yesu.
50003013	Bavukanyi, jeho kubwanje sinibwira yuko maze kugifata, ariko ico nkora ni iki kimwe gusa, nibagira ibiri inyuma, kandi nihutira ibiri imbere,
50003014	ndakovya gushika aho dutanguranirwa, ku mpera y'umuhamagaro w'Imana muri Kristo Yesu wo kuja mw'ijuru.
50003015	Nuko abatunganijwe uko tungana twiyumvire dutyo; kandi namba hari ico mwiyumvira ukundi, Imana izokibahishurira na co.
50003016	Mugabo rero, ukuri dushitsemwo, tube ari kwo tugenderamwo.
50003017	Bavukanyi, munyigane, mwitegereze abagenda batwigana, nk'uko mudufiseko akarorero.
50003018	Kuko benshi bagenda ukundi, abo nababwiye kenshi, n'ubu ndabababwira ndira, yuko ari abansi b'umusaraba wa Kristo.
50003019	Iherezo ryabo ni uguhona, imana yabo ni inda, biratana ibiteye isoni vyabo, ivyo isi ni vyo bababaye.
50003020	Tweho i wacu ni mw'ijuru, ni ho twiteze Umukiza ko azova, ni we Mwami Yesu Kristo,
50003021	azohindura imibiri y'amagorwa yacu, ishushanywe n'umubiri w'ubwiza bwiwe, nk'uko afise ubushobozi bumubashisha kwigarurira vyose.
50004001	Nuko rero, bavukanyi nkunda mporanira igishika, muri umunezero wanje n'igitsibo nambaye, abo nkunda, muhagarare mushikamye muri mu Mwami wacu.
50004002	Ndahanura Ewodiya, ndahanura na Sintike, ngo bahurize imitima mu Mwami wacu.
50004003	Kandi nawe dufatanije igikorwa vy'ukuri, ndakwinginga ngo wame ufasha abo bagore, kuko twarwaniye ubutumwa bwiza hamwe turi kumwe na Kilementi n'abandi bafatanije nanje, amazina yabo yanditswe mu gitabo c'ubugingo.
50004004	Mwame munezererwa mu Mwami wacu imisi yose; nongeye kubivuga; ni munezerwe.
50004005	Ubugwaneza bwanyu bumenywe n'abantu bose; Umwami wacu ari hafi.
50004006	Ntimugire ico mwiganyira, ariko muri vyose ivyo mugomba bimenyeshwe Imana, mu gusenga no mu kwinginga bifatanije no gukenguruka.
50004007	Maze amahoro y'Imana aruta uko yomenywa n'umuntu wese, azorinda imitima yanyu n'ivyiyumviro vyanyu muri Kristo Yesu. "
50004008	Ibisigaye bavukanyi, ivyo ukuri vyose, ivyo kwubahwa vyose, ibigororotse vyose, ibitanduye vyose, ivyo igikundiro vyose, ibishimwa vyose, ni haba hariho ingeso nziza, ni haba hariho gushimwa, mube ari vyo mwiyumvira.
50004009	Ivyo mwize, ivyo mwakiriye, ivyo mwumvise, ivyo mwambonanye, mube ari vyo mukora; ni ho Imana nyene amahoro izobana namwe.
50004010	Ariko ndanezererewe cane mu Mwami wacu kuko ubu mwahavuye mukongera kubabara ivyanje. Kandi mwaranabibabara, ariko mukabura uburyo.
50004011	Sindabivuze kubwo ubukene, kuko nize kubumbwa n'ivyo mfise uko ndi kose.
50004012	Nzi gucishwa bugufi, nzi no kugira umurengera; muri cose no muri vyose natiwe ibanga ryo mu vyo guhaga no mu vyo gusonza, ryo mu vyo kugira umurengera no mu vyo gukena.
50004013	Nshobozwa vyose n'uwumpa inkomezi. "
50004014	Ariko mwagize neza, kuko mwafatanije nanje amarushwa.
50004015	Kandi yemwe Bafilipi, namwe ni ico muzi yuko kw'itanguriro ry'ubutumwa bwiza, hamwe nava i Makedoniya, ata rindi shengero rya Kristo ryafatanije nanje mu vyo gutanga no guhabwa, atari mwebwe mwenyene.
50004016	Kuko n'i Tesalonike na ho mwandungikiyeyo ivyo kumara ubukene si rimwe ni kabiri kose.
50004017	Si uko ndondera ingabire, ariko ndondera imbuto zigwiririkanya amaronko yanyu.
50004018	Ariko ndafise ibinkwiye vyose, ndafise umurengera. Ndahaze, kuko mpawe na Epafurodito ivyo mwarungitse, ari umubabwe umota neza, ikimazi cemewe gihimbara Imana.
50004019	Kandi Imana yanje izobamara ubukene bwanyu bwose, nk'uko itunga ry'ubwiza ryayo riri ryo muri Kristo Yesu.
50004020	Nuko icubahiro kibe ico Imana yacu, ni yo Data wa twese, ibihe bitazoshira. Amina.
50004021	Muntahirize abera bose bo muri Kristo Yesu. Bavukanyi turi kumwe barabatasha.
50004022	Abera bose barabatasha, canecane abo mu rugo kwa Kayisari.
50004023	Ubuntu bw'Umwami Yesu Kristo bubane n'imitima yanyu.
51001001	Pahulo, nagizwe intumwa ya Kristo Yesu n'uko Imana yabigomvye, na Timoteyo umuvukanyi,
51001002	turabandikiye bavukanyi bo muri Kristo bera b'abizigirwa, muri i Kolosayi. Ubuntu n'amahoro biva ku Mana Data wa twese bibabemwo.
51001003	Dushima Imana Se w'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, twama tubasengera ubudasiba,
51001004	kuko twumvise ukwizera Kristo Yesu kwanyu, n'urukundo mufitiye abera bose,
51001005	kubwo ivyizigirwa mwabikiwe mw'ijuru, ivyo mwumvise kera, mw'ijambo ry'ukuri kw'ubutumwa bwiza,
51001006	bwabashitseko, nk'uko buri mw'isi yose bwama imbuto bugwira, kandi no muri mwebwe bugenza butyo, uhereye wa musi mwumviye mukamenya ubuntu bw'Imana vy'ukuri, "
51001007	nk'uko mwigishijwe n'uwo dukunda Epafura, umugurano mugenzi wacu, ni we mukozi wa Kristo wo kwizigirwa abagaburira ivya Kristo mu gishingo cacu,
51001008	kandi ni we yatumenyesheje urukundo rwanyu muhabwa na Mpwemu.
51001009	Ni co gituma natwe, uhereye igihe twavyumviye, tudahengeshanya kubasengera, no kubasabira ngo mwuzuzwe ukumenya ivyo igomba n'ubwenge bwose no kumenya ivyo impwemu.
51001010	Kugira ngo mugende nk'uko bibereye abo Umwami wacu, mumunezereza muri vyose, mwama imbuto mu bikorwa vyiza vyose, mugwizwa no kumenya Imana,
51001011	mushobozwa n'ubushobozi bwose, nk'uko inkomezi z'ubwiza bwayo ziri, ngo mwihangane rwose, ntimurambirwe, mubigiranye umunezero.
51001012	Mushime Data wa twese yabashoboje kuraganwa n'abera umugabane wo mu muco;
51001013	yadukijije ububasha bw'umwiza, atwimurira mu bwami bw' Umwana wiwe akunda.
51001014	Muri uwo ni ho dufise ugucungurwa, ni kwo guharirwa ivyaha vyacu.
51001015	Ni we shusho y'Imana itaboneka, ni we mfura mu vyaremwe vyose,
51001016	kuko muri we ari ho vyose vyaremewe, ivyo mw'ijuru n'ivyo mw'isi, ibiboneka n'ibitaboneka, uri intebe z'icubahiro, uri ubwami, uri ubukuru, uri ububasha; vyose vyaremwe na we, biremerwa kuba ivyiwe.
51001017	We yabayeho vyose bitarabaho, kandi muri we vyose ni ho bifataniye.
51001018	Ni we mutwe w'umubiri, ni wo shengero, kandi ni we tanguriro, ni we mfura mu kuva mu bapfuye, kugira ngo abe agaheta muri vyose.
51001019	Kuko Imana yahimbawe no kumuvyagizamwo ukwuzura kwayo kwose.
51001020	Yahimbawe kandi no kumuha kwuzuza vyose na yo, ari ivyo mw'isi, ari ivyo mw'ijuru, izanishije impore amaraso yo ku musaraba wiwe.
51001021	Namwe abari baratandukanijwe n'Imana kera, mugahindurwa abansi bayo mu mitima yanyu n'ivyo mwakoze bibi.
51001022	None ubu yarabujuje na yo abuzurije mu mubiri wiwe w'umuntu kubwo urupfu yapfuye, ngo abashikane imbere yayo muri abera, mudafise agasembwa, mutagira ico mwogawa;
51001023	asangwa muhora mwizeye, mushinzwe neza mutanyiganyiga, mudatirimuka mu vyizigiro biheshwa n'ubutumwa mwumvise, bwavuzwe mu baremwe bose bo musi y'ijuru, ubwo jewe Pahulo nacikiye umukozi wabwo.
51001024	None nezererewe amagorwa yanje yo kubwanyu, kandi ivyasigaye ku marushwa ya Kristo nanje ndabishitsa mu mubiri wanje, kubwo umubiri wiwe, ni wo shengero,
51001025	iryo nacikiye umukozi, nk'uko nahawe n'Imana ububwiriza bwo kugaburira mwebwe, kugira ngo nkwize ijambo ry'Imana rishitse,
51001026	ni ryo banga ryari ryarahishijwe uhereye kera hose n'ibihe vyose, ariko noneho ryahishuriwe abera bayo,
51001027	abo Imana yakunze kumenyesha itunga ry'ubwiza bw'iri banga, rivugwa mu banyamahanga, ni ryo Kristo ari muri mwebwe, ivyizigiro vyo kuzoronka ubwiza.
51001028	Natwe ni we twamamaza, duhanura umuntu wese, twigishisha umuntu wese ubwenge bwose, ngo dushikirize Imana umuntu wese ahinguriwe muri Kristo;
51001029	ico ni co kintamisha, ndabirwanira nk'uko ubushobozi bwiwe buri, bunkoreramwo bishimitse.
51002001	Ndagomba ko mumenya ukuntu ndabarwanira intambara, mwe n'abo i Lawodikiya n'abatarankubita ijisho bose uko bangana;
51002002	kugira ngo imitima yabo ireme, kuko bamatanirijwe mu rukundo ngo bahabwe itunga ryose ry'ugutahura ata mazinda, babone kumenya ibanga ry'Imana, ni ryo Kristo.
51002003	Muri we ni ho itunga ryose ry'ubwenge n'ukumenya ryahishijwe.
51002004	Mvuze ivyo kugira ngo ntihagire uwubahendagirisha akarimi gasosa.
51002005	Kuko naho ntari kumwe namwe ku mubiri, ndi kumwe namwe ku mutima, nezerewe kandi mbona ugushira hamwe kwanyu kwiza, n'ugushikama mu kwizera Kristo kwanyu.
51002006	Nuko nk'uko mwakiriye Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu, mube ari ko mugendera muri we,
51002007	mumushinzemwo imizi, mumwubakwamwo, mushikamishijwe n'ukwizera nk'uko mwigishijwe, murushiriza gushima.
51002008	Mwirinde, ntihakagire uwubagira imbohe, abanyagishije ubwenge bw'abantu ari ibihendo vy'ubusa, bikurikira akaronda k'imigenzo y'abantu, bikurikira ivya mbere vyo mw'isi, bidakurikira Kristo.
51002009	Kuko muri we ari ho haba ukwuzura kwose kw'Ubumana mu buryo bw'umubiri.
51002010	Kandi mwuzurizwa no kumubamwo, ni we mutwe w'ubukuru bwose n'ububasha bwose.
51002011	Kandi muri we mwahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo kutari uko intoke, hamwe mwiyambura akameremere k'umubiri, ni kwo guhimburwa kwo muri Kristo;
51002012	kuko mwahambanywe na we mw'ibatizwa, ni ho kandi mwazuranywe na we, kubwo kwizera ubushobozi bw' Imana yamuzuye mu bapfuye.
51002013	Kandi hamwe mwari mugipfuye mwishwe n'ibicumuro vyanyu n'ukudahimburwa igikoba c'ubugabo kw'imibiri yanyu, yabagiranye bazima na we, imaze kuduharira ibicumuro vyacu vyose,
51002014	ihanaguye n'ikete itwagiriza, irimwo amabwirizwa yaduhama, iyikura hagati yacu na yo, iyibamba ku musaraba.
51002015	Kandi yambuye abakuru n'abafise ububasha, ibateterereza mu maso ya bose, ibashorera bafashwe mpiri kubwo uwo musaraba.
51002016	Nuko ntihakagire uwubahinyura ku biribwa, mu vyo imisi mikuru, mu vyo ukwezi kubonetse canke mu vyo isabato.
51002017	Ivyo vyari igitutu c'ivyari birariye kuzoza, ariko umutumba ubwawo ni uwa Kristo.
51002018	Ntihakagire umuntu abagunga impera yanyu, nk'uko yigombera ubwiwe, ayibagungishije kwicisha bugufi no gusenga abamarayika, aguma mu vyo yabonye gusa, atewe kwihimbariza ubusa n'ubwenge bw'akameremere kiwe,
51002019	kandi atifatanya na wa Mutwe, kuri wo umubiri wawo wose, ufashijwe n'ingingo n'imitsi, ugateranywa neza na vyo, ni ho uronka gukura kwawo gutangwa n'Imana.
51002020	Asangwa mwarapfanye na Kristo, mukareka ivya mbere vy'isi, Ni igiki gituma mwemera kuganzwa na ya mabwirizwa, nk'abazokwama bari kw'isi--
51002021	ngo, Ntugafateko, ntugatamireko, ntugakoreko;
51002022	kandi ivyo vyose biba biheze iyo biriwe--mukumvira ivyagezwe n'abantu n'inyigisho zabo?
51002023	Ayo mabwirizwa koko afise ishusho y'ubwenge, kuko abwiriza gusenga nk'uko abantu biraritse, no kwicisha bugufi, no kwibabaza umubiri, ariko ntagira ishikanwa ryo kubuza ukwifuza kw'akameremere k'umuntu.
51003001	None rero asangwa mwarazuranywe na Kristo, murondere ibiri hejuru, iyo Kristo ari, avyagiye i buryo bw'Imana.
51003002	Mushire imitima ku vyo mw'ijuru, ntimuyishire ku biri mw'isi.
51003003	Kuko mwapfuye, kandi ubugingo bwanyu bukaba buhishanijwe hamwe na Kristo mu Mana.
51003004	Kristo, ni we bugingo bwacu, ni yerekanwa, namwe muzoca mwerekanwa muri kumwe mu bwiza bwiwe.
51003005	Nuko mwice ingingo zanyu ziri mw'isi, ubushakanyi, ibihumanya, ukwifuza kw'umubiri, ukwifuza kubi kwose, no kwifuza ivyo abandi, ni kwo gusenga ibigirwamana;
51003006	ivyo ni vyo bizanira ishavu ry'Imana abantu b'intabarirwa.
51003007	Namwe mwabigenderamwo kera, hamwe mwaba muri vyo.
51003008	Ariko noneho mwiyambure n'ibi vyose: ishavu, kujingitwa, urwanko rw'ubusa, gucokorana, kandi ntihakagire amajambo ateye isoni ava mu kanwa kanyu.
51003009	Ntimukabeshane, kuko mwiyambuye umuntu wa kera n'ibikorwa vyiwe,
51003010	mukambara umuntu musha, ahindurwa musha ngo agire ubwenge, amere nk'ishusho y'Iyamuremye.
51003011	Aho ntihaba Umugiriki canke Umuyuda, uwahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo canke uwutahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, uwuvuga indimi zidatahurika canke umunyarufuri, umugurano canke uwidegemvya; ariko Kristo ni vyose, kandi ari muri bose.
51003012	Nuko rero, nk'uko bibereye abatoranijwe n'Imana bera bakundwa na yo, mwambare umutima w'ikigongwe, ineza, ukwicisha bugufi, ugutekereza n'ukwihangana,
51003013	mwihanganirana, muharirana, iyo umuntu agize ico apfa n'uwundi. Nk'uko Umwami wacu yabahariye, namwe mube ari ko muharirana.
51003014	Ikigeretse kuri ivyo vyose mwambare urukundo, ni rwo mugozi uzana gutungana.
51003015	Kandi amahoro ya Kristo aganze mu mitima yanyu, ayo mwahamagariwe ngo mube umubiri umwe. Kandi mube abama bakenguruka.
51003016	Ijambo rya Kristo ribe muri mwebwe rigwiriye, ririmwo ubwenge bwose. Mwigishanye, muhanurane, muririmba zaburi n'indirimbo n'amatazirano y'ivya Mpwemu, muririmbire Imana mu mitima yanyu mubiheshwa n'ubuntu bwayo.
51003017	Kandi ivyo muzokora vyose, mu majambo no mu bikorwa, muhore mubikora vyose mw'izina ry'Umwami Yesu, mushima Imana Data wa twese kubwo uwo.
51003018	Bagore, mugamburukire abagabo banyu, nk'uko bibereye abari mu Mwami wacu.
51003019	Bagabo, mukunde abagore banyu, ntimubabere umururazi.
51003020	Bana, mwumvire abavyeyi banyu muri vyose, kuko ivyo ari vyo bishimwa mu Mwami wacu.
51003021	Ba se, ntimukaratse abana banyu, ngo ntibacike ivutu.
51003022	Bagurano, mwumvire ba shobuja bo ku mubiri muri vyose, atari iyo babahagarikiye gusa, nk'abanezereza abantu, ariko mubakorere mushize ubwira mu mitima yanyu, mwubaha Shobuja mukuru.
51003023	Ivyo mukora vyose, mubikore bivuye mu mutima, nk'abakorera Shobuja mukuru, ntimube nk'abakorera abantu,
51003024	muzi yuko muzohabwa impera na Shobuja mukuru, ni yo wa mugabane. Shobuja uwo Kristo ni we mukorera.
51003025	Kuko uwugabitanya azokwihorwa nk'uko yagabitanije. Kandi nta kurobanura ku butoni.
51004001	Ba shebuja, namwe ni mugirire abakozi banyu ibigororotse n'ibibereye, kuko muzi yuko namwe mufise Shobuja mw'ijuru.
51004002	Mukovye mu gusenga, mukubemwo maso, mushima;
51004003	kandi natwe nyene mudusengere, kugira ngo Imana itwugururire urugi rwo kuvuga ijambo ryayo, tuvuge ibanga rya Kristo, iryo mbohewe,
51004004	kugira ngo ndariserure nk'uko nkwiye kuvuga.
51004005	Mugendane ubwenge ku bo hanze, mugura uburyo mubugwiza.
51004006	Imvugo zanyu zamane ubuntu bw'Imana, zirunzwe umunyu, kugira ngo mumenye ingene mukwiye kwishura umuntu wese.
51004007	Tukiko umuvukanyi dukunda, umukozi w'umwizigirwa, dukorana mu Mwami wacu, azobiganira ivyanje vyose.
51004008	Ni we ndabatumyeko kubwo ivyo nyene, ngo mumenye ivyacu, kandi ngo aremeshe imitima yanyu,
51004009	ndamutumanye na Onesimo umuvukanyi w'umwizigirwa, uwo dukunda, yavuye i wanyu; bazobiganira ivyo ino vyose.
51004010	Arisitariko, uwo dusangiye umunyororo, arabatasha; na Mariko, mwene se wabo wa Barunaba, arabatasha, umwe mwabwirizwa ivyiwe. Ni yaramuka aje i wanyu muzomwakire.
51004011	Na Yesu, ari we Yusito, arabatasha. Abo bonyene bo mu bahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo ni bo bakorana nanje kubwo ubwami bw'Imana, kandi bamaze umubabaro.
51004012	Epafura w'i wanyu, umushumba wa Kristo Yesu, arabatasha, yama abarwanira mu gusenga kwiwe kugira ngo mushikame, mutunganye rwose, mumenya neza mudakekeranya ivyo Imana igomba vyose.
51004013	Ndamushingira intahe yuko abagirira umwete mwinshi, mwebwe n'abo i Lawodikiya n'abo i Hiyerapoli.
51004014	Luka, umuganga akundwa, na Dema, barabatasha.
51004015	Muntahirize abavukanyi b'i Lawodikiya, na Numfa, n'ishengero ryo mu nzu yiwe.
51004016	Kandi iki cete ni mwaheza kugisomerwa, muzokwitwaririke ko gisomerwa ishengero ry'i Lawodikiya; kandi namwe muzosome ikizova i Lawodikiya nyene.
51004017	Kandi muzobarire Arukipo muti: "Urabe igikorwa c'ubusuku wahawe mu Mwami wacu, ucuzuze."
51004018	Uku ni kwo gutasha kwanje Pahulo, kwanditswe n'ukwanje kuboko. Mwibuke iminyororo yanje. Ubuntu bubane namwe.
52001001	Pahulo, Siluwano na Timoteyo turabandikiye abo mw'ishengero ry'i Tesalonike, bari mu Mana Data wa twese no mu Mwami Yesu Kristo. Ubuntu bubabemwo n'amahoro.
52001002	Mwese tubashimira Imana imisi yose, tubahoza mu kanwa uko dusenze,
52001003	twibuka ubudasiba ibikorwa vyanyu biva ku kwizera, n'ubutame buva mu rukundo, n'ukwihangana kuva ku kwizigira Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, imbere y'Imana yacu, ni yo Data wa twese. "
52001004	Bavukanyi bakundwa n'Imana, tuzi yuko mwatoranijwe na yo.
52001005	Kuko ubutumwa bwacu butabashitseko ari amajambo yonyene ariko bwarimwo n'ubushobozi na Mpwemu Yera, no kumara amazinda rwose; namwe murazi ubugene twari tumeze hagati muri mwebwe kubwanyu.
52001006	Namwe mwaratwiganye, mwigana n'Umwami wacu, mumaze kwakirira ijambo ry'Imana mu marushwa menshi, munezerejwe na Mpwemu Yera,
52001007	bituma muba ikigereranyo c'abizera bose bari i Makedoniya no muri Akaya.
52001008	Kuko muri mwebwe humvikanye ijambo ry'Umwami wacu, kandi ntiryumvikanye i Makedoniya no muri Akaya honyene, ariko ukwizera Imana kwanyu kwaramamaye hose; bituma tutarinda kugira ico tuvuga muri ivyo.
52001009	Kuko bose bivugira ubwabo inkuru z'ingene twaje muri mwebwe, kandi ingene mwahindukiriye Imana, mugaheba ibigirwamana, ngo mukorere Imana nyakuri kandi nzima,
52001010	kandi ngo mwitege Umwana wayo ko ava mw'ijuru, umwe yazura imukuye mu bapfuye, ni Yesu, adukiza ishavu rigira rize.
52002001	Bavukanyi, ubwanyu murazi yuko ugushika muri mwebwe kwacu kutabaye uko ubusa;
52002002	ariko tumaze kubabarizwa i Filipi no kuhatetererezwa, nk'uko muzi, dushira amanga mu Mana yacu kubwira mwebwe ubutumwa bwiza bw'Imana turi mu ntambara nyinshi.
52002003	Kuko uguhanura kwacu kutava mu buzimire, canke mu buhumane, kandi atari uko ubugunge;
52002004	ariko nk'uko Imana yatwemeye ko turi abo kuzezwa ubutumwa, ni ko tuvuga. Ntituvuga nk'abagomba kunezereza abantu, ariko nk'abagomba kunezereza Imana isuzuma imitima yacu.
52002005	Kuko ata na rimwe twigeze kuvuga ijambo ducishije iruhande, murabizi, canke ijambo ryo guhisha ukunohoka, Imana ni yo cabona c'ivyo.
52002006	Kandi ntitwarondera icubahiro co ku bantu, ari kuri mwebwe canke ku bandi; naho tuba twarashoboye kubaremera, kuko turi intumwa za Kristo.
52002007	Ariko twaritonda hagati muri mwebwe, nk'uko umuvyeyi abungabunga abana biwe.
52002008	Ni ko twabagirira igishika, ni co catumye duhimbarwa no kubaha, si ubutumwa bwiza bw'Imana gusa, ariko n'ubwacu bugingo na bwo, kuko mwabaye abo dukunda rwose.
52002009	Bavukanyi, muribuka ubutame bwacu n'ubucumukure; twababwira ubutumwa bwiza bw'Imana. Twakora umurango n'ijoro, kugira ngo ntihagire uwo muri mwebwe turemera.
52002010	Mwebwe muri ivyabona hamwe n'Imana vy'ingene twamerera mwebwe abizera, turi abera, tugororoka, tutariko umugayo.
52002011	Nk'uko muzi ingene twari tumeze ku muntu wese muri mwebwe, nk'uko se amera ku bana biwe, tubahanura, tubaremesha, dushinga intahe,
52002012	kugira ngo mugende nk'uko bibereye ab' Imana, ibahamagarira kuja mu bwami bwayo no mu bwiza bwayo.
52002013	Natwe igituma dushima Imana ubudasiba, ni uko hamwe mwakira ijambo ry'ubutumwa mwatwumvanye, ni ryo ry'Imana, mutaryemeye nk'ijambo ry'abantu, ariko nk'ijambo ry'Imana, nk'uko riri koko, rikorera muri mwebwe abizera.
52002014	Namwe bavukanyi, mwiganye amashengero y'Imana y'i Yudaya, ari muri Kristo Yesu, kuko ivyo mwababajwe n'ubwoko bwanyu ari bimwe n'ivyo abo bababajwe n'Abayuda,
52002015	bishe Umwami Yesu n'abavugishwa n'Imana, kandi natwe baratwirukanye, ntibanezereje Imana, barwanya abantu bose;
52002016	batubuza kubarira abanyamahanga ngo bakire; na ntaryo buzuza ingero y'ivyaha vyabo. Ariko ishavu rirabashikiye kubamara rwose.
52002017	Ariko twebwe, bavukanyi, hamwe twatandukanywa namwe igihe gito ubwo amaso, ariko si mu mutima, twarushirije kugira umwete wo kubonana namwe imbonankubone, tubafitiye inkumbu nyinshi;
52002018	kuko twagomba kuza i wanyu, mbere jewe Pahulo kubigomba si rimwe ni kabiri kose, Satani akatubuza.
52002019	None ivyizigiro vyacu n'iki, canke umunezero, canke igitsibo co mu mutwe twirata? Mbega si mwebwe, imbere y'Umwami wacu Yesu aho azozira?
52002020	Kuko ari mwebwe cubahiro cacu n'umunezero wacu.
52003001	Nuko tutagishoboye kwihangana, dushima gusigara twenyene muri Atenayi,
52003002	dutuma Timoteyo, muvukanyi, umukozi w'Imana agabura ubutumwa bwiza bwa Kristo, ngo abakomeze abaremeshe ku vyo ukwizera kwanyu,
52003003	kugira ngo ntihagire uwo muri mwebwe anyiganyizwa n'ayo marushwa; kuko ubwanyu muzi yuko ari ico twashiriweho nyene.
52003004	Kandi hamwe twari kumwe namwe, twababuriye yuko tutazobura kubabazwa; kandi ni ko vyabaye, murabizi.
