52003005	Nanje ni co catumye ntuma iyo, bitakinkundiye kwihangana, kugira ngo menye ukwizera kwanyu, nikenga ko wa musukanyi yoba yarabasutse, natwe tukaba twaratamijwe n'ubusa.
52003006	Ariko none Timoteyo arashitse, avuye i wanyu, atuzaniye inkuru nziza y'ukwizera kwanyu n'urukundo rwanyu, kandi yuko mutwibuka neza imisi yose, mudukumbura mugomba kubonana natwe, nk'uko natwe tubakumbura.
52003007	Ni co catumye bavukanyi, turemeshwa kubwanyu n'ukwizera kwanyu, mu mubabaro wacu wose no mu marushwa.
52003008	Kuko none turiho, asangwa muhagaze mu Mwami.
52003009	Ni ishimwe ki twoshobora kwishura Imana kubwanyu, kubwo umunezero wose tubanezererwa imbere y'Imana yacu?
52003010	Dusenga cane ijoro n'umurango kugira ngo twibonanire namwe imbonankubone, tunonosore ivyasigaye ku kwizera kwanyu.
52003011	None Imana yacu ubwayo, ni yo Data wa twese, n'Umwami wacu Yesu, agorore inzira yacu yo kuza iyo.
52003012	Namwe Umwami wacu abagwirize, abongerereze urukundo mukundana, no gukunda abandi bose, nk'uko natwe tumeze kuri mwebwe;
52003013	kugira ngo aremeshe imitima yanyu, ntigire umugayo, ibe iyera imbere y'Imana yacu ni yo Data wa twese, izosangwe ityo aho Umwami wacu Yesu azozananira n'abera biwe bose.
52004001	Nuko bavukanyi, ibisigaye, turabinginga tubahanura mu Mwami Yesu, nk'uko mwize kuri twebwe ingene mukwiye kugenda no kunezereza Imana (kandi ni ko mugenda), murushirize cane kugenza mutyo.
52004002	Murazi ivyagezwe twahawe n'Umwami Yesu kubabarira ivyo ari vyo.
52004003	Ico Imana igomba, ni ukwezwa kwanyu, ko mwirinda ubushakanyi;
52004004	kugira ngo umuntu wese muri mwebwe amenye kuganziriza uwiwe mubiri mu kwezwa no mu kuwubaha,
52004005	atari mu buryo bwo kwangaza umutima mu vyifuzo, nk'uko abanyamahanga batazi Imana bagira;
52004006	ngo umuntu wese ntarenge ibikwiye, kandi ntagunge umuvukanyi wundi kuri ivyo, kuko Umwami wacu ari umuhozi kuri ivyo vyose, nk'uko twababuriye tuvyemeza.
52004007	Kuko Imana itaduhamagariye guhumana, ariko yaduhamagariye kwezwa.
52004008	Ni co gituma uwuvyanka ataba yanse umuntu ariko aba yanse Imana, kandi ari yo ibaha Mpwemu wayo Yera.
52004009	Ariko ivyo gukunda bavukanyi ntimurinda kuvyandikirwa, kuko ubwanyu mwigishijwe n' Imana gukundana;
52004010	kandi ni ko nyene mugiriranira n'abavukanyi bose b'i Makedoniya hose. Ariko bavukanyi turabahanura ngo murushirize kugira rwinshi.
52004011	Kandi mushishikare kwiyorosha, no gukora ivyanyu, no gukoresha amaboko yanyu, nk'uko twababariye,
52004012	kugira ngo mugendane ingeso nziza ku bo hanze, kandi mutagira ico mukenye.
52004013	Ariko bavukanyi, ntitugomba ko muyoberwa ivyo abasinzira itiro ry'urupfu, ngo ntimubabare nka ba bandi badafise ivyizigiro.
52004014	Uko twizera yuko Yesu yapfuye akazuka, tube ari ko twizera yuko abasinziririye muri Yesu, Imana izobazanana na we.
52004015	Iki ni co tubabwira, ni ijambo ry'Umwami twashikirijwe, yuko twebwe abazoba bakiriho, dusigaye gushitsa ku kuza kw'Umwami wacu, tutazokwitangira na gatoya imbere y' abasinziriye.
52004016	Kuko Umwami wacu ubwiwe azoza, amanutse avuye mw'ijuru, aranguruye ijwi rirenga, hamwe n'akamo k'umumarayika mukuru, n'inzumbeti y'Imana. Maze abapfiriye muri Kristo ni bo bazobanza kuzuka;
52004017	maze natwe abazoba bakiriho, dusigaye, tuzoca duteruranwa na bo mu bicu, dusanganirire Umwami mu kirere. Ni ho tuzokwama tubana n'Umwami.
52004018	Nuko mwiruranishe ayo majambo.
52005001	Ariko bavukanyi, ivyo ibihe n'imisi ntimurinda kuvyandikirwa.
52005002	Kuko ubwanyu muzi neza yuko umusi w'Umwami wacu uzoza nk'uko igisuma kiza mw'ijoro.
52005003	Aho bazoba bavuga bati: "Hari amahoro, nta nkomanzi; ni ho uguhona kuzobazako giturumbuka, nk'uko ibise biza ku mugore akuriwe, kandi ntibazokwikiza na gatoya."
52005004	Ariko mweho, bavukanyi, ntimuri mu mwiza, ngo uwo musi ubashikeko giturumbuka;
52005005	kuko mwese muri abana b'umuco n'abana b'umurango. Ntituri abo ijoro canke abo umwiza.
52005006	Nuko rero ntidusinzire nka ba bandi, ariko twame tugavye, twirinde ibiboreza.
52005007	Kuko abasinzira basinzira mw'ijoro, n'ababorerwa baborerwa mw'ijoro.
52005008	Ariko tweho, ko turi abo umurango, twirinde ibiboreza, twambaye icuma gikingira igikiriza c'ukwizera n'urukundo, kandi twambaye nk'inkofero ukwizigira agakiza.
52005009	Kuko Imana itadushiriyeho kuturakira, ariko yadushiriyeho guheshwa agakiza n'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo,
52005010	ni we yadupfiriye kugira ngo tubaneho na we, ari iyo turi maso canke dusinziriye itiro ry'urupfu.
52005011	Nuko muhanurane, mukomezanye, nk'uko mubikora nyene.
52005012	Ariko bavukanyi, turabinginga, mumenye abakora muri mwebwe bagatama, babaganza mu Mwami wacu, bakabahanura,
52005013	mububahe rwose mu rukundo kubwo igikorwa cabo. Mubane amahoro.
52005014	Kandi turabahanura, bavukanyi, muhanure abasaragurika batagomba gukora, muremeshe abarandutse imitima, muramire abanyantege nke, mwihanganire bose.
52005015	Mwirinde, ntihagire umuntu yihora uwundi ikibi yamugiriye, ariko mwame mukurikira iciza mu vyo mugiriranira no mu vyo mugirira abandi bose.
52005016	Munezerwe imisi yose;
52005017	musenge ubudasiba;
52005018	mwame mukenguruka muri vyose, kuko ico ari co Imana ibagombako muri Kristo Yesu.
52005019	Ntimukazimye Mpwemu;
52005020	ntimugakengere ivyo abavugishwa n'Imana;
52005021	musuzume vyose, mugumye ivyiza,
52005022	mwirinde icitwa ikibi cose.
52005023	Kandi Imana Nyenamahoro ibe ari yo ibeza rwose. Kandi impwemu yanyu, ubugingo n'umubiri wose hamwe bizigamwe, ngo bizosangwe bitagira umugayo, aho umwami wacu Yesu Kristo azozira.
52005024	Iyibahamagara ni iyo kwizigirwa; no kubikora izobikora.
52005025	Bavukanyi, mudusengere.
52005026	Muramukishe abavukanyi kugumbirana kwera.
52005027	Ndabarahiye Umwami wacu, iki cete ntikizobure gusomerwa mu bavukanyi bose.
52005028	Ubuntu bw'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane namwe.
53001001	Pahulo na Siluwano na Timoteyo turabandikiye abo mw'ishengero ry'i Tesalonike, bari mu Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo.
53001002	Ubuntu n'amahoro biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo bibe muri mwebwe.
53001003	Biradukwiye kwama tubashimira Imana, bavukanyi, nk'uko bikwiye, kuko ukwizera kwanyu gukura cane, n'urukundo rw'umuntu wese muri mwebwe mukundana rugwira.
53001004	Ni co gituma ubwacu tubirata mu mashengero y'Imana, kubwo ukwihangana kwanyu n'ukwizera mu guhamwa kwanyu kwose n'amagorwa mushinyiriza.
53001005	Ico ni ikimenyetso co guca imanza kw'Imana kugororotse, ngo muzokwemererwe gushika mu bwami bw'Imana, ubwo namwe mubabarizwa.
53001006	Kuko ari ibigororotse ku Mana kwishura amarushwa abayabatera,
53001007	no kwishura mwebwe abayaterwa kuruhukana natwe, aho Umwami Yesu azohishurirwa, ava mw'ijuru, azananye n'abamarayika b'ubushobozi bwiwe,
53001008	hagati mu muriro waka, yishure guhorwa abatamenye Imana n'abatumvira ubutumwa bwiza bw'Umwami wacu Yesu.
53001009	Bazohanwa, ni kwo guhona kw'ibihe bidashira, kuva mu maso y'Umwami no mu bwiza bw'ubushobozi bwiwe,
53001010	aho azozira gushimirwa mu bera biwe kuri wa musi, no gutangarirwa kubwo abamwizeye bose, kuko intahe twashinze muri mwebwe yemewe.
53001011	Ni co gituma tubasengera imisi yose, ngo Imana yacu ibemere ko mumeze nk'uko bibereye ihamagarwa ryanyu, kandi ishikishe ubushobozi iciza cose munezererwa n'igikorwa canyu cose kiva ku kwizera:
53001012	kugira ngo izina ry'Umwami wacu Yesu rishimagizwe muri mwebwe, namwe mushimagizwe muri we, nk'uko ubuntu bw'Imana yacu n'ubwo Umwami Yesu Kristo buri.
53002001	Turabinginga, bavukanyi, kubwo kuzoza kw'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo no kuzokoranirizwa kuri we kwacu,
53002002	ntimushoke munyiganyiga ngo mugwe igihumura, canke ngo muhagarike imitima, naho mwoba mubitewe n'impwemu canke n'ijambo canke n'ikete rimeze nk'irivuye kuri twebwe, rivuga yuko umusi w'Umwami wacu uhejeje gushika.
53002003	Ntihakagire umuntu abahenda mu buryo na bumwe, kuko utazoza, kwa kureka Imana kutabanje kuboneka, kandi wa muntu w'umugarariji atarahishurwa, ni we mwana wo kuranduka,
53002004	umurwanizi yishira hejuru y'icitwa Imana cose canke igisengwa; nuko azokwicara mu rusengero rw' Imana, yiyerekana ngo ni Imana.
53002005	Ntimwibuka yuko nababwiye ivyo nkiri kumwe namwe?
53002006	Kandi none murazi ikibuza, kugira ngo azohishurwe mu gihe ciwe.
53002007	Kuko ibanga ry'umugararizo n'ubu ririko rirakora, mugabo hari uwubibuza ubu, gushitsa igihe azokurirwaho.
53002008	Ni ho wa mugarariji azohishurirwa, umwe Umwami Yesu azokwicisha impwemu ziva mu kanwa kiwe, azomutituza uguseruka kw'ukuza kwiwe.
53002009	Ukuza kw'uwo mugarariji kuri mu buryo bw'inkomezi za Satani, kuri n'ubushobozi bwose n'ibimenyetso n'ibitangaza vy'ibinyoma,
53002010	n'ubugunge bwose bwo kugabitanya ku bahona, kuko batemeye gukunda ivyo ukuri ngo bakizwe.
53002011	Ni co gituma Imana ibarungikira ubuzimire bubakoreramwo, ngo bizere ibinyoma:
53002012	kugira ngo abatizeye ukuri bose, bagahimbarirwa ukugabitanya, batsindwe n'urubanza.
53002013	Ariko bavukanyi bakundwa n'Umwami wacu, biradukwiye kwama tubashimira Imana, kuko uhereye mu bihe vya kera Imana yabatoranije ngo muronkere agakiza mu kwezwa na Mpwemu no mu kwizera ukuri.
53002014	Ni vyo yabahamagariye, ibahamagarishije ubutumwa bwiza twajejwe, kugira ngo muhabwe ubwiza bw'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo.
53002015	Nuko bavukanyi, mushikame, mugumye ivyo mwashikirijwe, mwigishijwe, ari ivyo mwigishirijwe mu majambo canke mw'ikete ryacu.
53002016	Ariko, Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo ubwiwe, n'Imana Data wa twese, yadukunze, ikaduha kwirurwa imibabaro guhoraho, bo n'ivyizigiro vyiza biheshwa n'ubuntu bwayo,
53002017	babirure mu mitima yanyu, bayikomeze mu gikorwa cose ciza, n'ijambo ryose ryiza.
53003001	Ibisigaye bavukanyi mudusengere, ijambo ry'Umwami wacu ryamamare rishimagizwe, nk'uko biri no muri mwebwe,
53003002	kandi dukire abantu babi badadika; kuko ukwizera kudafiswe na bose.
53003003	Ariko, Umwami n'uwo kwizigirwa, ni we azobashinga neza abarinde wa Mubi.
53003004	Kandi twizigiye Umwami ku vyanyu, yuko ivyo tugeze mubikora kandi muzokwama mubikora.
53003005	Umwami arongore imitima yanyu, ayerekeze ku rukundo rw'Imana no ku kwihangana kwa Kristo.
53003006	Ariko bavukanyi, turabagera mw'izina ry'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, kuzibukira umuvukanyi wese w'umunebwe, canke adakurikira ivyo mwashikirijwe natwe.
53003007	Ubwanyu murazi ingene mukwiye kutwigana, kuko tutari abanebwe muri mwebwe,
53003008	ntitwarya ivyo kurya vy' umuntu n'umwe ku busa, ariko twagira ubutame n'ubucumukure, dukora ku murango no mw'ijoro, kugira ngo ntitugire umuntu muri mwebwe tugora.
53003009	Si uko tutavyemerewe, ariko ni ukugira ngo tubabere icitegererezo ngo mutwigane.
53003010	Kuko tukiri kumwe namwe twabageze iki, ngo umuntu wese ni yanka gukora ntakarye.
53003011	Kuko twumvise yuko hariho bamwe bo muri mwebwe bagenda basaragurika, bama bineganegera bakita mu bitabakwiye.
53003012	Ariko abameze bartyo turabagera tubahanura kubwo Umwami Yesu Kristo, gukora ibikorwa batekereje, babone kurya ivyo bironkeye ubwabo.
53003013	Ariko mweho bavukanyi, ntimurambirwe no gukora iciza.
53003014	Ni hagira umuntu atumvira ijambo ryacu ryo muri iri kete, mumwitegereze, ntimufatanye na we, kugira ngo amaramare.
53003015	Ariko ntimumwiyumvire ko ari umwansi wanyu, ariko mumuhanure nka umwana wa So.
53003016	Kandi Umwami Nyenamahoro ubwiwe, yame abaha amahoro ibihe vyose uburyo bwose. Umwami abane namwe mwese.
53003017	Uku ni kwo gutasha kwanje jewe Pahulo, kwanditswe n'ukwanje kuboko, ni co kimenyetso mu kete ryanje ryose: ni ko nandika.

54001001	Pahulo, intumwa ya Kristo Yesu, nk'uko vyagezwe n' Imana Umukiza wacu na Kristo Yesu ivyizigiro vyacu,
54001002	ndakwandikiye Timoteyo, umwana wanje nyakuri mu kwizera. Ubuntu, imbabazi n'amahoro biva ku Mana Data wa twese no kuri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu bikubeko.
54001003	Nuko guma muri Efeso, nk'uko nakugiriye inama hamwe naja i Makedoniya, kugira ngo uteshe ba bandi ntibigishe ibiteye ukundi.
54001004	Ntibababare ivyo imigani y'ibinyoma n'ivyo kuzura akaboze k'urufatane rw'imiryango katagira iherezo, bidafasha igikorwa c'Imana gikorera mu kwizera, ariko bizana impari.
54001005	Ariko inyanduruko y'ukwigisha kwacu ni ukugira ngo bagire urukundo ruva mu mutima utanduye, utarimwo ijwi ribagiriza ikibi, no ku kwizera kutari ukwo uburyarya.
54001006	Ivyo bamwe barabihushije, bata inzira, baja mu bitagira ikimazi biba ari vyo bavuga.
54001007	Bagomba kuba abigisha b'ivyagezwe, ariko ntibatahura ivyo bavuga n'ivyo bashingira intahe babishimikiye. "
54001008	Ariko turazi yuko ivyagezwe ari vyiza, iyo umuntu abigenjeje nk'uko bikwiye ivyagezwe,
54001009	azi yuko ivyagezwe bitashiriweho umugororotsi, ariko vyashiriweho abagarariji n'ibigaba, abatubaha Imana n'abanyavyaha, abanegura ivyayo n'abakora ibizira, abica ba se na ba nyina, abicanyi,
54001010	abashakanyi, abagabo basambana n'abandi bagabo, abanyaga abantu bakabashora, ababeshi, abarahira nabi, n'ibindi vyose birwanya ukwigisha kuzima,
54001011	gukurikira ubutumwa bw'ubwiza bw'Imana ishemagizwa, ubwo najejwe.
54001012	Ndashimira Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu yabinshoboje, kuko yanyiyumviriye ko ndi uwo kwizigirwa, akampa ubusuku;
54001013	naho nabanje kumutyoza, kumuhiga no kumwambika ibara. Ariko naragiriwe ikigongwe kuko nabikoze ntabizi ntarizera.
54001014	Kandi ubuntu bw' Umwami wacu bwiyongeranyako, bo n'ukwizera n'urukundo rubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu.
54001015	Iri jambo ni iryo kwizerwa, rikwiye kwemerwa rwose, yuko Kristo Yesu yazanywe mw'isi no gukiza abanyavyaha; muri bo jewe ndi agahebuza.
54001016	Ariko, icatumye ngirirwa ikigongwe ni ukugira ngo Yesu Kristo anyerekaniremwo gahebuza, ukwihangana kwiwe kwose, mbe icitegererezo c'abazomwizera bakaronka ubugingo budashira.
54001017	Umwami ahoraho, adapfa, ataboneka, ari we Mana imwe yonyene, igitinyiro n'icubahiro bibe ivyayo, ibihe bitazoshira. Amina.
54001018	Iri bwirizwa ndariguhaye, mwana wanje Timoteyo, nk'uko abavugishwa n'Imana bakuvuzeko ubwa mbere, ngo ufashwe na vyo kurwana intambara nziza.
54001019	Ugumye ukwizera, ufise umutima utarimwo ijwi rikwagiriza ikibi; iryo bamwe bashibuye bakamera nk'ubwato busavye mu vy'ukwizera.
54001020	Muri abo, umwe ni Humenayo na Alekisandero, abo nahaye Satani, kugira ngo bibigishe kudatyoza Imana.
54002001	Irya mbere y'ibindi vyose, ndabahanura kwingingira abantu bose, kubasengera, kubasabira no kubashimira Imana;
54002002	kandi canecane abami n'abashizwe hejuru bose, kugira ngo twame mu mahoro dutekereje, twubaha Imana turi inyankamugayo rwose.
54002003	Ivyo ni vyo vyiza vyemerwa mu maso y'Imana Umukiza wacu,
54002004	igomba ko abantu bose bakizwa bagashika ku kumenya ivyo ukuri.
54002005	Kuko hari Imana imwe, kandi hari Umuhuza umwe w'Imana n'abantu, na we nyene ni umuntu, ni Kristo Yesu,
54002006	yitanze ko incungu ya bose. Kandi ivyo bishingirwe intahe mu bihe vyavyo,
54002007	ni co nashiriweho kuba umusiguzi n'intumwa (mvuze ukuri, simbeshe) ni umwigisha wo kwigisha abanyamahanga ukwizera n'ivyo ukuri.
54002008	Nuko ndagomba ko abagabo basenga hose, batarika amaboko yera, bataratse, batagira ibihari.
54002009	Kandi n'abagore nyene, ndagomba ko bambara imyambaro biberanye, bagendane isoni badasaragurika kandi badashazisha gutsiba umushatsi, canke izahabu, canke ubudede, canke impuzu z'igiciro kinini,
54002010	ariko bashazishe ibikorwa vy'ingeso nziza, nk'uko bikwiye abagore bavuga yuko bubaha Imana.
54002011	Umugore yige atekereje agamburuka rwose.
54002012	Ariko sinkundira umugore ko yigisha canke ko aganza umugabo, ariko atekereze.
54002013	Kuko Adamu ari we yabanje kuremwa, hanyuma Eva.
54002014	Kandi Adamu si we yahenzwe, ariko umugore ni we yahenzwe, agwa mu bicumuro.
54002015	Yamara azokizwa kubwo ukuvyara, ni bashishikara kwizera no kugira urukundo no kwezwa, bifatanye no kwitonda.
54003001	Iri jambo ni iryo kwizerwa; umuntu ni yagomba kuzezwa ishengero, aba yifuje igikorwa ciza.
54003002	Nuko umuzezwashengero akwiye kutabako umugayo, kandi akwiye kuba umugabo afise umugore umwe gusa; abe uwutarenza urugero, yitonda, aganza ingeso ziwe, akunda gutanga indaro, afise ubwenge bwo kwigisha,
54003003	atari umunoho w'umuvinyu, canke umusinzi, ariko abe umugwaneza, atitoraguza, atari inkunzi y'amahera,
54003004	aganza neza abo mu rugo rwiwe, abana biwe bamwumvira, yanka umugayo wose.
54003005	(Uwutazi kuganza abo mu rugo rwiwe yoshobora ate kuzigama ishengero ry'Imana?)
54003006	Kandi ntakwiye kuba muto mu kwizera, kugira ngo ntiyikakishe, ngo atembe, agacirwako iteka wa mugarariji yaciriweko.
54003007	Kandi akwiye gushingirwa intahe neza n'abo hanze, kugira ngo ntatembere mu mugayo no mu mutego wa wa mugarariji.
54003008	Kandi n'abadiyakoni b'ishengero na bo nyene, bakwiye kuba inyankamugayo batavuga indimi zibiri, kandi ntibabe abatwawe n'umuvinyu mwinshi, canke abifuza inyungu mbi.
54003009	Ariko bagumye ibanga ry'ukwizera, bafise imitima itarimwo ijwi ribagiriza ikibi.
54003010	Kandi abo babanze kumenyerezwa, maze ni batabonekako umugayo babone gukora igikorwa c'ibango ryabo.
54003011	N'abagore nyene babe inyankamugayo, batarementaniriza abandi, batarenza urugero, bizigirwa muri vyose.
54003012	Umukozi w'ishengero wese abe umugabo afise umugore umwe gusa, aganza neza abana biwe n'abo mu rugo rwiwe.
54003013	Kuko abakoze neza ico gikorwa c'ibango ryabo bironkera ikibanza c'iteka n'umwidegemvyo mwinshi mu kwizera Kristo Yesu.
54003014	Nkwandikiye ivyo, nizigiye ko nzoza i wawe vuba.
54003015	Ariko ni naba ngitevye ni ukugira ngo uzomenye uko bikwiye kugenzwa mu ngoro y'Imana, ni yo shengero ry'Imana nzima, vyongeye ni yo nkingi ishigikiye ukuri.
54003016	Nta wuhakana yuko ibanga ryo kwubaha Imana ridahambaye cane, ni iri: umwe yerekanywe afise umubiri, akaboneka ko ari umugororotsi mu mpwemu, akabonwa n'abamarayika, akamenyekanishwa mu banyamahanga, akizererwa mw'isi, akaduzwa agahabwa ubwiza.
54004001	Ariko Mpwemu avuga avyeruye yuko mu bihe bizoza bamwe bazota ivyizerwa, bagashira umutima ku vyo impwemu zizimiza no ku vyo inyigisho z'abadayimoni,
54004002	bavugisha uburyarya bw'abanyabinyoma, batewe ikidodo mu mitima yabo ibagiriza ikibi,
54004003	babuza kurongora no kurya ivyo kurya, kandi ari vyo Imana yaremye kugira ngo abizera, bakamenya ivyo ukuri, babirye bashima.
54004004	Ico Imana yaremye cose ni ciza, ntiharimwo ico gutabwa, iyo cakiriwe n'uwushima;
54004005	kuko kiba gihezagiwe n'ijambo ry'Imana no gusenga.
54004006	Ni wibutsa abavukanyi ivyo, uzoba uri umukozi mwiza wa Kristo Yesu, yarerewe mu majambo y'ukwizera n'ayo inyigisho nziza wakurikiye.
54004007	Ariko imigani ihumanya n'iyo abakecuru ntuyemere. Wimenyereze kwubaha Imana;
54004008	kuko kwimenyereza kw'umubiri kugira ikimazi kuri bike, ariko kwubaha Imana kugira ikimazi kuri vyose, kuko kuzana isezerano ry'ubugingo bw'ubu n'ubuzoza.
54004009	Iryo jambo ni iryo kwizerwa rikwiye kwemerwa rwose.
54004010	Kuko igituma turuha tukama mu ntambara ari uko twizigiye Imana nzima, ni yo Mukiza w'abantu bose, canecane w'abizera.
54004011	Wame ubwiriza ivyo kandi uvyigisha.
54004012	Ntihakagire uwukugayira ubusore, ariko ubere abizera ikigereranyo mu vyo uvuga, mu ngeso zawe, mu rukundo, mu kwizera no ku mutima utanduye.
54004013	Gushitsa aho nzozira wame ugira umwete wo gusomera abantu, kubahanura no kubigisha.
54004014	Ntiwanjanjwe ku ngabire iri muri wewe, imwe waheshwa n'ivyo abavugishwa n' Imana mu kurambikwako ibiganza vy'abakuru.
54004015	Ivyo ubishireko umwete, uvyamemwo, kugira ngo kuja imbere kwawe kubonekere bose.
54004016	Wirinde ubwawe no ku vyo wigisha. Wame ushishikara ivyo, kuko ni wagira utyo uzokwikizanya n'abakwumva.
54005001	Ntuhambarire umutama, ariko umuhanure nka so, abakiri bato n'imisore ubahanure nk'abavukanyi bawe.
54005002	Abatamakazi nyene ubahanure nka ba nyoko, abakiri bato n'abigeme nka bashiki bawe, uri n'umutima utanduye na gatoya.
54005003	Wubahe abapfakazi b'inyakamwe vy'ukuri.
54005004	Ariko, umupfakazi wese, namba afise abana canke abuzukuru, ni babanze kwiga kwubaha Imana ku vyo bagirira ababo, no kwishura ivyiza abavyeyi babo; kuko ivyo ari vyo bishimwa mu maso y'Imana.
54005005	Umupfakazi w'inyakamwe asigaye ari umwe, yizigira Imana, agashishikara kwinginga no gusenga ku murango no mw'ijoro.
54005006	Ariko, uwihaye ukwifuza aba apfuye ahagaze.
54005007	Ubabwirize ivyo, kugira ngo ntibabeko umugayo.
54005008	Ariko umuntu ni atatunga abo mu nzu y'i wabo, canecane abiwe, azoba yihakanye ukwizera, kandi azoba abaye hanyuma y'uwutizera.
54005009	Ntihakagire umupfakazi yandikirwa gufashwa ataramara imyaka mirongo itandatu y'amavuka, kandi handikwe uwari afiswe n'umugabo umwe gusa.
54005010	Handikwe uwushimirwa ibikorwa vyiza, namba yararera abana, namba yaratanga indaro, yaroza ibirenge vy'abera, yarafasha abababaye, yarashishikara gukurikira ibikorwa vyiza vyose.
54005011	Ariko abapfakazi bakiri bato ntubemerere, kuko kwifuza kw'umubiri ni kwamara kubatera kugarariza Kristo bazogomba kurongorwa,
54005012	bagatsindwa n'urubanza kuko bavuye mw'isezerano ryabo rya mbere.
54005013	Kandi ikindi, biga kugira ubunebwe, bagenda imihana; ariko rero si ubunebwe gusa, ikigeretseko bararegeteranya bita mu bitari ivyabo, bavuga ivyo badakwiye.
54005014	Ni co gituma ngomba ko abapfakazi bakiri bato barongorwa, bakavyara abana, bakubaka ingo zabo, ntibahe umwansi urwitwazo rw'ibitutsi.
54005015	Kuko n'ubu bamwe bamaze guta inzira, ngo bakurikire Satani.
54005016	Umugore wese yizera namba afise incuti z'abapfakazi, abafashe, ishengero ntiriremerwe, ribone gufasha abapfakazi b'inyakamwe.
54005017	Abakuru b'ishengero baganza neza ni babiyumvire ko bakwiye guhabwa icubahiro kirushiriza, kandi canecane abacumukura mu kuvuga ijambo ry'Imana no mu kwigisha.
54005018	Kuko icanditswe kivuga, ngo Ntimuzorumye umunwa w'inka iriko irasekura ingano; kandi ngo Umukozi akwiye ingero yiwe.
54005019	Umukuru ntukemere ico bazomukuregako hatabonetse ivyabona bibiri canke bitatu.
54005020	Abakora ivyaha ubahanire mu maso ya bose, kugira ngo abandi na bo batinye.
54005021	Ndakwihanikiririza mu maso y'Imana na Yesu Kristo n'imbere y'abamarayika batoranijwe, witondere ivyo, ntuce urwo umwe, ntukore ivyo guca urwa nkunzi.
54005022	Ntukagire umuntu wihutira kurambikako ibiganza, kandi ntugafatanye n'abandi mu vyaha vyabo. Uzokwame wirinda ubuhumane.
54005023	Uhereye ubu ntunywe amazi gusa, ariko unywe n'utuvinyu dukeya kubwo mu nda hawe, kuko urwaragurika.
54005024	Hari abantu ivyaha vyabo biboneka bikabatanga mu kuja mu rubanza; hari n'abandi bibaza inyuma.
54005025	Kandi ibikorwa vyiza na vyo ni uko, hari ibiboneka; kandi n'ibitameze bityo ntibishobora kunyegezwa.
54006001	Abaja bose bari mu buja ni biyumvire ba shebuja ko bakwiye kwubahwa rwose, ngo izina ry'Imana n'ukwigisha ntibitukwe.
54006002	Kandi abafise ba shebuja bizera, ntibagayishwe n'uko ari abavukanyi, ariko barushirize kubakorera, kuko abagirirwa ico kimazi ari abizera n'abakundwa. Uzokwigishe ivyo, ubibahanure.
54006003	Umuntu ni yigisha ukundi, ntiyemere amajambo mazima, ari yo majambo y'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, n'inyigisho zihura n'ukwubaha Imana;
54006004	azoba yikakishije, ata co azi, arwaye ibihari, n'intambara z'amajambo, zivamwo igono, gutongana, ibitutsi, umwikeko mubi
54006005	n'ibihari bidashira vy'abantu bononekaye ubwenge, bakuweko ivyo ukuri, bibwira yuko kwubaha Imana ari ukwironkera inyungu.
54006006	Ariko kwubaha Imana gufatanije no kubumbwa n'ivyo ufise kuvamwo inyungu nyinshi koko.
54006007	Kuko ata co twazanye mw'isi kandi ata co dushobora kuyivanamwo.
54006008	Ariko iyo dufise ivyo turya n'ivyo twambara biba bitubumvye.
54006009	Ariko abagomba kuba abatunzi bagwa mu nyosha no mu mutego no mu kwifuza kwinshi kw'ubupfu gusinzikaza, kudobeza abantu mu bibonona bikabarandura.
54006010	Kuko gukunda amahera ari imizi y'ibibi vyose; ayo bamwe bifuje, bakazimira, bagata ukwizera, bitobekeranisha imibabaro myinshi.
54006011	Ariko weho, muntu w'Imana, wame uhunga ivyo, ariko ukurikire ukugororoka, ukwubaha Imana, ukwizera, urukundo, ukwihangana n'ubugwaneza.
54006012	Wame urwana intambara nziza yo kwizera, ucakire ubugingo budashira, ubwo wahamagariwe, ukabwaturira ukwatura kwiza mu maso y'ivyabona vyinshi.
54006013	Ndakubwiririza mu maso y'Imana ibeshaho vyose, no mu za Kristo Yesu yashingishije intahe ukwatura kwiza imbere ya Pontiyo Pilato,
54006014	witondere icagezwe, ntugire agasembwa, ntubeko umugayo, gushitsa ku guseruka kw' Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo,
54006015	kuzokwerekanwa mu gihe cakwo n'Inyabushobozi yonyene, ishemagizwa, ni yo Mwami w'abami, uwuganza abaganza.
54006016	Ni yo yonyene ifise ukudapfa, iba mu muco utegerwa, ata muntu yigeze ayibona, ata wushobora kuyibona. Icubahiro n'ubushobozi bidashira bibe ivyayo. Amina.
54006017	Wihanize abatunzi bo mu vy'iki gihe, ntibibone, canke kwishimira ubutunzi butari ubwo kwishimirwa, ariko bishimire Imana, iduha vyose bisesekaye, ngo tubinezererwe.
54006018	Kandi bakore iciza, babe abatunzi ku bikorwa vyiza, babe abanyabuntu bakunda gutanga,
54006019	bibikire ubutunzi buzoba itanguriro ryiza mu gihe kizoza, kugira ngo bacakire ubugingo nyakuri.
54006020	Ewe Timoteyo, wame uzigama ico wabikijwe, utere ibitugu ibizira vy'amajambo ahumanya n'ukurwana kw'ivyitwa ubwenge atari bwo,
54006021	ubwo bamwe bivuga ko babufise bakazimira, bagata ukwizera. Ubuntu bubane namwe.
55001001	Pahulo, intumwa ya Kristo Yesu, nk'uko Imana yagomvye, intumwa yo kuvuga isezerano ry'ubugingo bubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu,
55001002	ndakwandikiye Timoteyo, umwana wanje nkunda. Ubuntu, imbabazi n'amahoro biva ku Mana Data wa twese no kuri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu bikubeko.
55001003	Imana nkorera nkurikiye ba sogokuruza, mfise umutima utanduye, utarimwo ijwi rinyagiriza ikibi, ndayishimira yuko nkwibuka ubudasiba, uko nsenze, ijoro n'umurango.
55001004	Nibuka amosozi yawe, ngakumbura kukubona, ngo nuzure umunezero;
55001005	kuko nibutse ukwizera kutari ukwo uburyarya kuri muri wewe, kwabanje kuba muri nyogokuru Lowisi no muri nyoko Ewunike. Ndazi kandi ntakekeranya yuko kukurimwo nawe.
55001006	Ni co gituma ndakwibutsa kuvyura ya ngabire Imana yaguhaye ngo yake, yagushizwemwo no kurambikwako ibiganza vyanje.
55001007	Kuko Imana itaduhaye umutima w'isoni n'ubwoba; ariko yaduhaye uwo ubushobozi, urukundo n'ukwirinda. "
55001008	Nuko ntugire isoni zo gushingira intahe Umwami wacu, canke jewe imbohe yiwe. Ariko ufatanye nanje kwihanganira imibabaro kubwo ubutumwa bwiza, nk'uko ubushobozi bw'Imana bugushoboza,
55001009	yadukijije, ikaduhamagarisha umuhamagaro wera, udatewe n'ibikorwa vyacu, ariko utewe n'uko yabigabiye ubwayo, kandi utewe n'ubuntu bwayo, twaherewe muri Kristo Yesu ibihe vyose bitaraba.
55001010	Ariko none, bwaseruwe n'ukuboneka kw'Umukiza wacu Kristo Yesu, yahinduye urupfu ubusa, ubugingo no kutagipfa akabiserurisha ubutumwa bwiza.
55001011	Nashiriweho kuba umuvuzi, intumwa n'umwigisha w'ubwo butumwa.
55001012	Ni co gituma kandi mbabazwa ntya, yamara ntibintera isoni, kuko nzi uwo nizeye, kandi nzi ntakekeranya yuko ashobora kuzigama ikibitsanyo namubikije gushitsa kuri wa musi.
55001013	Shishikara mu karorero k'amajambo mazima wanyumvanye, ugashigikize ukwizera n'urukundo rubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu.
55001014	Ivyiza wabikijwe, ubizigamishe Mpwemu Yera atubemwo.
55001015	Urazi yuko abo muri Asiya bose banteye ibitugu, muri abo harimwo Fugelo na Herumogene.
55001016	Umwami agirire ikigongwe abo kwa Onesiforo, kuko yanduhura kenshi; kandi ntiyatewe n'isoni n'umunyororo wanje,
55001017	ariko, ashitse i Roma, agira umwete wo kundondera, arambona.
55001018	Umwami amuhe kuzoronka imbabazi ziva ku Mwami kuri wa musi. Kandi ivyo yankoreye muri Efeso uko bingana, nta wukurusha kubimenya.
55002001	Weho mwana wanje, ugirire ubushobozi mu buntu buri muri Kristo Yesu,
55002002	kandi ivyo wanyumvanye mu maso y'ivyabona vyinshi, ubishikirize abantu bo kwizigirwa, bazoshobora kuvyigisha n'abandi.
55002003	Ufatanye nanje kwihanganira imibabaro, nk'uko bikwiye umusoda mwiza wa Kristo Yesu.
55002004	Nta musoda yikwegera mu vy'ubu bugingo, ngo azohimbare uwamwandikiye ubusoda.
55002005	Kandi iyo umuntu arushanywa, ntahabwa igitsibo, kiretse arushanijwe nk'uko vyagezwe.
55002006	Umurimyi kuko ari we yacumukuye ni we akwiye kubanza gusoroma ku vyeze.
55002007	Umenye ivyo mvuze, kuko Umwami wacu azoguha ubwenge muri vyose.
55002008	Wame wibuka Yesu Kristo yazutse mu bapfuye, yakomotse mu ruvyaro rwa Dawidi, nk'uko ubutumwa nahawe buvuga;
55002009	ubwo mbabarizwamwo, no kubohwa nkabohwa, nk'inkozi y'ikibi; ariko ijambo ry'Imana ntiriboshwe.
55002010	Ni co gituma nihanganira vyose kubwo abatoranijwe, kugira ngo na bo baronke agakiza kari muri Kristo Yesu, gafatanije n'ubwiza budashira.
55002011	Iri jambo ni iryo kwizerwa, ngo Namba twarapfanye na we, tuzobanaho na we;
55002012	namba twihangana, tuzokwimikanwa na we; namba waramwihakanye, na we azotwihakana;
55002013	naho tutoba abizigirwa, we ahora ari umwizigirwa, kuko adashobora guhindagurika.
55002014	Wame ubibutsa ivyo, ubihanikiririza mu maso y'Imana ntibarwanire amajambo kuko bitagira ikimazi, bigwisha abumva.
55002015	Wame ugira umwete wo kwiha Imana nk'uwamaze kurama, umukozi atarinda guteterwa, aramiriza neza mw'ijambo ry'ukuri.
55002016	Ariko, ibihumanya vy'amajambo y'ubusa ubizibukire, kuko ababivuga bazoshishikara inzira yo kutubaha Imana,
55002017	kandi ijambo ryabo rizorandagurana nk'igisebe gishikurana kidakira. Muri abo umwe ni Humenayo na Fileto,
55002018	kuko bazimiye bakava mu vy'ukuri, bavuga ngo ukuzuka kwarahejeje kubaho, bagahenura ukwizera kwa bamwe.
55002019	Ariko ibuye ry' umushinge w'Imana wo kwubakako urakomeye, ryanditsweko iki kimenyetso, ngo Uhoraho arazi abiwe; kandi ngo Umuntu wese avuga izina ry' Uhoraho ave mu kugabitanya.
55002020	Mu nzu nini y'umutunzi ntihabamwo ibikoresho vy'ivyacuzwe mw'izahabu no mw'ifeza gusa, ariko habamwo n'ivyo ibiti n'ivyo ibumba, kandi bimwe babikoresha ivyo icubahiro, ibindi babikoresha ibiteye isoni.
55002021	Umuntu ni yiyeza, akitandukanya n'ivyo, azoba igikoreshwa c'icubahiro, cejejwe, kigirira nyene co ikimazi, catunganirijwe igikorwa ciza cose.
55002022	Ariko kwifuza kw'ubusore uguhunge, maze ukurikire ukugororoka, ukwizera, urukundo n'amahoro, ufatanya n'abambaza Umwami wacu n'imitima itanduye.
55002023	Ariko ibihari vy'ubupfu n'ivyo ubutungu ntukavyemere, uzi yuko bivyara impari z'ubupfu.
55002024	Kandi umushumba w'Umwami wacu ntakwiye gutongana, ariko akwiye kugira ineza kuri bose, no kuba uburyo bwo kwigisha, no kwihangana,
55002025	no guhanurisha uburwaneza abamuhaririza, ngo kumbure, bishobotse, Imana ibahe kwihana ngo bamenye ivyo ukuri,
55002026	bagaruke mu bwitonzi, bave mu mutego wa wa mugarariji yabafashe ngo bakore ivyo agomba.
55003001	Ariko umenye yuko mu misi y'iherezo hazoza ibihe bigoye.
55003002	Kuko abantu bazoba bikunda gusa, bakunda amahera, birarira, bibona, batukana, batumvira abavyeyi, intashima, abanegura ivyo Imana,
55003003	badakunda n'ababo, banka kwuzura, barementanya, batigarura, inkazi, badakunda ivyiza,
55003004	abaguranyi, ibirandamuke, abivyimvya, bakunda ibibahimbara bakabirutisha Imana.
55003005	Bafise ishusho yo kwubaha Imana, ariko bahakana ubushobozi bwakwo. Abameze batyo wame ubatera ibitugu.
55003006	Kuko muri bo harimwo abagabo banyegetera mu mazu, bagatwara abagore batagira imitima, baremerewe n'ivyaha, batwarwa n'ukwifuza kw'uburyo bwinshi,
55003007	bama biga, ariko nta ho bashobora gushitsa ku kumenya ukuri.
55003008	Nk'uko Yane na Yambure barwanije Mose, ni ko n'abo bagabo barwanya ukuri, abo ni abononekaye ubwenge, babaye ibihombe ku kwizera.
55003009	Mugabo ntibazoshobora kurengaho; kuko ubusazi bwabo buzogaragarira abantu bose, nk'uko ubwa ba bandi bwagaragaye.
55003010	Ariko weho wakurikiye neza ukwigisha kwanje, ingeso, imigabo, ukwizera, ukutarambirwa, urukundo, ukwihangana,
55003011	guhamwa n'imibabaro, nk'ivyambereyeko muri Antiyokiya, Ikoniyo n'i Lusitira; ivyo nihanganiye vyose mpamwa, kandi vyose Umwami wacu arabinkiza.
55003012	Mbere abagomba bose kugenda bubaha Imana bari muri Kristo Yesu, bazohamwa.
55003013	Ariko abantu babi, bo n'abahumbuzi, bazorushiriza kuba babi, bazimiza bakazimizwa.
55003014	Ariko weho ugume mu vyo wize, ukavyizezwa, kuko uzi abakwigishije.
55003015	Kandi uzi yuko uhereye mu buto bwawe wamye uzi ivyanditswe vyera bishobora kukumenyesha ubwenge bwo kukuzanira agakiza gaheshwa no kwizera Kristo Yesu.
55003016	Ivyanditswe vyose vyahumetswe n' Imana, kandi bifise akamaro ko kwigisha umuntu, kumuhana, kumutunganya no kumutoza indero nziza mu kugororoka;
55003017	kugira ngo umuntu w'Imana abe uwushitse, afise ibimukwiye vyose, ngo akore igikorwa ciza cose.
55004001	Ndakwihanikiririza mu maso y'Imana no mu ya Kristo Yesu azocira urubanza abazoba bariho n'abazoba bapfuye, kandi no kubwo kuzoboneka kwiwe n'ubwami bwiwe.
55004002	Uvuge ijambo ry'Imana, uhore ugavye mu gihe gikwiye no mu kidakwiye, uhane, wihanize, uhanure, mu kwihangana kwose no mu kwigisha.
55004003	Kuko igihe kizoza, batazokwemera kwumva ukwigisha kuzima; ariko kuko amatwi abarya yifuza kwumva ibibanezereza, bazokwirundaniriza abigisha bahuje n'ukwifuza kwabo,
55004004	kandi bazokwiziba amatwi, ngo ntibumve ukuri, bazozimira bakurikire imigani y'ibinyoma.
55004005	Ariko weho, wirinde muri vyose, wihanganire imibabaro, ukore igikorwa c'umuvuzi w'ubutumwa bwiza, ushitse igikorwa c'ibango ryawe.
55004006	Kuko jeho n'ubu ndiko ndasukwa nk'ibisukwa ku gicaniro, igihe co kwitahira kwanje kirashitse.
55004007	Narwanye intambara nziza, narangije urugendo, nazigamye ukwizera.
55004008	Ibisigaye mbikiwe igitsibo c'ukugororoka ico Umwami wacu, umucamanza agororotse, azompa kuri wa musi kandi si jewe jenyene nzogihabwa ariko kandi n'abakunze kuzoseruka kwiwe bose bazogihabwa.
55004009	Gira umwete wo kuza aho ndi vuba.
55004010	Dema yarantaye, kuko akunze ivyo iyi y'ubu, yigira i Tesalonike. Keresikenti yagiye i Galatiya Tito nawe i Dalumatiya.
55004011	Luka gusa ni we twasigaranye. Hitana Mariko, umuzane, kuko angirira ikimazi mu gikorwa c'ibango ryanje.
55004012	Ariko Tukiko namurungitse muri Efeso.
55004013	Aho uzozira uranzanira impuzu yo kwipfuka nasize i Tirowa kwa Karupo, n'ibitabo, kandi canecane uzozane ivyo insato.
55004014	Alekisandero umucuzi yangiriye inabi nyinshi. Umwami wacu azomwishura ibikwiranye n'ivyo yakoze.
55004015	Nawe umwirinde kuko yarwanije amajambo yacu cane. "
55004016	Mw'iburana ryanje rya mbere nta wanyunganiye, ariko bose barantaye; icompa ntibabiharurweko.
55004017	Ariko Umwami wacu ni we yampagarikiye, arandemesha, kugira ngo ubutumwa ndabuvuge nanje butagabanije, abanyamahanga bose babwumve. Nuko mva mu menyo y'intambwe.
55004018	Umwami wacu azonkiza ibibi vyose bangirira, azondokora kugira ngo anjane mu bwami bwiwe bwo mw'ijuru. Icubahiro kibe iciwe, ibihe bitazoshira. Amina.
55004019	Untahirize Purisikila na Akwila n'abo kwa Onesiforo.
55004020	Erasito yagumye i Korinto, ariko Tirofimo namusize i Mileto arwaye.
55004021	Gira umwete wo kuza agatasi katarashana. Ewubulo, Pudenti, Lino, Kilawudiya n'abavukanyi bose baragutasha.
55004022	Umwami abane n'umutima wawe. Ubuntu bw'Imana bubane namwe.
56001001	Jewe Pahulo, umushumba w'Imana, intumwa ya Yesu Kristo, ndabiherewe kwizeza abo Imana yatoranije no kwigisha kumenya ivyo ukuri gufatanije n'ukwubaha Imana.
56001002	Nkora nizigiye kuzoronka ubugingo budashira, ubwo Imana itazi kubesha yasezeranye kera, ibihe vyose bitarabaho.
56001003	Ariko mu bihe yitoranirije yerekanishije ijambo ryayo ubutumwa najejwe, nk'uko Imana Umukiza wacu yageze.
56001004	Ndakwandikiye Tito, umwana wanje nyakuri kubwo ukwizera dusangiye. Ubuntu n'amahoro bikubeko biva ku Mana Data wa twese no kuri Kristo Yesu Umukiza wacu.
56001005	Icatumye ndagusiga i Kirete kwari ukugira ngo utunganye ivyasigaye, kandi mu gisagara caho cose ngo uhashinge abakuru b'ishengero, nk'uko nabikubariye.
56001006	Abe umuntu atabonekako umugayo, afise umugore umwe gusa, afise abana bizera, bataregwa ko ari ibihumbu canke itagonda.
56001007	Kuko umuzezwashengero akwiye kutabako umugayo, nk'umukuru w'abakozi bo mu rugo w'Imana nyene; kandi ntakwiye kuba uwudakurwa kw'ijambo, ushangashirwa, umunywi w'umuvinyu, umusinzi canke uwunohokera inyungu mbi.
56001008	Ariko abe uwukunda gutanga indaro, akunda ivyiza, yitonda, agororoka, yera, yirinda,
56001009	agumya ijambo ryo kwizerwa rihura n'ukwigisha kwacu, kugira ngo abone guhanura abantu mu kwigisha kuzima no gutsinda abamuhaririza.
56001010	Kuko hariho benshi b'intagondwa, canecane n'abo mu bahimbuwe igikoba c'ubugabo, bavuga ibitagira ikimazi, n'inyosha mbi.
56001011	Bakwiye kuzibwa iminwa, kuko hari imiryango bagwisha igahenebera, bigisha ibidakwiye kubwo inyungu mbi.
56001012	Umwe muri bo w'umuvugishwa wabo yaravuze ati: "Na ntaryo Abanyakirete, ababeshi, ibikoko bibi n'abanebwe b'abakunzi b'inda."
56001013	Iyo ntahe yashinze ni iyo ukuri. Ni co gituma ukwiye kubahana cane, kugira ngo babe abahangaye mu kwizera,
56001014	ntibashire imitima ku migani y'ibinyoma y'Abayuda no ku vyagezwe vy'abantu batera ibitugu ukuri.
56001015	Ku badahumanye nta gihumanye, ariko ku banduye, batizera, nta kidahumanye, ariko ubwenge bwabo n'imitima ibagiriza vyaranduye.
56001016	Bavuga yuko bazi Imana, ariko bayihakanisha ivyo bakora; n'abo kwankwa urunuka, n'abatumvira Imana, no mu bikorwa vyiza vyose nta co bamaze.
56002001	Ariko weho uvuge ibihwanye na kwa kwigisha kuzima.
56002002	Bwira abatama ntibarenze urugero, babe inyankamugayo, badasaragurika, bagire kwizera kuzima no mu rukundo no mu kwihangana.
56002003	N'abatamakazi nyene, ubabwire bagende nk'uko bibereye abera, batarementaniriza abandi, batanohorwa imitima n'umuvinyu mwinshi, bigisha ivyiza,
56002004	kugira ngo batoze abagore bakiri bato ubwenge bwo gukunda abagabo babo n'abana babo,
56002005	no kudasaragurika, no kwirinda ubweruzi, no kwubaka ingo zabo, no kuba inda nziza, bagororokere abagabo babo, kugira ngo ijambo ry'Imana ntiritukwe.
56002006	N'imisore ni uko ubahanure ntibasaragurike;
56002007	nawe ubwawe wiyerekane muri vyose nk'ikigereranyo c'ibikorwa vyiza, ugire ukwigisha kudatosekaye, ube inyankamugayo,
56002008	ugire n'ijambo rizima ritogawa, kugira ngo umuntu ari mu ruhande rw' abansi amaramare, abuze ikibi yotuvuga.
56002009	Hanura abakozi bagororokere ba shebuja, babahimbare muri vyose, ata guharira,
56002010	badakorakora, ariko berekane ukuyoboka kwiza kwose, kugira ngo muri vyose basharize ivyigishwa vy'Imana, Umukiza wacu.
56002011	Kuko ubuntu bw'Imana bwaserutse, buzanira abantu bose agakiza,
56002012	butwigisha kwikunkumura ukutubaha Imana n'ukwifuza ivyo isi, bukatwigisha kwama tudasaragurika, tugororoka, twubaha Imana, muri kino gihe,
56002013	twitega ivyizigiro vy'amahirwe no kuzoseruka kw'ubwiza bwa Yesu Kristo, ni we Mana yacu ihambaye n'Umukiza,
56002014	yatwiguze kugira ngo aducungure, adukureko ivyo twagabitanije vyose, kandi yihumanurire ubwoko ngo babe icibare ciwe, barwane ishaka ry'ibikorwa vyiza.
56002015	Wame uvuga ivyo, ubahanura, ubahana, nk'uwufise ububasha rwose. Ntihakagire uwugukengera.
56003001	Ubibutse kugamburukira abakuru n'abafise ubushobozi, no kubumvira, no kwitegurira igikorwa ciza cose,
56003002	no kutagira uwo bambika ibara, no kutitoraguza no kwengenga, berekana ubugwaneza bwose ku bantu bose.
56003003	Kuko natwe nyene kera twari ibipfu, turi intabarirwa, tuzimizwa, tujakariye ukwifuza n'ukwinezereza vy'uburyo bwinshi, twama tugira urwanko n'igono, turi abo kwankwa natwe twankana.
56003004	Ariko ineza y'Imana Umukiza wacu n'urukundo ikunda abantu, bimaze kuboneka,
56003005	iradukiza, itadukirishije ibikorwa vyo kugororoka twakoze, ariko, ikurikije ubwinshi bw'imbabazi zayo, idukirisha ukwozwa kuzana ukuvyarwa ubwa kabiri, ikadukirisha uguhindurwa basha na Mpwemu Yera,
56003006	uwo yaducuncuburiyeko kubwa Yesu Kristo Umukiza wacu,
56003007	kugira ngo tugirwe intungane n'ubuntu bwayo, duce tuba abaragwa b'ubugingo budashira, nk'uko tuvyizigiye.
56003008	Iryo jambo ni iryo kwizerwa, ndagomba yuko utsindagira ivyo, ubikobereje, kugira ngo abizeye Imana bagire umwete wo gushishikara gukora ibikorwa vyiza. Ivyo ni vyiza, bigira ico bimarira abantu.
56003009	Ariko, impari z'ubupfu no kudondora ivyo amamuko yabo n'imitongano no guharira ivyo mu vyagezwe, wame ubizibukira, kuko bitagira ikimazi kandi ari ivyo ubusa.
56003010	Uwuzana ibice ni wamara kumuhanura ubwa mbere n'ubwa kabiri akanka, ntukamwemere,
56003011	kuko uzi yuko uwumeze atyo agoramye kandi akora ivyaha, yitsindisha.
56003012	Ni nagutumako Arutema canke Tukiko, uzogire umwete wo kunsanga i Nikopoli; kuko ari ho nagabiye kuzomara agatasi.
56003013	Witwaririke guherekeza no gusezera neza Zena umuhinga w'ivyagezwe, na Apolo, kugira ngo ntihazogire ico babura.
56003014	Kandi abacu na bo ni bige gushishikara gukora ibikorwa vyiza ngo babone kumara ubukene ababikwiye rwose, kugira ngo abacu ntibabure ico bamarira abandi.
56003015	Abo turi kumwe bose baragutasha. Untahirize abadukunda dusangiye ukwizera. Ubuntu bubane namwe mwese.
57001001	Pahulo, imbohe ya Kristo Yesu, na Timoteyo umuvukanyi, turakwandikiye Filemoni uwo dukunda, dusangiye igikorwa,
57001002	na Apiya mushiki wacu, na Arukipo tusangiye urugamba, hamwe n'ishengero ryo mu nzu yawe.
57001003	Ubuntu n'amahoro biva ku Mana, Data wa twese, no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo bibabemwo.
57001004	Ndashima Imana yanje ubudasiba, ndaguhoza mu kanwa uko nsenze,
57001005	kuko numvise urukundo rwawe n'ukwizera Umwami Yesu kwawe, ukwo wereka abera bose.
57001006	Ndagusaba ngo ugufatanya kwawe mu kwizera gushobore vyinshi kubwa Kristo, mu kumenyekanisha ivyiza vyose vyo muri twebwe.
57001007	Kuko urukundo rwawe rwanteye umunezero mwinshi rukandemesha, kandi imitima y'abera warayiruhuye, muvukanyi."
57001008	Kubwo ivyo, naho mfise muri Kristo uburenganzira bwose bwo kugutegeka gukora ibikwiye,
57001009	ndahisemwo kukwinginga kubwo urukundo, uko ndi kwose Pahulo umutama, kandi ubu hoho ndi imbohe ya Kristo Yesu.
57001010	Ndakwitwayeko kubwo umwana wanje Onesimo uwo navyariye mu minyororo yanje,
57001011	atakugirira ikimazi kera, ariko noneho atugirira ikimazi twempi.
57001012	Ni we nyene ndakurungikiye, ni we mutima wanje.
57001013	Mba ndamugumije kugira ngo ankorere mu gishingo cawe, mboshwe n'iminyororo y'ubutumwa bwiza.
57001014	Ariko nta co ngomba gukora ntakugishije inama, kugira ngo iciza ukora ntikibe ico ugoberewe, ariko ugikore ubikunze.
57001015	Kumbure icatumye atandukanywa nawe igihe gito kwari ukugira ngo uzomwamane imisi yose.
57001016	Atakiri umushumba wawe, ariko aruta umushumba, ari umwana wa So, akundwa. Akundwa nanje cane, ariko arushiriza gukundwa nawe, mu vyo umubiri no mu Mwami wacu. "
57001017	Nuko namba unyiyumvira ko dusangiye igikorwa, umwakire nk'uko nanje wonyakiriye.
57001018	Ariko asangwa hari ico yaguhemukiyeko, canke hari umwenda agufitiye, ubimparureko.
57001019	Ni jewe Pahulo nandikishije ukuboko kwanje yuko nzovyishura. Reka ndeke kukubwira yuko uri n'umwenda wanje, uwo mwenda ni wewe ubwawe.
57001020	Ego, muvukanyi, ndakubonemwo ikimazi mu Mwami wacu; unduhure umutima muri Kristo.
57001021	Ndakwandikiye nizigiye ko uzonyumvira, nzi yuko uzokora n'ibiruta ivyo mvuze.
57001022	Kandi n'ikindi, untegurire indaro; kuko nizigiye yuko muzompabwa kubwo amasengesho yanyu.
57001023	Epafura, mugenzanje tubohanywe muri Kristo, aragutasha,
57001024	Mariko, Arisitariko, Dema na Luka, abo dusangiye igikorwa, baragutasha.
57001025	Ubuntu bw'Umwami Yesu Kristo bubane n'imitima yanyu. Amina. "
58001001	Kera mu bihe vyinshi no mu buryo bwinshi, Imana yaganiriye ba sogokuruza ibicishije mu kanwa k'abavugishwa nayo.
58001002	Muri iyi misi y'iherezo yatuganiriye mu kanwa k'Umwana wayo, uwo yashiriweho kuba samuragwa wa vyose, ni we yahaye kurema isi.
58001003	Uwo, kuko ari ugukayangana kw'ubwiza bwayo, n'ishusho y'akameremere kayo, kandi ashigikiza vyose ijambo ry'ubushobozi bwiwe, ahejeje gushiraho umwuhagiro w'ivyaha, avyagira i buryo bw'icubahiro c'ubwami bwo mw'ijuru;
58001004	amaze kuba uwuhambaye kurusha abamarayika, nk'uko izina yarazwe rirengeye ayabo.
58001005	Ni nde wo mu bamarayika Imana yigeze kubarira iti: "Uri Ubura bwanje? Uwu musi ndakuvyaye?" Kandi iti: "Nzomubera Se. Na we azombera Umwana wanje?"
58001006	Kandi aho izokwongera kuzana imfura yayo mw'isi izovuga iti: "Abamarayika b'Imana bose bamusenge."
58001007	Kandi ivyo abamarayika yarabivuze iti: "Ihindura abamarayika bayo imiyaga, Abasavyi bayo ibahindura imbeya z'umuriro."
58001008	Ariko, ivyo Umwana wayo yabivuze iti: "Ubutware bwawe, Mana, buhangamye ibihe bidashira, Icumu ry'ubutware bwawe n'icumu ry'uwuganza atunganye.
58001009	Wakunze ukugororoka, wanka ubugarariji, Ni co catumye Imana, ni yo Mana yawe, ikurobanuza amavuta y'umunezero, ikakurutisha bagenzi bawe."
58001010	Kandi ni wewe, Uhoraho, mu bihe vya kera washizeho itanguriro ry'isi, Kandi amajuru n'igikorwa c'intoke zawe.
58001011	Ivyo bizoshira, ariko weho uzokwamaho; Ivyo vyose bizosaza nk'impuzu,
58001012	Kandi uzobizinga nk'umutamana, Bikuranwe n'ibindi nk'uko impuzu zikuranywa. Ariko weho uri uko wamye, Imyaka y'ukubaho kwawe ntizoshira.
58001013	Ariko ni nde wo mu bamarayika yigeze kubarira iti: "Icara i buryo bwanje, Ushitse aho nzohindurira abansi bawe indava yo musi y'ibirenge vyawe?"
58001014	Mbega abamarayika bose si impwemu ziyikorera, zitumwa gukora igikorwa kubwo abazoragwa agakiza?
58002001	Ni co gituma dukwiye kurushiriza kwitwaririka ivyo twumvise, kugira ngo ntidutwarwe akayombekere tukabivako.
58002002	Ko ijambo ryavugiwe mu kanwa k'abamarayika ryagumyeho, kandi ibicumuro vyose no kutaryumvira bikagererwa ingero bikwiranye;
58002003	tweho tuzokwikiza dute, ni twanjanjwa ku gakiza kangana gatyo? Kabanje kuvugwa n'Umwami wacu, kakadukomezwako n'abakumvise,
58002004	Imana ifatanije na bo kugashingira intahe, iyishingisha ibimenyetso, ibitangaza, ibikomeye vy'uburyo bwinshi n'ingabire za Mpwemu Yera zagabanganijwe nk'uko yagomvye.
58002005	Kuko atari abamarayika Imana yahaye gutwara isi izobaho, iyo tuvuga.
58002006	Ariko hari aho umuntu yashinze intahe ati: "Umuntu aho umwibuka, Canke umwana w'umuntu aho umugendera?"
58002007	Wamucishije bugufi, aba musi y'abamarayika gato. Wamwambitse ubwiza n'icubahiro nk'igitsibo, Wamuhaye kugaba ibikorwa vy'amaboko yawe.
58002008	Wamuhaye kuganza ibintu vyose, ubishira musi y'ibirenge vyiwe. Ko Imana yamuhaye kuganza ibintu vyose nta co yishigarije itamuhaye kukiganza. Ariko none ntiturabona ibintu vyose biganzwa na we.
58002009	Ariko, uwacishijwe bugufi, akaba musi y' abamarayika gato, ni we Yesu, tumubona yambitswe ubwiza n'icubahiro nk'igitsibo, kubwo imibabaro y'urupfu, kugira ngo ubuntu bw'Imana butume arogorera umuntu wese urupfu.
58002010	Mu vy'ukuri vyari bikwiye ko Imana yo irema vyose kandi ikabibeshaho itunganisha Yesu ukubabazwa; kugira ngo abana benshi baze mu bwiza bwiwe. Kuko Yesu wenyene ari we ndongozi ibarongora ku gakiza.
58002011	Kuko uweza ni abezwa bose bakomotse kuri Imwe; ni co gituma atagira isoni zo kubita abana ba Se
58002012	ati: "Nzobarira abavukanyi izina ryawe, Nzoririmba ndagutazira hagati y'ishengero."
58002013	Kandi ati: "Nzokwama ndayizigira." Kandi ati: "Ehe twe n'abana Imana yampaye."
58002014	Nuko rero, kuko abana bahuje inyama n'amaraso, na we ubwiwe yahuje ivyo na bo, kugira ngo abone uko apfa, kandi urupfu rwiwe aruhindurishe ubusa uwufise ubushobozi bw'urupfu, ni we wa mugarariji,
58002015	kandi ngo arokore abajakariye ubwoba bw'urupfu bose, imisi yose y'ukubaho kwabo.
58002016	Kuko tuzi neza ko abamarayika atari bo yatoye, ariko yatoye uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu.
58002017	Ni co catumye vyaramubereye gushushanywa na abana ba Se kuri vyose, ngo abe umuherezi mukuru wo mu vy'Imana, w'imbabazi kandi agororoka, abe indishi y'ivyaha vy'abantu.
58002018	Kuko ubwiwe ko yababajwe no kugeragezwa, ashobora no gutabara abageragezwa.
58003001	Nuko rero, bavukanyi bera, abasangiye ihamagarwa riva mw'ijuru, ni mwitegereze Yesu, intumwa n'umuherezi mukuru w'ivyo twizeye tukavyatura,
58003002	agamburukira iyamutoranije, nk'uko Mose yayoboka mu rugo rwayo hose.
58003003	Kuko uwo yiyumviriwe ko akwiye guhabwa icubahiro kiruta ica Mose, nk'uko ishimwe ry'uwubatse urugo riruta iryo urugo.
58003004	Kuko urugo rwose rugira uwurwubaka, ariko Imana ni yo yubatse ibintu vyose.
58003005	Kandi Mose yayoboka mu rugo rwayo hose nk'umushumba, kugira ngo abe icabona co gushingira intahe ibizovugwa hanyuma.
58003007	Nuko, nk'uko Mpwemu Yera avuga ati: "Uwu musi aho mwumvira Ijwi ryayo,
58003008	Ntimukomantaze imitima yanyu, nk'uko mwayikomantaje mu gihe co kuratsa, Kuri wa musi wo kugerageza mu bugaragwa,
58003009	Aho ba sogokuruza banyu bangeragereje bancaca, Bakabona ibikorwa vyanje imyaka mirongo ine.
58003010	Ni co catumye ngirira umwikomo abo ico gihe, Nkavuga ko bama bazimira mu mitima yabo, Kandi ntibamenya inzira zanje;
58003011	Nk'uko narahiranye ishavu ryanje Nti: "Ntibazoshika mu buruhukiro bwanje."
58003012	Bavukanyi, ni mwirinde, ntihagire uwo muri mwebwe agira umutima mubi utizera, umutera kureka Imana nzima.
58003013	Ariko muhanurane uko bukeye bicitwa uwu musi, ntihagire uwo muri mwebwe akomantazwa umutima n'uruhendo rw'icaha.
58003014	Kuko twacitse abasangiye Kristo, namba dukomeje rwose ivyizigiro vyacu twatanguranye gushitsa kw'iherezo;
58003015	bikivugwa, ngo uwu musi aho mwumvira ijwi ryayo, Ntimukomantaze imitima yanyu, nk'uko mwayikomantaje mu gihe co kuratsa.
58003016	Ni ba nde bamaze kwumva bakayiratsa? Mbega si abavuye i Misiri bose, barongowe na Mose?
58003017	Kandi ni ba nde yagiriye umwikomo imyaka mirongo ine? Si abacumuye, imivyimba yabo igahindikirana mu bugaragwa?
58003018	Ni ba nde yarahiye ko batazoshika mu buruhukiro bwayo? Si abatayumviye?
58003019	Kandi tubona ko batashoboye kubushikamwo, kuko batizeye.
58004001	Nuko, kuko isezerano ryo gushika mu buruhukiro bwayo rikiriho, twiyubare kugira ngo kumbure ntihagire uwo muri mwebwe yiyumvirwa ko akererewe.
58004002	Kuko natwe twabwiwe ubutumwa bwiza nka bo, ariko, ijambo bumvise ntiryabagiriye ikimazi, kuko ritavanzwe n'ukwizera mu mitima y'abaryumvise.
58004003	Kuko twebwe abizeye dushika muri ubwo buruhukiro, nk'uko yavuze iti: "Nk'uko narahiranye ishavu ryanje Ko batazoshika mu buruhukiro bwanje; naho yari yarahejeje ibikorwa vyayo, uhereye ku kuremwa kw'isi."
58004004	Kuko hari aho yavuze ku vyo umusi w'indwi nk'ibi iti: "Imana yaruhutse ku musi ugira indwi ibikorwa vyayo vyose."
58004005	Kandi na hano, ngo Ntibazoshika mu buruhukiro bwanje.
58004006	Nuko rero, kuko bukibikiwe bamwe ngo babushikemwo, ariko ababanje kubwirwa ubutumwa bwiza babujijwe kubushikamwo no kutumvira Imana,
58004007	yongera gutoranya umusi, ni wo uwu musi; ivugira mu kanwa ka Dawidi, igihe kirekire cane gihise, nk'uko tumaze kuvuga tuti: "Uwu musi aho mwumvira ijwi ryayo Ntimukomantaze imitima yanyu."
58004008	Kuko iyaba Yosuwa yarabaruhuye, ntiba yaravuze ubwa nyuma ivyo uwundi musi.
58004009	Nuko rero haracariho uburuhukiro bw'isabato bubikiwe abantu b'Imana.
58004010	Kuko uwushitse mu buruhukiro bwayo, na we aba aruhutse ibikorwa vyiwe, nk'uko Imana yaruhutse ivyayo.
58004011	Nuko tugire umwete wo gushika muri ubwo buruhukiro, ntihagire umuntu agwa, akurikiye ikigereranyo ca ba bandi co kutumvira Imana.
58004012	Kuko ijambo ry'Imana ari rizima, rifise ubushobozi, rifise ubugi buruta ubwo inkota zose, rikinjira n'aho ritanya ubugingo n'impwemu, rigatanya ingingo n'umusokoro, risuzuma ivyo umutima wiyumvira, ukagabira.
58004013	Kandi imbere yayo nta caremwe gihishijwe, ariko vyose vyambaye ubusa, biragaragara, imbere y'amaso y'Iyizotubaza ivyo twakoze.
58004014	Nuko, ko dufise umuherezi mukuru akomeye, yaciye mw'ijuru, ni Yesu Umwana w'Imana, tubangirize ivyo twizera tukavyatura.
58004015	Kuko umuherezi mukuru dufise, atari uwudashobora kubabarana natwe mu ntege nke zacu, ariko ni uwageragejwe uburyo bwose nkatwe, yamara we nta caha yakoze.
58004016	Nuko ni twegere intebe y'ubuntu dushize ubwoba, kugira ngo turonke ikigongwe, tubone ubuntu bwo kudutabara mu gihe gikwiye.
58005001	Umuherezi wese mukuru, kuko yarobanuwe mu bantu, ashirirwaho gukorera Imana kubwo abantu, kugira ngo ashikane amashikanwa, atange ikimazi, vyompi vy'ivyaha;
58005002	kandi ashobora kwihanganira inyoberwa n'abazimiye, kuko na we nyene hari aho agira intege nke.
58005003	Ni co gituma akwiye no kwitangira ibimazi vy'ivyaha vyiwe, nk'uko abitangira abandi bantu.
58005004	Nta muntu yiha ico cubahiro, kiretse ahamagawe n'Imana, nk'uko Aroni yahamagawe.
58005005	Ni ko biri, na Kristo si we yihaye ico cubahiro co kuba umuherezi mukuru, ariko yagihawe n'iyamubariye iti: "Uri Ubura bwanje, Uwu musi ndakuvyaye."
58005006	Nk'uko yavuze ahandi iti: "Uri umuherezi ibihe bidashira, Mu buryo bwa Melekisedeki."
58005007	Kristo mu misi yabaye mu mubiri, amaze kwinginga no gusenga cane iyashoboye kumukiza urupfu, atakamba cane arira, kandi amaze kwumvirwa kubwo kuyubaha kwiwe,
58005008	naho yari Umwana, yigishwa kwumvira Imana n'ivyo yababajwe,
58005009	kandi amaze guhingurwa rwose, abera abamwumvira bose inyanduruko y'agakiza kadashira,
58005010	Imana imaze kumwita umuherezi mukuru mu buryo bwa Melekisedeki.
58005011	Tumufiseko vyinshi vyo kuvuga, kandi bigoye isobanura, kuko mwabaye ibitumva.
58005012	Naho mwari mugeze kuba abigisha, kuko mumaze igihe kirekire mwiga, mukwiye kwongera kwigishwa namwe nyene ivya mbere vy'itanguriro ry'ivyavuzwe n'Imana. Kandi mwahindutse abakwiye gutungwa n'amata, si ukugaburirwa ivyo kurya bigumye.
58005013	Nuko uwutunzwe n'amata aba ataramenya ijambo ry'ukugororoka, kuko aba ari uruhinja.
58005014	Ariko, ivyo kurya bigumye ni ivyo abakuze, bafise ubwenge, maze kubwo kwama babukoresha, bumenyera gutandukanya ikibi n'iciza.
58006001	Nuko rero turengane ivya mbere vya Kristo, twigire imbere, dushike ku vyo gutunganywa rwose, ntidusubire gushiraho itanguriro ryo kwihana ibikorwa vy'impfagusa, no kwizera Imana,
58006002	no kwigisha ivyo kubatizwa, ivyo kurambikwako ibiganza, ivyo kuzuka kw'abapfuye, ivyo gutsindwa n'urubanza kw'ibihe bidashira.
58006003	Imana ni yabikunda turagenza dutyo.
58006004	Kuko abamaze kwakirwa n'umuco, bagatamira ingabire iva mw'ijuru, bagasangira Mpwemu Yera,
58006005	bagatamira ijambo ryiza ry'Imana, n'ububasha bwo mu gihe kizoza,
58006006	maze bakagwa bakabivamwo, ntibishoboka gusubira kubahindura bashasha ngo bihane. Kuko bongera kwibambira Umwana w'Imana, bakamuteterereza ahibonekeza.
58006007	Indimo zinyoye imvura yaziguyeko kenshi, iyo zimezemwo ibirimwa bikwiye abazirimiwe, zironka umugisha w'Imana.
58006008	Ariko iyo zimezemwo imikere n'ibitovu, ziba zisivye, ziba zisigaje gatoya zikavumwa, iherezo ryazo ni uguturirwa.
58006009	Ariko, abo nkunda, naho tuvuze dutyo, turazi ivyanyu tudakekeranya yuko birusha ivyo kuba vyiza, kandi bizanana n'agakiza.
58006010	Imana ntigabitanya ngo yibagire ibikorwa vyanyu n'urukundo mwerekanye ko mukunze izina ryayo, kuko mwatunga abera, na none mukibatunze.
58006011	Kandi turagomba cane yuko umuntu wese wo muri mwebwe yerekana uwo mwete nyene w'ivyizigiro vyuzuye gushitsa kw'iherezo;
58006012	kugira ngo ntimube ibinebwe, ariko mwigane abaheshwa n'ukwizera n'ukwihangana kuragwa ivyasezeranywe.
58006013	Hamwe Imana yasezeranira Aburahamu isezerano, kuko ata we yogira indahiro ayiruta, yarirahiye
58006014	iti: "Eka no kuguha umugisha nzowuguha, kandi no kukugwiza nzokugwiza."
58006015	Ni ko vyamubereye amaze kwihangana, ahabwa ivyasezeranywe.
58006016	Kuko abantu bagira indahiro uwubaruta, no mu mpari zabo zose indahiro irengeje ikaba ari yo iziheraheza.
58006017	Ni co catumye Imana, kuko igomba kurushiriza kwereka abaragwa b'ivyasezeranywe ingene imigabo yayo idahinduka, ishira hagati indahiro kuba umuhuza;
58006018	kugira ngo bibiri bidahinduka, ivyo Imana itabasha kubesheramwo, biduheshe kurema cane, twebwe ahashitse mu buhungiro, ni bwo kugumya cane ivyizigiro vyashizwe imbere yacu.
58006019	Ivyo vyizigiro tubifise nk'ikizirika umutima kigumye, gikomeye, cinjira hirya y'igitambara gikingiriye ahera cane,
58006020	aho Yesu yatwinjiriye, atwitangiye imbere, amaze guhinduka umuherezi mukuru w'ibihe bidashira mu buryo bwa Melekisedeki.
58007001	Uwo Melekisedeki, umwami w'i Salemu, umuherezi w'Imana Isumbavyose, ni we yasanganiye Aburahamu, aramuhezagira, hamwe Aburahamu yagaruka, avuye kunesha abami.
58007002	Ni we kandi Aburahamu yagabanirije ikigira icumi muri vyose, irya mbere asobanurwa, ngo Umwami agororoka, kandi irya kabiri yitwa Umwami w'i Salemu, risobanurwa, ngo Umwami w'amahoro.
58007003	Nta se, nta nyina, nta mamuko, nta tanguriro ry'imisi canke iherezo ry'ubugingo, ariko agereranywa n'Umwana w'Imana, kandi na ntaryo ahora ari umuherezi.
58007004	Nuko mwiyumvire uwo muntu ingene ahambaye, uwo Aburahamu sogokuruza mukuru yahaye icacumi co mu minyago iruta iyindi.
58007005	Kandi mu bana ba Lewi, ivyagezwe bigera yuko abahawe ubuherezi batangisha abantu icacumi, ni bo bavukanyi, naho abo bakomotse mu rura rwa Aburahamu.
58007006	Ariko wa wundi adaharurwa mu muryango wabo yatangishije Aburahamu ikigira icumi, kandi ahezagira nyene gusezeranywa.
58007007	Ariko nta wohakana ko uworoshe adahezagirwa n'uwumurengeye.
58007008	Kandi muri twebwe, abantu bapfa ni bo bahabwa icacumi, ariko muri ya yandi majambo cahawe uwushingirwa intahe ko ariho.
58007009	Kandi twoshobora kuvuga yuko Lewi, umwe ahabwa icacumi, na we yari yaragitanze muri Aburahamu,
58007010	kuko yari akiri mu rura rwa sekuruza, hamwe Melekisedeki yamusanganira.
58007011	None iyaba gutunganywa rwose kwazanywe n'ubuherezi bw'Abalewi,--kuko ku butware bwabwo ari ho ubwo bwoko bwahawe ivyagezwe,--ni iki catumye bigikwiye ko haboneka uwundi muherezi wo mu buryo bwa Melekisedeki, atavugwa mu buryo bwa Aroni?
58007012	Iyo ubuherezi buhindutse, ivyagezwe ntibibura guhinduka na vyo.
58007013	Kuko uwavuzweko ivyo, ari uwo mu wundi muryango, utigeze kuvamwo uwakoze igikorwa co ku gicaniro.
58007014	Birazwi yuko Umwami wacu yakomotse kuri Yuda, kandi uwo muryango Mose nta co yawuvuzeko c'ubuherezi.
58007015	Ivyo birushiriza guseruka rwose, ko haboneka uwundi muherezi, ahwanye na Melekisedeki,
58007016	atahawe ubuherezi n'uko vyashinzweho n'ivyagezwe vyo mu buryo bw'abantu, ariko yahawe ubushinzwe n'ubushobozi bw'ubugingo budashobora gukurwaho.
58007017	Kuko ashingirwa intahe, ngo uri umuherezi ibihe bidashira, Mu buryo bwa Melekisedeki.
58007018	Nuko rero icagezwe ca mbere cakuweho kubwo inkomezi nke zaco n'ikimazi gike,
58007019	(kuko ivyagezwe bitigeze kugira ico bihingura rwose) hasubizwaho ivyizigiro bikiruta, biduhesha kwegera Imana.
58007020	Kandi ivyo ntivyabaye hatariho indahiro.
58007021	Abalewi bo bahawe ubuherezi ata ndahiro; ariko iyabuhaye uwo yararahiye, imubwiye iti: "Uhoraho ararahiye," ntazokwicuza Ati: "Uri umuherezi ibihe bidashira."
58007022	Uko ni ko Yesu yabaye umwishinzi w'isezerano riruta rya rindi.
58007023	Kandi ba bandi Babaye abaherezi benshi, kuko urupfu rubabuza kwamaho;
58007024	ariko uwo we, kuko yamaho ibihe bidashira, afise ubuherezi budakurwaho.
58007025	Ni co gituma ashobora gukiza rwose abashikira Imana kubwiwe kuko na ntaryo yamaho ngo abasabire.
58007026	Vyari bitubereye kugira umuherezi mukuru ameze atyo, yera, atagira ubugunge, atanduye, yatandukanijwe n'abanyavyaha, yashizwe hejuru y'amajuru,
58007027	atarinda kubanza gutanga ibimazi vy'ivyaha vyiwe uko bukeye, nka ba baherezi bakuru bandi, hanyuma agatanga ivyo abandi bantu. Kuko ivyo yabikoze rimwe, hamwe yitanga.
58007028	Ivyagezwe bishiraho abanyantege nke kuba abaherezi bakuru, ariko ijambo ry'indahiro yaherukiye ivyagezwe rishiraho Umwana w'Imana yahinguwe rwose gushitsa ibihe bidashira.
58008001	Mu yo tuvuga, yose arutwa na rimwe, ni iri: dufise umuherezi mukuru ameze atyo, avyagiye i buryo bw'intebe y'Iyihambaye cane yo mw'ijuru,
58008002	akorera ahera, no mw'ihema nyakuri, ryashinzwe n'Uhoraho atari abantu.
58008003	Kuko umuherezi mukuru wese ashirirwaho gushikana amashikanwa no gucumita ibimazi. Ni co gituma wa wundi na we akwiye kugira ico ashikana.
58008004	Iyaba ari mw'isi ntiyobaye umuherezi, kuko hari abandi bashikana amashikanwa nk'uko ivyagezwe bibibwiriza.
58008005	Kandi abo bakorera igishushanyo n'igitutu c'ivyo mw'ijuru, nk'uko Mose yabwiwe n' Imana, agira akoreshe rya hema iti: "Ugire umwete wo gukoresha vyose, ubigereranye n'ikigereranyo werekewe kuri wa musozi."
58008006	Ariko none, igikorwa yahawe kirusha icabo kuba ciza, nk'uko ari umuhuza w'isezerano riruta iryabo, kuko ryashizweho n'ivyasezeranywe biruta ivyo iryabo.
58008007	Iyo rya rindi rya mbere ritabako agasembwa, ntihari hakwiye kuronderwa irindi.
58008008	Kuko yavuze ibagaya iti: "Ehe imisi igira ize," ni jewe Uhoraho ndabivuze, Aho nzosezerana isezerano rishasha n'inzu ya Isirayeli n'umuryango wa Yuda,
58008009	ridahwanye n'isezerano nasezeranye na ba sekuruza, Ku musi nabafata ukuboko nkabakura mu gihugu ca Misiri, Kuko batagumye mw'isezerano ryanje, Nanje sinabababara, ni jewe Uhoraho ndabivuze.
58008010	Kuko iri ari ryo sezerano nzosezerana n'umuryango w'Abisirayeli Hanyuma y'iyo misi, ni jewe Uhoraho ndabivuze. Nzoshira ivyagezwe vyanje mu bwenge bwabo, No ku mitima yabo kandi ni ho nzovyandika, Nanje nzobabera Imana, Na bo bazoba abantu banje.
58008011	Kandi ntibazokwigishanya, ngo umuntu wese yigishe mugenzi we, Canke ngo yigishe uwo bavukana ati: "Menya Uhoraho, Kuko bose bazonyimenyera, Uhereye k'uwo hasi ugashitsa k'uwuhambaye muri bo.
58008012	Kuko nzobagirira ikigongwe ku kugabitanya kwabo, Kandi ivyaha vyabo sinzovyibuka ukundi.
58008013	Ko avuga ati: "Isezerano rishasha rero irya mbere yarishajishije; ariko igisaza kikaba akaheze kiba kigira gikamangane.
58009001	Nuko isezerano rya mbere na ryo ryarimwo ibirongora ivyo ubuherezi, rifise n'ahera, ariko ho muri iyi si.
58009002	Kuko hari ihema ryubatswe, mu ryo hino harimwo igiterekwako amatara, imeza n'imitsima yagenewe gushikanirwa Imana yama kuri yo. Iryo ryitwa Ahera.
58009003	Kandi hirya y'igihuzu ca kabiri gikinze, hari ihema ryitwa Ahera Cane.
58009004	Harimwo igicaniro co guturirirako imibavu cakozwe mw'izahabu, harimwo n'isandugu y'isezerano yometsweko izahabu impande zose, irimwo urwavya rw'izahabu rurimwo manu, irimwo na ya nkoni ya Aroni yashurika, na vya bisate vy' amabuye vyanditsweko isezerano.
58009005	Kandi hejuru yayo hari abakerubi b'ubwiza bateye igitutu umutemere wo gutangirako ibimazi; ivyo ntidushobora kubidonda kimwekimwe ubu nyene.
58009006	Nuko ivyo vyateguwe bityo, abaherezi na ntaryo bama binjira mw'ihema ryo hino, kugira ngo bashitse ivyo ubuherezi.
58009007	Ariko mu rya kabiri hinjiramwo umuherezi mukuru wenyene, rimwe gusa uko umwaka uheze, ariko ntiyinjiramwo atajanye amaraso yo kwitangira no gutangirira ivyaha vy'abantu batabizi.
58009008	Mpwemu Yera amenyekanisha atyo yuko inzira ija ahera cane itaribwerekanwe, ihema rya mbere rikiriho.
58009009	Ni ryo kigereranyo c'igihe ca none, abakurikira ivyagezwe vyaryo bashikana ibimazi bagatanga ibimazi, ariko ku ruhande rw'ijwi ryo mu mutima ntibishobora gutunganya usenga,
58009010	kuko ivyo, hamwe n'ivyo ivyo kurya, ivyo kunywa, ivyo kwiyuhagira bo n'ukwoza vy'uburyo bwinshi, ari amabwirizwa yo mu buryo bw'abantu gusa, yashinzwe gushitsa igihe co gutunganywa.
58009011	Ariko Kristo amaze kuza, umuherezi mukuru w'ivyiza bizoza, aca mw'ihema rirusha rya rindi kuba irihambaye n'iritunganye rwose, ritakozwe n'intoke, bisobanurwa ngo ritari iryo mu vyaremwe vy'ubu.
58009012	Kandi amaraso y'impene canke ayo amashuri, si yo yamushikanye ahera cane, ariko yahashikanywe n'amaraso yiwe rimwe gusa, yironkeye ugucungura kw'ibihe bidashira.
58009013	None amaraso y'impene n'ayo impfizi bo n'umunyota w'inka yavutse ubwa mbere umijwe abahumanye, ko vyeza imibiri igahumanuka,
58009014	mbega amaraso ya Kristo, uwo yitanze ku Mana atagira agasembwa, abitewe na Mpwemu ahoraho, ntazorushiriza guhumanura imitima yanyu ngo ibikorwa vy'impfagusa biyivemwo, kugira ngo mubone ingene mukorera Imana nzima?
58009015	Ni co gituma aba umuhuza, ahesha isezerano risha, kugira ngo abahamagawe bahabwe umwandu udashira w'isezerano, bitewe n'uko habayeho urupfu rucungura abacumuye bakiganzwa n'isezerano rya mbere.
58009016	Kuko aho ikete ry'iragi riri hakwiye rwose yuko urupfu rw'uwaraze ruseruka.
58009017	Ikete ry'iragi kibeshwaho n'urupfu rwonyene, kuko ritagira ikimazi uwaraze akiriho.
58009018	Ni co gituma isezerano rya mbere ritasezeranywe ata maraso.
58009019	Mose amaze kubwira abantu bose amabwirizwa yose nk'uko vyagezwe, yakira amaraso y'ishuri n'ayo impene, amazi n'ubwoya bw'intama bujobetswe agahama, yakira na ezobu, acucagira bacucagirisha. Igitabo c'ivyagezwe, bo n'abantu bose,
58009020	arababwira ati: "Aya ni yo maraso y'isezerano Imana yabagereye."
58009021	Kandi ihema n'ibikoresho vyose vy'ivyo ubuherezi, na vyo ni uko abicucagira amaraso.
58009022	Nk'uko ivyagezwe biri, ibintu ni nka vyose vyozwa n'amaraso, kandi hatavuye amaraso ntihaba guharirwa ivyaha.
58009023	Nuko vyari bibereye ko ibigereranyo vy'ivyo mw'ijuru vyozwa n'ivyo bimazi, ariko, ivyo mw'ijuru ubwavyo bikozwa n'ibimazi biruta ivyo.
58009024	Kuko Kristo atinjiye ahera cane hakozwe n'intoke, h'ikigereranyo c'aho ukuri, ariko yinjiye mw'ijuru ubwaho, kugira ngo noneho aduserukire imbere y'amaso y'Imana.
58009025	Kandi ntiyashikanyweyo no kwitanga kenshi, nk'uko umuherezi mukuru yinjira ahera cane uko umwaka uheze, ajanye amaraso atari ayiwe;
58009026	kuko iyo biba bityo, aba yari akwiye kubabazwa kenshi uhereye ku kuremwa kw'isi. Yamara ubu yabonetse rimwe kw'iherezo ry'ibihe, kugira ngo akuzeho icaha ukwitanga.
58009027	Kandi nk'uko abantu babikiwe gupfa rimwe, hanyuma yaho hakaza imanza,
58009028	na Kristo ni uko, yamaze gutangwa rimwe ngo yishireko ivyaha vya benshi, azoboneka ubwa kabiri, atazanywe n'ivyaha, abonekere abamwiteze ngo abakize.
58010001	Ivyagezwe ko bifise igitutu c'ivyiza bizoza, bidafise ishusho bwite y'ivyo vyiza, nta ho vyoshobora guhingura abegera igicaniro, bibahingurisha ivyo bimazi nyene bahora batanga imyaka n'imyaka.
58010002	Iyo bibishobora, mbega ntibaba barasizeho kubitanga? Kuko abavyitangirira bamaze guhumanurwa rwose rimwe, bataba bakigira imitima irimwo ijwi ribagiriza ivyaha.
58010003	Ariko muri ivyo bimazi hari icibukiriza ivyaha uko umwaka uheze.
58010004	Kuko bidashoboka ko amaraso y'impfizi n'ayo impene akuraho ivyaha.
58010005	Ni co catumye, hamwe yaza mw'isi, avuga Ati: "Ibimazi n'amashikanwa ntiwabigomvye, Ariko wanteguriye umubiri."
58010006	Ibimazi bituriwe bitagabanije, n'ibimazi vy'ivyaha, ntivyaguhimbaye.
58010007	Mperako ndavuga nti: "Ehe ndaje, (Mu muzingo w'igitabo ni ko binyanditsweko) Nzanywe no gukora ivyo ugomba, Mana."
58010008	Ahejeje kuvuga haruguru ati: "Ibimazi n'amashikanwa, n'ibimazi bituriwe bitagabanije n'ibimazi vy'ivyaha, ntiwabigomvye kandi ntivyaguhimbaye (ni vyo bitangwa nk'uko bibwirijwe n'ivyagezwe),"
58010009	aherako aravuga ati: "Ehe nzanywe no gukora ivyo ugomba." Akuraho ivya mbere ngo ashinge ivya kabiri.
58010010	Ukwo kugomba kwayo ni kwo kwatumye twezwa, tubiheshwa n'uko umubiri wa Yesu Kristo watanzwe rimwe gusa.
58010011	Kandi umuherezi wese ahagarara uko bukeye akora ivyo ubuherezi, atanga kenshi ivyo bimazi nyene, ata ho vyoshobora gukuraho ivyaha na mba.
58010012	Ariko uwo we, amaze gutanga ikimazi kimwe c'ivyaha kidahinduka, avyagira i buryo bw'Imana,
58010013	aheraho, arorera igihe abansi biwe bazohindurirwa intebe yo musi y'ibirenge vyiwe.
58010014	Kuko ikimazi kimwe ari co yatunganishije rwose abezwa, ukazoshitsa ibihe bidashira.
58010015	Kandi na Mpwemu Yera ni we cabona kidushingira intahe y'ivyo. Amaze kuvuga
58010016	ati: "Iri ni ryo sezerano nzosezerana na bo Hanyuma y'iyo misi, ni jewe Uhoraho ndabivuze; Nzoshira ivyagezwe vyanje mu mitima yabo, No mu bwenge bwabo kandi ni ho nzovyandika; arongera
58010017	ati: "Kandi ivyaha vyabo n'ukugabitanya kwabo sinzovyibuka ukundi."
58010018	Ariko, aho ivyo bihariwe, ntihaba hakiriho gutanga ikimazi c'ivyaha.
58010019	Nuko bavukanyi, ko turi n'ubushizi bw'ubwoba bwo gushikanwa ahera cane n'amaraso ya Yesu,
58010020	duciye mu nzira yadutoboreye nshasha iri n'ubugingo, ica mu gihuzu gikinze, bisobanurwa ngo mu mubiri wiwe;
58010021	kandi ko dufise umuherezi akomeye aganza urugo rw'Imana.
58010022	Twegereze dufise imitima y'ukuri, twizeye ata mazinda, imitima yacu yogejwe ngo ivanwemwo ibitwagiriza bibi, imibiri yacu yuhagijwe amazi meza.
58010023	Tugumye ukwatura ivyizigiro vyacu ntikunyiganyige, kuko uwasezeranye ari uwo kwizerwa,
58010024	kandi twiyumviraneko, kugira ngo duterane umwete wo gukundana n'iryo ibikorwa vyiza.
58010025	Ntiduhebe gukoranira hamwe, nk'uko bamwe bagira, ariko duhanurane, kandi uko mubonye wa musi wegereza, murushirize kugenza mutyo.
58010026	Kuko namba dukora ivyaha ibigirankana, kandi tumaze guhabwa kumenya ivyo ukuri, ntihaba hagisigaye ikimazi c'ivyaha,
58010027	ariko haba hasigaye kwitegana ubwoba gutsindwa n'urubanza, no kwitega umuriro w'inkazi, uzorigata abansi b'Imana.
58010028	Uwukengereye ivyagezwe vya Mose, ivyabona bibiri canke bitatu biramwicisha, ata kagongwe.
58010029	Mugira ngo umuntu ntazoba akwiye guhanwa ibirushirije cane, asiribanze Umwana w'Imana, akiyumvira amaraso y'isezerano yamwejeje ko ari igihumane, agacokora Mpwemu w'ubuntu?
58010030	Kuko tuzi uwavuze ati: "Uguhora ni ukwanje, ni jewe nzobasubiriza mu nkoko." Kandi ati: "Uhoraho azocira urubanza abantu biwe.
58010031	Erega birateye ubwoba gukorokera mu maboko y'Imana nzima."
58010032	Ariko mwibuke imisi ya mbere, hamwe mwari mumaze kwakirwa n'umuco, mwihanganira ibisinzikaza vy'indwano nyinshi;
58010033	kimwe, mwacitse akamenyero mutukwa mubabazwa; ikindi, mwafatanije n'abagirirwa batyo.
58010034	Kuko mwababaranye n'ababoshwe, kandi mwemeye munezerewe kunyagwa ivyo mutunze, mumenya yuko mufise itunga riruta ivyo kuba ryiza, rikamaho.
58010035	Nuko ntimute ubushizi bw'ubwoba bwanyu! buri n'impera ikomeye.
58010036	Kuko mukwiye kwihangana, kugira ngo ni mwamara gukora ivyo Imana igomba mubone guhabwa ivyasezeranywe.
58010037	Kuko hasigaye igihe gito cane, Kandi uwugira aze, azoza, ntazoteba.
58010038	Ariko, umugororotsi wanje azobeshwaho n'ukwizera, Naho ni yisokora ntazohimbara umutima wanje.
58010039	Ariko tweho ntituri abo mu bisokora bagahona, ariko turi abo mu bizera, ubugingo bwabo bugakizwa.
58011001	Ukwizera ni ukumenya rwose ivyizigirwa, udakekeranya ngo ntibizoba, kandi ibitabonwa ni kwo kubitumenyesha ko ari ivyo ukuri.
58011002	Icatumye aba kera bashingirwa intahe ni uko bari bagufise.
58011003	Ukwizera ni kwo kutumenyesha yuko isi yaremwe n'ijambo ry'Imana, ni co catumye ibiboneka bitaremwe mu biseruka.
58011004	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Abeli aha Imana ikimazi kiruta ica Kayini, ni kwo kwamuhesheje gushingirwa intahe ko ari umugororotsi, hamwe Imana yashingira intahe ibimazi vyiwe yuko ari vyiza, kandi ni kwo kwatumye n'ubu akivuga, naho yapfuye.
58011005	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Henoki ajanwa mw'ijuru, ngo ntabone urupfu, kandi ntiyaboneka, kuko Imana yamujanye. Kuko yashingiwe intahe atarajanwa yuko yahimbaye Imana.
58011006	Kandi uwutizera ntibishoboka ko ayihimbara; kuko uwegera Imana akwiye kwizera yuko iriho, igaha impera abayirondera.
58011007	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Nowa yubaha, amaze kuburirwa n'Imana ibitaribwaboneke, akabaza ubwato bwo kurokora abo mu nzu yiwe, kandi ni kwo kwamuhaye gutsindisha abari mw'isi, no kuragwa ukugororoka kuzanwa n'ukwizera.
58011008	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Aburahamu yumvira Imana imuhamagaye, akaja ahantu yari abikiwe kuragwa. Nuko agenda, atazi iyo aja.
58011009	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye aba umwimuka mu gihugu yasezeraniwe, nk'ikitari iciwe, akabana mu mahema na Isaka na Yakobo, abaraganywe na we ivyo vyasezeranywe.
58011010	Kuko yari arorereye ca gisagara cubatswe kw'umushinge, umugezi n'umwubatsi waco n'Imana.
58011011	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye na Sara ashobozwa gusama inda, naho yari yaraciye, kuko yiyumviriye yuko iyasezeranye ari iyo kwizerwa.
58011012	Ni co catumye umuntu umwe--kandi uwo yari akaheze--yamukwako n'isinzi nk'inyenyeri zo kw'ijuru, kandi n'abangana n'umusenyi utoharurika uri kw'isesero ry'ikiyaga utoharurika.
58011013	Abo bose bapfuye bacizeye, batarahabwa ivyasezeranywe, ariko barabibona biri kure bakabisanganira, bakemera ko ari akavantara n'ingenzi kw'isi.
58011014	Abavuga batyo baba berekana yuko barondera igihugu cabo bwite.
58011015	Iyo baba barakumbuye ico bavuyemwo, baba barabonye uburyo bwo gusubirayo.
58011016	Ariko noneho barifuza igihugu kirushije ico kuba ciza, ni ico mw'ijuru. Ni co gituma Imana itamaramazwa no kwitwa Imana yabo, kuko yabateguriye igisagara.
58011017	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Aburahamu atanga Isaka ko ikimazi, hamwe yagezwa; mbere uwari yarakiranye igishika amasezerano, yariko aratanga umwana wiwe w'ikinege kw'ikimazi,
58011018	uwo yari yarabariwe ivyiwe, ngo Kuri Isaka ni ho uruvyaro rwawe ruzokwitirirwa;
58011019	kuko yishimiye yuko Imana ishobora no kuzura abapfuye, ni co catumye amugarurirwa nk'uwuzutse.
58011020	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Isaka ahezagira Yakobo na Esawu abahesha imigisha y'ibizoba.
58011021	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Yakobo, aho yagira acikane, ahezagira abana ba Yosefu bompi, agasenga yishimikije ipfundo ry'inkoni yiwe.
58011022	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Yosefu, aho yagira apfe, avuga ivyo kuvayo kw'Abisirayeli, agatanga amategeko y'ivyo amagufa yiwe.
58011023	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Mose, amaze kuvuka, anyegezwa n'abavyeyi biwe amezi atatu, kuko babonye ko ari akana keza, ntibatinya ibwirizwa ry'umwami.
58011024	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Mose, amaze gukura, yanka kwitwa umwana w'umukobwa wa Farawo,
58011025	agahitamwo kugiriranwa nabi n'abantu b'Imana, akabirutisha kumara igihe mu bihimbaro vy'ivyaha.
58011026	Kuko yiyumviriye yuko gucokoranwa na Kristo ari ubutunzi burengeye itunga ryo mu Misiri, kuko yatumbera ingero azogererwa.
58011027	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye ava mu Misiri, ntiyatinya ishavu ry'umwami, kuko yashikamye nk'aho abona Iyitaboneka.
58011028	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye ashinga Pasika, no kumijagira amaraso, kugira ngo uwuhonya imfura ntabakoreko.
58011029	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye baca mu Kiyaga Gitukura, nk' abaca ku musozi, ariko Abanyamisiri babigejeje, bararengerwa.
58011030	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye impome z'amabuye z'i Yeriko zisenyuka, bamaze kuzikikuza imisi indwi.
58011031	Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Rahabu, maraya, ataranduranwa n'abatumviye Imana, kuko yakiranye amahoro abaje gusuma urusaku.
58011032	Mvuge ikindi ki? Kuko igihe condengana ndondoye ivya Gideyoni, ivya Baraki, ivya Samusoni, ivya Yefuta, ivya Dawidi, ivya Samweli n'ivyo abavugishwa n'Imana,
58011033	baheshejwe n'ukwizera gutsinda abami, no gukora ibigororotse, no kuronka ivyasezeranywe, no kuziba iminwa y'intambwe,
58011034	no kuzimya ubukare bw'umuriro, no gukira ubugi bw'inkota, no guhindurwa mu ntege nke ngo zicike inkomezi, no kuba agahebuza mu ntambara, no kunesha ingabo z'abanyamahanga.
58011035	Abagore basubiye kubona abo babuze kuko bazutse, abandi bicishwa amahiri ntibemera gucungurwa, kugira ngo bazohabwe ukuzuka kurushiriza kuba kwiza.
58011036	Abandi bageragereshwa gushinyagurirwa no gukubitwa ibimoko, mbere bashirwa mu migozi no mu mabohero;
58011037	bicishijwe amabuye, bakerewemwo kubiri, barageragejwe, bicishijwe inkota, bayerera bambaye insato z'intama n'izo impene, bari baburaniwe, bababazwa, bagirirwa nabi,
58011038	(isi ntiyari ibabereye ko bayibamwo), bayerera mu bugaragwa no mu misozi no mu masenga yo mu vyobo.
58011039	Abo bose bamaze gushingirwa intahe kubwo ukwizera kwabo, ntibahabwa ivyasezeranywe,
58011040	kuko Imana yabonye kera ikirushiriza kutubera iciza, kugira ngo abo ntibatunganywe rwose tutari kumwe.
58012001	Nuko natwe, ko dukikijwe n'igipfungu c'ivyabona kingana gityo, twiyambure ibituremera vyose, n'icaha gikunda kutwizingirako vuba, dusiganirwe ivyo twashizwe imbere twihanganye,
58012002	dutumbereye Yesu wenyene, ni we nyanduruko yo kwizera kandi ni we yagusozereye. Uwo, kubwo umunezero yashizwe imbere, yihanganiye umusaraba, arihangana ntiyagira isoni zawo, avyagira i buryo bw'intebe y'Imana.
58012003	Nuko mushire imitima kuri uwo yihanganiye ibihari bihambaye bityo abanyavyaha bamuharirije, ntimudohoke, ntimwihebure mu mitima yanyu.
58012004	Ntimuragera ku kuvishwa amaraso murwanya icaha,
58012005	kandi mwibagiye rya jambo ribahubura ribahanura nk'abana, ngo Mwana wanje, ntugaye igikangiro c'Uhoraho, Kandi ntiwihebure ni yaguhana.
58012006	Kuko uwo Uhoraho akunda ari we ahana, Kandi akubita uwo yemera wese ko ari umwana wiwe.
58012007	Ico mukwiye kwihanganira ni ugutozwa indero nziza. Imana ibagirira nk'abana bayo. Ni umwana ki, adakangirwa na se?
58012008	Ariko namba mudakangirwa nk'ico abandi bose bakorerwa, muri ibivyarwa, ntimuri ubura bwayo.
58012009	Kandi twari dufise ba data b'imibiri, baradukangira, natwe tukabubaha. None ntituzorushiriza cane kugororokera Se w'impwemu tugahoraho?
58012010	Kuko ba bandi badukangira imisi mike nk'uko bagomba, ariko we adukangirira ikigira ikimazi, kugira ngo dusangire na we ukwera kwiwe.
58012011	Nta gikangiro kiboneka ko giteye umunezero ako kanya, atari umubabaro, ariko hanyuma abamenyerejwe na co kibamira imbuto zizana amahoro zo kugororoka.
58012012	Nuko mugorore amaboko acitse urudendevu, n'amavi aregarega.
58012013	Kandi muharurire ibirenge vyanyu inzira zigororotse, kugira ngo igihinyiza ntigikondoke, ariko gikire.
58012014	Mukurikire kugiriranira amahoro n'abantu bose, n'ukwezwa, kuko utejejwe atazoraba Umwami.
58012015	Mwizigame, ntihagire umuntu adashikira ubuntu bw'Imana, kandi ntihagire umuzi wo kurura umera, ukabahagarika imitima, abenshi bakandura.
58012016	Ntihabeho umushirasoni, canke igihumane nka Esawu, yagurishije ivyo kuba samuragwa kwiwe ingaburo imwe.
58012017	Kuko muzi yuko hanyuma, hamwe yagomba kuragwa umugisha, atemerewe, kuko atabonye uburyo bwo kwihana, naho yawurondera cane arira.
58012018	Ntimwegereye umusozi wokorwako, waka umuriro, kandi ntimwegereye umwiza w'umuzimagiza, uwo umuzitanya, igihuhuta,
58012019	inzumbeti ivuga n'ijwi ry'amajambo; abaryumvise binginga kutabwirwa irindi jambo.
58012020	Kuko batashoboye kwemera ivyagezwe, ngo Naho coba igitungwa gikoze kuri uwo musozi bacicishe amabuye.
58012021	Kandi ivyabonetse vyari ibiteye ubwoba, vyatumye Mose avuga ati: "Mfise ubwoba cane, ndahinda agashitsi."
58012022	Ariko mwegereye umusozi Siyoni, n'umurwa w'Imana nzima, Yerusalemu ho mw'ijuru, n'ikoraniro rikuru ry'isinzi ry'abamarayika,
58012023	n'ishengero ry'abana b'imfura banditswe mw'ijuru, mwegereye n'Imana umucamanza wa bose n'impwemu z'abagororotsi batunganijwe rwose.
58012024	Mwegereye na Yesu, umuhuza ahesha isezerano rishasha, mwegereye n'amaraso acucagirwa, avuga ivyiza kurusha aya Abeli.
58012025	Mwirinde ntimwanke kwumva Iyiriko iravuga. Ba bandi ko batakize, hamwe banka uwababuririye mw'isi, tweho tuzorushiriza cane kudakira, namba dutera ibitugu Iyituburira iri mw'ijuru.
58012026	Ijwi ryayo ryanyiganyigije isi ico gihe; ariko noneho irasezeranye ati: "Hasigaye rimwe, ngatigitisha, si isi gusa, ariko n'ijuru na ryo."
58012027	Iryo jambo, ngo Hasigaye rimwe, ryerekana gukurwaho kw'ibinyiganyizwa, kuko ari ivyaremwe, kugira ngo ibitoshobora kunyiganyizwa bigumeho.
58012028	Ni co gituma, kuko twakira ubwami budashobora kunyiganyizwa, dukwiye gukenguruka, kugira ngo tubone ingene dukorera Imana tuyihimbaye, tuyubaha tuyitinya;
58012029	kuko Imana yacu ari umuriro utongora.
58013001	Ni hagumeho urukundo rw'abavukanyi.
58013002	Ntimwibagire kugirira neza abashitsi; kuko bamwe bagize batyo bahaye indaro abamarayika batabizi.
58013003	Mwibuke ababoshwe nk'ababohanywe na bo. Mwibuke n'abagirirwa nabi, kuko namwe muri mu mubiri.
58013004	Umubano w'abarongoranye ni wubahwe na bose, kandi uburiri bwabo ntibuhumanywe kuko Imana izocira urubanza inshirasoni n'abasambanyi.
58013005	Gukunda amahera ntikube mu ngeso zanyu; ivyo mufise bibabumbe; kuko ubwayo yavuze iti: "Nta ho nzoguhemukira, nta ho nzoguta."
58013006	Ni co gituma tuvuga dushize ubwoba tuti: "Uhoraho ni umutabazi wanje, sinzotinya; None umuntu yoshobora kungira iki?"
58013007	Mwibuke ababaganza, bakababwira ijambo ry'Imana; mwitegereje iherezo ry'ingeso zabo, mwigane ukwizera kwabo.
58013008	Yesu Kristo uko yari ari ejo, n'uwu musi ni ko akiri, ni ko azokwama ibihe bidashira.
58013009	Ntimutwarwe n'inyigisho z'uburyo bwinshi zadutse; kuko iciza ari uko umutima ukomezwa n'ubuntu bw'Imana, ntukomezwe n'ivyo kurya, kuko abishize muri vyo bitabagiriye ikimazi.
