58013010	Dufise igicaniro, ico abakorera muri rya hema batemererwa kurirako.
58013011	Kuko imivyimba ya vya bitungwa, ivyo umuherezi mukuru ajana amaraso yavyo ahera kuba indishi y'ivyaha, ituririrwa inyuma y'amahema.
58013012	Ni co catumye na Yesu ababarizwa inyuma y'irembo, kugira ngo yezeshe abantu amaraso yawe.
58013013	Nuko tuve muri ayo mahema, tumusange inyuma yayo, twiremetse ugucokorwa kwiwe.
58013014	Kuko hano tutahafise igisagara kizokwamaho, ariko turondera ikizoza.
58013015	Nuko na ntaryo twame duha Imana ishikanwa ryo gukenguruka tubiheshwa n'uwo, ni co mbuto z'iminwa ishima izina ryayo.
58013016	Kugira neza no kugira ubuntu ntimukavyibagire, kuko ibimazi bimeze bityo ari vyo bihimbara Imana.
58013017	Mwumvire ababaganza, mubagamburukire; kuko ari bo bama bagavye bazigama imitima yanyu, nk'abazobibazwa. Mugenze mutyo kugira ngo babikore banezerewe, batitsa umutima, kuko bimeze bityo ata co vyomarira mwebwe.
58013018	Mudusengere, kuko tuzi tudakekeranya ko turi n'imitima itarimwo ijwi ritwagiriza ikibi, tugomba kugira ingeso nziza muri vyose.
58013019	Kandi ndabinginga nshimitse ngo mudusengere, kugira ngo ntebutswe kubagarukanirwa vuba.
58013020	Imana nyene amahoro, imwe yakura Umwami wacu Yesu mu bapfuye, ari we Mwungere mukuru w'intama, imukujeyo amaraso y'isezerano ry'ibihe bidashira,
58013021	ibe ari yo ibatunganya rwose mu ciza cose, kugira ngo mukore ivyo igomba, ikorera muri twebwe ibishimwa mu maso yayo, kubwa Yesu Kristo. Icubahiro kibe icayo ibihe bitazoshira. Amina.
58013022	Ariko bavukanyi, ndabahanura, mwihanganire iri jambo ribahanura, kuko ndabandikiye amajambo make.
58013023	Mumenye yuko umuvukanyi Timoteyo yarekuwe; ni yaza vuba tuzobonana namwe.
58013024	Muntahirize ababaganza bose, bo n'abera bose. Abo muri Italiya barabatasha.
58013025	Ubuntu bubane namwe mwese. Amina.
59001001	Yakobo, umushumba w'Imana n'uwo Umwami Yesu Kristo, ndabandikiye abo mu miryango icumi n'ibiri y'abasabagiye. Ni muganuke.
59001002	Mwiyumvire ko ari ivyo kunezererwa rwose, bavukanyi, ni mwagwa mu bibagerageza bitari bimwe,
59001003	mumenye yuko ibigeza ukwizera kwanyu bitera ukwihangana.
59001004	Ariko ukwihangana gukwiye guhingura igikorwa cakwo, ngo mubone gutungana rwose muhinguwe; mudahajije na kamwe.
59001005	Ariko asangwa hari uwo muri mwebwe akenye ubwenge, ni abusabe Imana, igabira bose ititangiriye itama, idaterana imiragwe, azobuhabwa.
59001006	Ariko asabe yizeye, ata co akekeranya, kuko uwukekeranya ameze nk'umupfunda wo mu kiyaga, utwarwa n'umuyaga, usimbaguritswa.
59001007	Uwo muntu ntiyiyumvire ko ari n'ico azohabwa n'Umwami Imana,
59001008	kuko ari umuntu w'imitima ibiri, ahindagurika mu nzira ziwe zose."
59001009	Ariko, umuvukanyi w'umufafara ni yirate ko akujijwe,
59001010	umutunzi na we, ni yirate ko acishijwe bugufi, kuko azoyoka nk'amashurwe y'ivyatsi.
59001011	Kuko izuba rirasa, rizanye indugumba, rikumisha ivyatsi, amashurwe yavyo agahunguruka, ubwiza bw'ishusho yayo bugashira. Uko ni ko umutunzi azoyonga mu ngendo ziwe.
59001012	Harahiriwe umuntu yihanganira ibimugerageza, kuko ni yamara kurama azohabwa igitsibo c'ubugingo, ico Imana yasezeraniye abayikunda.
59001013	Umuntu ni yageragezwa ngo akora ibibi, ntavuge ngo Imana ni yo ingerageje. Kuko Imana itageragezwa n'ibibi, kandi na yo nta we ibigerageresha.
59001014	Ariko umuntu wese ageragezwa, iyo akwezwe n'ivyo yifuza bikamusuka.
59001015	Maze ukwo kwifuza gutwara inda, kukavyara icaha, icaha kimaze gukura kikavyara urupfu.
59001016	Ntimuzimire, bavukanyi nkunda.
59001017	Gutanga kwose kwiza n'ingabire yose itunganye rwose biva mw'ijuru, vyururuka biva kuri Se w'imico, adashobora guhinduka canke kugira igitutu gitewe n'uguhindagurika.
59001018	Nk'uko yabigabiye ubwayo, yatuvyarishije ijambo ry'ukuri, kugira ngo tube nk'ivyeze ubwa mbere mu biremwa vyayo.
59001019	Ivyo murabizi, bavukanyi nkunda. Yamara umuntu wese ni yihutire kwumva, atebe kuvuga, atebe kuraka.
59001020	Kuko ishavu ry'umuntu ridakora ivyo ukugororoka kw'Imana.
59001021	Nuko rero, mwiyambure imyanda yose n'ububi busigaye, mwakirane ubugwaneza ijambo ritewe muri mwebwe, rishobora gukiza ubugingo bwanyu.
59001022	Kandi mube abakora ivyo iryo jambo, ntimube abaryumva gusa, mwibesha.
59001023	Kuko uwumva iryo jambo ntarikore, ameze nk'umuntu yirabiye mu cirore mu maso hiwe yavukanye.
59001024	Amaze kwiraba, akagenda, uwo mwanya agaca yiyibagira uko asa.
59001025	Ariko, uwitegereza ivyagezwe bitunganye rwose, ari vyo vy'umwidegemvyo, akabishishikara, atari uwumva akavyibagira, ariko ari uwubikora, ni we azohabwa umugisha mu vyo akora.
59001026	Umuntu ni yigira ngo n'umunyedini, ntafate ururimi, ariko agahenda umutima wiwe, idini y'uwo izoba ari iyo ubusa.
59001027	Idini itunganye itagira agasembwa imbere y'Imana Data wa twese, ni ukuraba impfuvyi n'abapfakazi mu marushwa yabo, no kwirinda ngo ntiwanduzwe n'ivyo isi.
59002001	Bavukanyi, kwizera Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo w'ubwiza ntikubemwo kurobanura abantu ku cubahiro.
59002002	Mw'ishengero ryanyu ni hinjiramwo umuntu yambaye impeta y'izahabu n'impuzu zishajije, hakinjira n'umworo yambaye impuzu mbi y'ubuhoma,
59002003	namwe mukitegereza uwambaye impuzu zishajije, mukamubarira muti: "Ni wicare hano heza;" kandi mukabarira nya mworo muti: "Weho hagarara hariya, canke icara hambavu y'ibirenge vyanje;"
59002004	none se ntimuba mwisobanuye, mukaba abacamanza biyumvira ibibi?
59002005	Ni mwumve, bavukanyi nkunda. Mbega Imana ntiyatoranirije aboro b'ivyo isi ngo babe abatunzi mu kwizera, no kuragwa ubwami yasezeraniye abayikunda?
59002006	Ariko mweho mwatetereje umworo. None abatunzi si bo babatwaza amanyama, bakaba ari bo babakwega babajana mu manza?
59002007	Si bo batyoza izina ryiza mwitirirwa?
59002008	Mugabo namba mushitsa icagezwe c'i bwami nk'uko canditswe, ngo Mukunde ababanyi banyu nk'uko mwikunda, muba mugize neza.
59002009	Ariko iyo murobanuye abantu ku cubahiro, muba mukoze icaha, mutsinzwe n'ivyagezwe ko mubaye abanyabicumuro.
59002010	Kuko umuntu wese azokwitondera ivyagezwe vyose, agatsitara kuri kimwe, azoba acumuye kuri vyose.
59002011	Uwavuze ati: "Ntugasambane," ni we yavuze ati: "Ntukice." "Nuko rero niyo utasambana ariko ukica, uzoba ucumuye ku vyagezwe.
59002012	Muvuge kandi mukore nk'abagira bacirwe urubanza n'ivyagezwe bizana umwidegemvyo.
59002013	Kuko urubanza rutagirira akagongwe uwutagize akagongwe. Ariko mu rubanza ikigongwe kiratsinda.
59002014	Vyomara iki ga bavukanyi, namba umuntu avuga yuko afise ukwizera, ata bikorwa akora? Mbega ukwo kwizera kwoshobora kumukiza?
59002015	Ni haba hariho uwo muvukana ari we wese yoba yambaye ubusa, agenda aburanirwa ku vyo kurya,
59002016	maze umwe muri mwebwe akamubwira ati: ""Genda amahoro, ususuruke, uhage""; ariko ntimumuhe ivyo umubiri ukena, vyomara iki?
59002017	Ni ko bimeze, n'ukwizera kutari n'ibikorwa, kuri kwonyene, kuba gupfuye.
59002018	Nk'umuntu yovuga ati: ""Weho ufise ukwizera, jeho mfise ibikorwa: nyereka ukwizera kwawe kutagira ibikorwa, nanje ndakwereka ukwizera kwanje guserurwa n'ibikorwa vyanje."" "
59002019	Wemera yuko Imana ari imwe. Ugize neza; abadayimoni na bo nyene baravyemera, bagahinda agashitsi.
59002020	Ariko wa muntu w'imburakimazi we, mbega ugomba kumenya ingene ukwizera kutagira ibikorwa ari uko ubusa?
59002021	Aburahamu sogokuruza, mbega ntiyahinduwe umwere n'ibikorwa, hamwe yari atanze umwana wiwe Isaka ko ishikanwa amutanze ku gicaniro?
59002022	Ntubona yuko ukwizera kwafatanije n'ibikorwa vyiwe, kandi ko ukwizera kwahinguwe rwose n'ibikorwa?
59002023	Kandi icanditswe kirashika, kivuga ngo Aburahamu yizeye Imana, ibimuharurako nk'ukugororoka; kandi yitwa umukunzi w' Imana.
59002024	Murabona yuko ibikorwa ari vyo bihindura umuntu intungane, atari ukwizera kwonyene.
59002025	Kandi na Rahabu maraya ni ko vyabaye. Mbega ntiyahinduwe umwere n'ibikorwa kuko yahaye za ntumwa indaro, akazirangira iyindi nzira?
59002026	Nk'uko umubiri utarimwo impwemu uba upfuye, ni ko ukwizera kutagira ibikorwa kumera, kuba gupfuye.
59003001	Bavukanyi, muri mwebwe ntihakabe benshi barondera kuba abigisha. Murazi ko tuzocirwa urubanza ruruta izo abandi.
59003002	Kuko twese dutsitara muri vyinshi. Umuntu wese adatsitara mu vyo avuga, aba ari umuntu atunganye rwose, ashobora no kuganza umubiri wiwe wose.
59003003	Iyo twambitse iminyororo mu minwa y'ifarasi, kugira ngo zidukurikire, duhindukiza n'imibiri yazo zose.
59003004	Kandi raba, n'amato naho yoba maninimanini ate, agakubebwa n'umuyaga uhuhuta cane, ingafe naho ari ntonto cane ni zo ziyerekeza aho abayatumbereza bagomba.
59003005	N'ururimi ni ko ruri. Ni urugingo rutoya, rukirarira ibikomeye. Raba ishamba, naho ryoba rinini rite, ridomekwa n'akariro gake.
59003006	Ururimi ni umuriro, ni ikibi kingana n'isi. Ururimi rwashizwe mu ngingo zacu, ruhumanya umubiri wose, rudomeka ukubaho kwacu kwose, na rwo ruba rwadometswe na Gehinomu.
59003007	Kuko amoko yose y'ibikoko n'ibiguruka n'ivyikwega n'ivyo mu kiyaga bigundwa n'abantu, kandi barabigunze;
59003008	ariko, ururimi nta muntu yoshobora kurugunda. Ni ububi bucambagirana, rwuzuye ubumara bwica.
59003009	Urwo ni rwo dushimisha Umwami Data wa twese, kandi ni rwo tuvumisha abantu, baremwe mw'ishusho y'Imana.
59003010	Mu kanwa kamwe havamwo umuhezagiro n'umuvumo. Bavukanyi, ivyo ntibikwiye kumera bityo.
59003011	Mbega iriba ryodudubiza amazi aryoshe n'ayo umururazi mu mbizi imwe?
59003012	Bavukanyi, Mbega umusukoni woshobora kwama elayo, canke umuzabibu wokwama insukoni? Ni ko amazi y'umunyu adashobora kuvamwo ayaryoshe.
59003013	Ni nde muri mwebwe w'umunyabwenge kandi w'umuhanga? Ni yerekanishe ibikorwa vyiwe ingeso nziza mu bugwaneza bufatanije n'ubwenge.
59003014	Ariko namba mugira ishari ry'inkazi mu mitima yanyu, mugakunda kwirema ibice, ntimwirate, mubesha, mucumura ku kuri.
59003015	Ubwo bwenge si bwo bwururuka buvuye mw'ijuru, ariko ubwo isi, ubwo abantu n'ubwo abadayimoni.
59003016	Kuko aho ishari riri, bo no kwirema ibice, ari ho umuvurungano uri, n'igikorwa kibi cose.
59003017	Ariko ubwenge buva mw'ijuru, irya mbere buratunganye, kandi n'ubwo amahoro, burengenga, bukunda kugirwa inama, bwuzuye imbabazi n'imbuto nziza, ntibukekeranya, ntibugira uburyarya.
59003018	Kandi imbuto zo kugororoka zibibwa mu mahoro n'ababanguranya.
59004001	Muri mwebwe intambara ziva hehe, n'imitongano iva hehe? Mbega ntibiva mu bibahimbara birwanira mu ngingo zanyu?
59004002	Murifuza, ariko ntimuhabwa. Murica, mugira ishari, ariko ntimushobora kuronka; murarwana muratabara. Ntimuhabwa kuko mudasaba.
59004003	Murasaba ntimuhabwe, kuko musaba nabi, kugira ngo muvyononere mu bibahimbara.
59004004	Yemwe basambanyi, ntimuzi yuko gucudika n'isi ari ukwankana n'Imana? Nuko umuntu wese agomba kuba incuti y'isi aba yigize umwansi w'Imana.
59004005	Canke mwiyumvira yuko ivyanditswe bivugira ubusa, ngo Uwo Mpwemu yatugerereyemwo atwiyegereza afuha?
59004006	Ariko itanga ubuntu burushirije. Ni co gituma ivuga iti: "Imana irwanya abibona, ariko abicisha bugufi ibaha ubuntu." "
59004007	Nuko mugamburukire Imana, ariko murwanye wa mugarariji, na we azobahunga.
59004008	Mwiyegereze Imana, na yo izobegera. Yemwe banyavyaha, ni mukarabe; yemwe abo imitima ibiri, ni mwiyeze imitima.
59004009	Mubabare, muboroge, murire; ibitwengo vyanyu bihinduke amaborogo, umunezero uhinduke umubabaro.
59004010	Mwicishe bugufi imbere y'Umwami Imana, na yo izobashira hejuru.
59004011	Bavukanyi, ntimuvuganane nabi. Uwuvuga nabi umuvukanyi, canke uwuhinyurira umuvukanyi ku mutima, aba avuze nabi ivyagezwe, ni vyo aba ahinyuye. Ariko iyo uhinyura ivyagezwe, ntuba uvyitondera, uba ubaye umucamanza wavyo.
59004012	Uwushinga ivyagezwe, ari we mucamanza, ni Imwe gusa; ni yo ishobora kurokora no guhonya. Ariko wewe uri iki, uhinyura mugenzawe? "
59004013	Umve rero, yemwe abavuga ngo uwu musi canke ejo tuzoja mu gisagara c'i naka, tuzomarayo umwaka, tudandaze, turonke inyungu;
59004014	ariko mutazi ibizoba ejo. Ubuzima bwanyu ni nk'iki? muri umwuka uboneka umwanya muto, ugahava uyongayonga.
59004015	Ariko mwari mukwiye kuvuga muti: "Umwami wacu ni yabikunda, tuzoramba, kandi tuzokora dutya canke dutya."
59004016	Yamara none mwirata ukwihayagiza kwanyu; ukwirata kwose bene ukwo ni kubi.
59004017	Nuko uwuzi gukora neza ntabikore, bimubera icaha.
59005001	Ehe rero, yemwe batunzi, ni murire muboroge kuko mugira mufutane.
59005002	Ubutunzi bwanyu buraboze, impuzu zanyu ziriwe n'inyenzi;
59005003	izahabu n'ifeza vyanyu binyengeterewe n'ingese; ingese zavyo zizoba icabona co kubagiriza, zizonyengetera imibiri yanyu nk'umuriro. Mwarundanije mu misi y'umuhero.
59005004	Ehe ingero z' abashwabuzi babashwaburiye imirima, izo mwabagunze, zirataka. Amaborogo y'ababashwaburiye yinjiye mu matwi y'Uhoraho Nyeningabo.
59005005	Mwidibamiye mw'isi, mwihaye ibibahimbara: mwaguwe mpishi mu mitima ku musi wo gukekagurwa.
59005006	Mwatsindishije intungane, muramwica, ntiyabarwanya. "
59005007	Nuko bavukanyi, mwihangane mushitse aho umwami Yesu azozira. Ehe umurimyi arorera imirima myiza, ayirindira yihanganye, gushitsa aho izoronkera imvura y' agatasi n'iyo urushana.
59005008	Nuko namwe mwihangane, mureme mu mitima, kuko ukuza kw' Umwami kuri hafi.
59005009	Ntimwidodomberanire, bavukanyi, kugira ngo ntimucirweko iteka. Ehe umucamanza ahagaze ku rugi.
59005010	Abavugishijwe mw'izina ry'Umwami Imana bababere ikigereranyo bavukanyi, co kubabazwa no kwihangana.
59005011	Ehe abihanganye tubita abahirwe. Mwarumvise ukwihangana kwa Yobu, mwabonye ivyo Umwami Imana yaherutse kumugirira, ingene yuzuye imbabazi no kugira ikigongwe.
59005012	Ariko bavukanyi, ikiruta vyose, ntimukarahire. Ntimurahire ijuru, isi canke iyindi ndahiro yose; ariko ijambo ryanyu ribe Ego, ego; Oya, oya; kugira ngo ntimucirirweko urubanza rubatsinda. "
59005013	Muri mwebwe ni haba hariho uwubabaye, ni asenge; namba hariho uwuroraniwe n'umutima, ni aririmbe ishimwe;
59005014	muri mwebwe namba hariho uwurwaye, ni atumeko abashingantahe b'ishengero, baze kumusengera, bamusige amavuta ya elayo mw'izina ry'Umwami wacu.
59005015	Kandi ugusenga gufatanije n'ukwizera kuzokiza umurwayi, Umwami azomuvyura; kandi asanzwe yarakoze ivyaha azobiharirwa.
59005016	Mwaturanire ivyaha vyanyu, musengeranire, kugira ngo mukire indwara. Ugusaba kw'umugororotsi kugira ikimazi kuri vyinshi mu gikorwa cakwo.
59005017	Eliya yari umuntu ameze nkatwe, asaba yinginga ngo imvura ntigwe, imvura imara imyaka itatu n'amezi atandatu itagwa mu gihugu;
59005018	yongera gusaba, ijuru rirekura imvura, isi imeza imirima yayo.
59005019	Bavukanyi, ni hagira umuntu muri mwebwe azimira, akava ku vy'ukuri, uwundi akamuzimurura,
59005020	mumenye yuko uwuzimuruye umunyavyaha, akamukura mu nzira yiwe yazimiriyemwo, aba amukirije ubugingo urupfu, kandi aba apfutse ivyaha vyinshi.
60001001	Petero, intumwa ya Yesu Kristo, ndabandikiye abatoranijwe b'abanyamahanga bo mu basanzariye i Ponto, i Galatiya, i Kapadokiya, muri Asiya n'i Bituniya,
60001002	mwatoranirijwe mu kweza kwa Mpwemu nk'uko Imana Data wa twese yabamenye uhereye kera, kugira ngo mwumvire Imana, mumijwe amaraso ya Yesu Kristo. Ubuntu n'amahoro bigwire muri mwebwe.
60001003	Imana y'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ari yo Se, iragahezagirwa, yatuvyaye ubwa kabiri nk'uko imbabazi zayo nyinshi ziri, kugira ngo tugire ivyizigiro bizima, ituvyaza ukuzuka mu bapfuye kwa Yesu Kristo,
60001004	ngo tuzokwegukire umugabane utazobora, utanduye, udatituka, mwabikiwe mw'ijuru,
60001005	mwebwe abazigamwa n'ubushobozi bw'Imana kubwo ukwizera, muzigamirwa agakiza kateguwe kuzohishurwa mu gihe c'iherezo.
60001006	Ivyo murabinezererwa cane, naho ubu ari igihe gito mubabazwa n'ibibagerageza vyinshi, kuko bitobura kuza;
60001007	kugira ngo ukwizera kwanyu kugezwe (kandi ukwo kwizera kurusha igiciro izahabu ishira, naho ivugutirwa mu muriro ikakaka) kuzoboneke kuri n'ishimwe n'ubwiza n'icubahiro mu guhishurwa kwa Yesu Kristo.
60001008	Uwo muramukunda naho mutigeze kumubona; kandi n'ubu, naho mutaramubona, muramwizera, bibatera kunezerwa akanyamuneza k'ubwiza katovugwa,
60001009	mugahabwa ikizanwa n'ukwizera kwanyu, ni co gakiza k'ubugingo bwanyu.
60001010	Ivyo ako gakiza, abavugishwa n'Imana, ari bo bavuze ubuntu mwagira muzohabwe, barabirondera, barabisesura,
60001011	basesa igihe ico ari co n'ibimenyetso vyaryo, cerekanwa na Mpwemu wa Kristo yari muri bo, yavuga yatagura ivyo imibabaro ya Kristo bitaribwabe, n'ivyo ubwiza bw'uburyo bwinshi bwagira buzoyiherukire.
60001012	Kandi bahishurirwa yuko atari bo bavyikorera, ariko ko ari mwebwe babikorera; ni vyo none mumaze kubarirwa n'abababwiye ubutumwa bwiza, bavugishijwe na Mpwemu Yera yatumwe ava mw'ijuru, kandi ivyo abamarayika bifuza kubirunguruka.
60001013	Nuko rero mwiteguye gukora mu mitima yanyu, mwirinde ibiboreza, mwizigire rwose ubuntu muzozanirwa mu kuzohishurwa kwa Yesu Kristo.
60001014	Mumere nk' abana bagamburuka, ntimwishushanye n'ukwifuza kwanyu kwa kera kwo mu gihe c'ukutamenya kwanyu.
60001015	Ariko nk'uko Iyabahamagaye ari iyera, namwe mube ari ko muba abera mu ngeso zanyu zose.
60001016	Kuko vyanditswe, ngo mube abera, kuko nanje ndi uwera.
60001017	Kandi ko Iyo mwambaza muyita So ari yo icira umuntu wese urubanza rukwiranye n'ivyo yakoze itarobanuye ku cubahiro, mumare igihe co kuba abanyamahanga mugende mwubashe Imana kandi muyitinya.
60001018	Muzi yuko ivyo mwacungujwe ngo muve mu ngeso zanyu z'imburakimazi mwarazwe na ba sogokuruza atari ibishira, nk'ifeza canke izahabu,
60001019	ariko mwacungujwe amaraso y'igiciro kinini, nk'ayo umwagazi w'intama utagira agasembwa canke ibara, ni yo ya Kristo.
60001020	Uwo yamenywe n'Imana kera, itanguriro ry'isi ritarashirwaho, ariko yerekanywe kw'iherezo ry'ibihe kubwanyu,
60001021	mwebwe abo yahaye kwizera Imana, ni yo yamuzuye mu bapfuye ikamuha ubwiza. Ni co gituma ukwizera kwanyu n'ivyizigiro vyanyu biba ku Mana.
60001022	Nuko rero, ko mwejesheje imitima kwumvira ukuri, kugira ngo mukunde abavukanyi bitari uruheyiheyi, mukovye mu gukundana bivuye mu mitima.
60001023	Kuko mwavyawe ubwa kabiri, mutavyawe n'imbuto ibora, ariko mwavyawe n'imbuto itabora, mubiheshejwe n'ijambo ry'Imana ririho rigahoraho.
60001024	Kuko, Abafise umubiri bose basa n'ivyatsi, Ubwiza bwabo bwose bumeze nk'amashurwe y'ivyatsi; Ivyatsi biruma, amashurwe agahunguruka,
60001025	Ariko ijambo ry'Uhoraho ryamaho ibihe bidashira. Kandi iryo ni ryo jambo ry'ubutumwa bwiza mwabwiwe.
60002001	Nuko rero mwiyambure inzigo yose, ubugunge bwose, uburyarya, ishari no kuvuga abandi nabi kwose,
60002002	mumere nk'inzoya zivutse vuba, mwifuze amata y'umutima adafunguye, kugira ngo abakuze abashitse ku gakiza;
60002003	asangwa mwarayumvirije mukumva yuko Umwami wacu agira neza.
60002004	Nuko mumwegere, ari we buye rifise ubugingo, ryagawe n'abantu, ariko ku Mana ryaratoronijwe, riri n'igiciro,
60002005	mwubakwe nk'amabuye afise ubugingo, kugira ngo mube inzu yo mu buryo bw'impwemu, mugire igikorwa cera c'ubuherezi, ngo Muzotange ibimazi mu buryo bw'impwemu, bishimwa n' Imana kubwa Yesu Kristo.
60002006	Kuko mu vyanditswe harimwo aya majambo, ngo Raba, ndashira i Siyoni ibuye rigumya imfuruka, ryatoranijwe, riri n'igiciro, Kandi uwuryizera ntazomaramazwa.
60002007	Nuko mwebwe abizera ni mwebwe mwagerewe ico giciro, ariko ku banka kwizera, ngo Ibuye abubatsi bagaye, Ni ryo ryahindutse irigumya imfuruka,
60002008	Ni ibuye ritsitaza ni urutare rugwisha; kuko batsitara kw'ijambo ry'Imana, bataryumvira; kandi ni co bashiriweho.
60002009	Ariko mweho muri ubwoko bwatoranijwe, muri abaherezi b'ibwami, muri ihanga ryera, abantu bashiriweho kuba inyegu yiharije, kugira ngo mukwize ishimwe ry'Iyabahamagaye, ikabakura mu mwiza, ikabashitsa mu muco wayo utangaje.
60002010	Kera nta bantu mwarimwo, ariko noneho muri abantu b'Imana; kera ntimwaribwagirirwe imbabazi, ariko noneho mwarazigiriwe.
60002011	Abo nkunda, ndabinginga, ko muri abanyamahanga n'ingenzi mwirinde ivyifuzo vy'umubiri birwanya ubugingo;
60002012	mugire ingeso nziza mu mahanga, kugira ngo, no ku vyo babavuga nabi nk'inkozi z'ibibi, ibikorwa vyanyu vyiza babona bizotume bahimbaza Imana ku musi ibagendeye.
60002013	Kubwo Umwami wacu, ni mugamburukire ubukuru bwose bwashizweho n'abantu; ari umwami, kuko ari we gahebuza;
60002014	canke abakuru, kuko ari bo atuma guhana inkozi z'ibibi no gushima inkozi z'ivyiza.
60002015	Kuko ivyo Imana igomba ari uko ugukora neza kwanyu kuba agahomerabunwa ku bantu b'imburabwenge batagira ico bazi,
60002016	ngo mube nk'abidegemvya, ariko atari ukugira umwidegemvyo wanyu umwitwikiro w'inzigo, ariko mube nk'abakozi b'Imana.
60002017	Mwubahe abantu bose; mukunde abavukanyi banyu; mutinye Imana; mwubahe umwami.
60002018	Bakozi, mugamburukire ba shobuja, mububashe rwose, atari ababagirira neza n'ababihaganira gusa, ariko n'abadadika.
60002019	Kuko igishimwa ari uko umuntu, namba ahanuwe n'ijwi ryo mu mutima gukora ivyo Imana igomba, yokwihanganira imibabaro ahowe ubusa.
60002020	Mwokwihanganira gukubitwa ibipfunsi muhowe icaha, mwokwihaya iki? Ariko mwokwihanganira kubabazwa muhowe gukora neza, ivyo ni vyo bishimwa ku Mana.
60002021	Ivyo ni vyo mwahamagariwe, kuko na Kristo yabababarijwe, akabasigarana akarorero, kugira ngo mugere ikirenge mu ciwe.
60002022	We nta caha yakoze, kandi nta bugunge bwabonetse mu kanwa kiwe;
60002023	yaratutswe, ntiyabasubiza; yarababajwe, ntiyabahigira; ariko yiha Iyidaca urwa nkunzi.
60002024	Ubwiwe yikoreye ivyaha vyacu mu mubiri wiwe, abambwe ku giti, kugira ngo dupfuye ku vyaha tubeho ku kugororoka; inguma ziwe ni zo zabakijije.
60002025	Kuko mwari muzimiye nk'intama, ariko noneho mugarutse ku Mwungere w'ubugingo bwanyu, ari we nyene abujejwe.
60003001	Namwe bagore ni uko, mugamburukire abagabo banyu, kugira ngo, naho bamwe batumvira ijambo ry'Imana, bareshwe n'ingeso nziza z'abagore babo, batagize ijambo bavuze,
60003002	ni babona ingeso zanyu zitunganye zifatanije n'ugutinya.
60003003	Ugushaza kwanyu ntikube ukwo ku rukoba kwo gutsiba umushatsi, ukwo kwambara izahabu canke ukwo kwambara impuzu nziza;
60003004	ariko kube uko umuntu ahishijwe wo mu mutima, ugushaza kudashira, ni kwo mutima w'ubugwaneza utekereje, ni kwo kw'igiciro kinini imbere y'Imana. "
60003005	Ni ko abagore bera bizigira Imana bashaza kera, bagamburukira abagabo babo,
60003006	nk'uko Sara yumvira Aburahamu, akamwita umwami wiwe; namwe muri abana b'uwo, ni mwahora mukora neza, mudaterwa ubwoba n'icobaca ivutu.
60003007	Namwe bagabo ni uko, mubane n'abagore banyu nk'abazi ibibereye, kuko ari nk'ibikoresho bidahwanije namwe inkomezi. Kandi mubahe icubahiro, kuko na bo ari abaraganwa namwe ubuntu bw'ubugingo, kugira ngo ugusenga kwanyu ntikugire ikigutesha.
60003008	Ibisigaye, mwese muhuze umutima, mubabarane, mukundane nk'abavukana, mugiriranire imbabazi, mwicishe bugufi mu mutima;
60003009	ntimugere ikibi ku kindi, canke igitutsi ku kindi; ariko muvyishurane n'umuhezagiro, kuko ico ari co mwahamagariwe, kugira ngo namwe muragwe umugisha.
60003010	Kuko handitswe, " ngo Uwugomba gukunda ubugingo, No kubona imisi myiza, N'abuze ururimi rwiwe, ntiruvuge ikibi, Ni iminwa yiwe ntivuge ivyo uguhendana,
60003011	Kandi azibukire ibibi, akore ivyiza; Arondere amahoro, ayakurikire, kugira ngo ayashikire.
60003012	Kuko inyonga z'Uhoraho ziri ku bagororotsi, N'amatwi yiwe ari ku vyo basenga, Ariko igitsure c'Uhoraho kiri ku bakora ibibi.
60003013	Kandi ni nde yobagirira nabi, ni mwagira ishaka ry'ivyiza?
60003014	Yamara naho mwobabazwa muhowe ukugororoka, mwoba muhiriwe. Ntimuzotinye ivyo babakangisha, ntimuhagarike imitima,
60003015	ariko mwubahe Kristo mu mitima yanyu ko ari we Mwami, muhore mwiteguye kwishura umuntu wese ababajije inyanduruko y'ivyizigiro biri muri mwebwe, ariko muri n'ubugwaneza, mutinya.
60003016	Mufise imitima itarimwo ijwi ribagiriza ikibi, kugira ngo no ku vyo muvugwa nabi, abatuka ingeso zanyu nziza zo muri Kristo bamaramare.
60003017	Ivyoba vyiza ni uko mwobabazwa muhowe gukora ivyiza, ari co Imana igomvye, hako muhorwa gukora ibibi.
60003018	Kuko na Kristo yababajwe rimwe ahorwa ivyaha, umugororotsi yababarijwe abagabitanya, kugira ngo adushikirize Imana; yishwe umubiri, ariko yahinduwe muzima mu buryo bw'impwemu,
60003019	ni bwo yagiyemwo abarira impwemu ziri mw'ibohero ijambo ry'Imana,
60003020	ni zo z'abatumviye Imana kera, hamwe ukwihangana kwayo kwari kukirorereye mu misi ya Nowa, bwa bwato bukibazwa; muri bwo harokokeye abantu bakeya, bashika umunani, bakirijwe mu mazi.
60003021	Ayo ni yo abakiza namwe ubu, mu buryo bw'ikigereranyo c'ukubatizwa, si ugukuraho ubuhoma bwo ku mubiri, ariko ni isezerano ry'umutima utagiriza ikibi usezeranye ku Mana, abakirisha ukuzuka kwa Yesu Kristo,
60003022	ari i buryo bw' Imana, kuko yagiye mw'ijuru, amaze guhabwa gutwara abamarayika, abanyabubasha n'abanyabushobozi.
60004001	Nuko kuko Kristo yababarijwe mu mubiri, mwitwaze nk'ibirwanisho bene uwo mutima, kuko uwubabarijwe mu mubiri aba amaze kureka icaha,
60004002	kugira ngo amare imisi isigaye akiri mu mubiri atagikorera ivyifuzo vy'abantu, ariko akora ivyo Imana igomba.
60004003	Kuko igihe cashize gihagije gukora ivyo abanyamahanga bakunda gukora, no kugendera mu ngeso z'isoni nke, izo kwifuza, kunohorwa n'umuvinyu, kudandahirwa, kurundana aho bateretse n'ibizira vyo gusenga ibigirwamana.
60004004	Birabatangaza yuko mudafatanya na bo kwirukira mu birenze urugero vy'ubuhumbu, bakabadendereza;
60004005	mugabo ni bo bazobazwa ivyo n'uwiteguye kuzoca imanza z'abakiriho n'abapfuye.
60004006	Kuko icatumye abapfuye na bo babariwe ubutumwa bwiza kwari ukugira ngo bacirirwe imanza mu mubiri mu buryo bw'abantu, ariko babeho mu mpwemu mu buryo bw' Imana.
60004007	Ariko umuhero wa vyose uri hafi. Nuko ni mwitonde rero, mwirinde, kugira ngo mubone uko mushishikara gusenga.
60004008	Ikiruta vyose, mukovye mu gukundana, kuko urukundo rupfuka ivyaha vyinshi.
60004009	Muhane indaro mutidodomba.
60004010	Nk'uko umuntu wese yagabiwe ingabire muzifashishe abandi, nk'uko bibereye ababwiriza beza b'ubuntu bw'Imana bw'uburyo bwinshi.
60004011	Umuntu iyo avuze, avuge nk'uwubivugishijwe n' Imana; umuntu iyo agaburira abandi, agabure nk'uwufise ubushobozi Imana itanga; kugira ngo Imana iterwe icubahiro muri vyose, kubwa Yesu Kristo, afise icubahiro n'ububasha ibihe bitazoshira. Amina.
60004012	Abo nkunda, umuriro uri hagati yanyu wo kubagerageza ntukabatangaze, nk'aho mubonye akatabonetse.
60004013	Ariko munezerezwe n'uko mufatanije n'imibabaro ya Kristo, kugira ngo no mu gihe co guhishurwa kw'ubwiza bwiwe muzonezerwe muhimbarwe.
60004014	Iyo mututswe muhowe izina rya Kristo, muba muhiriwe; kuko Mpwemu w'ubwiza, ari we Mpwemu w'Imana, aba kuri mwebwe.
60004015	Ntihakagire umuntu wo muri mwebwe ahorwa kuba umwicanyi, igisuma, inkozi y'ikibi canke kwita mu vyo atagezwemwo.
60004016	Ariko ni hagira uwuhorwa kuba Umukristo, ntamaramare, ariko aheshe Imana icubahiro kubwo iryo zina.
60004017	Kuko igihe gishitse c'uko urubanza rutangurira mu b'inzu y'Imana, none ko rutanguriye kuri twebwe, iherezo ry' abatumvira ubutumwa bwiza bw' Imana rizomera rite?
60004018	Kandi ko umugororotsi akizwa agarukiye ku manga, uwutubaha Imana n'umunyavyaha bazoboneka hehe?
60004019	Nuko rero abababazwa nk'uko Imana igomba ni babitse ubugingo bwabo uwo Muremyi wo kwizigirwa, bakore ivyiza.
60005001	Ndahanura abashingantahe b'ishengero bo muri mwebwe ndabahanura, kuko nanje ndi umushingantahe mugenzi wanyu, kandi ndi icabona c'imibabaro Kristo yababajwe, kandi mfatanije namwe ubwiza buzohishurwa.
60005002	Muragire ubusho bw'Imana bwo muri mwebwe, mutaburagira nk'abagoberewe, ariko mubikunze, nk'uko Imana igomba. Ntimuburagirishwe no kurondera inyungu mbi, ariko muburagire muvyitangiye.
60005003	Kandi ntimuragire nk'abatwaza amanyama amasho mwagabanganirijwe, ariko mube ivyitegererezo vy'ubusho.
60005004	Nuko Umwungere mukuru ni yerekanwa, muzokwambikwa mu mitwe igitsibo c'ubwiza kitazoshira.
60005005	Namwe abakiri bato, mugamburukire abakurambere. Mwese mukenyere ukwicisha bugufi kugira ngo mukorerane, kuko Imana irwanya abibona, ariko abicisha bugufi ikabaha ubuntu.
60005006	Nuko mwicishe bugufi muri musi y'ukuboko kw'Imana kw'ubushobozi, kugira ngo izobashire hejuru mu gihe gikwiye.
60005007	Muyikorere amaganya yanyu yose, kuko ibababara.
60005008	Mwirinde ibiboreza, mwame mugavye. Umurezi wanyu, ari we wa mugarariji, agendagenda nk'intambwe yivuga, arondera uwo arotsa.
60005009	Mumurwanye mufise ukwizera gushikamye, muzi yuko imibabaro ihwanye n'iyanyu ishitswa ku bavukanyi banyu bari mw'isi.
60005010	Kandi Imana igira ubuntu bwose, yabahamagariye ubwiza bwayo budashira muri muri Kristo, ni mwaheza kubabazwa akanya gato, izobahingura rwose ubwayo, izobaremesha, ibahe inkomezi.
60005011	Ububasha bube ubwayo ibihe bitazoshira. Amina.
60005012	Ndabandikiye ikete c'amajambo make, canditswe na Siluwano, umuvukanyi w'umwizigirwa uko niyumvira; ndabahanura nshinga intahe yuko ubwo ari bwo buntu bw' Imana bw'ukuri. Mubuhagararemwo mushikamye.
60005013	Ishengero ry'i Babuloni ry'abatoranijwe nkamwe rirabatasha, bo na Mariko, umwana wanje.
60005014	Muramukanishe kugumbirana kw'urukundo. Amahoro abe muri mwebwe mwese muri muri Kristo.
61001001	Simoni Petero, umukozi wa Yesu Kristo kandi intumwa yiwe, ndabandikiye mwebwe abahawe ukwizera kw'akaburarugero kungana n'ukwacu, muguheshejwe n'ukugororoka kwa Yesu Kristo, ni we Mana yacu n'Umukiza.
61001002	Ubuntu n'amahoro bigwire muri mwebwe, mubiheshwa no kumenya Imana neza na Yesu Umwami wacu.
61001003	Kuko ubushobozi bw'ubumana bwayo bwaduhaye ivyo ubugingo no kwubaha Imana vyose, tubiheshwa no kumenya neza uwaduhamagarishije ubwiza bwiwe n'ingeso ziwe nziza.
61001004	Ivyo vyatumye aduha ivyo yasezeranye vy'akaburarugero, bihambaye cane, kugira ngo bibatere gusangira n'Imana akameremere kayo, mumaze gutoroka muva mw'iborero ryazanywe mw'isi no kwifuza."
61001005	Mbere kubwo iyo nyanduruko nyene, ubwanyu ni mugire umwete rwose; ukwizera kwanyu mukwongereko ingeso nziza; ingeso nziza muzongereko ubwenge;
61001006	ubwenge mubwongereko ukwirinda; ukwirinda mukwongereko ukwihangana; ukwihangana mukwongereko ukwubaha Imana;
61001007	ukwubaha Imana mukwongereko ugukunda abavukanyi; ugukunda abavukanyi mukwongereko urukundo.
61001008	Kuko namba mugira ivyo, bikagwira, bituma mutaba abanyabute canke abatunguka ku vyo kumenya neza Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo.
61001009	Kuko uwutagira ivyo ni mpumyi, abona ibiri hafi gusa, yibagiye umwuhagiro w'ivyaha vyiwe vya kera.
61001010	Ni co gituma, bavukanyi, mukwiye kurushiriza kugira umwete wo gukomeza ihamagarwa ugutoranywa kwanyu. Ni mwakora ivyo, ntimuzotsitara na gatoya.
61001011	Kuko ni vyaba bityo, muzohabwa rwose kwinjira mu bwami budashira bwa Yesu Kristo, ni we Mwami n'Umukiza wacu.
61001012	Ni co gituma imisi yose ntazohengeshanya kubibutsa ivyo, naho mubizi mukaba mushikamye mu kuri kuri muri mwebwe.
61001013	Ndiyumvira yuko nkwiye kubakangura ndabibutsa, nkiri muri uyu mubiri.
61001014	Kuko nzi yuko igihe co kwamburwa umubiri wanje kiza kuza gitebutse, nk'uko Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo yamenyesheje.
61001015	Ariko nzogira umwete, kugira ngo ni namara gupfa muzoshobore kwama mwibuka ivyo.
61001016	Kuko tutakurikiye imigani yaremwe n'akenge, hamwe twabamenyesha ubushobozi bw' Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo no kuzoza kwiwe; ariko n'uko twiboneye n'amaso yacu icubahiro ciwe gihambaye.
61001017	Kuko yahawe n'Imana Data wa twese ishimwe n'ubwiza, aho ijwi rivuzwe n'ubwiza bukomeye cane ryamushikako, rikavuga riti: "Nguwu Umwana wanje nkunda akampimbara."
61001018	Iryo jwi twaryumvise rivuye mw'ijuru, aho twari kumwe na we kuri wa musozi wera.
61001019	Ariko turafise ijambo ryavugishijwe, ryarakomejwe kurushiriza. Mugira neza ko murishirako umutima, ni nk'itara ryakira ahacuze umwiza, rigakesha ijoro, rikageza aho ikinyenyeri co mu gaturuturu kizokwakira mu mitima yanyu.
61001020	Irya mbere mukwiye kumenya, ni uko ata jambo ry'abavugishwa n'Imana ryo mu vyanditswe rishobora gusobanurwa nk'uko umuntu avyigombera,
61001021	kuko ata jambo ry'abavugishwa n'Imana ryazanywe no kugomba kw'umuntu, ariko abantu bavuga ivyava ku Mana, barongowe na Mpwemu Yera.
61002001	Ariko hari abigira abavugishwa n'Imana kandi, mu bwoko bw'Abisirayeli, nk'uko no muri mwebwe hazobaho abigisha b'ibinyoma, bazozana inyigisho mu mpisho zirema ibice, zitera guhona. Bazokwihakana na Shebuja yabaguze, bihamagarire uguhona gutebutse.
61002002	Kandi ingeso zabo z'isoni nke benshi bazozikurikira; kubwo ivyo inzira y'ukuri bazoyitukisha.
61002003	Kandi ukunohokera inyungu kwabo kuzobatera kubungukirako, bababwiye amajambo y'amaremano. Ntibateba gutsindwa n'urubanza kwabo uhereye kera, no guhona kwabo ntiguhunyiza.
61002004	Kuko, ko Imana itagiriye ikigongwe abamarayika bakoze ivyaha, ariko ikabakororera i kuzimu, ikabashira mu vyobo vy'umwiza, ngo babikirwe gutsindwa n'urubanza;
61002005	kandi ko itagiriye ikigongwe isi ya kera, ariko igakiza Nowa, umwigisha w'ivyo kugororoka, hamwe n'abandi indwi, aho yazana umwuzure kw'isi y'abatayubaha;
61002006	kandi ibisagara vy'i Sodomu n'i Gomora, ko yabiciriye urubanza rwo gukomvomvorwa ikabigira umunyota, ikabishiraho kuba akarorero k'abazogenda batubaha Imana,
61002007	ikarokora Loti, umugororotsi, yababazwa cane n'ingeso z'isoni nke z'abatirinda--
61002008	kuko uwo mugororotsi, aho yaba muri bo, yagira akabonge uko bukeye mu mutima wiwe ugororoka kubwo ibikorwa vyabo vy'ubugarariji yabona, akumva;--
61002009	Umwami Imana arazi gukiza abamwubaha ibibagerageza, no kurindira abagabitanya mu gihano gushitsa ku musi w'imanza,
61002010	ariko canecane abagenda bakurikira ivyo akameremere kabo, bifuza ibihumanya bagakengera ababaganza. Nta co batinya, ntibakurwa kw'ijambo, ntibahindishwa agashitsi no gutuka abanyacubahiro,
61002011	ariko abamarayika naho barusha abo bantu inkomezi n'ubushobozi, ntibarega abo banyacubahiro ku Mwami Imana, ntibabatuka.
61002012	Ariko abo bantu bameze nk'ibikoko bitagira ubwenge, ibikoko bukoko, vyavukiye gutegwa no kwicwa, batuka ivyo batazi, uguhonya kwabo kuzobahonya na bo,
61002013	bababazwe n'ibibi, ni zo ngero z'ubukozi bw'ibibi bwabo. Bumva ibibahimbara ari ukwirirwa badayangwa, abo ni amarabaga n'agasembwa, badayangishwa n'ivyo bagunze, bagisangira namwe ivyiza.
61002014	Amaso yabo yuzuye ubusambanyi, ntahaga ivyaha, bahendahenda imitima idashikamye, bafise imitima yamugariye kunohokera inyungu, ni abana b'ibivume.
61002015	Bataye inzira igororotse, barazimira, bakurikira inzira ya Balamu, umwana wa Beyori, umwe yakunze ingero zo kugabitanya,
61002016	ariko aharirwa ubugaba bwiwe, hamwe indogoba itazi kuvuga yavuga ijwi nk'iryo umuntu, ikabuza ibisazi vy'uwo muntu avugishwa n'Imana.
61002017	Abo ni amasoko akamye, kandi ni ibipfungu bitwarwa n'igihuhuta, barindirijwe umwiza w'umuzitanya.
61002018	Bavuga ibitumvye vy'ubwibone bitagira ico bimaze, bahendahenda abariko baridohora mu bagenda bazimiye, babahendahendesha ukwifuza kw'umubiri n'isoni nke.
61002019	Babasezeranira umwidegemvyo, ariko ubwabo ni abaja b'ibihumanye; kuko icanesheje umuntu kiba kimuhinduye umuja waco.
61002020	Namba kumenya neza Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu n'Umukiza kwarabateye kudohoka, bakava mu vy'isi bihumanya, maze bakongera kuvyizingiramwo, bikabanesha, ivyo hanyuma vyabo birusha ivya mbere kuba bibi.
61002021	Icobaye ciza kuri bo, iyaba batigeze kumenya inzira yo kugororoka, hako basubira inyuma, bamaze kuyimenya, bagata icagezwe cera bahawe.
61002022	Ivyabashitseko ni ivyo uwu mugani w'ukuri ngo imbwa isubiye ku vyo idashwe; kandi, ngo ingurube yuhagiwe isubiye kwivurunga mu vyondo.
61003001	Abo nkunda, none iki ni co cete ca kabiri ndabandikiye, muri ivyo vyose ndakangura ivyiyumviro vyanyu bitagira agasembwa, ndabibutsa;
61003002	kugira ngo mwibuke amajambo yavuzwe kera n'abavugishwa n'Imana bera, mwibuke n'icagezwe c'Umwami ni we Mukiza, cavuzwe n'abatumwa babatumweko.
61003003	Irya mbere mukwiye kumenya ni uko mu misi y'iherezo hazoza abacokoranyi bacokorana, bakurikira ukwifuza kwabo,
61003004	babaza bati: "Isezerano ryo kuza kwiwe riri hehe se?" Kuko uhereye aho ba sogokuruza basinziririye, vyose bihora uko vyamye, uhereye ku kuremwa kw'isi.
61003005	Kuko biyobagiza ibigirankana yuko kera hari amajuru, n'isi yakuwe mu mazi n'ijambo ry'Imana, rikayirema mu mazi.
61003006	Ivyo vyatumye isi ya kera amazi ayirengera, iratikira.
61003007	Ariko amajuru y'ubu, bo n'isi, iryo jambo ryabizigamye ribirorereza umuriro gushitsa ku musi w'imanza, wo gutikira kw'abatubaha Imana.
61003008	Ariko abo nkunda, iri rimwe mweho ntimuryiyobagize, yuko ku Mwami Imana umusi umwe umeze nk'imyaka igihumbi, n'imyaka igihumbi imeze nk'umusi umwe.
61003009	Umwami Imana ntitebeje isezerano ryayo, uko bamwe biyumvira ko iritevya. Ariko yihanganira mwebwe, ntigomba ko hagira abahona, ariko igomba ko bose bihana.
61003010	Ariko umusi w' Umwami wacu uzoza nk'igisuma, aho amajuru azovaho, hakaba n'ukwasana guhambaye, ivyo itanguriro vyose bigashongeshwa n'ikibengebenge gikaze, isi n'ibikorwa biri muri yo bigatongoka.
61003011	None, ko ivyo vyose bizoshonga bityo, mukwiye kumera mute mu ngeso zera no mu kwubaha Imana,
61003012	no mu kurereka ukuza kw'umusi w'Imana muwuhahamiye, uzotuma amajuru ashongeshwa no gusha, kandi ivyo itanguriro vyose bikayagishwa n'ikibengebenge gikaze?
61003013	Ariko nk'uko yasezeranye, tureretse ijuru rishasha n'isi nshasha, ivyo ukugororoka kuzobamwo.
61003014	Ni co gituma, abo nkunda, kuko mureretse ivyo, mukwiye kugira umwete wo kuzosangwa mu mahoro, mutagira ikirabagu, mutariko umugayo imbere yiwe.
61003015	Mwiyumvire yuko kwihangana kw'Umwami wacu ari agakiza; nk'uko umuvukanyi akundwa Pahulo yabandikiye, uko ubwenge yahawe bungana.
61003016	Yagenjeje atyo mu vyete vyiwe vyose, aho yavuze ivyo; muri vyo harimwo bimwebimwe bigoye itahura, ivyo abantu ataco bazi badakomeye bakavyihindurira ukwabo, nk'uko bagira ivyanditswe bindi, bakihamagarira guhona.
61003017	None mweho, abo nkunda, kuko musanzwe muzi ivyo, mwirinde ngo ntimutwarwe n'ubuzimire bw'abatirinda, mugata ugukomera kwanyu.
61003018	Ariko mukurire mu buntu bwa Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu n'Umukiza, no mu kumumenya. Icubahiro kibe iciwe ubu no gushitsa umusi utagira iherezo. Amina.
62001001	Icariho uhereye mu ntango, ico twumvise, ico twabonye n'amaso yacu, ico twitegereje, intoke zacu zikagikorako, ivyo kuri Jambo w'ubugingo--
62001002	kandi ubwo bugingo bwarerekanywe, turabubona, turabushingira intahe, kandi turababarira ivyo ubwo bugingo budashira, bwamanye na Data wa twese, tukabwerekwa--
62001003	ico twabonye tukacumva ni co tubabwira namwe, kugira ngo namwe mufatanye natwe. Kandi natwe dufatanije na Data wa twese n'Umwana wiwe Yesu Kristo.
62001004	Twanditse ivyo kugira ngo umunezero wacu wuzure.
62001005	Ubu ni bwo butumwa twumvise bwavuye kuri we, tukabubabwira, yuko Imana ari umuco, kandi muri yo ko hatagira umwiza na mukeya.
62001006	Tuvuze yuko dufatanije na yo, tukagendera mu mwiza, kuba ari ukubesha, ntituba dukora ivyo ukuri.
62001007	Ariko tugendeye mu muco, nk'uko na yo iri mu muco, tuba dufatanije ubwacu, kandi amaraso ya Yesu Umwana wayo atwoza icaha cose.
62001008	Tuvuze yuko ata caha dufise, tuba twizimiza, ukuri ntikuba kuri muri twebwe.
62001009	Ni twatura ivyaha vyacu, ni yo yo kwizigirwa kandi igororoka, ivyo ni vyo bituma iduharira ivyaha vyacu, ikatwoza ukugabitanya kwose.
62001010	Tuvuze yuko ata caha twakoze, tuba tuyigize umubeshi, kandi n'ijambo ryayo riba ritari muri twebwe.
62002001	Bana banje bato, ndabandikiye ivyo kugira ngo ntimukore icaha. Kandi ni hagira umuntu akora icaha, dufise Umwitsa kuri Data wa twese, ni Yesu Kristo umugororotsi,
62002002	kandi uwo ni we ndishi y'ivyaha vyacu, mugabo si iyo ivyacu twenyene, ariko ni iyo ivyo abari mw'isi bose.
62002003	Iki ni co kitumenyesha ko tumuzi, ni twitondera ivyagezwe na we.
62002004	Uwuvuga ngo Ndamuzi, ntiyitondere ivyagezwe vyiwe, ni umubeshi, ukuri ntikuri muri we.
62002005	Ariko uwitondera ijambo ryiwe wese, ugukunda Imana kuba guhinguwe muri we vy'ukuri. Iki ni co kitumenyesha ko turi muri we;
62002006	uwuvuga ko ahora muri we, akwiye na we kugenda nk'uko uwo yagenda.
62002007	Abo nkunda, si icagezwe gishasha ndabandikiye, ariko ni icagezwe ca kera, mwamanye uhereye mu bihe vya kera. Ico cagezwe ca kera ni co rya jambo mwumvise.
62002008	Kandi ndabandikira icagezwe gishasha, kandi ico n'ico ukuri muri we no muri mwebwe. Kuko umwiza uriko urashira, umuco w'ukuri umaze kwaka.
62002009	Uwuvuga ko ari mu muco, akanka umuvukanyi wundi, aba akiri mu mwiza gushika n'ubu.
62002010	Uwukunda umuvukanyi wundi aguma mu muco, nta gitsitaza kiri muri we.
62002011	Ariko uwanka umuvukanyi wundi ari mu mwiza, kandi agendera mu mwiza, ntazi iyo aja, kuko umwiza wamuhumishije amaso.
62002012	Ndabandikiye bana bato, kuko mwahariwe ivyaha vyanyu kubwo izina ryiwe.
62002013	Ndabandikiye ba se, kuko mwamenye uwamyeho mu ntango. Ndabandikiye misore, kuko mwanesheje wa Mubi. Narabandikiye bana bato, kuko muzi Data wa twese.
62002014	Narabandikiye ba se, kuko muzi uwamyeho mu ntango. Narabandikiye misore, kuko mufise inkomezi, kandi ijambo ry'Imana rikaguma muri mwebwe, kandi mwanesheje wa Mubi.
62002015	Ntimugakunde isi, canke ibiri mw'isi. Umuntu ni yakunda isi, ugukunda Data wa twese ntikuzoba kuri muri we.
62002016	Kuko ikiri mw'isi cose ari ivyifuzo vy'umubiri, ivyifuzo vy'amaso n'ubwibone bw'ubu bugingo, bitanduruka kuri Data wa twese, ariko vyanduruka mw'isi.
62002017	Kandi isi iriko irashirana n'ivyifuzo vyayo, ariko uwukora ivyo Imana igomba yamaho ibihe bidashira.
62002018	Bana bato, ubu ni igihe c'iherezo; kandi nk'uko mwumvise yuko Antikristo azoza, n'ubu hamaze guseruka ba Antikristo benshi. Ni co gitumye tumenya ko ari igihe c'iherezo.
62002019	Bavuye muri twebwe, ariko ntibari abacu. Iyo baba bari abacu, baba baragumanye natwe; ariko icatumye batuvamwo kwari ukugira ngo bahinyuke bose ko atari abacu.
62002020	Namwe mwarobanujwe amavuta n'Uwera, kandi muzi vyose.
62002021	Sindabandikiye kuko mutazi ukuri, ariko ni uko mukuzi, kandi kuko ata binyoma biva mu kuri.
62002022	Umubeshi ni nde, atari uwuhakana ko Yesu ari Kristo? Ni we Antikristo, ahakana Data wa twese n'Umwana.
62002023	Umuntu wese ahakana Umwana, na Data wa twese ntamufise. Uwemera Umwana afise na Data wa twese.
62002024	Mweho ico mwumvise uhereye ku va mu ntango kigume muri mwebwe. Ico mwumvise uhereye mu bihe vya kera ni caguma muri mwebwe, namwe muzoguma mu Mwana no muri Se.
62002025	Iri ni ryo sezerano yadusezeraniye, n'ubugingo budashira.
62002026	Ivyo ni vyo ndabandikiye ku vy' abobazimiza.
62002027	Mweho ukurobanuzwa amavuta mwarobanujwe na we kuguma muri mwebwe, namwe ntimurinda kugira uwo kubigisha, ariko nk'uko ukwo kubarobanura kwiwe kubigisha vyose, kandi ari uko ukuri, atari ibinyoma, kandi nk'uko kwabigishije, ni ko muguma muri we.
62002028	Na none bana bato, mugume muri we, kugira ngo ni yahishurwa tuzoshire ubwoba, ntidutetererwe imbere yiwe aho azozira.
62002029	Ko muzi yuko uwo ari umugororotsi, murazi yuko uwukora ivyo ukugororoka wese yavyawe na we.
62003001	Murabe urukundo uko rungana Data wa twese yatugiriye, ko twitwa abana b'Imana; kandi ni ko turi. Ni co gituma ab'isi batatuzi, kuko batayimenye.
62003002	Abo nkunda, none turi abana b'Imana, ariko uko tuzomera ntikurahishurwa; ico tuzi, n'uko Yesu ni yahishurwa tuzosa na we, kuko tuzomuraba uko ari.
62003003	Kandi umuntu wese amuzigako ivyo, ariyeza, nk'uko uwo ari uwera.
62003004	Umuntu wese akora icaha akora ivyo ubugarariji; kandi icaha ni co mugararizo.
62003005	Kandi murazi yuko uwo yahishuwe kugira ngo akureho ivyaha, kandi ata caha kiri muri we.
62003006	Umuntu wese aguma muri we ntakora ivyaha; uwukora ivyaha wese ntiyamubonye kandi ntiyamumenye."
62003007	Bana bato, ntihakagire uwubazimiza. Uwukora ibigororotse ni we agororoka, nk'uko uwo agororoka.
62003008	Uwukora ivyaha ni uwa wa mugarariji, kuko uhereye mu ntango uwo mugarariji yamye akora ivyaha. Icatumye Umwana w'Imana ahishurwa ngiki; ni ukugira ngo asangangure ibikorwa vy'umwansi.
62003009	Umuntu wese yavyawe n'Imana ntakora ivyaha, kuko imbuto yayo iguma muri we; kandi ntashobora gukora ivyaha, kuko yavyawe n'Imana.
62003010	Iki ni co kimenyekanisha abana b'Imana n'abana b'Umugarariji: uwudakora ibigororotse wese si uwo Imana, canke uwudakunda umuvukanyi wundi.
62003011	Kuko ubu ari bwo butumwa mwumvise uhereye mu bihe vya kera, ngo dukundane;
62003012	ntiduse na Kayini, yari uwa wa Mubi, akica murumuna we. Kandi icatumye amwica ni igiki? Ni uko ibikorwa vyiwe vyari bibi, ivya murumuna we bikaba vyiza.
62003013	Bavukanyi, ntimutangazwe n'uko abo isi babanka.
62003014	Twebwe turazi yuko twavuye mu rupfu, twashitse mu bugingo, kuko dukunda abavukanyi bacu. Uwudakundana yama mu rupfu.
62003015	Uwanka umuvukanyi wundi ni umwicanyi; kandi murazi yuko ata mwicanyi yogira ubugingo budashira ngo bugume muri we.
62003016	Iki ni co kitumenyesha urukundo, ni uko uwo yatanze ubugingo bwiwe kubwacu. Natwe dukwiye gutanga ubugingo bwacu kubwa abavukanyi bacu.
62003017	Ariko uwufise ibintu vyo mw'isi, akabona umuvukanyi wundi akenye, akazitira imbabazi ziwe kuri uwo, mbega ugukunda Imana kwoguma muri we gute?
62003018	Bana bato, ntidukundane mu majambo canke ku rurimi, ariko dukundane mu vyo dukora no mu kuri.
62003019	Ico ni co kizotumenyesha ko turi abo ukuri, kandi tuzoshitsa umutima mu nda imbere yayo,
62003020	mu vyo imitima yacu idutsindisha vyose, kuko Imana iruta imitima yacu, kandi izi vyose.
62003021	Abo nkunda, imitima yacu iyo itadutsindishije, turashira ubwoba imbere y'Imana;
62003022	kandi ico dusaba cose tugihabwa na yo, kuko twitondera ivyagezwe vyayo, tugakora ibishimwa imbere yayo.
62003023	Kandi icagezwe cayo ngiki: ni uko twizera izina ry'Umwana wayo Yesu Kristo, tugakundana, nk'uko yatubariye.
62003024	Kandi uwitondera ivyagezwe vyayo aguma muri yo, na yo ikaguma muri we. Kandi ikitumenyesha yuko iguma muri twebwe, ni Mpwemu yaduhaye.
62004001	Abo nkunda, ntimwemere impwemu zose, ariko mugerageze impwemu ko zavuye ku Mana. Kuko abigira abavugishwa n' Imana benshi badutse mw'isi.
62004002	Iki abe ari co kibamenyesha Mpwemu w'Imana, impwemu yose yatura Yesu Kristo ko yaje afise umubiri, iba yavuye ku Mana,
62004003	kandi impwemu yose itatura Yesu ityo ntiba yavuye ku Mana; kandi iyo mpwemu iba ari iya Antikristo, iyo mwumvise ko izoza, kandi n'ubu iramaze gushika mw'isi.
62004004	Mweho muri abava ku Mana, bana bato, kandi ba bandi mwarabanesheje; kuko Uwuri muri mwebwe aruta uwuri mu b'isi.
62004005	Abo ni abava mw'isi, ni co gituma bavuga ivyo isi, abo isi bakabumvira.
62004006	Tweho turi abava ku Mana; uwuzi Imana aratwumvira; uwutava ku Mana ntatwumvira. Ico ni co kitumenyesha impwemu y'ukuri n'impwemu izimiza.
62004007	Abo nkunda, dukundane; kuko urukundo ruva ku Mana. Umuntu wese akundana yavyawe n' Imana, kandi azi Imana.
62004008	Uwudakundana, ntazi Imana, kuko Imana ari urukundo.
62004009	Iki ni co caseruye urukundo rw'Imana muri twebwe, ni uko Imana yarungitse Umwana wayo w'ikinege mw'isi, kugira ngo duheshwe ubugingo na we.
62004010	Iki ni co kirimwo urukundo, si uko twebwe twakunze Imana, ariko n'uko ari yo yadukunze, igatuma Umwana wayo kuba indishi y'ivyaha vyacu.
62004011	Abo nkunda, ko Imana yadukunze ityo, natwe dukwiye gukundana.
62004012	Nta wigeze kubona Imana. Dukundanye, Imana iguma muri twebwe, no kuyikunda kuba guhinguwe muri twebwe.
62004013	Iki ni co kitumenyesha yuko tuguma muri yo, na yo ikaguma muri twebwe, ni uko yaduhaye kuri Mpwemu wayo.
62004014	Natwe twarabibonye, tubishingira intahe, yuko Data wa twese yatumye Umwana wiwe kuba Umukiza w'isi yose.
62004015	Uwatura yuko Yesu ari Umwana w'Imana, Imana iguma muri we, na we akaguma mu Mana.
62004016	Natwe twamenye kandi twizeye urukundo Imana idufitiye. Imana ni urukundo; kandi uwuguma mu rukundo aguma mu Mana, Imana ikaguma muri we.
62004017	Ico ni co kimaze guhingura urukundo muri twebwe, kugira ngo tuzoshire ubwoba ku musi w'imanza, kuko uko ari, ari ko turi muri iyi si.
62004018	Nta bwoba buba mu rukundo, ariko urukundo ruhinguwe rwirukana ubwoba, kuko ubwoba bugendana n'igihano, kandi uwufise ubwoba ntarahingurirwa mu rukundo.
62004019	Twebwe tugira urukundo, kuko ari yo yabanje kudukunda.
62004020	Umuntu ni yavuga ati: "Ndakunda Imana," akanka umuvukanyi wundi, aba ari umubeshi, kuko uwudakunda umuvukanyi yabonye ntashobora gukunda Imana atabonye.
62004021	Kandi dufise iki cagezwe kuri yo, ngo Uwukunda Imana akunde n'uwundi muvukanyi.
62005001	Uwemera wese yuko Yesu ari Kristo, ni we yavyawe n'Imana. Kandi umuntu wese akunda uwo Muvyeyi, akunda n'uwavyawe na we.
62005002	Iki ni co kitumenyesha yuko dukunda abana b' Imana, ni twakunda Imana tugakora ivyagezwe vyayo.
62005003	Kuko ugukunda Imana ari uku, ni uko twitondera ivyagezwe vyayo; kandi ivyagezwe vyayo ntibigora.
62005004	Kuko icavyawe n'Imana cose kinesha isi; iyi ni yo ntsinzi yacu yatsinze isi, ni ukwizera kwacu.
62005005	Ni nde atsinda isi, atari uwizera yuko Yesu ari Umwana w'Imana?
62005006	Ni we Yesu Kristo yaje agaca mu mazi no mu maraso; si mu mazi yonyene, ariko ni mu mazi no mu maraso.
62005007	Kandi Mpwemu ni we abishingira intahe, kuko Mpwemu ari ukuri.
62005008	Kuko ibishingantahe ari bitatu, Mpwemu, amazi n'amaraso; kandi ivyo bitatu bihuriza hamwe.
62005009	Ko twemera intahe ishinzwe n'abantu, intahe y'Imana yo ni agaheta; kuko intahe y'Imana ari iyi, ari uko yashingiye intahe ivyo Umwana wayo.
62005010	Uwizera Umwana w' Imana ni we afise iyo ntahe muri we; uwutizera Imana aba ayigize umubeshi, kuko atemeye intahe Imana yashingiye Umwana wayo.
62005011	Kandi iyo ntahe ni iyi: ni uko Imana yaduhaye ubugingo budashira, kandi ubwo bugingo ko buri mu Mwana wayo.
62005012	Uwufise Umwana wayo ni we afise ubwo bugingo; uwudafise Umwana w' Imana ntafise ubwo bugingo.
62005013	Ivyo ndabibandikiye, mwebwe mwizeye izina ry'Umwana w' Imana, kugira ngo mumenye yuko mufise ubugingo budashira.
62005014	Kandi ubu ni bwo bushizi bw'ubwoba dufise kuri yo, ni uko iyo dusavye ikintu cose gihwanye n'ivyo igomba, itwumva.
62005015	Kandi ko tuzi yuko yumva ico dusavye cose, bitumenyesha yuko duhawe ivyo tuyisavye.
62005016	Umuntu ni yabona umuvukanyi wundi akora icaha kitari ico kumwicisha, asenge, azohesha ubugingo abakoze ivyaha bitari ivyo kubicisha. Hari icaha co kwicisha; ico si co mvuze ko asengera.
62005017	Kugabitanya kwose ni icaha, kandi hari icaha kitari ico kwicisha.
62005018	Turazi yuko umuntu wese avyawe n'Imana adakora ivyaha, ariko umwe yavyarwa n'Imana aramuzigama, kandi wa Mubi ntamukorako.
62005019	Turazi yuko turi abo Imana, kandi isi yose iri muri wa Mubi.
62005020	Kandi tuzi yuko Umwana w'Imana yaje, akaduha ubwenge ngo tumenye Iyo ukuri, kandi turi mu Y'ukuri, turi mu Mwana wayo Yesu Kristo. Iyo ni yo Mana nyakuri, n'ubugingo budashira.
62005021	Bana bato, mwirinde ibigirwamana.
63001001	Jewe umushingantahe ndakwandikiye, mwubahwa watoranijwe, mwe n'abana bawe abo nkunda vy'ukuri; kandi si jewe jenyene ndabakunda, ariko n'abazi ukuri bose barabakunda,
63001002	kubwo ukuri kuba muri twebwe, kukazogumana natwe ibihe bidashira.
63001003	Ubuntu, imbabazi n'amahoro, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no kuri Yesu Kristo, Umwana wa Data wa twese, bizobana natwe mu vyo ukuri no mu rukundo.
63001004	Ndanezerewe cane, kuko nasanze bamwe mu bana bawe bagendera mu kuri, nk'uko twagezwe na Data wa twese.
63001005	Kandi none ndakwinginga mwubahwa, si nk'uwukwandikira icagezwe gishasha, ariko ni ico twamanye uhereye mu bihe vya kera, ngo dukundane.
63001006	Uru ni rwo rukundo, ni uko tugenda dukurikira ivyagezwe na we. Ico ni co cagezwe, nk'uko mwumvise uhereye mu bihe vya kera, ko mukigenderamwo. " "
63001007	Kuko abayobeza benshi baserutse bakaja mw'isi, batemera ko Yesu Kristo yaje afise umubiri. Uwumeze atyo, ni we ayobeza, kandi ni we Antikristo.
63001008	Mwiyubare, ntimuhombe ivyo ibikorwa mwakoze, ariko ngo muhabwe ingero itagabanije.
63001009	Umuntu wese arenga ku nyigisho, akagenda kure mu bindi, ntagume mu vyo Kristo yigishije, ntafise Imana. Uwuguma mu vyo yigishije ni we afise Data wa twese n'Umwana.
63001010	Ni hagira umuntu aza i wanyu, akaza atazanye iyo nyigisho, ntimuzomwakire mu nzu zanyu, kandi ntimuzomuhe ikaze;
63001011	kuko uwuzomuha ikaze azoba afatanije na we mu bikorwa vyiwe bibi.
63001012	Naho nari mfise vyinshi vyo kubandikira, singomvye kuvyandikisha ubwino ku rupapuro; ariko nizigiye kuzoza i wanyu ngo tuvugane imbonankubone kugira ngo umunezero wanyu ube uwuzuye.
63001013	Abana b'umuvukanyi wawe yatoranijwe baragutasha. "
64001001	Jewe umushingantahe ndakwandikiye Gayo umukundwa, nkunda vy'ukuri.
64001002	Mukundwa, ndagusengera ngo umererwe neza muri vyose, uhore uhangamye, nk'uko ubugingo bwawe bumerewe neza.
64001003	Kuko nanezerewe cane hamwe abavukanyi baza bagashingira intahe ukuri kwawe, yuko ugendera mu kuri.
64001004	Nta wundi munezero mfise uruta uwu, kwumva ko abana banje bagendera mu kuri.
64001005	Mukundwa, wama uyoboka mu vyo ukorera abavukanyi vyose, kandi ari abanyamahanga;
64001006	na bo bashingiye intahe urukundo rwawe mu maso y'ishengero. Kandi uzoba ugize neza ni wabarungika, uko bibereye ab' Imana.
64001007	Kuko bavuye i wabo kubwo Izina rya Yesu, ata co batse abanyamahanga. "
64001008	Nuko twebwe dukwiye kwakira neza abameze batyo, kugira ngo dufatanye n'ukuri gukora igikorwa.
64001009	Hari ico nandikiye ishengero, ariko Diyotirefe, akunda kwishira imbere muri bo, ntatwemera.
64001010	Ni co gituma, ni naza, nzobibutsa ivyo akora, atuvuga amajambo mabi y'ubupfu, kandi ntagarukiza kuri ivyo gusa, ariko ubwiwe ntiyakira abavukanyi, n'ababigomba arababuza, akabaca mw'ishengero. "
64001011	Mukundwa, ntukigane ikibi, ariko wigane iciza. Uwukora ivyiza ni we w'Imana; uwukora ibibi ntiyabonye Imana.
64001012	Demetiriyo ashingirwa intahe na bose, kandi n'ukuri ubwakwo kurayimushingira, natwe nyene turayimushingira. Nawe urazi ko ivyo dushingira intahe ari ivyo ukuri.
64001013	Nari mfise vyinshi vyo kukwandikira, mugabo singomba kukwandikishiriza ubwino n'ikaramu;
64001014	ariko nizigiye ko nzokubona vuba, tukazovugana imbonankubone.
64001015	Amahoro abane nawe. Abakunzi barakuganutsa. Untahirize abakunzi, uko amazina yabo angana. "
65001001	Yuda, umukozi wa Yesu Kristo, kandi mwene nyina wa Yakobo, ndabandikiye abahamagawe, bakundwa kuko muri mu Mana Data wa twese, mukazigamirwa Yesu Kristo.
65001002	Imbabazi, amahoro n'urukundo bigwire muri mwebwe.
65001003	Bakundwa, hamwe nashiruka umwete wo kubandikira ivyo agakiza dusangiye, nari numvise ikingobera kubandikira ivyo kubahanura kurwanira cane ukwizera abera bahawe rimwe gusa.
65001004	Kuko hariho bamwe babajemwo binyegeteza, bandikiwe kera gucirwako urwo rubanza, batubaha Imana, bahindura ubuntu bw'Imana yacu isoni nke, bakihakana Yesu Kristo, ni we wenyene Databuja n'Umwami wacu. "
65001005	Ndagomba kubibutsa, naho vyose musanzwe mubizi, yuko Umwami Imana, imaze gukiza bwa bwoko ikabukura mu gihugu ca Misiri, hanyuma yahoneje abatizeye.
65001006	N'abamarayika batagumye mu bukuru bwabo, ariko bataye ahantu habo, ibarindira kuzocirwa urubanza rwo ku musi uhambaye, bari mu minyororo idashira no mu mwiza.
65001007	Kandi n'abantu b'i Sodomu n'i Gomora bo n'ibisagara vyari bihereranye na ho, kuko bitanze bakiha ubusambanyi nka ba bandi, n'ubusambanyi bw'ishano, ubwo imibiri itaremewe, ivyo bisagara vyashiriweho kuba akarorero, bibabazwa n'igihano c'umuriro utazima.
65001008	Ariko na barya nyene bahwanye na bo, inzozi zabo zibatera kwonona imibiri yabo, no gukengera ukuganzwa no gutuka abanyacubahiro.
65001009	Ariko na Mikayeli, umumarayika mukuru, hamwe yatongana na wa Mugarariji, aharira na we bapfa umuvyimba wa Mose, ntiyubahutse kumuhinyura ngo amucokore, ariko yamubwiye ati: "Uhoraho aguhane."
65001010	Ariko abo bantu batuka ivyo batazi; kandi ni ivyo bamenyeshwa n'akameremere kabo, nk'uko ibikoko bimeze bitagira ubwenge, na vyo nyene baravyiyononesha.
65001011	Bazobona ibara, kuko bajanye inzira ya Kayini, bakiroha mu buzimire bwa Balamu kubwo amaronko, bagahonera mu mugararizo wa Kora.
65001012	Abo ni impanuka mw'isangira ryanyu ry'urukundo, iyo basangira namwe ivyiza; ni abungere biragira ubwabo ata dusoni; ni ibicu bitagira amazi, bizungagizwa hose n'umuyaga; n'ibiti birumvye bitama, vyapfuye kabiri, vyaranduranywe n'imizi;
65001013	ni imipfunda yo mu kiyaga isuriranya, babimba ifuro ry'ibiteye isoni vyabo; ni inyenyeri ziyerera zibikiwe umwiza w'umuzimagiza ibihe bidashira.
65001014	Kandi Henoki, ni we yagira indwi uhereye kuri Adamu, yavugishijwe n'Imana ivyabo ati: "Ehe Uhoraho yazananye n'isinzi ry'abera biwe,
65001015	kugira ngo acire bose imanza, no kwemeza abatubaha Imana bose ko batsinzwe ku bikorwa vyose vyo kutubaha Imana bakoze batayubaha, n'amajambo yose akomeye abanyavyaha batubaha Imana bavuze bayirwanya."
65001016	Abo ni abidodomba n'abanyamwikomo bagenda bakurikira ukwifuza kwabo, akanwa kabo kavuga amajambo yuzuyemwo ukwirarira, bubahira abantu kubakuramwo amaronko.
65001017	Ariko mweho, bakundwa, mwibuke amajambo yavuzwe kera n'intumwa z'Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo;
65001018	ko bababwiye bati: "Mu gihe c'iherezo hazoboneka abacokoranyi bagenda bakurikira ukwifuza kwabo kwo kutubaha Imana."
65001019	Abo ni bo bazana kwirema ibice; ni abantu gusa, ntibafise Mpwemu.
65001020	Ariko mweho, bakundwa, mwiyubake ku kwizera kwanyu kwera cane, musengere muri Mpwemu Yera,
65001021	mwizigamire mu rukundo rw'Imana, mwiteze imbabazi z' Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo zibashitsa ku bugingo budashira.
65001022	Ababahaririza mubahanure.
65001023	Abandi mubakize, mubokore mu muriro; abandi mubagirire ikigongwe mutinya, mwanke n'impuzu itewe amarabaga n'umubiri.
65001024	Ariko, Iyishobora kubazigama ngo ntimutsitare, no kubahagarika imbere y'ubwiza bwayo mudafise agasembwa munezerewe cane,
65001025	ni yo Mana imwe yonyene, Umukiza wacu yadukirishije Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu, ubwiza, icubahiro n'inganji n'ububasha bibe ivyayo, uhereye kera hose, gushika n'ubu, ugashitsa ibihe bidashira. Amina.
66001001	Uguhishura kwa Yesu Kristo, ukwo yahawe n'Imana ngo yereke abakozi biwe ibigira bibeho vuba, agatuma umumarayika wiwe akabimenyesha umukozi wiwe Yohana,
66001002	yashingiye intahe ivyo yabonye vyose, ni vyo jambo ry'Imana, no gushinga intahe kwa Yesu Kristo.
66001003	Harahiriwe uwusoma, harahiriwe n'abumva amajambo y'uku kuvugishwa n'Imana, bakitondera ivyanditswe muri yo; kuko igihe kiri hafi.
66001004	Jewe Yohana ndabandikiye mwebwe abo mu mashengero indwi yo muri Asiya. Ndabipfurije ubuntu n'amahoro biva kuri Iyo iriho, yamyeho kandi igira ize, biva no ku Mpwemu indwi ziri imbere y'intebe yayo,
66001005	no kuri Yesu Kristo, icabona co kwizigirwa, imfura y'abari barapfuye, uwuganza abami bo mw'isi. Umwe adukunda, yatubohoje ivyaha vyacu amaraso yiwe,
66001006	akaduhindura ubwami, no kuba abaherezi b'Imana yiwe, ni yo Se; icubahiro n'inganji bibe ivyiwe ibihe bitazoshira. Amina.
66001007	Ehe arazanana n'ibicu, kandi ijisho ryose rizomwibonera, n'abamucumise bazomubona; kandi amoko yose yo mw'isi azoborogeshwa na we. Ni ko biri. Amina.
66001008	Jewe ndi Alufa na Omega, ni ko Umwami Imana avuze, iriho, kandi yamyeho, kandi igira ize, ni yo ishobora vyose.
66001009	Jewe Yohana, umwana wa So, musangiye amarushwa, ubwami n'ukwihangana biri muri Yesu, nari ku kizinga Patimo co mu kiyaga, bampora ijambo ry'Imana no gushingira intahe Yesu.
66001010	Ku musi w'Imana nari muri Mpwemu, numva inyuma yanje ijwi rirenga nk'iryo inzumbeti,
66001011	rivuga riti: "Ico ubona ucandike mu gitabo, ukirungikire amashengero indwi, ukirungike muri Efeso, i Simuruna, i Perugamo, i Tuwatira, i Sarudi, i Filadelufiya n'i Lawodikiya."
66001012	Mpindukira kuraba ijwi tuvuganye; mpindukiye mbona ibiterekwako amatara indwi vy'izahabu,
66001013	kandi hagati y'ivyo biterekwako amatara mbona uwusa n'Umwana w'umuntu, yambaye imyambaro ishika ku birenge, yambaye mu gikiriza umukaba w'izahabu.
66001014	Kandi umutwe wiwe n'umushatsi vyera nk'ubwoya bw'intama y'umwero, canke nk'ipampa ryera cane n'amaso yiwe yasa n'imbeya z'umuriro;
66001015	ibirenge vyiwe vyasa n'umuringa w'umwakaka, utukujwe n'umuriro; n'ijwi ryiwe ryari rimeze nk'iryo amazi menshi asuma,
66001016	kandi mu kuboko kwiwe kw'i buryo yarafise inyenyeri indwi, mu kanwa kiwe havamwo inkota ikarishe, mu nyonga hiwe hari hameze nk'izuba iyo ryatse mu nkomezi zaryo zose.
66001017	Ndamubonye, nikubita imbere y'ibirenge vyiwe nk'uwupfuye; maze anshirako ukuboko kw'i buryo ati: "Ntutinye; jewe ndi uwa mbere kandi ndi uwo iherezo,
66001018	kandi ndi muzima; nari narapfuye, kandi raba mpora ndi muzima ibihe bitazoshira, mfise impfunguzo z'urupfu n'izo i kuzimu."
66001019	Nuko wandike ivyo ubonye, ibiriho n'ibizoba hanyuma y'ivyo.
66001020	Ibanga ry'inyenyeri indwi izo umbonanye mu kuboko kwanje kw'i buryo n'ivyo ibiterekwako amatara indwi vy'izahabu, inyenyeri indwi ni zo bamarayika b'ayo mashengero indwi, ibiterekwako amatara indwi na vyo ni vyo mashengero indwi.
66002001	Andikira umumarayika w'Ishengero ryo muri Efeso uti: "Uwufashe inyenyeri indwi mu kuboko kw'i buryo, akagendera hagati y'ibiterekwako amatara indwi vy'izahabu, aravuga ibi,
66002002	ngo Ndazi ibikorwa vyawe n'ubutame bwawe n'ukwihangana, kandi yuko udashobora kwirengagiza ababi, ariko wagenzuye abiyita intumwa kandi atari zo, usanga ni abanyabinyoma.
66002003	Kandi ugira ukwihangana, wirengagije ivyo ugirirwa kubwo izina ryanje, ntiwacobogora.
66002004	Ariko mfise ico ndakugayako, yuko waretse urukundo rwawe rwa mbere.
66002005	Nuko ni wibuke aho wavuye ukagwa; wihane, ukore ibikorwa nk'ivya mbere. Ni yo utagira utyo, nzokuzako nkure igiterekwako itara cawe ahantu haco, kiretse wihanye.
66002006	Ariko ico ufise ni uko wanka ibikorwa vy'Abanikolayiti, ivyo nanje nanka.
66002007	Uwuri n'ugutwi ni yumve ico Mpwemu abwira amashengero. Uwunesha, nzomuha kurya ku vyamye ku giti c'ubugingo kiri muri Paradiso y'Imana."
66002008	Kandi wandikire umumarayika w'Ishengero ry'i Simuruna uti: "Uwa mbere kandi uwo iherezo, uwari yarapfuye kandi akaba muzima, aravuga ibi,
66002009	ngo Ndazi amarushwa yawe n'ubworo bwawe (yamara uri umutunzi), n'ibitutsi vy'abiyita Abayuda, atari bo, ariko ari isengero ry'Abayuda ya Satani.
66002010	Ntutinye ivyo ugira ubabazwe. Ehe uwo mugarariji agira ashire bamwe muri mwebwe mw'ibohero kugira ngo mugeragezwe, kandi muzogira amarushwa imisi icumi. Wame uyoboka gushitsa ku gupfa, nanje nzoguha igitsibo c'ubugingo.
66002011	Uwuri n'ugutwi ni yumve ico Mpwemu abwira amashengero. Uwunesha nta co urupfu rwa kabiri ruzomugira."
66002012	Kandi wandikire umumarayika w'Ishengero ry'i Perugamo uti: "Uwufise inkota ikarishe aravuga ibi,
66002013	ngo Ndazi aho uba, ko ari ho umurwa wa Satani uri; kandi wumiye kw'izina ryanje, ntiwihakanye kunyizera no mu misi ya Antipa, icabona canje, n'umugororotsi wanje, yiciwe i wanyu, aho Satani aba.
66002014	Ariko mfise ivyo ndakugayako bike, kuko i wanyu uhafise abakomeza inyigisho za Balamu, yigishije Balaki gushira igitsitaza imbere y'Abisirayeli, kugira ngo barye ivyashikaniwe ibigirwamana, bashegure.
66002015	Ni ko nawe, ufise abakomeza inyigisho z'Abanikolayiti nk'uko nyene.
66002016	Nuko rero ni wihane. Ni yo utihana nzokuzako vuba, kandi abo nzobarwanya, ndabakubite inkota yo mu kanwa kanje.
66002017	Uwuri n'ugutwi ni yumve ico Mpwemu abwira amashengero. Uwunesha nzomuha kuri manu yanyegejwe, kandi nzomuha ibuye ryera, kuri iryo buye handitsweko izina rishasha, nta muntu arizi, atari uwuzorihabwa.
66002018	Kandi wandikire umumarayika w'Ishengero ry'i Tuwatira uti: "Umwana w'Imana, afise amaso asa n'imbeya z'umuriro, ibirenge vyiwe bisa n'umuringa w'umwakaka, aravuga ibi,
66002019	ngo Ndazi ibikorwa vyawe, urukundo rwawe, ukwizera kwawe, ingene ushitsa ibango ryawe, ukwihangana kwawe, kandi ko ibikorwa vyawe vyo hanyuma biruta ivya mbere kuba vyinshi."
66002020	Ariko mfise ico ndakugayako, yuko ukundira urya mugore Yezebeli, yiyita uwuvugishwa n'Imana, akigisha akazimiza abakozi banje, kugira ngo bashegure barye ivyashikaniwe ibigirwamana.
66002021	Kandi namuhaye uburyo bwo kwihana, ntiyakunda kwihana ngo areke ugushegura kwiwe.
66002022	Ehe ndamutsinda ku buriri, ndarungikira abasambana na we amarushwa menshi, ni batihana ibikorwa vyiwe.
66002023	Kandi n'abana biwe nzobicisha urupfu, kandi amashengero yose azomenya yuko ari jewe nsesa mu mishaha no mu mitima, kandi nzokwishura umuntu wese wo muri mwebwe ibihwanye n'ivyo mwakoze.
66002024	Ariko mweho abasigaye mu b'i Tuwatira, abadafise iyo nyigisho mwese, batamenye ivyo ba bandi bita ivyo mu kuzimu vya Satani, ndababwira nti: "Nta wundi mutwaro ndabikoreza atari uwu;
66002025	ko mwumira ku co mufise mugashitsa aho nzozira."
66002026	Uwunesha akitondera ibikorwa vyanje agashitsa kw'iherezo, nzomuha ububasha bwo kuganza amahanga.
66002027	Azoyaragiza inkoni y'icuma, nk'uko bamenagura inzavya z'ibumba; nk'uko nanje nahawe na Data.
66002028	Kandi nzomuha ikinyenyeri co mu gaturuturu.
66002029	Uwuri n'ugutwi, ni yumve ico Mpwemu abwira amashengero.
66003001	Kandi wandikire umumarayika w'Ishengero ry'i Sarudi uti: "Uwufise Impwemu indwi z' Imana n'inyenyeri indwi," aravuga ibi, ngo Ndazi ibikorwa vyawe, ko uvugwa ko uri muzima, ariko uri uwapfuye.
66003002	Gira ube maso, ukomeze ibisigaye bigira bipfe; kuko ata bikorwa vyawe nabonye bisozerewe imbere y'Imana yanje.
66003003	Ni wibuke rero ingene wakiriye kandi wumvise, uvyitondere, wihane. Nuko rero ni yo utaba maso, nzoza nk'igisuma, nawe ntuzomenya igihe nzokwubira.
66003004	Ariko ufise amazina makeya y'abo i Sarudi batanduje impuzu zabo; ni bo bazogendana nanje bambaye impuzu zera, kuko bibabereye.
66003005	Uwunesha uko ni kwo azokwambikwa impuzu zera, kandi sinzosibanganya izina ryiwe mu gitabo c'ubugingo na mba, kandi nzokwatura izina ryiwe imbere ya Data, n'imbere y'abamarayika biwe.
66003006	Uwuri n'ugutwi, ni yumve ico Mpwemu abwira amashengero.
66003007	Wandikire umumarayika w'Ishengero ry'i Filadelufiya uti: "Uwera, uwo ukuri, uwufise urupfunguruzo rwa Dawidi, uwugurura ntihagire uwugara, kandi uwugara ntihagire uwugurura, aravuga ibi,
66003008	ngo Ndazi ibikorwa vyawe (ehe nashize imbere yawe urugi rwuguruye, nta wushobora kurwugara) yuko ufise ubushobozi buke, witondeye ijambo ryanje, ntiwihakanye izina ryanje.
66003009	Ehe ndaguhaye bamwe bo mu rusengero rw'Abayuda ba Satani, biyita Abayuda, atari bo, ariko babesha; ehe nzobagobera kuza, bikubite imbere y'ibirenge vyawe, bamenye yuko nagukunze.
66003010	Ko witondeye ijambo ryo kwihangana kwanje, nanje nzokurinda igihe co kugerageza, kigira kize mu bihugu vyose, kugerageza ababa mw'isi.
66003011	Ngira nze vuba; wumire ku co ufise, ntihagire uwugutwara igitsibo cawe.
66003012	Uwunesha nzomugira inkingi yo mu rusengero rw'Imana yanje, kandi ntazosohoka ukundi, nanje nzomwandikako izina ry'Imana yanje, n'iryo umurwa w'Imana yanje, ni wo Yerusalemu mushasha, wururuka uvuye mw'ijuru ku Mana yanje, kandi nzomwandikako izina ryanje rishasha.
66003013	Uwuri n'ugutwi ni yumve ico Mpwemu abwira amashengero."
66003014	Wandikire umumarayika w'Ishengero ry'i Lawodikiya uti: "Uwiyita Amina, icabona co kwizigirwa kandi c'ukuri, inkomoko y'ivyaremwe n'Imana, aravuga ibi,
66003015	ngo Ndazi ibikorwa vyawe, yuko udakonje kandi ntubire. Icompa ugakonja canke ukabira!
66003016	Nuko rero kuko uri akazuyazi, udakonje ntubire, ngira ndakudahwe.
66003017	Kuko uvuga uti: "Ndi umukire ndatunze kandi nta co nkenye; ntumenye yuko ari wewe mutindi, wafutanye, uri umworo, uri impumyi, ugenda gusa;
66003018	ndakugira inama, ungureko izahabu yatyorowe n'umuriro, ubone kuba umutunzi; ungureko n'impuzu zera, ubone kwambara, isoni z'ubwambure bwawe ntizigaragare; kandi ungureko n'umuti wo gusiga ku maso, ubone guhumuka.
66003019	Abo nkunda bose ndabakankamira, nkabakangira; nuko gira umwete, wihane.
66003020	Ehe mpagaze ku rugi, ndaramukije. Umuntu ni yumva ijwi ryanje, akugurura umwango, ndinjira i we, dusangire.
66003021	Uwunesha, nzomuha kwicarana nanje ku ntebe yanje y'ubwami, nk'uko nanje nanesheje nkicarana na Data ku ntebe yiwe.
66003022	Uwuri n'ugutwi, ni yumve ico Mpwemu abwira amashengero."
66004001	Hanyuma y'ivyo ndavye mbona mw'ijuru umwango wuguruye, kandi rya jwi nabanje kwumva rivugana nanje ari nk'iryo inzumbeti, rirambwira riti: "Duga uze hano, nkwereke ibikwiye kuzobaho hanyuma y'ivyo."
66004002	Ako kanya nja muri Mpwemu; kandi mbona intebe iteretse mw'ijuru, mbona n'Uwuyivyagiyeko.
66004003	Uwari avyagiye yasa n'akabuye k'igiciro kitwa yasipi n'akitwa sarudiyo; kandi umunywamazi wari ukikije iyo ntebe, usa n'akitwa simaragido.
66004004	Iyo ntebe yari ikikijwe n'izindi ntebe mirongo ibiri na zine; kuri izo ntebe mbona abakuru mirongo ibiri na bane bazicayeko, bambaye impuzu zera, no mu mitwe yabo hari ibitsibo vy'izahabu.
66004005	Kandi kuri ya ntebe y'ubwami hava imiravyo, amajwi n'imituragaro, kandi imuri indwi z'umuriro zakira imbere y'iyo ntebe, ni zo Mpwemu indwi z'Imana.
66004006	Kandi imbere y'iyo ntebe hari nk'ikiyaga c'ibirahuri, gisa n'urubona; kandi hagati aharabana n'iyo ntebe no kuyikikuza hari ibinyabugingo bine vyuzuye amaso imbere n'inyuma.
66004007	Ikinyabugingo ca mbere casa n'intambwe, ica kabiri casa n'inyana, ica gatatu cari gifise mu maso hasa n'aho umuntu, ica kane casa n'inkona iguruka.
66004008	Ivyo binyabugingo bine bifise amababa atandatutandatu, kandi vyuzuye amaso impande zose n'imbere mu nda; ntibiruhuka ku murango no mw'ijoro, vyama bivuga biti: "Uwera, Uwera, Uwera, ni we Mwami Imana Ishobora vyose, yamyeho, kandi iriho, kandi agira aze."
66004009	Kandi iyo vya binyabugingo bihaye uguhimbazwa, icubahiro n'ishimwe Iyivyagiye kuri ya ntebe, ni yo Ibaho ibihe bitazoshira,
66004010	ba bakuru mirongo ibiri na bane baca bikubita imbere y'Iyivyagiye kuri iyo ntebe, bagasenga Iyibaho ibihe bitazoshira, bagaterera ibitsibo vyabo imbere y'iyo ntebe, bavuga
66004011	bati: "Mwami wacu, Mana yacu, birakubereye guhabwa uguhimbazwa, icubahiro n'ububasha, kuko ari wewe waremye vyose; icatumye bibaho kandi icatumye biremwa, ni uko wabigomvye."
66005001	Mbona igitabo mu kuboko kw'i buryo kw'Iyivyagiye kuri ya ntebe, canditse imbere n'inyuma, gihomeshejwe udushashara indwi, tukimatanije duteweko ikimenyetso.
66005002	Mbona umumarayika w'inkomezi nyinshi asemereza ijwi rirenga ati: "Ni nde bibereye ko azingurura kirya gitabo ngo amene ibikimatanije?"
66005003	Ntihagira uwo mw'ijuru canke uwo kw'isi canke uwo i kuzimu ashobora kuzingurura ico gitabo canke kukiraba.
66005004	Nanje ndizwa cane n'uko hatabonetse uwubereye kuzingurura ico gitabo canke kukiraba.
66005005	Umwe muri ba bakuru arambarira ati: "Nta co urira; ehe Intambwe yo mu muryango wa Yuda, Umunago wo ku gishitsi ca Dawidi, yaranesheje, ngo azingurure igitabo, amene ibikimatanije indwi."
66005006	Mbona hagati ya ya ntebe na vya binyabugingo bine no hagati ya ba bakuru, Umwagazi w'Intama ahagaze, asa n'uwishwe, afise amahembe indwi n'amaso indwi, ni vyo Mpwemu indwi z'Imana, zatumwe kwama zija mw'isi yose.
66005007	Araza, agikura mu kuboko kw'i buryo kw'Iyivyagiye kuri ya ntebe.
66005008	Amaze gufata ico gitabo, vya binyabugingo bine na ba bakuru mirongo ibiri na bane baca bikubita imbere y'uwo Mwagazi, bose bafise inanga, n'inzavya z'izahabu zuzuye imibavu, ni yo gusenga kw'abera.
66005009	Baririmba indirimbo nshasha bati: "Birakubereye gufata igitabo, no kumena ibikimatanije, kuko wishwe, ugacungurira Imana abo mu miryango yose, mu ndimi zose, mu moko yose no mu mahanga yose, ubacunguje amaraso yawe,
66005010	ukabahindura ubwami bw'Imana yacu no kuba abaherezi bayo, kandi bazoba abami mw'isi."
66005011	Ndaraba, numva ijwi ry'abamarayika benshi bakikije ya ntebe na vya binyabugingo na ba bakuru; igitigiri cabo cari amasinzi n'amasinzi, ni ibihumbi ni ibihumbi.
66005012	Bavuga n'ijwi rirenga bati: "Umwagazi yishwe abereye guhabwa ububasha, ubutunzi, ubwitonzi, ubushobozi, icubahiro, guhimbazwa n'umugisha.
66005013	Kandi icaremwe cose co mw'ijuru, mw'isi, i kuzimu, hejuru y'ikiyaga n'ibiri muri vyo vyose, numva bivuga biti: "Iyivyagiye ku ntebe bo n'Umwagazi w'Intama, umugisha, icubahiro, ishimwe n'ububasha bibe ivyabo no guhimbazwa ibihe bitazoshira."
66005014	Kandi vya binyabugingo bine biravuga biti: "Amina." Bano bakuru bikubita hasi, barasenga.
66006001	Mbona Umwagazi w'Intama amena kamwe muri twa dushashara indwi tumatanije ca gitabo; numva kimwe muri vya binyabugingo bine kivuga nk'ijwi ry'inkuba kiti: "Ngwino."
66006002	Mbona ifarasi y'umwero, kandi uwuyicayeko yarafise umuheto, ahabwa igitsibo, agenda anesha, kandi ngo yame anesha.
66006003	Kandi amenye aka kabiri kamatanije ca gitabo, numva ikigira kabiri mu binyabugingo kiti: "Ngwino."
66006004	Haza iyindi farasi y'akagajo, uwuyicayeko ahabwa gukura amahoro mw'isi, ngo bicane; kandi ahabwa inkota ndende.
66006005	Kandi amenye aka gatatu kamatanije ca gitabo, numva ikigira gatatu mu binyabugingo kiti: "Ngwino." Mbona ifarasi y' agafyiri; kandi uwuyicayeko yarafise umunzane mu minwe.
66006006	Numva hagati y'ivyo binyabugingo bine nk'ijwi rivuga riti: "Ingero imwe y'ingano n'idenariyo-idenariyo, n'ingero zitatu za sayiri ni idenariyo-idenariyo; ariko amavuta n'umuvinyu ntugire ico ubikorako.
66006007	Kandi amenye aka kane kamatanije ico gitabo, numva ijwi ry'ikigira kane mu binyabugingo kiti: "Ngwino."
66006008	Mbona ifarasi ibenjutse; kandi uwuyicayeko yitwa Rupfu, Kuzimu na we aramukurikira; bahabwa ububasha ku kigira kane c'isi, ngo babicishe inkota, inzara, urupfu n'ibikoko vyo kw'isi.
66006009	Kandi amenye aka gatanu kamatanije ico gitabo, mbona musi y'igicaniro impwemu z'abishwe babahorwa ijambo ry'Imana no gushinga intahe bari bafise.
66006010	Batakambisha ijwi rirenga bati: "Databuja wera w'ukuri, uzogeza ryari kudaca imanza no kudahora abari mw'isi amaraso yacu?
66006011	Umuntu wese muri bo ahabwa imyambaro yera, babarirwa kumara iyindi misi baruhuka, gushitsa aho igitigiri c'abakozi bagenzi babo n'abavukanyi babo, bagira bicwe nka bo, kizoshikira.
66006012	Kandi mbona amena aka gatandatu kamatanije ico gitabo, isi iratigita cane; izuba ririrabura nk'igunira ry'ubwoya; ukwezi kwose guhinduka nk'amaraso.
66006013	Inyenyeri zo kw'ijuru zikorokera hasi, nk'uko umusukoni uzungagizwa n'igihuhuta ugahungurura insukoni zawo zitararunguriza.
66006014	Ijuru ririzinga, nk'umuzingo w'igitabo kizinzwe; imisozi yose n'ibizinga vyo mu kiyaga vyose bikurwa ahantu havyo.
66006015	Abami bo mw'isi, abaganwa n'abakuru b'intwazangabo z'abasoda, abatunzi, abanyenkomezi, abakozi bose n'abidegemvya bose binyegeza mu masenga no mu bitandara vyo ku misozi;
66006016	babarira imisozi n'ibitandara bati: "Ni mutugweko, muduhishe amaso y'Iyivyagiye kuri irya ntebe n'ishavu ry'Umwagazi w'Intama;
66006017	kuko umusi uhambaye w'ishavu ryabo ushitse, kandi ni nde ashobora guhagarara?"
66007001	Hanyuma y'ivyo, mbona abamarayika bane bahagaze ku mfuruka zine z'isi, bafashe imiyaga ine yo kw'isi, kugira ngo ntihagire umuyaga uhuha kw'isi canke ku kiyaga canke ku giti cose.
66007002	Kandi mbona umumarayika wundi aduga, ava mu buseruko, afise ikidomesho c' Imana nzima, asemerera n'ijwi rirenga, abarira ba bamarayika bane bahawe kwonona isi n'ikiyaga
66007003	ati: "Ntimugire ico mugira isi canke ikiyaga canke ibiti, tutaradoma ikimenyetso mu ruhanga rw'abakozi b'Imana yacu."
66007004	Numva igitigiri c'abadomweko ikimenyetso, ngo ni ibihumbi ijana na mirongo ine na bine, abadomweko ikimenyetso bo mu bwoko bwose bw'Abisirayeli.
66007005	Abo mu muryango wa Yuda bakidomweko ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri. Abo mu bwoko bwa Reyubeni ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri. Abo mu bwoko bwa Gadi ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri.
66007006	Abo mu bwoko bwa Asheri ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri. Abo mu bwoko bwa Nafutali ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri. Abo mu bwoko bwa Manase ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri.
66007007	Abo mu bwoko bwa Simeyoni ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri. Abo mu bwoko bwa Lewi ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri. Abo mu bwoko bwa Isakari ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri.
66007008	Abo mu bwoko bwa Zebuloni ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri. Abo mu bwoko bwa Yosefu ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri. Abo mu bwoko bwa Benyamini badomweko ikimenyetso ni ibihumbi icumi na bibiri.
66007009	Hanyuma y'ivyo mbona ishengero ryinshi, ata woshobora kuriharura, bo mu mahanga yose, imiryango yose, mu moko yose no mu ndimi zose, bahagaze imbere y'iyo ntebe n'imbere y'Umwagazi w'Intama, bambaye imyambaro yera, bari n'amashami y'ibigazi mu minwe.
66007010	Basemerera n'ijwi rirenga bati: "Agakiza ni ako Imana yacu ivyagiye kuri irya ntebe kandi ni ako Umwagazi w'Intama."
66007011	Abamarayika bose bari bahagaze bakikije ino ntebe, bakikije na ba bakuru na vya binyabugingo, bikubita hasi bubamye imbere y'intebe, basenga Imana
66007012	bati: "Amina, umugisha, guhimbazwa, ubwenge, ishimwe, icubahiro, ububasha n'ubushobozi ni ivyo Imana yacu ibihe bitazoshira. Amina."
66007013	Umwe muri ba bakuru arambaza ati: "Aba bambaye imyambaro yera ni ba nde, kandi bavuye hehe?"
66007014	Ndamwishura nti: "Mugenzi, ni wewe wobimenya." Arambwira ati: "Aba ni abavuye muri wa mubabaro mwinshi, kandi bamesuye imvune zabo bazezesha amaraso ya wa Mwagazi.
66007015	Ni co gituma baba imbere y'intebe y'Imana, bakayikorera mu rusengero rwayo ku murango no mw'ijoro. Kandi Iyivyagiye kuri irya ntebe izosanza ihema ryayo hejuru yabo.
66007016	Ntibazoba bakigira inzara ukundi, kandi ntibazoba bakigira inyota ukundi, kandi izuba ntirizobarabika canke indugumba yose,
66007017	kuko wa Mwagazi ari hagati aharabana n'iyo ntebe, azobaragira, kandi azobashora ku masoko y'amazi y'ubugingo; kandi Imana izohanagura amosozi yose ku maso yabo.
66008001	Kandi amenye ikigira indwi kimatanije ico gitabo, haba agacerere mw'ijuru nk'igice c'isaha.
66008002	Mbona abamarayika indwi bama bahagarara imbere y'Imana bahabwa inzumbeti indwi.
66008003	Haza uwundi mumarayika, ahagarara ku gicaniro, afise icotero c'izahabu, ahabwa imibavu myinshi ngo ayishire ku gusenga kw'abera bose kuri ku gicaniro c'izahabu kiri imbere y'iyo ntebe.
66008004	Umwotsi w'umubavu uva mu kuboko kw'umumarayika upfundukana n'ugusenga kw'abera imbere y'Imana.
66008005	Umumarayika ajana icotero, acuzuza umuriro wo ku gicaniro, ashiburira mw'isi, habaho imituragaro, amajwi, imiravyo no gutigita kw'isi.
66008006	Ba bamarayika indwi bafise inzumbeti indwi bagabiriza kuzivuza.
66008007	Uwa mbere aravuza. Haza urubura n'umuriro bivanze n'amaraso, bishiburirwa mw'isi ica gatatu c'isi kirasha, ica gatatu c'ibiti kirasha, ivyatsi bibisi vyose birasha.
66008008	Umumarayika wa kabiri aravuza. Ikimeze nk'igisozi kinini caka umuriro gishiburirwa mu kiyaga; ica gatatu c'ikiyaga gihinduka amaraso;
66008009	ica gatatu c'ivyaremwe vyo mu kiyaga bifise ubugingo kirapfa; ica gatatu c'amato kirahona.
66008010	Umumarayika wa gatatu aravuza, inyenyeri nini iva mw'ijuru iratibuka, yaka nk'urumuri, itibukira ku kigira gatatu c'inzuzi no ku masoko.
66008011	Iyo nyenyeri yitwa Mururazi. Ica gatatu c'amazi gihinduka umururazi, abantu benshi bicwa n'ayo mazi, kuko yarurishijwe.
66008012	Umumarayika wa kane aravuza. Ica gatatu c'izuba, icagatatu c'ukwezi n'ica gatatu c'inyenyeri birakubitwa, kugira ngo ica gatatu cavyo gicure umwiza, ica gatatu co mu bihe vy'umurango nticakirwe, no mw'ijoro ni uko.
66008013	Ndaraba, numva inkukuma iguruka hejuru mu kirere, ivuga n'ijwi rirenga iti: "Ibara, ibara, ibara riza kubonwa n'abari mw'isi kubwo ayandi majwi y'inzumbeti z'abamarayika batatu bahava bavuza."
66009001	Umumarayika wa gatanu aravuza. Mbona inyenyeri itibukiye mw'isi ivuye kw'ijuru; ihabwa urupfunguruzo rw'imanga yo mu kuzimu.
66009002	Yugurura iyo manga yo mu kuzimu, ipfundukamwo umwotsi nk'uwo itanure rinini, izuba n'ikirere bicurishwa umwiza n'umwotsi wo muri iyo manga.
66009003	Mu mwotsi havamwo inzige, zija mw'isi, zihabwa ububasha bwo gukora ivyo sikorupiyo zo kw'isi zibasha gukora.
66009004	Zibwirwa kutagira ico zigira ivyatsi vyo kw'isi canke ikintu cose kibisi canke igiti cose, atari abantu batadomweko ikimenyetso c'Imana mu ruhanga rwabo.
66009005	Zihabwa kutabica, ariko zihabwa kubababaza amezi atanu. Kandi ukubabaza kwazo kumeze nk'ukwa sikorupiyo iyo iriye umuntu.
66009006	Muri iyo misi abantu bazoba barondera urupfu, ariko ntibazorubona na gatoya; bazoba bifuza gupfa, urupfu rubahunge.
66009007	Kandi ishusho y'izo nzige yasa n'iyo amafarasi ateguriwe kuja mu ntambara, zari zambaye mu mitwe ibitsibo bisa n'izahabu, mu maso hazo hasa n'aho abantu.
66009008	Kandi zari zifise ubwoya bumeze nk'umushatsi w'abagore, amenyo yazo yari nk'ayo intambwe.
